devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet ।। jayati parāśarasūnuḥ satyavatīhṛdayanandano vyāsaḥ । yasyāsyakamalagalitaṃ vāṅmayam amṛtaṃ jagat pibati । pitāmahādyaṃ pravadanti ṣaṣṭhaṃ maharṣim akṣayyavibhūtiyuktam । nārāyaṇasyāṃsajam ekaputraṃ dvaipāyanaṃ vedamahānidhānam । ādyaṃ puruṣam īśānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam । ṛtam ekākṣaraṃ brahma vyaktāvyaktaṃ sanātanam ।। asac ca sadasac caiva yad viśvaṃ sadasatparam । parāvarāṇāṃ sraṣṭāraṃ purāṇaṃ param avyayam । maṅgalyaṃ maṅgalam viṣṇuṃ vareṇyam anaghaṃ śucim । namaskṛtya hṛṣīkeśaṃ carācaraguruṃ harim ।। naimiṣāraṇye kulapatiḥ śaunakas tu mahāmuniḥ । sautiṃ papraccha dharmātmā sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ । jajñe bahujñaṃ param atyudāraṃ yaṃ dvīpamadhye sutam ātmayogāt । parāśarāt satyavatī maharṣiṃ tasmai namo ajñānatamonudāya । yo gośataṃ kanakaśṛṅgamayaṃ dadāti viprāya vedaviduṣe bahuviśrutāya । puṇyāṃ ca bhāratakathāṃ śṛṇuyāc ca tadvat tulyaṃ phalaṃ bhavati tasya ca tasya caiva । śatāśvamedhasya yad atra puṇyaṃ catuḥsahasrasya śatakratoś ca । bhaved anantaṃ harivaṃśadānāt prakīrtitaṃ vyāsamaharṣiṇā ca । yad vājapeyena tu rājasūyād dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ hastirathena cānyat । tal labhyate vyāsavacaḥ pramāṇaṃ gītaṃ ca vālmīkimaharṣiṇā ca । dvaipāyanauṣṭhapuṭaniḥsṛtam aprameyaṃ puṇyaṃ pavitram atha pāpaharaṃ śivaṃ ca । yo bhārataṃ samadhigacchati vācyamānaṃ kiṃ tasya puṣkarajalair abhiṣecanena । yo harivaṃśaṃ lekhayati yathāvidhinā mahātapāḥ sapadi ।sa yāti hareḥ padakamalaṃ kamalaṃ madhupo yathā lubdhaḥ ।yaṃ brahma vedāntavido vadanti paraṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ tathānye । viśvād gateḥ kāraṇam īśvaraṃ sa tasmai namo vighnavināśanāya । saṃsāratāraṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ yogidhyeyam anuttamam । śṛṇoti harivaṃśaṃ yaḥ śraddhayā vaṃśavardhanam । pratyakṣaraṃ bhavet teṣāṃ kapilādānajaṃ phalam । yo dadāti harivaṃśapustakaṃ brāhmaṇāya viduṣe sadakṣiṇam । so aśvamedhaphalabhāg bhaven naraḥ satyam eva kathitaṃ maharṣiṇā । cakraṃ yasya bhujāgrahastalalitaṃ vidyutprabhaṃ rājate śaṅkho yasya virājate karatale saṃpūrṇacandraprabhaḥ । mālā yasya sacampakā satilakā sāśokanīlotpalā sa tvāṃ pātu ṣadardhavikramagatis trilokyanātho hariḥ । yo avidyādyair aśeṣair manasi vinihitaiḥ kleśasaṃjñais tridoṣair aspṛṣṭo nirguṇatvāt paramagururajaḥkarmabhis tatphalair vā । sarvajñatvādiyukto niratiśayasukhaprāptihetur yatīnāṃ so anādir vāsudevaḥ śamayatu duritaṃ sarvajanmārjitaṃ vaḥ । jitaṃ te puṇḍarīkākṣa namas te viśvabhāvana । namas te astu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣapūrvaja । śuklāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ śaśivarṇaṃ caturbhujam । prasannavadanaṃ dhyāyet sarvavighnopaśāntaye । vāgīśādyāḥ sumanasaḥ sarvārthānām upakrame । yaṃ natvā kṛtakṛtyāḥ syus taṃ namāmi gajānanam । indirākucapāṭīra paṅkasaṃkalitodaraḥ । dadyād amandam ānandam acirān no nṛkesarī । kālindījalakallola kolāhalakutūhalī । asatkīrtanakāntāra parivartanapāṃsulām । vācaṃ śaurikathālāpa gaṅgayaiva punīmahe । indīvarakaḷaśyāmaṃ indirānandakandaḷam । vandārujanamandāraṃ vande ahaṃ yadunandanam । vyāsaṃ vasiṣṭhanaptāraṃ śakteḥ putram akalmaṣam । parāśarātmajaṃ vande śukatātaṃ taponidhim । vyāsāya viṣṇurūpāya vyāsarūpāya viṣṇave । namo vai brahmanidhaye vāsiṣṭhāya namo namaḥ । bhāratānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ pārthivānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। daityānām atha siddhānāṃ guhyakānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।
vicitrāś ca kathāyogā janma cāgryam anuttamam ।। manaḥkarṇasukhaṃ tan māṃ prīṇāty amṛtasaṃmitam ।। na tu vṛṣṇyandhakānāṃ vai tad bhavān prabravītu me ।। dharmavit kathayām āsa kulaṃ teṣāṃ savistaram ।
tat te ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi vṛṣṇīnāṃ vaṃśam āditaḥ ।। janamejayo mahāprājño vaiśaṃpāyanam abravīt ।। kathitaṃ bhavatā vipra vistareṇa mayā śrutam ।। nāmabhiḥ karmabhiś caiva vṛṣṇyandhakamahārathāḥ ।।
tatra tatra samāsena vistareṇaiva cābhibho ।। ekaś ca me mato rāśir vṛṣṇayaḥ pāṇḍavās tathā ।। kathayasva kulaṃ teṣāṃ vistareṇa tapodhana ।। pūrvaṃ kathā samākhyātā vicitrā ca mahīpate ।
teṣāṃ pūrvavisṛṣṭiṃ ca vicitrām ā prajāpateḥ ।। sarvam etad aśeṣeṇa kathayasva dvijottama । yena vai śṛṇvatāṃ puṃsām aputratvaṃ praṇaśyati । evaṃ saṃcodito rājā vyāsaśiṣyo mahāmune । vistareṇānupūrvyā ca kathayām āsa tāṃ kathām ।। kathyamānāṃ mayā citrāṃ bahvarthāṃ śrutisaṃmitām ।।
yaś caināṃ dhārayed vipraḥ śrāvayed vā mahātmanām । svavaṃśadhāraṇaṃ kṛtvā svargaloke mahīyate ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ tasmān nirmame viśvam īśvaraḥ ।। sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇam ।।
bhūtabhedāś ca bhūtebhya iti sargaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। kīrtyamānaṃ śṛṇu mayā pūrveṣāṃ kīrtivardhanam ।। kīrtanaṃ sthirakīrtīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।। tasmai hiraṇyagarbhāya puruṣāyeśvarāya ca ।
ajāya prathamāyaiva variṣṭhāya prajāpate । brahmaṇe lokanāthāya gariṣṭhāya svayaṃbhuve । praṇamya prabhave pūrvaṃ tasmai amitatejase । ā vṛṣṇivaṃśād vakṣyāmi bhūtasargam anuttamam ।।
apa eva sasarjādau tāsu vīryam avāsṛjat ।। ayanaṃ tasya tāḥ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tatra jajñe svayaṃ brahmā svayaṃbhūr iti naḥ śrutam ।। tad aṇḍam akarod dvaidhaṃ divaṃ bhuvam athāpi ca ।।
apsu pāriplavāṃ pṛthvīṃ diśaś ca daśadhā dadhe ।। sasarja sṛṣṭiṃ tadrūpāṃ sraṣṭum icchan prajāpatim ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ ca mahātejāḥ so asṛjat sapta mānasān ।। nārāyaṇātmakānāṃ vai saptānāṃ brahmajanmanām ।।
sanatkumāraṃ ca ṛṣiṃ pūrveṣām api pūrvajam ।। skandaḥ sanatkumāraś ca tejaḥ saṃkṣipya tiṣṭhataḥ ।। kriyāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharṣibhir alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। sanaś ca yogatattvajñaṃ sanakaṃ ca sanandanam ।
ete sapta samākhyātā ṛṣayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ । yādāṃsi ca sasarjādau parjanyaṃ ca sasarja ha ।। mukhād devān ajanayat pitṝṃś ceśo api vakṣasaḥ । prajanāc ca manuṣyān vai jaghanān nirmame asurān ।
sādhyāṃs tair ayajan devān ity evam anuśuśrumaḥ ।। brahmāṇaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhittvā niścito bhagavān bhṛguḥ ।। stanaṃ tu dakṣiṇaṃ bhittvā brahmajena ca vigrahaḥ । niśrito bhagavān dharmaḥ sarvalokasukhāvahaḥ ।।
trayas tasya varāḥ putrāḥ sarvabhūtamanoharāḥ । kāmaḥ śamaś ca harṣaś ca tejasā lokadhāriṇaḥ ।। kāmasya tu ratir bhāryā śamasya prītir aṅganā । nandā bhāryā ca harṣasya trayo lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।
āpavasya prajāsargaṃ sṛjato hi prajāpateḥ ।। sṛjyamānāḥ prajā naiva vivardhante yadā tadā । divaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ caiva mahimnā vyāpya tiṣṭati ।। dvitīyam āpavasyaitan manor antaram ucyate ।।
manuṃ prajāpatiṃ viddhi sasarja prabhur īśvaraḥ । nārāyaṇavisargaḥ sa prajās tasyāpy ayonijāḥ ।। sthiravaṃśaś ca bhavati mṛtaḥ svarge mahīyate । ādisargaṃ viditvemaṃ yatheṣṭāṃ prāpnuyād gatim ।।
lebhe vai puruṣaḥ patnīṃ śatarūpām ayonijām ।। dharmeṇaiva mahārāja śatarūpā vyajāyata ।। bhartāraṃ dīptatapasaṃ puruṣaṃ pratyapadyata ।। tasyaikasaptatiyugaṃ manvantaram ihocyate ।।
priyavratottānapādau vīrāt kāmyā vyajāyata ।। sutā sutapasā yuktā mahatī lokadhāriṇī । kāmyāputrāś ca catvāraḥ samrāṭ kukṣir virāṭ prabhuḥ ।। priyavrataṃ samāsādya patiṃ sājanayat sutān ।
uttānapādāc caturaḥ sūnṛtā suṣuve sutān ।। utpannā vāci dharmeṇa dhruvasya jananī śubhā ।। uttānapādo ajanayat sūnṛtāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। tapas tepe mahārāja prārthayan sumahad yaśaḥ ।।
acalam caiva purataḥ saptarṣīṇāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। devāsurāṇām ācāryaḥ ślokam apy uśanā jagau ।। yam adya purataḥ kṛtvā dhruvaṃ saptarṣayaḥ sthitāḥ ।। prācīnagarbhaṃ vṛkatiṃ vṛkalaṃ vṛkatejasam ।
patnī prācīnagarbhasya sūnṛtā suṣuve nṛpa । nāmnodāradhiyaṃ putram indro yaḥ pūrvajanmani ।। udāradhīḥ sutaṃ bhadrā janayad vai divaṃjayam । ripuṃ ripuṃjayaṃ jajñe varāṅgī sā divaṃjayāt ।
ripuṃ ripuṃjayaṃ vipraṃ vṛkalam vṛkatejasam ।। ajījanat puṣkariṇyāṃ vairaṇyāṃ cākṣuṣo manum ।। kanyāyāṃ bharataśreṣṭha vairājasya prajāpateḥ ।। abhimanyuś ca daśamo naḍvalāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ ।।
aṅgaṃ sumanasaṃ svātiṃ kratum āṅgirasaṃ śivam ।। apacāreṇa venasya prakopaḥ sumahān abhūt ।। venasya pāṇau mathite saṃbabhūva mahān ṛṣiḥ ।। kariṣyati mahātejā yaśaś ca prāpsyate mahat ।।
baddhagodhāṅgulitravān । prajārakṣākṛtotsāhaḥ । pṛthur vainyas tadā cemāṃ rarakṣa kṣatrapūrvajaḥ ।। tasmāc caiva samutpannau nipuṇau sūtam agadhau ।।
prajānāṃ vṛttikāmena devaiḥ sarṣigaṇaiḥ saha ।। sarpaiḥ puṇyajanaiś caiva vīrudbhiḥ parvatais tathā ।। prādād yathepsitaṃ kṣīraṃ tena prāṇān adhāryan ।। śikhaṇḍinī havirdhānam antardhānād vyājāyata ।।
prācīnabarhiṣaṃ śukram gayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vrajājinau ।। havirdhānān mahārāja yena saṃvardhitāḥ prajāḥ ।। prācīnabarher abhavan pṛthivītalacāriṇaḥ ।। mahatas tapasaḥ pāre savarṇāyāṃ mahīpatiḥ ।।
putrān vai janayām āsa sarvalokābhipūjitān । sarve pracetasa nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi samudrasalileśayāḥ ।। arakṣyamāṇām āvavrur babhūvātha prajākṣayaḥ ।।
pratyāhṛtāḥ prajāḥ sarvāś cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ । daśa varṣasahasrāṇi na śekuś ceṣṭituṃ prajāḥ ।। prācetasam upastavya tapasaḥ sarvaparvataiḥ । mukhebhyo vāyum agniṃ ca te asṛjañ jātamanyavaḥ ।।
tān agnir adahad ghora evam āsīd drumakṣayaḥ ।। upagamyābravīd etān rājā somaḥ pratāpavān ।। vṛkṣaśūnyā kṛtā pṛthvī śāmyetām agnimārutau ।। bhaviṣyaṃ jānatā tāta dhṛtā garbheṇa vai mayā ।।
bhāryā vo astu mahābhāgā somavaṃśavivardhinī ।। asyām utpatsyate vidvān dakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। agnināgnisamo bhūyaḥ prajāḥ saṃvardhayiṣyati ।। saṃhṛtya kopaṃ vṛkṣebhyaḥ patnīṃ dharmeṇa māriṣām ।।
māriṣāyāṃ tatas te vai manasā garbham ādadhuḥ । dakṣo jajñe mahātejāḥ somasyāṃśena bhārata ।। acarāṃś ca carāṃś caiva dvipado atha catuṣpadaḥ ।। tadā prajāvivṛddhyarthaṃ mahātejāḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
śiṣṭāḥ somāya rājñe tu nakṣatrākhyā dadau prabhuḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaś caiva jajñire anyāś ca jātayaḥ ।। saṃkalpād darśanāt sparśāt pūrveṣāṃ sṛṣṭir ucyate ।। saṃbhavaḥ kathitaḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।।
vāmāṅguṣṭhāt tathā caiva tasya patnī vyajāyata । kathaṃ prācetasatvaṃ sa punar lebhe mahātapāḥ ।। dauhitraś caiva somasya kathaṃ śvaśuratāṃ gataḥ ।। ṛṣayo atra na muhyanti vidyāvantaś ca ye janāḥ ।।
punaś caiva nirudhyante vidvāṃs tatra na muhyati ।। tapa eva garīyo abhūt prabhāvaś caiva kāraṇam ।। prajāvān āyur uttīrṇaḥ svargaloke mahīyate ।। divyān bhogān avāpnoti rambhādistrībhir āvṛtaḥ ।
utpattiṃ vistareṇaiva vaiśaṃpāyana kīrtaya ।। yathā sasarja bhūtāni tathā śṛṇu mahīpate ।। ṛṣīn devān sagandharvān asurān atha rākṣasān ।। yakṣabhūtapiśācāṃś ca vayaḥpaśumṛgāṃs tathā ।
apadhyātā bhagavatā mahādevena dhīmatā । tataḥ saṃcintya tu punaḥ prajāhetoḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। sutāṃ sutapasā yuktāṃ mahatīṃ lokadhāraṇīm ।। asiknyāṃ janayām āsa dakṣa eva prajāpatiḥ ।।
nāśāya vacanaṃ teṣāṃ śāpāyaivātmanas tathā ।। dakṣasya vai duhitari dakṣaśāpabhayān muniḥ ।। taṃ bhūyo janayām āsa piteva munipuṃgavam ।। nirmathya nāśitāḥ sarve vidhinā ca na saṃśayaḥ ।।
brahmarṣīn purataḥ kṛtvā yācitaḥ parameṣṭhinā ।। kanyāyāṃ nārado mahyaṃ tava putro bhaved iti ।। sa tasyāṃ nārado jajñe bhūyaḥ śāpabhayād ṛṣiḥ ।। prajāpater dvijaśreṣṭha śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ ।।
samāgatā mahāvīryā nāradas tān uvāca ha ।। pramāṇaṃ sraṣṭukāmā vai prajā prācetasātmajāḥ । antar ūrdhvam adhaś caiva kathaṃ srakṣyatha vai prajāḥ ।। vāyor anaśanaṃ prāpya gatās te vai parābhavam ।
adyāpi na nivartante samudrebhya ivāpagāḥ ।। vairaṇyām eva putrāṇāṃ sahasram asṛjat prabhuḥ ।। pūrvoktaṃ vacanaṃ tāta nāradenaiva coditāḥ ।। jñātvā pramāṇaṃ pṛthvyāś ca sukhaṃ srakṣyāmahe prajāḥ ।।
ekāgrā svasthamanaso yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ । adyāpi na nivartante samudrebhya ivāpagāḥ ।। naṣṭeṣu śabalāśveṣu dakṣa kruddho abravīd vacaḥ । nāradaṃ nāśam ehīti garbhavāsaṃ vaseti ca । prayāto naśyati vibho tan na kāryaṃ vipaśyatā ।।
tadbhītyā nāradaṃ śaptvā kanyā evāsṛjat prabhuḥ । ṣaṣṭiṃ dakṣo asṛjat kanyā vairaṇyām iti na śrutam ।। tās tadā pratijagrāha bhāryārthe kaśyapaḥ prabhuḥ । somo dharmaś ca kauravya tathaivānye maharṣayaḥ । saptaviṃśati somāya catasro ariṣṭanemaye ।।
dve bhṛśāśvāya viduṣe tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। dharmapatnyo daśa tv etās tāsv apatyāni me śṛṇu ।। marutvatyāṃ marutvanto vasos tu vasavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। lambāyāś caiva ghoṣo atha nāgavīthī ca jāmijā ।।
saṃkalpāyās tu sarvātmā jajñe saṃkalpa eva ca ।। nāgavīthyāś ca jāminyā vṛṣalambā vyajāyata । sarvā nakṣatranāmnyas tu jyotiṣe parikīrtitāḥ ।। vasavo aṣṭau samākhyātās teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vistaram ।।
pratyūṣaś ca prabhasaś ca vasavo nāmabhiḥ śrutāḥ ।। dhruvasya putro bhagavān kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।। manoharāyāḥ śiśiraḥ prāṇo atha ramaṇas tathā ।। avijñātagatiś caiva dvau putrāv anilasya tu ।।
apatyaṃ kṛttikānāṃ sa kārttikeya iti smṛtaḥ ।। skandaḥ sanatkumāraś ca sṛṣṭaḥ pādena tejasaḥ । dvau putrau devalasyāpi kṣamāvantau manīṣiṇau ।। yogasiddhā jagat kṛtsnam asaktā vicacāra ha ।।
visvakarmā mahābhāgas tasyāṃ jajñe prajāpatiḥ ।। bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kartā śilpavatāṃ varaḥ ।। mānuṣāś copajīvanti yasya śilpaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। surabhiḥ kaśyapād rudrān ekādaśa vinirmame । mahādevaprasādena tapasā bhāvitā satī ।
tvaṣṭuś caivātmajaḥ śrīmān viśvarūpo mahāyaśāḥ ।। vṛṣākapiś ca śaṃbhuś ca kapardī raivatas tathā ।। mṛgavyādhaś ca sarpaś ca kapālī ca viśāṃ pate । śataṃ caivaṃ samākhyātaṃ rudrāṇām amitaujasām ।।
purāṇe bharataśreṣṭha yair vyāptāḥ sacarācarāḥ । lokā bharataśārdūla kaśyapasya nibodha me । anyaiḥ satyavratā rājan yābhir lokatrayaṃ dhṛtam । kadrūr muniś ca lokeśa tāsv apatyāni me śṛṇu ।। khaṣā caiva trayodaśa । kaśyapasya tu bhāryā vai । tuṣitā nāma te anyonyam ūcur vaivasvate antare ।।
hitārthaṃ sarvalokānāṃ samāgamya parasparam ।। manvantare prasūyāmas tan naḥ śreyo bhaviṣyati ।। mārīcāt kaśyapāj jātās te adityā dakṣakanyayā ।। pūrvajanmani sutapaḥ pṛśnirūpe babhūvatuḥ ।
aryamā caiva dhātā ca tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathaiva ca ।। aṃśo bhagaś cātitejā ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। vaivasvate antare te vai ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। tāsām apatyāny abhavan dīptāny amitatejasām ।।
tārāgaṇāḥ samastā ye gagane ye cakāsati । pratyaṅgirasajāḥ śreṣṭhā ṛco brahmarṣisatkṛtāḥ ।। ete yugasahasrānte jāyante punar eva ha ।। teṣām api ca rājendra nirodhotpattir ucyate ।।
tathā yugāni rājendra praḷayā manavas tathā । evaṃ devanikāyās te saṃbhavanti yuge yuge ।। kaśyapasyātmajāv etau sarvebhyaḥ pūrvajau matau । siṃhikā cābhavat kanyā vipracitteḥ parigrahaḥ ।।
saiṃhikeyā iti khyātās tasyāḥ putrā mahābalāḥ । gaṇas teṣāṃ tu rājendra daśasāhasra ucyate । teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ । asaṃkhyātā mahābāho hiraṇyakaśipoḥ śṛṇu । anuhrādaś ca hrādaś ca prahrādaś caiva vīryavān ।। saṃhrādaputrau sundaś ca nisundas tāv ubhau smṛtau । saṃhrādaputra āyuṣmāñ śibir bāṣkala eva ca ।
teṣāṃ madhye mahābhāga sarvatra samadṛg vaśī । prahrādaḥ paramāṃ bhaktiṃ ya uvāca janārdane । virocanaś ca prāhrādir balir jajñe virocanāt ।। dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca sūryaś ca candramāś cendratāpanaḥ ।।
bāṇas teṣām atibalo jyeṣṭhaḥ paśupateḥ priyaḥ ।। pārśvato me vihāraḥ syād ity evaṃ yācito varaḥ ।। bāṇasya cendradamano lohityām udapadyata । gaṇas teṣāṃ tu rājendra śatasāhasrasaṃmitaḥ । mahānābhaś ca vikrāntaḥ kālanābhas tathaiva ca ।।
tapasvino mahāvīryāḥ prādhānyena nibodha tān ।। śaṅkukarṇo vivādaś ca gaveṣṭhī duṃdubhis tathā । ayomukhaḥ śambaraś ca kapilo vāmanas tathā ।। vikṣobhaṇaś ca ketuś ca ketuvīryaśatahradau ।।
mahānābhaś ca vikrāntaḥ kālanābhas tathaiva ca । ekacakro mahābāhus tārakaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। svarbhānur vṛṣaparvā ca vipracittiś ca vīryavān ।। sūkṣmaś caiva nicandraś ca ūrṇanabho mahāhiriḥ । asilomā sukeśī ca śaṭhaś ca balako madaḥ । tathā gaganamūrdhā ca kumbhanābho mahāsuraḥ । pramado mayaḥ kupatho hayagrīvaś ca vīryavān ।। vaisṛpaḥ savirūpākṣaḥ supatho atha harāharau । hiraṇyakaśipuś caiva śatamāyaś ca śambaraḥ । śarabhaḥ śalabhaś caiva vipracittiś ca vīryavān ।
vipracittipradhānās te dānavāḥ sumahābalāḥ ।। eteṣāṃ yad apatyaṃ tu tan na śakyaṃ narādhipa । prasaṃkhyātuṃ mahīpāla putrapautram anantakam । upadānavī hayaśirāḥ śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī ।। bahvapatye mahāsattve mārīces tu parigrahaḥ ।।
caturdaśaśatān anyān hiraṇyapuravāsinaḥ । mārīcir janayām āsa mahatā tapasānvitaḥ ।। pitāmahaprasādena ye hatāḥ savyasācinā ।। prabhāyā nahuṣaḥ putro jayantaś ca sacīsutaḥ । pūruṃ jajñe atha śarmiṣṭhā duḥṣantam upadānavī ।
siṃhikāyām athotpannā vipracitteḥ sutās tathā ।। siṃhikeyā iti khyātās trayodaśa mahābalāḥ ।। vātāpir namuciś caiva ilvalaḥ khasṛmas tathā ।। rāhur jyeṣṭhas tu teṣāṃ vai candrasūryapramardanaḥ ।
śaraḥ potaraṇaś caiva vajranābhaś ca vīryavān ।। mūkaś caiva tuhuṇḍaś ca hradaputrau babhūvatuḥ । mārīcaḥ sundaputraś ca tāḍakāyāṃ vyajāyata । svarbhānuś ca mahāvīryo vaktrayodhī mahāsuraḥ ।
saramāṇas tathā caiva śarakalpaś ca vīryavān ।। teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। samutpannāḥ sumahatā tapasā bhāvitātmanaḥ ।। catasraḥ koṭayas tāś ca maṇimatyāṃ nivāsinaḥ । te apy avadhyās tu devānām arjunena vipātitāḥ । anekamāyākuśalā dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ ।
kākī śyenī ca bhāsī ca sugrīvī śucigṛdhrike ।। śyenī śyenāṃs tathā bhāsī bhāsān gṛdhrāṃś ca gṛdhrikā ।। aśvān uṣṭrān gardabhāṃś ca tāmrāvaṃśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। suparṇaḥ patatāṃ śreṣṭho dāruṇaḥ svena karmaṇā ।।
anekaśirasāṃ tāta khecarāṇāṃ mahātmanām ।। suparṇavaśagā nāgā jajñire anekamastakāḥ ।। airāvato mahāpadmaḥ kambalāśvatarāv ubhau ।। mahānīlamahākarṇau dhṛtarāṣṭrabalāhakau ।।
śaṅkhaś ca śaṅkhapālaś ca kapilo vāmanas tathā ।। ete cānye ca bahavo daṃdaśūkā viṣolbaṇāḥ । teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca garuḍena nipātitāḥ । caturdaśasahasrāṇi krūrāṇām uragāśinā ।
gaṇaṃ krodhavaśaṃ viddhi tatra sarve ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ ।। anāyuṣāyāḥ putrās tu pañcāśat sumahābalāḥ । surato guṇavṛttaś ca vikṣaro atha nṛpas tathā । gās tu vai janayām āsa surabhī mahiṣī tathā ।।
khasā tu yakṣaraksāṃsi munir apsarasas tathā ।। ete kaśyapadāyādāḥ kīrtitāḥ sthāṇujaṃgamāḥ ।। eṣa manvantare tāta sargaḥ svārociṣe smṛtaḥ ।। juhvānasya brahmaṇo vai prajāsarga ihocyate ।।
putratve kalpayām āsa svayam eva pitāmahaḥ ।। ditir vinaṣṭaputrā vai toṣayām āsa kaśyapam ।। vareṇa cchandayām āsa sā ca vavre varaṃ tadā ।। sa ca tasyai varaṃ prādāt prārthitaṃ sumahātapāḥ ।।
indraṃ putro nihantā te garbhe cec charadāṃ śatam ।। bhaviṣyati sutas te ayaṃ yady enaṃ dhārayiṣyasi ।। dhārayām āsa garbhaṃ tu śuciḥ sā vasudhādhipa ।। nityaṃ triṣavaṇaṃ snātā kṛcchracāndrāyaṇe ratā ।
rocayan vai gaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ devānām amitaujasām ।। jagāma partavāyaiva tapase saṃśitavrataḥ ।। dadhāra sā ca taṃ garbhaṃ samyak sā ca samanvitā ।। garbham ātmavadhārthāya jñātvā taṃ maghavān api । gate tu kāśyape tāta varadaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ । tasyāś caivāntaraprepsur vavande caraṇau diteḥ । śuśrūṣayāmy ahaṃ devi pādau te niyatavrate । evamuktā tu sā devī śakreṇāmitatejasā । uvāca vacanaṃ devī śakraṃ śatrunibarhaṇam ।। śuśrūṣaya mahābhāga niyatātmā mahādyute । tataḥ paśyasi saṃjātaṃ bhrātaraṃdīptatejasam ।। tac chrutvā vacanaṃ devyāḥ śuśrūṣanaparāyaṇaḥ । ūne varṣaśate cāsyā dadarśāntaram acyutaḥ ।।
vajrapāṇis tato garbhaṃ saptadhā taṃ nyakṛntata ।। mā rodīr iti taṃ śakraḥ punaḥ punar abhābravīt ।। tena rodanaśabdena ditiḥ sā pratyabudhyata । uvāca śakram ārtā sā kiṃ tv etat kṛpaṇaṃ kṛtam ।।
sa bhīto niścarat tasmād yonidvārāt puraṃdaraḥ । tataḥ pārśvagato devyāḥ pādayor nipapāta ha ।। aśucir devi suptāsi pādayoḥ kṛtamūrdhajā । mayātmavadhabhītena kṛtaṃ tat kṣantum arhasi ।।
evamuktā tu sā devī āha śakram idaṃ vacaḥ । sukṛtaṃ sādhu te putra na te bhavati duṣkṛtam ।। kiṃ tu vakṣyāmy ahaṃ kiṃcit tat kuruṣvārimardana । mamaiva putras tvaṃ deva rakṣa caitān yadīcchasi ।
bāḍham ity abravīd indra evam etan na saṃśayaḥ । maruto nāma devās te babhūvur bharatarṣabha ।। mā rodīr iti yac chabdas tvayoktaḥ pākaśāsana । maruto nāma teneme bhavantu yadi manyase ।
devāsureṣu yuddheṣu bhṛtyās tava kṛte vibho । pṛṣṭhato anugamiṣyanti vaśagās te puraṃdara ।। evaṃ bruvāṇāṃ tāṃ devīṃ prāha śakras tv idaṃ vacaḥ । devā ekonapañcāśat sahāyā vajrapāṇinaḥ ।।
kramaśas tāni rājyāni pṛthoḥ pūrvaṃ tu bhārata ।। parjanyas tapano vyaktas tasya sarvam idaṃ jagat ।। prayato bhava rājendra śṛṇuṣvaikamanās tataḥ । nāśuddhe nāśucau vāpi nāśiṣyāya kathaṃcana ।।
varṇayeyam ahaṃ rājan kṛtajñāya hitāya ca । svargyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ vedena saṃmitam । marutāṃ ca śubhaṃ janma śṛṇvataḥ paṭhato api vā । nāvṛttibhayam astīha paralokabhayaṃ kutaḥ ।।
tataḥ krameṇa rājyāni vyādeṣṭum upacakrame ।। yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva somaṃ rājye abhyaṣecayat ।। bṛhaspatiṃ tu viśveṣāṃ dadāv āṅgirasaṃ patim ।। bhṛgūṇām adhipaṃ caiva kāvyaṃ rājye abhiṣecayat ।
ādityānāṃ tathā viṣṇuṃ vasūnām atha pāvakam ।। daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca prahlādam amitaujasam ।। mātṝṇāṃ ca vratānāṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ ca tathā gavām । yakṣāṇāṃ rākṣasānāṃ ca pārthivānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ tu sādhyānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam । vipracittiṃ tu rājānaṃ dānavānām athādiśat । śailānāṃ himavantaṃ ca nadīnām atha sāgaram ।। gandhānāṃ marutāṃ caiva bhūtānām aśarīriṇām । śabdākāśavatāṃ caiva vāyuṃ ca balināṃ varam । nāgānāṃ vāsukiṃ cakre sarpāṇām atha takṣakam ।।
uccaiḥśravasam aśvānāṃ garuḍaṃ caiva pakṣiṇām ।। vanaspatīnāṃ rājānaṃ plakṣam evābhyaṣecayat ।। sāgarāṇāṃ nadīnāṃ ca meghānāṃ varṣaṇasya ca । ādityānāṃ adhipatiṃ parjanyam abhiṣiktavān ।। sarveṣāṃ daṃṣṭriṇāṃ śeṣaṃ rājānam abhyaṣecayat । sarīsṛpāṇāṃ sarpāṇāṃ rājānaṃ caiva takṣakam । sarvāpsarogaṇānāṃ ca kāmadevaḥ kṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ।। ṛtūnām atha māsānāṃ divasānāṃ tathaiva ca । pakṣāṇāṃ ca kṣapāṇāṃ ca muhūrtatithiparvaṇām ।। kalākāṣṭhāpramāṇānāṃ gaterayanayos tathā । gaṇitasyātha yogasya cakre saṃvatsaraṃ prabhum । diśāṃ pālān atha tataḥ sthāpayāmāsa bhārata ।।
diśāpālaṃ sudhanvānaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। putraṃ śaṅkhapadaṃ nāma rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। ketumantaṃ mahātmānaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। udīcyāṃ diśi durdharṣaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।।
saśailavanakānanā । sasāgarā ca sasarit । yathāpradeśam adyāpi dharmeṇa paripālyate ।। vedadṛṣṭena vidhinā rājarājyena rājabhiḥ ।।
vaivasvatāya manave pṛthivīrājyam ādiśat ।। mahadd hy etad adhiṣṭhānaṃ purāṇe pariniṣṭhitam ।। puṇyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ svargavāsakaraṃ śubham । yathā mahātmanā tena dugdhā ceyaṃ vasuṃdharā ।।
yathā daityaiś ca nāgaiś ca yathā yakṣair yathā drumaiḥ ।। yathā śailaiḥ piśācaiś ca gandharvaiś ca dvijottamaiḥ । rākṣasaiś ca mahāsattvair yathā dugdhā vasuṃdharā । vatsān kṣīraviśeṣāṃś ca sarvam evānupūrvaśaḥ ।। kruddhair maharṣibhis tāta kāraṇaṃ tac ca kīrtaya ।।
ekāgraḥ prayataś caiva śuśrūṣur janamejaya ।। kīrtayeyam ahaṃ rājan kṛtaghnasyāhitasya vā ।। rahasyam ṛṣibhiḥ proktaṃ śṛṇu rājan yathātatham ।। brāhmaṇebhyo namaskṛtya na sa śocet kṛtākṛtam ।।
atrivaṃśasamutpannas tv aṅgo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। jāto mṛtyusutāyāṃ vai sunīthāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। svadharmaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā kāmāl lokeṣv avartata ।। vedadharmān atikramya so adharmanirato abhavat ।।
prāvartanna papuḥ somaṃ hutaṃ yajñeṣu devatāḥ ।। āsīt pratijñā krūreyaṃ vināśe pratyupasthite ।। mayi yajño vidhātavyo mayi hotavyam ity api ।। ūcur maharṣayaḥ sarve marīcipramukhās tadā ।।
phaladāyī sa cāsmākaṃ yajñas te adyāpi nānyathā । adharmaṃ kuru mā vena naiṣa dharmaḥ satāṃ mataḥ ।। prajāś ca pālayiṣye aham iti te samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। venaḥ prahasya durbuddhir imam artham anarthavat ।।
śrutavīryatapaḥsatyair mayā vā kaḥ samo bhuvi । prabhavaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ । saṃmūḍhā na vidur nūnaṃ bhavanto māṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। dyāṃ vai bhuvaṃ ca rundheyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
anunetuṃ tadā venaṃ tataḥ kruddhā maharṣayaḥ ।। hanyatāṃ hanyatāṃ pāpa ity ūcus te parasparam ।। yo yajñapuruṣaṃ devam anādinidhanaṃ harim । vinindaty adhamācāro na sa yogyo bhuvaḥ patiḥ ।।
ity uktvā mantrapūtais taiḥ kuśair munigaṇā nṛpam । nijaghnur nihataṃ pūrvaṃ bhagavan nindanādinā ।। tasmin hate jagat sarvaṃ dasyubhūtaṃ abhūn nṛpa । tataḥ saṃmantrya ṛṣayo mamanthus tasya bhūbhujaḥ ।
tato asya savyam ūruṃ te mamanthur jātamanyavaḥ ।। hrasvo atimātraḥ puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇaś cāpi babhūva ha ।। tam atrir vihvalaṃ dṛṣṭvā niṣīdety abravīt tadā ।। dhīvarān asṛjac cāpi venakalmaṣasaṃbhavān ।।
adharmarucayas tāta viddhi tān venakalmaṣān ।। araṇīm iva saṃrabdhā mamanthus te maharṣayaḥ ।। dīpyamānaḥ svavapuṣā sākṣād agnir iva jvalan ।। sa dhanvī kavacī jātaḥ pṛthur eva mahātapāḥ ।
śarāṃś ca divyān rakṣārthaṃ kavacaṃ ca mahāprabham ।। samāpetur mahārāja venaś ca tridivaṃ yayau ।। trātaḥ sa puruṣavyāghra punnāmno narakāt tadā ।। toyāni cābhiṣekārthaṃ sarva evopatasthire ।।
sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni jaṃgamāni ca sarvaśaḥ ।। mahatā rājarājyena prajāpālaṃ mahādyutim ।। ādhirājye tadā rājā pṛthur vainyaḥ pratāpavān ।। anurāgāt tatas tasya nāma rājety ajāyata ।।
parvatāś ca dadur mārgaṃ dhvajasaṅgaś ca nābhavat ।। sarvakāmadughā gāvaḥ puṭake puṭake madhu ।। sūtaḥ sūtyāṃ samutpannaḥ sautye ahani mahāmatiḥ ।। pṛthoḥ stavārthaṃ tau tatra samāhūtau maharṣibhiḥ ।।
karmaitad anurūpaṃ vāṃ pātraṃ cāyaṃ narādhipaḥ ।। āvāṃ devān ṛṣīṃś caiva prīṇayāvaḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।। stotraṃ yenāsya kuryāva rājñas tejasvino dvijāḥ ।। kariṣyate tu yat karma cakravartī mahābalaḥ । guṇā bhaviṣyā ye cāsya tair ayaṃ stūyatāṃ nṛpaḥ ।
tau stutiṃ cakratur yuktaṃ sūtamāgadhakau nṛpa । yāni karmāṇi kṛtavān pṛthuḥ paścān mahābalaḥ ।। satyavāgdānaśīlo ayaṃ satyasaṃdho nareśvaraḥ । śrīmāñ jaitraḥ kṣamāśīlo vikrānto duṣṭaśāsanaḥ ।। dharmajñaś ca kṛtajñaś ca dayāvān priyabhāṣakaḥ । mānyamānayitā yajvā brahmaṇyaḥ sādhuvatsalaḥ । samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca vyavahārasthito nṛpaḥ । āśīrvādāḥ prayujyante sūtamāgadhabandibhiḥ ।।
anūpadeśaṃ sūtāya magadhaṃ māgadhāya ca ।। vṛttīnām eṣa vo dātā bhaviṣyati janeśvaraḥ ।। taṃ prajāḥ pṛthivīnātham upatasthuḥ kṣudhārditāḥ । oṣadhīṣu pranaṣṭāsu tasmin kāle hy arājake ।। tam ūcus tena tāḥ pṛṣṭās tatrāgamanakāraṇam । arājake naraśreṣṭha dharitryā sakalauṣadhīḥ । grastās tataḥ kṣayaṃ yānti prajāḥ sarvāḥ prajeśvara ।। tvaṃ no vṛttiprado dhātrā prajāpālo nirūpitaḥ । dehi naḥ kṣutparītānāṃ prajānāṃ jīvanauṣahīḥ । tvaṃ no vṛttiṃ vidhatsveti maharṣivacanāt tadā ।।
dhanur gṛhya pṛṣatkāṃś ca pṛthivīm ārdayad balī ।। tāṃ pṛthur dhanur ādāya dravantīm anvadhāvata ।। pradadarśāgrato vainyaṃ pragṛhītaśarāsanam ।। mahāyogaṃ mahātmānaṃ durdharṣam amarair api ।।
kṛtāñjalipuṭā bhūtvā pūjyā lokais tribhiḥ sadā ।। kathaṃ dhārayitā cāsi prajā rājan vinā mayā ।। matkṛte na vinaśyeyuḥ prajāḥ pārthiva viddhi tat ।। prajānāṃ pṛthivīpāla śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mama ।।
tasmād vadāmy upāyaṃ te taṃ kuruṣva yadīcchasi । upāyaṃ paśya yena tvaṃ dhārayethāḥ prajā nṛpa ।। annabhūtā bhaviṣyāmi yaccha kopaṃ mahādyute ।। ātmayogabalenemā dhārayiṣyāmy ahaṃ prajāḥ ।। tataḥ praṇamya vasudhā taṃ bhūyaḥ prāha pārthivam ।
sattveṣu pṛthivīpāla na dharmaṃ tyaktum arhasi ।। cintayitvā bahuvidhaṃ prajānāṃ hitakamyayā । kopaṃ nigṛhya dharmātmā vasudhām idam abravīt ।। bahūn vai prāṇino loke bhavet tasyeha pātakam ।।
tasmin hate nāsti bhadre pātakaṃ nopapātakam ।। ekasmin yatra nidhanaṃ prāpite duṣṭakāriṇi । bahūnāṃ bhavati kṣemaṃ tatra puṇyaprado vadhaḥ । yadi me vacanaṃ nādya kariṣyasi jagaddhitam ।। ātmānaṃ prathayitvāhaṃ prajā dhārayitā svayam ।।
saṃjīvaya prajāḥ sarvāḥ samarthā hy asi dhāraṇe ।। niyaccheyaṃ tvadvadhārtham udyataṃ ghoradarśanam ।। vatsaṃ tu mama taṃ paśya kṣareyaṃ yena vatsalā ।। yathā viṣyandamānaṃ me kṣīraṃ sarvatra bhāvayet ।।
dhanuṣkoṭyā tadā vainyas tena śailā vivardhitāḥ ।। pṛthur vainyas tadā rājā mahīṃ cakre samāṃ tataḥ । manvantareṣv atīteṣu viṣam āsīd vasuṃdharā ।। svabhāvenābhavaṃs tasyā samāni viṣamāṇi ca । cākṣuṣasyāntare pūrvam āsīd evaṃ tadā kila । pravibhāgaḥ purāṇāṃ vā grāmāṇāṃ vā tadābhavat ।। naiva satyānṛtaṃ tatra na lobho na ca matsaraḥ ।
vaivasvate antare tasmin sāṃprate samupasthite । vainyāt prabhṛti rājendra sarvasyaitasya saṃbhavaḥ ।। tatra tatra prajāḥ sarvā nivāsaṃ samarocayan ।। kṛcchreṇa mahatā yukta ity evam anuśuśruma ।।
sve pāṇau puruṣavyāghra dudoha pṛthivīṃ tataḥ ।। sasyāni tena vai dugdhā vainyeneyaṃ vasuṃdharā । tenānnena prajās tāta vartante adyāpi nityaśaḥ ।। vatsaḥ somo abhavat teṣāṃ dogdhā cāṅgirasaḥ sutaḥ ।।
kṣīram āsīd anupamaṃ tapo brahma ca śāśvatam ।। kāñcanaṃ pātram ādāya dugdheyaṃ śrūyate mahī ।। kṣīram ūrjaskaraṃ caiva yena vartanti devatāḥ ।। rājataṃ pātram ādāya svadhām amitavikramaiḥ ।।
antakaś cābhavad dogdhā kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।। alābupātram ādāya viṣaṃ kṣīraṃ narottama ।। nāgānāṃ bharataśreṣṭha sarpāṇāṃ ca mahīpate ।। tadāhārās tadācārās tadvīryās tadapāśrayāḥ ।।
āyasaṃ pātram ādāya māyāḥ śatrunibarhaṇīḥ ।। ṛtvig dvimūrdhā daityānāṃ madhur dogdhā mahābalaḥ ।। vartayanty amitaprajñās tad eṣām amitaṃ balam ।। āmapātre mahārāja purāntardhānam akṣayam ।।
dogdhā rajatanābhas tu pitā maṇivarasya yaḥ । yakṣātmajo mahātejās triśīrṣaḥ sumahātapāḥ । dogdhā tu dhanadaḥ svāminn evaṃ taiś ca vasuṃdharā । tena te vartayantīha paramarṣir uvāca ha ।।
śāvaṃ kapālam ādāya prajā bhoktuṃ nararṣabha ।। vatsaḥ sumālī kauravya kṣīraṃ rudhiram eva ca ।। vartayanti piśācāś ca bhūtasaṃghās tathaiva ca ।। vatsaṃ citrarathaṃ kṛtvā śucīn gandhān narottama ।।
gandharvarājo atibalo mahātmā sūryasaṃnibhaḥ ।। oṣadhīr vai mūrtimatī ratnāni vividhāni ca ।। pātraṃ tu śailam evāsīt tena śailāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। pālāśaṃ pātram ādāya cchinnadagdhaprarohaṇam ।।
sarvakāmadughā dogdhrī pṛthivī janamejaya । sarvakāmadughā dogdhrī sarvasasyaprarohiṇī ।। madhukaiṭabhayoḥ kṛtsnā medasābhipariplutā ।। teneyaṃ medinī devī procyate brahmavādibhiḥ ।
duhitṛtvam anuprāptā devī pṛthvīti cocyate ।। sasyākaravatī sphītā purapattanamālinī ।। namasyaś caiva pūjyaś ca bhūtagrāmair na saṃśayaḥ ।। pṛthur eva namaskāryo vṛttidaḥ sa sanātanaḥ ।।
ādirājo namaskāryaḥ pṛthur vainyaḥ pratāpavān ।। ādirājo namaskāryo yodhānāṃ prathamo nṛpaḥ ।। sa ghorarūpān saṃgrāmān kṣemī tarati kīrtimān ।। pṛthur eva namaskāryo vṛttidātā mahāyaśāḥ ।।
pṛthur eva namaskāryaḥ śreyaḥ param abhīpsubhiḥ ।। pātrāṇi ca mayoktāni kiṃ bhūyo varṇayāmi te ।। ya idaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ pṛthoś caritam āditaḥ । putrapautrasamāyukto modate suciraṃ bhuvi । uktāni bharataśreṣṭha vainyasyeha mahātmanaḥ । kim anyad bharataśreṣṭha pṛcchasi tvaṃ nareśvara । yaḥ śṛṇoti sadā bhaktyā sa svargī nātra saṃśayaḥ । teṣāṃ pūrvavisṛṣṭiṃ ca vaiśaṃpāyana kīrtaya ।।
manvantarakathāṃ brahmañ chrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ ।। manvantarāṇāṃ kauravya saṃkṣepaṃ tv eva me śṛṇu ।। vaivasvataś ca kauravya sāṃprato manur ucyate ।। uttamākhyas tāmasaś cā bhūtāṃ raivatacakṣuṣau । aṣṭamo dakṣasāvarṇir dharmasāvarṇir eva ca । rudraputras tu sāvarṇir bhavitaikādaśo manuḥ ।
raivato brahmasāvarṇiḥ sūryasāvarṇir eva ca । tathaiva merusāvarṇāś catvāro manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ṛṣīṃs teṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi putrān devagaṇāṃs tathā ।। pulastyaś ca vasiṣṭhaś ca saptaite brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।।
yāmā nāma tathā devā āsan svāyaṃbhuve antare ।। jyotiṣmān dyutimān havyaḥ savanaḥ putra eva ca ।। etat te prathamaṃ rājan manvantaram udāhṛtam ।। ete maharṣayas tāta vāyuproktā mahāvratāḥ ।।
havirdhraḥ sukṛtir jyotir āpo mūrtir ayasmayaḥ ।। kīrtitāḥ pṛthivīpāla mahāvīryaparākramāḥ ।। idaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vakṣyāmi tan nibodha narādhipa ।। hiraṇyagarbhasya sutā ūrjā jātāḥ sutejasaḥ ।।
auttameyān mahārāja daśa putrān manoramān ।। bhānavas tatra devāś ca manvantaram udāhṛtam ।। kapīvān akapīvāṃś ca tatra saptarṣayo nṛpa ।। satyā devagaṇāś caiva tāmasasyāntare manoḥ ।।
putrāṃś caiva pravakṣyāmi tāmasasya manor nṛpa । taporatir akalmāṣas tanvī dhanvī paramṭapaḥ ।। vāyuproktā mahārāja caturthaṃ caitad antaram ।। satyanetras tathātreya ete saptarṣayo apare ।।
pāriplavaś ca raibhyaś ca manor antaram ucyate ।। dhṛtimān avyayo yuktas tattvadarśī nirutsukaḥ ।। raivatasya manoḥ putrāḥ pañcamaṃ caitad antaram ।। bhṛgur nabho vivasvāṃś ca sudhāmā virajās tathā ।।
cākṣuṣasyāntare tāta manor devān imāñ śṛṇu ।। lekhāś ca nāma rājendra pañca devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। uruprabhṛtayo rājan ṣaṣṭhaṃ manvantaraṃ smṛtam ।। ṣaṣṭaṃ manvantaraṃ proktaṃ saptamaṃ tu nibodha me ।
gautamo atha bharadvājo viśvāmitras tathaiva ca ।। saptamo jamadagniś ca ṛṣayaḥ sāṃprataṃ divi ।। ādityāś cāśvinau caiva devau vaivasvatau smṛtau ।। ikṣvākupramukhāś caiva daśa putrā mahātmanaḥ ।।
manoḥ samabhavad rājan dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata । rājan putrāś ca pautrāś ca dikṣu sarvāsu bhārata ।। sthitā dharmavyavasthārthaṃ lokasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca ।। kṛtvā karma divaṃ yānti brahmalokam anāmayam ।।
atītā vartamānāś ca krameṇaitena bhārata ।। manvantarāṇi sarvāṇi nibodhānāgatāni me ।। parameṣṭhisutās tāta merusāvarṇatāṃ gatāḥ ।। mahatā tapasā yuktā merupṛṣṭhe mahaujasaḥ ।।
anāgatāś ca saptaite loke asmin manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। manor antaram āsādya sāvarṇasyeha tāñ śṛṇu ।। bhāradvājas tathā drauṇir aśvatthāmā mahādyutiḥ ।। ete sapta mahātmāno bhaviṣyā munisattamāḥ ।।
devatānāṃ guṇās tatra trayaḥ proktāḥ svayaṃbhuvā । mārīcasyaiva te putrāḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ । brahmaṇaḥ sadṛśāś caite dhanyāḥ saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। abhijātyātha tapasā mantravyākaraṇais tathā । brahmalokapratiṣṭhās tu smṛtā brahmarṣayo amalāḥ ।। bhūtabhavyabhavajjñānaṃ buddhā caiva tu yaiḥ svayam । tapasā vai prasiddhā ye saṃgatā pravicintakāḥ । mantravyākaraṇādyaiś ca aiśvaryāt sarvaśaś ca ye ।। etān bhāryān dvijo jñātvā naiṣṭhikāni ca nāma ca । saptaite saptabhiś caiva guṇaiḥ saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। dīrghāyuṣo mantrakṛta īśvarā dīrghacakṣuṣaḥ । buddhyā pratyakṣadharmāṇo gotraprāvartakās tathā ।। kṛtādiṣu yugākhyeṣu sarveṣv eva punaḥ punaḥ । pravartayanti te varṇān āśramāṃś caiva sarvaśaḥ । saptarṣayo mahābhāgāḥ satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।। teṣāṃ caivānvayotpannā jāyante hi punaḥ punaḥ । mantrabrāhmaṇakartāro dharme praśithile tathā ।। yasmāc ca varadāḥ sapta parebhyaś cāparāḥ smṛtāḥ । tasmān na kālo na vayaḥ pramāṇam ṛṣibhāvane ।। eṣa saptarṣikoddeśo vyākhyātas te mayā nṛpa । sāvarṇasya manoḥ putrān bhaviṣyāñ śṛṇu sattama । saṃbandhāc ca svayaṃtejāḥ saṃbuddhāś ca yataḥ svayam । yasmāc chaṃsanti te brahma tasmād brahmarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ । sāvarṇasya manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyā daśa bhārata ।। kṣamayā nṛpa sāvarṇā bhaviṣyāñ śṛṇu bhārata । yaśaś cāpnoti sumahad āyuṣmāṃś ca bhaven naraḥ ।
caturdaśe manobhāvye uragambhīrabudhnakāḥ । putrā [vai cā]kṣuṣā devā śukrādyāś ca tapasvinaḥ । atītanāgatānāṃ vai maharṣīṇāṃ sadā naraḥ ।। devatānāṃ gaṇāḥ proktāḥ pañca vai bharatarṣabha । taraṃgabhīrur vapraś ca tarasvān ugra eva ca ।। abhimānī pravīraś ca jiṣṇuḥ saṃkrandanas tathā । tejasvī sabalaś caiva bhautyasyaite manoḥ sutāḥ ।। bhautyasyaivādhikāre tu pūrṇe kalpas tu pūryate । ity ete anāgatātītā manavaḥ kīrtitā mayā । namaskṛtvā jayet svargaṃ brāhmaṇo nātra saṃśayaḥ । kṣatriyo jayate śatrūn vaiśyaḥ śūdro yathepsitam ।
yathāpradeśam adyāpi sarvataḥ paripālyate । prajābhis tapasā caiva saṃhārānte ca nityaśaḥ ।। kṛtatretādiyuktāni manor antaram ucyate ।। prajānāṃ patayo rājan dhanyam eṣāṃ prakīrtanam ।।
na śakyam antaṃ teṣāṃ vai vaktuṃ varṣaśatair api ।। manvantareṣu saṃhāraḥ śrūyate bharatarṣabha ।। pūrṇe yugasahasre tu kalpo niḥśeṣa ucyate ।। brahmāṇam agrataḥ kṛtvā sahādityagaṇair vibho ।।
yogaṃ yogīśvaraṃ devam ajaṃ kṣetrajam acyutam । avyaktaḥ śāśvato devas tasya sarvam idaṃ jagat ।। tatra saṃvartate rātriḥ sakalaikārṇave tadā । nārāyaṇodare nidrāṃ brāhmaṃ varṣasahasrakam ।। tāvantam iti kālaṃ sā rātrir ity abhiśabditā । nidrāyogam anuprāpto yasyām ante pitāmahaḥ ।। sā ca rātrir apakrāntā sahasrayugaparyayā । tadā prabuddho bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । punaḥ sisṛkṣayā yuktaḥ sargāya vidadhe manaḥ ।। saiva smṛtiḥ purāṇeyaṃ tadvṛttaṃ tadviceṣṭitam । devasthānāni tāny eva kevalaṃ ca viparyayaḥ ।। tato dagdhāni bhūtāni sarvāṇy ādityaraśmibhiḥ । devarṣiyakṣagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ । jāyante ca punas tāta yuge bharatasattama ।। yathartāv ṛtuliṅgāni nānārūpāṇi paryaye । dṛśyante tāni tāny eva tathā brāhmīṣu rātriṣu ।। niṣkramitvā prajākāraḥ prajāpatir asaṃśayam । ye ca vai mānavā devāḥ sarve caiva maharṣayaḥ ।। te saṃgatāḥ śuddhasaṅgāḥ śaśvad dharmavisargataḥ । na bhavanti punas tāta yuge bharatasattama ।। tat sarvaṃ kramayogena kālasaṃkhyāvibhāgavit । sahasrayugasaṃkhyānaṃ kṛtvā divasam īśvaraḥ ।। rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāṃ kṛtvā ca bhagavān vibhuḥ । saṃharaty atha bhūtāni sṛjate ca punaḥ punaḥ । vyaktāvyakto mahādevo harir nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ । visargaṃ bharataśreṣṭha sāṃpratasya mahādyute ।।
nityaḥ sarvagataḥ sūkṣmaḥ śāśvataḥ puruṣottamaḥ । yatrotpanno mahātmā sa harir vṛṣṇikule prabhuḥ ।। sarvāsuravināśāya sarvalokahitāya ca । sureṇur iti vikhyātā triṣu lokeṣu bhāminī ।।
saṃjñā nāma svatapasā dīpteneha samanvitā ।। gātreṣu paridagdhaṃ vai nātikāntam ivābhavat ।। ajānan kāśyapas tasmān mārtaṇḍa iti cocyate ।। yenātitāpayāmāsa trīṃl lokān kaśyapātmajaḥ ।।
ādityo janayāmāsa kanyāṃ dvau ca prajāpatī ।। yamaś ca yamunā caiva yamajau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। māyāmayī tu sā saṃjñā tasyāś chāyā samutthitā ।। sthitāsmi tava nirdeśe śādhi māṃ varavarṇini ।।
tvayeha bhavane mahyaṃ vastavyaṃ nirviśaṅkayā ।। saṃbhāvyās te na cākhyeyam idaṃ bhagavate tvayā ।। ākhyāsyāmi mataṃ tubhyaṃ gaccha devi yathāsukham ।। tvaṣṭuḥ samīpam agamad vrīḍiteva manasvinī ।।
bhartuḥ samīpaṃ gaccheti niyuktā ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। cintām avāpa mahatīṃ strīṇāṃ dhik ceṣṭitaṃ tv iti । nininda bahudhātmānaṃ strītvaṃ cātinininda sā ।। sthātavyaṃ na kvacit strīṇāṃ dhig asvātantryajīvitam । śaiśave yauvane vārddhe pitṛbhartṛsutād bhayam ।। tyaktaṃ bhartṛgṛhaṃ maugdhyād bata durvṛttayā mayā । avijñātāpi vedhāyām atha patyur niketanam ।। tatrāsti sā savarṇā vai paripūrṇamanorathā । naṣṭaṃ bhartṛgṛhaṃ maugdhyāc chreyo atra na pitur gṛhe । kurūn athottarān gatvā tṛṇāny eva cacāra sā ।। ādityo janayāmāsa putram ātmasamaṃ tadā ।।
manur evābhavan nāmnā sāvarṇa iti cocyate ।। cakārābhyadhikaṃ snehaṃ na tathā pūrvajeṣu vai ।। padā saṃtarjayāmāsa saṃjñāṃ vaivasvato yamaḥ ।। caraṇaḥ patatām eṣa taveti bhṛśaduḥkhitā ।।
śāpo nivarted iti ca provāca pitaraṃ tadā ।। seyam asmān apāhāya yavīyāṃsaṃ bubhūṣati ।। bālyād vā yadi vā mohāt tad bhavān kṣantum arhati ।। yasmāt te pūjanīyāhaṃ tarjitāsmi tvayā suta । tasmāt tavaiṣa caraṇaḥ patiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ । apatyaṃ durapatyaṃ syān nāmbā kujananī bhavet ।
tava prasādāc caraṇo na paten mama gopate ।। yas tvaṃ dharmaparo nityaṃ dharmaṃ saṃtyaktavān imam । yena tvām āviśat krodho dharmajñaṃ satyavādinam ।। yuktam eva hi te kartuṃ tava mātṛvaco anagha ।
kṛmayo māṃsam ādāya yāsyanti tu mahītale ।। tava pādān mahāprājña tataḥ saṃprāpsyase sukham । śāpasya parihāreṇa tvaṃ ca trāto bhaviṣyasi ।। sā tat pariharantī sma nācacakṣe vivasvataḥ ।।
ātmānaṃ sa samādhāya yogāt tathyam apaśyata । mūrdhajeṣu ca jagrāha sā cātmānaṃ śaśaṃsa ha । ātmānaṃ gopayāmāsa saṃyogāt tasya naiva tu । mūrdhajeṣu ca jagrāha samaye atigate tu sā । vivasvān atha tac chrutvā kruddhas tvaṣṭāram abhyagāt ।। nirdagdhukāmaṃ roṣeṇa sāntvayāmāsa vai tadā ।।
asahantī sma tat saṃjñā vane carati śāḍvalam ।। nityaṃ tapasy abhiratāṃ vaḍavārūpadhāriṇīm । parṇāhārāṃ kṛśāṃ dīnāṃ jaṭilāṃ maladhāriṇīm । hastihastaparikliṣṭāṃ vyākulāṃ padminīm iva ।
ślāghyāṃ yogabalopetāṃ yogam āsthāya gopate ।। rūpaṃ nirvartayāmy adya tava kāntam ariṃdama ।। rūpaṃ vivasvataś cāsīt tiryagūrdhvasamaṃ tu vai । tenāsau saṃbhṛto devo rūpeṇa tu vibhāvasuḥ ।। tasmāt tvaṣṭuḥ sa vai vākyaṃ bahu mene prajāpatiḥ । samanujñātavāṃś caiva tvaṣṭāraṃ rūpasiddhaye । bhramim āropya tat tejaḥ śātayāmāsa bhārata ।।
kṛtavān aṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ na vyaśātayad avyayam ।। yat sūryād vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaḥ śātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā । tvaṣṭaiva tejasā tena viṣṇoś cakram akalpayat ।। triśūlaṃ caiva śarvasya śibikāṃ dhanadasya ca । śaktiṃ guhasya devānām anyeṣāṃ ca varāyudham ।। tat sarvaṃ tejasā tena viśvakarmā hy akalpayat । kāntāt kāntataraṃ draṣṭum adhikaṃ śuśubhe tadā ।। mukhe nirvartitaṃ rūpaṃ tasya devasya gopateḥ । tataḥprabhṛti devasya mukham āsīt tu lohitam ।। mukharāgaṃ tu yat pūrvaṃ mārtaṇḍasya mukhacyutam । ādityā dvādaśaiveha saṃbhūtā mukhasaṃbhavāḥ ।। dhātāryamā ca mitraś ca varuṇo aṃśo bhagas tathā । indro vivasvān pūṣā ca parjanyo daśamas tathā । tatas tvaṣṭā tato viṣṇur ajaghanyo jaghanyajaḥ ।। harṣaṃ lebhe tato devo dṛṣṭvādityān svadehajān । gandhaiḥ puṣpair alaṃkārair bhāsvatā mukuṭena ca ।। evaṃ saṃpūjayāmāsa tvaṣṭā vākyam uvāca ha ।। gaccha deveśa svāṃ bhāryāṃ kurūṃś carati cottarān । vaḍavārūpam āsthāya vane carati śāḍvale ।। tāṃ tathārūpam āsthāya svāṃ bhāryāṃ śubhalīlayā । adhṛṣyāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tejasā niyamena ca ।।
vaḍavāvapuṣā rājaṃś carantīm akutobhayām । maithunāya viveṣṭantīṃ parapuṃso viśaṅkayā ।। devau tasyām ajāyetām aśvinau bhiṣajāṃ varau ।। mārtaṇḍasyātmajāv etāv aṣṭamasya prajāpateḥ ।।
saṃjñāyāṃ janayāmāsa vaḍavāyāṃ sa bhārata । sā tu dṛṣṭvaiva bhartāraṃ tutoṣa janamejaya ।। dharmeṇa rañjayāmāsa dharmarāja imāḥ prajāḥ ।। pitṝṇām ādhipatyaṃ ca lokapālatvam eva ca ।।
bhāvyaḥ so anāgate tasmin manuḥ sāvarṇike antare ।। bhrātā śanaiścaraś cāsya grahatvaṃ sa tu labdhavān ।। nāsatyau yau samākhyātau svarvaidyau tu babhūvatuḥ । revanto api tathā rājann aśvānāṃ śāntido abhavat । tad apratihataṃ yuddhe dānavāntacikīrṣayā ।।
abhavat sā saricchreṣṭhā yamunā lokabhāvanī ।। dvitīyo yaḥ sutas tasya sa vijñeyaḥ śanaiścaraḥ ।। grahatvaṃ sa tu lebhe vai sarvalokānupūjitam । āpadaṃ prāpya mucyeta prāpnuyāc ca mahad yaśaḥ ।।
ikṣvākuś caiva nābhāgaś ca dhṛṣṇuḥ śaryātir eva ca ।। karūṣaś ca pṛṣadhraś ca navaite puruṣarṣabha ।। anutpanneṣu navasu putreṣv eteṣu bhārata ।। mitrāvaruṇayor aṃśe manur āhutim ājuhot ।।
āhutyāṃ hūyamānāyāṃ devagandharvamānuṣāḥ । tuṣṭiṃ tu paramāṃ jagmur munayaś ca tapodhanāḥ । aho asya tapaso vīryam aho śrutam aho dhanam । divyasaṃhananā caiva iḍā jajña iti śrutiḥ ।। anugacchasva māṃ bhadre tam iḍā pratyuvāca ha ।। dharmayuktamidaṃ vākyaṃ putrakāmaṃ prajāpatim ।
tayoḥ sakāśaṃ yāsyāmi na māṃ dharmo hato ahanat ।। aṃśe asmi yuvayor jātā devau kiṃ karavāṇi vām ।। manunā cāham uktā vai anugacchasvamām iti । mitraś ca varuṇaś cobhāv ūcatur yan nibodha tat ।।
satyena caiva suśroṇi prītau svo varavarṇini ।। manor vaṃśakaraḥ putras tvam eva ca bhaviṣyasi ।। jagatpriyo dharmaśīlo manor vaṃśavivardhanaḥ ।। budhenāntaram āsādya maithunāyopavartitā ।।
janayitvā tataḥ sā tam iḍā sudyumnatāṃ gatā ।। utkalaś ca gayaś caiva vinatāśvaś ca bhārata ।। dik pūrvā bharataśreṣṭha gayasya tu gayā smṛtā ।। daśadhā tadgataṃ kṣatram akarot pṛthivīm imām ।।
yūpāṅkitā vasumatī yasyeyaṃ savanākarā । kanyābhāvāc ca sudyumno nainaṃ guṇam avāptavān ।। pratiṣṭhā dharmarājasya sudyumnasya kurūdvaha ।। cakravartī mahārāja babhūva janamejaya ।
sudyumnaḥ kārayām āsa pratiṣṭhāne nṛpakriyām । dhṛṣṇukaś cāmbarīṣaś ca daṇḍaś cetīha te trayaḥ । yaś cakāra mahātmā vai daṇḍakāraṇyam uttamam ।। vanaṃ tal lokavikhyātaṃ tāpasānām anuttamam ।
tatra praviṣṭamātras tu naraḥ pāpāt pramucyate ।। sudyumnaś ca divaṃ yāta eḍam utpādya bhārata । utkalasya trayaḥ putrās triṣu lokeṣu viśrutāḥ । mānaveyo mahārāja strīpuṃsor lakṣaṇair yutaḥ ।।
dhṛtavāṃs tam iḍety evaṃ sudyumnaś cetiviśrutaḥ । pṛṣadhro hivaddhitvā tu guror gāṃ janamejaya । śāpāc chūdratvam āpannaḥ putras tasya mahātmanaḥ । ambarīṣo abhavat putraḥ pārthivarṣabhasattama ।। karūṣasya tu kārūṣāḥ kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥ । sahasraṃ kṣatriyagaṇo vikrāntaḥ saṃbabhūva ha ।।
nābhāgāriṣṭaputrāś ca kṣatriyā vaiśyatāṃ gatāḥ ।। prāṃśor eko abhavat putraḥ prajāpatir iti śrutaḥ । nariṣyantasya dāyādo rājā daṇḍadharo damaḥ । putraḥ kanyā sukanyā ca yā patnī cyavanasya ha ।।
ānartaviṣayaś cāsīt purī cāsīt kuśasthalī ।। jyeṣṭhaḥ putraśatasyāsīd rājyaṃ prāpya kuśasthalīm ।। tasya putraśataṃ tv āsīt kanyā cāpikurūdvaha । muhūrtabhūtaṃ devasya martyaṃ bahuyugaṃ prabho ।।
bhojavṛṣṇyandhakair guptāṃ vāsudevapurogamaiḥ ।। kanyāṃ tāṃ baladevāya suvratāṃ nāma revatīm ।। rohiṇyā sahitaś candro yathā śacyā śacīpatiḥ । reme rāmo api dharmātmā revatyā sahitaḥ sukhī ।।
na jarā revatīṃ prāptā raivataṃ ca kakudminam ।। sthitā pṛthivyām adyāpi śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ ।। ṛtucakraṃ prabhavati brahmaloke sadānaghā ।। hatā puṇyajanais tāta rākṣasaiḥ sā kuśasthalī ।।
tad vadhyamānaṃ rakṣobhir diśaḥ prākramad acyutā ।। vidrutasyaca rājendra tasya bhrātṛśatasya vai । teṣāṃ tu te bhayākrāntaḥ kṣatriyās tatra tatra ha । teṣāṃ ye te mahārāja śāryātā iti viśrutāḥ ।। sarvaśaḥ sarvagahanaṃ praviṣṭāḥ kurunandana ।।
teṣu tatra kṛpāṃ cakre brahmā lokapitā mahaḥ । karūṣasya tu kārūṣāḥ kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥ ।। prāṃśor eko abhavat putraḥ prajāpatiriti śrutaḥ । śāpāc chūdratvam āpanno navaite parikīrtitāḥ ।।
vaivasvatasya tanayā manor vaibharatarṣabha । tasya putraśataṃ tv āsīd ikṣvākor bhūridakṣiṇam ।। prāptaḥ paramadharmajña so ayodhyādhipatiḥ prabhuḥ ।। uttarāpathadeśasya rakṣitāro viśāṃ pate ।।
vasātipramukhāś cānye rakṣitāro viśāṃ pate ।। ikṣvākus tu vikukṣiṃ vai aṣṭakāyām athādiśat । māṃsam ānaya śrāddhārthaṃ mṛgān hatvā mahābala । bhakṣayitvā śaśaṃ tāta śaśādo mṛgayāṃ gataḥ ।। śaśādanāc chaśādo abhūc chaśādo vanamāviśat ।
ikṣvākau saṃsthite tāta śaśādaḥ puram āvasat ।। prāptaḥ paramadharmātmā yo ayodhyādhipatikriyām । indrasya vṛṣabhūtasya kakutstho ajayatāsurān । pūrvam āḍībake yuddhe kakutsthas tena sa smṛtaḥ ।
anenās tu kakutsthasya pṛthur ānenasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ārdrasya yuvanāśvas tu śrāvastas tasya cātmajas ।। śrāvastasya tu dāyādo bṛhadaśvo mahīpatiḥ ।। yaḥ sa dhundhuvadhād rājā dhundhumāratvam āgataḥ ।।
yadarthaṃ kuvalāśvaḥ san dhundhumāratvam āgataḥ ।। sarve vidyāsu niṣṇātā balavanto durāsadāḥ । babhūvātha pitā rājye kuvalāśvaṃ nyayojayat ।। yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ ।kuvalāśvaṃ sutaṃ rājye ।
tam uttaṅko atha viprarṣiḥ prayāntaṃ pratyavārayat ।। nirudvignas tapaś cartuṃ na hi śaknomi pārthiva ।। tvayā hi pṛthivī rājan rakṣyamāṇāmahātmanā । bhaviṣyati nirudvignā nāraṇyaṃ gantum arhasi ।। pālane hi mahān dharmaḥ prajānām iha dṛśyate । na tathā dṛśyate araṇye mā te bhūd buddhir īdṛśī ।। īdṛśo na hi rājendra dharmaḥ kva cana dṛśyate । prajānāṃ pālane yo vai purā rājarṣibhiḥ kṛtaḥ । rakṣitavyāḥ prajā rājñā tās tvaṃ rakṣitum arhasi । samudro vālukāpūrṇa ujjānaka iti smṛtaḥ ।।
antarbhūmigatas tatra vālukāntarhito mahān ।। śete lokavināśāya tapa āsthāya dāruṇam ।। yadā tadā mahī tāta calati sma sakānanā ।। ādityapatham āvṛtya saptāhaṃ bhūmikampanam ।।
tena tāta na śaknomi tasmin sthātuṃ sva āśrame ।। lokāḥ svasthā bhavantv adya tasmin vinihate tvayā ।। yas taṃ mahāsuraṃraudraṃ haniṣyati mahābalam । sa ca vikhyātakīrtis tu cakravartī nasaṃśayaḥ ।
tejasā svena te viṣṇus teja āpyāyayiṣyati ।। vīryaṃ hi sumahat tasya devair api durāsadam ।। kuvalāśvaṃ sutaṃ prādāt tasmai dhundhunibarhaṇe ।। bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha dhundhumāro na saṃśayaḥ ।।
jagāma parvatāyaiva tapase saṃśitavrataḥ ।। prāyād uttaṅkasahito dhundhos tasya nibarhaṇe ।। uttaṅkasya niyogād vai lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। eṣa śrīmān nṛpasuto dhundhumāro bhaviṣyati ।।
devadundubhayaś caiva praṇedur bharatarṣabha ।। samudraṃ khānayām āsa vālukārṇavam avyayam ।। babhūva sa mahātejā bhūyo balasamanvitaḥ ।। dhundhur āsādito rājan diśam āvṛtya paścimām ।।
somasya bharataśreṣṭha dhārormikalilo mahān ।। ekaviṃśati putrāṇāṃ sahasram amitaujasām । tasya putraśataṃ dagdhaṃ tribhir ūnaṃ tu rakṣasā ।। āsasāda mahātejā dhundhuṃ dhundhuvināśanaḥ ।।
yogī yogena vahniṃ ca śamayām āsa vāriṇā ।। uttaṅkaṃ darśayām āsa kṛtakarmā narādhipaḥ ।। dadataś cākṣayaṃ vittaṃ śatrubhiś cāparājayam ।। putrāṇāṃ cākṣayāṃl lokān svarge ye rakṣasā hatāḥ ।।
daṇḍāśvakapilāśvau tu kumārau tu kanīyasau ।। haryaśvasya nikumbho abhūt kṣatradharmarataḥ sadā ।। akṛśāśvaḥ kṛśāśvaś ca saṃhatāśvasutau nṛpa ।। vikhyātā triṣu lokeṣu putraś cāpi prasenajit ।।
abhiśaptā tu sā bhartrā nadī sā bāhudā kṛtā ।। yuvanāśvasya tanayaś cakravartī jajāna ha । kaṃ dhārayati kumāro ayaṃ nyasto rorūyate bhṛśam । māndhātar vatsa mā rodīr itīndro deśinīm adāt ।
māndhātā yuvanāśvasya trilokavijayī nṛpaḥ ।। pativratā ca jyeṣṭhā ca bhrātṝṇām ayutasya sā ।। purukutsaṃ ca dharmajñaṃ mucukundaṃ ca pārthivam ।। narmadāyām athotpannaḥ saṃbhūtas tasya cātmajaḥ ।।
sudhanvanaḥ sutaś cāpi viṣṇuvṛddhir iti smṛtaḥ । viṣṇuvṛddhā iti khyātās tasya vaṃśyā narādhipāḥ । ete tv aṅgirasaḥ pakṣe kṣetropetā dvijātayaḥ ।। saṃbhūtasyāparaḥ putro anaraṇyo mahāyaśāḥ ।
rāvaṇena hato yo asau trilokajayinā purā ।। trasadaśvo naras tasya haryaśvas tasya cātmajaḥ । haryaśvasya dṛṣadvatyāṃ jajñe sumanasaḥ sutaḥ ।। tasya putro abhavad rājā sudhanvā ripumardanaḥ ।
sudhanvanaḥ sutaś cāpi tridhanvā nāma pārthivaḥ ।। tasya satyavrato nāma kumāro abhūn mahābalaḥ ।। yena bhāryā hṛtā pūrvaṃ kṛtodvāhā parasya vai ।। jahāra kanyāṃ kāmāt sa kasya cit puravāsinaḥ ।।
ekasmin divase rāja putro atyantaparākramī । dadarśa vicaran svīye pattane cārulocanām । udvāhayantīṃ vedikāyāṃ vaiśyavaryasya kasya cit ।। anullaṅghitamaryādāṃ saptapadyā vicakṣaṇaḥ । bhartrā pānigrahayutāṃ balād gṛhya mahīpatiḥ । gāndharveṇa vivāhena svayaṃ udvāhayad balāt ।। vaiśyāḥ sarve samāgamya rājānam idam ūcatuḥ । kumāreṇa hṛtā kanyā vedikāyā mahadbalāt । rājñā na rakṣito lokas tadā naṣṭo bhaved dhruvam ।। na pūrvais taiḥ kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ na kariṣyati cāpadi । yathā kumāreṇa kṛtaṃ rājan karma vigarhitam । tam adharmeṇa saṃyuktaṃ pitāsūryāruṇo jahau । apadhvaṃseti bahuśo vadan krodhasamanvitaḥ ।। nāhaṃ putreṇa putrārthī tvayādya kulapāṃsana ।।
na ca taṃ vārayām āsa vasiṣṭho bhagavān ṛṣiḥ ।। pitrā tyakto avasad vīraḥ pitāpy asya vanaṃ yayau ।। acirān narapater vasiṣṭhasyāvicārataḥ । parityāgāt kumārasya nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।।
yadā dvādaśa varṣāṇi tena naṣṭābhavat prajā । svāhākāraḥ svadhākāro vaṣaṭkāro api nābhavat । rāṣṭre tasya mahīpasya dharmanāśo abhavat tadā । samā dvādaśa rājendra tenādharmeṇa vai tadā ।।
saṃnyasya sāgarānūpe cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।। etasminn eva samaye viśvāmitrasya vai sutāḥ । catvāro vedavidvāṃsaḥ kṣudhayā paripīḍitāḥ ।। viśvāmitre gate dūraṃ tapase atimahātmani । procuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve mātaraṃ prati bhārata ।। vikrīya tanayaṃ mātar jīvyatāṃ yadi rocate । mariṣyāmo anyathā sarve kṣudhayā paripīḍitāḥ । vikrīya tanayaṃ jīva yāvadāgamanaṃ pituḥ ।। sarvanāśe samutpanne ardhaṃ tyajati mānavaḥ । ardhena kurute kāryam iti paurātanī śrutiḥ ।। tyajed ekaṃ kulasyārthaṃ grāmasyārthaṃ kulaṃ tyajet । grāmaṃ janapadasyārthaṃ ātmārthaṃ sakalaṃ tyajet ।। tasmād vikrīya tanayān mātar jīva yathāsukham । anyathā nidhanaṃ sarve gamiṣyāmas tvayā saha ।। ayodhyāyāṃ mahātmāno dhyānavanto mahattarāḥ । gṛhvanti manujāḥ sarve dāsārthaṃ samupāgatān ।। tasmād vikrīya māṃ mātaḥ pūrvaṃ bhakṣaya pūrvajam । paścād vikrīya tāṃ sarvān no ced varṣati vāsavaḥ । śeṣasya bharaṇārthāya vyakrīṇād gośatena vai ।। maharṣiputraṃ dharmātmā mokṣayām āsa bhārata ।।
viśvāmitrasya tuṣṭyartham anukampārtham eva ca ।। mahāvrataṃ tadā roṣaṃ vasiṣṭho manasākarot । maharṣiḥ kauśikas tāta tena vīreṇa mokṣitaḥ ।। viśvāmitrakalatraṃ tad babhāra vinaye sthitaḥ ।।
viśvāmitrāśramābhyāśe māṃsaṃ tad avabandhata ।। pitur niyogād avasat tasmin vanagate nṛpe ।। yājyopādhyāyasaṃyogād vasiṣṭhaḥ paryarakṣata ।। vasiṣṭhe abhyadhikaṃ manyuṃ dhārayām āsa nityadā ।।
na vārayām āsa munir vasiṣṭhaḥ kāraṇena hi ।। na ca satyavratas tasmād dhṛtavān saptame pade ।। satyavratas tadā roṣaṃ vasiṣṭhe manasākarot ।। na ca satyavratas tasya tam upāṃśum abudhyata ।।
tena dvādaśa varṣāṇi nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। tenārthaṃ caiva vihitā dikṣās tātahatā bhuvi । kulasya niṣkṛtis tāta kṛtā sā vai bhaved iti ।। abhiṣekṣyāmy ahaṃ putram asyety evaṃ matir muneḥ ।।
upāṃśuvratam āsthāya mahat satyavratonṛpa । sarvakāmaduhāṃ dogdhrīṃ dadarśa sa nṛpātmajaḥ ।। daśadharmagato rājā jaghāna janamejaya ।। mattaḥ pramatta unmattaḥ śrāntaḥ kruddho bubhukṣitaḥ । tvaramāṇaś ca bhītaś ca lubdhaḥ kāmī ca te daśa ।
bhojayām āsa tac chrutvā vasiṣṭho apy asya cukrudhe ।। kruddhas tu bhagavānvākyam idam āha nṛpātmajan । yadi te dvāv imau śaṅkū na syātāṃ vai kṛtau punaḥ ।। aprokṣitopayogāc ca trividhas te vyatikramaḥ ।।
triśaṅkur iti hovāca triśaṅkus tena sa smṛtaḥ ।। chandyamāno vareṇātha guruṃ vavre nṛpātmajaḥ ।। saśarīro vraje svargam ity evaṃ yācito muniḥ । taṃ munir yājayām āsa pitriye rājye abhiṣicya tu ।
miṣatāṃ devatānāṃ ca vasiṣṭhasya ca kauśikaḥ ।। saśarīraṃ tadā taṃ tu divamāropayat prabhuḥ । divam āropayāmāsa saśarīraṃ mahātapāḥ । kumāraṃ janayām āsa hariścandram akalmaṣam ।। āhartā rājasūyasya sa samrāḍ iti viśrutaḥ ।।
yenedaṃ rohitapuraṃ kāritaṃrājyasiddhaye ।। kṛtvā rājyaṃ sa rājarṣiḥ pālayitvā tathā prajāḥ । saṃsārāsāratāṃ jñātvā dvijebhyas tat puraṃ dadau । harito rohitasyātha cañcur hārīta ucyate ।
vijayaś ca sudevaś ca cañcuputrau babhūvatuḥ । jetā kṣatrasya sarvasya vijayas tena sa smṛtaḥ ।। rurukas tanayas tasya rājadharmārthakovidaḥ । harito jajñivāṃs tataḥ tathaiva loke dharmātmā ।
rohitasya vṛkaḥ putro vṛkād bāhus tu jajñivān ।। śakair yavanakāmbojaiḥ pāradaiḥ pahlavaiḥ saha । nātyarthaṃ dhārmikaś tāta sa hi dharmayuge abhavat ।। aurvasyāśramam āsādya bhārgaveṇābhirakṣitaḥ ।।
jigāya pṛthivīṃ hatvā tālajaṅghān sahehayān ।। kṣatriyāṇāṃ kuruśreṣṭhāḥ pāradānāṃ ca dharmavit ।। kimarthaṃ ca śakādīnāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahaujasām ।। etan me sarvam ācakṣva vistareṇa tapodhana ।।
hehayais tālajaṅghaiś ca śakaiḥ sārdhaṃ viśāṃ pate ।। kātisarpā māhiṣikāḥ pāradāṣṭaṅkaṇāḥ śakāḥ । ete hy api gaṇāḥ pañca hehayārthe parākraman ।। patnyā cānugato duḥkhī vane prāṇān avāsṛjat ।।
vṛddhaṃ taṃ pañcatāṃ prāptaṃ tatpatny anumariṣyatī । aurveṇa jānatātmānaṃ prajāvantaṃ nivāritā । sapatnyā ca garas tasyā dattaḥ pūrvam abhūt kila ।। aurvas tāṃ bhārgavas tāta kāruṇyāt samavārayat ।। vyajāyata mahābāhuṃ sagaraṃ nāma pārthivam ।।
āgneyaṃ taṃ mahābhāgām amarair api duḥsaham ।। ājahāra ca lokeṣu kīrtiṃ kīrtimatāṃ varaḥ ।। pahlavāṃś caiva niḥśeṣān kartuṃ vyavasito nṛpaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā praṇipetur manīṣiṇam ।।
sagaraṃ vārayām āsa teṣāṃ dattvābhayaṃ tadā ।। dharmaṃ jaghāna teṣāṃ vai veṣānyātvaṃ cakāra ha ।। yavanānāṃ śiraḥ sarvaṃ kāmbojānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārāḥ kṛtās tena mahātmanā ।।
kolisarpā māhiṣakā darvāś colāḥ sakeralāḥ ।। vasiṣṭhavacanād rājan sagareṇa mahātmanā ।। khaśās tu ṣārāś cīnāś ca madrāḥ kiṣkandhakās tathā । kauntalāś ca tathā vaṅgāḥ śālvāḥ kauṅkaṇakās tathā । aśvaṃ vicārayām āsa vājimedhāya dīkṣitaḥ ।।
tasyotsṛṣṭaṃ paśuṃ yajñe jahārāśvaṃpuraṃdaraḥ । hṛtvā kapilapārśve taṃ baddhvāgān nagarīṃ punaḥ ।। sumatyās tanayā dṛptāḥ pitur ādeśakāriṇaḥ । tāni ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi hayarakṣaṇatatparāḥ ।
sa taṃ deśaṃ tadā putraiḥ khānayām āsa pārthivaḥ ।। viṣṇuṃ kapilarūpeṇa svapantaṃ puruṣaṃ tadā ।। hayam anveṣamāṇās te samantān nyakhanan mahīm । prāgudīcyāṃ diśi hayaṃ dadṛśuḥ kapilāntike ।। eṣa vājiharaś cora āste mīlitalocanaḥ । hanyatāṃ hanyatāṃ pāpa iti ṣaṣṭisahasriṇaḥ । muṣṭiprahārair ahanann unmimeṣa tadā muniḥ । sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sādhyaṃnārāyaṇaṃ tathā ।। tasya gatvā samīpe tu so ayaṃ cora iti bruvan । gṛhyatāṃ badhyatām eṣa no aśvahartā sudurmatiḥ ।। tatas te pāśam udyamya grahituṃ taṃ mahādyutim । upākrāmaṃs tadā sarve sagarāḥ kālacoditāḥ । dadṛśuḥ sāgarāḥ sarve sāyudhās taṃpradudruvuḥ । dagdhāḥ sarve mahārāja catvāras tv avaśeṣitāḥ ।।
śūraḥ pañcajanaś caiva tasya vaṃśakarā nṛpā ।। aṃśumantaṃ tadājñāpya pātram aśvārtham acyutam । pratīkṣamāṇas tatraiva dīkṣitaḥ saṃvyatiṣṭhata ।। pitṝṇāṃ padavīṃ gatvā sa dadarśa hariṃ prabhum । mūrdhnā praṇamya taṃ devaṃ prahvībhāvena cāsthitaḥ । tataḥ sa bhagavān devo dattvā cāśvaṃvaraṃ dadau । sagarāya mahārāja ।
putraṃ samudraṃ ca vibhuḥ svarge vāsaṃ tathākṣayam ।। putrāṇāṃ cākṣayāṃl lokāṃs tasya yecakṣuṣā hatāḥ । sāgaratvaṃ ca lebhe sa karmaṇā tena tasya ha ।। putrāṇāṃ ca sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭis tasyeti naḥ śrutam ।।
vikrāntāḥ ṣaṣṭisāhasrā vidhinā kena vā dvija ।। jyeṣṭhāvidarbhaduhitā keśinī nāma viśrutā । kanīyasī tu yā tasya patnī paramadharmiṇī । ariṣṭanemiduhitā rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi ।
aurvas tābhyāṃ varaṃ prādāt tan nibodha narādhipa ।। ekaṃ vaṃśadharaṃ tv ekā yatheṣṭaṃ varayatv iti ।। ekaṃ vaṃśadharaṃ tv ekā tathety āha tato muniḥ ।। keśiny asūta sagarād asamañjasamātmajam ।
itarā suṣuve tumbaṃ bījapūrṇām iti śrutiḥ ।। saṃbabhūvur yathākālaṃ vavṛdhuś ca yathāsukham ।। dhātrīś caikaikaśaḥ prādāt tāvatīḥ poṣaṇe nṛpa ।। kumārās te yathākālaṃ sagaraprītivardhanāḥ ।।
śukrād alābūmadhyād vai jātāni pṛthivīpateḥ ।। ekaḥ pañcajano nāma putro rājā babhūva ha ।। asamañja iti prāhus tasya putro'ṃśumān abhūt । dilīpas tasya tanayaḥ khaṭvāṅga iti viśrutaḥ ।।
trayo abhisaṃdhitā lokā buddhyā satyena cānagha ।। kīrtimān sa mahābhāgaḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ । samudram ānayac caināṃ duhitṛtve tv akalpayat ।। tasmād bhāgīrathī gaṅgā kathyate vaṃśacintakaiḥ ।
nābhāgas tu śrutasyāsīt putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।। ayutājit tu dāyādaḥ sindhudvīpasya vīryavān ।। divyākṣahṛdayajño vai rājā nalasakho balī ।। sudāsas tasya tanayo rājā indrasakho abhavat ।
sudāsasya sutas tv āsīt saudāso nāma pārthivaḥ । khyātaḥ kalmāṣapādo vai nāmnā mitrasaho abhavat ।। vasiṣṭhas tumahātejāḥ kṣetre kalmāṣapādake । aśmakaṃ janayām āsa ikṣvākukulavṛddhaye । aśmakāc caiva kārūṣo mūlakastatsuto abhavat । mūlakasyāpi dharmātmā rājā śataratho abhavat ।। tasmāc chatarathāj jajñe rājā elabilo balī । āsīd ailabilaḥ śrīmān vṛddhaśarmā pratāpavān ।। dalas tasyātmajaś cāpi tato jajñe śalo nṛpaḥ । ūrṇo nāma sa dharmātmā śalaputro babhūva ha । putro viśvasahas tasya pitṛkanyā vyajāyata । rajo nāma sutas tasya śṛṅkhalas tasya cātmajaḥ । anaraṇyas tu putro abhūd viśrutaḥ sarvakarmaṇaḥ ।।
anamitro raghuś caiva pārthivarṣabhasattamau ।। anamitrasutaḥ stambaḥ śaṅkhaṇas tasya cātmajaḥ । dīrghabāhur dilīpasya raghur nāmnābhavat sutaḥ ।। ayodhyāyāṃmahārāja raghur āsīn mahābalaḥ ।
rāmo daśarathāj jajñe dharmārāmo mahāyaśāḥ ।। atithis tu kuśāj jajñe niṣadhas tasya cātmajaḥ ।। nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīkas tu kṣemadhanvā tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। devānīkasya dāyādo ahīnagas tu pratāpavān ।
ahīnagos tu dāyādaḥ sahasvān nāma pārthivaḥ ।। sudhanvanaḥ sutaś caiva tatojajñe nalo nṛpa । uktho nāma sa dharmātmā nalaputro babhūva ha । vajranābhaḥ sutas tasya ukthasya ca mahātmanaḥ । pāriyātro mahāyaśāḥ nalas tasyātmajaś caiva । śaṅkhas tasya suto vidvān dhyuṣitāśva iti śrutaḥ । dhyuṣitāśvasuto vidvān rājā viśvasahaḥ kila ।। hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo brahmiṣṭhas tasya cātmajaḥ । puṣpas tasya suto vidvān arthasiddhis tu tatsutaḥ ।। sudarśanaḥ sutas tasya agnivarṇaḥ sudarśanāt । agnivarṇasya śīghras tu śīghrasya tu maruḥ sutaḥ ।। marus tu yogam āsthāya kalāpadvīpam āsthitaḥ । tasyāsīd viśrutavataḥ putro rājā bṛhadbalaḥ । prasusruto marusutaḥ susaṃdhis tasya cātmajaḥ । susaṃdhes tu suto marṣaḥ sahasrān nāma nāmataḥ । āsīt sahasrataḥ putro rājā viśrutavān iti । vīrasenātmajaś caiva yaś cekṣvākukulodvahaḥ ।। ete vivasvato vaṃśe rājāno bhūritejasaḥ ।।
prajānān eti sāyujyam ādityasya vivasvataḥ ।। vipāpmā virajāścaiva āyuṣmāṃś ca bhavaty uta । pitṝṇām ādisargaṃ ca ka ete pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ ।। iti devavidaḥ prāhur etad icchāmi vedituṃ ।।
yathā ca kṛtam asmābhiḥ śrāddhaṃ prīṇāti vai pitṝn ।। etad vai śrotum icchāmi pitṝṇāṃ sargam uttamam ।। mārkaṇḍeyena kathitaṃ bhīṣmāya paripṛcchate ।। evam eva purā praśnaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi ।।
gītaṃ sanatkumāreṇa mārkaṇḍeyāya pṛcchate ।। bhīṣmas tu dharmarājāya proktavān etad acyuta । etad ākhyātam icchāmi kiṃ kurvāṇo na śocati ।। tatparaḥ prayataḥ śrāddhī pretya ceha ca modate ।।
puṣṭikāmasya puṣṭiṃ ca prayacchanti yudhiṣṭhira ।। prāṇināṃ niyataṃ hy uktam karmajaṃ phalam ucyate ।। pituḥ pitāmahaṃ caiva triṣu piṇḍeśu nityadā ।। ke vā te pitaro nye sma kān yajāmo vayaṃ punaḥ ।।
ke ca lokā na jānīmo vayaṃ punar upasthitāḥ । etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ vistareṇa mahādyute ।। yathā dattaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vai tāraṇāyeha kalpate ।। ye ca te pitaro nye sma yān yajāmo vayaṃ punaḥ ।
pitrā mama purā gītaṃ lokāntaragatena vai ।। taṃ pitā mama hastena bhittvā bhūmim ayācata ।। raktāṅgulitalenātha yathā dṛṣṭaḥ purā mayā ।। kuśeṣv eva tadā piṇḍaṃ dattavān avicārayan ।।
uvāca bharataśreṣṭha prīyamāṇo mayānagha ।। satputreṇa tvayā putra dharmajñena vipaścitā ।। yathā caturthaṃ dharmasya rakṣitā labhate phalam । pāpasya hi tathā mūḍhaḥ phalaṃ prāpnoty arakṣitā । vyavasthānaṃ ca dharmeṣu kartuṃ lokasya cānagha ।।
prajās tad anuvartante pramāṇācaritaṃ sadā ।। kṛtāḥ pramāṇaṃ prītiś ca mama nirvartitātulā ।। dadāni tvaṃ pratīcchasva triṣu lokeṣu durlabham ।। tvatto bhyanujñāṃ saṃprāpya mṛtyuḥ prabhavitā tava ।।
tad brūhi bharataśreṣṭha yat te manasi vartate ।। abruvaṃ kṛtakṛtyo haṃ prasanne tvayi sattama ।। praśnam icchāmy ahaṃ kiṃcid vyāhṛtaṃ bhavatā svayam ।। chettāsmi saṃśayaṃ tāta yan māṃ pṛcchasi bhārata ।।
gataṃ sukṛtināṃ lokaṃ jātakautūhalas tadā ।। te vātha pitaro nye vā kān yajāmo vayaṃ punaḥ ।। lokāntaragatāṃs tāta kiṃ nu śrāddhasya vai phalam ।। kān yajanti sma lokā vai sadevanaradānavāḥ । sayakṣoragagandharvāḥ sakiṃnaramahoragāḥ ।
tad brūhi mama dharmajña sarvajño hy asi me mataḥ ।। etac chrutvā vacas tasya bhīṣmasyovāca vai pitā । pitaraś ca yathodbhūtāḥ śṛṇu sarvaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। sayakṣarakṣogandharvāḥ sakiṃnaramahoragāḥ ।।
jagat sadevagandharvam iti brahmānuśāsanam ।। te te śreyo vidhāsyanti sarvakāmaphalapradāḥ ।। asmān āpyāyayiṣyanti svargasthān api bhārata ।। eṣa vai pitṛbhaktaś ca viditātmā ca bhārgavaḥ ।।
enaṃ pṛccha mahābhāgam ity uktvāntaradhīyata ।। praśnaṃ tam evānvapṛcchaṃ yan me pṛṣṭaḥ purā pitā ।। bhīṣma vakṣyāmi tattvena śṛṇuṣva prayato nagha ।। pitṛbhaktyaiva labdhaṃ ca prāgloke paramaṃ yaśaḥ ।।
adhiruhya giriṃ meruṃ tapo tapyaṃ suduścaram ।। vimānaṃ mahad āyāntam uttareṇa gires tadā ।। aṅguṣṭhamātraṃ puruṣam agnāv agnim ivāhitam ।। saṃniviṣṭaṃ vimānasthaṃ pādyārghyābhyāṃ apūjayam ।।
daivataṃ hy asi devānām iti me vartate matiḥ ।। na te tapaḥ sucaritaṃ yena māṃ nāvabudhyase ।। rūpeṇa na mayā kaścid dṛṣṭapūrvaḥ pumān kvacit ।। sa mām uvāca tejasvī vācā madhurayā punaḥ । kautūhalaparijñāne yat tad brahman dadāmi te ।
tapovīryāt samutpannaṃ nārāyaṇaguṇātmakam ।। so smi bhārgava bhadraṃ te kaṃ kāmaṃ karavāṇi te ।। bhrātaraḥ sapta durdharṣā yeṣāṃ vaṃśāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। marīcir atrir bhagavān pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ । aṅgirāś ca vasiṣṭhaś ca saptaite brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।
marīcis tu tathā vidvān devagandharvasevitāḥ । trīṃl lokāṇ dhārayantīmān devadānavapūjitāḥ ।। prajādharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca vartayāmo mahāmune ।। tasmāt sanatkumāreti nāmaitan me pratiṣṭhitam ।।
eṣa dṛṣṭo si bhavatā kaṃ kāmaṃ karavāṇi te ।। anujñāto bhagavatā prīyatā tena bhārata ।। ciccheda saṃśayaṃ bhīṣma sa tu deveśvaro mama ।। rame tvayāhaṃ viprarṣe śṛṇu sarvaṃ yathātatham ।।
tam utsṛjya tadātmānam ayajaṃs te phalārthinaḥ ।। na sma kiṃcit prajānanti tato loko vyamuhyata ।। anugrahāya lokānāṃ tatas tān abravīt prabhuḥ ।। putrāṃś ca paripṛcchadhvaṃ tato jñānam avāpsyatha ।।
tebhyas te prayatātmānaḥ śaśaṃsur tanayās tadā ।। śaṃsanti kuśalā nityaṃ cakṣuṣmanto hi tattvataḥ ।। gamyatāṃ putrakāś ceti putrair uktāś ca te tadā ।। pitāmaham upāgacchan saṃśayacchedanāya vai ।।
tasmād yad uktā yūyaṃ tais tat tathā na tad anyathā ।। te tu jñānapradātāraḥ pitaro vo na saṃśayaḥ ।। devāś ca pitaraś caiva tad budhyadhvaṃ divaukasaḥ ।। brahmaṇā chinnasaṃdehāḥ prītimantaḥ parasparam ।।
yad uktaṃ caiva yuṣmābhis tat tathā na tad anyathā ।। tasmād bhavantaḥ pitaro bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। rākṣasā dānavā nāgāḥ phalaṃ prāpsyanti tasya tat ।। āpyāyyamānaṃ yuṣmābhir vardhayiṣyanti nityadā ।।
samudraparvatavanaṃ jaṃgamājaṃgamair vṛtam ।। tebhyaḥ puṣṭiṃ prajāś caiva dāsyanti pitaraḥ sadā ।। bhāvayiṣyanti satataṃ śrāddhadānena pūjitāḥ ।। evam ājñā kṛtā pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।
putrāś ca pitaraś caiva vayaṃ sarve parasparam ।। anyonyapitaro hy ete devāś ca pitaraś ca ha ।। sanatkumāreṇa punaḥ pṛṣṭavān devam avyayam ।। nibodha tan me gāṅgeya nikhilaṃ sarvam āditaḥ ।।
vartanti devapravarā devānāṃ somavardhanāḥ ।। catvāro mūrtimanto vai traya eṣāṃ amūrtayaḥ ।। prabhāvaṃ ca mahattvaṃ ca vistareṇa tapodhana ।। teṣāṃ nāmāni lokāṃś ca kīrtayiṣyāmi tac chṛṇu ।।
amūrtayaḥ pitṛgaṇās te vai putrāḥ prajāpateḥ ।। yajanti tān devagaṇā vidhidṛṣṭena karmanā ।। manojavāḥ svadhābhakṣāḥ sarvakāmasamanvitāḥ । ete yogaṃ parityajya mahātmano bhavanty uta । punar yugasahasrānte jāyante brahmavādinaḥ ।।
yānti yogagatiṃ siddhāḥ punar āvṛttidurlabhām ।। āpyāyayanti ye pūrvaṃ somaṃ yogabalena vai ।। eṣa vai prathamaḥ kalpaḥ somapānāṃ anuttamaḥ ।। patnī himavataḥ śreṣṭhā yasyā maināka ucyate ।।
parvatapravaraḥ śubhro nānāratnasamācitaḥ ।। aparṇām ekaparṇāṃ ca tṛtīyām ekapāṭalām ।। lokān saṃtāpayām āsus tās tisraḥ sthāṇujaṃgamān ।। nyagrodham ekaparṇā tu pāṭalaṃ caikapāṭalā । āśrite dve aparṇā tu aniketā tapo acarat । daśavarṣasahasrāṇi duścaraṃ devadānavaiḥ ।
pāṭalāpuṣpam ekaṃ ca vidadhe caikapāṭalā ।। pūrṇe pūrṇasahasre tu āhāraṃ dve pracakratuḥ । u mā iti niṣedhantī mātṛsnehena duḥkhitā ।। umety evābhavat khyātā triṣu lokeṣu sundarī ।।
tathaiva nāmnā teneha viśrutā yogadharmiṇī । etat tu trikumārīkaṃ jagat sthāsyati bhārgava । etāsāṃ tapasā dagdhaṃ yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati । sarvās tā vai mahābhāgāḥ sarvāś ca sthirayauvanāḥ । tā lokamātaraś caiva brahmacāriṇya eva ca । sarvāś ca brahmavādinyaḥ sarvāś caivordhvaretasaḥ ।।
mahāyogabalopetā mahādevam upasthitā ।। dattakaś cośanās tasyāḥ putras tu bhṛgunandanaḥ । patnī dattā mahābrahman yogācāryāya dhīmate ।। puṣṭis tāsāṃ kumārīṇāṃ tṛtīyā caikapāṭalā । putraṃ śataśalākasya jaigīṣavyam upasthitā । tasyāpi śaṅkhalikhitau smṛtau putrāv ayonijau ।
ete cāpi mahābhāge yogācāryāv upasthite ।। agniṣvāttā iti khyātāḥ sarva evāmitaujasaḥ ।। agniṣvāttāḥ śrutās tatra pitaro ye pariśrutāḥ । acchodaṃ nāma tad divyaṃ saro yasyāḥ samutthitam ।।
tayā na dṛṣṭapūrvās te pitaras tu kadācana । apyamūrtān atha pitṝn sā dadarśa śucismitā । saṃbhūtā mānasī teṣāṃ pitṝn svān nābhijānatī । vrīḍitā tena duḥkhena babhūva varavarṇinī । nāmnā vasum iti khyātam āyoḥ putraṃ yaśasvinam ।। adrikāpsarasāyuktaṃ vimāne adhiṣṭhitaṃ divi । pitaraṃ prārthayitvānyaṃ yogabhraṣṭā papāta ha ।।
trasareṇupramāṇāni sāpaśyat teṣu tān pitṝn ।। apaśyat patamānā sā vimānatrayam antikāt । trasareṇupramāṇāṃs tāṃs tatrāpaśyat svakān pitṝn । trāyadhvaṃ ity uvācārtā patantī tān avākśirāḥ ।। tataḥ prasādayām āsa svān pitṝn dīnayā girā ।।
bhraṣṭaiśvaryā svadoṣeṇa patasi tvaṃ śucismite ।। tair eva tatkarmaphalaṃ prāpnuvantīha devatāḥ ।। manuṣyas tv anyadehena śubhāśubham iti sthitiḥ । yāni karmāṇi devatve tāni santy eva mānuṣe ।
tasmāt tvaṃ tapasaḥ putri pretyeha prāpsyase phalam ।। dhyātvā prasādaṃ te cakrus tasyāḥ sarve anukampayā ।। utpannasya pṛthivyāṃ tu mānuṣeṣu mahātmanaḥ । kanyaiva bhūtvā lokān svān punaḥ prāpsyasi durlabhān ।।
matsyayonau samutpannā sutā rājño bhaviṣyasi । sa vedam ekaṃ brahmarṣiś caturdhā vibhajiṣyati ।। vicitravīryaṃ dharmajñaṃ tathā citrāṅgadaṃ prabhum ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ vicitravīryaṃ ca citrāṅgadam ataḥ param ।
prāpyaitat sumahābhāge kutsitena svakarmaṇā । vyatikramāt pitṝṇāṃ ca janma prāpsyasi kutsitam ।। aṣṭāviṃśe bhavitrī tvaṃ dvāpare matsyayonijā ।। matsyayonau anupamā rājñas tasya vasoḥ sutā ।।
adrikā matsyabhūtā sā gaṅgāyamunasaṃgame । tasyāṃ jajñe tu sā kanyā rājño vīreṇa caiva hi । yatra barhiṣado nāma pitaro divi viṣrutāḥ ।। nāgāḥ sarpāḥ suparṇāś ca bhāvayanty amitaujasaḥ ।। mahātmāno mahābhāgās tejoyuktās tapasvinaḥ ।।
traya ete gaṇāḥ proktā dharmamūrtidharāḥ śubhāḥ । bhavitrī dvāparaṃ prāpya yugaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varā ।। vyāsād araṇyāṃ saṃbhūto vidhūmo agnir iva jvalan ।। kanyāṃ putrāṃś ca caturo yogācāryān mahābalān ।।
putrāṃś ca caturo yogā cāryā vedeṣu kovidāḥ । kanyāṃ kīrtimatīṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ yogamātāṃ ca yoginīm । kṛtvīṃ kanyāṃ kīrtimatīṃ yogāṃ yogasya mātaram । brahmadattasya jananī mahiṣī tv aṇuhasya yā ।।
śrutvā sa janakād dharmān vyāsād amitabuddhimān । mahāyogī tadā gantā punar āvartinīṃ gatim ।। ādityakiraṇopetam apunar mārgam āsthitaḥ । ādityaraśmibhiḥ pīto hy apunar vāram eṣyati । yat tat padam anudvignam avyayaṃ brahma śāśvatam । kathā yatra samutpannā vṛṣṇyandhakakulānvayā ।।
samutpannāḥ svadhāyāṃ tu kāvyād agneḥ kaveḥ sutāḥ ।। sarvakāmasamṛddheṣu dvijās tān bhāvayanty uta ।। tavaiva vaṃśe yā dattā śukasya mahiṣī dvija ।। marīcigarbhān sā lokān samāvṛtya vyavasthitā ।।
upahūtāḥ smṛtās te vai pitaro bhāsvarā divi । tān kṣatriyagaṇās tāta bhāvayanti phalārthinaḥ ।। rājarṣer jananī tāta dilīpasya mahātmanaḥ ।। tadā devayuge tāta vājimedhe mahāmakhe ।।
satyavantaṃ mahātmānaṃ te api svargajito narāḥ ।। yajamāno dilīpas tu tadā dṛṣṭo manīṣibhiḥ । yasyāśvamedhāvabhṛthe saha tena divaṃ gatāḥ । samutpannasya pulahān mahātmāno dvijarṣabhāḥ ।। tāṃs tu vaiśyagaṇās tāta bhāvayanti phalārthinaḥ ।।
yayāter jananī brahman mahiṣī nahuṣasya ca ।। tapasā vā prayatnena dṛśyante māṃ svacakṣuṣā । ity ete pitaro devā devāś ca pitaraḥ punaḥ । utpannā ye svadhāyāṃ tu somapā vai kaveḥ sutāḥ ।। mānasā nāma te lokā yatra vartanti te divi ।।
purukutsasya yā patnī trasaddasyor janany api ।। jananī trasadasyoś ca purukutsaparigrahaḥ । purukutsasya sā bhāryā trasaddasyuś ca tatsutaḥ । pravartayati śrāddhāni naṣṭe dharme prajāpatiḥ ।। tasmād enaṃ svadharmeṇa śrāddhadevaṃ vadanti vai ।।
dattaṃ svadhāṃ purodhāya śrāddhe prīṇāti vai pitṝn ।। udagāyanam apy agnāv agnyabhāve apsu vā punaḥ ।। ajeṣu tāmravarṇeṣu goṣu vā kapilāsu ca । śṛṅgāmbhaḥpariṣiktāsu snuṣāsu ramaṇīṣu ca । aprajāsu savatsāsu dātavyāḥ śucipiṇḍakāḥ । svargam ārogyam evātha yad anyad api cepsitam ।।
pitaraḥ puṣṭikāmasya prajākāmasya vā punaḥ । puṣṭiṃ prajāṃ ca svargaṃ ca prayacchanti pitāmahāḥ । āyur dhanaṃ sukhaṃ caiva svargam ārogyam eva ca । dadyuḥ pitāmahāḥ prītyā yad anyad vāpi cepsitam । devatānāṃ hi pitaraḥ pūrvam āpyāyanaṃ smṛtam ।। sthiraprasādāś ca sadā tān namasyasva bhārgava ।। śreyas te adya vidhāsyāmi pratyakṣaṃ kuru tat svayam ।।
gatim etām apramatto mārkaṇḍeya niśāmaya ।। tvadvidhenāpi siddhena dṛśyate māṃsacakṣuṣā ।। jagāma gatim iṣṭāṃ vai dvitīyo agnir iva jvalan ।। prasādāt tasya devasya durjñeyaṃ bhuvi mānuṣaiḥ ।।
yogadharmam anuprāpya bhraṣṭā duścaritena vai ।। mahatas tamasaḥ pāre mānasasya visaṃjñitāḥ ।। aprāpya yogaṃ te sarve saṃyuktāḥ kāladharmaṇā ।। jātāḥ kauśikadāyādāḥ kurukṣetre nararṣabha ।।
tatas te punar ājātiṃ bhraṣṭāḥ prāpsyanti kutsitāṃ ।। smṛtir utpatsyate prāpya tāṃ tāṃ jātiṃ jugupsitām ।। brāhmaṇyaṃ pratilapsyanti tato bhūyaḥ svakarmaṇā ।। bhūyaḥ siddhim anuprāptāḥ sthānaṃ prāpsyanti śāśvatam ।।
yogadharme ca nirataḥ prāpsyase siddhim uttamām ।। yogo hi durlabho nityam alpaprajñaiḥ kadācana । labdhvāpi nāśayanty enaṃ vyasanaiḥ kaṭutāmitāḥ ।। adharmeṣv eva vartante ardayante guruṃ sadā । yācante na tv ayācyāni rakṣanti śaraṇāgatān । nāvamanyanti kṛpaṇān mādyante na dhanoṣmaṇā । yuktāhāravihārāś ca yuktaceṣṭāḥ svakarmasu । dhyānādhyayanayuktāś ca na naṣṭānugaveṣiṇaḥ ।। nopabhogaratā nityaṃ na māṃsamadhubhakṣaṇāḥ । na kāmaparamā nityaṃ na viprasevinas tathā ।। nānāryasaṃkathāsaktā nālasyopahatās tathā । nātyantamānasaṃsaktā goṣṭhīṣu niratās tathā । prāpnuvanti narā yogaṃ yogo vai durlabho bhuvi ।। praśāntāś ca jitakrodhā mānāhaṃkāravarjitāḥ । kalyāṇabhājanaṃ ye tu te bhavanti yatavratāḥ ।। evaṃvidhās tu te tāta brāhmaṇā hy abhavaṃs tadā । smaranti hy ātmano doṣaṃ pramādakṛtam eva tu । dhyānādhyayanayuktāś ca śānte vartmani saṃsthitāḥ । śāntiṃ te paramām āśu labhante nātra saṃśayaḥ । tasmāt tvam api dharmajña yogadharmaparo bhava । variṣṭhaṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ taṃ samācara bhārgava ।। ity uktvā bhagavān devas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
upāsataś ca deveśaṃ varṣāṇy aṣṭādaśaiva me ।। paścāc chiṣyasakāśāt tu kālaḥ saṃvidito mama ।। cakṣur divyaṃ savijñānaṃ prādur āsīn mamānagha ।। āpageya kurukṣetre yān uvāca vibhur mama ।।
pitṛvartīti vikhyāto nāmnā śīlena karmaṇā ।। aṇuhāt pārthivaśreṣṭhāt kāmpilye nagarottame ।। yathovāca mahābhāgo mārkaṇḍeyo mahātapāḥ । tasya vaṃśam ahaṃ rājan kīrtayiṣyāmi tac chṛṇu । rājā dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho yasya putro mahāyaśāḥ ।।
kathaṃ ca saptamas teṣāṃ saṃbabhūva narādhipaḥ ।। kanyāṃ pradadyād yogātmā kṛtvīṃ kīrtimatīṃ prabhuḥ ।। brahmadattasya caritaṃ tad bhavān vaktum arhati ।। mārkaṇḍeyena kathitās tad bhavān prabravītu me ।।
pitāmahasya me rājan babhūveti mayā śrutam ।। rutajñaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। kaṇḍarīkaś ca yogātmā tasyaiva sacivo abhavat ।। yathovāca mahātejā mārkaṇḍeyo mahātapāḥ ।।
brahmadattasya paurāṇaṃ pauravasya mahātmanaḥ ।। bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ suhotro nāma dhārmikaḥ । suhotrasyāpi dāyādo hastī nāma babhūva ha । tenedaṃ nirmitaṃ pūrvaṃ puraṃ vai hastināpuram ।। hastinaś cāpi dāyādās trayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ । ajamīḍho dvimīḍhaś ca puramīḍhas tathaiva ca । ajamīḍhasya dhūminyāṃ jajñe bṛhadiṣur nṛpa । āsīd bṛhadiṣoḥ putro bṛhaddharmeti viśrutaḥ । bṛhaddharmeti vikhyāto rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।।
putro viśvajitaś cāpi senajit pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। vatsaś cāvantako rājā yasyaite pari vatsakāḥ ।। pṛthuṣeṇasya pāras tu pārān nīpo atha jajñivān ।। pārasya tanayaḥ śrīmān nīpo nāma mahāyaśāḥ ।
nīpā iti samākhyātā rājānaḥ sarva eva te ।। kāmpilye samaro nāma sa ceṣṭasamaro abhavat ।। putrāḥ paramadharmajñāḥ pāraputraḥ pṛthur babhau ।। jajñe sarvaguṇopeto vibhrājas tasya cātmajaḥ ।।
babhau śukasya jāmātā kṛtvībhartā mahāyaśāḥ ।। yogātmā tasya tanayo viṣvaksenaḥ paraṃtapaḥ ।। brahmadattasya tanayo viṣvaksena iti śrutaḥ ।। cakṣuṣī tasya nirbhinne pakṣiṇyā pūjanīyayā । suciroṣitayā rājan brahmadattasya veśmani । athāsya putras tv aparo brahmadattasya jajñivān । viṣvaksena iti khyāto mahābalaparākramaḥ ।
bhallāṭaś ca kumāro abhūd rādheyena hataḥ purā ।। bhallāṭaputro durbuddhir abhavaj janamejayaḥ ।। ugrāyudhena yasyārthe sarve nīpā vināśitāḥ ।। darpānvito darparuciḥ satataṃ cānaye rataḥ ।।
kimarthaṃ caiva bhavatā nihatas tad bravīhi me ।। dhṛtimāṃs tasya putras tu tasya satyadhṛtiḥ sutaḥ ।। dṛḍhanemisutaś cāpi sudharmā nāma pārthivaḥ ।। sārvabhauma iti khyātaḥ pṛthivyāṃ ekarāṭ tadā ।।
mahataś cāpi putras tu nāmnā rukmarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। putro rukmarathasyāpi supārśvo nāma pārthivaḥ । supārśvatanayaś cāpi sumatir nāma dhārmikaḥ । jajñe saṃnatimān rājā saṃnatir nāma vīryavān ।।
śiṣyo hiraṇyanābhasya kausalyasya mahātmanaḥ । caturviṃśatidhā tena proktās tāḥ sāmasaṃhitāḥ । smṛtās te prācyasāmānaḥ kārtā nāmnā tu sāmagāḥ ।। kārtir ugrāyudhaḥ so atha vīraḥ pauravanandanaḥ ।
nīpo nāma mahārāja pāñcālādhipatir hataḥ ।। ugrāyudhasya dāyādaḥ kṣemyo nāma mahāyaśāḥ ।। kṣemyāt suvīro nṛpatiḥ suvīrāt tu nṛpaṃjayaḥ । nṛpaṃjayād bahuratha ity ete pauravāḥ smṛtāḥ । pradīptacakro balavān nīpāntakaraṇo abhavat ।। ugrāyudhas tu durbuddhiḥ straiṇo duṣṭaḥ sadābhavat । rājakanyāṃ jahārātha munipatnīpradharṣakaḥ ।
pitary uparate mahyaṃ śrāvayām āsa kilbiṣam ।। ugrāyudhasya rājendra dūto abhyetya vayo abravīt ।। strīratnaṃ mama bhāryārthe prayaccha kurupuṃgava ।। tvayā rājye ca te sthitim ।
caturaṅgayutāny adya । pradāsyāmi yathākāmam ahaṃ vai ratnabhāg bhuvi ।। śāsane mama tiṣṭhasva na hi te śāntir anyathā ।। dūtāntaritam etad vai vākyam agniśikhopamam ।।
śarīraṃ me adahat tasya vākyaṃ caitad durātmanaḥ । ājñaptavān vai saṃgrāme senādhyakṣāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। śatravo vidravanty ājau darśanād eva bhārata ।। dṛṣṭvā krodhaparītātmā yuddhāyaiva mano dadhe ।।
ṛtvigbhir devakalpaiś ca suhṛdbhir narapuṃgava ।। kāraṇaṃ śrāvitaś cāsmi yuktarūpaṃ tadānagha ।। na caiṣa prathamaḥ kalpo yuddhaṃ nāma kadācana ।। prayokṣyāmas tataḥ śuddho daivatāny abhivādya ca ।।
brāhmaṇair abhyanujñātaḥ prayāsyasi jayāya vai ।। āśauce vartamānena vṛddhānām iti śāsanam ।। taṃ haniṣyasi vikramya śambaraṃ maghavān iva ।। śrotavyam iti tac chrutvā nivṛtto asmi narādhipa ।।
tasmin kāle kuruśreṣṭha karma cārabdham uttamam ।। anunīyamāno durbuddhir anunetuṃ na śakyate ।। paradārābhilāṣeṇa sadyas tāta nivartitam ।। na hīdṛśam anāyuṣyaṃ loke kiṃcana vidyate । yādṛśaṃ puruṣasyeha paradāropasevanam ।
hataṃ svakarmaṇā tat tu pūrvaṃ sadbhiś ca ninditam ।। kṛtasvastyayano vipraiḥ prāyodhayam ahaṃ ripum ।। tryaham unmattavad yuddhaṃ devāsuram ivābhavat ।। papātābhimukhaḥ śūras tyaktvā prāṇān ariṃdama ।।
hate nīpeśvare caiva hate cogrāyudhe nṛpe ।। drupadasya pitā rājan mamaivānumate tadā ।। tato abhūd drupado rājā droṇas tena nirākṛtaḥ । ahicchatraṃ sakāmpilyaṃ droṇāyāthāpavarjitam ।।
kāmpilyaṃ drupadāyaiva prāyacchad viditaṃ tava ।। vaṃśaḥ kārtsnyena vai prokto vīrasyogrāyudhasya ca ।। gītaṃ sanatkumāreṇa mārkaṇḍeyāya pṛcchate ।। tannibodha mahārāja saptajātiṣu bhārata ।।
brahmadattatṛtīyānāṃ yogināṃ brahmacāriṇām ।। śrāddhe pratiṣṭhito lokaḥ śrāddhād yogaḥ pravartate । brahmadattena yat prāptaṃ saptajātiṣu bhārata ।। pīḍayāpy atha dharmasya kṛte śrāddhe purānagha ।।
yat prāptaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ pūrvaṃ tan nibodha narottama । sanatkumāranirdiṣṭān apaśyaṃ sapta vai dvijān ।। divyena cakṣuṣā tena yān uvāca purā vibhuḥ । khasṛmaḥ pitṛvartī ca nāmabhiḥ karmabhis tathā ।।
pitary uparate sarve vratavantas tadābhavan ।। samānavatsāṃ kapilāṃ sarve nyāyāgatāṃ tadā ।। krūrā buddhiḥ samabhavat tāṃ gāṃ vai hiṃsituṃ tadā ।। na cāśakyanta te tābhyāṃ tadā vārayituṃ dvijāḥ ।।
sa sarvān abravīd bhrātṝn kopād dharmasamanvitaḥ ।। prakurvīmahi gāṃ samyak sarva eva samāhitāḥ ।। pitṝn abhyarcya dharmeṇa nādharmo asmin bhaviṣyati ।। pitṛbhyaḥ kalpayitvainām upayujyanta bhārata ।।
ārjavāt sa tu vatsaṃ taṃ pratijagrāha vai dvijaḥ ।। kālena samayujyanta sarva evāyuṣaḥ kṣaye ।। lubdhakasyātmajās tāta balavanto manasvinaḥ ।। smṛtiḥ pratyavamarśaś ca teṣāṃ jātyantare abhavat ।।
svadharmaniratāḥ sarve lobhānṛtavivarjitāḥ ।। śeṣaṃ dharmaparāḥ kālam anudhyānti svakarma tat ।। vaidhaso mātṛvartī ca vyādhāḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। mātā ca pūjitā vṛddhā pitā ca paritoṣitaḥ ।।
tadā dhanūṃṣi te tyaktvā vane prāṇān avāsṛjan ।। trāsodvegena saṃvignā ramye kālaṃjare girau ।। paṇḍito ghasmaro nādī nāmabhis te abhavan mṛgāḥ ।। āsan vanecarāḥ kṣāntā nirdvandvā niṣparigrahāḥ ।।
maruṃ sādhya jahuḥ prāṇāṃl laghvāhārās tapasvinaḥ ।। tathaivādyāpi dṛśyante girau kālañjare acyuta ।। śubhāc chubhatarāṃ yoniṃ cakravākatvam āgatāḥ ।। tyaktvā sahacarīdharmaṃ munayo dharmacāriṇaḥ ।।
niḥspṛho nirmamaḥ kṣānto nirdvaṃdvo niṣparigrahaḥ । nirvṛttir nibhṛtaś caiva śakunā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। te brahmacāriṇaḥ sarve śakunā dharmacāriṇaḥ । nirāhārā jahuḥ prāṇāṃs tapoyuktāḥ sarittaṭe ।। atha te sodarā jātā haṃsā mānasacāriṇaḥ । jātismarāḥ susaṃbaddhāḥ saptaiva brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। viprayonau yato mohān mithyopacarito guruḥ । tiryagyonau tato jātāḥ saṃsāre paribabhramuḥ ।। yadā tu pitṛkāryārthaḥ kṛtaḥ svārthe vyavasthitaiḥ । tato jñānaṃ ca jātiṃ ca te hi prāpur guṇottaram । sunetraś ca svatantraś ca śakunā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhas tu kaṇḍarīko abhūd brahmadattas tu saptamaḥ ।। yogasya cābhinirvṛttyā pratibhānāc ca śobhanāt ।।
tathaiva tatsthitaṃ brahma saṃsāreṣv api vartatām ।। yogadharmam anudhyānto viharanti sma tatra ha ।। mānasaṃ tu saraḥ prāpya haṃsā bhūtvā jalaukasaḥ । nīpānām īśvaro rājā vibhrājaḥ pauravānvayaḥ ।।
śrīmān antaḥpuravṛto vanaṃ tat praviveśa ha ।। dṛṣṭvāyāntaṃ śriyopetaṃ bhaveyam aham īdṛśaḥ ।। khinno hy asmy upavāsena tapasā niṣphalena ca ।। nṛpatvam aham icchāmi yadi me sukṛtaṃ bhavet ।
āvāṃ te sacivau syāvas tava priyahitaiṣiṇau ।। evaṃ te samayaṃ cakruḥ suvāktaṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। avaraṃ varaṃ prārthayase tasmād vākyaṃ nibodha me ।। bhaviṣyataḥ sakhāyau ca dvāv imau sacivau tava ।।
tāṃs trīn abhīpsato rājyaṃ vyabhicārapradharṣitān ।। tān ayācanta caturas trayas te sahacāriṇaḥ ।। sarveṣām eva vacanāt prasādānugataṃ tadā ।। itaś cyutāś ca mānuṣyaṃ prāpya yogam avāpsyatha ।।
pitṛprasādo hy asmābhir asya prāptaḥ kṛtena vai ।। asmākaṃ jñānasaṃyogaḥ sarveṣāṃ yogasādhanaḥ ।। puruṣāntaritaṃ śrutvā tato yogam avāpsyatha ।। padmagarbho aravindākṣaḥ kṣīragarbhaḥ sulocanaḥ ।
ūrubinduḥ subinduś ca haimagarbhas tu saptamaḥ । haṃsā jātā mahātmāno mānaseṣu saraḥsu ca ।। sumanāḥ suvāk suśuddhaś ca tattvadarṣī ca tattvavit । sunetraś ca suhotraś ca dvijā nāmabhir eva ca ।।
te brahmacāriṇaḥ sarve vihagāḥ kāmacāriṇaḥ । vāyvambubhakṣāḥ satataṃ śarīrāṇy upaśoṣayan ।। cacārāntaḥpuravṛto nandanaṃ maghavān iva ।। nirvedāc ca tam evārtham anudhyātvā puraṃ yayau ।।
aṇudharmaratir nityam aṇuho adhyagamat padam ।। sattvaśīlaguṇopetāṃ yogadharmaratāṃ sadā ।। sanatkumāreṇa tadā saṃnidhau mama śobhanā ।। yathā te kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ pitṛsargeṣu vai mayā ।।
prāyāt saras tapaś cartuṃ yatra te sahacāriṇaḥ ।। tyaktvā kāmāṃs tapas tepe sarasas tasya pārṣvataḥ ।। putratvaṃ prāpya yogena yujyeyam iti bhārata ।। mahātapāḥ sa vibhrājo virarājāṃśumān iva ।।
saras tac ca kuruśreṣṭha vaibhrājam iti śabditam ।। yogabhraṣṭās trayaś caiva dehanyāsakṛto abhavan ।। smṛtimanto atra catvāras trayas tu parimohitāḥ ।। yathāsyāsīt pakṣibhāve saṃkalpaḥ pūrvacintitaḥ ।।
jñānadhyānatapaḥpūtā vedavedāṅgapāragāḥ । jātau śrotriyadāyādau vedavedāṅgapāragau ।। pāñcālaḥ pañcamas tatra kaṇḍarīkas tathāparaḥ ।। dvivedaḥ kaṇḍarīkas tu chandogo adhvaryur eva ca ।।
pāñcālakaṇḍarīkābhyāṃ tasya saṃvid abhūt tadā ।। pūrvajātikṛtenāsan dharmakāmārthakovidāḥ ।। abhiṣicya tadā rājye parāṃ gatim avāptavān ।। asitasya yogadurdharṣā saṃnatir nāma bhārata ।।
saṃnatiṃ saṃnatimatīṃ devalād yogadharmiṇīm ।। upayeme vidhānena brahmadatto narādhipaḥ । te jātāḥ śrotriyakule sudaridre sahodarāḥ ।। vedādhyayanasaṃpannāś catvāro acchinnadarśinaḥ ।।
te yoganiratāḥ siddhāḥ prasthitāḥ sarva eva hi ।। adharma eṣa yuṣmākaṃ yan māṃ tyaktvā gamiṣyatha ।। kāmān abhīpsitān sarvān mama kṛtvādya putrakāḥ । śuśrūṣām aprayuktvā ca kathaṃ vai gantum arhatha ।।
kariṣyāmo vidhānaṃ te yena tvaṃ vartayiṣyasi ।। śrāvayethāḥ samāgamya brahmadattam akalmaṣam ।। yathepsitāṃś ca sarvārthān gaccha tāta yathāsukham ।। yogadharmam anuprāpya paramāṃ nirvṛtiṃ yayuḥ ।।
yoginaḥ paramātmānaḥ saṃyatenāntarātmanā । yogātmā tapasā yukto viṣvaksena iti śrutaḥ ।। vijahāra prahṛṣṭātmā yathā śacyā śatakratuḥ ।। kāminīṃ kāminas tasya yācataḥ krośato bhṛśam ।।
brahmadatto mahāhāsam akasmād eva cāhasat ।। nirāhārā bahutithaṃ babhūvāmitrakarśana ।। tvayāvahasitā rājan nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe ।। uvāca cainaṃ kupitā naiṣa bhāvo asti pārthiva ।।
tapaḥphalena vā rājan vidyayā vā narādhipa ।। yady eṣa vai prabhāvas te sarvasattvarutajñatā । prāṇān vāpi parityakṣye rājan satyena te śape ।। śaraṇyaṃ sarvabhūteśaṃ bhaktyā nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।।
dadarśa darśane rājā devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim ।। ity uktvā bhagavān devas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। brahmadatto api rājarṣiḥ sarvasattvarutajñatām । upadiṣya ca bhāryāyai vanāt pratyāgataḥ puram । ślokaṃ so adhītya putrebhyaḥ kṛtakṛtya ivābhavat ।।
na dadarśāntaraṃ cāpi ślokaṃ śrāvayituṃ tadā ।। praviveśa purīṃ prīto ratham āruhya kāñcanam ।। camaravyajanaṃ cāpi bābhravyaḥ samavākṣipat ।। śrāvayām āsa rājānaṃ ślokaṃ taṃ sacivau ca tau ।।
haṃsāḥ sarasi mānase । te sma jātāḥ kurukṣetre brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ । prasthitā dūram adhvānaṃ । cakravākāḥ sarid dvīpe yūyaṃ tebhyo avasīdatha ।।
