sacivau cāsya pāñcālaḥ kaṇḍarīkaś ca bhārata ।। dṛṣṭvā babhūvur asvasthāḥ paurāś cāgantavaś ca ha ।। pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ pratyāgacchad ariṃdama ।। brāḥmaṇaṃ vipulair arthair bhogaiś ca samayojayan ।।
jagāma brahmadatto atha sadāro vanam eva ha ।। uvāca paramaprītā yogād vanagataṃ nṛpam ।। coditaḥ krodham uddiśya saktaḥ kāmeṣu vai mayā ।। tava cāntarhito yogas tataḥ saṃsmārito mayā ।।
prāpya yogaṃ vanād eva gatiṃ prāpa sudurlabhām ।। prāpya yogagatiṃ siddho viśuddhaḥ svena karmaṇā ।। yogācāryagatiṃ prāpa yaśaś cāgryaṃ mahātapāḥ ।। tad dhārayasva gāṅgeya śreyasā yokṣyase tataḥ ।।
tiryagyoniṣu te jātu na bhaviṣyanti karhicit ।। yogadharmo hṛdi sadā parivarteta bhārata ।। ya imaṃ śrāvayec chrāddhe pitṝn prīṇāti puṇyakṛt । akṣayaṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ vai prītir bhavati śāśvatī ।।
ye paṭhanti ca śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti ca ye dvijān । tato manogatiṃ yāti siddhānāṃ bhuvi durlabhām ।। śrāddhasya phalam uddiśya somasyāpyāyanāya vai ।। vṛṣṇivaṃśaprasaṅgena tasya vaṃśaṃ nibodha me ।।
athātaḥ śrūyatāṃ rājan vaṃśaḥ somasya pāvanaḥ । yasminn ailādayo bhūpāḥ kīrtyante puṇyakīrtayaḥ ।। yatra jāto hariḥ sākṣāt kṛṣṇas trailokyapāvanaḥ । sahasraśirasaḥ puṃso nābhihradasaroruhāt ।।
jātasyāsīt suto dhātur atriḥ pitṛsamo guṇaiḥ । brahmaṇo mānasāt pūrvaṃ prajāsargaṃ vidhitsataḥ । karmaṇā manasā vācā śubhāny eva cacāra ha ।। kāṣṭhakuḍyaśilābhūta ūrdhvabāhur mahādyutiḥ ।।
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi divyānīti hi naḥ śrutam ।। somatvaṃ tanur āpede mahābuddhasya bhārata ।। netrābhyāṃ vāri susrāva daśadhā dyotayad diśaḥ ।। sametya dhārayām āsur na ca tāḥ tam aśaknuvan ।।
papāta bhāsayaṃl lokāñ śītāṃśuḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ।। tatas tābhiḥ sahaivāśu nipatāta vasuṃdharām ।। ratham āropayām āsa lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। yukto vājisahasreṇa siteneti hi naḥ śrutam ।।
tuṣṭuvur brahmaṇaḥ putrā mānasāḥ sapta ye śrutāḥ ।। ṛgbhir yajurbhiḥ sāmabhir atharvāṅgirasair api ।। āpyāyamānaṃ lokāṃs trīn bhāvayām āsa sarvataḥ ।। triḥsaptakṛtvo atiyaśāś cakārābhipradakṣiṇām ।।
oṣadhyas tāḥ samudbhūtās tejasā prajvalanty uta ।। poṣṭā hi bhagavān somo jagato jagatīpate ।। tapas tepe mahābhāga padmānāṃ daśatīr daśa ।। nidhis tāsām abhūd devaḥ prakhyātaḥ svena karmaṇā ।।
bījauṣadhīnāṃ viprāṇām apāṃ ca janamejaya ।। trīṃl lokān bhāvayām āsa svabhāsā bhāsvatāṃ varaḥ ।। dadau prācetaso dakṣo nakṣatrāṇīti yā viduḥ ।। samājahre rājasūyaṃ sahasraśatadakṣiṇam ।।
hiraṇyagarbhaś codgātā brahmā brahmātvam eyivān ।। sanatkumārapramukhair ādyair brahmarṣibhir vṛtaḥ ।। tebhyo brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaś ca bhārata ।। kīrtir dhṛtiś ca lakṣmīś ca nava devyaḥ siṣevire ।।
taṃ mūrdhny upāghrāya tadā somo dhātā prajāpatiḥ । virarājāti rājendro daśadhā bhāvayan diśaḥ ।। vibabhrāma matis tāta vinayād anayāhṛtā ।। jahāra tarasā sarvān avamatyāṅgiraḥsutān ।।
naiva vyasarjayat tārāṃ tasmā aṅgirase tadā ।। sa saṃrabdhas tadā tasmin devācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ । sa hi śiṣyo mahātejāḥ pituḥ pūrvaṃ bṛhaspateḥ ।। pārṣṇigrāho abhavad devaḥ pragṛhyājagavaṃ dhanuḥ ।।
uddiśya devān utsṛṣṭaṃ yenaiṣāṃ nāśitaṃ yaśaḥ ।। devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca lokakṣayakaraṃ mahat ।। brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmur ādidevaṃ pitāmaham ।। dadāv aṅgirase tārāṃ svayam eva pitāmahaḥ ।।
madīyāyāṃ na te yonau garbho dhāryaḥ kathaṃ cana ।। satyaṃ kathaya me subhru kasya garbhas tavodare । tyaja tyajāśu durbuddhe matkṣetrād āhitaṃ paraiḥ ।। nāhaṃ tvāṃ bhasmasāt kuryāṃ striyaṃ sāṃtānike sati । śrutvā bṛhaspater vākyaṃ roṣeṇa vyākulābhavat । iṣīkāstambam āsādya jvalantam iva pāvakam ।। tataḥ saṃśayam āpannās tārām akathayan surāḥ ।।
kumāro mātaraṃ prāha kupito alīkalajjayā । kiṃ na vocasy asadvṛtte ātmāvadyaṃ vadāśu me । tadā tāṃ śaptum ārabdhaḥ kumāro dasyuhantamaḥ ।। yad atra tathyaṃ tad brūhi tāre kasya suto hy ayam ।।
somasyeti mahātmānaṃ kumāraṃ dasyuhantamam ।। pratikūlaṃ ca gagane samabhyuttiṣṭhate budhaḥ ।। urvaśyāṃ jajñire yasya putrāḥ sapta mahātmanaḥ ।। jagāma śaraṇāyātha pitaraṃ so atrim eva ca ।।
sa rājayakṣmaṇā muktaḥ śriyā jajvāla sarvaśaḥ ।। vaṃśam asya mahārāja kīrtyamānam ataḥ śṛṇu ।। somasya janma śrutvaiva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। naro vigatakalmaṣaḥ śraddadhānaḥ prasannātmā ।
tejasvī dānaśīlaś ca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। āhartā cāgnihotrasya yajñānāṃ ca divo mahīm ।। atīva triṣu lokeṣu yaśasāpratimaḥ sadā ।। urvaśī varayām āsa hitvā mānaṃ yaśasvinī ।।
pañca ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa cāṣṭau ca bhārata ।। alakāyāṃ viśālāyāṃ nandane ca vanottame ।। gandhamādanapādeṣu meruśṛṅge tathottare ।। urvaśyā sahito rājā reme paramayā mudā ।।
rājyaṃ sa kārayām āsa prayāge pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। uttare jāhnavītīre pratiṣṭhānemahāyaśāḥ । eka evapurā devaḥ praṇavaḥ sarvavāṅmayaḥ । devo nārāyaṇo nānya eko agnivarṇa eva ca ।। purūravasa evāsīt trayī tretāmukhe nṛpa । agninā prajayā rājā lokaṃ gāndharvam eyivān । viśvāyuś caiva dharmātmā śrutāyuś ca tathāparaḥ । dṛḍhāyuś ca vanāyuś ca śatāyuś corvaśīsutāḥ ।।
svarbhānutanayāyāṃ ca prabhāyāṃ jajñire nṛpa । dambho rajir anenāś ca triṣu lokeṣu viśrutāḥ ।। rājeyam iti vikhyātaṃ kṣatram indrabhayāvaham ।। devāś caivāsurāś caiva pitāmaham athābruvan ।।
brūhi naḥ sarvabhūteśa śrotum icchāmahe vacaḥ ।। yotsyate te vijeṣyanti trīṃl lokān nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। yato dhṛtiś ca śrīś caiva dharmas tatra jayas tathā ।। abhyayur jayam icchanto vṛṇvānā bharatarṣabha ।।
rājā paramatejasvī somavaṃśavivardhanaḥ ।। ūcur asmajjayāya tvaṃ gṛhāṇa varakārmukam ।। athovāca rajis tatra tayor vaidevadaityayoḥ । svārthajñaḥ svārtham uddiśya yaśaḥ svaṃ ca prakāśayan । indro bhavāmi dharmeṇa tato yotsyāmi saṃyuge ।।
devāḥ prathamatobhūyaḥ pratīyur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ । evaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ nṛpate kāmaḥ saṃpadyatāṃ tava ।। śrutvā suragaṇānāṃ tu vākyaṃ rājā rajis tadā । papracchāsuramukhyāṃs tu yathā devān apṛcchata ।। dānavā darpapūrṇās tu svārtham evānugamya ha । pratyūcus taṃ nṛpavaraṃ sābhimānam idaṃ vacaḥ । asmākam indraḥ prahrādo yasyārthe vijayāmahe ।। sa tatheti bruvann eva devair apy abhicoditaḥ । jaghāna dānavān sarvān ye vadhyā vajrapāṇinā ।।
nihatya dānavān sarvān ājahāra rajiḥ prabhuḥ ।। rajiputro aham ity uktvā punar evābravīd vacaḥ ।। yasyāham indraḥ putras te khyātiṃ yāsyāmi karmabhiḥ ।। tathety evābravīd rājā prīyamāṇaḥ śatakratum ।।
dāyādyam indrād ājahrur ācārāt tanayā rajeḥ ।। samākrāmanta bahudhā svargalokaṃ triviṣṭapam ।। hṛtarājyo abravīc chakro hṛtabhāgo bṛhaspatim ।। brahmarṣe yena tiṣṭheyaṃ tejasāpyāyitaḥ sadā ।।
hataujā durbalo mūḍho rajiputraiḥ kṛto vibho ।। nābhaviṣyat tvatpriyārtham akartavyaṃ mayānagha ।। tathā tāta kariṣyāmi mā te bhūd viklavaṃ manaḥ ।। teṣāṃ ca buddhisaṃmoham akarod ṛṣisattamaḥ ।।
nāstivādārthaśāstraṃhi dharmavidveṣaṇaṃ param । paramaṃ tarkaśāstrāṇām asatāṃ tan manonugam । na hi dharmapradhānānāṃ rocate vai kathāntare ।। te tad bṛhaspatikṛtaṃ śāstraṃ śrutvālpacetasaḥ । pūrvoktadharmaśāstrāṇām abhavan dveṣiṇaḥ sadā ।। pracakrur nyāyarahitaṃ tanmataṃ bahu menire । tenādharmeṇa te pāpāḥ sarva eva kṣayaṃ gatāḥ ।। trailokyarājyaṃ śakras tu prāpya duṣprāpam eva ca । bṛhaspatiprasādād dhi parāṃ nirvṛtim abhyagāt । brahmadviṣaś ca saṃvṛttā hatavīryaparākramāḥ ।। hatvā rajisutān sarvān kāmakrodhaparāyaṇān ।। śṛṇuyād dhārayed vāpi na sa daurātmyam āpnuyāt ।।
rajeḥ pañca śatāny āsan putrāṇām amitaujasām । devair abhyarthito daityān hatvendrāyādadād divam ।। indras tasmai punar hatvā gṛhītvā caraṇau rajeḥ । ātmānam arpayām āsa prahrādādyariśaṅkitaḥ ।। pitary uparate putrā yācamānāya no daduḥ । guruṇā hūyamāne agnau balabhit tanayān rajeḥ । avadhīd dhvaṃsitān mārgān na kaś cid avaśeṣitaḥ । arogaś ca bhavet tāta yāvajjīvam akalmaṣaḥ । utpannāḥ pitṛkanyāyāṃ virajāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ । ṣaḍ ime nahuṣasyāsann indrayāṇīva dehinaḥ । suyātiḥ ṣaṣṭhas teṣāṃ vai yayātiḥpārthivo abhavat ।
yatir jyeṣṭhas tu teṣāṃ vai yayātis tu tataḥ param ।। rājyaṃ naicchad yatiḥ pitrā dattaṃ tatpariṇāmavit । yatra praviṣṭaḥ puruṣa ātmānaṃ nāvabudhyate । tenāsau mokṣam āsthāya brahmabhūto abhavan muniḥ ।।
pitari dhvaṃsite sthānād indrāṇyā dharṣaṇād dvijaiḥ । prāpito ajagaratvaṃ vai yayātir abhavan nṛpaḥ । śarmiṣṭhām āsurīṃ caiva tanayāṃ vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī ।। yuktaṃ manojavaiḥ śubhrair yena bhāryāṃ samudvahat ।।
yayātir yudhi durdharṣas tathā devān savāsavān ।। yāvat tava sanāmā vai pauravo janamejaya ।। brahmahatyāyutaḥ pāpa indraḥ kruddho aharad ratham । jagāma sa ratho nāśaṃ śāpād gargasya dhīmataḥ ।।
vākkrūraṃ hiṃsayām āsa brahmahatyām avāpa saḥ ।। paurajānapadais tyakto na lebhe śarma karhicit ।। indrotaṃ śaunakaṃ rājā śaraṇaṃ pratyapadyata ।। sa lohagandho vyanaśat tasyāvabhṛtham etya ha ।।
dattaḥ śakreṇa tuṣṭena lebhe tasmād bṛhadrathaḥ ।। bṛhadrathāt krameṇaiva gato bārhadrathaṃ nṛpam । pradadau vāsudevāya prītyā kauravanandana ।। vyabhajat pañcadhā rājyaṃ putrāṇāṃ nāhuṣas tadā ।।
pratīcyām uttarasyāṃ tu druhyuṃ cānuṃca nāhuṣaḥ ।। madhye pūruṃ ca rājānam abhyaṣiñcat sa nāhuṣaḥ ।। prajās teṣāṃ purastāt tu vakṣyāmi nṛpasattama ।। jigāya pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ saptadvīpavatīṃ nṛpaḥ ।
paravān abhavad rājā bhāram āveśya bandhuṣu ।। prītimān abhavad rājā yayātir aparājitaḥ ।। jarāṃ me pratigṛhṇīṣva putra kṛtyāntareṇa vai ।। jarāṃ tvayi samādhāya taṃ yaduḥ pratyuvāca ha ।।
notsahe jarayā sthātum antarā prāptayā tava । aviditvā sukhaṃ grāmyaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ naiti pūruṣaḥ । anapākṛtya tāṃ rājan na grahīṣyāmi te jarām ।। tasmāj jarāṃ na te rājan grahītum aham utsahe ।। pratigrahītuṃ dharmajña putram anyaṃ vṛṇīṣva vai ।।
uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho yayātir garhayan sutam ।। mām anādṛtya durbuddhe yad ahaṃ tava deśikaḥ ।। arājyā te prajā mūḍha bhavitrīti narādhipa ।। evam evābravīd rājā pratyākhyātaś ca tair api ।।
yathā te kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ mayā rājarṣisattama ।। tad eva vacanaṃ rājā pūrum apy āha bhārata ।। jarāṃ tvayi samādhāya tvaṃ pūro yadi manyase ।। ko nu loke manuṣyendra pitur ātmakṛtaḥ pumān । pratikartuṃ kṣamo yasya prasādād vindate param ।। adhamo aśraddhayā kuryād akartoccaritaṃ pituḥ । so api tadvayasā kāmāñ jujuṣo avyāhatendrayaḥ ।
yayātir api rūpeṇa pūroḥ paryacaran mahīm ।। viśvācyā sahito reme vane caitrarathe prabhuḥ ।। yadāvitṛptaḥ kāmānāṃ bhogeṣu ca narādhipaḥ । tataḥ pūroḥ sakāśād vai svāṃ jarāṃ pratyapadyata ।।
varaṃ cāsmai dadau prīto vipulaṃ vaṃśam īśvaraḥ । ācandrārkagrahā bhūmir bhaved iti matir mama । apauravā na tu mahī bhaviṣyati kadā cana । yābhiḥ pratyāharet kāmān sarvaśo aṅgāni kūrmavat ।। sa sukhī dhṛtimān dhanyaḥ paratreha ca modate । haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।।
yadā na kurute bhāvaṃ sarvabhūteṣv amaṅgalaṃ । samadṛṣṭes tadā puṃsaḥ sarvāḥ sukhamayā diśaḥ । nālam ekasya tat sarvam iti matvā śamaṃ vrajet ।। utpannasya ruroḥ śṛṅgaṃ vardhamānasyavardhate । karmaṇā manasā vācā brahma saṃpadyate tadā ।।
yadā necchati na dveṣṭi brahma saṃpadyate tadā ।। yā dustyajā durmatibhir yā na jīryati jīryataḥ । yo asauprāṇāntiko rogas tāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ tyajataḥ sukham ।। jīryanti jīryataḥ keśā dantā jīryanti jīryataḥ । dhanāśā jīvitāśā ca jīryato api na jīryati ।। yac ca kāmasukhaṃ loke yac ca divyaṃ mahat sukham । tṛṣṇākṣayasukhasyaite nārhataḥ ṣoḍaśīṃ kalām । tāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ duḥkhanivahāṃ śarmakāmo drutaṃ tyajet । cakṣuḥśrotre ca jīryete tṛṣṇaikātaruṇāyate । kālena mahatā cāpi cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।। anaśnan deham utsṛjya sadāraḥ svargam āptavān ।।
yair vyāptā pṛthivī sarvā sūryasyeva gabhastibhiḥ ।। yatra nārāyaṇo jajñe harir vṛṣṇikulodvahaḥ ।। dhanyasya mahato dharmyaṃ śrīmato dhīmatastathā । yayāteś caritaṃ nityam idaṃ śṛṇvan narādhipa ।।
mucyate pātakebhyaś ca aputrī na bhavet kadā । vistareṇānupūrvyā ca tad bhavān vaktum arhati ।। vistareṇānupūrvyā ca yatra jāto asi pārthiva ।। druhyoścānor yadoś caiva turvasoś ca paraṃtapa ।।
rājā cābhayado nāma manasyor abhavat sutaḥ ।। sudhanvanaḥ subāhus tu raudrāśvas tasya cātmajaḥ ।। saṃpātis tasya cātmajaḥ ।saṃpātes tu rahasyātī । daśāpsarasi sūnavaḥ ।
ṛceyuś prathamas teṣāṃ । kakṣeyuḥ sthaṇḍileyuś ca saṃnateyus tathaiva ca ।। ṣaṣṭhaś caiva ruceyuś ca jaleyuś caivasaptamaḥ । dharmeyuś ca dṛḍheyuś ca vaneyur daśamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
vananityo vaneyuś ca putrikāś ca daśa striyaḥ ।। daśaite apsarasaḥ putrā vaneyuś cāvamaḥ smṛtaḥ । ghṛtācyām indriyāṇīva mukhyasya jagadātmanaḥ । tathā gopabalā ca strī ratnakūṭā ca tā daśa ।। rudrāyāṃ janayām āsa somaṃ putraṃ yaśasvinam ।।
tamobhibhūte loke ca prabhā yena pravartitā ।। vacanāt tasya viprarṣer na papāta divo mahīm ।। yajñeṣv atridhanaṃ caiva surair yasya pravartitam ।। daśa putrān mahātmānas tapasy ugre ratān sadā ।।
svastyātreyā iti khyātāḥ kiṃ tv atridhanavarjitāḥ ।। sabhānaraś cākṣuṣaś ca paramekṣus tathaiva ca ।। kālānalasya dharmajñaḥ sṛñjayo nāma vai sutaḥ ।। janamejayo mahārāja puraṃjayasuto abhavat ।।
puraṃjayān mahārāja putro abhūjjanamejayaḥ । deveṣu sa parijñātaḥ pratiṣṭhitayaśās tathā ।। jajñe vīraḥ suragaṇaiḥ pūjitaḥ sa mahāmanāḥ ।। uśīnaraṃ ca dharmajñaṃ titikṣuṃ ca mahābalam ।।
nṛgā kṛmī navā darvā pañcamī ca dṛṣadvatī ।। tapasā caiva mahatā jātā vṛddhasya cātmajāḥ ।। navāyās tu navaḥ putro darvāyāḥ suvrato abhavat ।। śibes tu śibayas tāta yaudheyās tu nṛgasya ha ।।
suvratasya tathāmbaṣṭhā titikṣos tu prajāḥ śṛṇu ।। śibiputrān nibodha me ।।śibeś ca putrāś catvāro vīrā vai lokaviśrutāḥ । vṛṣadarbhaḥ suvīraś ca kaikeyo madrakas tathā ।। teṣāṃ janapadāḥ sphītāḥ kaikeyā madrakās tathā । vṛṣadarbhāḥ suvīrāś ca । uṣadratho mahābāhus tasya phenaḥ suto abhavat ।। balir mānuṣayonau tu sa rājā kāñcaneṣudhiḥ ।।
putrān utpādayām āsa pañca vaṃśakarān bhuvi ।। bāleyā brāhmaṇāś caiva tasya vaṃśakarā bhuvi ।। saṃgrāme cāpy ajeyatvaṃ dharme caiva pradhānatām । trailokyadarśanaṃ cāpi prādhānyaṃ prasave tathā ।
balasyāpratimatvaṃ vai dharmatattvārthadarśanam । caturo niyatān varṇāṃs tvaṃ ca sthāpayiteti ha ।। tasya te tanayāḥ sarve kṣetrajāmunipuṃgavāḥ । saṃbhūtā dīrghatapasaḥ sudeṣṇāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ ।
balis tān abhiṣicye ha pañca putrān akalmaṣān ।। kṛtārthaḥ so api yogātmā yogam āśritya sa prabhuḥ । adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ kālāpekṣī caraty uta । kālena mahatā rājan svaṃ ca sthānam upāgamat ।।
kaliṅgāḥ puṇḍrakāś caiva prajās tv aṅgasya me śṛṇu ।। dadhivāhanaputras tu rājā divirathas tathā ।। vidvān dharmaratho nāma tasya citrarathaḥ sutaḥ ।। yajatā saha śakreṇa somaḥ pīto mahātmanā ।।
lomapāda iti khyāto yasya śāntā sutābhavat ।। ṛṣyaśṛṅgaprabhāvena jajñe kulavivardhanaḥ ।। campasya tu purī campā yā pūrvaṃ mālinī babhau ।। avatārayām āsa mahīṃ mantrair vāhanam uttamam ।।
rājā bhadrarathaḥ smṛtaḥ । putro bhadrarathasyāsīd bṛhatkarmā prajeśvaraḥ । bṛhaddarbhaḥ sutas tasya yasmāj jajñe bṛhanmanāḥ ।। bṛhanmanās tu rājendro janayām āsa vai sutam ।
nāmnā jayadrathaṃ nāma yasmād dṛḍharatho nṛpaḥ ।। āsīd dṛḍharathasyāpi viśvajij janamejaya । dāyādas tasya karṇas tu । tasya putraśataṃ tv āsīd aṅgānāṃ kulavardhanam ।।
vikarṇasya sutas tv āsīd aṅgadaḥkulavardhanaḥ । bṛhaddarbhasuto yas tu rājā nāmnābṛhanmanāḥ । tasya patnīdvayam cāsīc caidyasyaite sute śubhe । yaśodevī ca sattvī ca tābhyāṃ vaṃśaḥ sa bhidhyate ।। jayadrathas tu rājendra yaśodevyāṃ vyajāyata । brahmakṣatrottaraḥ sattvyāṃ vijayo nāma viśrutaḥ ।। vijayasya dhṛtiḥ putras tasya putro dhṛtavrataḥ । dhṛtavratasya putras tu satyakarmā mahāvrataḥ ।। satyakarmasutaś cāpi sūtas tv adhirathas tu vai । yaḥ karṇaṃ pratijagrāha tataḥ karṇas tu sūtajaḥ ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ karṇaṃ prati mahābalam । karṇasya vṛṣasenas tu vṛṣas tasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ । dhārmikaḥ sarvavarṇas tu senastasyātmajo abhavat । satyavratā mahātmānaḥ prajāvanto mahārathāḥ ।। śṛṇu vaṃśam anuproktaṃ yatra jāto asi pārthiva ।। anādhṛṣyas tu rājarṣir ṛceyuś caikarāṭ smṛtaḥ । ṛceyor jvalanā nāma bhāryā vai takṣakātmajā ।
matinārasutāś cāsaṃs trayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। gaurī kanyā cavikhyātā māndhātṛjananī śubhā । sarve vedavratasnātā brahmaṇyāḥ satyavādinaḥ ।। sarvekṛtāstrā balinaḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ । putro apratirathasyāsīt kaṇvaḥ samabhavan nṛpaḥ । medhātithiḥ sutas tasya yasmāt kāṇvo abhavad dvijaḥ ।
brahmavādiny adhitrī ca taṃsus tām adhyagacchata ।। brahmavādī parākrāntas tasya bhāryopadānavī ।। tataś cotpādayām āsa caturaḥ purunandanān । duḥṣantam atha suḥṣantaṃ pravīram anaghaṃ tathā ।।
sa sarvadamano nāma nāgāyutabalo mahān ।। śakuntalāyāṃ bharato yasya nāmnā stha bhāratāḥ ।। duḥṣantaṃ prati rājāṇaṃ vāg uvācāśarīriṇī । mātā bhastrā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa eva saḥ । bharasva putraṃ duḥṣanta māvamaṃsthāḥ śakuntalām ।। retodhāḥ putra unnayati naradeva yamakṣayāt । tvaṃ cāsya dhātā garbhasya satyam āha śakuntalā । mātṝṇāṃ tāta kopeṇa yathā te kathitaṃ tadā ।।
ayājayad bharadvājo mahadbhiḥ kratubhir vibhuḥ ।। atraivodāharantīmaṃ bharadvājasya dhīmataḥ । dharmasaṃkramaṇaṃ cāpi marudbhir bharatāya vai । tato atha vitatho nāma bharadvājāt suto abhavat ।। tato atha vitathe jāte bharatas tu divaṃ yayau । vitathaṃ cābhiṣicyātha bharadvājo vanaṃ yayau । vitathasya tu dāyādo bhuvamanyur babhūva ha । mahābhūtopamāś cāmī catvāro bhuvamanyujāḥ । bṛhatkṣatro mahāvīryo naro gārgyaś ca vīryavān ।। narasya sāṃkṛtiḥ putras tasya putrau mahābalau । varavī rantidevaś ca te ca kātyāyanāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। dāyādā api gārgyasya śibir vidvān babhūva ha । smṛtāḥ śaibyās tato gārgyāḥ kṣatrotpannā dvijātayaḥ ।। mahāvīryasutaś cāsīd dhīmān nāmnā purukṣayaḥ । tasya bhāryā viśālā tu suṣuve tat sutatrayam । traiyākṣaṇaṃ puṣkariṇaṃ tṛtīyaṃ suṣuve kapim ।। kapīnāṃ pravarā hy ete trayaḥ proktā maharṣayaḥ । gārgyāḥ saṃkṛtayaḥ kāpyāḥ kṣatrotpannā dvijātayaḥ । saṃśritāṅgirasaḥ pakṣaṃ sarve jātā mahābalāḥ ।। bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ suhotro nāma dhārmikaḥ । suhotrasya tu dāyādo hastī nāma babhūva ha । tenedaṃ nirmitaṃ pūrvaṃ puraṃ gajasamāhvayam ।। hastinaś cāpi dāyādās trayaḥ paramakīrtayaḥ । ajamīḍhasya putrās tu jātāḥ kurukulodvaha ।। tapaso ante sumahato rājño vṛddhasya dhārmikāḥ । bharadvājaprasādena jātā vaṃśavivardhanāḥ ।। ajamīḍhasya keśinyāṃ kaṇvaḥ samabhavat sutaḥ । medhātithiḥ sutas tasya tasmāt kāṇvāyanāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
suhotraṃ sutahotāraṃ gayaṃ gargaṃ tathaiva ca ।। suhotrasya ca putras tu cyavano nāma dhārmikaḥ । kāśikaś ca mahāsattvas tathā gṛtsamatiḥ prabhuḥ ।। kāśyasya kāśayo rājan putro dīrghatapās tathā ।।
dhanvaṃtares tu tanayaḥ ketumān iti viśrutaḥ ।। suto bhīmarathasyāsīd divodāsaḥprajeśvaraḥ । divodāsa iti khyātaḥ sarvarakṣaḥpraṇāśanaḥ ।। śūnyāṃ niveśayām āsa kṣemako nāma rākṣasaḥ ।।
śūnyā varṣasahasraṃ vai bhavitrīti nararṣabha ।। viṣayānte purīṃ ramyāṃ gomatyāṃ saṃnyaveśayat ।। bhadraśreṇyasya pūrvaṃ tu purī vārāṇasībhavat । yaduvaṃśaprasūtasya tapasy abhiratasya ca । hatvā niveśayām āsa divodāsaḥ prajeśvaraḥ ।।
pratardanasya putrau dvau vatso bhārgava eva ca ।। hehayasya tu dāyādyaṃ hṛtavān vai mahīpatiḥ ।। tasyānvaye suhotro abhūd rājā paramadhārmikaḥ । divodāsena bālo hi ghṛṇayā sa visarjitaḥ ।।
vairasyāntaṃ mahārāja kṣatriyeṇa vidhitsatā ।। so apy evaṃ putrasaṃhāraṃ kurvan pañcatvamāgataḥ । alarkaṃ prati rājānaṃ śloko gītaḥ purātanam । ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣaśatāni ca ।।
tasyāsītsumahadrājyaṃ rūpayauvanaśālinaḥ । lopāmudrāprasādena paramāyur avāpa saḥ ।। ramyāṃ niveśayām āsa purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ nṛpaḥ ।। kṣemako nāma pārthivaḥ ।
kṣemakasya tu putro vai । kṣemasya ketumān putro varṣaketus tato abhavat ।। ānartas tu vibhoḥ putraḥ sukumāras tato abhavat ।। karantur nāma nṛpatis tasya putrau babhūvatuḥ ।
brahmaṇyau satyasaṃpannau bhārgo vatsas tathaiva ca । vatsasya vatsabhūmis tu bhārgabhūmis tu bhārgavāt ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca bharatarṣabha ।। karmabhis te tapomūlaiḥ sthitāḥkurukulodvaha ।
ajamīḍho dvimīḍhaś ca purumīḍhaś ca vīryavān ।। nīlī ca keśinī caiva dhūminī ca varāṅganā ।। ya ājahre mahāsattraṃ sarvamedham mahāmakham ।। necchataḥ plāvayām āsa tasya gaṅgā ca tat sadaḥ ।।
sauhotrir abravīd gaṅgāṃ kruddho bharatasattama ।। asya gaṅge avalepasya sadyaḥ phalam avāpnuhi ।। upaninyur mahābhāgāṃ duhitṛtvāya jāhnavīm ।। gaṅgāśāpena dehārdhaṃ yasyāḥ paścān nadīkṛtam ।।
ajakasya tu dāyādo balākāśvo mahīpatiḥ ।। pahlavaiḥ saha saṃvṛddho rājā vanacaraiḥ sa ha ।। labheyam iti taṃ śakras trāsād abhyetya jajñivān ।। viśvāmitras tu gādheyo rājā viśvarathaś ca ha ।।
ṛcīkāj jamadagnis tu satyavatyām ajāyata ।। prakhyātās triṣu lokeṣu teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। śālāpatir hiraṇyākṣo reṇur yasyātha reṇukā ।। teṣāṃ khyātāni gotrāṇi kauśikānāṃ mahātmanām ।।
pārthivā devarātāś ca sālaṅkāyanasauśravāḥ ।। ṛṣyantaravivāhyāś ca kauśikā bahavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। saṃbandho hy asya vaṃśe asmin brahmakṣatrasya viśrutaḥ ।। bhārgavaḥ kauśikatvaṃ hi prāptaḥ sa munisattamaḥ ।।
dṛṣadvatīsutaś cāpi viśvāmitrād athāṣṭakaḥ ।। ājamīḍho aparo vaṃśaḥ śrūyatāṃ bharatarṣabha ।। purujātiḥ suśāntes tu bāhyāśvaḥ purujātitaḥ ।। mudgalaḥ sṛñjayaś caiva rājā bṛhadiṣus tathā ।।
pañceme rakṣaṇāyālaṃ deśānām iti viśrutāḥ ।। alaṃ saṃrakṣaṇe teṣāṃ pāñcālā iti viśrutāḥ ।। sarva ete mahātmānaḥ kṣatropetādvijātayaḥ । ete hy aṅgirasaḥ pakṣaṃ saṃśritāḥ kaṇvamaudgalāḥ ।।
mudgalasya suto jyeṣṭho brahmarṣiḥ sumahātapāḥ । indrasenā yato garbhaṃ vadhryaśvaṃ pratyapadyata ।। vadhryaśvān mithunaṃjajñe menakāyām iti śrutiḥ । divodāsaś ca rājarṣir ahalyā ca yaśasvinī ।। śaradvatasya dāyādam ahalyā saṃprasūyata । śatānandam ṛṣiśreṣṭhaṃ tasyāpi sumahāyaśāḥ । putraḥ satyadhṛtir nāma dhanurvedasya pāragaḥ ।। tasya satyadhṛte reto dṛṣṭvāpsarasam agrataḥ । atha skannaṃ śarastambe mithunaṃ samapadyata ।। kṛpayā tac ca jagrāha śaṃtanur mṛgayāṃ gataḥ । kṛpaḥ smṛtaḥ sa vai tasmād gautamī ca kṛpī tathā । ete śāradvatāḥ proktā ete te gautamāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi divodāsasya saṃtatim । divodāsasya dāyādo brahmarṣir mitrayur nṛpaḥ ।। maitreyāṇāṃ tataḥ somo maitreyās tu tataḥ smṛtāḥ । ete vipañcitāḥ pakṣāḥ kṣatropetās tu bhārgavāḥ । sutaḥ pañcavanasyāpi somadatto mahīpatiḥ ।।
sahadevasutaś cāpi somako nāma pārthivaḥ ।। ajamīḍhāt punar jātaḥ kṣīṇe vaṃśe tu somakaḥ । teṣāṃ yavīyān pṛṣato drupadasya pitā prabhuḥ ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tudrupadād dhṛṣṭaketuś ca tatsutaḥ ।। ājamīḍhāḥ smṛtā hy ete mahātmānas tu somakāḥ । putrāṇām ajamīḍhasya somakatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।
tṛtīyā tava pūrveṣāṃ jananī pṛthivīpate ।। tapo varṣāśataṃ tepe strībhiḥ paramaduścaram ।। agnihotrakuśeṣv eva suṣvāpa janamejaya ।। ṛkṣaṃ sā janayām āsa dhūmavarṇaṃ sudarśanam ।।
yaḥ prayāgād apakramya kurukṣetraṃ cakāra ha ।। tad vaitat sa mahābhāgo varṣāṇi subahūny atha । tapyamāne tadā śakro yatrāsya varado babhau । tasyānvavāyaḥ sumahān yasya nāmnā stha kauravāḥ ।। parīkṣic ca mahābāhuḥ pravaraś cārimejayaḥ ।।
sudhanvanas tu dāyādaḥ suhotro matimān smṛtaḥ । cyavanas tasya putras tu rājā dharmārthakovidaḥ ।। cyavanāt kṛtayajñas tu iṣṭvā yajñaiḥ sa dharmavit । viśrutaṃ janayām āsa putram indrasakhaṃ nṛpaḥ ।। caidyoparicaraṃ vīraṃ vasuṃ nāmāntarikṣagam । caidyoparicarāj jajñe girikā sapta mānavān ।। mahāratho magadharāḍ viśruto yo bṛhadrathaḥ । pratyagrahaḥ kuśaś caiva yam āhur maṇivāhanam । mārutaś ca yaduś caiva matsyakālī ca sattamaḥ ।। bṛhadrathasya dāyādaḥ kuśāgro nāma viśrutaḥ । kuśāgrasyātmajo vidvān ṛṣabho nāma vīryavān ।। dāyādas tasya vikrānto rājā satyahitaḥ smṛtaḥ । tasya putraḥ sa dharmātmā nāmnā ūrjas tu jajñivān । ūrjasya saṃbhavaḥ putro yasya jajñe sa vīryavān ।। śakale dve sa vai jāto jarayā saṃdhitaḥ sa tu । jarayā saṃdhito yasmāj jarāsaṃdhas tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sarvakṣatrasya jetāsau jarāsaṃdho mahābalaḥ । jarāsaṃdhasya putro vai sahadevaḥ pratāpavān ।। sahadevātmajaḥ śrīmān udāyiḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ । udāyir janayām āsa putraṃ paramadhārmikam । śrutadharmeti nāmānaṃ magadhān yo avasad vibhuḥ । vṛṣabhasya tudāyādaḥ puṣpavān nāma dhārmikaḥ । janamejayasya dāyādās traya eva mahārathāḥ । jahnos tukathayiṣyāmi yatra jāto asi pārthiva ।। jahnus tv ajanayat putraṃ surathaṃ nāma bhūmipam ।
śrutaseno agrasenau ca bhīmasenaś ca nāmataḥ ।। ete sarve mahābhāgā vikrāntā balaśālinaḥ । surathasya tu vikrāntaḥ putro jajñe vidūrathaḥ ।। dvitīyaḥ sa babhau rājā nāmnā tenaiva saṃjñitaḥ ।।
bhīmasenās trayo rājan dvāv eva janamejayau ।। devāpir bāhlikaś caiva traya eva mahārathāḥ ।। bāhlikasya tu rājyaṃ vai saptabāhlyaṃ viśāṃ pate ।। jajñire somadattāt tu bhūrir bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ ।।
cyavanasya putraḥ kṛtaka iṣṭaś cāsīn mahātmanaḥ ।। śāṃtanus tv abhavad rājā kauravāṇāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥ ।। śāṃtanoḥsaṃpravakṣyāmi yatra jāto asi pārthiva ।। gāṅgaṃ devavrataṃ nāma putraṃ so ajanayat prabhuḥ । sa tu bhīṣma iti khyātaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ pitāmahaḥ । śāṃtanor dayitaṃ putraṃ dharmātmānam akalmaṣam ।।
dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pāṇḍuṃ ca viduraṃ cāpy ajījanat ।। dhṛtarāṣṭras tu gāndhāryāṃ putrānajanayac chatam । teṣāṃ duryodhanaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarveṣām eva sa prabhuḥ । abhimanyoḥ parīkṣit tu pitā tava janeśvara ।। turvasos tu pravakṣyāmi druhyoś cānor yados tathā ।।
gobhānos tu suto rājā triśānur aparājitaḥ ।। anyas tv āvikṣito rājā maruttaḥ kathitas tava ।। duhitā saṃmatā nāma tasyāsīt pṛthivīpateḥ ।। duḥṣantaṃ pauravaṃ cāpi lebhe putram akalmaṣam ।।
pauravaṃ turvasor vaṃśaḥ praviveśa nṛpottama ।। śarutthāmād athākrīḍaś catvāras tasya cātmajāḥ ।। teṣāṃ janapadāḥ sphītāḥ pāṇḍyaś colaś ca keralāḥ ।। aṅgārasetus tatputro marutāṃ patir ucyate ।।
yuddhaṃ sumahad āsīd dhi māsān pari caturdaśa ।। gāndhāradeśajāś caiva turagā vājināṃ varāḥ ।। pracetasaḥ sucetās tu kīrtitā hy anavo mayā ।। yador vaṃśaṃpravakṣyāmi jyeṣṭhasyottamatejasaḥ । vistareṇanupūrvyā ca gadato me niśāmaya । yasya śravaṇamātreṇa pātakebhyaḥpramucyate ।
sahasradaḥ payodaś ca kroṣṭā nīlo añjikas tathā ।। śatajin nāma pārthivaḥ । śatajitaḥ sutāḥ khyātās । hehayaś ca hayaś caiva rājan veṇuhayas tathā ।।
dharmanetrasya kāntas tu kāntaputrās tato abhavan ।। sāhañjasya mahiṣmāṃs tu bhadraśreṇyaś catatsutaḥ । sāhañjanī nāmapurī tena rājñā niveśitā ।। sāhañjasya tu dāyādo mahiṣmān nāma pārthivaḥ । māhiṣmatī nāma purī yena rājñā niveśitā ।। āsīn mahiṣmataḥ putro bhadraśreṇyaḥ pratāpavān । vārāṇasyadhipo rājā kathitaḥ pūrvam eva tu । bhadraśreṇyasya dāyādo durdamo nāma viśrutaḥ ।। durdamasya suto dhīmān kanako nāma nāmataḥ । kanakasya tu dāyādāś catvāro lokaviśrutāḥ । kṛtāgniś ca caturtho abhūt kṛtavīryāt tathārjunaḥ ।। jigāya pṛthivīm eko rathenādityavarcasā ।।
dattam ārādhayām āsa kārtavīryo atrisaṃbhavam ।। pūrvaṃ bāhusahasraṃ tu prārthitaṃ paramaṃ varam ।। ugreṇa pṛthivīṃ jitvā dharmeṇaivānurañjanam ।। saṃgrāme vartamānasya vadhaṃ cābhyadhikād raṇe ।।
yogād yogeśvarasyāgre prādurbhavati māyayā ।। sasamudrā sanagarā ugreṇa vidhinā jitā ।। prāptāni vidhinā rājñā śrūyante janamejaya ।। sarve kāñcanayūpāś ca sarve kāñcanavedayaḥ ।।
gandharvair apsarobhiś ca nityam evopaśobhitāḥ ।। varīdāsātmajo vidvān mahimnā tasya vismitaḥ ।। yajñair dānais tapobhir vā vikrameṇa śrutena vā ।। pañcāśītisahasrāṇi avyāhatabalaḥ samāḥ । akarod arjuno rājyaṃ hariṃ caivānvahaṃ smaran । anaṣṭavittasmaraṇe bubhuje akṣayyaṣaḍvasu ।
rathī dvīpān anucaran yogī saṃdṛśyate nṛbhiḥ ।। anaṣṭadravyatā caiva na śoko na ca vibhramaḥ । prabhāveṇa mahārājñaḥ prajā dharmeṇa rakṣataḥ ।। sa sarvaratnabhāk samrāṭ cakravartī babhūva ha । sa eva paśupālo abhūt kṣetrapālaḥ sa eva ca । sa eva vṛṣṭyā parjanyo yogitvād arjuno abhavat ।। sa vai bāhusahasreṇa jyāghātakaṭhinatvacā । bhāti raśmisahasreṇa śaradīva ca bhāskaraḥ ।। sa hi nāgān manuṣyeṣu māhiṣmatyāṃ mahādyutiḥ । karkoṭakasutāñ jitvā puryāṃ tasyāṃ nyaveśayat ।। sa vai vegaṃ samudrasya prāvṛṭkāle ambujekṣaṇaḥ । krīḍann iva bhujodbhinnaṃ pratisrotaś cakāra ha ।। luṇṭhitā krīḍatā tena phenasragdāmamālinī । caladūrmisahasreṇa śaṅkitābhyeti narmadā ।। tasya bāhusahasreṇa kṣubhyamāṇe mahodadhau । bhayān nilīnā niśceṣṭāḥ pātālasthā mahāsurāḥ ।। cūrṇīkṛtamahāvīciṃ calanmīnamahātimim । mārutāviddhaphenaugham āvartakṣobhaduḥsaham ।। prāvartayat tadā rājā sahasreṇa ca bāhunā । devāsurasamākṣiptaḥ kṣīrodam iva mandaraḥ ।। mandarakṣobhacakitā amṛtotpādaśaṅkitāḥ । sahasotpatitā bhītā bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpottamam ।। natā niścalamūrdhāno babhūvus te mahoragāḥ । sāyāhne kadalīkhaṇḍaiḥ kampitās tasya vāyunā ।। sa vai baddhvā dhanur jyābhir utsiktaṃ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ । laṅkeśaṃ mohayitvā tu sabalaṃ rāvaṇaṃ balāt । nirjityaiva samānīya māhiṣmatyāṃ babandha tam ।। śrutvā tu baddhaṃ paulastyaṃ rāvaṇaṃ tv arjunena tu । tato gatvā pulastyas tam arjunaṃ dadṛśe svayam । mumoca rakṣaḥ paulastyaṃ pulastyenānuyācitaḥ ।। yasya bāhusahasrasya babhūva jyātalasvanaḥ । yugānte tv ambudasyeva sphuṭato hy aśaner iva ।। aho bata mṛdhe vīryaṃ bhārgavasya yad acchinat । rājño bāhusahasraṃ tu haimaṃ tālavanaṃ yathā ।। tṛṣitena kadā cit sa bhikṣitaś citrabhānunā । pañcāśītisahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ vai narādhipaḥ । uvāsa tām anusarann avagāḍhomahārṇavaṃ । cakāroddhatavelāntam akālaprāvṛḍuddhataṃ । purāṇigrāmaghoṣāṃś ca viṣayāṃś caiva sarvaśaḥ । jajvāla tasya sarvāṇi citrabhānur didhakṣayā ।।
sa tasya puruṣendrasya prabhāveṇa mahātmanaḥ । dadāha kārtavīryasya śailāṃś caiva vanāni ca ।। sa śūnyam āśramaṃ ramyaṃ varuṇasyātmajasya vai । dadāha balavadbhītaś citrabhānuḥ sa haihayaḥ ।
yaṃ lebhe varuṇaḥ putraṃ purā bhāsvantam uttamam । vasiṣṭhaṃ nāma sa muniḥ khyāta āpava ity uta । yatrāpavas tu taṃ krodhāc chaptavān arjunaṃ vibhuḥ ।। arjuno nāma kauravyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ kuntinandanaḥ ।।
rāmo nāmamahābāhur jāmadagnyaḥ pratāpavān । tapasvī brāhmaṇaś ca tvāṃ haniṣyati sa bhārgavaḥ ।। prabhāveṇa narendrasya prajā dharmeṇa rakṣataḥ ।। varaś caiṣa hi kauravya svayam eva vṛtaḥ purā ।।
kṛtāstrā balinaḥ śūrā dharmātmāno yaśasvinaḥ ।। kārtavīryasya tanayā vīryavanto mahārathāḥ ।। tasya putrāḥ śatākhyās tu tālajaṅghā iti śrutāḥ ।। vītihotrāḥ sujātāś ca bhojāś cāvantayas tathā ।।
bharatāś ca sujātāś ca bahutvān nānukīrtitāḥ ।। madhoḥ putraśataṃ tv āsīd vṛṣaṇas tasya vaṃśabhāk ।। yādavā yadunā cāgre nirucyante ca hehayāḥ ।। śūrāś ca śūravīrāś ca śūrasenās tathānagha ।। śūrasena iti khyātas tasya deśo mahātmanaḥ ।
kārtavīryasya yo janma kathayed iha nityaśaḥ ।। vittavāṃś ca bhavec caiva dharmaścaiva vivardhate । yathā sṛṣṭir yador jātā tathā svarge mahīyate । kimarthaṃ tad vanaṃ dagdham āpavasya mahātmanaḥ । kārtavīryeṇa vikramya tan me brūhi prapṛcchataḥ ।। rakṣitā sa hi rājarṣiḥ prajānām iti naḥ śrutam । kathaṃ sa rakṣitā bhūtvā nāśayām āsa tadvanam ।। ādityo viprarūpeṇa kārtavīryam upasthitaḥ । tṛptim ekām prayacchasva ādityo aham upasthitaḥ ।। bhagavan kena tṛptis te bhaved brūhi vibhāvaso । kīdṛśaṃ bhojanaṃ dadmi śrutvā te vidadhāmy aham ।। sthāvaraṃ dehi me sarvam āhāraṃ vadatāṃ vara । tena tṛpsir bhaven mahyaṃ tena tuṣṭiś ca pārthiva ।। na śakyaṃ sthāvaraṃ sarvaṃ tejasā mānuṣeṇa tu । nirdagdhuṃ tapatāṃ śreṣṭha tvām eva praṇamāmy aham ।। tuṣṭas te ahaṃ śarān dadmi cākṣayān sarvatomukhān । ye [pra]kṣiptāḥ saṃjvalanti mama tejaḥsamanvitāḥ ।। āviṣṭas tejasā me adya sthāvaraṃ śoṣayiṣyasi । śuṣkaṃ bhasma kariṣyāmi tena tṛptir narādhipa ।। tataḥ śarāṃs tadādityo arjunāya tadā dadau । tataḥ sa prācyam adahat sthāvaraṃ sarvam eva tat ।। āśramān atha grāmāṃś ca ghoṣāṃś ca nagarāṇy api । tapovanāni ramyāṇi vanāny upavanāni ca ।। evaṃ sa prācyam adahat tataḥ sarvaṃ pradakṣiṇam । nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmir dagdhā sā yogatejasā ।। etasminn eva kāle tu āpavo jalam āśritaḥ । daśa varṣasahasrāṇi jalavāsī mahān ṛṣiḥ ।। pūrṇe vrate mahātejā udatiṣṭhan mahān ṛṣiḥ । krodhāc chaśāpa rājarṣiṃ kīrtitaṃ vai yathā mayā । bhūtānīva mahārāja pañca sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। vaśī bhavati pañcānām ātmajānāṃ tatheśvaraḥ ।।
dhāraṇāc chravaṇāc caiva pañcavargasya bhārata ।। lobhate manujaḥ śraiṣṭhyaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate । yador vaṃśadharasyeha yajvanaḥ puṇyakarmaṇaḥ ।। yasyānvavāyajo viṣṇur harir vṛṣṇikulaprabhuḥ ।।
gāndhārī janayām āsa anamitraṃ mahābalam ।। teṣāṃ vaṃśas tridhā bhūto vṛṣṇīnāṃ kulavardhanaḥ ।। jajñāte tanayau vṛṣṇeḥ śvaphalkaś citrakas tathā ।। nāsti vyādhibhayaṃ tatra nāvarṣabhayam apyuta ।।
trīṇi varṣāṇi viṣaye nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। śvaphalkaparivarte ca vavarṣa harivāhanaḥ ।। sā mātur udarasthā tu bahūnvarṣagaṇān kila । nivasantī na vai jajñe garbhasthāṃ tāṃ pitābravīt ।। jāyasva śīghraṃ bhadraṃ te kimartham iha tiṣṭhasi । provāca cainaṃ garbhasthā kanyā gāṃ ca dine dine ।। yadi dadyāṃ tato adyāhaṃ jāyayiṣyāmi tāṃ pitā । tathety uvāca taṃ cāsyāḥ pitā kāmam apūrayat । gāndinīṃ nāma sā gāṃ tu dadau vipreṣu nityaśaḥ ।।
akrūraḥ suṣuve tasmāc chvaphalkād bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ।। arikṣepas tathopekṣaḥ śatrughno athārimardanaḥ ।। āvāhaprativāhau ca sundarā ca varāṅganā ।। viśrutā sāmbamahiṣī kanyā cāsyapunarnavā । rūpayauvanasaṃpannā sarvabhūtamanoharā ।। akrūrāt kāśikanyāyāṃ satyaketur ajāyata ।
prasenaś copadevaś ca jajñāte devavarcasau ।। aśvagrīvo aśvabāhuś ca supārśvakagaveṣaṇau ।। subāhur bahubāhuś ca śraviṣṭhāśravaṇe striyau ।। mahiṣyāṃ jajñire śūrād bhojyāyāṃ puruṣā daśa ।।
jajñe yasya prasūtasya dundubhyaḥ prāṇadan divi ।। papāta puṣpavarṣaṃ ca śūrasya bhavane mahat ।। yasyāsīt puruṣāgryasya kāntiś candramaso yathā ।। anādhṛṣṭiḥ kanavako vatsavān atha gṛñjimaḥ ।।
rājādhidevī ca tathā pañcaitā vīramātaraḥ ।। pṛthāṃ duhitaraṃ vavre kuntis tāṃkurunandana । śūraḥ pūjyāya vṛddhāya kuntibhojāya tāṃ dadau । tasmāt kuntīti vikhyātā kuntibhojātmajā pṛthā । śrutadevyāṃ kekayas tu pañca putrān akalmaṣān । sutardanapurogāṃs tu janayām āsa bhārata ।।
rājādhidevī rājendra putrau paramadharmikau । vindānuvindāv āvantyau suṣuve bharatarṣabha । śrutaśravāyāṃ caidyas tu śiśupālo mahābalaḥ ।। yo hato rājasūye vai kṛṣṇena sumahātmanā ।
pṛthukīrtyāṃ tu saṃjajñe tanayo vṛddhaśarmaṇaḥ ।। pṛthāṃ duhitaraṃ cakre kauntyas tāṃ pāṇḍur āvahat ।। loke apratiratho vīraḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ ।। śaineyaḥ satyakas tasmād yuyudhānas tu sātyakiḥ ।।
asaṅgo yuyudhānasya bhūmis tasyābhavatsutaḥ । bhūmer yugaṃdharaḥ putra iti vaṃśaḥ samāpyate । paṇḍitānāṃ paraṃ prāhur devaśravasam uddhavam ।। paṇḍitaṃ nāma rājendra lebhe devaśravāḥsutam । nivṛttaśatruṃ śatrughnaṃ śrutadevā vyajāyata ।।
śrutadevāt tu naiṣādiḥ so asmābhir yaḥpariśrutaḥ । ekalavyo mahārāja niṣādaiḥ parivardhitaḥ ।। vasudevasya vai putro vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān । adbhir dadau sutaṃ vīraṃ śauriḥ kauśikam aurasam ।।
dadau putraṃ svakaṃ śauriḥ kumāramamitaujasam । cārudeṣṇaṃ sucāruṃ ca pañcālaṃ kṛtalakṣaṇam ।। raukmiṇeyo mahābāhuḥ kanīyān bharatarṣabha ।। cārūn adyopayokṣyāmaś cārudeṣṇahatān iti ।।
vīraś cāśvahanuś caiva vīrau tāv atha gṛñjimau ।। jugupsamāno bhojatvād rājasūyamavāpa saḥ । ajātaśatruḥ śatrūṇāṃ jajñe tasya vināśanaḥ ।। vasudevasya tu sutān kīrtayiṣyāmy tāñ śṛṇu ।।
prakṛtānupayuktatvād vistarān nānukīrtanam । dhārayan vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ nānarthair iha yujyate ।। jyeṣṭhā patnī mahārāja dayitānakadundubheḥ ।। yāḥ patnyo vasudevasya caturdaśa varāṅganāḥ । pauravī rohiṇī nāma madirāpi tathāparā । vaiśākhī ca tathā bhadrā sunāmnī caiva pañcamī ।। sahadevā śāntidevā śrīdevā devarakṣitā । vṛkadevy upadevī ca devakī caiva saptamī ।। sutanur vaḍavā caiva dve ete paricārike ।
durdamaṃ damanaṃ śvabhraṃ piṇḍārakakuśīnarau ।। citrā subhadreti punar vikhyātā kurunandana ।। kīrtimantaṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca bhadrasenam udāradhī । mṛtyuṃ samardanaṃ bhadraṃ saṃkarṣaṇam ahīśvaram ।
vipulaṃ teṣv aṣṭatamo svayam eva hariḥ kila । rāmāc ca niśaṭho jajñe revatyāṃ dayitaḥ sutaḥ ।। akrūrāt kāśikanyāyāṃ satyaketur ajāyata ।। ye putrā jajñire śūrā namatas tān nibodhata ।।
upāsaṅgaṃ varaṃ lebhe tanayaṃdevarakṣitā । agāvahaṃ mahātmānaṃ vṛkadevī vyajāyata ।। vijayaṃ lomapādaṃ ca vardhamānaṃ ca devakī ।। ete svayaṃ mahātmanā upadevyāṃ ca jajñire । sutanū ca narāvī ca śaurer āstāṃ parigrahaḥ ।। pauṇḍraś ca kapilaś caiva vasudevasutāv ubhau । narākhyāṃ kapilo jajñe pauṇḍraś ca sutanūsutaḥ । tayor nṛpo abhavat pauṇḍraḥ kapilas tu vanaṃ yayau ।। pūrvyāṃ samabhavad dvīpo vasudevān mahābalaḥ । jarā nāma niṣādānāṃ prabhuḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām । jijñāsāṃ pauruṣe cakre na caskande atha pauruṣam ।।
kṛṣṇāyasasamācakhyo na pumāṃstvaṃ napuṃsakaḥ । ghoṣakanyām upādāya maithunāyopacakrame ।। dhārayām āsa gārgyasya garbhaṃ durdharam acyutam ।। vṛṣapūrvārdhakāyās tam avahan vājino raṇe ।।
yavanasya mahārāja sa kālayavano abhavat ।। vṛṣṇyandhakakulaṃ tasya nārado akathayad vibhuḥ ।। dūtaṃ ca preṣayām āsa vṛṣṇyandhakaniveśane ।। sametā mantrayām āsur jarāsaṃdhabhayena ca ।।
tyaktvā gṛhān dhanaṃ sarve palāyanta manoratham । kuśasthalīṃ dvāravatīṃ niveśayitum īpsavaḥ ।। evaṃ devo mahābāhuḥ pūrvaṃ kṛṣṇaḥprajāpatiḥ । vihārārthaṃ manuṣyāṃśo mānuṣeṣv abhyajāyata । parvasu śrāvayed vidvān nirṛṇaḥ sa sukhī bhavet ।।
vārjinīvatam icchanti svāhiṃ svāhākṛtāṃ varam ।। mahākratubhir īje yo vividhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ ।। citraiś citrarathas tasya putraḥ karmabhir anvitaḥ ।। śaśabinduḥ paraṃ vṛttaṃ rājarṣīṇām anuṣṭhitaḥ ।।
śaṃsanti ca purāṇajñāḥ pārthaśravasam antaram ।। uṣato yajñam akhilaṃ svadharmam uṣatāṃ varaḥ ।। udyatas tasya dharmātmā bhavat putravatāṃvaraḥ । maruttas tasya tanayo rājarṣir abhavan nṛpaḥ ।।
cacāra paramaṃ dharmam amarṣāt pretyabhāvavit ।। babhūva rukmakavacaḥ śataprasavataḥ sutaḥ ।। dhanvināṃ niśitair bāṇair avāpa śriyam uttamām ।। rukmeṣuḥ pṛthurukmaś ca jyāmaghaḥ pālito hariḥ ।।
tābhyāṃ pravrājito rājyāj jyāmagho avasad āśrame ।। jagāma ratham āsthāya deśam anyaṃ dhvajī rathī ।। ṛkṣavantaṃ giriṃ jitvā śuktimatyām uvāsa saḥ ।। aputro api ca rājā sa nānyāṃ bhāryām avindata ।।
ratham āropya sā nītā patnyarthaṃ strīniveśanam ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā ruṣitā śaibyā bhartāram idam abravīt । kimartham iyam ānītā sapatnī durnayā mama । bhāryām uvāca saṃtrāsāt snuṣeti sa nareśvaraḥ ।।
na hi prasūtā putreṇa nānyā bhāryāsti te'nagha । snuṣā saṃbandhavāg eṣā katamena sutena te । abravīt tad upaśrutya jyāmaghorājasattamaḥ । yas te janiṣyate putras tasya bhāryeti jātabhīḥ ।।
putryāṃ vidarbhaṃ subhāgā caitrā pariṇatā satī ।। paścād vidarbho ajanayac chūrau raṇaviśāradau ।। lomapādaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu putraṃparamadhārmikam ।। lomapādātmajo babhrur āhvatis tasya cātmajaḥ । āhvateḥ kaiśikaś caiva vidvān paramadhārmikaḥ । kaiśikasya cidiḥ putras tasmāc caidyā nṛpāḥ smṛtāḥ । kunter dhṛṣṭaḥ suto jajñe raṇadhṛṣṭaḥ pratāpavān ।।
āvantaś ca daśārhaś ca balī viṣṇuharaś ca yaḥ ।। jīmūtaputro vṛkatis tasya bhīmarathaḥ sutaḥ ।। tasya cāsīd daśarathaḥ śakunis tasya cātmajaḥ ।। devakṣatro abhavat tasya daivakṣatrir mahātmanaḥ ।।
madhūnāṃ vaṃśakṛd rājā madhur madhuravāg api ।। putro maruvasas tathā । āsīn maruvasaḥ putraḥ । mātā jajñe atha vaidarbhyāṃ bhadravatyāṃ kurūdvaha ।।
sarvasattvaguṇopetaḥ sātvatāṃ kīrtivardhanaḥ ।। yatrāsan sadguṇopetāḥ sātvatāḥ kulavardhanāḥ । yujyate parayā prītyā prajāvāṃś ca bhavaty uta ।। bhajinaṃ bhajamānaṃ ca divyaṃ devāvṛdhaṃ nṛpam ।।
teṣāṃ visargāś catvāro vistareṇeha tāṅ śṛṇu ।। āstāṃ bhārye tayos tasmāj jajñire bahavaḥ sutāḥ ।। ete bāhyakasṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānād vijajñire ।। upabāhyakasṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānād vijajñire ।।
putraḥ sarvaguṇopeto mama syād iti niścitaḥ ।। sadopaspṛśatas tasya cakāra priyam āpagā ।। kalyāṇatvān narapates tasya sā nimnagottamā ।। bhavet sarvaguṇopeto rājño devāvṛdhasya ca ।
jāyet tasmāt svayaṃ hanta bhavāmy asya sahavratā ।। varayām āsa nṛpatiṃ tām iyeṣa ca sa prabhuḥ ।। tasyām ādhatta garbhaṃ sa tejasvinamudāradhīḥ । putraṃ sarvaguṇopetaṃ babhruṃ devāvṛdhān nṛpāt ।।
guṇān devāvṛdhasyātha kīrtayanto mahātmanaḥ ।। babhruḥ śreṣṭho manuṣyāṇāṃ devair devāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ ।। ete amṛtatvaṃ saṃprāptā babhror daivāvṛdhād iti ।। kīrtimāṃś ca mahātejāḥ sātvatānāṃ mahārathaḥ ।
tasyānvavāyaḥ sumahān bhojā ye mārtikāvatāḥ ।। kukuraṃ bhajamānaṃ ca śamiṃ kambalabarhiṣam ।। jajñe punar vasus tasmād abhijit tu punar vasoḥ ।। āhukaś cāhukī caiva khyātau khyātimatāṃ varau ।।
imāś codāharanty atra gāthāḥ prati tam āhukam ।। aśīticarmaṇā yukto nāhukaḥ prathamaṃ vrajet ।। nāśuddhakarmā nāyajvā yo bhojam abhito vrajet ।। sopāsaṅgānukarṣāṇāṃ dhvajināṃ savarūthinām ।
rathānāṃ meghaghoṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu । rūpyakāñcanakakṣyāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi daśāpi ca ।। ā bhūmipālān bhojān svān atiṣṭhan kiṃkiṇīkinaḥ ।। āhukīṃ cāpy avantibhyaḥ svasāraṃ dadur andhakāḥ ।।
devakaś cograsenaś ca devagarbhasamāv ubhau ।। kumāryaḥ sapta cāpyāsan vasudevāya tā dadau ।। vṛkadevy upadevī ca sunāmnī caiva saptamī ।। rāṣṭrapālo atha sutanur anādhṛṣṭiś ca puṣṭimān ।।
sutanū rāṣṭrapālī ca kaṅkā caiva varāṅganā ।। ugrasenaḥ sahāpatyo vyākhyātaḥ kukurodbhavaḥ ।। ātmano vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ prajāvān āpnute naraḥ ।। rājādhidevaḥ śūras tu vidūrathasuto abhavat ।।
dattātidattau balinau śoṇāśvaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ ।। śravaṇā ca śraviṣṭhā ca svasārau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। svayaṃbhojaḥ svayaṃbhojād dhṛdikaḥ saṃbabhūva ha ।। kṛtavarmāgrajas teṣāṃ śatadhanvā tu madhyamaḥ ।।
sudāntaś cādhidāntaś ca kīnāśo dāmadambhakau ।। kroṣṭoḥ putro anamitras tu tasmād vai devamīḍhuṣaḥ । asamaujās tathā vīro nāsamaujāś ca tāv ubhau ।। sudaṃṣṭraṃ ca sucāruṃ ca kṛṣṇam ity andhakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
ete cānye ca bahavo andhakāḥ kathitās tava । andhakānām imaṃ vaṃśaṃ dhārayed yas tu nityaśaḥ । ātmano vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ । gāndhārī janayām āsa sumitraṃ mitranandanam ।। anamitram amitrāṇāṃ jetāraṃ ca mahābalam ।। prasenaś cātha satrājic chatrusenājitāv ubhau ।।
divyaṃ syamantakaṃ nāma samudrād upalabdhavān ।। tasya satrājitaḥ sūryaḥ sakhā prāṇasamo abhavat । sa kadācin niśāpāye rathena rathināṃ varaḥ । abdhikūlam upaspraṣṭum upasthātuṃ yayau ravim । tasyopatiṣṭhataḥ sūryaṃ vivasvān agrataḥ sthitaḥ । aspaṣṭamūrtir bhagavāṃs tejomaṇḍalavān prabhuḥ ।। atha rājā vivasvantam uvāca sthitam agrataḥ । yathaiva vyomni paśyāmi sadā tvāṃ jyotiṣāṃ pate । tejomaṇḍalinaṃ devaṃ tathaiva purataḥ sthitam । ko viśeṣo asti me tvattaḥ sakhyenopāgatasya vai । etac chrutvā tu bhagavān maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam ।। svakaṇṭhād avamucyaiva ekānte nyastavān bhuvi । tato vigrahavantaṃ taṃ dadarśa nṛpatis tadā । prītimān atha taṃ dṛṣṭvā muhūrtaṃ kṛtavān kathām । tam abhiprasthitaṃ bhūyo vivasvantaṃ sa satrajit । lokān udbhāsayasy etān yena tvaṃ satataṃ prabho ।। tad etan maṇiratnaṃ me bhagavan dātum arhasi । tataḥ syamantakamaṇiṃ dattavāṃs tasya bhāskaraḥ । sa tam ābadhya nagarīṃ praviveśa mahīpatiḥ । taṃ janāḥ paryadhāvanta sūryo ayaṃ gacchatīti ha । purīṃ vismāpayitvā sa rājā tv antaḥpuraṃ yayau ।। tat prasenajite divyaṃ maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam । dadau bhrātre narapatiḥ premṇā satrājid uttamam । satrājit svagṛhaṃ śrīmat kṛtakautukamaṅgalam । praviśya devasadane maṇiṃ viprair nyavedayat ।। dine dine svarṇabhārān aṣṭau sa sravati prabho । avatārya galāt tūrṇam ekānte saṃnyaveśayat । tataḥ satrājitaḥ sūryaṃ jvalantaṃ vapuṣā tadā । praṇipatya mahātmānaṃ kṛtāñjalir avasthitaḥ ।। stutvā ca vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ prīṇayām āsa bhāskaram । tataḥ prasanno bhagavān vṛṇīṣva varam īpsitam ।। ity uvāca sa rājānaṃ sa ca vavre maṇiṃ tadā । sa cāpi taṃ maṇiṃ dattvā tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। satrājic ca mahārāja maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam । kālavarṣī ca parjanyo na ca vyādhibhayaṃ bhavet ।। govindo na ca taṃ lebhe śakto api na jahāra saḥ ।।
syamantakakṛte siṃhād vadhaṃ prāpa vanecarāt ।। nihatya maṇiratnaṃ tam ādāya bilam āviśat ।। prārthanāṃ tāṃ maṇer buddhvā sarva eva śaśaṅkire ।। āhariṣye maṇim iti pratijñāya vanaṃ yayau ।।
devadvijātibhakto ayaṃ śriyaḥ sarvecaro api ca । yatra praseno bhṛgayām ācarat tatra cāpy atha । ṛkṣavantaṃ girivaraṃ vindhyaṃ ca girim uttamam ।। sāśvaṃ hataṃ prasenaṃ tu nāvindac caiva taṃ maṇim ।। ṛkṣena nihato dṛṣṭaḥ pādair ṛkṣasya sūcitaḥ ।।
mahaty ṛkṣabile vāṇīṃ śuśrāva pramaderitām ।। krīḍāpayantyā maṇinā mā rodīr ity atheritām ।। sukumāraka mā rodīs tava hy eṣa syamantakaḥ ।। praviśya cāpi bhagavāṃs tam ṛkṣabilam añjasā ।
sthāpayitvā biladvāri yadūṃl lāṅgalinā saha । śārṅgadhanvā bilasthaṃ tu jāmbavantaṃ dadarśa ha ।। bāhubhyām eva govindo divasān ekaviṃsatim ।। sa vai bhagavatānena yuyudhe svāminātmanaḥ । puruṣaṃ prākṛto matvā kupito nānubhāvavit । dvaṃdvayuddhaṃ sutumulam ubhayor vijigīṣatoḥ । āyudhāśmadrumair dorbhiḥ kravyārthe śyenayor iva ।
adṛṣṭvā nirgamaṃ śaureḥ praviṣṭasya bilaṃ janāḥ । pratīkṣya dvādaśāhāni duḥkhitāḥ svapuraṃ yayuḥ । punar dvāravatīm etya hataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ nyavedayan ।। niśamya devakī rājan rukmiṇy ānakaduṃdubhiḥ । suhṛdo jñātayo aśocan bilāt kṛṣṇam anirgatam ।
jāmbavantaṃ vinirjitya vāsudevo mahābalam । lebhe jāmbavatīṃ kanyām ṛkṣarājasya saṃmatām ।। anunīyarkṣarājānaṃ niryayau ca tadā bilāt ।। dvārakām agamat kṛṣṇaḥ śriyā paramayā yutaḥ ।
dadau satrājite taṃ vai sarvasātvatasaṃsadi ।। ātmā viśodhitaḥ pāpād vinirjitya syamantakam ।। khyātimantas trayas teṣāṃ bhaṅgakāras tu pūrvajaḥ ।। kumāryaś cāpi tisro vai dikṣu khyātā narādhipa ।।
tathā padmāvatī caiva bhāryāḥ kṛṣṇasya tā dadau ।। jajñāte guṇasaṃpannau viśrutau guṇasaṃpadā ।। jajñāte tanayau pṛśneḥ śvaphalkaś citrakas tathā ।। gāṃdīṃ tasyās tu gāṃdītvaṃ sadā gāḥ pradadau hi sā ।।
akrūro atha mahābhāgo yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। girikṣipas tathopekṣaḥ śatruhā cārimejayaḥ ।। āvāhaprativāhau ca sundarā ca varāṅganā ।। rūpayauvanasaṃpannā sarvasattvamanoharā ।।
sudevaś copadevaś ca jajñāte devavarcasau ।। aśvaseno aśvabāhuś ca supārśvakagaveṣaṇau ।। subāhur bahubāhuś ca śraviṣṭḥāśravaṇe striyau ।। veda mithyābhiśāpās taṃ na spṛśanti kadācana ।।
adāt tad dhārayad babhrur bhojena śatadhanvanā ।। akrūro antaram anvicchan maṇiṃ caiva syamantakam ।। rātrau taṃ maṇim ādāya tato akrūrāya dattavān ।। samayaṃ kārayāṃ cakre nāvedyo ahaṃ tvayācyute ।।
mamādya dvārakā sarvā vaśe tiṣṭhaty asaṃśayam ।। prayayau ratham āruhya nagaraṃ vāraṇāvatam ।। bhartur nivedya duḥkhārtā pārśvasthāśrūṇy avartayat ।। kulyārthe ca sa bhrātṝṇāṃ nyayojayata sātyakim ।।
pūrvajaṃ halinaṃ śrīmān idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। syamantakaḥ sa madgāmī tasya prabhur ahaṃ vibho ।। syamantako mahābāho saha nau sa bhaviṣyati ।। tato rathaṃ samāruhya rāmakṛṣṇau mahābalau । śatadhanvavināśāya nagarād vāraṇāvatād । śatadhanvā tato bhīto vijñāyācyutam āgatam ।
śatadhanvā tato akrūram avaikṣat sarvatodiśam ।। śakto api śāṭhyād dhārdikyaṃ nākrūro abhyupapadyata ।। yojanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ hayayā pratyapadyata ।। bhojasya vaḍavā rājan yayā kṛṣṇam ayodhayat ।।
tataḥ kruddhau bhojakṛṣṇau tvaritau tu mahābalau । vañcayitvā tataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śatadhanvātibuddhimān । pūrvāṃ diśaṃ jagāmāśu hayayā vātavegayā । atha drutam agāt kṛṣṇo rathena rathināṃ varaḥ । balena sahito rājan prayayau tasya mārgaṇe । dṛṣṭvā rathasya svāṃ vṛddhiṃ śatadhanvānam ārdayat ।। kham utpetur atha prāṇāḥ kṛṣṇo rāmam athābravīt ।। padbhyāṃ gatvā hariṣyāmi maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam ।।
mithilām abhito rājañ jaghāna paramāstravit ।। nivṛttaṃ cābravīt kṛṣṇaṃ ratnaṃ dehīti lāṅgalī ।। dhikśabdapūrvam asakṛt pratyuvāca janārdanam ।। kṛtyaṃ na me dvārakayā na tvayā na ca vṛṣṇibhiḥ ।।
sarvakāmair upacitair maithilenābhipūjitaḥ ।। nānārūpān kratūn sarvān ājahāra nirargalān ।। syamantakakṛte prājño gāṃdīputro mahāyaśāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣāṇi dharmātmā yajñeṣu viniyojayat ।।
bahvannadakṣiṇāḥ sarve sarvakāmapradāyinaḥ ।। gadāśikṣāṃ tato divyāṃ balabhadrād avāptavān ।। ānīto dvārakām eva kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā ।। hatvā satrājitaṃ yuddhe sahabandhuṃ mahābalī ।।
śvaphalkatanayāyāṃ tu tārāyāṃ narasattamau । bhaṅgakārasya tanayau viśrutau ca mahābalau । jajñāte andhakamukhyasya śatrughno bandhumāṃś ca tau । varāt tu bhaṅgakārasya sa kṛṣṇapratimo abhavat । apayāte tadākrūre nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। tataḥ prasādayām āsur akrūraṃ kukurāndhakāḥ ।। pravavarṣa sahasrākṣaḥ kacche jalanidhes tadā ।।
akrūraḥ pradadau dhīmān prītyarthaṃ kurunandana ।। sabhāmadhyagataṃ prāha tam akrūraṃ janārdanaḥ ।। tat prayacchasva mānārha mayi mānāryakaṃ kṛthāḥ ।। sa saṃrūḍho asakṛtprāptas tataḥ kālātyayo mahān ।।
pradadau taṃ maṇiṃ babhrur akleśena mahāmatiḥ ।। dadau hṛṣṭamanāḥ kṛṣṇas taṃ maṇiṃ babhrave punaḥ ।। ābadhya gāṃdinīputro virarājāṃśumān iva ।। yas tv evaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ । sukhānāṃ tat sakalpānāṃ phalabhāgī bhaviṣyati । ā brahmabhavanāc cāpi yaśaḥkhyātir na saṃśayaḥ । bhaviṣyati naraśreṣṭha satyam etad bravīmi te । tataḥ sarve yaduvarā hṛṣṭāḥ prāñjalayas tadā । vavandire mahātmānaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ kamalalocanam ।
śrotum icchāmy aśeṣeṇa hareḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ ।। prādurbhāvaḥ purāṇeṣu viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ । satāṃ kathayatāṃ eva vārāha iti naḥ śrutam । na jāne tasya caritaṃ vidhiṃ naiva ca vistaram । na karmaguṇasaṃtānaṃ na hetuṃ na manīṣitam । kimātmako varāhaḥ sa kā mūrtiḥ kā ca devatā । kimācāraḥ prabhāvo vā kiṃ vā tena purā kṛtam । yajñārthaṃ samavetānāṃ miṣatāṃ ca dvijanmanām । mahāvarāhacaritaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyaneritam । yathā nārāyaṇo brahman vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ । daṃṣṭrayā gāṃ samudrasthāṃ ujjahārārisūdanaḥ । yā cāsya prakṛtir brahmaṃs tāṃ ca vyākhyātum arhasi ।। vasudevakule dhīmān vāsudevatvam āgataḥ ।।
devalokaṃ samutsṛjya martyalokam ihāgataḥ ।। kimarthaṃ divvyam ātmānaṃ mānuṣye saṃnyayojayat ।। mānuṣye sa kathaṃ buddhiṃ cakre cakrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।। sa kathaṃ gāṃ gato viṣṇur gopatvam agamad vibhuḥ ।।
śrīgarbhaḥ sa kathaṃ garbhe striyā bhūcarayā dhṛtaḥ ।। sthāpitā jagato mārgās trivargaprabhavās trayaḥ ।। lokam ekārṇavaṃ cakre dṛśyādṛśyena vartmanā ।। viṣāṇāgreṇa vasudhām ujjahārārisūdanaḥ ।।
dadau jitvā vasumatīṃ surāṇāṃ surasattamaḥ ।। pūrvadaityo mahāvīryo hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥ ।। pātālastho arṇavagataṃ papau toyamayaṃ haviḥ ।। sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ yam āhur vai yuge yuge ।।
ekārṇavagate loke tat paṅkajam apaṅkajam ।। garuḍasthena cotsiktaḥ kālanemir nipātitaḥ ।। nirjitaś ca mahādaityas tārakaś ca mahāsuraḥ । yaḥ śete śāśvataṃ yogam āsthāya timiraṃ mahat ।।
śakraṃ ca yo daityagaṇāvaruddhaṃ garbhāvasāne nakṛśaṃ cakāra ।। kṛtvā ca devāṃs tridivasya devāṃś cakre sureśaṃ puruhūtam eva ।। pātrāṇi dakṣiṇā dīkṣā camasolūkhalāni ca । agnim āhavanīyaṃ ca vedīṃ caiva kuśān sruvam ।।
arāṃs trīṇi ca yaś cakre havyakavyapradān makhe ।। bhāgārthe yajñavidhinā yogajño yajñakarmaṇi ।। sadasyāny ajamānāṃś ca medhādīṃś ca kratūttamān ।। yugānurūpaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā lokān anu parikraman ।।
muhūrtās tithayo māsā dinasaṃvatsarās tathā ।। āyuḥ kṣetrāṇy upacayo lakṣaṇaṃ rūpasauṣṭhavam ।। sṛṣṭā lokās trayo anantā yenānantyena vartmanā ।। gatāgatābhyāṃ yo netā tatreha ca vidhīśvaraḥ ।।
cāturvarṇyasya prabhavaś cāturvarṇyasya rakṣitā ।। digantaro nabhobhūto vāyur vāyuvibhāvanaḥ ।। yaḥ paraṃ śrūyate jyotir yaḥ paraṃ śrūyate tapaḥ ।। nārāyaṇaparā vedā nārāyaṇaparāḥ kriyāḥ ।
nārāyaṇaparo dharmo nārāyaṇaparā gatiḥ । nārāyaṇaparaṃ satyaṃ nārāyaṇaparaṃ tapaḥ । nārāyaṇaparo mokṣo nārāyaṇaparaṃ param । ādityādis tu yo divyo yaś ca daityāntako vibhuḥ ।।
setur yo lokasetūnāṃ medhyo yo medhyakarmaṇām ।। somabhūtaś ca bhūtānām agnibhūto agnivarcasām ।। vinayo nayavṛttānāṃ tejas tejasvinām api ।। vigraho vigrahārhāṇāṃ gatir gatimatām api ।।
devā hutāśanaprāṇāḥ prāṇo agner madhusūdanaḥ ।। māṃsāt tu medaso janma medaso asthi nirucyate ।। śukrād narbhaḥ samabhavad rasamūlena karmaṇā ।। garbhoṣmasaṃbhavo jñeyo dvitīyo rāśir ucyate ।।
bhāvau rasānugāv etau vīryaṃ ca śaśipāvakau ।। kaphasya hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ nābhyāṃ pittaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। nābhikaṇṭhāntarasthas tu tatra devo hutāśanaḥ ।। pittam agniḥ smṛtas tv evam agnīṣomamayaṃ jagat ।।
vāyuḥ praveśanaṃ cakre saṃgataḥ paramātmanā ।। tato aṅgāni visṛjati bibharti parivartayan । prāṇāpānau samānaś ca udāno vyāna eva ca ।। apānaḥ paścimaṃ kāyam udānordhvaṃ śarīriṇaḥ ।।
bhūtāvāptis tatas tasya jāyatendriyagocarā ।। tasyendriyāṇi śiṣṭāni svaṃ svaṃ yogaṃ pracakrire ।। chidrāṇy ākāśayonīni jalasrāvaḥ pravartate ।। grāmyāś ca viṣayāś caiva yasya vīryāt pravartitāḥ ।।
naidhane asmin kathaṃ loke naratvaṃ viṣṇur āgataḥ ।। kathaṃ gatir gatimatām āpanno mānuṣīṃ tanum ।। śrotum icchāmi viṣṇos tu vṛṣṇīnāṃ ca yathākramam ।। viṣṇor utpattim āścaryaṃ mamācakṣva mahāmune ।।
karmaṇāścaryabhūtasya viṣṇos tattvam ihocyatām ।। vyāpino devadevasya saṃbhavaṃ vaktum arhasi । yathāśakti tu vakṣyāmi śrūyatāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ ।। hanta viṣṇoḥ samastās tvaṃ śṛṇu divyāḥ pravṛttayaḥ ।।
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ sahasrakaram avyayam ।। sahasrayugaparyantaṃ sahasraparivatsaram । sahasraśatadhā bhūtvā pralayaṃ kārayet tu yaḥ । sahasradaṃ sahasrādiṃ sahasrabhujam avyayam ।। pātrāṇi ca pavitrāṇi vediṃ dīkṣāṃ caruṃ sruvam ।।
adhvaryuṃ sāmagaṃ vipraṃ sadasyaṃ sadanaṃ savam ।। prāgvaṃśaṃ yajñabhūmiṃ ca hotāraṃ cayanaṃ ca yat ।। prāyaścittāni cārghyaṃ ca sthaṇḍilāni kuśāṃs tathā ।। āhur vedavido viprā yaṃ yajñaṃ śāśvataṃ vibhum ।।
sarvayajñamukhaṃ devaṃ sarvayajñapravartinam । bhūyaś caiva bhaviṣyantīty evam āha pitāmahaḥ ।। kimarthaṃ bhagavān viṣṇur vasudevakule abhavat ।। sureśo ripusūdanaḥ ।devalokaṃ samutsṛjya ।
vāsudevasya māhātmyaṃ caritaṃ ca mahādyuteḥ ।। prādurbhāvāṃś ca vakṣyāmi puṇyān devaguṇair yutān ।। chāndasībhir udārābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ samalaṃkṛtān । śuciḥ prayatavāg bhūtvā nibodha janamejaya । idaṃ purāṇaṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiś ca saṃmitam । hanta te kathayiṣyāmi viṣṇor divyāṃ kathāṃ śṛṇu । yadā yadā hi dharmasya glānir bhavati bhārata । dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya tadā saṃbhavati prabhuḥ । tasya hy ekā mahārāja mūrtir bhavati sattama । nityaṃ diviṣṭhā yā rājaṃs tapaś carati duścaram । dvitīyā cāsya śayane nidrāyogam upāyayau । prajāsaṃhārasargārthaṃ kim adhyātmavicintakam । pūrṇe yugasahasre tu devadevo jagatpatiḥ ।।
pitāmaho lokapālāś candrādityau hutāśanaḥ । devāḥ saptarṣayaś caiva tryambakaś ca mahāyaśāḥ ।। vāyuḥ samudrāḥ śailāś ca tasya dehe samāśritāḥ । purāṇadevo atha purāṇi cakre pradīptavaiśvānaratulyatejāḥ ।।
naṣṭe devāsuranare pranaṣṭoragarākṣase ।। hatau prabhavatā tena tayor dattvāmitaṃ varam ।। puṣkare yatra saṃbhūtā devāḥ sarṣigaṇāḥ purā ।। purāṇaṃ kathyate yatra vedaśrutisamāhitam ।।
yatra viṣṇuḥ suraśreṣṭho vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ ।। mahīṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ saśailavanakānanām । agnijihvo darbhalomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ ।। ājyanāsaḥ sruvas tuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvano mahān ।।
prāyaścittanakho dhīraḥ paśujānur mahāvṛṣaḥ ।। vāyvantarātmā mantrasphig vikṛtaḥ somaśoṇitaḥ ।। prāgvaṃśakāyo dyutimān nānādīkṣābhir ācitaḥ ।। nānāchandogatipatho guhyopaniṣadāsanaḥ ।
chāyāpatnīsahāyo vai maṇiśṛṅga ivocchritaḥ ।। rasātalatale magnāṃ rasātalatalaṃ gataḥ । ekārṇavajale bhraṣṭām ekārṇavagatiḥ prabhuḥ ।। pūrvaṃ lokahitārthāya daṃṭrābhyām ujjahāra gām । tataḥ svasthānam ānīya pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīśvaraḥ । mumoca pūrvaṃ manasā dhārayitvā dharādharān । sadyo jagāma nirvāṇaṃ medinī tasya dhāraṇāt । cakāra ca namaskāraṃ tasmai devāya vedhase ।
sahasraśīrṣo devādiś cakāra jagatīṃ punaḥ ।। uddhṛtā pṛthivī devī sāgarāmbudharā purā ।। yatra bhūtvā mṛgendreṇa hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥ ।। daityānām ādipuruṣaś cakāra tapa uttamam ।।
jalopavāsas tasyāsīt sthānamaunadṛḍhavrataḥ ।। brahmā prītamanās tasya tapasā niyamena ca ।। vimānenārkavarṇena haṃsayuktena bhāsvatā ।। rudrair viśvasahāyaiś ca yakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥ ।।
nakṣatraiś ca muhūrtaiś ca khecaraiś ca mahāgrahaiḥ ।। rājarṣibhiḥ puṇyatamair gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ ।। brahmā brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho daityaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmam āpnuhi ।।
na mānuṣāḥ piśācā vā hanyur māṃ devasattama ।। śapeyus tapasā yuktā varam etaṃ vṛṇomy aham ।। na śuṣkeṇa na cārdreṇa syān na cānyena me vadhaḥ ।। pāṇiprahāreṇaikena sabhṛtyabalavāhanam । yo māṃ nāśayituṃ śaktaḥ sa me mṛtyur bhaviṣyati । nākāśe vā na bhūmau vā rātrau vā divase api vā । nāntar vā na bahir vāpi syād vadho me pitāmaha । paśubhir vā mṛgendrair vā pakṣibhir vā sarīsṛpaiḥ ।
salilaṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca nakṣatrāṇi diśo daśa ।। dhanadaś ca dhanādhyakṣo yakṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣādhipaḥ ।। evam uktas tu daityena svayaṃbhur bhagavāṃs tadā । uvāca daityarājaṃ taṃ prahasan nṛpasattama । na divā na ca rātrau vā na me mṛtyur bhaviṣyati । sarvān kāmān imāṃs tāta prāpsyasi tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
vairājaṃ brahmasadanaṃ brahmarṣigaṇasevitam ।। śrutvā devā varaṃ taṃ ca dattaṃ salilayoninā । vibhuṃ vijñāpayām āsur devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ । varapradānaṃ śrutvaiva pitāmaham upasthitāḥ ।। tat prasīdasva bhagavan vadho asya pravicintyatām ।।
sraṣṭā ca havyakavyānām avyaktaḥ prakṛtir dhruvaḥ ।। provāca bhagavān vākyaṃ sarvān devagaṇāṃs tadā ।। tapaso ante asya bhagavān vadhaṃ viṣṇuḥ kariṣyati ।। svāni sthānāni divyāni jagmus te vai mudā yutāḥ ।।
hiraṇyakaśipur daityo varadānena darpitaḥ ।। satyadharmaratān dāntān purā dharṣitavāṃs tu saḥ ।। trailokyaṃ vaśam ānīya svarge vasati dānavaḥ ।। yajñiyān akarod daityān ayajñīyāś ca devatāḥ ।।
maruto apsarasaś caiva gandharvā brahmaviddvijāḥ । ṛṣināgāḥ suparṇāś ca ye cānye apy evamādayaḥ । śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇum upatasthur mahābalam ।। nārāyaṇaṃ vibhuḥ devāḥ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇyaṃ gatāḥ ।।
tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo dhātā brahmādīnāṃ surottama ।। kṣayāya ditivaṃśasya śaraṇaṃ tvaṃ bhavasva naḥ ।। tathaiva tridivaṃ devāḥ pratipadyata māciram ।। avadhyam amarendrāṇāṃ dānavendraṃ nihanmi tam ।।
hiraṇyakaśipo rājann ājagāma hariḥ sabhām ।। sabhāṃ hiraṇyakaśipor jagāma harir īśvaraḥ । nārasiṃhena vapuṣā pāṇiṃ saṃspṛśya pāṇinā ।। jīmūtaghanadīptaujā jīmūta iva vegavān ।।
devādir ditijān vīro nṛsiṃhaḥ samupādravat । samutpatya nakhais tīkṣṇair vidārya nihato yudhi । dṛptair daityagaṇair guptaṃ hatavān ekapāṇinā ।। yatra vāmanam āśritya rūpaṃ daityavināśanam ।। vikramais tribhir akṣobhyāḥ kṣobhitās te mahāsurāḥ ।।
vegavān ketumān ugraḥ sogravyagro mahāsuraḥ ।। prahrādo aśvaśirāḥ kumbhaḥ saṃhrādo gaganapriyaḥ ।। vepanaś ca mahārathaḥ । bṛhatkīrtir mahājihvaḥ ।
śarabhaḥ śalabhaś caiva kupanaḥ kopanaḥ krathaḥ ।। dīrghajihvo arkanayano mṛdupādo mṛdupriyaḥ ।। candrahantā krodhahantā krodhavardhana eva ca ।। gariṣṭhaś ca variṣṭhaś ca pralambanarakāv ubhau ।।
asilomā pulomā ca bāṣkalaḥ pramado madaḥ ।। ekākṣaś candrahā rāhuḥ saṃhrādaḥ sṛmaraḥ svanaḥ ।। aśmayantrāyudhopetā bhiṇḍipālāyudhās tathā ।। pāśamudgarahastā vai tathā laguḍapāṇayaḥ ।।
nānāpraharaṇā ghorā nānāveṣā mahājavāḥ ।। kharoṣṭravadanāś caiva varāhavadanās tathā ।। ākhudarduravaktrāś ca ghorā vṛkamukhās tathā ।। nakrameṣānanāḥ śūrā gojāvimahiṣānanāḥ ।।
garuḍānanāḥ khaḍgamukhā mayūravadanās tathā ।। cīrasaṃvṛtagātrāś ca tathā valkalavāsasaḥ ।। nānāveṣadharā daityā nānāmālyānulepanāḥ ।। kramamāṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśam upāvartanta sarvaśaḥ ।।
rūpaṃ kṛtvā mahābhīṃaṃ jahārāśu sa medinīm ।। nabhaḥ prakramamāṇasya nābhyāṃ kila samāsthitau ।। viṣṇor amitavīryasya vadanty evaṃ dvijātayaḥ ।। dadau śakrāya vasudhāṃ viṣṇur balavatāṃ varaḥ ।।
vedavidbhir dvijair etat kathyate vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ ।। dattātreya iti khyātaḥ kṣamayā parayā yutaḥ ।। cāturvarṇye ca saṃkīrṇe dharme śithilatāṃ gate ।। prajāsu śīryamāṇāsu dharme cākulatāṃ gate ।।
cāturvarṇyam asaṃkīrṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tena mahātmanā ।। varadena varo datto dattātreyeṇa dhīmatā ।। śatāni daśa bāhūnāṃ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। durnirīkṣyo arivṛndānāṃ yuddhasthaś ca bhaviṣyasi ।।
kathito vai mahārāja yathāśrutam ariṃdama । bhūyaś ca jāmadagnyo ayaṃ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ ।। rāmo arjunam anīkasthaṃ jaghāna nṛpatiṃ prabhuḥ ।। dharṣayitvā yathākāmaṃ krośamānaṃ ca meghavat ।।
paraśvadhena dīptena jñātibhiḥ sahitasya vai ।। triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ pṛthivī tena niḥkṣatriyā kṛtā ।। sarvapāpavināśāya vājimedhena ceṣṭavān ।। mārīcāya dadau prītaḥ kaśyapāya vasuṃdharām ।।
dadau tasmin mahāyajñe vājimedhe mahāyaśāḥ ।। tiṣṭhate devavac chrīmān mahendre parvatottame ।। kṛṣṇājinottarīyaṃ ca jaṭāmakuṭamaṇḍalī । jāmadagnya iti khyātaḥ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ ।।
jajñe daśarathasyātha putraḥ padmāyatekṣaṇaḥ ।। loke rāma iti khyātas tejasā bhāskaropamaḥ ।। tam apy āhur manuṣyendraṃ sarvabhūtapates tanum ।। vadhārthaṃ devaśatrūṇāṃ durdharāṇi surair api ।।
nihatau ca nirāśau ca kṛtau tena mahātmanā ।। bhagnaṃ māheśvaraṃ cāpaṃ krīḍatā līlayā purā ।। lakṣmaṇānucaro rāmaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। pūrvocitatvādyā lakṣmīr bhartāram anugacchati ।।
janasthāne vasan kāryaṃ tridaśānāṃ cakāra saḥ ।। jaghāna puruṣavyāghrau gandharvau śāpavikṣatau ।। surendravajrāśanitulyasāraiḥ śaraiḥ śarīreṣu viyojitau balāt ।। vālī vinihataḥ saṃkhye sugrīvaś cābhiṣecitaḥ ।।
yatrāvadhyaṃ rākṣasendraṃ rāvaṇaṃ yudhi durjayam ।। trailokyarāvaṇaṃ krūraṃ rākṣasaṃ rākṣaseśvaram ।। durnirīkṣyaṃ suragaṇair varadānena darpitam ।। mahābhraghanasaṃkāśaṃ mahākāyaṃ mahābalam ।।
sabhrātṛputrasacivaṃ sasainyaṃ krūraniścayam । rāvaṇaṃ nijaghānāśu rāmo bhūtapatiḥ purā ।। samare yuddhaśauṇḍena tathānye cāpi rākṣasāḥ ।। daśāśvamedhāñ jārūthyān ājahāra nirargalān ।।
na vittaharaṇaṃ cāsīd rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। sarvam āsīj jagaddāntaṃ rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। na ca sma vṛddhā bālānāṃ pretakāryāṇi kurvate ।। śūdrāś caiva hi varṇāṃs trīñ śuśrūṣanty anahaṃkṛtāḥ ।।
rāma eko abhavad bhartā rāmaḥ pālayitābhavat ।। arogāḥ prāṇinaś cāsan rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। pṛthivyāṃ sahavāso abhūd rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। rāmo rāmo rāma iti prajānām abhavat kathāḥ । rāmārāmaṃ jagadbhūtaṃ rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।
rāme nibaddhās tattvārthā māhātmyaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ ।। ājānabāhuḥ sumukhaḥ siṃhaskandho mahābhujaḥ ।। ayodhyādhipatir bhūtvā rāmo rājyam akārayat ।। avyucchinno abhavad rāṣṭre dīyatāṃ bhujyatām iti ।।
ati sūryaṃ ca candraṃ ca rāmo dāśarathir babhau ।। hitvāyodhyāṃ divaṃ yāto rāghavo asaumahābalaḥ ।। rāvaṇaṃ sagaṇaṃ hatvā divam ācakrame prabhuḥ ।। vikhyāto māthure kalpe sarvalokahitāya vai ।।
ariṣṭaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ keśiṃ pūtanāṃ daityadārikām ।। daityān mānuṣadehasthān sūdayām āsa vīryavān ।। narakaś ca hataḥ saṃkhye yavanaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। durācārāś ca nihatāḥ pārthivā ye mahītale ।।
navame dvāpare viṣṇur aṣṭāviṃśe purābhavat । vedavyāsas tadā jajñe jātūkarṇyapuraḥsaraḥ । eko vedaś caturdhā tu kṛtas tena mahātmanā । janito bhārato vaṃśaḥ satyavatyāḥ sutena ca । atītāḥ kathitā rājan kathyante cāpy anāgatāḥ । kalkī viṣṇuyaśā nāma bhūyaś cotpatsyate prabhuḥ ।। saṃbhalagrāmako dvijaḥ । sarvalokahitārthāya । daśamo bhāvyasaṃpanno yājñavalkyapuraḥsaraḥ । kṣapayitvā ca tān sarvān bhāvinārthena coditān । gaṅgāyamunayor madhye niṣṭhāṃ prāpsyati sānugaḥ । tataḥ kāle vyatīte tu sāmātye sahasainike । nṛpeṣv atha pranaṣteṣu tadā tv apragrahāḥ prajāḥ ।। kṣaṇena nirvṛte caiva hatvā cānyonyam āhave । parasparahṛtasvāś ca nirākrandāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ । evaṃ kaṣṭam anuprāptāḥ kalisaṃdhyāṃśake tadā । prajāḥ kṣayaṃ prayāsyanti sārdhaṃ kaliyugena ha । kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmiṃs tataḥ kṛtayugaṃ punaḥ । prapatsyate yathānyāyaṃ svabhāvād eva nānyathā । anukarṣan sa vai senāṃ hastyaśvarathasaṃkulām । pragṛhītāyudhair viprair vṛtaḥ śatasahasraśaḥ । niḥśeṣāñ śuddharājāṃs tāṃs tadā sa tu kariṣyati । pāṣaṇḍān mlecchajātīṃś ca dasyūṃś caiva sahasraśaḥ । nātyarthaṃ dhārmikā ye ca ye ca dharmadviṣaḥ kvacit । udīcyā madhyadeśasthāḥ pārvatīyās tathaiva ca । prācyān pratīcyāṃś ca tathā vindhyapṛṣṭhaparānugān । tathaiva dākṣiṇātyāṃś ca draviḍān siṃhalaiḥ saha । gāndhārān pāradāṃś caiva pahlavān yavanāñ śakān । tukhārān barbarāṃś caiva śvānikān daradān khaśān । lambakāṃś ca maruṃdhāṃś ca kirātāṃś caiva sa prabhuḥ । pravṛttacakro balavān dasyūn āmantako balī । adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ pṛthivīṃ vicariṣyati । mānuṣaḥ sa tu saṃjajñe devasyāgrasya dhīmataḥ । pūrvajanmani viṣṇuḥ sa pramatir nāma vīryavān । gātreṇa vai candramasaḥ pūrṇe kaliyuge abhavat । ity etā vāsudevasya daśa saṃbhūtayaḥ smṛtāḥ । taṃ taṃ kālaṃ ca kāryaṃ ca taṃ tathoddeśakāriṇam । aṃśena triṣu lokeṣu tāṃs tān yonīn viśaty api । pañcaviṃśotthitaḥ kalkī pañcāśaccharadāṃ samāḥ । vinighnan sarvabhūtāni mānuṣāṃś caiva sarvaśaḥ । kṛtvā bījāvaśeṣāṃ tu mahīṃ krūreṇa karmaṇā । saṃyodhayitvā ca khalān prāyas tān apy adhārmikān । tad eṣa vai tadā kalkī caritārthaḥ sasainikaḥ । prajānāṃ sādhayitvā ca saṃsiddhārthaḥ punaḥ svayam । vṛthānyonyaṃ prakupitān saṃhariṣyati mohitān । purāṇi hatvā grāmāṃś ca tadā duṣpragrahāḥ prajāḥ । pranaṣṭaśrutidharmāś ca naṣṭavarṇāśramās tathā । hvasvā alpāyuṣaś caiva bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge । saritparvatasevinyaḥ patramūlaphalāśanāḥ । cīrapatrājinadharā gahvaraṃ ghoram āśritāḥ । alpāyuṣo naṣṭavārtā bahubādhāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ ।
prādurbhāvāḥ purāṇeṣu gīyante brahmavādibhiḥ ।। purāṇaṃ vartate yatra vedaśrutisamāhitam ।। kīrtitaṃ kīrtanīyasya sarvalokaguroḥ prabhoḥ ।। viṣṇor amitavīryasya yaḥ śṛṇoti kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto dhanaputrapaśūṃl labhet । nāśubhaṃ vidyate tasya putravān dyutimān bhavet । ṛddhiṃ samṛddhiṃ vipulāṃś ca bhogān prāpnoti śīghraṃ bhagavatprasādāt ।। vaikuṇṭhatvaṃ ca deveṣu kṛṣṇatvaṃ mānuṣeṣu ca ।। saṃpratyatītāṃ bhāvyāṃ ca śṛṇu rājan yathātatham ।।
nārāyaṇo hy anantātmā prabhavo avyaya eva ca ।। brahmā śakraś ca somaś ca dharmaḥ śukro bṛhaspatiḥ ।। eṣa viṣṇur iti khyāta indrād avarajo abhavat ।। vadhārthaṃ suraśatrūṇāṃ daityadānavarakṣasām ।।
so asṛjat pūrvapuruṣaḥ purākalpe prajāpatīn ।। tebhyo abhavan mahātmabhyo bahudhā brahma śāśvatam ।। kīrtitaṃ kīrtanīyasya kīrtyamānaṃ nibodha me ।। āsīt trailokyavikhyātaḥ saṃgrāmas tārakāmayaḥ ।।
ghnanti devān sagandharvān sayakṣoragacāraṇān ।। trātāraṃ manasā jagmur devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।। sārkacandragrahagaṇaṃ chādayanto nabhastalam ।। anyonyavegābhihatāḥ pravavuḥ sapta mārutāḥ ।।
rarāsa ghorair utpātair dahyamānam ivāmbaram ।। nyubjāni ca vimānāni prapatanty utpatanti ca ।। arūpavanti rūpāṇi tasminn utpātalakṣaṇe ।। timiraughaparikṣiptā na rejuś ca diṣo daśa ।।
dyaur na bhāty abhibhūtārkā ghoreṇa tamasā vṛtā ।। vapuḥ saṃdarśayām āsa divyaṃ kṛṣṇavapur hariḥ ।। tejasā vapuṣā caiva kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇam ivācalam ।। dhūmāndhakāravapuṣaṃ yugāntāgnim ivotthitam ।।
cāmīkarakarāsaktam āyudhair upaśobhitam ।। nandakānanditakaraṃ śarāśīviṣadhāriṇam ।। viṣṇuśailaṃ kṣamāmūlaṃ śrīvṛkṣaṃ śārṅgaśṛṅgiṇam ।। candrārkacakraracite mandarākṣadhṛtāntare ।।
tārakācitrakusume grahanakṣatravandhure ।। dadṛśus te sthitaṃ devaṃ divyalokamaye rathe ।। jayaśabdaṃ puraskṛtya śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। tuṣṭuvuś ca jagannāthaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim । jaya deva jagannātha jaya deva janārdana । jaya deva prabho viṣṇo jaya śaṅkhagadādhara । namas tubhyaṃ hṛṣīkeśa namo deva janārdana । ādideva jagannātha bhūtabhāvanabhāvana । namas tubhyaṃ prabho viṣṇo bhūtādipataye namaḥ । nama ādyāya bījāya puruṣāya namo namaḥ । namo astu te jagannātha namo bhūyo mahātmane । kiṃ vānena jagannātha namaskāreṇa keśava । rakṣa naḥ sakalān devān daityapāśavipāśitān ।
manaś cakre vināśāya dānavānāṃ mahāmṛdhe ।। uvāca devatāḥ sarvāḥ sapratijñam idaṃ vacaḥ ।। jitā me dānavāḥ sarve trailokyaṃ pratigṛhyatām ।। devāḥ prītiṃ parāṃ jagmuḥ prāpyevāmṛtam uttamam ।।
pravavuś ca śivā vātāḥ prasannāś ca diśo daśa ।। dīptimanti ca tejāṃsi cakrur arkaṃ pradakṣiṇam ।। virajaskā babhur mārgā nākamārgādayas trayaḥ ।। āsañ śubhānīndriyāṇi narāṇām antarātmasu ।।
yajñeṣu ca haviḥ svādu śivam āpa ca pāvakaḥ ।। sarve lokā mudānvitāḥ । babhūvur adhikāś caiva । prītyā paramayā yuktā devadevasya bhūpateḥ ।
viṣṇor dattapratijñasya śrutvārinidhane giram ।। nihanmi dānavāndṛptān yuṣmākaṃ vigrahaiḥ saha । giraṃ te dānavān ugrān menire nihatān yudhi । udyogaṃ vipulaṃ cakrur yuddhāya yudhi durjayāḥ ।। catuścakraṃ suvapuṣaṃ sukalpitamahāyudham ।।
racitaṃ ratnajālaiś ca hemajālaiś ca śobhitam ।। divyāstratūṇīradharaṃ payodharanināditam ।। gadāparighasaṃpūrṇaṃ mūrtimantam ivārṇavam ।। sapatākadhvajodagraṃ sādityam iva mandaram ।।
yuktam ṛkṣasahasreṇa sahasrāmbudanāditam ।। atiṣṭhat samarākāṅkṣī meruṃ dīpta ivāṃśumān ।। śailotkarimasaṃkāśaṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam ।। timirodgārikiraṇaṃ garjantam iva toyadam ।।
āyasaiḥ parighaiḥ pūrṇaṃ kṣepaṇīyaiś ca mudgaraiḥ ।। śobhitaṃ trāsanīyaiś ca tomaraiḥ saparaśvadhaiḥ ।। yuktaṃ kharasahasreṇa so adhyārohad rathottamam ।। pramukhe tasya sainyasya dīptaśṛṅga ivācalaḥ ।।
syandanaṃ vāhayām āsa sapatnānīkamardanam ।। varāhaḥ pramukhe tasthau sāvaroha ivācalaḥ ।। sphuraddantauṣṭhavadanaḥ saṃgrāmaṃ so abhyakāṅkṣata ।। vyūhito dānavair vyūhaiḥ paricakrāma vīryavān ।।
śvetaśailapratīkāśo yuddhāyābhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।। yuddhāyātiṣṭhad āyasto dharādhara ivāparaḥ ।। abhavad daityasainyasya madhye ravir ivoditaḥ ।। daityavyūhagato bhāti sanīhāra ivāṃśumān ।।
pramukhe devasenāya rarāja girisaṃnibhaḥ । hasaṃs tiṣṭhati daityānāṃ pramukhe sumukho grahaḥ ।। siṃhavyāghragatāś cānye varāharkṣagatāḥ pare ।। nānāpakṣigatāḥ kecit kecit pavanavāhanāḥ ।।
ekapādā dvipādāś ca nanṛtur yuddhakaṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। dṛptaśārdūlanirghoṣā nedur dānavapuṃgavāḥ ।। bāhubhiḥ parighākārais tarjayanti sma dānavāḥ ।। cikrīḍus te śataghnībhiḥ śitadhāraiś ca mudgaraiḥ ।।
cakraiś ca daityapravarāś cakrur ānanditaṃ balam ।। kāṅkṣanto vijayaṃ yuddhe dānavā yuddhadurmadāḥ । devān abhimukhaṃ tasthau meghānīkam ivoddhatam ।। balaṃ raṇaughābhyudayābhyudīrṇaṃ yuyutsayonmattam ivābabhāse ।।
surāṇāṃ sarvasainyasya vistaraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ śṛṇu ।। sabalāḥ sānugāś caiva saṃnahyanta yathākramam ।। grāmaṇīḥ sarvadevānām āruroha suradvipam ।। sucārucakracaraṇo hemavajrapariṣkṛtaḥ ।।
dīptimadbhiḥ sadasyaiś ca brahmarṣibhir abhiṣṭutaḥ ।। gupto balāhakagaṇaiḥ parvatair iva kāmagaiḥ ।। havir dhāneṣu gāyanti viprā makhamukhe sthitāḥ ।। indraṃ samupanṛtyanti śataśo hy apsarogaṇāḥ ।।
yukto hayasahasreṇa manomārutaraṃhasā ।। kṛtsnaḥ parivṛto merur bhāskarasyeva tejasā ।। tasthau suragaṇānīke daityān nādena bhīṣayan ।। śaṅkhamuktāṅgadadharo bibhrat toyamayaṃ vapuḥ ।।
śaṅkhamuktāmalatanuḥ śītībhūto ayam ambupaḥ । vāyvīritajalodgāraiḥ kurvaṃl līlāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। maṇiśyāmottamavapur hārabhārārpitodaraḥ ।। varuṇaḥ pāśahastaḥ san devānīke vyatiṣṭhata ।
yuddhavelām abhilaṣan bhinnavela ivārṇavaḥ ।। maṇiśyāmottamavapuḥ kubero naravāhanaḥ । rājarājeśvaraḥ śrīmān gadāpāṇir adṛśyata ।। prekṣamāṇaḥ śivasakhaḥ sākṣād iva śivaḥ svayam ।।
kṣaumavāsāḥ śivaḥ sākṣāc chivarūpaḥ svayaṃ svayam । varuṇaḥ paścimaṃ pakṣam uttaraṃ naravāhanaḥ ।। svāṃ svāṃ diśaṃ rarakṣus te tasya devabalasya ha ।। śriyā jājvalyamānena dīpyamānaiś ca raśmibhiḥ ।।
tridivadvāracitreṇa tapatā lokam avyayam ।। cacāra madhye devānāṃ dvādaśātmā dineśvaraḥ ।। himatoyaprapūrṇābhir bhābhir āplāvayañ jagat ।। śaśacchāyāṅkitatanuṃ naiśasya tamasaḥ kṣayam ।।
oṣadhīnāṃ paritrāṇaṃ nidhānam amṛtasya ca ।। dadṛśur dānavāḥ somaṃ himapraharaṇaṃ sthitam ।। saptaskandhagato lokāṃs trīn dadhāra cacāra ca ।। saptasvaragatā yasya yonir gībhir udīryate ।।
yam āhur ākāśagamaṃ śīghragaṃ śabdayoninam ।। pravavau vyathayan daityān pratilomaḥ satoyadaḥ ।। cikrīḍur asibhiḥ śubhrair nirmuktair iva pannagaiḥ ।। yakṣaiś ca sumahābhogaiḥ pannagair garuḍair api ।
śarabhūtāḥ surendrāṇāṃ cerur vyāttamukhā divi ।। upatasthuḥ suragaṇān prahartuṃ dānavaṃ balam ।। kṛṣṇavartmā yugāntābho viśvasya jagataḥ prabhuḥ ।। bhūmyāpovyomabhūtātmā syāmaḥ śāntikaro arihā ।।
jagayonir jagadbījo jagadgurur udāradhīḥ । saparīveṣam udyantaṃ savitur maṇḍalaṃ yathā ।। kareṇa kālīṃ vapuṣā śatrukālapradāṃ gadām ।। dadhārāyudhajātāni śārṅgādīni mahāyaśāḥ ।।
pavanādhikasaṃpātaṃ gaganakṣobhaṇaṃ khagam ।। amṛtārambhanirmuktaṃ mandarādrim ivocchritam ।। mahendreṇāmṛtasyārthe vajreṇa kṛtalakṣaṇam ।। vicitrapatravasanaṃ dhātumantam ivācalam ।।
tīkṣṇatuṇḍogranakharaṃ calatpakṣasamākulam । bhogibhogāvasaktena maṇiratnena bhāsvatā ।। yugānte sendracāpābhyāṃ toyadābhyām ivāmbaram ।। ketuveṣapraticchannaṃ mahākāyaniketanam ।।
sthitaḥ samaradurjeyo daityasainyaṃ vilokayan । suparṇaḥ svena vapuṣā suparṇaṃ khecarottamam ।। dahaṃs tasthau surānīke daityān ativibhīṣayan । gīrbhiḥ paramamantrābhis tuṣṭuvuś ca gadādharam ।।
namas te astu hṛṣīkeśa jahi daityabalaṃ vibho । namas trimūrtaye tubhyaṃ haribrahmaśivātmane । namas traividyarūpāya ṛksāmayajuṣe namaḥ । namo astu yogicintyāya teṣāṃ yogapradāyine । namo vikalpaśūnyāya namo vijñaptirūpine । yaṃ ca jñānamayaṃ tejaḥ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ । taṃ natāḥ sma jagannāthaṃ jahi daityagaṇān hare । tvāṃ stotuṃ hi vayaṃ deva śaktā varṣaśatair api । na hi deva jagannātha jayasva puruṣottama । itīritāṃ giriṃ śrutvā gantum abhyudyato hariḥ । vārirājaparikṣiptaṃ devarājavirājitam ।। yayau hitaṃ devapathaṃ dīptabhāskaratejasam । pavanāviddhanirghoṣaṃ saṃpradīptahutāśanam ।।
balaṃ balavaduddhūtaṃ yuddhāya samavartata ।। svasty astv iti stuvaṃs tatra devān āṅgiraso abravīt । svasty astu daityebhya iti uśanā vākyam abravīt ।। svasti daityebhya iti cāpy uśanā vākyam ādade ।
surāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca parasparajayaiṣiṇām ।। sarvadevamayo yas tu sarvadharmamayas tu yaḥ । tasya viṣṇoḥ sureśasya tejasā vidhṛtāḥ surāḥ । sabalāḥ sānugāś caiva tridaśāś ca madotkaṭāḥ । prahartuṃ dānavaṃ sainyaṃ tarasā hi samabhyayuḥ । samīyur yudhyamānā vai parvatā iva parvataiḥ ।। dharmādharmasamāyuktaṃ darpeṇa vinayena ca ।।
utpatadbhiś ca gaganaṃ sāsihastaiḥ samantataḥ ।। cāpair visphāryamāṇaiś ca pātyamānaiś ca mudgaraiḥ ।। jagatas trāsajananaṃ yugasaṃvartakopamam ।। dānavāḥ samare jaghnur devān indrapurogamān ।।
viṣaṇṇamanaso devā jagmur ārtiṃ mahāmṛdhe ।। bhinnoraskā ditisutair vemū raktaṃ vraṇair bahu ।। praviṣṭā dānavīṃ māyāṃ na śekus te viceṣṭitum ।। balaṃ surāṇām asurair niṣprayatnāyudhaṃ kṛtam ।।
śakro daityabalaṃ ghoraṃ viveśa bahulocanaḥ ।। tāmasenāstrajālena tamobhūtam athākarot ।। ghoreṇa tamasāviṣṭāḥ puruhūtasya tejasā ।। vapūṃṣi daityasaṃghānāṃ tamobhūtāny apātayan ।।
petus te dānavagaṇāś chinnapakṣā ivācalāḥ ।। dānavaṃ devasadanaṃ tamobhūtam ivābabhau ।। yugāntoddyotajananīṃ sṛṣṭām aurveṇa vahninā ।। daityāś cādityavapuṣaḥ sadya uttasthur āhave ।।
bhejire candraviṣayaṃ śītāṃśusalilahradam ।। śaśaṃsur vajriṇe devāḥ saṃtaptāḥ śaraṇaiṣiṇaḥ ।। codito devarājena varuṇo vākyam abravīt ।। aurvaḥ pūrvaṃ sa tejasvī sadṛśo brahmaṇo guṇaiḥ ।।
upatasthur munigaṇā devā devarṣibhiḥ saha ।। ṛṣiṃ vijñāpayām āsa purā paramatejasam ।। ṛṣivaṃśeṣu bhagavañś chinnamūlam idaṃ kulam ।। kaumāraṃ vratam āsthāya kleśam evānuvartase ।।
ekadehāni tiṣṭhanti viviktāni vinā prajāḥ ।। bhavāṃs tu tapasā śreṣṭhaḥ prajāpatisamadyutiḥ ।। ādadhat svorjitaṃ tejo dvitīyāṃ kuru vai tanum ।। jagarhe tān ṛṣigaṇān vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।।
ārṣaṃ vai sevatāṃ karma vanyamūlaphalāśinaḥ ।। brahmacaryaṃ sucaritaṃ brahmāṇam api cālayet ।। asmākaṃ tu vanaṃ vṛttir vanyāśramanivāsinām ।। aśmakuṭṭā daśatapāḥ pañcasaptatapāś ca ye ।।
brahmacaryaṃ puraskṛtya prārthayanti parāṃ gatim ।। evam āhuḥ pare loke brahmacaryavido janāḥ ।। ye sthitā brahmacaryeṇa brāhmaṇā divi te sthitāḥ ।। nāsti loke yaśomūlaṃ brahmacaryāt paraṃ tapaḥ ।।
brahmacaryaṃ samādhatte kim ataḥ paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। brahmacaryaṃ ca caryā ca trayaṃ syād dambhasaṃjñitam ।। yad iyaṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā ।। mukhanetravikāreṇa sparśanair bhāṣaṇena ca ।
smaraṇaṃ sundarīṇāṃ ca manaso vikṛtiḥ purā । tasyām utpattim āsādya tasyāṃ bījaṃ ka āvehat । pāpātmā vikalo mūḍho bhavādṛśa iti śrutiḥ । smṛtvā brahmapadāt khinno dṛṣṭvā śukraṃ pramuñcati ।
sṛṣṭvā vidrāvayaty ātmā tasyāṃ bījaṃ ka āvahet । brahmacarye yadā bhūte bhaved yadi viniścayaḥ । prāṇino dadhati ke ratiṃ tato । yoṣitāṃ vapuṣi nirghṛṇe aśucau ।
brahmacaryam aparaṃ suniścitāḥ । kurmahe yad abhikāṅkṣitaṃ hṛdi । sṛjadhvaṃ mānasān putrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā ।। na dārayogaṃ bījaṃ vā vratamuktaṃ tapasvinām ।।
vyāhṛtaṃ sadbhir atyartham asadbhir iva me matam ।। dārayogaṃ vinā srakṣye putram ātmatanūruham ।। vanyenānena vidhinā didhakṣantam iva prajāḥ ।। mamanthaikena darbheṇa sutasya prabhavāraṇim ।।
jagato dahanākāṅkṣī putro agniḥ samapadyata ।। didhakṣann iva lokāṃs trīñ jajñe paramakopanaḥ ।। kṣudhā me bādhate tāta jagad dhakṣye tyajasva mām ।। nirdahan sarvabhūtāni vavṛdhe so antako analaḥ ।।
sarvalokapatiḥ prabhuḥ । ājagāma munir yatra vyasṛjat putram uttamam । sa dadarśorum ūrvasya dīpyamānaṃ sutāgninā । aurvakopāgnisaṃtaptāṃl lokāṃś ca ṛṣibhiḥ saha ।
tam uvāca tato brahmā । putredaṃ dhāryatāṃ tejo lokānāṃ kriyatāṃ dayā ।। tathyam etan mama vacaḥ śṛṇu tvaṃ vadatāṃ vara ।। bhojanaṃ cāsya dāsyāmi yena prīto bhaviṣyati ।
matim etāṃ dadātīha paramānugrahāya vai ।। bhagavaṃs tarpitaḥ putraḥ kair havyaiḥ prāpsyate sukham ।। vidhāsyati bhavān asya vīryatulyaṃ mahaujasaḥ ।। mama yonir jalaṃ vipra tac ca me toyapaṃ mukham ।।
taddhavis tava putrasya visṛjāmy ālayaṃ ca tat ।। sahitau vicariṣyāvo niṣprāṇanakarāv iha ।। dahanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sadevāsurarakṣasām ।। praviveśārṇavamukhaṃ nikṣipya pitari prabhām ।।
aurvasyāgneḥ prabhāvajñāḥ svāṃ svāṃ gatim upāśritāḥ ।। aurvaṃ praṇatasarvāṅgo vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha ।। tapasā te muniśreṣṭha parituṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। bhṛtya ity avagantavyaḥ ślāghyo asmi yadi karmaṇā ।।
yat sīdeyaṃ muniśreṣṭha tavaiva syātparājayaḥ ।। śiṣyo asmi te tapaḥśreṣṭha surebhyo me bhayaṃ nuda । nāsti te tapasānena bhayam adyeha suvrata ।। nirindhanām agnimayīṃ duḥsparśāṃ pāvakair api ।।
rakṣiṣyaty ātmapakṣaṃ ca parāṃś ca pradahiṣyati ।। jagāma tridivaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ kṛtārtho dānaveśvaraḥ ।। aurveṇa nirmitā pūrvaṃ pāvakenorvasūnunā ।। śāpo hy asyāḥ purā dattaḥ sṛṣṭā yenaiva tejasā ।।
tenāhaṃ saha saṃgamya yādobhiś ca samāhitaḥ । māyām etāṃ haniṣyāmi tvatprasādān na saṃśayaḥ ।। saṃdideśāgrataḥ somaṃ yuddhāya śiśirāyudham ।। asurāṇāṃ vināśāya jayārthaṃ ca divaukasām ।।
tvanmayaṃ sarvalokānāṃ rasaṃ rasavido viduḥ ।। parivartasy ahorātraṃ kālaṃ jagati yojayan ।। na viduḥ soma devāś ca ye ca nakṣatrayoginaḥ ।। tamaḥ protsārya vapuṣā bhāsayasy akhilaṃ jagat ।।
abdakṛt kālayogātmā ījyo yajñaraso avyayaḥ ।। śītāṃśur amṛtādhāraś capalaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ ।। saumyas tvaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ timiraghnas tvam ṛkṣarāṭ ।। śamayasvāsurīṃ māyāṃ yayā dahyāma saṃyuge ।।
eṣa varṣāmi śiśiraṃ daityamāyāpakarṣaṇam ।। vimāyān vimadāṃś caiva daityasaṃghān mahāhave ।। veṣṭayanti sma tān ghorān daityān meghagaṇā iva ।। jaghnatur himapātaiś ca pāśapātaiś ca dānavān ।।
mṛdhe ceratur ambhobhiḥ kṣubdhāv iva mahārṇavau ।। jagatsaṃvartakāmbhodaiḥ pravṛttair iva saṃvṛtam ।। tāṃ māyāṃ śamayām āstāṃ devau daiteyanirmitām ।। na śekuś calituṃ daityā viśiraskā ivādrayaḥ ।।
himaplāvitasarvāṅgā niruṣmāṇa ivāgrayaḥ ।। vimānāni vicitrāṇi prapatanty utpatanti ca ।। mayo dadarśa māyāvī dānavān divi dānavaḥ ।। pādapotkaṭakūṭāgrāṃ kandarākīrṇakānanām ।।
īhāmṛgagaṇākīrṇāṃ pavanāghūrṇitadrumām ।। prathitāṃ pārvatīṃ māyāṃ sasṛje sa samantataḥ ।। nijaghne devasaṃghāṃs tān dānavāṃś cāpy ajīvayat ।। aśmabhiś cāyasaghanaiḥ kiraddevagaṇān raṇe ।।
abhavad dyaur asaṃhāryā pṛthivī parvatair iva ।। nāniruddho drumagaṇair devo adṛśyata saṃyuge ।। niṣprayatnaṃ surānīkaṃ varjayitvā gadādharam ।। sahiṣṇutvāj jagatsvāmī na cukrodha gadādharaḥ ।।
devāsuravimardaṃ sa draṣṭukāmo janārdanaḥ ।। māyāyā mayasṛṣṭāyāḥ pravṛddhāyāḥ śamāya vai । tataḥ pravṛddhāv anyonyaṃ pravṛddhajvālaveginau । coditau viṣṇuvākyena tau māyām apakarṣatām ।।
dagdhā sā pārvatī māyā bhasmabhūtā nanāśa ha ।। daityasenāṃ dadahatur yugānteṣv iva mūrcchitau ।। ceratur dānavānīke krīḍantāv anilānalau ।। dānavānāṃ vimāneṣu vimāneṣu samantataḥ ।।
māyāvadhe vinirvṛtte stūyamāne gadādhare ।। saṃprahṛṣṭeṣu deveṣu sādhu sādhv iti sarvaśaḥ ।। dikṣu sarvāsu śuddhāsu pravṛtte dharmasaṃstare ।। prakṛtistheṣu lokeṣu nṛṣu cāritrabandhuṣu ।।
virājamānā devās tu tato munigaṇaiḥ saha । yajñaśobhiṣu deveṣu svargārthaṃ darśayatsu ca ।। bhāve tapasi śuddhānām abhāve pāpakarmaṇām ।। tripādavigrahe dharme adharme pādavigrahe ।।
svadharmastheṣu varṇeṣu loke asminn āśrameṣu ca ।। gīyamānāsu gāthāsu devasaṃstavanādiṣu । praśāntakalmaṣe loke śānte tamasi dāruṇe ।। tanmayā vimalā lokās tābhyāṃ jayakṛtakriyāḥ ।।
kālanemir iti khyāto dānavaḥ pratyadṛśyata ।। mandarotkīrṇasaṃkāśo mahārajatasaṃvṛtaḥ ।। kakṣe mahati saṃvṛddho nidāgha iva pāvakaḥ ।। trailokyāntaravistāri dhārayan vipulaṃ vapuḥ ।।
īrayan mukhaniḥśvāsair vṛṣṭimanto balāhakān ।। didhakṣantam ivāyāntaṃ sarvān devagaṇān mṛdhe ।। saṃvartakāle tṛṣitaṃ dṛptaṃ mṛtyum ivotthitam ।। lambābharaṇapūrṇena kiṃcic calitavarmaṇā ।।
dānavān devanihatān uttiṣṭhata iti bruvan ।। vīkṣanti sma surāḥ sarve bhayavitrastalocanāḥ ।। trivikrame vikramantaṃ nārāyaṇam ivāparam ।। prākrāmadasuro yuddhe trāsayan sarvadevatāḥ ।।
kālanemir babhau daityaḥ saviṣṇur iva mandaraḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā kālam ivāyāntaṃ kālanemiṃ bhayāvaham ।। vyavardhata mahātejās tapānte jalado yathā ।। uttasthur apariśrāntāḥ prāpyevāmṛtam uttamam ।।
tārakāmayasaṃgrāme satataṃ jitakāśinaḥ । rejur āyodhanagatā dānavā yuddhakaṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। prekṣatāṃ cābhavat prītir dānavaṃ kālaneminam ।। te'pi sarve bhayaṃ tyaktvā hṛṣṭā yoddhum upasthitāḥ ।।
vipracittisutaḥ śvetaḥ kharalambāv ubhāv api ।। svarbhānuś cāmaraprakhyo vaktrayodhī mahāsuraḥ ।। dānavāḥ kṛtino jagmuḥ kālaneminam uttamam ।। kālakalpaiś ca musalaiḥ kṣepaṇīyaiś ca mudgaraiḥ ।।
paṭṭisair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca parighaiś cottamāyasaiḥ ।। yugair yantraiś ca nirmuktair argalaiś cāgratāḍitaiḥ ।। dānavā yuddhadurdharṣāḥ saṃgrāmamukhataḥ sthitāḥ । sarpair lelihyamānaiś ca visarpadbhiś ca sāyakaiḥ ।।
vikośaiś cāsibhis tīkṣṇaiḥ śūlaiś ca śitanirmalaiḥ ।। kālanemiṃ puraskṛtya tasthuḥ saṃgrāmamūrdhani ।। dyaur nimīlitanakṣatrā ghananīlāmbudāgame ।। dīptā śītoṣṇatejobhyāṃ candrabhāskaratejasā ।।
toyadāviddhavasanā grahanakṣatrahāsinī ।। saṃpradīptāgnipavanā nārāyaṇaparāyaṇā ।। rarājāstravatī bhīmā yakṣagandharvaśālinī ।। dvāvāpṛthivyoḥ saṃyogo yathā syād yugaparyaye ।।
kṣamāparākramamayaṃ darpasya vinayasya ca ।। pūrvāparābhyāṃ saṃrabdhāḥ sāgarābhyām ivāmbudāḥ ।। vanābhyāṃ pārvatīyābhyāṃ puṣpitābhyāṃ yathā gajāḥ ।। sa dyāṃ divaṃ bhuvaṃ caiva diśaś ca samapūrayat ।।
duṃdubhīnāṃ ca ninadā daityam antardadhuḥ svanam ।। babhañjur bāhubhir bāhūn dvaṃdvam anye yuyutsavaḥ ।। sasarjur ājau nistriṃśān gadā gurvīś ca dānavāḥ ।। paripetur bhṛśaṃ kecin nyubjāḥ kecic ca jajñire ।।
samīyus te susaṃrabdhā roṣād anyonyam āhave ।। rathā rathair nirudhyante padātāś ca padātibhiḥ ।। nabhaḥ svasvāna hi yathā nabhasye jaladasvanaiḥ ।। babhūvātha prasaktānāṃ nabhasīva payomucām ।
saṃbādham eke saṃprāpya na śekuś calituṃ rathāḥ ।। saṃhrādamānābharaṇā jaghnus tatrāsicarmiṇaḥ ।। kṣarajjalānāṃ sadṛśā jaladānāṃ samāgame ।। devadānavasaṃkṣubdhaṃ saṃkulaṃ yuddham ābabhau ।।
anyonyabāṇavarṣaṃ tad yuddhadurdinam ābabhau ।। vyavardhata samudraughaiḥ pūryamāṇa ivāmbudaḥ ।। gātrān nāgaśiraḥprakhyā viniṣpetur balāhakāḥ ।। sāgniniṣpeṣapavanā mukhān niścerur arciṣaḥ ।।
pañcāsyāḥ kṛṣṇavapuṣo lelihanta ivoragāḥ ।। divyam ākāśam āvavre parvatair ucchritair iva ।। saṃdhyātapagrastaśikhaḥ sākṣān merur ivācalaḥ ।। apātayad devagaṇān vajreṇeva mahāgirīn ।।
