na śekuś calituṃ devāḥ kālanemihatā yudhi ।। yakṣagandharvapatagāḥ petuḥ saha mahoragaiḥ ।। na śekur yatnavanto api yatnaṃ kartuṃ vicetasaḥ ।। jitvetthaṃ devatānīkaṃ gadām āvidhya dānavaḥ । airāvatagataṃ śakram uvācāsurasattamaḥ । āgacchāgaccha devendra nirjito asi mayā raṇe । adyaprabhṛti devendro na tvaṃ bhavasi vṛtrahan । eṣa te gadayā śakra śiro bhetsyāmi paśyataḥ ।। adyaprabhṛti devendro dānavendro aham acyuta । bhaviṣyāmi na saṃdeho hatvā tvām ugrapauruṣam । iti bruvāṇaṃ samare vṛtrahā vajram ādade । jaghāna tarasā śakro vajreṇa hi sa dānavam । vajraṃ tadvakṣasi prāpya bahudhā samapadyata ।। aśaktaṃ vajram āsīt tu dānavaṃ hantum ojasā । punaḥ papāta sahasā śakrasyaiva tadā karam । kālanemis tu sahasā gadām ādāya yatnataḥ । airāvatasya rabhasā jaghānaikaṃ sa mastakam । sa vinirbhinnakumbhas tu papāta dharaṇītale ।। sasrāva rudhiraṃ tīkṣṇaṃ gajarājas tadā balī । punaś ca gadayā rājaṃs tadā samaramūrdhani । jaghāna dānavendras tu vṛtrahantāram ojasā । utsṛjya sahasā śakro gajarājaṃ puraṃdaraḥ । bhinnavarmāsthinicayo mukhāc choṇitam udvaman ।। papātorvyāṃ mahārāja kiṃcid viśramya bhūtale । utsṛjya sahasā śakraḥ svargalokaṃ mahīpate । manuṣyalokaṃ saṃprāpya mānuṣīṃ tanum āvrajat ।
airāvatagataḥ saṃkhye calituṃ na śaśāka ha ।। nirvyāpāraḥ kṛtas tena vipāśo varuṇo mṛdhe ।। agnimārutayor nāśaṃ kṛtvā sa ditijeśvaraḥ । jaghāna devarājam ca somaṃ varuṇam aśvinau । ādityavasurudrādīn aśeṣāṃś ca divaukasaḥ । tato atīva prakurvīta āpo vasur amitrahā । kālanemiṃ jaghānājau śaktyā guha ivāparaḥ ।। śaktyā nirbhinnahṛdayo dhātumān iva parvataḥ । susrāva rudhiraṃ bhūmau kālanemir mahāsuraḥ । tato atikrodhatāmrākṣaḥ śaktim udyamya vegavān । svaśaktyā tāḍayām āsa vasum urvyāṃ papāta saḥ । dhanadaś ca kṛtāntaś ca varuṇaś ca śacīpatiḥ ।। ekadaiva nijaghnus te sāyudhair anibarhaṇaiḥ । nivārya tāni śastrāṇi tāñ jaghāna pṛthak pṛthak । yamena preṣitaṃ daṇḍaṃ jagṛhe sa mahāsuraḥ । taṃ dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve lokapālā mahaujasaḥ । jaghāna vajreṇa ruvā devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ ।। vajreṇa nihato daityo na cakampe girir yathā । punar vajreṇa taṃ daityam indro mārutavartmani । sthitas tadā jṛmbhaṇena jigīrṇe sāyudhaṃ hariḥ । praviveśa susūkṣmeṇa kukṣiṃ rūpeṇa vṛtrahā । tatkṣaṇād eva devendraḥ pārśvaṃ nirbhidya niryayau ।। kavacenābhiguptaḥ sa nārāyaṇamayena ca । tataḥ śūlam amoghaṃ tu śaṃkaro hantum ādade । prajāpatir uvācedaṃ mayā dattavaro balī । na śūlena na cānyena hantuṃ śakyo mahāsuraḥ । śūlaṃ etad amoghaṃ ca mā prayuñkṣva mahāsure ।। ity uktaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ sa saṃjahārāyudhaṃ svakam । etasminn antare devāḥ kālanemibhayāturāḥ । ūcuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ mahātmāno gīrbhiḥ stutvā janārdanam । mumucuḥ svāni śastrāṇi śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ । vilapaṃl lokapāleśas tyājito dhanadakriyām ।।
tadaiva lokapālāś ca nihatās tena saṃyugam । yāmyām avasthām amaro nītaḥ svāṃ diśam āviśat ।। lokapālās tu te sarve mānuṣīṃ tanum āsthitāḥ । vihāya svapadaṃ rājan vivadanti sma mānuṣe । dikṣu sarvāsu dehaṃ svaṃ caturdhā vidadhe tadā ।।
jahāra lakṣmīṃ somasya taṃ cāsya viṣayaṃ mahat ।। sāyanaṃ cāsya viṣayaṃ jahāra dinakarma ca ।। vāyuṃ ca tarasā jitvā cakārātmavaśānugam ।। cakārātmavaśe vīryād dehabhūtāś ca sindhavaḥ ।।
sthāpayām āsa jagatīṃ suguptāṃ dharaṇīdharaiḥ ।। sarvalokamayo daityaḥ sarvalokabhayāvahaḥ ।। pāvakānilasaṃghāto rarāja yudhi dānavaḥ ।। taṃ tuṣṭuvur daityagaṇā devā iva pitāmaham ।।
vedo dharmaḥ kṣamā satyaṃ śrīś ca nārāyaṇāśrayā ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ padam anvicchan yayau nārāyaṇāntikam ।। dānavānāṃ vināśāya bhrāmayantaṃ gadāṃ śubhām ।। svārūḍhaṃ svarṇapatrāḍhyaṃ śikhinaṃ kāśyapaṃ khagam ।।
dānavo viṣṇum akṣobhyaṃ babhāṣe kṣubdhamānasaḥ ।। arṇavāvāsinaś caiva madhor vai kaiṭabhasya ca ।। yena naḥ saṃyugeṣv adya bahavo dānavā hatāḥ ।। yena dānavanārīṇāṃ sīmantoddharaṇaṃ kṛtam ।।
ananto bhoginām apsu svayaṃbhūś ca svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।। asya krodhaṃ samāsādya hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥ ।। ājyaṃ maharṣibhir dattam aśnuvanti tridhā hutam ।। asya cakraṃ praviṣṭāni kulāny asmākam āhave ।।
savitus tejasā tulyaṃ cakraṃ kṣipati śatruṣu ।। atikrāntasya kālasya phalaṃ prāpsyati durmatiḥ ।। adya madbāṇaniṣpiṣṭo mayy eva praṇamiṣyati ।। imaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ hatvā dānavānāṃ bhayāvaham ।।
jātyantaragato hy eṣa mṛdhe bādhati dānavān ।। jaghānaikārṇave ghore tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhau ।। viniveśya svake ūrau nihatau dānaveśvarau । pitaraṃ me jaghānaiko hiraṇyakaśipuṃ purā ।।
yajñakāle baler yo vai kṛtvā vāmanarūpatām । trīṃl lokāṃś ca jahāraiṣa kramamāṇas tribhiḥ kramaiḥ ।। mayā saha samāgamya sadevo vinaśiṣyati ।। vāgbhir apratirūpābhir yuddham evābhyarocayat ।।
kṣamābalena manasā sasmitaṃ vākyam abravīt ।। hatas tvaṃ darpajair doṣaiḥ kṣamāṃ yo atītya bhāṣase ।। na tatra puruṣāḥ santi yatra garjanti yoṣitaḥ ।। prajāpatikṛtaṃ setuṃ ko bhittvā svastimān vrajet ।।
sveṣu sveṣu ca sthāneṣu sthāpayiṣyāmi devatāḥ ।। jahāsa dānavaḥ krodhād dhastāṃś cakre ca sāyudhān ।। krodhād rudhiraraktākṣo viṣṇor vakṣasy atāḍayat ।। udyatāyudhanistriṃśāḥ sarve viṣṇum abhidravan ।।
na cacāla harir yuddhe akampyamāna ivācalaḥ ।। mumoca jvalitāṃ ghorāṃ saṃrabdho garuḍopari ।। sa tena tāḍitaḥ pakṣī cacāla ca punaḥ punaḥ । hariṇā vardhitabalo na moham upagacchati ।
yena tasya suparṇasya patitā mūrdhni sā gadā ।। tadāgamat padā bhūmiṃ pakṣī vyathitavigrahaḥ । loṣṭaiḥ sarṣṭiśilābhiś ca vajrapraharaṇais tataḥ । jaghnus te samare viṣṇuṃ gopālaṃ ca mahāraṇe । bhramantaṃ ghūrṇamānaṃ ca stutiṃ devāḥ pracakrire । jaya deva mahābāho madhukaiṭabhanāśana । hiraṇyakaśipor vakṣo nakhalāṅgaladāraṇa । uttasthau ca raṇād viṣṇur amaraiḥ saṃstutaḥ purā । hataṃ viṣṇuṃ samājñāya śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau sa dānavaḥ । mṛdaṅgāṃś ca tridhā tatra vādayanto mahāsurāḥ । tālāśrayāś ca nanṛtur mahotsava ivābabhau । krodhāt saṃraktanayano vaikuṇṭhaś cakramādade ।। bhujāś cāsya vyavardhanta vyāpnuvanto diśo daśa ।।
vavṛdhe sa punar lokān krāntukāma ivaujasā ।। ṛṣayaḥ saha gandharvais tuṣṭuvur madhusūdanam ।। namo astu devadeveśa śaṅkhacakragadādhara । viṣṇo kṛṣṇa hṛṣīkeśa jahi daityaṃ mahābalam । namas tubhyaṃ virūpākṣa śaṃkarasya jagatpate । pāhi naḥ sakalān asmāñ jahi daityaṃ mahābalam । padbhyām ākramya vasudhāṃ diśaḥ pracchādya bāhubhiḥ ।।
dīptāgnisadṛśaṃ ghoraṃ darśanīyaṃ sudarśanam ।। medosthimajjārudhiraiḥ siktaṃ dānavasaṃbhavaiḥ ।। sragdāmamālāvitataṃ kāmagaṃ kāmarūpiṇam ।। maharṣiroṣair āviṣṭaṃ nityam āhavadarpitam ।।
kravyādāni ca bhūtāni tṛptiṃ yānti mahāmṛdhe ।। cakram udyasya samare krodhadīpto gadādharaḥ ।। ciccheda bāhūṃś cakreṇa śrīdharaḥ kālaneminaḥ ।। tasya daityasya cakreṇa pramamātha balād dhariḥ ।।
kabandhāvasthitaḥ saṃkhye viśākha iva pādapaḥ ।। urasā pātayām āsa garuḍaḥ kālaneminam ।। nipapāta divaṃ tyaktvā kṣobhayan dharaṇītalam ।। sādhu sādhv iti vaikuṇṭhaṃ sametāḥ pratyapūjayan ।।
te sarve bāhubhir vyāptā na śekuś calituṃ raṇe ।। pāṭayan kasyacid vaktraṃ madhye kāṃścid agṛhyata ।। gaganād bhraṣṭasarvāṅgā nipetur dharaṇītale ।। tasthau śakrapriyaṃ kṛtvā kṛtakarmā gadādharaḥ ।।
taṃ deśam ājagāmāśu brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। devadevo hariṃ devaṃ pūjayan vākyam abravīt ।। vadhenānena daityānāṃ vayaṃ ca paritoṣitāḥ ।। tvam eko asya mṛdhe hantā nānyaḥ kaścana vidyate ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ kadanaṃ kṛtvā mām api pratigarjati ।। yad ayaṃ kālatulyābhaḥ kālanemir nipātitaḥ ।। brahmarṣayas tvāṃ tatrasthāḥ pratīkṣante sadogatāḥ ।। ahaṃ maharṣayaś caiva tatra tvāṃ vadatāṃ vara । vidhivac cārcayiṣyanti gīrbhir divyābhir acyuta ।
sureṣv api sadaityeṣu varāṇāṃ varado bhavān ।। asminn eva mṛdhe viṣṇo śakrāya sumahātmane ।। devāñ śakramukhān sarvān uvāca śubhayā girā ।। śravaṇāvahitair devaiḥ puraskṛtya puraṃdaram ।।
dānavā vikramopetāḥ śakrād api mahattarāḥ ।। vairocaniś ca daityendraḥ svarbhānuś ca mahāgrahaḥ ।। yāmyāṃ yamaḥ pālayatām uttarāṃ ca dhanādhipaḥ ।। abdaṃ hy ṛtumukhaṃ sūryo bhajatām ayanaiḥ saha ।।
hūyantām agnayo viprair vedadṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। śrāddhena pitaraś caiva tṛptiṃ yāntu yathāsukham ।। trayo varṇāś ca lokāṃs trīṃs tarpayantv ātmajair guṇaiḥ ।। dakṣiṇāś cāpi vartantāṃ yathoktaṃ sarvasatriṇām ।।
tarpayantaḥ pravartantāṃ śivaiḥ saumyaiś ca karmabhiḥ ।। trailokyamātaraḥ sarvāḥ sāgaraṃ yāntu nimnagāḥ ।। svasti vo astu gamiṣyāmi brahmalokaṃ sanātanam ।। visrambho vo na gantavyo nityaṃ kṣudrā hi dānavāḥ ।।
saumyānām ṛjubhāvānāṃ bhavatāṃ cārjavā matiḥ ।। ahaṃ tu duṣṭabhāvānāṃ yuṣmāsu sudurātmanām । asamyag vartamānānāṃ mohaṃ dāsyāmi devatāḥ । yadā ca sudurādharṣaṃ dānavebhyo bhayaṃ bhavet । tadā samupagamyāśu vidhāsye vas tato abhayam । jagāma brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ brahmalokaṃ mahāyaśāḥ ।। dānavānāṃ ca viṣṇoś ca yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi ।।
brahmalokaṃ gato brahman vaikuṇṭhaḥ kiṃ cakāra ha ।। viṣṇur daityavadhe vṛtte devair akṛtasatkriyaḥ ।। kaṃ vā dadhāra niyamaṃ sa vibhur bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।। śriyam āpnoti vipulāṃ surāsuranarārcitām ।।
kathaṃ ca brahmalokastho dhuraṃ vahati laukikīm ।। vistareṇa yathātattvaṃ sarvam icchāmi veditum ।। brahmalokaṃ yathārūḍho brahmaṇā saha modate ।। yat tu śakṣyāmy ahaṃ vaktuṃ tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।
eṣa devamayaś caiva devāś caitan mayā divi ।। yat pravṛttaṃ ca devebhyas tad viddhi madhusūdanāt ।। taṃ somam agniṃ lokaṃ ca veda viṣṇuṃ pitāmahaḥ ।। mathyamāneṣu bhūteṣu tathā loko janārdanāt ।।
tathā vedaiś ca devaiś ca lokaiś ca vidito hariḥ ।। tathā prāṇeśvarāvāptir devānāṃ divi vaiṣṇavī ।। lokatantradharo hy eva mantrair mantra ivārcyate ।। eṣa pāraṃ paraṃ caiva lokānāṃ veda mādhavaḥ ।।
śṛṇu vai yat tadā vṛttaṃ brahmaloke purātanam ।। vavande tān ṛṣīn sarvān viṣṇur ārṣeṇa karmaṇā ।। avandata mahātejāḥ kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ vidhim ।। bhāgaṃ yajñiyam aśnānaṃ svadeham aparaṃ sthitam ।।
paricakrāma so acintyo brahmalokaṃ sanātanam ।। makheṣu ca brahmarṣibhiḥ śataśaḥ kṛtalakṣaṇān ।। yajñair ijyantam ātmānam paśyaṃs tatra cacāra ha ।। arghyodyatabhujāḥ sarve pavitrān taritānanāḥ ।।
namo astu te hṛṣīkeśa madhukaiṭabhasūdana । dāmodara namas te astu padmapatrāyatekṣaṇa ।। prabhus tvaṃ sarvadevānāṃ lokānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥ । tvaṃ yajñas tvaṃ vaṣaṭkāras tvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
idaṃ yajñiyam ātithyaṃ mantrataḥ pratigṛhyatām ।। atithis tvaṃ hi mantroktaḥ sa dṛṣṭaḥ satataṃ mataḥ ।। avaiṣṇavasya yajñasya na hi karma vidhīyate ।। sadakṣiṇamahāyajñās tvatprasūtir janārdana ।
yady ātmānam ihāsmābhir ijyamānaṃ nirīkṣase ।। mumude brahmalokastho brahmaiva hi pitāmahaḥ ।। paurāṇaṃ brahmasadanaṃ divyaṃ nārāyaṇāśramam ।। praṇamya cādidevāya brahmaṇe padmayonaye ।।
praviśann eva bhagavān āyudhāni vyasarjayat ।। svadhiṣṭhitaṃ bhūtagaṇaiḥ śāśvataiś ca maharṣibhiḥ ।। timiraughaparikṣiptam apradhṛṣyaṃ surāsuraiḥ ।। vapuṣā padmanābhasya sa deśas tejasā vṛtaḥ ।।
sa sahasraśirā bhūtvā śayanāyopacakrame ।। upatasthe mahātmānaṃ nidrā taṃ kālarūpiṇī ।। viśvasya jagataḥ prabhum ।nārāyaṇaṃ viśvabījam । harir ekārṇavoktena vratena vratināṃ varaḥ ।।
upāsāṃ cakrire viṣṇuṃ devāḥ sarṣigaṇās tadā ।। ādyasya sadanaṃ padmaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sūryasaṃnibham ।। sahasrapatraṃ varṇāḍhyaṃ sukumāraṃ vibhūṣitam । āvartayati lokānāṃ sarveṣāṃ kālaparyayam ।।
prajānāṃ paṅktayo hy oghair niṣpatanti viśanti ca ।। caturdhā svāṃ gatiṃ jagmuḥ kṛtāntoktena karmaṇā ।। viṣṇuṃ nidrāmayaṃ yogaṃ praviṣṭaṃ tamasāvṛtam ।। na vidus taṃ kvacit suptaṃ kvacid āsīnam āsane ।।
ko bhogavān ko dyutimān kṛṣṇāt kṛṣṇataraś ca kaḥ ।। vākyair brahmapadaiś cāpi pramāṇaiḥ sarvalakṣaṇaiḥ । na cainaṃ śekur anveṣṭuṃ karmato janmato api vā ।। purāṇaṃ taṃ purāṇeṣu ṛṣayaḥ saṃpracakṣate ।।
mahāpurāṇāt prabhṛti paraṃ tasya na vidyate ।। tat purāṇād ṛte tasya caritaṃ naiva vidyate । tenemāḥ śrutayo vyāptā vaidikā laukikāś ca yāḥ ।। dānavānām abhāvāya jāgarti madhusūdanaḥ ।।
tataḥ svapiti gharmānte jāgarti jaladakṣaye ।। sa hi yajñāś ca vedāś ca yajñāṅgāni ca sarvaśaḥ । yā tu yajñagatiḥ proktā sa eṣa puruṣottamaḥ । śaratpravṛttayajño hi jāgarti madhusūdanaḥ ।। śaratprabhṛti yajñā hi jāgrati śrīdhare harau ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ karma kurvāṇaḥ supte viṣṇau puraṃdaraḥ ।। akasmād dveṣiṇī ghorā kālarātrir mahīkṣitām ।। jīvitārdhaharī ghorā sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ bhuvi ।। śaktaḥ prasahituṃ vegaṃ majjann iva mahārṇave ।।
naiśā bhavati lokasya nidrā sarvasya laukikī ।। mṛtyukāle ca bhūtānāṃ prāṇān nāśayate bhṛśam ।। sakhī sarvaharasyaiṣā māyā viṣṇuśarīrajā ।। lokān alpena kālena bhajate bhūtamohinī ।।
dhriyate sevanīyena patineva pativratā ।। śete sma hi tadā viṣṇur mohayañ jagad avyayaḥ ।। jagmuḥ kṛtayugaṃ caiva tretā caiva yugottamam ।। prābudhyata mahātejāḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ ।।
ime te brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ devā darśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। vardhayanti hṛṣīkeśa ṛṣayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।। śṛṇu viṣṇo śubhāṃ vācaṃ bhūvyomāgnyanilāmbhasām ।। stuvanti deva divyābhir geyābhir gīrbhir añjasā ।।
kāraṇaṃ kiṃcid utpannaṃ devānāṃ kāryagauravāt ।। jahi nidrāṃ jagaddhetoḥ keśaveśa janārdana । tvayi supte jagat suptaṃ tvayi jāgrati jāgṛtam ।। mīlanaṃ kuru devānāṃ devadeva jagatpate । kiṃ tvaṃ svapiṣi govinda naṣṭe jagati sāṃpratam । naṣṭaprāyaṃ jagat paśya sadevāsuramānuṣam । udatiṣṭhad dhṛṣīkeśaḥ śriyā paramayā jvalan ।। vivakṣataḥ prakṣubhitāñ jagadarthe samāgatān ।।
tattvadṛṣṭārthayā vācā dharmahetvarthayuktayā ।। kasya vā kena vā kāryaṃ kiṃ vā mayi na vartate ।। nṛṇām āyāsajananaṃ śīghram icchāmi veditum ।। śivāya bhavatām arthe sthitaḥ kiṃ karavāṇi vaḥ ।।
uvāca paramaṃ vākyaṃ hitaṃ sarvadivaukasām ।। yeṣāṃ bhavān abhayadaḥ karṇadhāro raṇe raṇe ।। dharme prayatamānānāṃ mānavānāṃ kuto bhayam ।। nākāladharmaṇā mṛtyuḥ śaknoti prasamīkṣitum ।।
ṣaḍbhāgam upayuñjānā na bhedaṃ kurvate mithaḥ ।। akarair viprayuktārthāḥ kośam āpūrayan sadā ।। atīkṣṇad aṇḍāś caturo varṇāñ jugupur añjasā ।। caturaṅgabalair yuktāḥ ṣaḍguṇān upayuñjate ।।
yajanti ca yathākālaṃ yajñair vipuladakṣiṇaiḥ ।। śrāddhaiś ca medhyaiḥ śataśas tarpayanti pitāmahān ।। vaidikaṃ laukikaṃ caiva dharmaśāstroktam eva ca ।। bhūyaḥ kṛtayugaṃ kartum utsahante narādhipāḥ ।।
yathārthaṃ ca vavur vātā virajaskā diśo daśa ।। vātāḥ śivasugandhinaḥ । nirmalaṃ cābhavad vyoma । candramāś ca sanakṣatraḥ saumyaṃ carati yogataḥ ।। havyaiś ca vividhais tṛptaḥ śubhagandho hutāśanaḥ ।।
tarpayatsu mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ nṛṇāṃ kālabhayaṃ kutaḥ ।। rājñāṃ balair balavatāṃ pīḍyate vasudhātalam ।। pṛthivī samanuprāptā naur ivāsann aviplavā ।। jalotpīḍākulā svedaṃ darśayantī muhur muhuḥ ।।
nṛṇāṃ ca rāṣṭrair vistīrṇaiḥ śrāmyatīva vasuṃdharā ।। yac coktaṃ brahmasadane brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā । tac chṛṇuṣva mahābāho rahasyam idam uttamam । rāṣṭre rāṣṭre ca bahavo grāmāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ।। grāmāyutāḍhyai rāṣṭraiś ca bhūmir nirvivarīkṛtā ।।
prāptā mamālayaṃ viṣṇo bhavāṃś cāsyāḥ parā gatiḥ ।। yathā na sīdet tatkāryaṃ jagaty eṣā hi śāśvatī ।। kriyālopaś ca lokānāṃ dūṣitaṃ ca jagad bhavet ।। sahajāṃ yā kṣamāṃ tyaktvā calatvam acalā gatā ।।
bhārāvataraṇārthaṃ hi mantrayāmas tvayā saha ।। narāṇāṃ ca trayo varṇā brāhmaṇān anuyāyinaḥ ।। sarve vedaparā viprāḥ sarve vipraparā narāḥ ।। yathā dharmavadho na syāt tathā mantraḥ pravartatām ।।
rājñāṃ caiva vadhaḥ kāryo dharaṇyā bhāranirṇaye ।। vrajāma meruśikharaṃ puraskṛtya vasuṃdharām ।। etāvad uktvā rājendra brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । pṛthivyā saha viśvātmā virarāma mahādyutiḥ । pratasthe durdinākāraḥ sadurdina ivācalaḥ ।।
sa jatāmaṇḍalaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ bibhrat kṛṣṇavapur hariḥ ।। śrīvatso rājate śrīmān stanadvayamukhāñcitaḥ ।। hariḥ so abhavad ālakṣyaḥ sasaṃdhyābhra ivācalaḥ ।। anujagmuḥ surāḥ sarve tadgatāsaktacakṣuṣaḥ ।।
dadṛśur devatās tatra svāṃ sabhāṃ kāmarūpiṇīm ।। kāñcanastambhacaraṇāṃ vajrasaṃghātatoraṇām ।। ratnajālāntaravatīṃ kāmagāṃ ratnabhūṣitām ।। maṇipravālasopānāṃ vaidūryamaṇiśobhitām ।
muktājālasamākīrṇāṃ kiṃkiṇīśataśobhitām । devamāyādharāṃ divyāṃ nirmitāṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।। yathānideśaṃ tridaśā viviśus te sabhāṃ śubhām ।। bhadrāsaneṣu pīṭheṣu kuthāsv āstaraṇeṣu ca ।।
mā śabda iti sarvatra pracakrāma sabhāṃ śubhām ।। babhāṣe dharaṇī vākyaṃ svedāt karuṇabhāṣiṇī ।। tvayā dhāryā tv ahaṃ deva tvayā vai dhāryate jagat । tvaṃ dhārayasi bhūtāni bhuvanaṃ tvaṃ bibharṣi ca ।। yat tvayā dhāryate kiṃcit tejasā ca balena ca । tatas tava prasādena mayā paścāt tu dhāryate ।। tvayā dhṛtaṃ dhārayāmi nādhṛtaṃ dhārayāmy aham । na hi tad vidyate bhūtaṃ yat tvayā nānudhāryate ।। tvam eva kuruṣe deva nārāyaṇa yuge yuge । mahābhārāvataraṇaṃ jagato hitakāmyayā ।। tavaiva tejasā krāntāṃ rasātalatalaṃ gatām । trāyasva māṃ suraśreṣṭha tavaiva śaraṇaṃ gatām ।। dānavaiḥ pīḍyamānāhaṃ rākṣasaiś ca durātmabhiḥ । tvām eva śaraṇaṃ nityam upayāsye sanātanam ।। tāvan me asti bhayaṃ bhūyo yāvan na tvāṃ kakudminam । śaraṇaṃ yāmi manasā śataśo hy upalakṣaye । māṃ ca badhvā kṛtau pūrvaṃ mṛṅmayau dvau mahāsurau ।।
mahārṇave prasvapataḥ kāṣṭhakuḍyasamau sthitau ।। tau divaṃ chādayantau tu vavṛdhāte mahāsurau ।। ekaṃ mṛdutaraṃ mene kaṭhinaṃ veda cāparam ।। mṛdus tv ayaṃ madhur nāma kaṭhinaḥ kaiṭabho abhavat ।।
sarvam ekārṇavaṃ lokaṃ yoddhukāmau sunirbhayau ।। ekārṇavāmbunicaye tatraivānataradhīyata ।। rocayām āsa vasatiṃ guhyāṃ brahmā caturmukhaḥ ।। bahūn varṣagaṇān apsu śayānau na cakampatuḥ ।।
ājagmatus tam uddeśaṃ yatra brahmā vyavasthitaḥ ।। brahmaṇā tāḍito viṣṇuḥ padmanālena vai purā । utpapātāśu śayanāt padmanābho mahādyutiḥ ।। ekārṇave tadā loke trailokye jalatāṃ gate ।।
na ca tāv asurau yuddhe tadā śramam avāpatuḥ ।। ūcatuḥ prītamanasau devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ hariṃ ।। āvāṃ jahi na yatrorvī jalena samabhiplutā ।। so hy āvāṃ yudhi nirjetā tasyāvāṃ vihitau sutau ।।
janmatur nidhanaṃ cāpi tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhau ।। medo mumucatur daityau mathyamānau jalormibhiḥ ।। nārāyaṇaś ca bhagavān asṛjat sa punaḥ prajāḥ ।। prabhāvāt padmanābhasya śāśvatī ca nṛṇāṃ kṛtā ।।
viṣāṇenāham ekena toyamadhyāt samuddhṛtā ।। baleḥ sakāśād daityasya viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ।। anāthā jagato nāthaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā ।। akṣatrāṇāṃ guruḥ somo mama nārāyaṇo guruḥ ।।
mayā dhṛtaṃ dhārayate sarvam etad gadādharaḥ ।। roṣāt triḥsaptakṛtvo ahaṃ kṣatriyair viprayojitā ।। bhārgaveṇa pituḥ śrāddhe kaśyapāya niveditā ।। rajasvaleva yuvatiḥ kaśyapaṃ samupasthitā ।।
vīrapatnīvratam idaṃ vīrapatni niṣevase ।। patayo me hatā brahman bhārgaveṇa mahātmanā ।। vidhavā śūnyanagarā na dhārayitum utsahe ।। rakṣet sagrāmanagarāṃ yo māṃ sāgaramālinīm ।।
tato māṃ mānavendrāya manave saṃprayacchata ।। vipulenāsmi kālena pārthivāt pārthivaṃ gatā ।। bhuktā rājakulaiś cāpi maharṣikulasaṃmitaiḥ ।। te sma kālavaśaṃ prāpya mayy eva pralayaṃ gatāḥ ।।
kṣatriyāṇāṃ balavatāṃ saṃgrāmeṣv anivartinām ।। jagaddhitārthaṃ kuruta rājñāṃ hetuṃ raṇakṣaye ।। ekaś cakradharaḥ śrīmān abhayaṃ me prayacchatu ।। bhāro yady avaroptavyo viṣṇur eṣa bravītu mām ।।
mā bhair dharaṇi kalyāṇi śāntiṃ vraja samāhite । eṣa tvām ucitaṃ sthānaṃ sthāpayāmi vasiṃdhare । etasyāhaṃ prasādena śramaṃ tyakṣyāmi devatāḥ । tadarthakṛtyaṃ saṃcintya pitāmaham athābruvan ।। śarīrakartā lokānāṃ tvaṃ hi lokasya ceśvaraḥ ।। yad vā kāryaṃ dhaneśena svayaṃ nārāyaṇena vā ।।
ādityair vasubhir vāpi rudrair vā lokabhāvanaiḥ ।। marudbhir vā suraśreṣṭhaiḥ pāvakenāpi ca prabho । bṛhaspatyuśanobhyāṃ vā kālena kalināpi vā ।। yakṣarākṣasagandharvaiś cāraṇair vā mahoragaiḥ ।।
gaṅgāmukhābhir divyābhiḥ saridbhir vā sureśvara ।। yadi te pārthivaṃ kāryaṃ kāryaṃ pārthivavigrahe ।। antarikṣagatā ye ca pṛthivyāṃ ye ca pārthivāḥ ।। ayonijāś cāpi tanūḥ sṛjāma jagatītale ।।
devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ prāha vākyaṃ lokapitāmahaḥ ।। sṛjadhvaṃ svaśarīrāṃśāṃs tejasātmasamān bhuvi ।। bhāvayanto bhuvaṃ devīṃ labdhvā tribhuvanaśriyam ।। pṛthivyāṃ saṃbhavam imaṃ śrūyatāṃ yan mayā kṛtam ।।
āse sārdhaṃ tanūjena kaśyapena mahātmanā ।। itivṛttaiś ca bahubhiḥ purāṇaprabhavair guṇaiḥ ।। nirūpayaṃs taṃ deveśaṃ pramāṇair bahulakṣaṇaiḥ । samīpam ājagāmāśu yuktas toyadamārutaiḥ ।।
yādogaṇavicitreṇa saṃchannas toyavāsasā ।। yuktaś candramasā pūrṇaḥ sābhragambhīranisvanaḥ ।। kledayām āsa capalair lāvaṇair ambuvisravaiḥ ।। uktaḥ saṃrabdhayā vācā śānto asīti tato mayā ।।
saṃhatormitaraṅgaughaḥ sthito rājaśriyā jvalan ।। sakāraṇāṃ matiṃ kṛtvā yuṣmākaṃ hitakāmyayā ।। gacchārṇava mahīpālo rājaiva tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। bhaviṣyasi nṛṇāṃ bhartā bhāratānāṃ kulodvahaḥ ।।
sutanur yaśasā loke śaṃtanus tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। iyam apy āgatā gaṅgā tavārthe varavarṇinī । rūpiṇī vai saric chreṣṭhā tatra tvām upayāsyati ।। māṃ prabho devadeveśa kimarthaṃ śaptavān asi ।।
aśapo asadṛśair vākyair ātmajaṃ māṃ kim ātmanā ।। yady ahaṃ calito brahman ko atra doṣo mamātmanaḥ ।। atra me bhagavan kiṃ nu vidyate śāpakāraṇam ।। parvaṇā cenduyuktena tribhiḥ kṣubdho asmi kāraṇaiḥ ।।
kṣantum arhasi me brahmañ śāpo ayaṃ vinivartyatām ।। kāruṇyaṃ kuru deveśa pramāṇaṃ yady avekṣase ।। maddoṣāt samadoṣāyāḥ prasādaṃ kartum arhasi ।। prasādaṃ kuru me brahman vidyate śāpakāraṇam ।
akāraṇajñaṃ devānāṃ trastaṃ śāpānileritam ।। śāpe asmin saritāṃ nātha bhaviṣyaṃ śṛṇu kāraṇam ।। ādhatsva saritāṃ nātha tyaktvemāṃ sāgarīṃ tanum ।। pālayaṃś caturo varṇān raṃsyase salileśvara ।।
tat kālaramaṇīyāṅgī gaṅgā paricariṣyati ।। imaṃ salilasaṃkledaṃ vismariṣyasi sāgara ।। prājāpatyena vidhinā gaṅgayā saha sāgara ।। teṣām utpādanārthāya tvaṃ mayā viniyojitaḥ ।।
vibhāvasos tulyaguṇān surāṇāṃ prītivardhanān ।। praveṣṭāsi tanuṃ tyaktvā punaḥ sāgara sāgarīm ।। bhaviṣyaṃ paśyatā bhāraṃ pṛthivyāḥ pārthivātmakam ।। vasavo yatra gaṅgāyāṃ utpannās tridivaukasaḥ ।।
sapteme vasavaḥ prāptāḥ sa ekaḥ parilambate ।। vicitravīryo dyutimān āsīd rājā pratāpavān ।। pāṇḍuś ca dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca vikhyātau puruṣarṣabhau ।। śubhe kuntī ca mādrī ca devayoṣopame bhuvi ।।
gāndhārī bhuvi vikhyātā bhartur nityaṃ vrate sthitā ।। putrāṇāṃ hi tayo rājñor bhavitā vigraho mahān ।। yugāntapratimaṃ caiva bhaviṣyati mahad bhayam ।। viviktapurarāṣṭraughā kṣitiḥ śaithilyam eṣyati ।।
kṣayaṃ yāsyanti śastreṇa pārthivāḥ saha vāhanaiḥ ।। dhakṣyate śaṃkarasyāṃśaḥ pāvakenāstratejasā ।। samāptam idam ākhyāsye tṛtīyaṃ dvāparaṃ yugam ।। tiṣyaṃ prapatsyate paścād yugaṃ dāruṇamānuṣam ।।
utsannasatyasaṃyogaṃ vardhitānṛtasaṃcayam ।। bhaviṣyanti narāḥ sarve loke nasthavirāyuṣaḥ ।। aṃśāvataraṇaṃ sarve surāḥ kuruta māciram ।। vigrahasya kalir mūlaṃ gāndhāryāṃ viniyujyatām ।।
jātarāgāḥ pṛthivyarthe sarve saṃgrāmalālasāḥ ।। sṛṣṭo ayaṃ naiṣṭhiko rājñām upāyo lokaviśrutaḥ ।। pṛthivī saha kālena vadhāya pṛthivīkṣitām ।। naraṃ caiva purāṇarṣiṃ śeṣaṃ ca dharaṇīdharam ।।
gandharvāpsarasaś caiva rudrādityāṃs tathāśvinau ।। yathā te kathitaṃ pūrvam aṃśāvataraṇaṃ mayā ।। kṣīrikāvṛkṣasaṃghātā vajrasaṃhananās tathā ।। giriśṛṅgaprahartāraḥ sarve parighayodhinaḥ ।।
kuruvaṃśe ca devās te pāñcāleṣu ca pārthivāḥ ।। sarvāstrajñā maheṣvāsā vedavrataparāyaṇāḥ ।। sarvarddhiguṇasaṃpannā yajvānaḥ puṇyakarṃiṇaḥ । utpateyur athākāśaṃ kṣobhayeyur mahodadhim ।।
nārāyaṇe samāveśya lokāñ śāntim upāgamat ।। prajānāṃ vai hitārthāya prabhuḥ prāṇadhaneśvaraḥ ।। kule pūjye yaśaskāmo jajñe nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। aṃśāvataraṇe vṛtte surāṇāṃ bhārate kule ।।
aśvinor devabhiṣajor bhāge vai bhāskarasya ca ।। vasūnām aṣṭame bhāge prāg eva dharaṇīṃ gate ।। bhāge somasya vahneś ca varuṇasya ca gāṃ gate ।। gandharvoragayakṣāṇāṃ bhāgāṃśeṣu gateṣv atha ।।
bhāge avatīrṇe mitrasya yamasyāṃśe tathaiva ca । varuṇasya gate tv aṃśe pṛthivīṃ janamejaya । tiṣṭhan nārāyaṇasyāṃśe nāradaḥ pratyadṛṣyata ।। savyāpavṛttaṃ vipulaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍalam udvahan ।। vīṇāṃ gṛhītvā mahatīṃ kakṣāsaktāṃ sakhīm iva ।।
daṇḍī kamaṇḍaludharaḥ sākṣāc chakra ivāparaḥ ।। mudrāsamarpitakaraḥ sumanoveṣṭitāṅgavān । maharṣir vigraharucir vidvān gāndharvavedavit ।। gātā caturṇāṃ vedānām udgātā prathamartvijām ।।
devagandharvalokānām ādivaktā mahāmuniḥ । sthito devasabhāmadhye saṃrabdho viṣṇum abravīt ।। svaraiś ca saptabhir viṣṇuṃ jagau vipraḥ sa nāradaḥ । ṣaḍjaṃ prathamam āvidhya ṛṣabhaṃ ca tataḥ param ।। miśrayitvā ca gāndhāraṃ tato dhaivatamadhyamau । pañcamaṃ ca tataḥ kurvan niṣādaṃ tadanantaram ।। kākalīṃ ca vimātrāṃ tu tato dve ca śrutī prabho । tisras tisras tathā rājaṃl layaiś ca saha sarvaśaḥ ।। tānatānāgaṇānāṃ ca vivicya kramaśaḥ prabhuḥ । taiś cāpi saptabhir vācyaṃ vācakaiś cāpi sarvaśaḥ । anantavīryaṃ deveśaṃ jagau brahmapuraḥsaram ।। etaiḥ saptabhir ādyeśaṃ vicinvan prabhavaṃ tathā । evaṃ samāpya geyaṃ tu vākyam etad uvāca ha । kṣayāya pṛthivīndrāṇāṃ sarvam etad akāraṇam ।।
nṛnārāyaṇayukto ayaṃ kāryārthaḥ pratibhāti me ।। devadeva pṛthivyarthe prayoktuṃ kāryam īdṛśam ।। śreṣṭho yogavatāṃ yogī gatir gatimatām api ।। vasuṃdharāyāḥ sāhyārtham aṃśaṃ svaṃ nānuyuñjase ।।
jagatyāṃ saṃtariṣyanti kāryāt kāryāntaraṃ gatāḥ ।। tava saṃcodanārthaṃ vai śṛṇu cāpy atra kāraṇam ।। teṣāṃ śṛṇu gatiṃ viṣṇo ye gatāḥ pṛthivītalam ।। niviṣṭā yamunātīre sphītā janapadāyutā ।।
ghoraṃ madhuvanaṃ nāma yatrāsau nyavasat tadā ।। lavaṇas tasya putro abhūn mahābalaparākramaḥ । trāsanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ bale mahati tasthivān ।। sadaivatagaṇāṃl lokān udvāsayati darpitaḥ ।।
rājyaṃ śāsati dharmajñe rākṣasānāṃ bhayāvahe ।। preṣayām āsa rāmāya dūtaṃ paruṣavādinam ।। na ca sāmantam icchanti rājāno baladarpitam ।। jetavyā ripavaḥ sarve sphītaṃ viṣayam icchatā ।।
jetavyānīndriyāṇy ādau taj jaye hi dhruvo jayaḥ ।। nayānām upadeśena nāsti lokasamo guruḥ ।। balajyeṣṭhasya nṛpater nāsti sāmantajaṃ bhayam ।। amitrāṇāṃ priyakarair mohair adhṛtir īśvaraḥ ।।
naitad aupayikaṃ manye mahat te karma kutsitam ।। prahṛtaṃ rākṣase nīce naiṣa dṛṣṭaḥ satāṃ vidhiḥ ।। yat tvayā nihato mohād dūṣitāś ca vanaukasaḥ ।। strīnimittaṃ hato yuddhe grāmyān dharmān avekṣatā ।।
yudhyasvādya mayā sārdhaṃ mṛdhe yady asi vīryavān ।। dhairyād asaṃbhrāntavapuḥ sasmitaṃ rāghavo abravīt ।। yan māṃ kṣipasi doṣeṇa vedātmānaṃ ca susthiram ।। yadi vā me hṛtā bhāryā tasya kā paridevanā ।।
jāgarti ca yathā daivaṃ sadā satsv itareṣu ca ।। nātmaślāghiṣu nīceṣu praharantīha madvidhāḥ ।। tasya daityasya durbuddhe mṛdhe pratikariṣyati ।। anujñāto narendreṇa rāghaveṇa mahātmanā ।।
cakre niveśaṃ saumitrir vanānte yuddhalālasaḥ ।। jaghane tad vanaṃ kṛtvā yuddhāyābhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।। ubhayor eva dhṛtayoḥ śūrayo raṇamūrdhani ।। na ca tau yuddhavaimukhyaṃ śramaṃ vāpy upajagmatuḥ ।।
tataḥ sa śūlarahitaḥ paryahīyata dānavaḥ ।। sa gṛhītvāṅkuśaṃ caiva devair dattavaraṃ raṇe । karṣaṇaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ lavaṇo virarāsa ha ।। śirodharāyāṃ jagrāha so aṅkuśena cakarṣa ha । praveśayitum ārabdho lavaṇo rāghavānujam । śiraś ciccheda khaḍgena lavaṇasya mahāmṛdhe ।। aṅkuśaṃ caiva ciccheda daityasya ca śiro mahat ।
tad vanaṃ tasya daityasya cicchedāstreṇa buddhimān ।। bhavāya tasya deśasya purīṃ paramadharmavit ।। śatrughnena purā sṛṣṭā hatvā taṃ dānavaṃ raṇe ।। sphītā rāṣṭrasamākīrṇā samṛddhabhavanākulā ।।
prāṃśuprākārasaṃpannā parikhārgalamekhalā ।। susaṃvṛtadvāramukhī catvarodgārahāsinī ।। ardhacandrapratīkāśā yamunātīraśobhitā ।। kṣetrāṇi rasavanty asyāḥ kāle devaś ca varṣati ।।
aṃśāvataraṇe vṛtte surāṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām । nārāyaṇaṃ samabhyetya nārado vākyam abravīt ।। yamunāyās taṭe ramye mathurā nāma viśrutā । niviṣṭo viṣayaś caiva śūrasenas tato abhavat ।। ugrasena iti khyāto mahāsenaparākramaḥ ।। kālanemir mahādaityaḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye ।।
rājā pṛthivyāṃ vikhyātaḥ siṃhavispaṣṭavikramaḥ ।। bhayadaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ satpathād bāhyatāṃ gataḥ ।। yuktas tenaiva darpeṇa prajānāṃ lomaharṣaṇaḥ ।। nātmarājyapriyakaraś caṇḍaḥ kararuciḥ sadā ।।
sa badhvā pitaraṃ rājā mathurām abhyarakṣata । kravyādo bādhate lokān āsureṇāntarātmanā ।। keśī nāma hayo jātaḥ sa tasyaiva jaghanyajaḥ ।। vṛndāvane vasaty eko nṛṇāṃ māṃsāni bhakṣayan ।।
gavām aritvam āpannaḥ kāmarūpī mahāsuraḥ ।। sa kuñjaratvam āpanno daityaḥ kaṃsasya vāhanaḥ ।। kuñjaratvam agād daityaḥ kaṃsasyaiva sa vāhanaḥ । pralambo nāma bhūtvāsau vaṭaṃ bhāṇḍīram āśritaḥ ।।
śikharo nāma balavān ya āsīd dānavarṣabhaḥ । ghoraṃ tālavanaṃ daityaś caraty utsārayan prajāḥ ।। mallau raṅgagatau tau tu jātau cāṇūramuṣṭikau ।। prāgjyotiṣe tau bhaumasya narakasya pure ratau ।।
mānuṣaṃ vapur āsthāya bādhante bhuvi mānavān ।। tava prasādāt teṣāṃ vai dānavānāṃ kṣayo bhavet ।। pṛthivyāṃ bibhyati tvatto nānyasya tu kathaṃcana ।। divaś cyutasya daityasya gatir bhavati medinī ।।
durlabhaṃ svargagamanaṃ tvayi jāgrati keśava ।। dānavānāṃ vināśāya visṛjātmānam ātmanā ।। tāsu sṛṣṭās tvayā devāḥ saṃbhaviṣyanti bhūtale ।। setsyate ca sa kāryārtho yasyārthe bhūmir āgatā ।।
tad āgaccha hṛṣīkeśa kṣitau tāñ jahi dānavān ।। pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vākyaṃ vareṇyaḥ prabhur īśvaraḥ ।। tasya samyakpravṛttasya śrūyatām uttaraṃ vacaḥ ।। yāṃ yāṃ tanuṃ samāsthāya daityaḥ puṣyati vigraham ।।
keśinaṃ cāpi jānāmi daityaṃ turagavigraham ।। ariṣṭaṃ caiva jānāmi daityaṃ vṛṣabharūpiṇam ।। sā ca me viditā vipra pūtanā duhitā baleḥ ।। vainateyabhayād vipra sarpam ajñātarūpiṇam ।।
prāgjyotiṣapure cāpi narakaṃ sādhu tarkaye ।। mānuṣe pārthive loke mānuṣatvam upāgatam । bāṇaṃ ca śoṇitapure guhapratimatejasam । dṛptaṃ bāhusahasreṇa devair api sudurjayam । śiśupālaṃ ca jānāmi tau haṃsaḍimakau tathā । jānāmi pauṇḍraṃ sālvaṃ ca taṃ kālayavanaṃ tathā ।। ekalavyaṃ ca jānāmi ye cānye duṣṭacāriṇaḥ । tān sarvān nihaniṣyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā । tac ca sarvaṃ vijānāmi yathā sthāsyanti te nṛpāḥ ।। teṣāṃ puruṣadehānām aparāvṛttivartinām ।।
saṃprāpya pārthivaṃ lokaṃ mānuṣatvam upāgataḥ ।। tena tena vidhānena yena yaḥ śāntim eṣyati ।। amīṣām amarendrāṇāṃ hantavyā ripavo yudhi ।। suradevarṣigandharvair etac cānumataṃ mama ।।
nivāsaṃ tu na me brahmā vidadhāti pitāmahaḥ ।। tān ahaṃ samare hanyāṃ tan me brūhi pitāmaha ।। bhuvi yas te janayitā jananī ca bhaviṣyati ।। yādavānāṃ mahadvaṃśam akhilaṃ dhārayiṣyasi ।।
sthāpayiṣyasi maryādāṃ nṛṇāṃ tan me niśāmaya ।। jahāra yajñiyā gāvaḥ payodāś ca mahāmakhe ।। pradīyamānā gās tās tu naicchatāṃ varuṇasya vai ।। uvāca bhagavan gāvo guruṇā me hṛtā iti ।।
anvavartata bhārye dve aditiṃ surabhiṃ tathā ।। caranti sagārān sarvān rakṣitāḥ svena tejasā ।। akṣayaṃ yāḥ kṣaranty agraṃ payo devāmṛtopamam ।। tvayā niyamyāḥ sarve vai tvaṃ hi naḥ paramā gatiḥ ।।
na vidyate lokaguro na syur vai lokasetavaḥ ।। mama gāvaḥ pratīyantāṃ tato gantāsmi sāgaram ।। lokānāṃ tvatpravṛttānām ekaṃ gobrāhmaṇaṃ smṛtam ।। gobrāhmaṇaparitrāṇāt paritrātaṃ jagad bhavet ।।
gavāṃ kāraṇatattvajñaḥ kaśyape śāpam utsṛjam ।। sa tenāṃśena jagatīṃ gatvā gopatvam eṣyati ।। te apy ubhe tasya vai bhārye saha tenaiva yāsyataḥ ।। tābhyāṃ saha sa gopatve kaśyapo bhuvi raṃsyate ।
vasudeva iti khyāto goṣu tiṣṭhati bhūtale ।। tatrāsau goṣu nirataḥ kaṃsasya karadāyakaḥ ।। devakī rohiṇī caiva vasudevasya dhīmataḥ ।। surabhī rohiṇī devī cāditir devakī tv abhūt ।
jayāśīrvacanais tv ete vardhayanti divaukasaḥ ।। devakīṃ rohiṇīṃ caiva garbhābhyāṃ paritoṣaya ।। vardhayasva mahābāho purā traivikrame yathā ।। gopakanyāsahasrāṇi ramayaṃś cara medinīm ।।
vanamālāparikṣiptaṃ dhanyā drakṣyanti te vapuḥ ।। pītāmbaradharaṃ caiva nīlakuñcitamūrdhajam । vanamālākṛtoraskaṃ mayūravyajanākulam । bāle tvayi mahābāho loko bālatvam eṣyati ।। goṣu gopā bhaviṣyanti sahāyāḥ satataṃ tava ।
majjato yamunāyāṃ ca ratim āpsyanti te tvayi ।। yas tvayā tāta ity uktaḥ putra ity eva vakṣyati ।। sa hi dhanyataro loke yasya tvaṃ putratāṃ gataḥ । sa hi puṇyakṛtāṃ śreṣṭho yas tvāṃ putreti kīrtayet ।। ye namasyanti deva tvāṃ gopālakṛtalakṣaṇam । te hi puṇyakṛtāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ praṇamyāḥ sarvajantubhiḥ । kā ca dhārayituṃ śaktā viṣṇo tvām aditiṃ vinā ।।
vayam apy ālayaṃ svaṃ gacchāmo madhusūdana ।। ity uktvā devadeveśaṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । jagāma sa prabhur gehaṃ devāś cāpi yathāgatam । jagāma viṣṇuḥ svaṃ deśaṃ kṣīrodasyottarāṃ diśam ।। tribhis tasyaiva vikrāntair nityaṃ parvasu pūjitā ।।
ātmānaṃ yojayām āsa vasudevagṛhe prabhuḥ ।। ।। ।। śrīvājivadanāya namaḥ ।। ।। atha dvitīyaṃ viṣṇuparva samārabhyate ।।
vedavyāsaguṇāvāsa vidyādhīśa satāṃ vaśa । māṃ nirāśaṃ gatakleśaṃ kurvan āśaṃ hare aniśam । vināśaśaṃsī kaṃsasya nārado mathurāṃ yayau ।। preṣayām āsa kaṃsasya ugrasenasutasya vai ।। sa dūtaḥ kathayām āsa muner āgamanaṃ nṛpe । dvāḥsthaṃ viditavistāraṃ dvāri tiṣṭhati nāradaḥ । iti śrutvā sa kaṃsasya dvārapālas tvarann iva ।। gatvā tu tvaritaṃ rājann uvāca madhureśvaram । eṣa tiṣṭhati rājendra nārado lokanāradaḥ ।
nirgajāmāsuraḥ kaṃsaḥ svapuryāḥ padmalocanaḥ ।। tejasā jvalanākāraṃ vapuṣā sūryavarcasam ।। āsanaṃ cāgnivarṇābhaṃ visṛjyopajahāra vai ।। uvāca cograsenasya sutaṃ paramakopanam ।।
gate tv evaṃ mama vacaḥ śrūyatāṃ gṛhyatāṃ ca vai ।। evaṃ gate mahārāja śrūyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama । gataḥ sūryasakhaṃ tāta vipulaṃ meruparvatam ।। āplutaṃ me sutīrthāsu saritsu saha daivataiḥ ।।
divyāṃ tripathagāṃ dṛṣṭvā puṇyāṃ bhāgirathīṃ nadīm । divyā tripathagā dṛṣṭā puṇyā bhāgīrathī nadī । smaraṇād eva sarveṣām aṃhasāṃ yā vibhedinī । upaspṛṣṭaṃ ca tīrtheṣu divyeṣu ca yathākramam ।।
devagandharvanirghoṣair apsarobhiś ca nāditam ।। saṃgṛhya vīṇāṃ saṃsaktām agacchaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sabhām ।। divyāsanagatān devān apaśyaṃ sapitāmahān ।। bhavataḥ sānugasyeha vadhopāyaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।।
asyā garbho aṣṭamaḥ kaṃsa sa te mṛtyur bhaviṣyati ।। paraṃ rahasyaṃ devānāṃ sa te mṛtyur bhaviṣyati ।। tatas te tan mahad bhūtaṃ divyaṃ na kathayāmy aham ।। yatnaś ca kriyatāṃ kaṃsa garbhasthe yadi śakyate ।।
bhujyantāṃ sarvakāmārthāḥ svasti te astu vrajāmy aham ।। dāsyantāṃ dānavistarāḥ ।bhujyantāṃ kaṃsa kāmāś ca । jahāsoccais tataḥ kaṃsaḥ pakāśadaśanaś ciram ।। hāsyaḥ khalu sa sattveṣu nārado na viśāradaḥ ।।
āhavasthaḥ śayāno vā pramato matta eva vā ।। ko asti yo mānuṣe loke māṃ kṣobhayitum utsahet ।। nṛpakṣipaśusaṃghānāṃ karomi kadanaṃ mahat ।। ariṣṭo vṛṣabhaś caiva pūtanā kāliyas tathā ।।
praharadhvaṃ ca sarveṣu ye asmākaṃ pakṣadūṣakāḥ ।। nāradena hi garbhebhyo bhayaṃ naḥ samudāhṛtam ।। māṃ ca vo nātham āśritya nāsti devakṛtaṃ bhayam ।। suśliṣṭān api lokeṣu bhedayaṃl labhate ratim ।।
ghaṭayāno narendrāṇāṃ tantrīvairāṇi caiva ha ।। viveśa kaṃso bhavanaṃ dahyamānena cetasā ।। yattā bhavata sarve vai devakyā garabhakṛntane ।। mūlād eva hi hantavyaḥ so anartho yatra saṃśayaḥ ।।
svairaṃ caratu visrabdhā madbalair yatnam āsthitaiḥ ।। pariṇāme tu garbhasya śeṣaṃ jñāsyāmahe vayam ।। strībhir varṣavaraiś caiva vaktavyaṃ na ca kāraṇam ।। śrūyatāṃ yena daivaṃ hi madvidhaiḥ pratihanyate ।।
yatnena cānukūlena daivam apy anuvartate ।। bhayena mantrayām āsa śrutārtho nāradāt sa vai ।। atha brahmatanūjas tu nārado munipuṃgavaḥ । viṣṇave sarvam ācakhyau yathā kaṃsaviceṣṭitam । śrutvaiva kaṃsarājasya ceṣṭitaṃ jagatīpatiḥ ।
antardhānaṃ gato viṣṇuś cintayām āsa vīryavān ।। aṣṭame ca mayā garbhe kāryam ādhānam ātmanaḥ ।। yatra te garbhaśayanāḥ ṣadgarbhā nāma dānavāḥ ।। amarapratimā yuddhe putrā vai kālaneminaḥ ।।
āryakaṃ vai parityajya hiraṇyakaśipuṃ purā । tapyamānās tapas tīvraṃ jaṭāmaṇḍaladhāriṇaḥ ।। samāḥ sahasram ayutam ambuvāyuvicāriṇaḥ । bho bho dānavaśārdūlās tapasāhaṃ sutoṣitaḥ ।
brūta vo yasya yaḥ kāmaḥ ko varo vaḥ pradīyatāṃ ।। yadi no bhagavān prītaḥ śrūyatāṃ no varo varaḥ ।। śāpapraharaṇaiś cāpi niyataiḥ paramarṣibhiḥ ।। mā bhūd vadho no bhagavan dadāsi yadi no varam ।।
bhavadbhir yad idaṃ proktaṃ sarvam etad bhaviṣyati ।। tato hiraṇyakaśipuḥ saroṣo vākyam abravīt ।। tasmād vas tyājitaḥ snehaḥ śatrubhūtāṃs tyajāmy aham ।। sa eva vo garbhagatān pitā sarvān vadhiṣyati ।।
bhaviṣyanti tataḥ kaṃso garbhasthān vo vadhiṣyati ।। śaptvā caivaṃ tato daityān daityeśo roṣamūrcchitaḥ । pātāle jalagarbhasthāṃś cakārāmitavikramaḥ । jñātvā haris tu taṃ śāpaṃ kaṃsasya ca viniścayam । ṣaḍgarbhāḥ saṃyatāḥ santi jalagarbhagṛheśayāḥ ।। nidrayā kālarūpiṇyā sarvān antarhitān iva ।।
prāṇeśvarāṃś ca niṣkṛṣya nidrāyai pradadau tadā ।। gaccha nidre mayotsṛṣṭā devakībhavanāntikam ।। ṣaḍgarbhān dānavottamān । sarvaprāṇeśvarī caiva ।
ṣaṭsu garbheṣu devakyā yojayasva yathākramam ।। kaṃsasya viphale yatne devakyāḥ saphale śrame ।। yena sarvasya lokasya devi devī bhavīṣyasi ।। bhaviṣyanti mamāsrāṇi tathā bāhusthitāni te । śārṅgaśaṅkhagadācakra musalaṃ śūlam eva ca ।
sa saṃkrāmayitavyas te saptame māsi rohiṇīm ।। bhaviṣyaty agrajo bhrātā mama śītāṃśudarśanaḥ ।। aṣṭame mayi garbhasthe kaṃso yatnaṃ kariṣyati ।। yaśodā nāma bhadraṃ te bhāryā gopakulodvahā ।।
navamyām eva saṃjāto kṛṣṇapakṣasya vai tithau ।। ardharātre kariṣyāmi garbhamokṣaṃ yathāsukham ।। prāpsyāvo garabhavyatyāsaṃ prāpte kaṃsasya śasane ।। āvayor garbhavyatyāse kaṃso gacchatu mūḍhatām ।।
tatas taddhastavibhraṣṭā madyogād bhavitā śubhā । nirasyamānā gagane sthānaṃ prāpsyasi śāśvatam ।। bibhratī vipulān bāhūn mama bāhūpamān bhuvi ।। pātrīṃ ca pūrṇāṃ madhunaḥ paṅkajaṃ ca sunirmalam ।।
śaśiraśmiprakāśena hāreṇorasi rājatā ।। candrasāpatnyabhūtena tvaṃ mukhena virājitā ।। bhujagābhoganirghoṣair bāhubhiḥ parighopamaiḥ ।। bhujagābhair bhujair bhīmair bhūṣayantī diśo daśa । aṣṭabhiḥ śobhayanty ugraiḥ śārṅgacakrāsidhāribhiḥ ।
aṅgajena mayūrāṇām aṅgadena ca bhāsvatā ।। kaumāraṃ vratam āsthāya atridivaṃ tvaṃ gamiṣyasi ।। abhiṣekeṇa divyena daivataiḥ saha yokṣyate ।। kuśikasya tu gotreṇa kauśikī tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।।
tataḥ sthānasahasreais tvaṃ pṛthivīṃ śobhayiṣyasi ।। tau ca kṛtvā manasi māṃ sānugau nāśayiṣyasi ।। bhaviṣyasi mahābhāge varadā kāmarūpiṇī ।। tithau navamyāṃ pūjāṃ ca prāpsyase sapaśukriyām ।।
na teṣāṃ durlabhaṃ kiṃcit putrato dhanato api vā ।। dasyubhir vā niruddhānāṃ tvaṃ gatiḥ paramā nṛṇām ।। saṃdhyā lakṣmīr vapur medhā kāntiḥ śraddhā kriyā gatiḥ । saṃdhyā rātriḥ prabhā nidrā kālarātris tathaiva ca ।।
tvāṃ tu stoṣyanti ye bhaktyā stavenānena vai śubhe । tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati ।। āryāstavaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathoktam ṛṣibhiḥ purā । nārāyaṇīṃ namasyāmi devīṃ tribhuvaneśvarīm । vyādhimṛtyubhayaṃ caiva pūjitā śamayiṣyasi ।। bhaviṣyasi mahābhāge varadā kāmarūpiṇī । aham apy ātmano vṛttiṃ vidhāsye goṣu gopavat ।
svavṛddhyartham ahaṃ caiva kariṣye kaṃsaghātanam ।। sā cāpi taṃ namaskṛtya tathāstv iti vinirgatā ।। yaś caitat paṭhate stotraṃ śṛṇuyād vāpy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ । sarvārthasiddhiṃ labhate naro nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ । jagrāha sapta tān garbhān yathāvat samudāhṛtān ।।
āpannaṃ saptamaṃ garbhaṃ sā nināyātha rohiṇīm ।। nidrayā sahasāviṣṭā papāta dharaṇītale ।। apaśyantī ca taṃ garbhaṃ muhūrtaṃ vyathitābhavat ।। rohiṇīm iva somasya vasudevasya rohiṇīm ।।
saṃkarṣaṇo nāma śubhe tava putro bhaviṣyati ।। viveśa rohiṇī veśma suprabhā rohiṇī yathā ।। yadarthaṃ sapta te garbhāḥ kaṃsena vinipātitāḥ ।। jāgrataḥ prayatāḥ sarve māsān saṃkhyāya śastriṇaḥ ।
sa tatra garbhavasatiṃ vasaty ātmecchayā hariḥ ।। yasminn ahani deveśaṃ garbham ādatta devakī । viṣṇoḥ śarīrajāṃ nidrāṃ viṣṇor nirdeśakāriṇīm ।। devakī ca yaśodā ca suṣuvāte samaṃ tadā ।।
nandagopasya bhāryā vai kaṃsagopasya saṃmatā ।। aṣṭamyāṃ śrāvaṇe māse kṛṣṇapakṣe mahātithau । rohiṇyām ardharātre ca sudhāṃśor udaye tathā । muhūrte abhijite prāpte sārdharātre vibhūṣite ।।
jajvaluś cāgnayaḥ śāntā jāyamāne janārdane ।। jyotīṃsi ca prakāśanta jāyamāne janārdane ।। abhijin nāma nakṣatraṃ jayantī nāma śarvarī । muhūrto vijayo nāma yatra jāto janārdanaḥ ।। avyaktaḥ śāśvataḥ sūkṣmo harinārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ । jāyate bhagavāṃs tatra nayanair mohayañ jagat । ākāśāt puṣpavarṣaṃ ca vavarṣa tridiveśvaraḥ ।।
antardhānagatāḥ sarve munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ । astuvan niśi deveśaṃ jāyamānaṃ janārdanam ।। eṣa eva jagatsvāmī vasudevasya veśmani । bālyaṃ vapuḥ samāsthāya tūṣṇīm āste atha paśyata ।। paśyatainaṃ suviśrabdhāḥ sākṣāl lokeśvaraṃ prabhum । mānuṣīṃ tanum āsthāya lambantaṃ devakīkare ।। eṣa hantuṃ durātmānaṃ kaṃsam āvirbhaviṣyati ।। namas tasmai jagaddhātre viṣṇave kṛṣṇarūpiṇe । acintyavibhave tasmai viśvakartre namo namaḥ । arthyābhir gīrbhir evaṃ taṃ jāyamānaṃ janārdanam । maharṣayaḥ sagandharvā upatasthuḥ sahāpsarāḥ ।। jāyamāne hṛṣīkeśe prahṛṣṭam abhavaj jagat । indraś ca tridaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ tuṣṭāva madhusūdanam ।। vasudevas tu taṃ rātrau jātaṃ putram adhokṣajam । śrīvatsalakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā yutaṃ divyaiś ca lakṣaṇaiḥ । devakī ca tato dīnā tam uvāca śucismitā । upasaṃhara sarvāsu divyaṃ rūpam idaṃ hare ।। jānātu māvatāraṃ te kaṃso ayaṃ ditijāntaka । uvāca vasudevas taṃ rūpaṃ saṃhara vai prabho । bhīto ahaṃ deva kaṃsasya tasmād evaṃ vadāmy aham । mama putrā hatās tena tava jyeṣṭhāmbujekṣaṇa ।। vasudevavacaḥ śrutvā rūpaṃ saṃharad acyutaḥ । anujñāpya pitṛtvena nandagopagṛhaṃ naya । ugrasenamate tiṣṭhan yaśodāyai dadau tadā । evaṃ samākule kāle suṣupū rakṣiṇas tadā ।। na kevalaṃ rakṣitāraḥ sāyudhā mohitāḥ kila । sā purī madhurā sarvā suṣvāpa harimāyayā । vasudevād ṛte tasmād devakyāś ca mahīpate ।। vasudevas tato gatvā devakīgarbhaveśma tat । dadarśa devadeveśaṃ rātrau jātam adhokṣajam ।। nīlakuñcitakeśāntam unnidrāmbujavaktrakam । nīlameghanibhaṃ kāntaṃ tejoraśim amānuṣam ।। śayānam ambuje patre vaṭapatre yathā purā । prācīnaśirasaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ paścimanyastapādakam ।। tatra dṛṣṭo jarāyur na na ca prasavavedanā ।। devakī sumukhī dṛṣṭvā sāsīnā putralokinī । atyantavismayāviṣṭā vasudevena sābhavat ।
śayānam aṅke devakyā rātrāv ādāya yādavaḥ । yaśodāyā gṛhaṃ bhīto viveśa sutavatsalaḥ ।। tayā hṛtapratyayasarvavṛttiṣu ।dvāḥstheṣu paureṣv anuśāyiteṣv atha ।dvāras tu saravāḥ pihitā duratyayā ।bṛhatkapāṭāyasakīlaśṛṅkhalaiḥ ।।tāḥ kṛṣṇavāhe vasudeva āgate ।svayaṃ viśīryanta tamo yathā raveḥ ।vavarṣa parjanya upāṃśugarjitaṃ ।śeṣo anvagād vāri nivārayan phaṇaiḥ ।।magho ativarṣaty asakṛd yamānujā ।gambhīratoyaughajavormiphenilā ।bhayānakāvartaśatākulā nadī ।mārgaṃ dadau sindhur iva śriyaḥ pateḥ ।।nandavrajaṃ śaurir upetya tatra tān ।gopān prasuptān upalabhya nidrayā ।sutaṃ yaśodāśayane nidhāya tam ।sutām upādāya punar gṛhān agāt ।। gṛhya tāṃ dārikāṃ cāpi devakīśayane anyasat ।।
suptā eva tadā sarve rakṣiṇo viṣṇumāyayā । vasudevaḥ kṛtārtho vai nirjagāma niveśanāt ।। bahir antaḥ puradvāraḥ sarvāḥ pūrvavad āvṛtāḥ । tato bāladhvaniṃ śrutvā gṛhapālāḥ samutthitāḥ ।। te tu tūrṇam upavrajya devakyā garbhajanma tat । ācakhyur bhojarājāya yad udvignaḥ pratīkṣate । nivedayāmāsa tadā kanyāṃ tāṃ varavarṇinīm ।।
bhīto nivedayām āsa jātā naḥ kanyaketi ha । ājagāma gṛhadvāraṃ vasudevasya vīryavān ।। dīyatāṃ śīghram ity evaṃ vāgbhiḥ samabhitarjayat ।। uvāca devakī dīnā bāṣpaviklavayā girā ।
dārikā putra jāteti kaṃsaṃ tūvāca devakī ।। dārikeyaṃ hataivaiṣā paśyasva yadi manyase ।। hataivaiṣā yadā kanyā jātety uktvā vṛthāmatiḥ ।। kaṃsasya purato nyastā pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīsamā ।।
sāvadhūtā śilāpṛṣṭhe aniṣpiṣṭā divam utpatat ।। hāraśobhitasarvāṅgī mukuṭojjvalabhūṣitā । kanyaiva cābhavan nityaṃ divyā devair abhiṣṭutā ।। rathavistīrṇajaghanā candravaktrā caturbhujā ।।
payodharasvanavatī saṃdhyeva sapayodharā ।। nṛtyatī hasatī caiva viparītena bhāsvatī ।। jahāsa ca mahāhāsaṃ kaṃsaṃ ca ruṣitābravīt ।। sahasā ca samutkṣipya śilāyāṃ vinipātitā ।।
pāṭayitvā karair deham uṣṇaṃ pāsyāmi śoṇitam ।। khaṃ sā devālayaṃ devī sagaṇā vicacāra ha ।। sā kanyā vavṛdhe atra vṛṣṇisadmani pūjitā । putravat pālyamānā sā devī devājñayā tadā ।। viddhi caināṃ athotpannām aṃśād devīṃ prajāpateḥ । ekānaṃśāṃ yogakanyāṃ rakṣārthaṃ keśavasya tu ।। tāṃ vai sarve sumanasaḥ pūjayanti sā yādavāḥ । devavaddivyavapuṣaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃrakṣito yayā । ekānaṃśeti yām āhur utpannāṃ mānavā bhuvi । vivikte devakīṃ caiva vrīḍitaḥ pratyabhāṣata ।।
anyathaivānyato devi mama mṛtyuḥ samutthitaḥ ।। daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa na cātikrāntavān aham ।। hetubhūtas tv ahaṃ teṣāṃ sati kālaviparyaye ।। kālo nayati sarvaṃ vai hetubhūtaś ca madvidhaḥ ।।
āgamiṣyanti vai devi yathābhāgam upadravaḥ । idaṃ tu kaṣṭaṃ yaj jantuḥ kartāham iti manyate । evaṃprāyā nṛṇāṃ yonir nāsti kālasya saṃsthitiḥ ।। madgatas tyajyatāṃ roṣo jānāmy apakṛtaṃ svayam ।। ity uktavantaṃ kaṃsaṃ sā devakī vākyam abravīt ।
uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha vatseti kaṃsaṃ māteva jalpatī ।। kāraṇaṃ tvaṃ na vai putra kṛtānto hy atra kāraṇam ।। mūrdhnā padbhyāṃ nipatatā svaṃ ca karma jugupsatā ।। yuvāpi mṛtyor vaśagaḥ sthaviro mṛta eva tu ।।
kālamūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ hetubhūtas tvam eva hi । jāto apy ajātatāṃ yāti vidhātrā yatra nīyate ।। mṛtyunāpahṛte pūrvaṃ śeṣo hetuḥ pravartate ।। mātāpitros tu kāryeṇa janmatas tūpapadyate ।।
praviveśa susaṃrabdho dahyamānena cetasā । kṛtye pratihate dīno jagāma vimanā bhṛśam ।। svavadhaṃ cintyamānas tu kanyāvākyam anusmaran । prajātāṃ putram evāgre candrāt kāntatarānanam ।।
gacchānayā saha tvaṃ tu vrajam eva yaśodayā ।। yadā ca rohiṇī putraṃ prasūtā kamalekṣaṇā । yaśodāpi tadaiveyaṃ prasūtā tanayaṃ vibho । rauhiṇeyaṃ ca me putraṃ parirakṣa śiśuṃ vraje ।। pālayasva tadā tāta pramādabahule vraje ।
bālye caṇḍatamaḥ sarvas tatra yatnaparo bhava ।। yo aham ekasya putrasya na paśyāmi śiśor mukham ।। asmād dhi me bhayaṃ kaṃsān nirghṛṇād vai śiśor vadhe ।। vighnā hi bahavo loke bālān uttrāsayanti hi ।।
ubhāv api samaṃ premṇā nirīkṣasva yathāsukham ।। śobhetāṃ govraje tasmin nandagopa tathā kuru ।। tatrāsau vasati krūro māṃsabhojī durātmavān । tatra vāse tu bhetavyaṃ keśinaḥ pāpadarśinaḥ ।।
goṣṭheṣu gobhyo vatsebhyo rakṣyau te dvāv imau śiśū ।। yamunā naiva gantavyā tasyāṃ vasati kāliyaḥ । ime tvāṃ tvarayantīha pakṣiṇaḥ savyadakṣiṇāḥ ।। yānaṃ yaśodayā sārdham āruroha mudā yutaḥ ।।
śayane taṃ śiśuṃ caiva saṃveśya mṛdusaṃstare । saṃveśayāmāsa śiśuṃ śayanīye mahāmatiḥ ।। bahūdakena mārgena yamunātīraśobhinā ।। yamunātīrasaṃbaddhaṃ śītamārutasevitam ।।
gobhis tṛṇanimagnābhiḥ syandantībhir alaṃkṛtam ।। viṣāṇaskandhaghātaiś ca vṛṣāṇāṃ ghṛṣṭapādapam ।। sṛgālamṛgasiṃhaiś ca vasāmedośibhir vṛtam ।। svādupuṣpaphalaṃ ramyaṃ paryāptatṛṇasaṃstaram ।।
hambhāravaiś ca vatsānāṃ sarvataḥ kṛtanisvanam ।। paryanteśv āvṛtaṃ vanyair bṛhadbhiḥ patitair drumaiḥ ।। karīṣākīrṇavasudhaṃ kaṭacchannakuṭīmaṭham ।। dāmanīprāyabahulaṃ gargarodgāranisvanam ।।
navanītaparikṣiptam ājyagandhavibhūṣitam । manthānavalayodgārair gopīnāṃ janitasvanam ।। dārakair dārikābhiś ca parasparasamākulam । sarpiṣā pacyamānena surabhīkṛtamārutam ।।
vanyapuṣpāvataṃsābhir gopakanyābhir āvṛtam ।। sīmantamadhurālāpāḥ smitabhrūlalitekṣaṇāḥ । sītkārabhrūvilāsaiś ca cetobuddhimanoharāḥ । sarvās tāś candravadanā gopanāryaḥ suśobhanāḥ ।। tāsāṃ nūpuraśabdena mekhalānāṃ svanena ca । svanantīnāṃ ca śabdena mayūrā nanṛtus tadā । yamunātīramārgeṇa jalahārībhir āvṛtam ।। takravikrayayuktābhir dadhisarpiḥkrayeṣu ca ।
niveśaṃ rocayāmāsa parivarte sukhāśraye ।। tatra taṃ bālasūryābhaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gūḍhaṃ nyaveśayat ।। vasudevaprayuktaś ca tayor gargo mahātapāḥ । akaroj jātakarmādyāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā yathākramam । brāhmaṇebhyo dhanaṃ dattvā bhojanaṃ ca yathākramam । gopāś caivotsavaṃ cakrur gobhyo viprebhya eva ca । govraje nandagopasya ballavatvaṃ prakurvataḥ ।।
[gargo] gopakule tatra vasudevapracoditaḥ । pracchanna eva gopānāṃ saṃskārān akarot tayoḥ । jyeṣṭhaḥ saṃkarṣaṇo nāma yavīyān kṛṣṇa eva tu ।। vyavardhata gavāṃ madhye sāgarasya ivāmbudaḥ ।। vistareṇātha vakṣyāmi bālasya caritaṃ mahat । avadhānaparo bhūtvā śṛṇu rājan yad icchasi ।। sa tatra yogam āsthāya dānavāṃś cāvadhīt kila ।। kaścid danoḥ suto vīraḥ kṛṣṇasya vadhakāṅkṣayā । nandasya priyatām āyāc chākaṭaṃ vapur udvahan ।
yaśodā taṃ samutsṛjya jagāma yamunāṃ nadīm ।। aṅguṣṭham āsye nikṣipya pādābhyāṃ paricikṣipan । hāsyaṃ kurvañ śiśuḥ kṛṣṇo netrābhyāṃ parivibhraman ।। karaṃ kareṇa saṃpīḍya pādaṃ pādena pīḍayan ।
anekābhiḥ sa līlābhir lokāṃs tadgatamānasān । kalmaṣaṃ kṣālayan viṣṇus tadgatāsaktacetasām । ruroda madhuraṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pādāv ūrdhvaṃ prasārayan ।। añjanena parikṣiptaṃ mukham unnamayan hariḥ ।
nyubjaṃ payodharākāṅkṣī cakāra ca ruroda ca ।। snātā prasnavadigdhāṅgī baddhavatseva saurabhī ।। hāheti kṛtvā tvaritā dārakaṃ jagṛhe tadā ।। svasti me dārakāyeti prītyā bhītā ca sābhavat ।।
tvayy adhaḥ śakaṭe supte śakaṭe ca viloḍite ।। paryaste śakaṭe putra yā tvā paśyāmy apāvṛtam ।। kāṣāye vāsasī bibhran nandagopo vrajāntikam ।। apāstadhūrvibhagnākṣaṃ śakaṭaṃ cakramāli vai ।।
api me svasti putrāyety asakṛd vacanaṃ vadan ।। vṛṣayuddhaṃ vinā kena paryastaṃ śakaṭaṃ mama ।। na vijānāmy ahaṃ kena śakaṭaṃ pātitaṃ bhuvi ।। āgatā ca viparyastam apaśyaṃ śakaṭaṃ bhuvi ।।
asmābhiḥ saṃpatadbhis tu dṛṣṭam etad yadṛcchayā ।। nandagopas tu tac chrutvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayau । prahṛṣṭaś caiva bhītaś ca kim etad iti cintayan । na ca te śraddadhur gopāḥ sarve mānuṣabuddhayaḥ । svasthāne śakaṭaṃ caiva cakrabandham akārayan ।। nando aṅkam enam āropya bhūreṇuṃ parigṛhya ca । pradakṣiṇaṃ śiraḥ kurvan mantram etaj jajāpa ha । viṣṇus te pūrvataḥ pātu rudro rakṣatu dakṣiṇam । brahmā ca paścimaṃ pāyāt skando rakṣatv athottaram । upariṣṭāt tathā sūryaḥ pāyāc cādhaś ca vāsukiḥ । pāyāc ca tvām atho vatsa śiṣṭāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ samīraṇaḥ । svastiṃ karotu bhagavān pinākī vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ । gāvo rakṣantu sarvatra bhūmiḥ pātu sadāśivaḥ । evam uccārya nandas tu kṛṣṇaṃ pasparśa sarvaśaḥ । sa eva mantro bālānāṃ rakṣāyai parikīrtitaḥ । kasyacit tv atha kālasya sakunīveṣadhāriṇī ।
pūtanā nāma śakunī thorā prāṇabhayaṃkarī । ājagāmārdharātre vai pakṣau krodhād vidhunvatī । tasmai stanaṃ durjaravīryam ulbaṇaṃ । ghorāṅkam ādāya śiśor dadāv atha ।
gāḍhaṃ karābhyāṃ bhagavān prapīḍya । prāṇaiḥ samaṃ roṣasamanvito apibat ।। sā muñca muñca bālam iti prabhāṣiṇī । niṣpīḍyamānākhilajīvamarmaṇi ।
vivṛtya netre caraṇau bhujau muhur । viklinnagātrā kṣipatī ruroda ha ।। tasyāḥ svanenātigabhīraraṃhasā । sādrir mahī dyauś ca cacāla sagrahā ।
rasā diśaś ca pratinedire janāḥ । petuḥ kṣitau vajranipātaśaṅkayā ।। niśācarītthaṃ vyathitastanā vyasur । vistārya keśāṃś caraṇau bhujāv api ।
prasārya goṣṭhe nijarūpam āśritā । vajrāhato vṛtra ivāpatan nṛpa ।। patamāno api taddehas trigavyūtyantaradrumān । cūrṇayām āsa rājendra mahad āsīt tad adbhutam ।।
īṣāmātrogradaṃṣṭrāsyaṃ girikandaranāsikam । gaṇḍaśailastanaṃ raudraṃ prakīrṇāruṇamūrdhajam । andhakūpagabhīrākṣaṃ pulinārohabhīṣaṇam । baddhasetubhujorvaṅghri śūnyatoyahradodaram ।
bālaṃ ca tasyā urasi krīḍantam akutobhayam । gopyas tūrṇaṃ samabhyetya jagṛhur jātasaṃbhramāḥ ।। yaśodārohiṇībhyāṃ tāḥ samaṃ bālasya sarvataḥ । rakṣām vidadhire samyag gopucchabhramaṇādibhiḥ ।।
gomūtreṇa snāpayitvā punar gorajasārbhakam । rakṣāṃ cakruś ca śakṛtā dvādaśāṅgeṣu nāmabhiḥ । tato ardharātrasamaye śakuniḥ pratyadṛśyata ।। nililye śakaṭākṣe sā prasnavotpīḍavarṣiṇī ।।
tasyāḥ stanaṃ papau kṛṣṇaḥ prāṇaiḥ saha nanāda ca ।। stanyaṃ tadviṣasaṃmiśraṃ rasyam āsīj jagadguroḥ । patantīṃ tāṃ tu saṃdṛśya śakunīṃ bhayaviklavām । prayāṇe śīghracapalāṃ vāśamānāṃ ca visvaram । pādāṅguṣṭena tāṃ kṛṣṇaś cakrākrāntām akārayat । cakrākrāntā tu śakunī papāta ca mamāra ca । nanāda ca mahānādaṃ punaḥ punar asau hariḥ । sa nandagopo gopāś ca yaśodā ca suviklavā ।। śakuniṃ nihatāṃ bhūmau vajreṇeva vidāritām ।।
nandagopaṃ puraskṛtya gopās taṃ paryavārayan ।। nādhyagacchanta ca tadā hetuṃ tatra kadācana । āścaryam āścaryam iti bruvanto anuyayur gṛhān । yaśodāṃ nandagopas tu papracchāgatasaṃbhramaḥ ।। putrasya me bhayaṃ bhīru bhīrutvaṃ samupāgatam ।।
dārakeṇa sahānena suptā śabdena bodhitā ।। kaṃsād bhayaṃ cakārograṃ vismayaṃ ca jagāma ha ।। pañca saṃvatsarān prāptau śobhayānau vrajaṃ muhuḥ । kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇau cobhau riṅginau samapadyatām ।।
ekamantradharau kāntau bālacandrārkavarcasau ।। ekaveṣadharāv ekaṃ puṣyamāṇau śiśuvratam ।। ekacaryau mahāvīryāv ekasya śiśutāṃ gatau ।। kṛtsnasya jagato gopau saṃvṛttau gopadārakau ।।
anyonyakiraṇagrastau candrasūryāv ivāmbare ।। rejatuḥ pāṃśudigdhāṅgau dṛptau kalabhakāv iva ।। tau tatra paridhāvetāṃ kumārāv iva pāvakī ।। krīḍantau vatsaśālāsu śakṛddigdhāṅgamūrdhajau ।।
janaṃ ca vipra kurvāṇau hasantau ca kvacit kvacit ।। rejatuś candravadanau dārakau sukumārakau ।। atiprasaktau ghoṣeṣu ghoṣam āpūrya dārakau । nāśaknuvad vārayitum nandagopaḥ sudurmadau ।।
uvāca śiśurūpeṇa carantaṃ jagataḥ prabhum । ehi vatsa piba stanyaṃ durvoḍhuṃ mama saṃprati ।। etāvantam itaḥ kālaṃ kvā gato asi gṛhād bahiḥ । ity ādāya kare putraṃ gṛhān nirvāsya sā ruṣā ।
ānāyya śakaṭīmūlaṃ bhartsayantī punaḥ punaḥ ।। vyagrāyām tu yaśodāyām nirjagāma tato aṅgaṇāt ।। so aṅgaṇān niḥsṛtaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ karṣamāṇa udūkhalam ।। niścakrāma śiśur madhyāt karṣamāṇa udūkhalam ।।
lagnaṃ tābhyāṃ samūlābhyām arjunābhyāṃ cakarṣa ha ।। samūlaviṭapau bhagnau sa tu madhye jahāsa vai ।। tad dāma tasya bālasya prabhāvād abhavad dṛḍham ।। krandantyo vismayantyaś ca yaśodānikaṭaṃ yayuḥ ।।
ehy āgaccha yaśodeti saṃbhrame kiṃ vilambase ।। tāv etau tava putrasya patitāv upari drumau । putrasyopari tāv etau patitau te mahīruhau ।। jahāsa madhye vṛkṣābhyāṃ tava putraḥ sa bālakaḥ ।।
prahasann eva vṛkṣābhyāṃ madhye krīḍann ivāṅgaṇe । putram ānaya jīvantuṃ muktaṃ mṛtyumukhād iva ।। taṃ deśam agamad yatra patitau tau mahādrumau ।। dāmnā nibaddham udare karṣamāṇam udūkhalam ।।
paryagacchat tato draṣṭuṃ gopeṣu mahad adbhutam ।। jajalpur jātasaṃbhrāntā sarve vismitacetasaḥ । kenemau pātitau vṛkṣau ghoṣasyaivāgrapādapau ।। vinā hastikṛtaṃ doṣam kenemau pātitau drumau ।।
imau nipatitau bhūmau vitoyau jaladāv iva ।। yadīmau ghoṣaracitau ghoṣakalyāṇakāriṇau । yatra te dārako mukto vimūlābhyām avikṣataḥ ।। pūtanāyā nipātaś ca drumayoḥ śakaṭasya ca ।।
utpātā hy atra dṛśyante kathayanto naśobhanam ।। niveśya cāṅke suciraṃ mṛtaṃ punar ivāgatam ।। nātṛpyat prekṣamāṇo vai kṛṣṇaṃ kamalalocanam । sa ca gopajanaḥ sarvo ghoṣam eva jagāma ha ।।
yena dāmnā nibaddho asāv udare sudṛḍhaṃ vraje । ghoṣe dāmodara iti gopībhiḥ parigīyate ।। kṛṣṇasya bharataśreṣṭha ghoṣe nivasatas tadā ।। tasminn eva vrajasthāne saptavarṣau babhūvatuḥ ।।
babhūvatur vatsapālau kākapakṣadharāv ubhau ।। gopavīthyāṃ sumadhuraṃ gāyantau kāmarūpiṇau । śuśubhāte vanagatau triśīrṣāv iva pannagau ।। vanamālākṛtoraskau drumapotāv ivodgatau ।।
saśikyatumbakarakau gopaveṇaupravādakau ।। parṇavādyasamāyuktau dadhyodanakarau kṛtī । kiṃkiṇījālasaṃbaddhakaṭideśavibhūṣitau ।। kakṣakūṭasamālambiśikyasthadhṛtapāyasau । kālayantau ca daṇḍena vatsān vatsau diśaṃ prati ।। gulmeṣu madhumādhvīkaṃ mārgamāṇāvitas tataḥ । khādantau vanyamūlāni pibantau madhumākṣikam ।। dadatau madhumūlāni dārakebhyaḥ samantataḥ । khādantau khādayantau ca mūlāni ca phalāni ca ।। tindukaṃ bhakṣayantu ca gopair āpatya bhūtale । kīlair āpatya vṛkṣebhyaḥ khādayantu phalāni ca । dadhyodanaṃ prabhuñjānau kvacit kakṣavilambitam । kvacic ca pānasaṃbhrāntau kvacit pāyasamoditau ।
kvacid vṛkṣeṣu viśrāntau sthalīṣv iva yathāsukham । parṇaśayyāsu saṃsuptau kvacin nidrāntaraiṣiṇau ।। vatsān anu yathākāmaṃ carantau vatsapālakau । vatsapucchān samādhūya vikṣiptantau pṛthak pṛthak । evaṃ tu vatsapālau tau śobhayām āsatur vanam ।
cañcūryantau ramantau sma kiśorāv iva cañcalau ।। gāyantu ca kvacid geyān susvaraṃ madhurasvaram । utkarṇaṃ mṛgasaṃghaṃ ca kurvantau gītanisvanaiḥ ।। gajān paravaśān geyaiḥ kurvantau ca gahāvane । lokam itthaṃ carantau ca ramayantau ca ceṣṭitaiḥ । ārya nāsmin vane śakyaṃ gopālaiḥ saha krīḍitum ।। prakṣīṇatṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca gopair mathitapādapam ।।
tāny ākāśanikāśāni dṛśyante adya yathāsukham ।। sarve goṣṭhāgniṣu gatāḥ kṣayam akṣayavarcasaḥ ।। tāni dūrāvakṛṣṭāni mārgitavyāni bhūmiṣu ।। akarmaṇyeṣu vṛkṣeṣu sthitaviprasthitadvijam ।।
saṃvāsasyāsya mahato janenotsāditadrumam । nirvihaṃgam idaṃ śūnyaṃ nirvyañjanam ivāśanam ।। utsannasaṃcayatṛṇo ghoṣo ayaṃ nagarāyate ।। vanānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ gāvas tāś cāsmākaṃ parā gatiḥ ।
tasmād anyad vanaṃ yāmaḥ pratyagravayasendhanam ।। tasmād vanaṃ navatṛṇaṃ gacchantu dhanino vrajāḥ ।। praśastā vai vrajā loke yathā vai cakracāriṇaḥ ।। na tṛṇaṃ bhuñjate gāvo nāpi tatpayaso hitam ।।
carāmaḥ sahitā gobhiḥ kṣipraṃ saṃvāhyatāṃ vrajaḥ ।। nāmnā vṛndāvanaṃ nāma svāduvṛkṣaphalodakam ।। kadambapādapaprāyaṃ yamunātīrasaṃśritam ।। gopīnāṃ sukhasaṃcāraṃ cārucitravanāntaram ।।
bhrājate dīrghaśikharo nandanasyeva mandaraḥ ।। bhāṇḍīro nāma śuśubhe nīlamegha ivāmbare ।। prayātā nandanasyeva nalinī saritāṃ varā ।। kālindīṃ ca nadīṃ ramyāṃ drakṣyāvaś carataḥ sukham ।।
sukhaṃ carantaṃ drakṣyāvaḥ kālindīṃ ca nadīṃ śubhām । saṃvāhayāma bhadraṃ te kiṃcid utpādya kāraṇam ।। prādurbabhūvuḥ śataśo raktamāṃsavasāśanāḥ ।। viniṣpetur bhayakarāḥ sarvataḥ śataśo vṛkāḥ ।।
niṣpatanti sma bahavo vrajasyotsādanāya vai । gopīṣu ca yathākāmaṃ vraje trāso abhavan mahān ।। triṃśadviṃśatibaddhāś ca śatabaddhās tathāpare ।। pañcāśatṣaṣṭibaddhāś ca catvāriṃśat tathaiva ca ।
kṛṣṇasya kṛṣṇavadanā gopānāṃ bhayavardhanāḥ ।। niśi bālān haradbhiś ca vṛkair utsādyate vrajaḥ ।। na vanāt kiṃcid āhartuṃ na ca vā tarituṃ nadīm ।। trastā hy udvignamanaso gatās tasmin vane avasan ।
vrajo niṣpandaceṣṭaḥ sa ekasthānacaraḥ kṛtaḥ ।। sastrīpuṃso atha ghoṣo vai samasto amantrayat tadā ।। yan nirbhayaṃ sukhakaraṃ sukhasaṃcāramārutam । yac chivaṃ ca sukhāḍhyaṃ ca gavāṃ caiva sukhāvaham ।।
yāvad vṛkair vadhaṃ ghoraṃ na naḥ sarvo vrajo vrajet ।। vṛkāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavaktrāṇāṃ bibhīmo niśi garjatām ।। vṛkair vyāpāditety evaṃ krandanti sma gṛhe gṛhe ।। vrajasyotthāpanaṃ cakrur ghoṣavṛddhāḥ samāgatāḥ ।।
vrajasya ca niveśāya gavāṃ caiva sukhāya ca ।। nandagopo bṛhadvākyaṃ bṛhaspatir ivādade ।। śīghram ājñāpyatāṃ ghoṣaḥ sajjībhavata māciram ।। śīghram gāvaḥ prakālyantāṃ yujyantāṃ śakaṭāni ca ।।
vṛndāvanam itaḥ sthānān niveśāya ca gamyatām ।। tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya nandagopasya bhāṣitam । udatiṣṭhad vrajaḥ sarvaḥ śīghraṃ gamanalālasaḥ ।। uttiṣṭhati vraje tasmin gopakolāhalo hy abhūt ।।
vyāghraghoṣamahāghoṣo ghoṣaḥ sāgaraghoṣavān ।। niṣpapāta vrajāt paṅktis tārāpaṅktir ivāmbarāt ।। śakracāpāyate paṅktir gopīnāṃ mārgagāminī ।। gopā mārgagatā bhānti sāvarohā iva drumāḥ ।।
oghaiḥ pavanavikṣiptair niṣpatadbhir ivārṇavaḥ ।। dravyāvayanirdhūtaṃ kīrṇaṃ vāyasamaṇḍalaiḥ ।। niveśaṃ vipulaṃ cakre niveśāya gavāṃ hitam ।। madhye yojanavistāraṃ tāvad dviguṇam āyatam ।।
nikhātocchritaśākhāgrair abhiguptaṃ samantataḥ ।। adbhiḥ prakṣālyamānābhir gargarībhis tatas tataḥ ।। stambhanībhir dhṛtaiś cāpi śakaṭaiḥ parivartitaiḥ ।। chādanārthaṃ prakīrṇaiś ca kaṭais tṛṇagṛhais tathā ।।
śodhamānair gavāṃ sthānaiḥ sthāpyamānair udūkhalaiḥ ।। savatsacarmāstaraṇaiḥ paryaṅkaiś cāvaropitaiḥ ।। śākhāś cākarṣamāṇābhir gopībhiś ca samantataḥ ।। viśasadbhiḥ kuṭhāraiś ca kāṣṭhāny api tarūn api ।।
ramyaṃ vananiveśaṃ vai svabhivṛṣṭyāmṛtopamam ।। vṛndāvanam anuprāptā nandanopamakānanam ।। śivena manasā dṛṣṭaṃ tadvanaṃ vanacāriṇā ।। varṣatīvāmṛtaṃ deve tṛṇaṃ tatravyavardhata ।।
yatra tiṣṭhati lokānāṃ bhavāya madhusūdanaḥ ।। kṛṣṇena vihitaṃ vāsaṃ tam adhyāsanta nirvṛtāḥ ।। yatra tiṣṭhati deveśo devadevo janārdanaḥ । na tatra prāṇināṃ duḥkhaṃ sa ca sarvasukhāvahaḥ । ceratur vatsayūthāni cārayantau sunirvṛttau ।।
krīḍatoḥ saha gopālair yamunāṃ cāvagāhatoḥ ।। gate tasmin mahāgharme rajaḥpūrais tirohitaiḥ । babhūvādarśanaḥ sūryo bhūmiś cādarśayat tṛṇam ।। saṃmārjitatalā bhūmir yauvanastheva lakṣyate ।।
naṣṭadāvāgnidhūmāni vavāni pracakāśire ।। madaraktāḥ pravṛttāś ca kekāḥ paṭuravāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। yauvanasthaṃ kadambānāṃ navābhrair bhrājate vapuḥ ।। trāsitaṃ jaladair uṣṇaṃ toṣitā vasudhā jalaiḥ ।।
jalair balāhakotsṛṣṭair ucchvasantīva parvatāḥ ।। mahīmahārajaḥpūrais tulyam āpadyate nabhaḥ ।। saṃpradīptaṃ ivābhāti phullanīpadrumaṃ vanam ।। pārthivaṃ gandham āghrāya lokaḥ kṣubhitamānasaḥ ।।
navaiś ca śikhivikruṣṭair ekavarṇā vasuṃdharā ।। haryantas tīrajān vṛksān vistarāṃ yānti nimnagāḥ ।। na tyajanty agamāgrāṇi śrāntā iva patatriṇaḥ ।। udareṣu navābhrāṇāṃ majjatīva divākaraḥ ।।
anveṣyamārgā vasudhā bhāti śāḍvalamālinī ।। srotobhiḥ parikṛttāni patanti śikharāṇi ca ।। palvalodgīrṇaraktena pūryante vanarājayaḥ ।। bhāntyātivṛṣṭyā mātaṅgā gāṃ gatā iva toyadāḥ ।।
rauhiṇeyo mithaḥ kāle kṛṣṇaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। gagane tava gātrāṇāṃ varṇacorān samutthitān ।। kāmināṃ hṛdayasyāśu nighnatas tān samantataḥ । tvam ivājñātavasatiṃ candro vasati vārṣikīm ।।
nīlotpaladale kāle bhāti vṛndāvanaṃ vanam । saṃprāpte durdine kāle durdinaṃ bhāti vai nabhaḥ ।। govardhano yathā ramyo bhāti govardhano giriḥ ।। bhrājante kṛṣṇasāraṅgāḥ kānaneṣu mudānvitāḥ ।।
tṛṇāni śatapatrākṣa patrair gūhanti medinīm ।। sasasyānāṃ ca sīmānāṃ na lakṣmīr vyatiricyate ।। dāmodaroddāmaravāḥ prāgalbhyaṃ yānti toyadāḥ ।। vibāṇajyena dhanuṣā tavedaṃ madhyamaṃ padam ।।
meghaiḥ śītātapakaro viraśmir iva raśmimān ।। avyavacchinnadhāraughaiḥ samudraughanibhair ghanaiḥ ।। gandhaiḥ kolāhalā vānti vātā madanadīpanāḥ ।। bhāty agādham aparyantaṃ sasāgaram ivāmbaram ।।
śakracāpāyudhadharaṃ yuddhasajjam ivāmbaram ।। praticchannāni bhāsante śikharāṇi ghanair ghanaiḥ ।। varṇasārūpyatāṃ yāti gaganaṃ sāgarasya vai ।। śītāh sapṛṣatodgārāḥ karkaśā vānti mārutāḥ ।।
magnasūryasya nabhaso nābhibhānti diśo daśa ।। cetanaṃ puṣkaraṃ kośaiḥ kṣudhādhmātaiḥ samantataḥ । na ghṛṇīnāṃ na ramyāṇāṃ vivekaṃ yānti kṛṣṭayaḥ । saṃhatānāṃ dvirephānāṃ niveśaṃ yānti paṅkayaḥ । paśya vṛndāvanaṃ kṛṣṇa vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ yathā ।। kathayann eva balavān vrajam eva jagāma ha ।।
tatkālaṃ jñātibhiḥ sārdhaṃ ceratus tau mahad vanam ।। cacāra tadvanavaraṃ kāmarūpī varānanaḥ ।। śrīvatsenorasā yuktaḥ śaśāṅka iva lakṣmaṇā ।। sukumārābhitāmreṇa krāntavikrāntagāminā ।।
sūkṣme vasāno vasane sasaṃdhya iva toyadaḥ ।। bhujābhyāṃ sādhuvṛttābhyāṃ pūjitābhyāṃ divaukasaiḥ ।। rarāja tasya tadbālye ruciroṣṭhapuṭaṃ mukham ।। vṛttaṃ ṣaṭpadapaṅktībhir yathā syāt padmamaṇḍalam ।।
rarāja mālā śirasi nakṣatrāṇāṃ yathā divi ।। meghakālāmbudaśyāmo nabhasya iva mūrtimān ।। rarāja barhipatreṇa mandamārutakampinā ।। parṇavādyaṃ śrutisukhaṃ vādayānaḥ kvacid vane ।।
gokule ambudharaśyāmaś cacāra dyutimān prabhuḥ ।। govardhanasya ca gireḥ parṇavādyaṃ śruteḥ sukham । meghanādaprativyūhair nāditāsu samantataḥ ।। kandalāmaladantīṣu sravantīṣu navaṃ jalam ।।
abhīkṣṇaṃ niḥśvasantīṣu yoṣitsv iva samantataḥ ।। tāsu kṛṣṇo mudaṃ lebhe saumyāsu vanarājiṣu ।। dadarśa vipulodagraṃ śākhinaṃ śākhināṃ varam ।। gaganārdhocchritākāraṃ pavanābhogakāriṇaṃ ।।
phalaiḥ pravālaiś ca ghanaṃ sendracāpaghanopamam ।। viśālamūlāvatataṃ pavanāmbhodadhāriṇam ।। kurvāṇaṃ śubhakarmāṇaṃ tiro varṣantam avyayam ।। dṛṣṭvā tatra matiṃ cakre nivāsāya divā prabhuḥ ।।
reme vai divasaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ purā svargagato yathā ।। ramayanti sma bahavo vanyaiḥ krīḍanakais tadā ।। gopālāḥ kṛṣṇam evānye gāyanti sma ratipriyāḥ ।। parṇavādyāntare veṇuṃ tumbīvīṇāṃ ca tatra ha ।।
jagāma yamunātīraṃ latālaṃkṛtapādapam ।। tāṃ ca padmotpalavatīṃ dadarśa yamunāṃ nadīm ।। toyavātoddhatair vegair avanāmitapādapām ।। anyonyamithunaiś caiva sevitāṃ mithunecaraiḥ ।।
jalajaiḥ kusumaiś citrāṃ jalajair haritodakām ।। āvartanābhigambhīrāṃ padmalomānurañjitām ।। cakravākastanataṭāṃ tīrapārśvāyatānanām ।। mīnākṣicapalāṃ kāntāṃ kāntaśaivalamūrdhajām ।
rucirotpalapatrākṣīṃ natabhrūṃ jalajekṣaṇām ।। dīrghasrotāyatabhujām ābhogaśravaṇāyatām ।। kāśacāmīkaraṃ vāso vasānāṃ haṃsalakṣaṇām ।। vāriplavaplavakṣaumāṃ sārasārāvanūpurām ।।
śvāpadocchiṣṭasalilām āśramasthānasaṃkulām ।। siddhārādhyamahādeva sikatāliṅgamaṇḍitām । munimṛtkuṇḍikāpūra samūdbhūtamahāravām । siddhayoṣit kucasrasta kuṅkumakṣodapiṅgalām । sutīrthāṃ sarvapāpaghnīṃ nṛṇāṃ tadgatacetasām । cacāra ruciraṃ kṛṣṇo yamunām upaśobhayan ।। dīrghaṃ yojanavistāraṃ dustaraṃ tridaśair api ।।
toyapaiḥ śvāpadais tyaktaṃ śūnyaṃ toyacaraiḥ khagaiḥ ।। duḥkhopasarpyaṃ tīreṣu sasarpair vipulair bilaiḥ ।। viṣāraṇigatasyāgner dhūmena pariveṣṭitam ।। ākāśād apy asaṃcāryaṃ khagair ākāśagocaraiḥ ।।
samantād yojanaṃsāgraṃ tīreṣv api durāsadam ।। vajrasyottaratas tasya krośamātre nirāmaye ।। agādhaṃ dyotamānaṃ ca kasyedaṃ sumahad dhradam ।। uragādhipatiḥ sākṣād dhrade vasati dārunaḥ ।।
bhayāt patagarājasya suparṇasyoragāśinaḥ ।। bhayāt tasyoragapater nāyaṃ deśo niṣevyate ।। sāvarohadrumaṃ ghoraṃ kīrṇaṃ nānālatādrumaiḥ ।। tair āptakāribhir nityaṃ sarvataḥ parirakṣitam ।।
kartavyamārgau bhrājete hradasyāsya taṭāv ubhau ।। yathevaṃ saridambhodā bhavec chivajalāśayā ।। ayaṃ ca sevyaḥ kartavyo hradaḥ śītajalāśraya । sa saṃkarṣaṇaṃ āmantrya keśavas tv idam abravīt । ātmānam ātmano vākyaṃ provāca sa priyaṃvadaḥ । idaṃ vanaṃ nadī ceyaṃ śaraṇyam iti me matiḥ । na nisarpanti dṛśyante sattvānīha mahītale । sarvartusukhasaṃcārā sarvatīrthasukhāśrayā ।।
amīṣām utpathasthānāṃ śāsanārthaṃ durātmanām ।। vinipatya hrade ghore damayiṣyāmi kāliyam ।। evaṃ kṛte bāhuvīryaṃ loke khyātiṃ gamiṣyati । mama jpādatalasparśād dīrghajīvī bhaved ayam । kadambaḥ puṣpaphalavān samārādhyaś ca matpriyaiḥ ।। so ayaṃ kadambaśikharaḥ sarvaprāṇisukhāvahaḥ । adyāpi bhrājate viṣṇoḥ pādasaṃsparśaśobhayā । ārohac capalaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kadambaśikharaṃ yuvā ।।
hradamadhye akaroc chabdaṃ nipatann ambujekṣaṇaḥ ।। nīlotpaladalaśyāmo hrade tasmin papāta ha । saṃprāśicyata vegena bhidyamāna ivārṇavaḥ ।। uttiṣṭhad udakāt sarpo roṣaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ ।।
tato raktāntanayanaḥ kāliyaḥ samadṛśyata ।। pṛtubhiḥ pañcabhir ghoraiḥ śirobhiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। sphurann iva sa roṣeṇa jvalann iva ca tejasā ।। tasya krodhāgnipūrṇena vaktreṇābhūc ca mārutaḥ ।।
sadhūmāḥ pannagendrasya mukhān niścerur arciṣaḥ ।। kṣaṇena bhasmasān nītā yugāntapratimena vai ।। sadhūmāḥ pannagendrās te nipetur amitaujasaḥ ।। niryatnacaraṇākāras tasthau girir ivācalaḥ ।।
te kṛṣṇaṃ sarpapatayo na mamāra ca vīryavān ।। saṃdaśyamāno daśanair na cacāla sa keśavaḥ । vyacarat suciraṃ kālaṃ kṛṣṇo vai kāliye hrade । krandamānā vrajaṃ jagmur bāṣpasaṃdigdhayā girā ।। bhakṣyate sarparājena tad āgacchata māciram ।।
eṣa te kṛṣyate putraḥ sarpeṇeti mahāhrade ।। ārtaḥ skhalitavikrāntas taṃ jagāma hradottamam ।। ākrīḍaṃ pannagendrasya janas taṃ samupāgamat ।। idaṃ kiṃ tv iti saṃbhrāntāḥ kasyedaṃ karma ceti vai ।
hāhākāraṃ prakurvantas tasthus tīre hradasya vai ।। apare hā hatāḥ smeti rurudur bhṛśaduḥkhitāḥ ।। saṃditaṃ sarpabhogena kṛṣyamāṇaṃ yathā mṛgam ।। putraṃ katham imaṃ dṛṣṭvā yaśode nāvadīryate ।।
nyasya putramukhe dṛṣṭiṃ niścetanam avasthitam ।। praviśāmo na yāsyāmaḥ sarvā dāmodaraṃ vinā ।। vinā kṛṣṇaṃ na yāsyāmo vivatsā iva dhenavaḥ ।। vilāpaṃ nandagopasya yaśodāṃ rudatīṃ tathā ।
saṃkarṣaṇas tu saṃkruddho babhāṣe kṛṣṇam avyayam ।। damyatām eṣa vai kṣipraṃ sarparājo viṣāyudhaḥ ।। paridevanti karuṇam sarve mānuṣabuddhayaḥ ।। vikrīḍyāsphoṭayad bāhū tad bhittvā bhogabandhanam ।।
śiro asya kṛṣṇo jagrāha svahastenāvanāmya ca ।। so asya mūrdhni sthitaḥ kṛṣṇo nanarta rucirāṅgadaḥ ।। lāsyaṃ bahuvidhaṃ kṛṣṇo vidadhe tasya mūrdhani ।। tasya nṛttaṃ smaran viṣṇor harṣo adya mama jāyate । romṇāṃ sarveṣu gātreṣu rājann udgamayan sadā । asyaiḥ sarudhirodgāraiḥ kātaraṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
damito ahaṃ hataviṣo vaśagas te varānana ।। kasya vā vaśatāṃ yāmi jīvitaṃ me pradīyatām ।। namas te brahmarudrendra surāsuranamaskṛta । śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ prapanno asmi jīvitaṃ me pradīyatām ।। aparādhaṃ kṛtaṃ yat tu mūḍhenākṛtabuddhinā । darpānvitena ca mayā na tat saṃsmartum arhasi ।। prasanne tvayi deveśa vainateyo na māṃ haret । tasmād vidhatsva yat kāryaṃ mayā kartavyam īśvara । ity uktvā sa śirobhis tu kṛṣṇapādāv apūjayat । akruddha eva bhagavān pratyuvācorageśvaram ।।
gacchārṇavajalaṃ sarpa saputraḥ sahabāndhavaḥ ।। tava bhṛtyas tanūjo vā kṣipraṃ vadhyaḥ sa me bhavet ।। sthāne tv iha bhaved doṣas tavāntakaraṇo mahān ।। garudaḥ pannagaripus tvayi na prahariṣyati ।।
evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena patatrivaraketunā । paśyatām eva gopānāṃ jagāmādarśanaṃ hradāt ।। vismitās tuṣṭuvur gopāś cakruś caiva pradakṣiṇam ।। dhanyo asy anugṛhīto asi yasya te putra īdṛśaḥ ।।
āpatsu śaraṇaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prabhuś cāyatalocanaḥ ।। sarvais tīrthaiḥ sukhaṃ gāvo vicariṣyanti naḥ sadā ।। mahadbhūtaṃ na jānīmaś channam agnim iva vraje ।। jagmur gopagaṇā ghoṣaṃ devāś caitrarathaṃ yathā ।।
tam eva ceratur deśam sahitau rāmakeśavau ।। giriṃ govardhanaṃ ramyaṃ vasudevasutāv ubhau ।। dadṛśāte atha tau vīrau ramyaṃ tālavanaṃ mahat ।। ceratuḥ paramaprītau vṛṣapotāv ivodgatau ।।
darbhaprāyasthalībhūtaḥ sumahān kṛṣṇamṛttikaḥ ।। phalāgraśākhibhir bhāti nāgahastair ivocchritaiḥ ।। aho tālaphalaiḥ pakvair vāsiteyaṃ vanasthalī ।। tālapakvāni sahitau pātayāvo laghukramau ।।
rasenāmṛtakalpena bhaviṣyantīti me matiḥ ।। pātayaṃs tālapakvāni cālayām āsa tāṃs tarūn ।। nirmāṇabhūtam iriṇaṃ puruṣādālayopamam ।। pāṣāṇair atha rājendra bahubhiḥ parvatopamaiḥ । pakvāni caiva rājendra pātayām āsa kāmataḥ ।
kharayūthena mahatā vṛtaḥ samupasevate ।। nṛpakṣiśvāpadagaṇāṃs trāsayānaḥ sa durmatiḥ ।। nāmarṣayata saṃkruddhas tālasvanam iva dvipaḥ ।। stabdhākṣo heṣitapaṭuḥ khurair nirdārayan mahīm ।।
āpatann eva dadṛśe rauhiṇeyam avasthitam ।। rauhiṇeyaṃ kharo duṣṭaḥ so adaśad daśanāyudhaḥ ।। jaghānorasi daityaḥ sa rauhiṇeyaṃ nirāyudham ।। āvarjitamukhaskandhaṃ prairayat tālamūrdhani ।।
kharas tālaphalaiḥ sārdhaṃ papāta dharaṇītale ।। jñātīṃs tathāparāṃs tasya cikṣepa tṛṇarājani ।। te sarve tālapakvaiś ca nipetur dharaṇītale । babhāse channajaladā dyaur ivāvyaktaśāradī ।।
ramyaṃ tālavanaṃ tadd hi bhūyo ramyataraṃ babhau ।। caranti sma sukhaṃ gāvas tattālavanam uttamam ।। vītaśokā vanaṃ sarve cañcūryante sma te sukham ।। drumaparṇāsane kṛtvā tau yathārhaṃ niṣidatuḥ ।।
tattālavanam utsṛjya bhūyo bhāṇḍīraṃ āgatau ।। sphītasasyaprarūḍhāni vīkṣamāṇau vanāni ca ।। nāmabhir vyāharantau ca savatsā gāḥ paraṃtapau ।। vanamālākṛtoraskau bālaśṛṅgāv ivarṣabhau ।।
mahendrāyudhasaṃsaktau śuklakṛṣṇāv ivāmbudau ।। vanamārgeṣu kurvāṇau vanyaveṣadharāv ubhau ।। ceratur lokasiddhābhiḥ krīḍābhir aparājitau ।। tajjātiguṇayuktābhiḥ krīḍābhiś ceratur vanam ।।
prāptau paramaśākhāḍhyaṃ nyagrodhaṃ śākhināṃ varam ।। aśmabhiḥ kṣepaṇīyaiś ca tau vyāyāmam akurvatām ।। muditau siṃhavikrāntau yathākāmaṃ viceratuḥ ।। pralambo abhyāgamat teṣāṃ chidrānveṣī tayos tadā ।।
lobhayānaḥ sa tau vīrau hāsyaiḥ krīḍanakais tathā ।। mānuṣaṃ vapur āsthāya pralambo dānavottamaḥ ।। gopālavapuṣaṃ gopā manyamānāḥ svabāndhavam ।। dṛṣṭiṃ paridadhe kṛṣṇe rauhiṇeye ca dāruṇām ।।
rauhiṇeyavadhe yatnam akarod dānavottamaḥ ।। prakrīḍitāś ca te sarve dvau dvau yugapad utpatan ।। saṃkarṣaṇas tu plutavān pralambena sahānaghaḥ ।। pradrutā laṅghayanto vai te anyonyaṃ laghuvikramāḥ ।।
gopālaiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣīyair gopālās tv apare jitāḥ ।। bhāṇḍīraskandham uddiśya maryādāṃ punar āgaman ।। drutaṃ jagāma vimukhaḥ sacandra iva toyadaḥ ।। aviṣahyaṃ manyamānaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ dānavapuṃgavaḥ । vahan drutataraṃ prāgād avarohaṇataḥ param ।
vavṛdhe sumahākāyaś candrākrānta ivāmbudaḥ ।। svaṃ vapur darśayām āsa pralambo dānavottamaḥ ।। dīpyamānānano daityaḥ sūryākrānta ivāmbudaḥ ।। raudraḥ śakaṭacakrākṣo nāmayaṃs caraṇaiḥ kṣitim ।।
dhīraḥ pralambaḥ prayayau toyalamba ivāmbudaḥ ।। sāgaropaplavagataṃ kṛtsnaṃ lokam ivāntakaḥ ।। uhyamāna ivaikena kālameghena candramāḥ ।। daityaskandhagataḥ śrīmān kṛṣṇaṃ cedam uvāca ha ।।
pradarśayitvā mahatīm māyāṃ mānuṣarūpiṇīm ।। pralambasya pravṛddhasya darpād dviguṇavarcasaḥ ।। abhijño rauhiṇeyasya vṛttasya ca balasya ca ।। yas tvaṃ jaganmayaṃ guhyaṃ guhyād guhyataraṃ gataḥ ।।
avagacchātmanātmānam samudrāṇāṃ samāgame ।। ātmavṛttapravṛttāni saṃsmarādyaṃ ca vai vapuḥ ।। vāyur lokāyur ucchvāso manaḥsraṣṭā manus tava ।। sahasraśīrṣo viśvātmā śatajihvaḥ śatodaraḥ ।
sahasrapatranābhas tvaṃ sahasrāṃśudharo arihā ।। yat tvayā noktapūrvaṃ hi kas tad anveṣṭum arhati ।। viditaṃ yat tavaikasya devā api na tad viduḥ ।। yat tu te kṛtrimaṃ rūpaṃ tad arcanti divaukasaḥ ।।
yasya caivaṃvidhaṃ rūpaṃ paśyanti tridivaukasaḥ । tvaṃ hi sūkṣmo mahān ekaḥ sūkṣmair api durāsadaḥ ।। acalā prāṇināṃ yonir dhārayaty akhilaṃ jagat ।। caturyugeśo lokānāṃ cāturhotraphalāśanaḥ ।।
ubhāv ekaśarīrau svo jagadarthe dvidhā kṛtau ।। ahaṃ vā śāśvataḥ kṛṣṇas tvaṃ vā śeṣaḥ purātanaḥ । āvayor dehamātreṇa dvidhedaṃ dhāryate jagat ।। dvāv eva vihitau hy āvām ekadehau mahābalau ।।
mūrdhni devaripuṃ deva vajrakalpena muṣṭinā ।। sa balena tadā pūrṇas trailokyāntaracāriṇā ।। balenāyujyata tadā mahatānyena dīptimān । muṣṭinā vajrakalpena mūrdhni vīraḥ samāhanat ।।
tena muṣṭiprahāreṇa kapālaṃ tad dvidhābhavat । jānudbhyāṃ jagatīṃ caiva gatāsuḥ sa jagāma ha ।। pralambasyāmbarasthasya meghasyeva vidīryataḥ ।। bahugairikasaṃyuktaṃ śailaśṛṅgād ivodakam ।।
paryaṣvajata kṛṣṇaṃ vai rauhiṇeyaḥ pratāpavān ।। tuṣṭuvur nihate daitye jayāśīrbhir mahābalam ।। vicaranty aśarīriṇyo vācaḥ surasamīritāḥ । baladeveti nāmasya devaiś coktaṃ divi sthitaiḥ ।।
karmajaṃ nihate daitye devair api durāsade ।। vane vicarator māsau vyatiyātau sma vārṣikau ।। prāptaṃ śakramahaṃ vīrau gopāṃś cotsavalālasān ।। ko ayaṃ śakramaho nāma yena vo harṣa āgataḥ ।।
śrūyatāṃ tāta śakrasya yadarthaṃ maha iṣyate ।। tasya cāyaṃ kratuḥ kṛṣṇa lokapālasya śāśvataḥ ।। tasyaivājñākarāḥ sasyaṃ janayanti navāmbubhiḥ ।। saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān prīṇayaty akhilaṃ jagat ।।
vartayāmopabhujjānās tarpayāmaś ca devatāḥ ।। pṛthivyāṃ tarpitāyāṃ ca sāmṛtaṃ lakṣyate jagat ।। tena saṃvardhitā gāvas tṛṇaiḥ puṣṭāḥ sapuṃgavāḥ ।। dṛśyate yatra dṛśyante vṛṣṭimanto balāhakāḥ ।।
tāḥ kṣaranti navaṃ kṣīraṃ medhyaṃ meghaughadhāritam ।। javenāvarjitaṃ caiva garjatīti janā viduḥ ।। vajrāśanisamāḥ śabdā bhavanty agamabhedinaḥ ।। vajrāśanisamāñ śabdān garjanto gagane sthitāḥ ।
bahubhiḥ kāmagair meghaiḥ śakro bhṛtyair iveśvaraḥ ।। kvacic chīkaramuktābhaṃ kurvadbhir gaganaṃ ghanaiḥ ।। kvacidbhinnāñjanākāraiḥ kvacicchīkaravarṣibhiḥ । maṇḍayaty eva devendro viśvam eva nabho ghanaiḥ । parjanyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ bhavāya bhuvi varṣati ।।
yasmāt prāvṛḍ iyaṃ kṛṣṇa śakrasya bhuvi bhāvinī । mahaiḥ sureśam arcanti vayam anye ca mānavāḥ ।। prabhāvajño api śakrasya vākyaṃ dāmodaro abravīt ।। gāvo asmaddaivataṃ viddhi girayaś ca vanāni ca ।।
vidyayā yo yayā yuktas tasya sā daivataṃ param ।। saiva pūjyārcanīyā ca saiva tasyopakāriṇī । dvāv anarthau sa labhate pretya ceha ca mānavaḥ ।। vanāntā girayaḥ sarve sā cāsmākaṃ gatir dhruvā ।।
praviśya tās tās tanavo ramante sveṣu sānuṣu ।। vanāni svāni rakṣanti trāsayanto drumacchidaḥ ।। ghnanti tān eva durvṛttān pauruṣādena karmaṇā ।। giriyajñā vayaṃ gopā ijyo asmābhir girir vane ।।
kurmaḥ kṛtvā sukhaṃ sthānaṃ pādape vātha vā girau ।। sarvaghoṣasya saṃdohaḥ kriyatāṃ kiṃ vicāryate ।। gāvo girivaraṃ sarvās tato yāntu vanaṃ punaḥ ।। śaratpramuditā ramyā gatameghajalāśayā ।।
kaṭhoratṛṇam ābhāti nirmayūrarutaṃ vanam ।। vivartante jaladharā vimadā iva kuñjarāḥ ।। parṇotkaraghanāḥ sarve prasādaṃ yānti pādapāḥ ।। vinā ca meghanādena nirmayūrarutaṃ vanam । nadyo bahuvidhākārā jalaṃ svacchaṃ vahanti ca ।
pūrṇacandrāmalacchatraṃ sābhiṣekam ivāmbaram ।। sarvāṇi tanutāṃ yānti jalāni jaladakṣaye ।। haṃsalakṣaṇahāsinyaḥ patiṃ yānti samudragāḥ ।। samam abhyutsmayantīva śarvarīṣv itaretaram ।।
nirviṣṭaramaṇīyeṣu vaneṣu ramate manaḥ ।। kedārāḥ saritaś caiva sarāṃsi ca śriyājvalan ।। śriyā jvalatpaṅkajāni tāmrāṇi ca sitāni ca । utpalāni ca nīlāni bhejire vārijāṃ śriyam ।।
abhavad vyabhramākāśam abhūc ca nibhṛto rṇavaḥ ।। mayūrāṅgaruhair bhūmir bahunetreva lakṣyate ।। haṃsasārasavinyāsair yamunā yāti saṃyatā ।। sasyādā jalajādāś ca mattā viruruvuḥ khagāḥ ।।
tāni śaṣpāṇy abālāni kaṭhinatvaṃ gatāni vai ।। eṣa vītamale vyomni hṛṣṭo vasati candramāḥ ।। vanānāṃ dviguṇā lakṣmīḥ sasyair guṇavatī mahī ।। manāṃsi ca manuṣyāṇāṃ prasādam upayānti vai ।।
śaratprajvalitaṃ tejas tīkṣṇaraśmir viśoṣayan ।। anyonyarāṣṭrābhimukhāḥ pārthivāḥ pṛthivīkṣitaḥ ।। manas tiṣṭhati kāntāsu citrāsu vanarājiṣu ।। asanāh saptaparṇāś ca kovidārāś ca puṣpitāḥ ।।
ikṣusasyā nikupyāś ca priyaṅguś ca viśeṣataḥ । sṛmarāḥ picukāś caiva ketakyaś ca samantataḥ ।। śaratprakāśayoṣeva goṣṭheṣv aṭati rūpiṇī ।। patatriketanaṃ devaṃ bodhayanti divaukasaḥ ।।
nīlacandrārkavarṇaiś ca racitaṃ bahubhir dvijaiḥ । phalaiḥ pravālaiś ca ghanam indracāpaghanopamam । bhavanākāraviṭapaṃ latāparam amaṇḍitam । viśālamūlāvanataṃ pavanābhogamaṇḍitam ।
arcayāma giriṃ devaṃ gāś caiva saviśeṣataḥ ।। ghaṇṭābhiś ca pralambābhiḥ puṣpaiḥ śāradikais tathā ।। pūjyantāṃ tridaśaiḥ śakro girir asmābhir ijyatām ।। yadāsti mayi vaḥ prītir yadi vā suhṛdo vayam ।।
tata etan mama vacaḥ kriyatām avicāritam ।। tadvāg amṛtam ākhyātaṃ pratyūcur aviśaṅkayā ।। prīṇayaty eva naḥ sarvān buddhir vṛddhikarī nṛṇām ।। bhayeṣv abhayadas tvaṃ nas tvaṃ caiva suhṛdāṃ suhṛt ।।
kṛtsno vasati śāntārir yathā svargagatas tathā ।। boddhavyāc cābhimānāc ca vismitāni manāṃsi naḥ ।। uttamas tvaṃ ca martyeṣu deveṣv iva puraṃdaraḥ ।। pratāpena ca tīkṣṇena dīptyā pūrṇatayāpi ca । uttamas tvaṃ ca martyeṣu deveṣv iva divākaraḥ ।
uttamas tvaṃ ca martyeṣu deveṣv iva niśākaraḥ ।। syāt te śaktidharas tulyo na tu kaścana mānuṣaḥ ।। kas tal laṅghayituṃ śakto velām iva mahodadheḥ ।। tvatpraṇīto adya gopānāṃ gavāṃ hetoḥ pravartatām ।।
lehyasya pāyasasyārthe droṇyaś ca vipulāyatāḥ ।। trirātraṃ caiva saṃdohaḥ sarvaghoṣasya gṛhyatām ।। pravartatāṃ ca yajño ayaṃ sarvagopasusaṃkulaḥ ।। tūryapraṇādaghoṣaiś ca vṛṣabhāṇāṃ ca garjitaiḥ ।।
dadhihrado ghṛtāvartaḥ payaḥkulyāsamākulaḥ ।। tuṣṭagopajanākīrṇo gopanārīmanoharaḥ ।। bhakṣyāṇāṃ rāśayas tatra śataśaś copakalpitāḥ । gandhamālyaiś ca vividhair dhūpair uccāvacais tathā । yajñaṃ gires tithau saumye cakrur gopā dvijaiḥ saha ।।
māṃsaṃ ca māyayā kṛṣṇo girir bhūtvā samaśnute ।। īdṛśaṃ hy abhavat tatra gopānāṃ bharatarṣabha । uttasthuḥ prītamanasaḥ svasti vācya yathāsukham ।। saṃtṛpto asmīti divyena rūpeṇa prajahāsa vai ।।
prajahāsa girer mūrdhni sthitaḥ kamalalocanaḥ । girimūrdhni sthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ jagmuḥ pradhānataḥ ।। saha taiḥ praṇato gopair vavandātmānam ātmanā ।। bhagavaṃs tvadvaśe yuktā dāsāḥ kiṃ kurma kiṃkarāḥ ।।
adyaprabhṛti yājyo ahaṃ goṣu yady asti vo dayā ।। mama prabhāvāc ca gavām ayutāny eva bhokṣyatha ।। raṃsye ca saha yuṣmābhir yathā divigatas tathā ।। eṣāṃ prītaḥ prayacchāmi gopānāṃ vipulaṃ dhanam ।।
evaṃ mama parā prītir bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। parivavrur girivaraṃ savṛṣāṇi sahasraśaḥ ।। sasragāpīḍaśṛṅgāgrāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। bhakticchedānuliptāṅgā raktapītāsitāmbarāḥ ।।
babhrājur adhikaṃ gopāḥ samavāye tadādbhute ।। gopālās tv apare gāś ca jagṛhur vegagāminaḥ ।। antardhānaṃ jagāmāśu tena dehena so giriḥ ।। giriyajñapravṛttena tenāścaryeṇa vismitaḥ ।।
gopāḥ sabālavṛddhā vai tuṣṭuvur mudhusūdanam । nṛtyaṃ gītaṃ prakurvāṇāḥ sahakṛṣṇā vrajaṃ yayuḥ । saṃvartakaṃ nāma gaṇaṃ toyadānām athābravīt ।। yadi vo matpriyaṃ kāryaṃ rājabhaktipuraskṛtam ।। nandagopādayo gopā vidviṣanti mamotsavam ।।
tā gāvaḥ saptarātreṇa pīḍyantāṃ vṛṣṭimārutaiḥ ।। srakṣyāmi vṛṣṭiṃ vātaṃ ca vajrāśanisamaprabham ।। hatās tāḥ savrajā gāvas tyakṣyanti bhuvi jīvitam ।। pratyāhate vai kṛṣṇena śāsane pākaśāsanaḥ ।।
mahe pratihate viṣṇoḥ śāsanāt pākaśāsanaḥ । ākāśaṃ chādayāmāsuḥ sarvataḥ parvatopamāḥ ।। timirāvṛtam ākāśaṃ cakrus te jaladās tadā ।। nāgā ivānye gagane cerur jaladapuṃgavāḥ ।।
durdinaṃ vipulaṃ cakruś chādayanto nabhas talam ।। sthūlanāgoruhastānāṃ satataṃ sarvatodiśam । dhārābhis tulyarūpābhir vavṛṣus te balāhakāḥ ।। durvigāhyam aparyantam agādhaṃ durdinaṃ mahat ।।
parvatābheṣu megheṣu khe nadatsu samantataḥ ।। ativṛṣṭena lokasya virūpam abhavad vapuḥ ।। candrasūryāṃśurahitaṃ khaṃ babhūvātiniṣprabham ।। meghayuktena vātena ghūrṇitam viśvatomukham ।
ābabhau sarvatas tatra bhūmis toyamayī yathā ।। vivṛddhiṃ nimnagā yātāḥ plavagāḥ saṃplavaṃ gatāḥ ।। tarjitānīva kampante tṛṇāni tarubhiḥ saha ।। iti gopagaṇā vākyaṃ vyāharanti bhayārditāḥ ।।
tenotpātāmbuvarṣeṇa gāvo viprahatā bhṛśam । hṛṣṭalomārdratanavaḥ kṣāmakukṣipayodharāḥ ।। kāścit savatsāḥ patitā gāvaḥ śīkaravejitāḥ ।। vimukhāḥ śrāntasakthyaś ca nirāhārāḥ kṛśodarāḥ ।।
trāhīti vadanair dīnaiḥ kṛṣṇam ūcur ivārtavat ।। gavāṃ paśya mahābāho vedanāṃ paramāturāḥ । gopāṃś cāsannavadanān kopaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ samādadhe ।। gāś cāpi paramāturāḥ ।roṣatāmrekṣaṇaḥ śrīmān ।aho dhārṣṭyaṃ surapater mām anādṛtya saṃprati । gavāṃ vadhaḥ kṛtas tasya gopānāṃ ca tathā kṛtaḥ ।
ātmānam ātmanā vākyam idam āha priyaṃvadaḥ ।। kalpayeyaṃ gavāṃ sthānaṃ varṣatrāṇāya durdharam ।। trāsyante savrajā gāvo madvaśyaś ca bhaviṣyati ।। ity uktvaikena hastena kṛtvā govardhanācalam ।
dadhāra līlayā kṛṣṇaś chatrākam iva bālakaḥ । dorbhyāṃ utpāṭayāmāsa kṛṣṇo girir ivāparaḥ ।। samūlaviṭapaskandhaś cacāla sa mahāgiriḥ । ghaṇāghaṇakṛtaḥ śailaḥ saprāṇa iva niḥśvasan । gṛhabhāvaṃ gatas tatra gṛhākāreṇa varcasā ।।
śilāḥ praśithilāś celur niṣpetuś ca sapādapāḥ ।। rakṣiṣyan godhanaṃ viṣṇur gopānāṃ gopatir hariḥ । gomadhyasthitagovindo gopān rakṣan sagokulān ।। dadhāra godhanaṃ viṣṇur godharaṃ ca vilambayan । gopān vismāpayan gopo gomārge saṃsthito hariḥ । ādyaṃ vapuś ca gṛhṇāno lokānām īśvareśvaraḥ ।। vyarthaṃ cakāra govindo godharasya samīhitam । govardhanasyāsya gireḥ khe khaṇāyitavigrahaḥ । vidhṛtaiś cocchritaiḥ śṛṅgair agamaḥ khagamo abhavat ।। bhidyamānāśmanicayaś cacāla dharaṇīdharaḥ ।।
vāyoś ca ghūrṇamānasya vidyutāṃ bhramatām api । viṣṇutejobhibhūtānām adṛśyanta vapūṃṣi ca । vividus te janā rūpaṃ vāyos tasya ca garjataḥ ।। miśrīkṛta ivābhāti girir uddāmabarhiṇaḥ ।।
gandharvaṛṣayaś caiva vāco muñcanti susvarāḥ ।। rītīr nirvartayāmāsa kāñcanāñ janarājatīḥ ।। girer meghaṃ praviṣṭāni tasya śṛṅgāṇi cābhavan ।। puṣpam uccāvacaṃ bhūmau vyaśīryata samantataḥ ।।
dvijihvapatayaḥ kruddhāḥ khecarāḥ khe samantataḥ ।। utpatyotpatya gaganāt punaḥ petur avāṅmukhāḥ ।। gargarā iva mathyanto neduḥ śārdūlapuṃgavāḥ ।। vyāvṛttadehaḥ sa girī ramya evopalakṣyate ।।
stambhitasyeva rudreṇa tripurasya vihāyasi ।। nīlābhrapaṭalac channaṃ tadgiricchatram ābabhau ।। bāhūpadhāne kṛṣṇasya prasupta iva khe giriḥ ।। nirālamba ivābhāti giriḥ sa śikharair vṛtaḥ ।।
sajvarāṇīva śailasya vanāni śikharāṇi ca ।। tvaryamāṇā mahendreṇa toyaṃ mumucur akṣayam ।। cakrārūḍha ivābhāti deśo nṛpatipīḍitaḥ ।। puraṃ puraskṛtya yathā sphīto janapado mahān ।।
provāca goptā gopānāṃ prajāpatir iva sthitaḥ ।। kṛtaṃ girigṛhaṃ gopā nivātaśaraṇaṃ gavām ।। na trāsa iha vaḥ kāryo maddhastād dhi nipātane । vātavarṣabhayenālaṃ tattrāṇaṃ vihitaṃ hi vaḥ । yathāvrajaṃ yathāyūthaṃ yathāsāraṃ ca vai sukham ।।
yuthaśaś ca vibhajyātha vasadhvaṃ gopasattamāḥ । pañcakrośapramāṇena krauśaikaṃ vistaro mahān । trailokyam apy utsahate grasituṃ kiṃ punar vrajam ।। gopānāṃ tumulo jajñe meghanādaś ca bāhyataḥ ।।
tasya śailasya vipulaṃ pradaraṃ gahvarodaram ।। dadhāraikena hastena śailaṃ priyam ivātithim ।। viviśur varṣabhītāni tad gṛhaṃ girinirmitam ।। mithyāpratijño jaladān vārayāmāsa vai vibhuḥ ।।
jagāma saṃvṛto meghair vṛtrahā svargam uttamam ।। gatābhre vimale vyomni divase dīptabhāskare ।। khaṃ ca sthānaṃ tato ghoṣaḥ pratyayāt punar eva saḥ ।। prīto niveśayāmāsa dhruvāya varado vibhuḥ ।।
kṛṣṇasya darśanaṃ śakro rocayāmāsa vismitaḥ ।। āruhyairāvataṃ nāgam ajagāma mahītalam ।। kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakarmāṇaṃ puruhūtaḥ puraṃdaraḥ ।। gopaviṣadharaṃ viṣṇuṃ parijajñe puraṃdaraḥ ।।
paryāptanayanaḥ śakraḥ sarvair netrair udaikṣata ।। surāṇāṃ kāryasiddhyarthaṃ nityaṃ karmasu niṣṭhitam । sūpaviṣṭaṃ śilāpṛṣṭe śakraḥ sa vrīḍito abhavat ।। antardhānagataś chāyām cakāroragabhojanaḥ ।।
