chāyayā ca tayā yuktaṃ keśavaṃ yajñarūpiṇam । upatasthe gajaṃ hitvā kṛṣṇaṃ balaniṣūdanaḥ ।। rarāja devarājo vai vajrapūrṇakaraḥ prabhuḥ ।। kuṇḍalābhyāṃ sa divyābhyāṃ satataṃ śobhitānanaḥ ।
pañcastabakalambena devabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। sahasrapatrakāntena dehabhūṣaṇakāriṇā । īkṣamāṇaḥ sahasreṇa netrāṇāṃ kāmarūpiṇām । tridaśājñāpanārthena meghanirghoṣakāriṇā ।
praṇāma akaroc chakraḥ kṣantavyam iti cābravīt । tuṣṭāva ca hariṃ viṣṇuṃ gopaveṣavibhūṣitam ।। namas te devadeveśa bhūtabhāvanabhāvana । hiraṇyaretase tubhyaṃ namaḥ somapradāyine ।।
namo vedaikatattvārtha tannibodhana bodhana । namaḥ praṇavavācyāya vācakāya namo namaḥ ।। namas te viśvarūpāya namo lokahitāya te । namo gopavirūpāya namo godharadhāriṇe ।।
namaḥ purāṇarūpāya namas te madhusūdana ।। kiṃ vānena jagannātha namaskāreṇa keśava । yā yās tu devadevasya mūrtayo mūrtimattara । namas tābhyas tathā viṣṇo sarvābhyaḥ sarvakāmada ।।
kṣantavyaṃ mama deveśa kṛtaṃ gopālanandana । ajñānād etha vā jñānād roṣād vā yadunandana ।। samartheṣv asamartheṣu roṣaḥ prasphurati prabho । na kenacid bhavāñ śāsyaḥ śāstā sarvasya vai prabho ।।
tvannimittam idaṃ sarvam aindraṃ mama sudurlabham । tvatprasādaj jagannātha devānām īśvaro yataḥ ।। tataś ca devadeveśa kṣantavyaṃ dāsa ity aham । ity uktvātha punar vākyaṃ vyājahāra śacīpatiḥ ।।
kṛṣṇaṃ kamalapatrākṣam abālaṃ bālarūpiṇam । atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśaṃ śrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇam । upaviṣṭaṃ śilāpṛṣṭhe kṛtvā karmātimānuṣam ।। na hi dāseṣu kopo asti svāmināṃ svāmisattama ।
atha divyena madhuram vyājahāra svareṇa tam ।। atidaivaṃ kṛtaṃ karma tvayā prītimatā gavām ।। yat tvayā rakṣitā gāvas tenāsmi paritoṣitaḥ ।। dhṛto veśma ivākāśe ko hy etena na vismayet ।।
ativṛṣṭiḥ kṛtā kṛṣṇa gavāṃ vai saptarātrikī ।। devaiḥ sadānavagaṇair durnivāryā mayi sthite ।। samagraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tejo vinigūhasi roṣitaḥ ।। tvayi mānuṣyam āpanne yuktenaivaṃ svatejasā ।।
devānām yad bhavān netā sarvakāryapurogamaḥ ।। dvitīyaṃ nānupaśyāmi dhuraṃ yas te samudvahet ।। evaṃ tvam asi devānāṃ magnānāṃ dvijavāhana ।। brahmaṇā sādhu nirdiṣṭaṃ dhātubhya iva kāñcanam ।।
na tvānugantuṃ śakto vai paṅgur drutagatiṃ yathā ।। garutmān pakṣiṇāṃ śreṣṭho devatānāṃ bhavān varaḥ ।। nāgānām upariṣṭād bhūḥ pṛthivyupari mānuṣāḥ ।। ākāśasyopari ravir dvāraṃ svargasya bhānumān ।।
yatrāhaṃ kṛṣṇa devānām aindre vinihitaḥ pade ।। tvayā hi lokanāthena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā । tatra somagatiś caiva jyotiṣāṃ ca mahātmanām ।। sa hi sarvagataḥ kṛṣṇa mahākāśagato mahān ।।
yāṃ na vidmo vayaṃ sarve pṛcchanto api pitāmaham ।। pitāmaho api bhagavāṃs tvatprasādād yadṛcchayā । yāṃ yoganiratā viṣṇo bhajante brahmavādinaḥ । pṛthivī karmaśīlānāṃ kṣetraṃ sarvasya karmaṇaḥ ।। gatiḥ śamadamāḍhyānāṃ svargaḥ sukṛtakarmaṇām ।।
gavām eva hi goloko durārohā hi sā gatiḥ ।। dhṛto dhṛtimatā vīra nighnatopadravaṃ gavām ।। brahmanaś ca mahābhāga gauravāt tava cāgataḥ ।। aditer garbhaparyāye pūrvajas te purātanaḥ ।।
megharūpeṇa tat sarvaṃ kṣantum arhasi me vibho ।। brahmaṇaḥ śṛṇu me vākyaṃ gavāṃ ca gajavikrama ।। karmabhis toṣitā divyais tava saṃrakṣaṇādibhiḥ ।। yad vayaṃ puṃgavaiḥ sārdhaṃ vardhāmaḥ prasavais tathā ।।
śriyaṃ śakṛtpavitreṇa tarpayiṣyāma kāmagāḥ ।। adyaprabhṛti no rājā tvam indro vai bhaviṣyasi ।। ebhis tvam abhiṣicyasva mayā hastāvanāmitaiḥ ।। govinda iti lokās tvāṃ stoṣyanti bhuvi śāśvatam ।।
upendra iti kṛṣṇa tvām gāsyanti divi devatāḥ ।। eṣām ardhaṃ prayacchāmi śaratkālaṃ tu paścimam ।। mamāmbuprabhavaṃ darpaṃ tadā tyakṣyanti barhinaḥ ।। śāntiṃ sarve gamiṣyanti jalakālavicāriṇaḥ ।।
sahasraraśmir ādityas tāpayan svena tejasā ।। yāvat sukhatarais toyair vipluteṣu pluteṣu ca ।। haṃsasārasapūrṇeṣu nadīnāṃ pulineṣu ca । goṣu caiva prahṛṣṭāsu kṣarantīṣu payo bahu ।।
ākāśe śastrasaṃkāśe haṃseṣu vicaratsu ca ।। taḍāgeṣu ca kānteṣu toyeṣu vimaleṣu ca । kalamāvanatāgrāsu pakvakedārapaṅktiṣu ।। sasasyāyāṃ ca sīmāyāṃ manoharyāṃ muner api ।।
ikṣumatsu ca deśeṣu pravṛtteṣu makheṣu ca ।। loke asmin kṛṣṇa nikhile yathaiva tridive tathā ।। mahendraś cāpy upendraś ca mahīyetāṃ mahītale ।। mānavāḥ praṇamiṣyanti teṣāṃ nāsty anayāgamaḥ ।।
svargalokādayānīya maṇipīṭhaṃ surādhipaḥ । niveśya kṛṣṇaṃ ratnaiḥ prāṅ muktādyair abhiṣecayat । kṛtvā nīrājanaṃ divyair alaṃkṛtya ca bhūṣaṇaiḥ । abhiṣekeṇa govindaṃ yojayāmāsa yogavit ।। stanaiḥ prasnavasaṃyuktaiḥ siṣicuḥ kṛṣṇam avyayam ।। siṣicus toyadhārābhir abhiṣicyantam avyayam ।।
vavarṣuḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ ca nedus tūryāṇi cāmbare ।। vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca jābālir atha kāśyapaḥ । viśvāmitro bharadvājaḥ kaṇvo atrir bhagavān prabhuḥ । ete ca munayaḥ sarve siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ ।
ekārṇavavimuktaṃ ca dadhāra vasudhā vapuḥ ।। ītayaḥ praśamaṃ jagmur jagmur nirvairatāṃ nṛpāḥ ।। kṛṣṇe abhiṣita etāni sarvāṇi kurunandana । nirvairāṇyabhavaṃs tāta krūrāṇy api nisargataḥ । pravālapuṣpaśabalāḥ phalavantaś ca pādapāḥ ।।
alaṃkṛtā gātraruhair vātubhir bhānti parvatāḥ ।। āsīt kṛṣṇābhiṣeke hi divyasvargarasokṣitaḥ ।। divyaśuklāmbaradharam devarājo abravīd idam ।। śrūyatāmaparaṃ cāpi mamāgamanakāraṇam ।।
ariṣṭaś ca madāviṣṭo rājarājyaṃ tataḥ kuru ।। sa te rakṣyaś ca mānyaś ca sakhye ca viniyujyatām ।। tvadvaśe vartamānaḥ sa prāpsyate vipulaṃ yaśaḥ ।। bhaviṣyaty anurūpaś ca tvām ṛte na ca raṃsyate ।।
ubhābhyām api saṃyoge yāsyanti nidhanaṃ nṛpāḥ ।। mama putro arjuno nāma jātaḥ kuntyāṃ kurūdvahaḥ ।। taṃ pravekṣyanti vai sarve rājānaḥ śastrayodhinaḥ ।। samare rājadharmeṇa yojayiṣyanti mṛtyunā ।।
nānuyāsyanti rājāno devā vā tvāṃ vinā prabho ।। tasya yogo vidhātavyas tvayā govinda matkṛte ।। jñātā tvam eva lokānām arjunasya ca nityaśaḥ ।। rakṣitasya tvayā tasya na mṛtyuḥ prabhaviṣyati ।।
ātmā te ahaṃ yathā śaśvat tathaiva tava so arjuna ।। devatānāṃ kṛto rājā purā jyeṣṭhakramād aham ।। satyenopetya devā vai yojayanti ripukṣaye ।। iha sauhṛdatāṃ yātu bhūtvā sahacaraḥ purā ।।
voḍhavyā puṃgaveneva dhūḥ sarvā raṇavāhinī ।। abhitas tan mahadyuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati mahīkṣitām ।। vijayasyārjuno bhoktā yaśasā tvaṃ tu yokṣyase ।। yady ahaṃ te surāś caiva satyaṃ ca priyam acyuta ।।
prītena manasā yuktaḥ prativākyaṃ jagāda ha ।। yat tvayābhihitaṃ cedaṃ na kiṃcit parihāsyate ।। jāne pitṛṣvasā dattā pāṇḍor vasumatīpateḥ ।। bhīmasenaṃ ca jānāmi vāyoḥ saṃtānajāṃ tanum ।।
nāgāyutasamaprāṇam anekāsuramardanam । nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca mādryāḥ kukṣibhavāv ubhau ।। pitṛṣvasari karṇaṃ vai prasūtaṃ sūtatāṃ gatam ।। duryodhanamukhāḥ śakra kauravāṇāṃ mahābalāḥ ।
pāṇḍor uparamaṃ caiva śāpāśaninipātajam ।। nārjunasya ripuḥ kaścin mamāgre prabhaviṣyati ।। kuntyā niryātayiṣyāmi nivṛtte bhārate mṛdhe ।। bhṛtyavat tat kariṣyāmi tava snehena yantritaḥ ।।
praṇamya devadevasya mūrdhnā śakraḥ padāmbujam । kṛṣṇasya sākṣāt tridivaṃ jagāma tridaśeśvaraḥ ।। etad ākhyānam āyuṣyāṃ puṇyaṃ pāpaprāṇāśanam । parjanyaprītijanakam avagrahanivārakam । sarvasaukhyapriyakaraṃ devaguhyam anuttamam । govardhanadharaḥ śrīmān viveśa vrajam eva ha ।।
dhanyāḥ smo anugṛhītāḥ smas tvaddhṛtena nagena ha ।। tava prasādād govinda devatulya mahādyute ।। dhāraṇenāsya śailasya vidmas tvāṃ kṛṣṇam avyayam ।। vasūnāṃ vā kimarthaṃ ca vasudevaḥ pitā tava ।।
kṛṣṇa divyā ca te ceṣṭā śaṅkitāni manāṃsi naḥ ।। lokapālopamaś caiva gās tvaṃ kiṃ parirakṣasi ।। asmākaṃ bāndhavo jāto yo asi so asi namo astu te ।। namo astu kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti namo gopālabandhave । namo bālāya goptre ca gopaveṣāya bāndhava ।। namas te śiśusiṃhāya namo bhūdharadhāriṇe । devāyātha variṣṭhāya yakṣāya ca namo namaḥ ।। namas te nandaputrāya yaśodāyāḥ sutāya ca । ko bhavān kaś ca vā devaḥ kimarthaṃ no abhirakṣasi ।
vayaṃ tavaanugāḥ sarve bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। pratyuvāca smitaṃ kṛtvā jñātīn sarvān samāgatān ।। tathāhaṃ nāvagantavyaḥ svajātīyo asmi bāndhavaḥ ।। tato bhavantaḥ śroṣyanti māṃ ca drakṣyanti tattvataḥ ।।
parijñānena kiṃ kāryam yady eṣo anugraho mama ।। baddhamaunā diśaḥ sarve bhejire pihitānanāḥ ।। śāradīnāṃ niśānāṃ ca manaś cakre ratiṃ prati ।। vṛṣāṇāṃ jātarāgāṇāṃ yuddhāni samayojayat ।।
vane sa vīro gāś caiva jagrāha grāhavad vibhuḥ ।। kaiśorakaṃ mānayānaḥ saha tābhir mumoda ha ।। pibanti nayanākṣepair gāṃ gataṃ śaśinaṃ yathā ।। bhadravastreṇa vasitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kāntataro abhavat ।।
śobhamāno hi govindaḥ śobhayām āsa taṃ vrajam ।। vicitraṃ caritaṃ ghoṣe dṛṣṭvā tat tasya bhāsvataḥ ।। namas te kṛṣṇa gopeti prasīda prabhaveti ca । bhrāmitākṣaiś ca vadanair nirīkṣante varāṅganāḥ ।।
kṛṣṇaṃ gopāṅganā rātrau mṛgayanti ratipriyāḥ ।। gāyantyaḥ kṛṣṇacaritaṃ dvaṃdvaśo gopakanyakāḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya gatigāminyas taruṇyas tā varāṅganāḥ ।। cerur vai caritaṃ tasya kṛṣṇasya vrajayoṣitaḥ ।।
muditāś cānukurvantyaḥ krīḍanti vrajayoṣitaḥ ।। vrajaṃ gatāḥ sukhaṃ cerur dāmodaraparāyaṇāḥ ।। cerur dāmodaraparāḥ sukhaṃ nāryo vrajaṃ gatāḥ । ramayantyo yathā nāgaṃ sapramodāḥ kareṇavaḥ ।।
pibanty atṛptā vanitāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇamṛgekṣaṇāḥ ।। ratyantaragatā rātrau pibanti ratilālasāḥ ।। jagṛhur niḥsṛtāṃ vāṇīṃ sāmnā dāmodareritām ।। cāru visraṃsire keśāḥ kucāgre gopayoṣitām ।।
atha dāmodaraḥ kāścij jagrāha ratilālasaḥ ।। evaṃ gopāṅganāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ ramayanti manoramāḥ । alaṃkṛtāḥ sumadhuraṃ gāyantyo madhuvihvalāḥ ।। kṛṣṇo api madhuraktākṣo gopīnāṃ harṣavardhanaḥ । papau tāsāṃ mukhaṃ viṣṇur ghūrṇayan netraṣaṭpadam ।। aparāṃ vāsasī gṛhya cucumbe gopakanyakām । āliliṅge atha kāṃcit tu kṛṣṇo madavilocanaḥ ।। anyayā saha govindaḥ śete līlāvidhānavit । anyasyā vāsasī gṛhya dṛṣṭvā cāru papau mukham । anyāṃ lilekha govindo nakhaiḥ śātaiś ca keśavaḥ ।। anyāṃ ca keśe saṃgṛhya mukham unnamya līlayā । āliliṅge atha govindo gopaveṣatiraskṛtaḥ ।। ekāṃ saṃgṛhya saṃtyajya kāṃcid anyām avāsṛjat । paśyantyā ramayām āsa kāṃcid anyām arīramat ।। āhūya kāṃcid deveśaḥ kāṃcid anyām arīramat । tāṃ punaḥ sahasā gṛhya tatsamakṣam arīramat ।। tāś ca gopyaḥ svabhartṛṃś ca saṃtyajya harim eva ha । ayam eva hi no jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaś ceti varāṅganāḥ । kṛṣṇe ca devadeveśe paraṃ bhāvaṃ samāyayuḥ । śāradīṣu sacandrāsu niśāsu mumude sukhī ।। trāsayan samado goṣṭhān ariṣṭaḥ pratyadṛśyata ।। kṣuratīkṣṇāgracaraṇaḥ kālaḥ kāla ivāparaḥ ।।
garvitāviddhalāṅgūlaḥ kaṭhinaskandhabandhanaḥ ।। śakṛnmūtropaliptāṅgo gavām udvejano bhṛśam ।। viṣāṇāvalgitagatir lambatā kaṇṭhacarmaṇā ।। yuddhasañjaviṣāṇāgro dviṣadvṛṣabhasūdanaḥ ।।
daityo vṛṣabharūpeṇa goṣṭhān viparidhāvati ।। bhajamānaś ca capalo gṛṣṭīḥ saṃpracacāra ha ।। goṣṭheṣu na ratiṃ lebhe vinā yuddhaṃ sa govṛṣaḥ ।। kasyacit tv atha kālasya sa vṛṣaḥ keśavāgrataḥ । ājagāma balodragro vaivasvatavaśe sthitaḥ । sa tatra gās tu prasabhaṃ bādhamāno madotkaṭaḥ ।
trāsayāmāsa duṣṭātmā vaivasvata pathe sthitaḥ ।। cakāra nirvṛṣaṃ goṣṭhaṃ nirvatsaśiśupuṃgavam ।। tam ārād abhidhāvantaṃ nardamānaṃ mahāvṛṣam । abhyadhāvata govindo daityaṃ vṛṣabharūpiṇam ।।
ruṣitas talaśabdena yuddhākāṅkṣī nanarda ha ।। tasmāt sthānān na vyacalat kṛṣṇo girir ivācalaḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya nidhanākāṅkṣī tūrṇam abhyutpapāta ha ।। kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇāñjananibhaṃ vṛṣaṃ prati vṛṣopamaḥ ।।
mumoca vaktrajaṃ phenaṃ nastato atha sa śabdavat ।। rejatur meghasamaye saṃsaktāv iva toyadau ।। apīḍayad ariṣṭasya kaṇṭhaṃ klinnam ivāmbaram ।। tenaiva prāharad vaktre sa mamāra bhṛśaṃ hataḥ ।।
papāta rudhirodgārī sāmbudhāra ivāmbudaḥ ।। sādhu sādhv iti bhūtāni tatkarmāsyābhituṣṭuvuḥ ।। aravindābhanayanaḥ punar eva rarāja ha ।। upāsāṃcakrire hṛṣṭāḥ svarge śakram ivāmarāḥ ।।
udvegam agamat kaṃsaḥ śaṅkamānas tato bhayam ।। dhenuke pralayaṃ nīte pralambe ca nipātite ।। goṣu trātāsu ca tathā spṛhaṇīyena karmaṇā ।। dṛśyamāne vināśe ca saṃnikṛṣṭe mahābhaye ।।
acintyaṃ karma tac chrutvā vardhamāneṣu śatruṣu ।। visaṃjñendriyabhūtātmā gatāsupratimo abhavat ।। niśi stimitamūkāyām mathurāyāṃ janādhipaḥ ।। satyakaṃ dārukaṃ caiva kahvāvarajam eva ca ।।
bhayesakhaṃ ca rājānaṃ vipṛthuṃ ca pṛthuśriyam ।। bhūritejasam akṣobhyaṃ bhūriśravasam eva ca ।। ugrasenasuto rājā provāca mathureśvaraḥ ।। nyāyavṛttāntakuśalās trivargasya pravartakāḥ ।।
parvatā iva niṣkampā vṛtte mahati tasthuṣaḥ ।। tasthivāṃso mahāvṛtte niṣkampā iva parvatāḥ । rājamantradharāḥ sarve sarve dhanuṣi pāragāḥ ।। āśramāṇāṃ nisargajñā varṇānāṃ kramapāragāḥ ।।
bhettāraḥ pararāṣṭrāṇāṃ trātāraḥ śaraṇārthinām ।। dyaur api anugṛhītā syād bhavadbhiḥ kiṃ punar mahī ।। rudrāṇām iva vaḥ krodho dīptir aṅgirasām iva ।। dhṛtaṃ yadukulaṃ vīrair bhūtalaṃ parvatair iva ।।
vardhamāno mamānartho bhavadbhiḥ kim upekṣitaḥ ।। vardhamāna ivāmbhodo mūlaṃ naḥ parikṛntati ।। kāraṇān nandagopasya sa suto gopito gṛhe ।। nadanmegha ivoṣṇānte sa durātmā vivardhate ।।
nandagopasya bhavane jātasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ ।। atidevair amānuṣyaiḥ karmabhiḥ so anumīyate ।। stanapānepsunā pītā prāṇaiḥ saha durāsadā ।। tathaiva tena bālena pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā । śayane vai śayānena śakaṭaṃ parivartitam ।। tathā bālena balinā ane jātau bṛhattarau । samūlaviṭapau bhagnau sahajau yamalārjunau ।
nandagopasuto yogaṃ kṛtvā ca punar utthitaḥ ।। tasyāgrajo mahāvīryo balabhadro durātmavān । bālena muṣṭinaikena sa hataḥ prākṛto yathā ।। nirjalaṃ gokulaṃ kṛtvā dhṛto govardhano giriḥ ।।
kena vā nararūpeṇa śakyo govardhano giriḥ । uddhartuṃ govraje satyaṃ na jāne apy adbhutaṃ tataḥ ।। idam atyadbhutaṃ sarvaṃ varṣaṃ vāsavanirmitam । nivāritaṃ saptadinaṃ kim ataḥ param adbhutam ।
abālo bālyam āsthāya ramate bālalīlayā ।। saṃnikṛṣṭaṃ bhayaṃ caiva keśino mama ca dhruvam ।। yuddhakāṅkṣī hi sa yathā tiṣṭhatīva mamāgrataḥ ।। kva ca devaprabhāvena krīḍitavyaṃ vraje mama ।।
ko apy eṣa ramate devaḥ śmaśānastha ivānalaḥ ।। aho yādavaśreṣṭhā vai kathayantu samāhitāḥ । idam apy aparaṃ manye śrotavyaṃ yadupuṃgavāḥ । yathā mama tathā yūyaṃ jānītha sakalaṃ vacaḥ । vāmanena tu rūpeṇa jahāra pṛthivīm imām ।। devarājāya tu tadā dattavān kila keśavaḥ ।
hato hiraṇyakaśipur dānavānāṃ pitāmahaḥ ।। hatvā tu dānavaṃ saṃkhye rājānaṃ kṛtavān hariḥ । bhavena cyāvitā daityāḥ purā tat tripuraṃ ghnatā ।। praviśya cāsurīṃ māyām anāvṛṣṭiṃ cakāra ha ।।
vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthāya ujjahārārṇavān mahīm ।। sabhūdharavanām urvīṃ śakrāya pradadau hariḥ । surāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca yuddhaṃ cakre sudāruṇam ।। dadhāra mandaraṃ viṣṇur akūpāra iti śrutiḥ ।।
vapur vāmanam āsthāya nindanīyaṃ purā vapuḥ । tribhiḥ kramais tu trīlokāñ jahāra tridivālayam । sa eva rāmasaṃjño vai rāvaṇaṃ vyaśasat tadā ।। sa eva bhagavān viṣṇur bhūtvā bhārgavanandanaḥ । paraśvadhane śātena jaghāna kṛtavīryajam ।। triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ pṛthivīṃ hatvā kṣatriyapuṃgavān । hayamedhe tadā yajñe kāśyapāya dadau kila । sādhayaty ātmanaḥ kāryaṃ surāṇām arthasiddhaye ।।
matsādhanepsayā prāpto nārado māṃ yad uktavān ।। asya buddhiviśeṣeṇa vayaṃ kātaratāṃ gatāḥ ।। dvitīyaṃ sa hi māṃ vipraḥ punar evābravīd vacaḥ ।। vasudevena te rātrau karma tad viphalīkṛtam ।।
tāṃ yaśodāsutāṃ viddhi kṛṣṇaṃ ca vasudevajam ।। vasudevena saṃdhāya mitrarūpeṇa śatruṇā ।। hatvā śumbhaniśumbhau dvau dānavau nagacāriṇau ।। arcyate dasyubhir ghorair mahāpaśubalipriyā ।।
mayūrāṅgadacitraiś ca barhabhāraiś ca bhūṣitā ।। chāgayūthaiś ca saṃpūrṇam aviruddhaiś ca pakṣibhiḥ ।। vṛkṣagambhīranibiḍaṃ kāntāraiḥ sarvato vṛtam ।। sthānaṃ tasyā nage vindhye nirmitaṃ svena tejasā ।।
vasate paramaprītā daivatair api pūjitā ।। atra me nāradaḥ prāha sumahat karma kāraṇam ।। sa hi te sahajo mṛtyur bāndhavaś ca bhaviṣyati ।। bāndhavo dharmato mahyaṃ hṛdayenāntako ripuḥ ।।
netre tudati tasyaiva vaktreṇāmiṣagṛddhinā ।। cchinatti mama mūlāni bhuṅkte ca mama pārśvataḥ ।। na kṛtaghnasya loko asti bāndhavasya viśeṣataḥ ।। yaḥ kṛtaghno anubandhena prītiṃ vahati dāruṇām ।।
apāpe pāpahṛdayo yaḥ pāpam anutiṣṭhati ।। sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ punarāvṛttidurlabham । niyamair guruvṛttena tvayā bāndhavakāmyayā ।। yuddhavyuparame te tu sahāśnanti mahāvane ।।
vadhyate yo antaraprepsuḥ svajano yāti vikriyām ।। gaccha gaccha yathākāmaṃ vasudeva narādhama ।। tad dattaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ piṇḍaṃ yad dattaṃ tava jānatā । tac chvabhyo yadi dattaṃ syāc chreyo mama bhaviṣyati ।
amarṣī vairaśīlaś ca sadā pāpamatiḥ śaṭhaḥ ।। vasudeva vṛthāvṛddha yan mayā tvaṃ puraskṛtaḥ ।। yasya buddhiḥ pariṇatā sa vai vṛddhatamo nṛṇām ।। na tena vṛddho bhavati yenāsya palitaṃ śiraḥ ।
kevalaṃ vayasā vṛddho yathā śaradi toyadaḥ ।। hate kaṃse mama suto mathurāṃ pālayiṣyati ।। jijīviṣur na sa hy asti yo hi tiṣṭhen mamāgrataḥ ।। tat te pratikariṣyāmi putrayos tava paśyataḥ ।।
kṛtapūrvaḥ kariṣye vā viśeṣeṇa tu bāndhave ।। pitṛṣvasur me bhartā ca yadūnāṃ prathamo guruḥ ।। gurvarthaṃ pūjitaḥ sadbhir yadubhir dharmabuddhibhiḥ ।। yadūnāṃ yūthamukhyasya yasya te vṛttam īdṛśam ।।
satsu yāsyanti puruṣā yadūnām avaguṇṭhitāḥ ।। aviśvāsyaṃ kṛtaṃ karma vācyāś ca yadavaḥ kṛtāḥ ।। śāntim ekatare śāntiṃ gate yāsyanti yādavāḥ ।। tiṣṭha vā gaccha vā mūḍha yatheṣṭaṃ mama pārśvataḥ ।। hantuṃ svajanam udvṛttaṃ so ayaṃ yadukulodvahaḥ । mā bhūd ayaṃ parīvādo loke yādavasattamāḥ । anyathā vadhayogyo asi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।
nandagopaṃ ca gopāṃś ca karadān mama śāsanāt ।। śīghram āgaccha nagaraṃ gopaiḥ sarvaiḥ samanvitaḥ ।। draṣṭum icchati vai kaṃsaḥ sabhṛtyaḥ sapurohitaḥ ।। dṛḍhapratikṛtī caiva śṛṇomi vyāyatodyamau ।।
tābhyāṃ saha niyotsyete tau yuddhakuśalāv ubhau ।। pitṛṣvasuḥ sutau mukhyau vrajavāsau vanecarau ।। rājā dhanurmahaṃ nāma kārayiṣyati vai sukhī ।। janasyāmantritasyārthe yathā syāt sarvam avyayam ।।
yathākāmapradānāya bhojyādhiśrayaṇāya ca ।। saṃkarṣaṇaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca draṣṭuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ।। dṛṣṭvā tu tau mahāvīryau tad vidhāsyāmi yad dhitam ।। na gacchetāṃ yathākālaṃ nigrāhyāv api tau mama ।।
madhureṇaiva tau mandau svayam evānayāśu vai ।। yadi vā nopajapto asi vasudevena suvrata ।। tathā kartavyam etad dhi yathā tāv āgamiṣyataḥ । ity uktvā virarāmaiva kaṃsaḥ sa madhureśvaraḥ । sāgarākāram ātmānaṃ niṣprakampam adhārayat ।।
kṣamāṃ manasi saṃdhyāya nottaraṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। dhig dhig ity asakṛt te vai śanair ūcur avāṅmukhāḥ ।। jalam dṛṣṭveva tṛṣitaḥ preṣitaḥ prītimān abhūt ।। paśyāmi devadeveśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam । yogināṃ yogagamyaṃ tam īśvaraṃ sakaleśvaram ।। paśyāmi bālaṃ govindaṃ gopaveṣavibhūṣitam । saṃkarṣaṇasahāyaṃ taṃ padmapatranibhekṣaṇam ।। adya me saphalaṃ janma dṛṣṭo yena mayā hariḥ ।। mayūrāṅgadacitrāṅgaṃ tumbavīṇāvimiśritam । drakṣyāmi lokanāthaṃ taṃ gopīstanavilālasam ।। yadi māṃ cakṣuṣā samyak prītiyuktena paśyati । tadānīṃ saphalaṃ janma mama taṃ paśyato harim ।। yaṃ dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ sarve viramante tapobalāt । sa māṃ vakṣyati kiṃcit tu vacanaṃ vāgvidāṃ varaḥ ।। evaṃ vicintya manasā gantuṃ śīghrataro abhavat ।
prītimān puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ draṣṭuṃ dānapatiḥ svayam ।। nipīḍya śravaṇān hastair menire taṃ gatāyuṣam ।। provāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ samāsāt kaṃsam ojasā ।। ayukto garhitaḥ sadbhir bāndhaveṣu viśeṣataḥ ।।
na hi tvāṃ yādavā vīra balāt kurvanti yādavam ।। ikṣvākuvaṃśajo rājā vinivṛttaḥ svavaṃśakṛt ।। sahajaṃ te śiras tāta jaṭī muṇḍo api vā bhava ।। durjātīyena yena tvam īdṛśo janitaḥ sutaḥ ।।
pareṇoktā guṇā gauṇyaṃ yānti vedārtasaṃmitāḥ ।। bālaḥ kulāntakṛn mūḍho yeṣāṃ tvam anuśāsitā ।। na vācā sādhitaṃ kāryam ātmā ca vivṛtaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। kṣepaṇaṃ kaḥ śubhaṃ manyed dvijasyeva vadhaṃ kṛtam ।।
krodho hi teṣāṃ pradahel lokān antargatān api ।। dharmasya gatir anveṣyā matsyasya gatir apsv iva ।। vācā dunoṣi marmaghnyā amantroktā yathāhutiḥ ।। tatra mithyāpralāpaṃ te nindāmi kṛpaṇaṃ vacaḥ ।।
dāruṇo api pituḥ putraḥ kaḥ putre dāruṇaḥ pitā । putrārthe hy āpadaḥ kaṣṭāḥ pitaraḥ prāpnuvanti hi ।। putrās te hy āpadaḥ kaṣṭāt pitaraṃ tārayanti tu । manyase yady akartavyaṃ pṛcchasva pitaraṃ svakam ।।
tvayā yādavaputrāṇāṃ vairajaṃ viṣam arjitam ।। kimartham ugrasenena śiśus tvaṃ na vināśitaḥ ।। tasmād bruvanti putreti putraṃ dharmavido janāḥ ।। pitrā putras tu goptaś cet ko doṣo vada sāṃpratam । rakṣitas tava pitrāsi kimarthaṃ vada bāliśa ।। anena tava vākyena śatravo yādavāḥ kṛtāḥ ।
tvaṃ cāpi vidhṛtas tābhyāṃ jātavaireṇa cetasā ।। vasudeve tvayā kṣipte vāsudeve ca kopite ।। tyakṣyāmahe vayaṃ sarve bhavantaṃ yadi sādhavaḥ । asanto vayam evātra loke khyātā narādhama ।।
yadi saktāḥ parityaktuṃ putra tvāṃ sāṃprataṃ vayam । sarvān asmān parityajya gacchasīti na saṃśayaḥ । śaṃsanti hīmāni bhayaṃ nimittāny aśubhāni te ।। puryā vaidhavyaśaṃsīni kāraṇair anumīmahe ।।
vakram aṅgārakaś cakre vyāharanti kharaṃ dvijāḥ ।। budhena paścimā saṃdhyā vyāptā ghoreṇa tejasā । vaiśvānarapathe śukro hy aticāraṃ cacāra ha ।। ketunā dhūmaketos tu nakṣatrāṇi trayodaśa । bharaṇyādīni bhinnāni nānuyanti niśākaram । ubhe saṃdhye purīṃ ghorā paryeti bahu vāśatī ।। calaty aparvaṇi mahī girīṇāṃ śikharāṇi ca ।।
pratilomaṃ ca yānty ete vyāharanto mṛgadvijāḥ ।। dhūmotpātair diśo vyāptāḥ śuṣkāśanisamāhatāḥ ।। calitā devatāḥ sthānāt tyajanti vihagā nagān ।। tāni sarvāṇi paśyāmo nimittāny aśubhāni vai ।।
animittāgatakrodhaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭabhayo hy asi ।। mohāt kṣipasi durbuddhe kutas te śāntir ātmanaḥ ।। ahitaṃ svasya vaṃśasya na tvāṃ vayam upāsmahe ।। puṇḍarīkapalāśākṣaṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam ।।
bālaṃ cābālasadvṛttam īśvaraṃ sakaleśvaram । yogidhyeyaṃ sadādṛśyaṃ santaṃ sadasadātmakam ।। yo hi drakṣyati taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tasmai bhūyo namo namaḥ ।। ādyānām ādyam ādiṃ ca sakalaṃ niṣkalaṃ hariṃ । yo hi drakṣyati taṃ devaṃ tasmai bhūyo namo namaḥ ।। vayam eva nirānandās vayā guptā yataḥ sadā । yeṣāṃ tvam īśvaro adhanyas teṣāṃ śāntiḥ kuto ratiḥ । kṛṣṇo jñātīn samānāyya sa saṃdhānaṃ kariṣyati ।। kālasaṃpakvavijñāno brūhi tvaṃ yad yad icchasi ।। gaccha kṛṣṇasya nilayaṃ prītis te tena rocatām ।।
anyathā tu gatiḥ kaṃsa tava nāstīti niścayaḥ । kiṃcid apy abruvan krodhād viveśa svaṃ niveśanam ।। jagmur vigatasaṃkalpāḥ kaṃsavaikṛtaśaṃsinaḥ ।। jagāma rathamukhyena manasas tulyagāminā ।।
pitṛtulyena śaṃsanti bāndhavena samāgamam ।। keśinaḥ preṣito dūto vadhāyopendrakāraṇāt ।। vṛndāvanagato gopān bādhate sma durāsadaḥ ।। durdānto vājidaityo asau karoti kadanaṃ mahat ।।
durdamaḥ kāmacārī ca kesarī niravagrahaḥ ।। yatrāste sa hi duṣṭātmā keśī turagadānavaḥ ।। heṣitaiḥ spardhate vāyum plutair laṅghyate nabhaḥ ।। ākampitasaṭo raudraḥ kaṃsasya caritānugaḥ ।।
kṛtaṃ turagadaityena sarvān gopāñ jighāṃsatā ।। na nṛbhir godhanair vāpi sevyate vanavṛttibhiḥ ।। madāc calitavṛttena nṛmāṃsāny aśnatā bhṛśam ।। jagāma ghoṣasaṃvāsaṃ coditaḥ kāladharmaṇā ।।
krandamānā jagannātham kṛṣṇaṃ nātham upāśritāḥ ।। dattvābhayaṃ tu kṛṣṇo vai keśinaṃ so abhidudruve ।। heṣamāṇo javodagro govindābhimukho yayau ।। pratyujjagāma govindas toyadaḥ śaśinaṃ yathā ।।
manuṣyabuddhayo gopāḥ kṛṣṇam ūcur hitauṣiṇaḥ ।। kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahābāho jñātīnāṃ nandivardhana । jagatām abhayado asi tvaṃ trāyasvāsmān viśeṣataḥ । upasarpyo bhavān bālaḥ pāpaś caiṣa durāsadaḥ ।। uttamaś ca hayendrāṇāṃ dānavo apratimo yudhi ।।
svadhyaḥ sarvasattvānāṃ prathamaḥ pāpakarmaṇām ।। keśinā saha yuddhāya matiṃ cakre arisūdanaḥ ।। padbhyām ubhābhyāṃ sa hayaḥ krodhenārujate drumān ।। valayo abhrataraṃgābhāḥ susruvuḥ krodhajaṃ jalam ।।
himakāle yathā vyomni nīhāram iva candramāḥ ।। sa phenair gātranirgīrṇaiḥ prokṣayāmāsa sarvataḥ ।। rajasā sa hayaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ cakārāruṇamūrdhajam ।। dantān nirdaśamānas tu keśī kṛṣṇam upādravat ।।
purvābhyāṃ caraṇābhyāṃ vai kṛṣṇaṃ vakṣasy atāḍayat ।। kṛṣṇasya dānavo ghoraṃ prahāram amitaujasaḥ । adaśad bāhuvivaraṃ kṛṣṇasya ruṣito hayaḥ ।। rarāja keśī meghena saṃsaktaḥ kha ivāṃśumān ।।
vegena vāsudevasya krodhād dviguṇavikramaḥ ।। bāhum ābhoginaṃ kṛtvā mukhe kruddhaḥ samādadhat ।। punar ābhoginaṃ bāhuṃ tadvaktragatam añjasā । kṛṣṇaḥ prasārayāmāsa līlayā dānavaṃ hasan ।
daśanair mūlanirmuktaiḥ saphenaṃ rudhiraṃ vaman ।। akṣiṇī vikṛte cakre visṛte muktabandhane ।। utkarṇo naṣṭacetās tu sa keśī bahvaceṣṭata ।। svinnārdralomā śrāntas tu niryatnacaraṇo abhavat ।।
vyābhugna iva gharmānte candrārdhakiraṇair ghanaḥ ।। prabhātāvanataś candraḥ śrānto merum ivāśritaḥ ।। keśino vaktranirdhūtā vividhā daśanā bhuvi । petuḥ śaradi nistoyāḥ sitābhrāvayavā iva ।।
sa tu keśī bhṛśaṃ śrāntaḥ kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā । svabhujaṃ svāyataṃ kṛtvā pāṭito balavat tadā ।। sa pāṭito bhujenājau kṛṣṇena vikṛtānanaḥ । keśī nadan mahānādaṃ dānavo vyathitas tadā ।। vighūrṇamānaḥ srastāṅgo mukhād rudhiram udvaman । bhṛśaṃ vyaṅgīkṛtavapur nikṛttārdha ivācalaḥ ।। vyāditāsyo mahāraudraḥ so asuraḥ kṛṣṇabāhunā । nipapāta yathā kṛtto nāgo hi dvidalīkṛtaḥ । sa papātāśu vegena bhujāyāmena pāṭitaḥ । paśor iva mahāghoraṃ nihatasya pinākinā ।। droṇībhyāṃ māṃsapūrṇābhyāṃ pinākibhavane yathā । keśinas te dvidhā bhūte dve ardhe rejatuḥ kṣitau ।।
vajreṇa vinikṛttārdhau parvatāv iva bhūtale । vṛddhas tāla ivāraṇye gajendradaśanāṅkitaḥ ।। kṛṣṇaḥ padmapalāśākṣo hasaṃs tatraiva tasthivān ।। babhūvur muditāḥ sarve hatavighnā hataklamāḥ ।।
abhyanandan priyair vākyaiḥ pūjayantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। daityaḥ kṣiticaraḥ kṛṣṇa hayarūpaṃ samāsthitaḥ ।। ghnatā pāpam imaṃ tāta keśinaṃ hayam āhave ।। naike cānye janapadā hatānena durātmanā ।।
nṛlokaṃ nirnaraṃ kṛtvā cartukāmo yathāsukham ।। api devasamūheṣu kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivītale ।। evaṃ te tuṣṭuvur gopāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ kamalalocanam । prīto asmi viṣṇo deveśa kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti cāsakṛt ।।
namas tubhyaṃ jagannātha devadeva janārdana । namas tubhyaṃ namas tubhyaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādhara ।। namas te jñānarūpāya keśavāya ca cakriṇe । nama ādyāya bījāya nirguṇāya guṇātmane ।। namaḥ sahasraśirase tvāṃ nato asmi janārdana । namāmi lokanāthaṃ tvāṃ namas te devarūpiṇe ।। namas te astu hṛṣīkeśa pāhi naḥ sarvato hare । iti stutvā jagannāthaṃ punar evābravīd vacaḥ । tvayy eva kevalaṃ yuktam tridive tryambake api vā ।। idaṃ narahayaṃ yuddham darṣṭuṃ svargād ihāgataḥ ।। ahaṃ tv anena govinda karmaṇā paritoṣitaḥ ।।
kurvāṇasya vapur ghoram keśino duṣṭacetasaḥ ।। eṣo asya mṛtyur antāya vihito viśvayoninā ।। keśavo nāma nāmnā tvaṃ khyāto loke bhaviṣyasi ।। kṛtyaśeṣaṃ ca te kāryaṃ śaktas tvam asi māciram ।।
viḍambayantaḥ krīḍanti līlāṃ tvadbalam āśritāḥ ।। hastaprāptāni yuddhāni rājñāṃ tridivagāminām ।। avakāśā vibhajyante śakraloke mahīkṣitām ।। abhitas tan mahadyuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati mahīkṣitām ।।
bhedakāle narendrāṇāṃ pakṣagrāho bhaviṣyasi ।। śriyaṃ tyakṣyanti rājānas tvatprabhāvān na saṃśayaḥ ।। devatānāṃ divisthānāṃ jagataś ca jagatpate ।। kaṃse bhūyaḥ sameṣyāmi śāsite sādhayāmy aham ।।
bahunāpi kim uktena pāhi viprān yathāsukham । jānāmi tvāṃ mahābāho devānām api daivatam । evam uktvā tu sa tadā nāradaḥ khaṃ jagāma ha । tatheti sa samābhāṣya punar gopān samāsadat । gopān kṛṣṇaḥ samāsādya vrajam eva viveṣa ha ।। saṃdhyāraktatale vyomni śaśāṅke pāṇḍumaṇḍale ।।
īṣat tamaḥ saṃvṛtāsu dikṣu sarvāsu sarvataḥ ।। naktaṃcareṣu hṛṣṭeṣu piśitām iṣakāṅkṣiṣu ।। saṃdhyāmayīm iva guhāṃ saṃpraviṣṭe divākare ।। vanyair vaikhānasair mantrair hūyamāne hutāśane ।।
asakṛd vyāharantīṣu baddhavatsāsu dhenuṣu ।। saninādeṣu gopeṣu kālyamāne ca godhane ।। kāṣṭhabhārānataskandhair gopair abhyāgatais tathā ।। īṣad vigāhamānāyāṃ rajanyāṃ divase gate ।।
bhāskare tejasi gate saumye tejasy upasthite ।। agnīṣomātmake saṃdhau vartamāne jaganmaye ।। dagdhādrisadṛśe vyomni kiṃcit tārāgaṇākule ।। śaṃsadbhiḥ syandanenāśu prāpto dānapatir vrajam ।।
rauhiṇeyasya cākrūro nandagopasya cāsakṛt ।। padāni tasyākhilalokapāla ।kirīṭajuṣṭāmalapādareṇoḥ ।dadarśa goṣṭhe kṣitikautukāni ।vilakṣitāny abjayavāṅkuśādyaiḥ ।।taddarśanāhlādavivṛddhasaṃbhramaḥ ।premṇordhvaromāśrukalākulekṣaṇaḥ ।rathād avaskandya sa teṣv aceṣṭata ।prabhor amūny aṅghrirajāṃsy aho iti ।।dehabhṛtām iyān artho hitvā dambhaṃ bhiyaṃ śucam । saṃdeśād yo harer liṅga darśanaśravaṇādibhiḥ । tato nivedito gopair idaṃ tad iti yādavaḥ । avaruhya tato yānāt praviveśa mahābalaḥ ।। harṣapūrṇena vaktreṇa sāśrunetreṇa caiva hi ।
vatsamadhye sthitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ savatsam iva govṛṣam ।। netrābhyāṃ yādavo viṣṇum ākulaṃ samudaikṣata ।। acintayat tadākrūro loke matsadṛśo na hi । ya enaṃ lokanāthaṃ taṃ sakalaṃ dṛṣṭavān aham ।।
nārāyaṇam aṇīyāṃsaṃ sthūlāt sthūlataraṃ harim ।। ko ayaṃ matsadṛśo loke dṛṣṭavān yo aham īśvaram । ehi keśava tāteti pravyāharata dharmavit ।। avyaktayuvanaṃ kṛṣṇam akrūraḥ praśaśaṃse ha ।।
saṃpūrṇajalameghābhaḥ parvatapravarākṛtiḥ ।। dviṣannidhanadakṣābhyāṃ bhujābhyāṃ sādhu bhūṣitaḥ ।। gopaveṣadharo viṣṇur udagrāgratanūruhaḥ ।। kuṇḍalottamayogyābhyāṃ śravaṇābhyāṃ vibhūṣitaḥ ।।
dvābhyāṃ bhujābhyāṃ dīrghābhyāṃ vṛttābhyām upaśobhitaḥ ।। pīte vasāno vasane so ayaṃ viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ ।। trailokyākrāntibhūtābhyāṃ bhuvi padbhyām avasthitaḥ ।। dvitīya udyataś caiva gadāsaṃyogam icchati ।।
śobhate adya bhuvi śreṣṭhas tridaśānāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥ ।। gopālo yādavaṃ vaṃśaṃ kṣīṇaṃ vistārayiṣyati ।। vaṃśam āpūrayiṣyanti oghā iva mahārṇavam ।। nihatāmitrasāmantaṃ sphītaṃ kṛtayuge yathā ।।
rājñāṃ bhaviṣyaty upari na ca rājā bhaviṣyati ।। purā puraṃdaro rājā devatānāṃ triviṣṭape ।। sthāpayiṣyati rājānam ugrasenaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। brāhmaṇair brahmavādaiś ca purāṇo ayaṃ hi gīyate ।।
tathā hy asyotthitā buddhir mānuṣyam upasevitum ।। viṣṇutvaṃ manasā caiva pūjayiṣyāmi mantravat ।। viṣṇuṃ tvāṃ pūjayiṣyāmi manasā caiva mantravān । amānuṣaṃ vedmi cainaṃ ye cānye divyacakṣuṣaḥ ।।
stoṣye devaṃ jagannāthaṃ vārāhaṃ vāmanaṃ harim । namāmi puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ naranārāyaṇākṛtim । namāmi vāmanaṃ viṣṇuṃ trailokyākrāntapauruṣam । sahānena gamiṣyāmi savrajo yadi maṃsyate ।। viveśa nandagopasya kṛṣṇena saha saṃsadam ।। gopavṛddhān samānīya provācāmitadakṣiṇaḥ ।।
śvaḥ purīṃ mathurāṃ tāta gamiṣyāmaḥ śivāya vai ।। kaṃsājñayā samucitaṃ karam ādāya vārṣikam ।। vayaṃ caiva pragantāro ratham āsthāya saṃgatāḥ । taṃ drakṣyatha samṛddhaṃ ca svajanaṃ ca sameṣyatha ।।
dīnaṃ putravadhaśrāntaṃ yuvām atha sameṣyathaḥ ।। daśānte śoṣitaṃ vṛddhaṃ duḥkhaiḥ śithilatāṃ gatam ।। dahyamānaṃ divā rātrau sotkaṇṭhenāntarātmanā ।। devakīṃ devasaṃkāśāṃ sidantīṃ vihataprabhām ।।
viyogaśokasaṃtaptāṃ vivatsām iva saurabhīm ।। svarbhānuvadanagrastāṃ śaśāṅkasya prabhām iva ।। tvatpravṛttena śokena sīdantīṃ vai tapasvinīm ।। arūpajñāṃ tava vibho vaktrasyāsyenduvarcasaḥ ।।
apatyārtho nu kas tasyā varaṃ hy evānapatyatā ।। saputrā tv aphale putre dhik prajātena tapyate ।। pareṣām apy abhayado na sā śocitum arhati ।। tvatkṛte bhartsyamānau tau kaṃsenādīrghadarśinā ।।
tāṃ śokasalile magnām uttārayitum arhasi ।। putrayogena saṃyojya kṛṣṇa dharmam avāpsyasi ।। vipulaś ca dhṛtaḥ śailo yathā vai bhūdharas tvayā ।। paraprāṇaharaḥ keśī duṣṭātmā ca hatas tvayā ।।
yathā dharmam avāpnoṣi tat kṛṣṇa paricintyatām ।। te sarve cakrur aśrūṇi netrair duḥkhānvitā bhṛśam ।। andhena kiṃcid uktvaiva kaṃso nirbhartsitaḥ kila । mātā te devakī kṛṣṇa kaṃsasya sahate avaśā ।।
ṛṇaṃ vai pratikartavyaṃ yathāyogam udāhṛtam ।। parityajetāṃ tau śokaṃ syāc ca dharmas tavātulaḥ ।। dharmas te vipulo ananto bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ । bāḍham ity eva tejasvī na ca cukrodha keśavaḥ ।।
akrūravacanaṃ śrutvā saṃceluḥ kaṃsaśāsanāt ।। sajjaṃ copāyanaṃ kṛtvā gopavṛddhāḥ pratasthire ।। yathāsāraṃ yathāyūtham upanīya payo ghṛtam ।। te sarve gopapatayo gamanāyopatasthire ।।
rauhiṇeyatṛtīyasya sā niśā vyatyavartata ।। naiśākare raśmijāle kṣaṇadākṣayasaṃhṛte ।। pratyūṣapavanāsāraiḥ kledite dharaṇītale ।। śītāṃśuḥ śāntakiraṇo niṣprabhaḥ samapadyata ।।
eko nāśayate rūpam eko vardhayate vapuḥ । manthāvartanapūrṇeṣu gargareṣu nadatsu ca ।। gopair āpūryamāṇeṣu ghoṣarathyāsu sarvaśaḥ ।। tvaritāḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā jagmuḥ syandanavāhanāḥ ।।
trayo rathagatā jagmus trilokapatayo yathā ।। syandanaṃ tāta rakṣasva yatnaṃ ca kuru vājiṣu ।। pragāḍhaṃ yatnam āsthāya kṣaṇaṃ tāta pratīkṣatām ।। divyair bhāgavatair mantraiḥ sarvalokaprabhuṃ yataḥ ।।
guhyaṃ bhāgavataṃ devaṃ sarvalokasya bhāvanam । sahasraśirasaṃ devam anantaṃ nīlavāsasam ।। sarvaṃ tad amṛtaprakhyam aśiṣyāmy amaro yathā ।। samājas tatra sarpāṇāṃ śāntyarthaṃ vai bhaviṣyati ।।
nivṛtto bhujagendrasya yāvad asmi hradottamāt ।। āvāṃ khalu na śaktau svas tvayā hīnāv ihāsitum ।। evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena praṇamya manasā harim । rasātale sa dadṛśe sarpalokam imaṃ yathā ।।
rasātale hradāntaś ca darśanāgamanaṃ yathā । lāṅgalāsaktahastāgram musalāpāśritodaram ।। kuṇḍalaikadharaṃ mattam suptam amburuhekṣaṇam ।। svāsīnaṃ svastikābhyāṃ ca varābhyāṃ ca mahīdharam ।।
jātarūpamayaiḥ padmair mālayā cchannavakṣasam ।। padmanābhaṃ sitābhrābham bhābhir jvalitatejasam ।। pūjyamānaṃ dvijihvendrair vāsukipramukhaiḥ prabhum ।। avījayetāṃ taṃ devam dharmāsanagataṃ prabhum ।।
vṛto anyaiḥ sacivaiḥ sarpaiḥ karkoṭakapuraḥsaraiḥ ।। rājānaṃ snāpayāmāsuḥ snātam ekārṇavāmbubhiḥ ।। koṭikandarpasundaram । dakṣiṇāvartasusnigdha- ।
sahasraśubhanāmānam arkacandrekṣaṇadyutim । pītāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ sūpaviṣṭaṃ dadarśa ha ।। saṃkarṣaṇam ivāsīnaṃ taṃ divyaṃ viṣṭaraṃ vinā ।। tasya saṃstambhayāmāsa vākyaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ svatejasā ।।
sa ca bhāgavatair mantrair arcayitvā gadādharam । stutvā ca devam īśānaṃ varadaṃ bhaktavatsalam । ātmānaṃ kṛtakṛtyānām agresaram amaṃsta saḥ । udatiṣṭhat punas toyād vismito amitadakṣiṇaḥ ।। udīkṣamāṇāv anyonyaṃ dadarśādbhutarūpiṇau ।। ijyate yatra devaḥ sa nīlavāsāḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
dadarśa kṛṣṇam akrūraḥ pūjyamānaṃ yathāvidhi ।। rathaṃ tenaiva mārgeṇa jagāmāmitadakṣiṇaḥ ।। kīdṛśaṃ nāgalokasya vṛttaṃ bhāgavate hrade ।। manye dṛṣṭaṃ tvayāścaryaṃ hṛdayaṃ te yathācalam ।।
kiṃ bhaviṣyati lokeṣu careṣu sthāvareṣu ca ।। tad ihāpi yathā tatra paśyāmi ca ramāni ca ।। ataḥ parataraṃ kṛṣṇa nāścaryaṃ draṣṭum utsahe ।। ko vāyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vismayaṃ bhavatā vinā । namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyaṃ vismayāya jagatpate । namo astu devadeveśa tubhyaṃ sarvātmane namaḥ । namo astu viṣṇave tubhyam ameyāya jagatpate ।। kiṃ vānena jagannātha kṛtakṛtyo asmi sāṃpratam । kṛtyaśeṣaṃ sadā viṣṇo kim utsṛjasi sāṃpratam ।
yāvann āstaṃ vrajaty eṣa divasānte divākaraḥ ।। kṛṣṇena sahitāḥ prāptās tathā saṃkarṣaṇena ca । asasāda purīṃ rasyāṃ mathurāṃ kaṃsapālitām । viviśuḥ pūḥpradhānāṃ vai kāle raktadivākare ।।
praveśitau buddhimatā akrūreṇārkatejasā ।। tyaktavyā tāta gamane vasudevagṛhe spṛhā ।। bhartsyate ca divā rātrau neha sthātavyam ity api ।। tad yuvābhyāṃ hi kartavyaṃ pitrarthaṃ sukham uttamam । yathā sukham avāpnoti tad vai kāryaṃ hitānvitam । nāhaṃ yuvābhyāṃ rahitaḥ pravekṣye mathurāṃ purīm । tyaktuṃ nārhasi māṃ nātha bhaktaṃ te bhaktavatsala ।। āgaccha yāma gehān naḥ sanāthān kurv adhokṣaja । punīhi pādarajasā gṛhān no gṛhamedhinām । yacchaucenānutṛpyanti pitaraḥ sāgnayaḥ surāḥ ।। āpas te aṅghryavanejanyas trīn lokān śucayo apunan । śirasādhatta yāḥ śarvaḥ svayaṃ tāḥ sagarātmajāḥ ।। devadeva jagannātha puṇyaśravaṇakīrtana । yadūnām uttamaḥśloka nārāyaṇa namo astu te ।
prekṣantau mathurāṃ vīra rājamārgaṃ ca dhārmika ।। tasyaiva tu gṛhaṃ sādho gacchāvo yadi manyase । evam ukto bhagavatā so akrūro vimanā iva । purīṃ praviṣṭaḥ kaṃsāya karmāvedya gṛhaṃ yayau । akrūro api namaskṛtya manasā viṣṇum avyayam । jagāma kaṃsapārśvaṃ tu prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā । tau ca devau jagannāthau balakeśavasaṃjñitau । ālānābhyām ivotsṛṣṭau kuñjarau yuddhakāṅkṣiṇau ।। dārakāś ca tayor mārgam anuvavruḥ samantataḥ ।
ayācetāṃ tatas tāni vāsāṃsi virajāni vai ।। rājño vāsāṃsi yau mūrkhau yācetāṃ nirbhayāv ubhau ।। kāmarāgāṇi śataśo rajāmi vividhāni ca ।। jātarāgāv idaṃ dṛṣṭvā raktam ācchādanaṃ bahu ।।
mūrkhau prākṛtavijñānau vāso yācitum arhatha ।। prāptāriṣṭāya mūrkhāya sṛjate vāṅmayaṃ viṣam ।। gatāsuḥ sa papātorvyāṃ rajako vyastamastakaḥ ।। tvaritaṃ muktakeśyaś ca jagmuḥ kaṃsaniveśanam ।।
kṛṣṇo api balabhadraś ca vāsāṃsy ādāya sarvataḥ । paridhāya tu tau pūrvaṃ śobhayetāṃ mahāmatī ।। dārakebhyas tato dattvā suślakṣṇāni mṛdūni ca । te ca sarve suvasanā virejuḥ śataśas tathā ।। śeṣāṇi tu tadā kṛṣṇo vāsāṃsi subahūny api । ācchichācchidya sahasā ciccheda ca pipeṣa ca ।। bhasmasād akarot tasya rajakasya niveśanam । yathāyogaṃ yathābhogyaṃ yathāyogaṃ ni[darśya] ca । vīthīṃ mālyāpaṇānāṃ vai gandhāghrātau dvipāv iva ।। prabhūtamālyāpaṇavāl lakṣmīvān mālyajīvanaḥ ।।
dehīty uvāca tatkālaṃ mālākāram akātaram ।। bhavatoḥ svam idaṃ ceti provāca priyadarśanaḥ ।। śrīs tvāṃ matsaṃśrayā saumya dhanaughair abhivartsyate ।। kṛṣṇasya patito mūrdhnā pratijagrāha taṃ varam ।।
sa bhṛśaṃ bhayasaṃvigno nottaraṃ pratyapadyata ।। adyāpi tasya prabhavo vaṃśo bhavati ratnavān । kīrtimān balavān nityaṃ keśavena tadā kṛtaḥ ।। viṣṇoḥ prasādaḥ sumahān sadārakṣat tadanvayam । kubjāṃ dadṛśatur bhūyaḥ ānulepanabhājanām ।। nayasy ambujapatrākṣi kṣipram ākhyātum arhasi ।।
kṛṣṇaṃ jaladagambhīraṃ vidyutkuṭilagāminī ।। dṛṣṭvaiva tvāravindākṣa vismitāsmi varānana । sthitāsmy āgaccha bhadraṃ te hṛdayasyāsi me priyaḥ ।। mahārājasya dayitāṃ niyuktām anulepane ।।
tām uvāca tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sairandhrīṃ prahasann iva । sugandham etad rājārhaṃ ruciraṃ rucirānane । āvayor gātrasadṛśaṃ dīyatām anulepanam ।। draṣṭuṃ dhanurmahaṃ divyaṃ rāṣṭraṃ caiva maharddhimat ।।
tataḥ sā praṇatā bhūtvā pradadāv anulepanam । rājārham idam agryaṃ ca tad gṛhāṇānulepanam ।। kṛṣṇo atha balabhadraś ca tadādāyānulepanam । aṅgāni cāpy alimpetāṃ śubhaṃ ca susugandhi ca ।। mālayātha tadā viṣṇur baddhayā bahupuṣpayā । govindo gopatiḥ kṛṣṇo rarāja kṛtaśekharaḥ । saṃkarṣaṇo atha balavān rarāja bahumālayā । tīrthagau paṅkadigdhāṅgau yamunāyāṃ yathā vṛṣau ।।
dārakāś ca tathā sarve virejuḥ kṛtaśekharāḥ । vikṛtaṃ bhūṣayanto api prabhāvāc chārṅgadhanvanaḥ । śanaiḥ saṃtolayāmāsa kṛṣṇo līlāvidhānavit ।। jahāsoccaiḥ stanataṭā ṛjuyaṣṭir latā yathā ।। kva yāsyasi mayā ruddhaḥ kānta tiṣṭha gṛhāṇa mām ।।
vīkṣamāṇau prahasitau kubjāyāḥ śrutavistarau ।। yatheṣṭaṃ gamyatāṃ bhadre nāhaṃ tādṛgvidho naraḥ । tatas tau kubjayā muktau praviṣṭau rājasaṃsadam ।। gūḍhaceṣṭānanau bhūtvā praviṣṭau rājaveṣma tat ।।
himavadvanasaṃbhūtau siṃhāv iva balotkaṭau ।। papracchatuś ca tau vīrāv āyudhāgārikaṃ tadā ।। āyāgabhūtaṃ kaṃsasya darśayasva yadīcchasi ।। anāropyam asaṃbhedyaṃ devair api savāsavaiḥ ।।
dorbhyāṃ kamalapatrākṣaḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।। āropayāmāsa balī nāmayāmāsa cāsakṛt ।। dvidhābhūtam abhūn madhye dhanur āyāgabhūṣitam ।। dhanuṣo bhajyamānasya śabdaḥ khaṃ rodasī diśaḥ । pūrayām āsa yaṃ śrutvā kaṃsas trāsam upāgamat ।। tadrakṣiṇaḥ sānucarā kupitā ātatāyinaḥ । gṛhītukāmā āvavrur gṛhyatāṃ vadhyatām iti ।। atha tān durabhiprāyān vilokya balakeśavau । kruddhau dhanvana ādāya śakale tāṃś ca jaghnatuḥ ।। balaṃ ca kaṃsaprahitaṃ hatvā śālāmukhāt tataḥ । niṣkramya ceratur dṛptau nirīkṣya purasaṃpadaḥ ।। tayos tad adbhutaṃ vīryaṃ niśamya puravāsinaḥ । tejaḥ prāgalbhyarūpaṃ ca menire vibudhottamau ।
niścakrāma mahāvegaḥ sa ca saṃkarṣaṇo yuvā ।। cacālāntaḥpuraṃ sarvaṃ diśaś caiva pupūrire ।। nirgamya tv āyudhāgārāj jagmatur gopasaṃnidhau ।। vegenāyudhapālas tu gacchan saṃbhrāntamānasaḥ । samīpaṃ nṛpater gatvā kākocchvāso abhyabhāṣata ।।
nirvṛttam asmin kāle yaj jagataḥ saṃbhramopamam ।। nīlapitāmbaradharau pītaśvetānulepanau ।। tāv antaḥpuram ajñātau praviṣṭau kāmaveginau । saumyau mahasya codyuktāv āgatau puruṣarṣabhau ।
mayā dṛṣṭau parivyaktaṃ rucirācchādanasrajau ।। jagrāha tad dhanūratnaṃ durgrahaṃ daivatair api ।। āropayitvā vegena nāmayāmāsa līlayā ।। muṣṭideśe vikūjitvā dvidhābhūtam abhajyata ।।
tataḥ pracalitā bhūmir naiva bhāti ca bhāskaraḥ । dhanuṣo bhaṅganādena bhramatīva nabahstalam ।। tad adbhutam ahaṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ । bhayād bhayadasatrūṇāṃ tad ihākhyātum āgataḥ ।। na jānāmi mahārāja kau tāv amitavikramau । ekaḥ kailāsasaṃkāśa eko añjanagiriprabhaḥ । jagāma tad dvidhā kṛtvā na jāne ko apy asau nṛpa ।। visṛjyāyudhapālaṃ vai praviveśa gṛhottamam ।। babhūva vimanā rājā cintayan bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ ।।
kathaṃ bālo vigatabhīr avamatya mahābalam । prekṣamāṇas tu puruṣair dhanur bhaṅktvā vinirgataḥ ।। yasyārthe dāruṇaṃ karma kṛtvā lokavigarhitam । pitṛsvasrātmajān bhītaḥ ṣaḍevāhaṃ upasthitam ।।
daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa na śakyam ativartitum । nāradoktaṃ ca vacanaṃ nūnaṃ mahyam upasthitam ।। evaṃ rājā vicintyātha niṣkramya sa gṛhottamāt । prekṣāgāraṃ jagāmāśu mañcānām avalokakaḥ ।।
śreṇīnāṃ dṛḍhasaṃyuktair mañcavāṭair nirantaram ।। kuṭībhiś ca pravṛddhābhir ekastambhaiś ca bhūṣitam ।। udakpravaṇasaṃśliṣṭaṃ mañcārohaṇam uttamam ।। channaṃ tad vedikābhiś ca mānavaughabharakṣamam ।।
śvaḥ sacitrāḥ samālyāś ca sapatākās tathaiva ca ।। kriyantāṃ mañcavāṭāś ca valabhīvīthayas tathā ।। paṭās taraṇaśobhāś ca balayaś cānurūpataḥ ।। udabhārasahāḥ sarve sakāñcanaghaṭottarāḥ ।।
prāśnikāś ca nimantryantāṃ śreṇyaś ca sapurogamāḥ ।। samāje mañcaśobhāś ca kalpyantāṃ sūpakalpitāḥ ।। samājavāṭān niṣkramya viveśa svaṃ niveśanam ।। cāṇūrasyāprameyasya muṣṭikasya tathaiva ca ।।
kaṃsasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya hṛṣṭau viviśatus tadā ।। uvāca kaṃso nṛpatiḥ sopanyāsam idaṃ vacaḥ ।। pūjitau ca yathānyāyaṃ satkārārhau viśeṣataḥ ।। kartavyaṃ me mahat karma bhavadbhyāṃ svena tejasā ।।
saṃkarṣaṇaś ca kṛṣṇaś ca bālāv api jitaśramau ।। nipātān antaraṃ śīghraṃ hantavyau nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। nāvajñā tatra kartavyā kartavyo yatna eva hi ।। āyatāṃ ca tadātve ca śreyo mama bhaviṣyati ।।
ūcatur yuddhasaṃmattau mallau cāṇūramuṣṭikau ।। hatāv ity avagantavyau pretarūpau tapasvinau ।। āvābhyāṃ roṣayuktābhyāṃ pramukhasthau vanaukasau ।। hatvā tau goṣu saṃvṛddhau dāsyāvas tava bhūtalam । vyapaitu te bhayaṃ rājann āvāṃ mallottamau mṛdhe ।। ity uktvāspoṭanaṃ cakre mattamalladvayaṃ tathā । siṃhanādaṃ ca tac cakre bhūgolakavidārakam ।
anujñātau narendreṇa svagṛhaṃ pratijagmatuḥ ।। hastī kuvalayāpīḍaḥ samājadvāri tiṣṭhatu ।। dānotkaṭakaṭaś caṇḍaḥ prativāraṇaroṣaṇaḥ ।। vasudevasutau nīcau yathā syātāṃ gatāyuṣau ।।
bhavetāṃ ghātitau raṅge paśyeyam aham utkaṭau ।। chinnamūlo nirālambaḥ sabhāryo vinaśiṣyati ।। vinaśiṣyanti chinnāśā dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ nipātitam ।। purīṃ niryādavāṃ kṛtvā vicariṣyāmy ahaṃ sukhī ।।
śeṣāś ca me parityaktā yādavāḥ kṛṣṇapakṣiṇaḥ ।। mānuṣeṇālpavīryeṇa yathā mām āha nāradaḥ ।। prekṣituṃ saha sā strībhir gatā vanakutūhalāt ।। cacāra nagaśṛṅgeṣu kandareṣu nadīṣu ca ।।
śṛṇvantī kāmajananīr vācaḥ śrotrasukhāvahāḥ ।। abhīkṣṇam abhiśṛṇvantī strīdharmam abhirocayat ।। hṛdyaḥ kusumagandhāḍhyo vavau manmathabodhanaḥ ।। mumucur gandham adhikaṃ saṃtatāsāramūrchitāḥ ।।
nīpā dīpā ivābhānti puṣpakaṇṭakadhāriṇaḥ ।। yauvanastheva vanitā khaṃ dadhārārtavaṃ vapuḥ ।। ugrasenasya rūpeṇa mātaraṃ me pradharṣayat ।। śaṅkitā cābhavat paścāt tasya gauravadarśanāt ।।
kaś ca tvaṃ vikṛtākāro yenāsmi malinīkṛtā ।। patyur me rūpam āsthāya nīca nīcena karmaṇā ।। jugupsitā ca vatsyāmi patipakṣair nirākṛtā ।। aviśvāsyam anāyuṣyaṃ paradārābhimarśanam ।।
ahaṃ vai drumilo nāma saubhasya patir ūrjitaḥ ।। mānuṣaṃ patim āśritya hīnavīryaparākramam ।। ny hy āsīnn iyatā buddhir mānuṣīṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। prasūtā devasaṃkāśān putrān amitavikramān ।।
śuddhā keśānvidhunvantī bhāṣase yad yad icchasi ।। kaṃso nāma ripudhvaṃśī tava putro bhaviṣyati ।। uvāca vyathitā devī dānavaṃ duṣṭavādinam ।। santi striyo nīcavṛttāḥ santi caiva pativratāḥ ।।
dhṛtās tābhis trayo lokāḥ sarve vai kulapāṃsana ।। na me bahumatas tv eṣa śṛṇu cāpi yad ucyate ।। bhaviṣyati sa te mṛtyur yaś ca dattas tvayā sutaḥ ।। tenaiva rathamukhyena divyenāpratigāminā ।
jagāma ca purīṃ dīnā mātā tad ahar eva me ।। mām evam uktvā bhagavān nārado munisattamaḥ । dīpyamānas tapovīryāt sākṣād agnir iva jvalan ।। vallakīṃ vādyamānas tu saptasvaravimūrchitām । gāyano lakṣyavīthīṃ ca jagāma brahmaṇo antikam ।। śṛṇuṣvedaṃ mahāmātra nibodha vacanaṃ mama । tathyaṃ coktaṃ nāradena traikālajñena dhīmatā ।। ahaṃ balena vīryeṇa nayena vinayena ca । prabhāveṇaiva śauryeṇa tejasā vikrameṇa ca ।। satyena caiva dānena nānyo asti sadṛśaḥ pumān । viditvā sarvam ātmānaṃ vacanaṃ śraddadhāmy aham । mātāpitṛbhyāṃ saṃtyaktaḥ sthāpitaḥ svena tejasā ।। tad imau ghātayitvā tu hastinā gopakilbiṣau ।
badhvā ca pitaraṃ rājye sthito asmi ca balīyasā । etān api haniṣyami hatvā gopālakāv ubhau ।। sthiro bhava mahāmātra samājadvāri mā ciram ।। samāgatau ca tau dṛṣṭvā jahi gopālakāv ubhau ।
saṃkīryata mahāraṅgaḥ paurair yuddhadidṛkṣubhiḥ ।। rājabhir viṣayāntasthaiḥ pradhānapuruṣais tataḥ । nārībhir māthurīyābhiḥ śyāmābhiḥ saṃghasaṃsthitāḥ ।। pīnastanībhiḥ kaṃsasya tathā bilvapayodharaiḥ । aparākhaṇḍitābhis tu mañjarīsadṛśaiḥ stanaiḥ । bhrū dhanurdṛṣṭiviśikhaṃ nāsā jyā siñjati tataḥ । ghnanty ākṛṣya ca kṛṣṇaṃ tāḥ kaṃsena viniyojitāḥ ।। kandalīdaṇḍakāṇḍena badhvā taṃ mohapāśakaiḥ । nābhīhrade ca gambhīre kālayākhye parājite ।। kaṃsadhātrīsṛtāṃ snātvā dantaiś chinnastanīṃ tataḥ । pāṇibhyāṃ tatkucau gopo na samarthaḥ pradharṣitum ।। śakaṭasya ca bhaṅgaṃ sa yathā kāritavāñ śiśuḥ । asmākaṃ śakaṭībhaṅgaṃ yugmayoḥ kucayos tataḥ ।। ariṣṭaṃ hatavān yo ayaṃ kakudā sadṛśau stanau । ghātayiṣyati gopo ayaṃ mallābhyāṃ balavattaraḥ । sagavākṣārdhacandrāś ca satalottamabhūṣitāḥ ।। alaṃkṛtair virājadbhiḥ śāradair iva toyadaiḥ ।।
samājavāṭaḥ śuśubhe sa meghaughair ivārṇavaḥ ।। śreṇīnāṃ ca gaṇānāṃ ca mañcā bhānty acalopamāḥ ।। rejuḥ kāñcanacitrāṇi ratnajvālākulāni ca ।। rejur javanikākṣepaiḥ sapakṣā iva khe nagāḥ ।।
maṇīnāṃ ca vicitrāṇāṃ vicitrāś cerur arciṣaḥ ।। śobhitā vāramukhyābhir vimānapratimaujasaḥ ।। prakīrṇāś ca kuthāś citrāḥ sapuṣpastabakadrumāḥ ।। phalāvadaṃśapūrṇāś ca cāṅger yaḥ pānayojitāḥ ।।
rejuḥ prastaraśas tatra prakāśā mañcasaṃcayāḥ ।। strīnāṃ prekṣāgṛhā bhānti rājahaṃsā ivāmbare ।। rukmapatranibhastambhaś citraniryogaśobhitaḥ ।। śobhito mālyadāmaiś ca nivāsakṛtalakṣaṇaḥ ।।
samājavāṭe saṃstabdhe kampamānārṇavaprabhe ।। nandagopādayo gopā bhojarājasamāhṛtāḥ । niveditopāyanās te ekasmin mañca āviśan । tiṣṭhatv iti samājñāpya prekṣāgāram athāyayau ।। śuśubhe śvetamukuṭaḥ śvetābhra iva candramāḥ ।।
rūpam apratimaṃ dṛṣṭvā paurāḥ procur jayāśiṣaḥ ।। tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ । puraṃdaraṃ puraskṛtya jagmur yuddhadidṛkṣavaḥ ।। vimānasthās tu te sarve virejuḥ sitacāmarāḥ । śakro apy airāvatagataḥ śuśubhe ca samātaliḥ ।। ūrvaśīpramukhāḥ sarvā vāramukhyās tadābhavan । śakrapārśvagatās tās tu sitacāmarapāṇayaḥ ।। dilīpapramukhās te tu munayo rājasattamāḥ । anekayugaparyantaṃ sthitā divi ca śakravat । bhagavantaṃ jagannāthaṃ draṣṭuṃ gopavibhūṣitam । nāradād yās tu munayo yuddhaṃ draṣṭuṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।। mallābhyāṃ devayoḥ sārdhaṃ raṅgamadhye samutthitam । amaraughais tadākāśaṃ nibiḍaṃ samapadyata ।। raṅgavāṭas tadā caiva janaiḥ sarvaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ । dyauś cāpi devasaṃghaiś ca nibiḍābhūd viyaccaraiḥ । ekākāraṃ samabhavad bhūtalaṃ ca nabhaḥsthalam । tisraś ca bhāgaśaḥ kakṣyāḥ prāviśan balaśālinaḥ ।। vasudevasutau hṛṣṭau raṅgadvāram upasthitau ।।
ballavau vastrasaṃvītau suravandanabhūṣitau । ūrdhvapīḍau sragāpīḍau bāhuśastrakṛtodyamau । āsphoṭayantāv anyonyaṃ bāhū caivārgalāpamau । raṅgadvāraṃ samāsādya tasmin gajam avasthitam । apaśyat kuvalayāpīḍaṃ kṛṣṇo ambaṣṭhapraṇoditam ।। baddhvā parikaraṃ śauriḥ samuhya kuṭilālakān ।
uvāca hastipaṃ vācā meghanādagabhīrayā ।। ambaṣṭhāmbaṣṭha mārgaṃ nau dehy apākrama mā ciram । no cet sakuñjaraṃ hatvā nayāmi yamasādanam ।। evaṃ nirbhartsito ambaṣṭhaḥ kupitaḥ kopitaṃ gajam ।
codayām āsa kṛṣṇāya kālāntakayamopamam । tena mattena nāgena codyamānena vai bhṛśam ।। cakāra codito yatnaṃ nihantuṃ balakeśavau ।। kaṃsasyamatsaraṃ caiva jagarhe sa durātmanaḥ ।।
anena gajamukhyena hantuṃ vyavasitaḥ kila ।। aho tu kaṃso durmedhāḥ kim ato vismayaḥ paraḥ । iti saṃcintya bhagavān balabhadram udaikṣata ।। tasya tāṃ jagṛhe buddhiṃ balabhadro durātmanaḥ । yo mām anena nāgena pradharṣayitum icchati ।। sahasotpatya govindaś cakre tālasvanaṃ prabhuḥ ।। karaṃ ca śrīdharas tasya pratijagrāha vakṣasā ।।
babādhe taṃ gajaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pavanas toyadaṃ yathā ।। vimuktaḥ pādamadhyāc ca kṛṣṇo dvipam amohayat ।। gajaḥ sveṣv eva gātreṣu mathyamāno rarāsa ha ।। madaṃ susrāva roṣāc ca gharmāpāya yathā ghanaḥ ।।
nidhanāya matiṃ cakre kaṃsadviṣṭena cetasā ।। dorbhyāṃ viṣāṇam utpāṭya tenaiva prāharat tadā ।। hanyamānaḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ cakārārto rarāsa ha ।। kaṭābhyām atisusrāva vegavad bhūri śoṇitam ।।
śailapṛṣṭhārdhasaṃlīnaṃ vainateya ivoragam ।। jaghānaikaprahāreṇa gajāroham atholbaṇam ।। papāta samahāmātro vajrabhinna ivācalaḥ ।। tatas tau tu gajāṅgāni pragṛhya raṇakarkaśau । gajasya pādarakṣāṃś ca jaghnatuḥ puruṣarṣabhau ।। tāṃś ca hatvā viviśatur madhyaṃ raṅgasya tāv ubhau । nāsatyāv aśvinau svargād avatīrṇāv ivecchayā ।। vṛṣṇyandhakāś ca bhojāś ca dadṛsur vanamālinau । kṣveḍitotkruṣṭanādena bāhvor āsphoṭitena ca ।। siṃhanādaiś ca tālaiś ca harṣayām āsatur janam ।। tau dṛṣṭvā bhojarājas tu viṣasāda vṛthāmatiḥ । paurāṇām anurāgaṃ ca harṣaṃ cālakṣya bhārata ।
avatīrṇo arṇavākāraṃ samājaṃ sahapūrvajaḥ ।। mallānām aśanir nṛṇāṃ naravaraḥ strīṇāṃ smaro mūrtimān ।gopānāṃ svajano asatāṃ kṣitibhujāṃ śāstā svapitroḥ śiśuḥ ।mṛtyur bhojapater virāḍ aviduṣāṃ tattvaṃ paraṃ yogināṃ ।vṛṣṇīnāṃ paradevateti vidito raṅgaṃ praviṣṭo hariḥ ।devāś ca munayaḥ sarve namaskṛtvā gadādharam । vimānasthās tato yuddhaṃ dṛṣṭiṃ draṣṭuṃ samādadhuḥ ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahābāhur baladevena saṃyutaḥ । janāṃś ca manasā pūjya kaṃsaṃ hantuṃ samudyataḥ । pūrvajaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā kṛṣṇaṃ kamalalocanam ।। līlākṛtāṅgadaṃ vīraṃ madena rudhireṇa ca ।।
bāhuśabdaprahāreṇa cālayantaṃ vasuṃdharām ।। kṛṣṇaṃ bhṛśāyastamukhaḥ saroṣaṃ samudaikṣata ।। raṅgasthā api te sarve netrair animiṣais tathā । dadṛśuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā । candrārdhabimbasaṃyukto yathaikaśikharo giriḥ ।।
janaughapratinādena pūryamāṇa ivābabhau ।। tataḥ krodhābhitāmrākṣaḥ kaṃsaḥ paramakopanaḥ । cāṇūram ādiśad yuddhe kṛṣṇasya sumahābalam ।। andhraṃ mallaṃ ca nikṛtiṃ muṣṭikaṃ ca mahābalam । baladevāya sakrodho dideśādricayopa-mam । yodhavyaṃ saha kṛṣṇena tvayā yatnavateti vai ।। abhyavartata yuddhāya apāṃ pūrṇo yathā ghanaḥ ।।
āha cainaṃ sa govindaṃ vyapaneṣyāmi te madam । acirād drakṣyase gopa mama vaivasvataṃ balāt ।। tac chrutvaiva tu govindo babhāṣe taṃ gatāyuṣam । tādṛśaṃ tava sāmarthyaṃ drakṣyāmi balam uttamam । acirād drakṣyase malla tvayā vātha mayādhama ।। darśayasva samarthaś cet tvadbalaṃ kathyase adhama । evam uktvā tu govindo nanāda vividhaṃ bahu । yādavās tatra sahitā idaṃ vacanam abruvan ।। bāṇapakṣaṃ parityaṃ ca yuddhaṃ sāmnā nirīkṣya ca । kriyābalasamājñātam aśastraṃ nirmitaṃ purā ।।
karīṣeṇa ca mallasya satataṃ prakriyā smṛtā ।। sthitau bhūmigatau caiva yathā tau mārgam āsthitau । niyudhyataś ca paryāyaḥ prāśnikaiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।। balastho vā sthito raṅge jñeyaḥ kakṣyāntareṇa vai ।।
nirghātānantaraṃ kiṃcin na kartavyaṃ vijānatā ।। bālaḥ kṛṣṇo mahān andhras tatra na syād vicāraṇā ।। prāvalgata ca govindo vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha ।। yuddhaṃ mama sahānena rocate bāhuśālinā ।।
na hy ahaṃ bāhuyodhānāṃ dūṣayiṣyāmi yan matam ।। kaṣāyasya ca saṃsargaḥ samayo hy eṣa kalpitaḥ ।। reṅge ca niyatā siddhir etad yuddhamukhe vratam ।। atra vai nigrahaḥ kāryas toṣayiṣyāmy ahaṃ jagat ।।
bāhuyodhī sarīreṇa karmabhiś cānucintyatām ।। raṅgapratāpakāmena mallamārgaś ca dūṣitaḥ ।। raṅgasiddhis tu mallānāṃ pratimallanighātajā ।। hatasyāpi raṇe sastrair nākapṛṣṭhaṃ vidhīyate ।।
sā hi prāṇāntikā yātrā mahadbhiḥ sādhu pūjitā ।। mṛtasya raṅge kaḥ svargo jayato vā kuto ratiḥ ।। yotsyāma bālā balibhir bāhubhiḥ saha saṃkaṭe । evam uktvā tataḥ kṛṣṇaś cāṇūraṃ samapadyata ।
āsphoṭya bāhū rājendra cāṇūraḥ kṛṣṇam abhyayāt ।। tāv ubhau siṃhavikrāntau mattāv iva mahāgajau । yuyudhāte tadānyonyam ebhir mallapariśramaiḥ । pratāpārthe hatā mallā mallahantur vadho hi saḥ ।।
ubhābhyām abhavad ghoraṃ vāraṇābhyāṃ yathā vane ।। saṃnipātāvadhūtaiś ca pramāthonmathanais tathā ।। tāv ubhāv api saṃśliṣṭau yathā śailamayau tathā । kīlair vajranipātaiś ca prasṛṣṭābhis tathaiva ca ।।
jānubhiś cāsmanirghoṣaiḥ śirobhiś cāvaghaṭṭitaiḥ ।। balaprāṇena śūrāṇāṃ samājotsavasaṃnidhau ।। sādhu vādāṃś ca mañceṣu ghoṣayanty apare janāḥ ।। diviṣṭhāś ca tathā devāḥ sādhu sādhv iti cābruvan ।
nyavārayata tūryāṇi kaṃsaḥ savyena pāṇinā ।। khe saṃgatāny avādyanta devatūryāṇy anekaśaḥ ।। svayam eva pravādyanta tūryaghoṣāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। cerur vidyādharaiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛṣṇasya jayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।।
iti saptarṣayaḥ sarve ūcuś caiva nabhogatāḥ ।। balam āhārayāmāsa kaṃsasyābhāvadarśivān ।। mukutāc cāpi kaṃsasya papāta maṇir uttamaḥ ।। prāharan muṣṭinā mūrdhni vakṣasyāhatya jānunā ।।
tāpanīye yathā ghaṇṭe vakṣyopari vilambite ।। cāṇūro vigataprāṇo jīvitānte mahītale ।। saṃniruddho mahāmārgaḥ sa śaileneva lakṣyate ।। jagrāha muṣṭikaṃ raṅge kṛṣṇas tosalakaṃ punaḥ ।।
muṣṭinā cāhanad bhṛśam । papāta rudhirodgārī tatkṣaṇād gatajīvitaḥ । agamad baladevo andhram । sameyātāṃ rāmakṛṣṇau kālasya vaśavartinau ।। nirghātāvanatau bhūtvā raṅgamadhye vavalgatuḥ । bhrāmayitvā śataguṇaṃ niṣpipeṣa mahītale ।।
mukhād rudhiram atyartham ājagāma mumūrṣataḥ ।। andhramallaṃ mahāmallo maṇḍalāni vidarśayan ।। śirasy abhyahanad vīro vajreṇeva mahāgirim ।। papātābhimukhas tatra tato nādo mahān abhūt ।।
krodhasaṃraktanayanau raṅgamadhye vavalgatuḥ ।। andhre tadā mahāmalle muṣṭike ca nipātite ।। bhayakṣobhitasarvāṅgāḥ sarve tatrāvatasthire ।। prasnavotpīḍitā kṛṣṇaṃ devakī samudaikṣata ।।
vasudevo jarāṃ tyaktvā snehena taruṇāyate ।। papur hi netrabhramarair nimeṣāntaragāmibhiḥ ।। abhavad roṣaniryāsaḥ kṛṣṇasaṃdarśaneritaḥ ।। dīptam antargataṃ tasya hṛdayaṃ mānasāgninā ।।
kaṃsavaktrasya roṣeṇa raktasūryāyate vapuḥ ।। udyatasyeva sūryasya prasṛtāḥ pādapaṅktayaḥ ।। yathā ravikaraspṛṣṭā vṛkṣāvaśyāyabindavaḥ । gopāv etau samājaughān niṣkrāmyetāṃ vanecarau ।।
gopānām api me rājye na kaścit sthātum arhati ।। āyasair nigaḍākārair lohapāśair nigṛhyatām ।। avṛddhārheṇa daṇḍena kṣipram adyaiva vadhyatām ।। eṣāṃ hriyantāṃ gāvaś ca yac cāsti vasu kiṃcana ।।
dadarśāyastanayanaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ satyaparākramaḥ ।। jñātīnāṃ ca vyathāṃ dṛṣṭvā visaṃjñāṃ caiva devakīm ।। ārurukṣur mahābāhuḥ kaṃsanāśārtham acyutaḥ ।। asajjan vāyunā kṣipto yathā vidyud ghanād ghanam ।।
kevalaṃ kaṃsapārśvasthaṃ dadṛśuḥ puravāsinaḥ ।। ākāśād iva govindaṃ mene tatrāgataṃ vibhum ।। tam āviśantam ālokya mṛtyum ātmana āsanāt । manasvī sahasotthāya jagṛhe so asicarmaṇī ।। taṃ khaḍgapāṇiṃ vicarantam āśu ।śyenaṃ yathā dakṣiṇasavyam ambare ।samagrahīd durviṣahogratejā ।yathoragaṃ tārkṣyasutaḥ prasahya ।kiṃcid dayāparāmṛṣṭo hantuṃ naicchat sa keśavaḥ । ātmabhrātaram ājñāya nāyudhaṃ pātayat tadā ।। kāmācārapravṛttinyā striyā vai lālito naraḥ । kāmācāreṣu niḥśaktaḥ śvasann iva viṣīdate ।। sthitaḥ kaṃsas tu mañceṣu prasvinnaḥ sarvagātrakaiḥ । iti cintāsamāviṣṭaṃ dayāviṣṭaṃ ca keśavam ।। antarīkṣasamutpannā tatra vāṇī babhūva ha । jahi kaṃsaṃ yavīyāṃsam āyudhaiś ca vivarjitam ।। etac chrutvā tu kaṃsaṃ sa sahasotthitavāṃs tataḥ । vadan vākyaṃ janān vīkṣya vepamāno yathā nagaḥ ।। jahi keśava devānāṃ kuru kāryānuśāsanam । devam ūrjastaraṃ jñātvā yathā yatno hi pauruṣaḥ ।। ekadaiveṣu bhejāte sarvalokaśubhāvahaḥ । jahi gopa mahābāho prāṇā [hi] tvarayanti mām ।। kaivalyam āpnuyāṃ svarge tvatkarāmbujasāyakaiḥ । mūrdhajeṣu parāmṛṣṭaḥ kaṃso vai raṅgasaṃsadi ।।
sirasas tasya kṛṣṇena parāmṛṣṭasya pāṇinā ।। tathaiva ca visaṃmūḍho vihvalaḥ samapadyata ।। na śaśāka mukhaṃ draṣṭuṃ kaṃsaḥ kṛṣṇasya vai tadā ।। pralambābhyāṃ ca bāhubhyāṃ gātrair visṛtabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।
veṣṭamānaḥ samākṣiptaḥ kaṃsaḥ kṛṣṇena tejasā ।। śirasy abhyahanat kṛṣṇo muṣṭinā balavad balī । yenaiva muṣṭinā viṣṇur yathā syāt prāṇasaṃśayaḥ । keśeṣu balavad gṛhya kaṃsaṃ kleśārhatāṃ gatam ।। vaitaneyakaroddhūtaḥ patagendra ivābhavat ।
samājavāṭe parikhāṃ dehakṛṣṭāṃ cakāra ha ।। kṛṣṇo visarjayāmāsa kaṃsadeham adūrataḥ ।। krameṇa viparītena pāṃsubhiḥ paruṣīkṛtaḥ ।। na vibhāti viparyastaṃ vipalāśaṃ yathāmbujam ।।
kaṇṭhagrāhān nirastāsur vīramārgān nirākṛtaḥ ।। māṃsacchedaghanāḥ sarve nakhāgrā jīvitacchidaḥ ।। vavande vasudevasya pādau nihatakaṇṭakaḥ ।। sāsiñcat prasnavotpīḍaiḥ kṛṣṇam ānandaniḥsṛtaiḥ ।।
abhiṣekaṃ tadā cakre devakī kṛṣṇam avyayam । ugrasenasya ca tadā vavande śirasā hariḥ । hatvā putraṃ mahāvīryaṃ sabalo yadusaṃsadi । papraccha kuśalaṃ kṛṣṇo dīpyamānaḥ svatejasā ।। bāhubhyām eva tarasā sunāmānam apothayat ।। bāhunā vasunāmānaṃ baladevo vyapothayat ।
svapitur bhavanaṃ vīrau jagmatur hṛṣṭamānasau ।। te ca devāḥ samunayo hate kaṃse durātmani । namaskṛtya jagannāthaṃ svaṃ svaṃ jagmur yathālayam । tuṣṭuvuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vijayinaṃ vibhum ।। hatvā pūtānikāṃ vibhajya śakaṭaṃ bhaṅktvārjunau dānavān ।saptāhatya vināśya kāliyaviṣaṃ niṣpīḍya riṣṭetaram ।hatvā keśinam unmadaṃ viṣataruṃ coddhṛtya govardhanaṃ ।yaḥ kaṃsaṃ sagajendramallam avadhīt tasmai namo viṣṇave ।।pralambadhenukaprāṇa hāriṇe muṣṭikadviṣe । sunāmonmāthine nityaṃ dhīmate haline namaḥ ।। iti stutvā bahuvidhaṃ te devā hṛṣṭamānasāḥ । kaṃsapatnyo hataṃ kaṃsaṃ samantāt paryavārayan ।। bhāryāḥ sma dṛṣṭvā śocanti mṛgyo mṛgavadhe yathā ।।
vīraptnyo hate vīre tvayi vīravratapriye ।। kṛpaṇaṃ rājaśārdūla vilapāmaḥ sabāndhavāḥ ।। tvayi pañcatvam āpanne nāthe asmākaṃ mahābale ।। latā iva viceṣṭantyaḥ śayanīyāni neṣyati ।।
dahaty arko mukhaṃ kāntaṃ nistoyam iva paṅkajam ।। śirodharāyāṃ saṃlīnau satataṃ kuṇḍalapriya ।। atyantaṃ śiraso lakṣmīṃ yo dadhāty arkasaprabhaḥ ।। kathaṃ dīnena kartavyaṃ tvayi lokāntaraṃ gate ।।
patīnām aparityajyās tvaṃ tu nas tyajya gacchasi ।। asmāsu prekṣamāṇāsu tvam ākṣipyāśu nīyase । kālatulyaḥ sapatnānāṃ tvaṃ kṣipram apanīyase ।। kathaṃ vatsyāma vidhavā nātha kārpaṇyam āśritāḥ ।।
tvaṃ hi naḥ sā gatiś chinnā kṛtāntena balīyasā ।। aho kṛtāntasya vaśaṃ gantavyaṃ sarvajantubhiḥ । roditavye dhruve magnāḥ kva gacchāmas tvayā vinā ।। kṣaṇena ca vihīnāḥ sma anityā hi nṛṇāṃ gatiḥ ।।
ekaduṣkṛtakāriṇyaḥ sarvāḥ vaidhavyalakṣaṇāḥ ।। tvayi kāmavaśāḥ sarvāḥ sa nas tyajya kva gacchasi ।। asmākaṃ tvam anāthānāṃ nātho hy asi suropama । prativākyaṃ jagannātha dātum arhasi mānada ।।
gamanaṃ te mahārāja dāruṇaṃ pratibhāti naḥ ।। tatas tvaṃ prasthito vīra vihāyemaṃ gṛhe janam ।। ārtanādaṃ rudantīṣu yan nehādyāvabudhyase ।। ye parityajya dārān svān nirapekṣā vrajanti ha ।।
svargastrīṇāṃ priyāḥ śurās teṣām api ca tāḥ priyāḥ ।। prahṛtaṃ naḥ kṛtāntena sarvāsām antarātmasu ।। jarāsaṃdhabalaṃ jitvā hatvā rājñāṃ ca saṃyuge । jitvā devagaṇaṃ yuddhe yakṣān api ca saṃyuge ।
kathaṃ mānuṣamātreṇa hatas tvaṃ jagatīpate ।। amartyair ajito yuddhe martyenāsi kathaṃ hataḥ ।। ratnasarvasvaharaṇaṃ jitvā pāśadharaṃ kṛtam ।। sāyakair jaladān bhittvā balād varṣaṃ pravartitam ।।
preṣayāṇā varārhāṇi ratnāny ācchādanāni ca ।। kathaṃ prāṇāntikaṃ ghoram īdṛśaṃ bhayam āgatam ।। apramattāḥ pramattāḥ sma kṛtāntena nirākṛtāḥ ।। vākyamātreṇa yāsyeti kartavyo naḥ parigrahaḥ ।।
alaṃ dūrapravāsena nivarta mathurādhipa ।। śayānasya hi te bhūmau kasmān nodvijate manaḥ ।। prahṛtaṃ kena sarvāsu nārīsv evaṃ sudāruṇam ।। kiṃ vayaṃ sati gantavye saha bhartrā rudāmahe ।।
kva me vatsaḥ kva me putra iti rorūyate bhṛśam ।। hṛdayena vidīrṇena śrāmyamāṇā punaḥ punaḥ ।। hā hatāsmīti vāśantī papāta bhuvi duḥkhitā । snuṣāṇām ārtanādena vilalāpa ruroda ca ।।
kṛtvā putreti karuṇaṃ vilalāpārtayā girā ।। kim idaṃ tvaritaṃ tāta prasthānaṃ kṛtavān asi ।। tāta naivaṃvidhā bhūmau śerate kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ ।। balajyeṣṭhena lokeṣu rākṣasānāṃ samāgame ।।
bāndhavebhyo bhayaṃ ghoram anivāryaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। jñātibhyo bhayam utpannaṃ śarīrāntakaraṃ mahat ।। vinamrasya hy anaukasya vaktur vigraham ṛcchataḥ । jātivigrahabhūtasya [nūnaṃ] mṛtyur bhaviṣyati । uvāca rudatī vākyaṃ vivatsā saurabhī yathā ।।
śayānaṃ vīraśayane vajrāhatam ivācalam ।। pretatvam upapannasya gatasya yamasādanam ।। gaccha vijñāpyatāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kaṃsasaṃskārakāraṇāt ।। pretakāryāṇi kāryāṇi mṛtaḥ kim aparādhyate ।।
putrasya mukham īkṣantī vilalāpaiva sā bhṛśam ।। tvāṃ patiṃ supatiṃ prāpya yā vipannamanorathāḥ ।। kathaṃ drakṣyāmi śuṣyantaṃ kāsārasalilaṃ yathā ।। prasthito dīrgham adhvānaṃ parityajyya priyaṃ janam ।।
ācchidya mama mandāyā nīyase nayakovida ।। nāmāni ca gṛhītāni samyagvṛttāni tair guṇaiḥ । rudanti tava bhṛtyānāṃ kulāni kulayūthapa ।। trāhi dīnaṃ janaṃ sarvaṃ puram antaḥpuraṃ tathā ।।
jagāmāstaṃ dinakaraḥ saṃdhyārāgeṇa rañjitaḥ ।। putraśokābhisaṃtapto viṣapīta iva skhalan ।। paścānutāpād dhyāyantaṃ kaṃsasya nidhanāvilam ।। vigarhamāṇam ātmānaṃ tasmin yādavasaṃsadi ।।
kṛṣṇaḥ provāca nikhilaṃ sarveṣām upaśṛṇvatām । vaidhavyaṃ strīsahasrāṇāṃ kaṃsasyāsya kṛte kṛtam ।। evam ārtaṃ rudantīṣu mayā bhartari pātite ।। kṛtāntasyānabhijñātaḥ strīṇāṃ kāruṇyasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
sutām udvejanīyasya pāpeṣv abhiratasya ca ।। akliṣṭaṃ maraṇaṃ śreyo na vidviṣṭasya jīvitam ।। dhikśabdapatitaś caiva jīvite cāsya kā dayā ।। ihāpi yaśasā yuktas tatrasthair upadhāryate ।।
narā dharmapravṛttāś ca na nṛpo vikṛto bhavet ।। iṣṭadharmeṣu lokeṣu kartavyaṃ pāralaukikam ।। kartāraḥ sulabhā loke duṣkṛtasyeha karmaṇaḥ ।। mūlacchedaḥ kṛtas tasya viparītasya karmaṇaḥ ।।
na ced dhanyāṃ durācāraṃ vinaṅkṣyati tadā jagat । kaḥ kuryāt khalv idaṃ kāryaṃ badhvā pitaram ojasā । rājyaṃ sakalasāmantaṃ kariṣyati sadā hi saḥ । paurāś ca puryāṃ śreṇyaś ca sāntvyatāṃ sarva eva hi ।। ugraseno mahātejāḥ kṛṣṇam asrāvilekṣaṇam । pralapantaṃ jagāmaivaṃ yādavānāṃ ca saṃsadi ।
ugraseno yadūn gṛhya putrakilbiṣaśaṅkitaḥ ।। vṛṣṇibhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ śiniprabhṛtibhis tadā । bāṣpasaṃdigdhayā vācā dīnayā sajjamānayā ।। svadharmādhigatā kīrtir nāma viśrāvitaṃ bhuvi ।।
sthāpito yādavo vaṃśo garvitāḥ suhṛdaḥ kṛtāḥ ।। mitrāṇi tvāṃ bhajiṣyanti saṃśrayiṣyanti cārthinaḥ ।। saṃdhivigrahamukhyās tvāṃ praṇamiṣyanti mantriṇaḥ ।। pratigṛhāṇa kṛṣṇedaṃ kaṃsasya balam avyayam ।।
pratīcchantu niyuktā vai tvadīyāḥ kṛṣṇa puruṣāḥ । striyo hiraṇyaṃ vāsāṃsi yac cānyad vasu kiṃcana ।। pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ medinyāṃ yadūnāṃ śatrusūdana ।। tvaṃ gatiś cāgatiś caiva yadūnāṃ yadunandana ।
tava prasādād govinde pretakāryaṃ kriyate ha ।। sasnuṣo ahaṃ sabhāryaś ca cariṣyāmi mṛgaiḥ saha ।। ānṛṇyaṃ laukikaṃ kṛṣṇa gataḥ kila bhavāmy aham ।। toyapradānamātreṇa kaṃsasyānṛṇyam āpnuyām ।।
prāpnotu sugatiṃ tatra kṛpaṇaḥ paścimāṃ kriyām ।। pratyuvācograsenaṃ vai sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ ।। kālayuktam idaṃ tāta tvayaitad bhāṣitaṃ vacaḥ । yat tvaṃ evaṃvidhaṃ brūṣe gate arthe duratikrame ।।
kule mahati te janma vedān viditavān asi । kathaṃ na jñāyate tāta niyatir duratikramā ।। sthāvarāṇāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ jaṅgamānāṃ ca pārthiva । pūrvajanmakṛtaṃ karma kālena paripacyate ।।
śrutavanto arthavantaś ca dātāraḥ priyadarśanāḥ । brahmaṇyā nayasaṃpannā dīnānugrahakāriṇaḥ ।। lokapālasamās tāta mahendrasamavikramāḥ । kṣitipālāḥ kṛtāntena nīyante nṛpasattama ।।
dhārmikāḥ sarvabhāvajñāḥ prajāpālanatatparāḥ । kṣatradharmaparā dāntāḥ kālena nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ।। svayam eva kṛtaṃ karma śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham । prāpte kāle tu tat karma dṛśyate sarvadehinām ।।
eṣā hy antarhitā māyā durvijñeyā surair api । yathāyaṃ muhyate loko hy atra karmaiva kāraṇam ।। kālenābhihataḥ kaṃsaḥ pūrvakarmapracoditaḥ । na hy ayaṃ kāraṇaṃ tatra kālaḥ karma ca kāraṇam ।।
sūryasomamayaṃ tāta kṛtsnaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam । kālena nidhanaṃ gatvā kālenaiva ca jāyate । kālas tu sarvabhūtānāṃ nigrahe pragrahe rataḥ । tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni kālasya vaśagāni vai ।।
svadoṣeṇaiva dagdhasya sūnos tava narādhipa । nāhaṃ vai kāraṇaṃ tatra kālas tatra tu kāraṇam ।। atha vāhaṃ bhaviṣyāmi kāraṇaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ । palāyanaparaḥ kālaḥ kiṃ kariṣyaty akāraṇam ।
kālas tu balavān rājan durvijñeyā hi sā gatiḥ ।। parāvaraviśeṣajñā yāṃ yānti samadarśinaḥ । gatiḥ kālasya sā yena sarvaṃ kālasya gocaram । bravīmi yad ahaṃ tāta tad anuṣṭhīyatāṃ vacaḥ ।।
na cāpi rājyalubdhena mayā kaṃso nipātitaḥ ।। vyaṅgabhūtaḥ kulasyāsya sānujo vinipātitaḥ ।। prītimān vicariṣyāmi kāmacārī yathā gajaḥ ।। na me kāryaṃ nṛpatvena vijñāpyaṃ kriyatām idam ।।
vijayāyābhiṣicyasva svarājye rājasattama ।। mayā nisṛṣṭaṃ rājyaṃ svaṃ cirāya pratigṛhyatām ।। etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ nottaraṃ pratyabhāṣata । vrīḍito adhomukhas tasthau kṛṣṇasya purato nṛpaḥ । abhiṣekeṇa govindo yojayām āsa yogavit ।।
cakāra saha kṛṣṇena kaṃsasya nidhanakriyām ।। anujagmuḥ purīmārge devā iva śatakratum ।। paścimaṃ kaṃsasaṃskāraṃ cakrus te yadupuṃgavāḥ ।। naiṣṭhikena vidhānena cakrus te tasya satkriyām ।।
saṃskṛtaś ca yathānyāyaṃ naidhanena citāgninā ।। saṃskāraṃ lambhayām āsuḥ saha kṛṣṇena yādavāḥ ।। akṣayaṃ cāpi pretebhyo bhāṣamāṇāḥ pratasthire ।। akṣayaṃ bhāṣamāṇaś ca pretebhyaś ca pratasthire । hiraṇyasya suvarṇasya daśa koṭīs tathā hariḥ । gāvo ratnāni vāsāṃsi grāmān nagarasaṃmatān ।। dadau kaṃsaṃ samuddiśya brāhmaṇebhyo nṛpottamaḥ ।
puraskṛtyograsenaṃ vai viviṣur mathurāṃ purīm ।। sarvān svajātisaṃbandhān digbhyaḥ kaṃsabhayārditān । yaduvṛṣṇyandhakamadhu dāśārhakukurādikān ।। sabhājitān samāśvāsya videśāvāsakarśitān । nyavāsayat svageheṣu vittaiḥ saṃtarpya viśvakṛt ।। kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇabhujair guptā labdhamanorathāḥ । svagṛhe remire siddhāḥ kṛṣṇarāmagatajvarāḥ ।। vīkṣanto ahar ahaḥ prītā mukundavadanāmbujam । nityapramuditaṃ śrīmān sadayasmitavīkṣaṇam । mathurāṃ yādavādhīnāṃ purīṃ tāṃ sukham āvasat ।। atha nandaṃ samāsādya bhagavān devakīsutaḥ । saṃkarṣaṇaś ca rājendra pariṣvajyedam ūcatuḥ ।। pitur yuvābhyāṃ snigdhābhyāṃ poṣitau lalitau bhṛśam । pitror abhyadhikā prītir ātmajeṣv ātmano api hi ।। sa pitā sā ca jananī yau puṣṇītāṃ svaputravat ।। śiśūn bandhubhir utsṛṣṭān ākalpaiḥ poṣarakṣaṇaiḥ ।। yāta yūyaṃ vrajaṃ tāta vayaṃ ca snehaduḥkhitān । jñātīn vo draṣṭum eṣyāmo vidhāya suhṛdāṃ sukham ।। evaṃ sāntvayya bhagavān sa nandavrajam acyutaḥ । vāsolaṃkārarūpāgryai rañjayām āsa sādaram ।। ity uktas tau pariṣvajya nandaḥ praṇayavihvalaḥ । pūrayann aśrubhir netre saha gopair vrajaṃ yayau ।
cakāra mathurāṃ vīrah sa ratnākarabhūṣaṇām ।। dhanurvedacikīrṣārtham ubhau tāv abhijagmatuḥ ।। cakratuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣau vidyāgrahaṇalālasau । pratijagrāha tāu kāśyo vidyāḥ prādāc ca kevalāḥ ।।
ahorātraiś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sāṅgaṃ vedam adhīyatām ।। sāṅgaṃ vedam adhīyatāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā dinais tathā । lekhyaṃ ca gaṇitaṃ cobhau prāpnutāṃ yadunandanau । gāndhavavedaṃ kṛtsnaṃ ca tathā lekhyāś ca tāv ubhau ।
hastiśikṣāśvaśikṣāś ca dvādaśāhena cāpnutām ।। tāv ubhau jagmatur vīrau guruṃ sāṃdīpaniṃ tataḥ । dhanurvedacikīrṣārthaṃ dharmajñau dharmacāriṇau ।। tāv iṣvāsavarācāryam abhigamya praṇamya ca ।
tena tau satkṛtau rājan vicarantāv avantiṣu ।। pañcāśadbhir ahorātrair daśāṅgaṃ supratiṣṭhitam । sarahasyaṃ dhanurvedaṃ sakalaṃ tāv avāpnutām । acireṇaiva kālena gurus tāv abhyaṣikṣayat ।।
mene tāv āgatau devāv ubhau candradivākarau ।। pūjayantau mahādevaṃ sākṣāt tryakṣam avasthitam ।। gurvarthaṃ kiṃ dadānīti rāmeṇa saha bhārata ।। putram icchāmy ahaṃ dattaṃ yo mṛto lavaṇāmbhasi ।।
prabhāse tīrthayātrāyāṃ taṃ me tvaṃ punar ānaya ।। gatvā samudraṃ tejasvī viveśāntarjalaṃ hariḥ ।। tam āha kṛṣṇaḥ kvāsau bhoḥ putraḥ sāṃdīpaner iti ।। timirūpeṇa taṃ bālaṃ grastavān iti mādhava ।।
unmathya salilād asmād grastavān iti bhārata । na cāsasāda taṃ bālaṃ guruputraṃ tadācyutaḥ ।। yaḥ sa devamanuṣyeṣu pāñcajanya iti śrutaḥ ।। gatvā yamapuraṃ viṣṇuḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ । āsanasthaṃ tato viṣṇuḥ provāca yamam ūrjitam । dīyatāṃ putra ity evaṃ kāśyasāṃdīpaner iti ।। tam uvāca tato viṣṇuṃ mṛtyunā cāhṛto hare । evam uktas tadā kṛṣṇo yamenāmitavikramaḥ । aho dhārṣṭyaṃ tato mṛtyor ity uktvā dhanur ādade ।। ādāya niśitaṃ bāṇaṃ dīyatām iti cābravīt । kruddhaṃ viṣṇuṃ samājñāya dattavān kila bālakam ।
āsasāda ca taṃ bālaṃ guruputraṃ tadācyutaḥ । śaṅkham āpūrya govindas trāsayām āsa vai janam । tato yamo abhyupāgamya vavande taṃ gadādharam । kim āgamanakṛtyaṃ te kiṃ karomīti cābravīt ।।
tam uvācātha vai kṛṣṇo guruputraḥ pradīyatām । tayos tatra tadā yuddham āsīd ghorataraṃ mahat । ānināya guroḥ putraṃ ciranaṣṭaṃ yamakṣayāt ।। dīrghakālagataḥ pretaḥ punar āsīc charīravān ।।
sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ vismayaḥ samajāyata ।। ratnāni ca mahārhāṇi punar āyāj jagatpatiḥ ।। ānāyyāvedayām āsa gurave vāsavānujaḥ ।। acirān mukhyatāṃ prāptau sarvaloke dhanurbhṛtām ।।
prādāt kṛṣṇaḥ pratītāya saha ratnair udāradhīḥ ।। sametya mumude rājan pūjayan rāmakeśavau ।। āyātau mathurāṃ bhūyo vasudevasutāv ubhau ।। sabālā hṛṣṭamanasa ugrasenapurogamāḥ ।।
sabālavṛddhā sā caiva purī samabhivartata ।। rathyāḥ patākāmālinyo bhrājanti sma samantataḥ ।। govindāgamane atyarthaṃ yathaivendramahe tathā ।। stavāśīḥprathamā gāthā yādavānāṃ priyaṃkarāḥ ।।
sve pure nirbhayāḥ sarve krīḍadhvaṃ saha bāndhavaiḥ ।। tebhyo agacchan videśebhyaḥ kaṃsenodvijitāś ca ye । mathurāyāṃ babhau rājan govinde samupasthite ।। naranārīgaṇāḥ sarve bhejire manasaḥ sukham ।।
daivatāni ca sarvāṇi hṛṣṭāny āyataneṣv api ।। tāni sarvāṇy adṛśyanta purīṃ prāpte janārdane ।। hariyuktena govindo viveśa mathurāṃ purīm ।। anujagmur yadugaṇāḥ śakraṃ devagaṇā iva ।।
praviṣṭau hṛṣṭavadanau candrādityāv ivācalam ।। pareṇa tejasopetau surendrāv iva rūpinau । mumudāte yaduvarau vasudevasutāv ubhau ।। udyāneṣu vicitreṣu phalapuṣpāvanāmiṣu । ceratuḥ sumahātmānau yādavaiḥ parivāritau ।। raivatasya samīpeṣu saritsu vimalāsu ca । padmapatrasamṛddhāsu kāraṇḍavayutāsu ca । evaṃ tau bālyam uttīrṇau balabhadrajanārdanau ।
ugrasenānugau bhūtvā kaṃ cit kālaṃ mumodatuḥ ।। uṣitvā caturo māsān nandagopa udāradhīḥ । rāmakṛṣṇau samāliṅgya yadubhiś cānumoditaḥ । vasudevābhyanujñātaḥ svam eva śakaṭaṃ yayau । etad vo bālacaritaṃ sakalaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ । yathāśrutaṃ yathāyogaṃ yathājñānam udāhṛtam । kṛṣṇaṃ keśavam acyutaṃ muraripuṃ śauriṃ hariṃ śārṅgiṇaṃ ।viṣṇuṃ viśvasṛjaṃ caturbhujaṃ śrīvallabhaṃ śrīdharam ।jiṣṇuṃ daityaripuṃ tridhāmanilayaṃ trailokyanāthaṃ paraṃ ।govindaṃ puruṣaṃ namāmi śirasā nārāyaṇaṃ cakriṇam । śuśrāva nihataṃ kaṃsaṃ jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān ।। duhitṛbhyāṃ mahīpatiḥ ।tato nāticirāt kālāj ।astiḥ prāptiś ca kaṃsasya mahiṣyau bharatarṣabha । hate bhartari duḥkhārte īyatuḥ svapitur gṛhān । sa sādhanena mahatā pākaśāsanavikramaḥ ।
kṛṣṇasya vadham anvicchan madhurām anvavartata । jighāṃsur hi yadūn kruddhaḥ kaṃsasyāpacitiṃ caran ।। ayaśo hy ātmano rakṣaṃl lokanirvādaśaṅkayā । duhitṛprītikāmārthaṃ madhurām avarodhakaḥ । akṣauhinyaikaviṃśatyā senayā ca tadā saha । te dve ca kaṃsarājāya dadau hṛṣṭaḥ sa māgadhaḥ ।।
tena te vidhave syātām ubhe kṛṣṇena māgadhe । jīvaty eva tathā rājan vīre rājñāṃ purogame । ubhe kaṃsasya te bhārye prādād bārhadratho nṛpaḥ ।। śūraseneśvaro rājā yathā te bahuśo śrutaḥ ।।
vasudevo abhavan nityaṃ kaṃso na mamṛṣe ca tam ।। ugraseno abhavad rājā bhojavṛṣṇyandhakair vṛtaḥ ।। madhurāṃ pālayām āsa keśavānumate sthitaḥ । sa tad apriyam ākarṇya śokāmarṣayuto nṛpaḥ ।
ayādavīṃ mahīṃ kartuṃ cakre paramam udyamam ।। akṣauhiṇībhir viṃśatyā tisṛbhiś cāpi saṃyutaḥ । yadurājadhānīṃ mathurāṃ roddhum abhyāgato nṛpaḥ । kṛtvā sarvasamudyogaṃ krodhād abhiyayau yadūn ।।
mitrāṇi jñātayaś caiva saṃyuktāḥ suhṛdas tathā ।। ye nṛpāḥ parvatāt tasmād gomantād vrīḷitā gatāḥ । te ca sarve yadūn hantuṃ jarāsaṃdhaṃ samanvayuḥ । maheṣvāsā mahāvīryā jarāsaṃdhapriyaiṣiṇaḥ ।।
āhvṛtiḥ kauśikaś caiva bhīṣmakaś ca narādhipaḥ ।। vāsudevārjunābhyāṃ yaḥ spardhate sma sadā bale ।। aṅgarājaś ca balavān vaṅgānām adhipas tathā ।। suhmeśvaraś ca vikrānto videhādhipatis tathā ।।
sālvarājaś ca vikrānto daradaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। gāndhārarājaḥ subalo nagnajic ca mahābalaḥ ।। kāśmīrarājo gonardo daradādhipatir nṛpaḥ । duryodhanādayaś caiva dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābalāḥ । tam anvayur jarāsaṃdhaṃ vidviṣanto janārdanam ।।
ūṣuḥ saṃrudhya mathurāṃ parikṣipya balais tadā ।। apaśyan vṛṣṇayaḥ sarve puraskṛtya janārdanam ।। tān āgatān nṛpān rājan māgadhān rājasattamān । tvarate khalu kāryārtho devatānāṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
lakṣyante hi dhvajāgrāṇi rathānāṃ vātaraṃhasām ।। chatrāṇy ārya virājante procchritāni sitāni ca ।। abhivartanti naḥ śubhrā yathā khe haṃsapaṅktayaḥ ।। āvayor yuddhanikaṣaḥ prathamaḥ samarātithiḥ ।।
yuddhārambhaḥ prayoktavyo balaṃ tāvad vimṛśyatām ।। jarāsaṃdham abhiprepsuś cakāra baladarśanam ।। ātmānam ātmanā vākyam uvāca hṛdi mantravit ।। ye vināśam iheṣyanti śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।।
svargagāni tathā hy eṣāṃ vapūṃṣi pracakāśire ।। bhūmir nirantarā ceyaṃ balarāṣṭrābhisaṃvṛtā ।। bhaviṣyati narendraughaiḥ śataśo vinipātitaiḥ ।। evaṃ cintayatas tasya kṛṣṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ । evaṃ saṃcintya bhagavān yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ । saṃkarṣaṇena sahitas tasthau girir ivācalaḥ ।
narādhipasahasraughair anuyāto mahādyutiḥ ।। rathaiḥ sāṃgrāmikair yuktair asaṅgagatibhiḥ kva cit ।। mahāmātrottamārūḍhaiḥ kalpitai raṇakovidaiḥ ।। vājibhir meghasaṃkāśaiḥ plavadbhir iva pattibhiḥ ।।
sahasrasaṃkhyāsaṃyuktair utpatadbhir ivoragaiḥ ।। nṛpo abhiyāto balavāñ jarāsaṃdho dhṛtavrataḥ ।। heṣamāṇaiś ca turagaiḥ kṣveḍamāṇaiś ca pattibhiḥ ।। akṣauhiṇyā ca viṃśatyā anuyāto narādhipaḥ ।
sa rājā sāgarākāraḥ sasainyaḥ pratyadṛśyata ।। kṣveḍitāsphoṭitaravaṃ meghasainyam ivābabhau ।। turagaiś ca javopetaiḥ pattibhiḥ khagamair iva ।। gharmānte sāgaragataṃ yathaivābhrabalaṃ tathā ।।
parivārya purīṃ sarve niveśāyopacakrire ।। śuklaparyantapūrṇasya yathā rūpaṃ mahodadheḥ ।। ārohaṇārthaṃ puryās te samīyur yuddhalālasāḥ ।। niviṣṭā mantrayāmāsur yuddhakālakutūhalāḥ ।।
yugānte bhidyamānānāṃ sāgarāṇāṃ yathā svanaḥ ।। cerur mā śabda ity evaṃ bruvanto rājaśasanāt ।। līnamīnagrahasyeva niḥśabdasya mahodadheḥ ।। jarāsaṃdho bṛhad vākyaṃ bṛhaspatir ivādade ।।
sarvato nagarī ceyaṃ janaughaiḥ parivāryatām ।। kāryā bhūmiḥ samā sarvā jalaughaiś ca pariplutā । ūrdhvaṃ cāpāni vāhyantāṃ prāsā vai tomarās tathā ।। nṛpaś ca yuddhamārgajñā vinyasyantām adūrataḥ ।।
yāvad etau raṇe gopau vasudevasutāv ubhau । saṃkarṣaṇaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca ghātayāmi śitaiḥ śaraiḥ । ākāśam api bāṇaughair niḥsaṃpātaṃ yathā bhavet ।। teṣu teṣv avakāśeṣu śīghram āruhyatāṃ purī ।।
kaśmīrarājo gonardaḥ karūṣādhipatis tathā ।। nagaryāḥ paścimaṃ dvāraṃ kṣipram ārohayantv iti ।। rukmī ca bhojādhipatiḥ sūryākṣaś caiva mālavaḥ ।। pāñcālānām adhipatir drupadānāṃ mahābalaḥ ।
dakṣiṇaṃ nagaradvāraṃ śīghram ārodhayantv iti । chāgaliḥ purumitraś ca virāṭaś ca mahīpatiḥ ।। bhūriśravās trigartaś ca bāṇaḥ pañcanadas tathā ।। ārohantāṃ vimardantāṃ vajrapratimagauravāḥ ।।
ekalavyo bṛhatkṣatraḥ kṣatradharmā jayadrathaḥ ।। vaidiśo vāmadevaś ca sāketaś ca sinīpatiḥ ।। tvarayanto abhidhāvantu vātā iva balāhakān ।। dakṣiṇaṃ nagaradvāraṃ pālayiṣyāma daṃśitāḥ ।।
vajrāvapātapratimaṃ prāpnotu tumulaṃ bhayam ।। apare vividhaiḥ śastrair dārayantu purīm imām ।। kāryā bhūmisamā sarvā bhavadbhir vasudhādhipaiḥ ।। evam uktvā jarāsaṃdhaḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ ।
pratijagmur daśārhās taṃ vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ ।। tāv āgatau tadā dṛṣṭvā yādavau sainyam agragau । ruṣāha māgadho vīkṣya he kṛṣṇa puruṣādhama । na tvayā yoddhum icchāmi bālakeneti lajjayā ।। tava rāma yada śraddhā yuddhe sthairyaṃ samudvaha । hato vā maccharaiś channa dehaḥ svar yāhi māṃ jahi ।। na vai śūrā vikatthante darśayanty eva pauruṣam । na gṛhṇīmo vaco rājan nāturasya mumūrṣataḥ । alpānāṃ bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ vyatiṣaktarathadvipam ।। ugrasenaṃ puraskṛtya vāsudevahalāyudhau । rathasthāv abhivartetāṃ yuddhāya raṇakovidau ।
kṣubdhaṃ naravarānīkaṃ trastasaṃmūḍhavāhanam ।। makarāv iva saṃrabdhau samudrakṣobhaṇāv ubhau ।। tayoḥ prayudhyatoḥ saṃkhye matir āsīd dhṛtātmanoḥ । āyudhānāṃ purāṇānām ādāne kṛtalakṣaṇā ।।
lelihānāni divyāni mahānti sudṛḍhāni ca ।। tṛṣitāny āhave bhoktuṃ nṛpamāṃsāni vai bhṛśam ।। prabhayā bhāsamānāni daṃśitāni diśo daśa ।। dhanuṣāṃ pravaraṃ śārṅgaṃ gadā kaumodakī ca ha ।।
tābhyāṃ samavatīrṇāni yādavābhyāṃ mahāraṇe ।। taṃ sarpam iva sarpantaṃ divyamālākulaṃ mṛdhe ।। savyena sātvatāṃ śreṣṭho jagrāha musalottamam ।। nāmnā śārṅgam iti khyātaṃ viṣṇur jagrāha vīryavān ।।
viṣaktā kumudākṣasya nāmnā kaumodakīti sā ।। samare rāmagovindau ripūṃs tān pratyayudhyatām ।। dviṣatsu pratikurvāṇau parākrāntau yatheśvarau ।। viceratur yathā devau vasudevasutāv ubhau ।
cacāra samare vīro dviṣatām antako yathā ।। cakāra roṣaṃ saphalaṃ nāgeṣu ca hayeṣu ca ।। rāmo virājan samare nirmamantha yathācalān ।। jarāsaṃdhāntikaṃ vīrāḥ samarārtāḥ prajagmire ।।
dhig etāṃ kṣatravṛttiṃ vaḥ samare kātarātmanām ।। bhrūṇahatyām ivāsahyāṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। atha vā tiṣṭhata rathaiḥ prekṣakāḥ samavasthitāḥ । yāvad etau raṇe gopau preṣayāmi yamakṣayam ।।
sthito asmi yuddhe saṃrabdhaḥ kṣatriyā vijayāya hi । sṛjantaḥ śarajālāni hṛṣṭā yoddhuṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।। nāgaiś cāmbhodasaṃkāśair mahāmātrapracoditaiḥ ।। svāropitadhanuṣmantaḥ sutūṇīrāḥ satomarāḥ ।।
raṇe te abhigatā rejuḥ syandanasthā mahīkṣitaḥ ।। gadābhiś caiva gurvībhiḥ kṣepaṇīyaiś ca mudgaraiḥ ।। etasminn antare tatra devānāṃ nandivardhanaḥ । etasminn antare rājā jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān । dadhmau śaṅkhaṃ mahānādaṃ diśaḥ sarvā vinādayan ।। tac chrutvā devadevo api pāñcajanyam anuttamam । yasya nādena vitrastā divisthāḥ sarvadevatāḥ । kim u sainyāni sarvāṇi vitrastānīti kā kathā । tadābhyayāj jarāsaṃdhaṃ śarair vivyādha cāṣṭabhiḥ ।।
so api vidhvāṣṭabhir viṣṇum ugrasenaṃ dadarśa ha । pārśvasthaṃ ca harer āha śṛṇu rājan vaco mama ।। tvaṃ kim āsīn nṛpo rānan vṛṣṇīnāṃ sāṃprataṃ vada । ajñānām agraṇīḥ sa tvaṃ ko anyas tvatsadṛśo bhuvi ।। yat tu dattaṃ kilānena piṇḍam ātmajaghātinā । tad bhuṅkte tad bhavān nityaṃ vadāndha kim ataḥ param ।। hatvā cāyaṃ sutaṃ śauris tava rājaka nirdayaḥ । tvām eva rājye saṃsthāpya sāṃprataṃ yuddhalālasaḥ ।। tasya bhṛtyatvam āyāsi rājaśabdaṃ samudvahan । kevalaṃ vayasā vṛddho na tu jñānena rājaka ।। nirlajja bhogasaṃsakta kṣudrajanto nṛpādhama । ito yāhi vṛthāvṛddha tvāṃ draṣṭuṃ nāham utsahe ।। atha yuddhaṃ samālipsuḥ kṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭha mamāgrataḥ । haniṣye tvāṃ hi sabalaṃ sahariṃ sabalaṃ tathā ।। ity uktvā dhanur ādāya tasthau tatpuratas tadā ।। tac chrutva roṣatāmrākṣo babhāṣe māgadhaṃ hariḥ । antardhānaṃ gatas tasmād gomantāt parvatottamāt ।। tvam idānīṃ samāyāsi balaiḥ sarvaiḥ samanvitaḥ । sthito asmi yuddhasaṃrabdhaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ kṣayāvahaḥ ।। sa evāsmi śiśū rājan bhavān api sa eva hi । naitad yuktaṃ vṛthā rājann ugrasenaṃ prabhāṣitum । mām eva vada rājendra śatrur asmi tava prabho । drakṣyase yat kṛtaṃ rājan mayā sāṃpratam īdṛśam ।। atha kiṃ bahunoktena śiraś chetsyāmi te nṛpa । na karoṣi yadi tvaṃ hi rājendrādya palāyanam ।। ity uktvā pañcaviṃśatyā nṛpaṃ vivyādha keśavaḥ । jaghāna turagāṃś cājau yatamānasya vīryavān ।। dhanuś ciccheda rājendra jarāsaṃdhasya keśavaḥ । dhvajaṃ cāsya praciccheda sārathiṃ ca jaghāna ha ।। rathaṃ cāsya praciccheda sarvakṣatrasya paśyataḥ । viratho vidhanuṣkaś ca tasthau bhūtalam āsthitaḥ । senānīḥ kauśikaś caiva kṛṣṇaṃ vivyādhatuḥ śaraiḥ ।।
javenābhyardayac cāpi tān arīñ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ ।। bahubhir bahudhā vīraḥ samantāt svarṇabhūṣaṇaiḥ । kauśikaḥ pañcabhiś cāpi jarāsaṃdhaś ca saptabhiḥ ।। dhanur anyat samādāya magadhendro mahīpatiḥ ।
ugrasenaṃ samājaghne śareṇa niśitena ha ।। sa śaro atha mahārāja rājānaṃ sa vyacūcudat । pitā kaṃsasya rājendra śarair vivyādha saptabhiḥ ।। saptatyā ca jarāsaṃdhaṃ punaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ ।
jarāsaṃdhaḥ samājaghne rājānaṃ yadunandanam । śarair daśasahasraiś ca mādhavasya hi paśyataḥ ।। ugraseno dhanuṣpāṇir dhanuś cāsya dvidhākarot ।। punar ādāya cāpaṃ tu jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān ।
ugrasenaṃ viṃśatibhiḥ śaraiḥ suniśitair api ।। vivyādha rājarājānaṃ baladevasya paśyataḥ । dhanuś cāsya dvidhā rājan muṣṭideśe tathākarot ।। ādāya niśitaṃ bāṇaṃ jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān ।
vivyādha rājan rājendro rājānaṃ hṛdaye prabhuḥ ।। aśvāṃś caiva praciccheda śareṇa nataparvaṇā । rathaṃ cāsya dvidhā cakre dhvajaṃ ca prādunon nṛpaḥ ।। rathāc caiva pradudrāva vṛṣṇīnāṃ nṛpasattamaḥ ।।
kauśikaś citrasenaś ca jarāsaṃdho mahīpatiḥ । janārdanaṃ mahārāja samājaghnus tribhis tribhiḥ । jarāsaṃdhaḥ śarair bhagno vasudevasya paśyataḥ । pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiś caiva baladevaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ ।।
baladevo dhanuś cājau bhallenāsya dvidhākarot ।। abhyadravat susaṃkruddho jighāṃsur musalāyudham ।। gadayā ca jaghānāśvān kopāt sa magadheśvaraḥ ।। rāmaṃ cābhyadravad vīro jarāsaṃdho mahābalaḥ ।
tayos tu yuddham abhavat parasparavadhaiṣiṇoḥ ।। citrasenas tu saṃsaktaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmeṇa māgadham । ratham anyaṃ samāruhya jarāsaṃdham avārayat ।। tato balena mahatā gajānīkena cāpy atha । ubhayor antare tābhyāṃ saṃkulaṃ samapadyata । rāmakṛṣṇāgragān bhojān āsasāda mahābalaḥ ।। prādur babhūva tumulaḥ senayor ubhayos tayoḥ ।।
ubhayoḥ senayo rājan prādur āsīn mahāsvanaḥ ।। utpapāta rajaś cāpi khuranemisamuddhatam ।। anyonyam abhigarjantaḥ śūrās tatrāvatasthire ।। gajāś cātibalās tatra saṃnipetur abhītavat ।।
tatas teṣāṃ mahārāja nṛpāṇāṃ jayakāṅkṣiṇām । vṛṣṇībhiḥ saha yodhānāṃ jarāsaṃdhasya dāruṇaḥ ।। baladevaṃ puraskṛtya sainyasyārdhena daṃśitāḥ ।। pālitaṃ cedirājena jarāsaṃdhena cābhibho ।।
sṛjantaḥ śaravarṣāṇi samabhityaktajīvitāḥ ।। hṛṣīkeśaṃ puraskṛtya sainyasyārdhena daṃśitāḥ ।। devakenāpi rājendra tathā madreśvareṇa ca । prācyaiś ca dākṣiṇātyaiś ca guptavīryabalānvitaiḥ ।।
śaktyṛṣṭiprāsabāṇaughān sṛjatāṃ tumulaṃ mahat ।। rājādhidevo mṛduraḥ śvaphalkaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। vyūhasya pakṣaṃ te savyaṃ pratīyur dviṣatāṃ mṛdhe ।। tatra yuddhaṃ samabhavan mahad devāsuropamam ।
alpānāṃ bahubhiḥ sardhaṃ vāsudevavyapāśrayāt ।। evaṃ yuddham abhūt teṣāṃ śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhanam । bhīrūṇāṃ trāsajananaṃ yamarāṣṭravivardhanam । rājabhiś cāpi bahubhir veṇudārimukhaiḥ saha ।।
pratīcyaiś ca balodagrair dhārtarāṣṭraiś ca pālitam । māgadhasya mahāmātyair nṛpaiś caivānuyāyibhiḥ ।। dvaṃdvayuddhaṃ samabhavat senayor ubhayos tadā । gadena cedirājasya dantavaktrasya śaṃbhunā ।।
vindānuvindāv āvantyau yuyudhānena saṃgatau । ekalavyo mahārāja pradyumnenātha saṃgataḥ । yuddham āsīd dhi sainyānāṃ sainikair bharatarṣabha ।। ahāni pañca caikaṃ ca ṣaṭ saptāṣṭau ca dāruṇam । rathā rathair vimiśraiś ca yodhā yuyudhire nṛpa ।।
mahendrasyeva vṛtreṇa dāruṇo lomaharṣaṇaḥ ।। avekṣya rukmiṇīṃ kṛṣṇo rukmiṇaṃ na vyapothayat ।। jvalanārkāṃśusaṃkāśān āśīviṣaviṣopamān । vārayām āsa kṛṣṇo vai śarāṃs tasya tu śikṣayā । ubhayoḥ senayo rājan māṃsaśoṇitakardamaḥ ।। piśācā rākṣasāś caiva māṃsaśoṇitalālasāḥ ।
tasmin vimarde yodhānāṃ saṃkhyāvyaktir na vidyate ।। āvṛnvann abhyayād vīras taṃ ca rājā sa māgadhaḥ ।। abhyavartata vegena syandanenāśugāminā । anyonyaṃ vividhair astrair vidhvā vidhvā vinedatuḥ । gade gṛhītvā vikrāntāv anyonyam abhidhāvatām ।।
dadṛśāte mahātmānau girī saśikharāv ubhau ।। saṃrabdhāv abhidhāvantau gadāyuddheṣu viśrutau ।। mattāv iva gajau yuddhe anyonyam abhidhāvatām ।। samantataś cāpsarasaḥ samājagmuḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।
pitāmahaś ca bhagavān yuddhaṃ draṣṭuṃ samāgataḥ । śuśubhe abhyadhikaṃ rājan divaṃ jyotir gaṇair iva ।। savyaṃ maṇḍalam āvṛtya baladevas tu dakṣiṇam ।। dantābhyām iva mātaṅgau nādayantau diśo daśa ।।
