jarāsaṃdhasya caraṇe parvatasyeva dīryataḥ ।। gadā gadābhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vindhyaṃ girim ivācalam ।। sehe dhairyeṇa mahatā śikṣayā ca vyapohayat ।। evaṃ tau tatra saṃgrāme vicarantau mahābalau । maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi viceratur ariṃdamau ।। vyāyacchantau ciraṃ kālaṃ pariśrāntau ca tasthatuḥ । samāśvāsya muhūrtaṃ tu punar anyonyam āhatām ।। evaṃ tau yodhamukhyau tu samaṃ yuyudhatuś ciram । na ca tau yuddhavaimukhyam ubhāv eva prajagmatuḥ ।। athāpaśyad gadāyuddhe viśeṣaṃ tasya vīryavān । rāmaḥ kruddho gadāṃ tyaktvā jagrāha musalottamam ।। tam udyataṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā musalaṃ ghoradarśanam । amoghaṃ baladevena kruddhena tu mahāraṇe । kruddho atha rāmabhadras tu gadayā taṃ jagāma ha । jarāsaṃdho atha gadayā balabhadraṃ samāhanat ।। prathamas tv atha rāmeṇa gadāpādaḥ samādade । dvitīyo magadhendreṇa tṛtīyaṃ tu halāyudhaḥ । caturthaṃ tu jarāsaṃdhaḥ pañcamaṃ tu yadūdvahaḥ ।। tayoḥ pādaprahāraś ca cālayām āsa medinīm ।। tato devāḥ sagandharvā yakṣāś ca paramarṣayaḥ । bhītāḥ svastīti caivāhur lokānāṃ brahmaṇaś ca ha ।। tataḥ kruddho jarāputras tāḍayām āsa vakṣasi । śoṇitaṃ codvaman rāmaḥ śramaṃ ca samavāpa ha ।। viśramya bhūmau kiṃcit tu punar utthāya yādavaḥ । āhatya gadayā mūrdhni siṃhanādaṃ samānadat ।। papāta ca mahīṃ vīro gatāsur iva niḥśvasan । hato hato jarāsaṃdha ity ūcur yādaveśvarāḥ ।। saṃjñāṃ ca pratilabhyāśu jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān । gadayā ca samājaghne vakṣasy eva halāyudham ।। mūrcchāṃ caiva samāpede saṃjñāṃ ca pratilabdhavān । tato rudhirarāśis tu babhau jalam ivodgataḥ ।। gadājarjarasarvāṅgau rejatuḥ kiṃśukāv iva । samādīptau tu rājendra virathau vidhanurdharau ।। gadāhatau mahāvīrau kevalau yuddharaṅginau । śuśubhāte gadāhastau parasparavadhaiṣiṇau ।। dvāv eva mṛtyū rājendra saṃgatāv iva śobhitau ।। tataḥ kruddho haladharaś chettum aicchaj jarāsutam । ūrū ca pothayām āsa gadayā rājasaṃsadi ।। ūrvo raktaṃ samāpede majjā samabhavat tataḥ । tato halī jarāsaṃdhaṃ śiraś chettum udaikṣata ।
uvāca baladevaṃ taṃ samudyatahalāyudham । na tvayā rāma vadhyo ayam alaṃ khedena mādhava ।। acireṇaiva kālena prāṇāṃs tyakṣyati māgadhaḥ ।। tau vyupāramatāṃ caiva vṛṣṇayas te ca pārthivāḥ ।।
dīrghakālaṃ mahārāja nighnatām itaretarām ।। te sarve nirjitā rājan kṛṣṇena ripughātinā । jarāsaṃdhena sahitā viprajagmur yathāgatam । astaṃ yāte dinakare nānusasrus tadā niśi ।। vṛṣṇayaś ca mahābhāgāḥ kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇāśrayāḥ ।
purīṃ praviviśur hṛṣṭāḥ keśavenābhipūjitāḥ ।। khāc cyutāny āyudhāny eva tāny evāntardadhus tadā ।। jarāsaṃdho api nṛpatir vimanāḥ svapuraṃ yayau । rājānaś cānugā ye asya svarāṣṭrāṇy eva te yayuḥ । vṛṣṇayaḥ kuruśārdūla rājā hy atibalaḥ sa vai ।। ko nāma hi jarāsaṃdhaṃ raṇe jetuṃ mahīpatiḥ । śaknuyāl lokavikhyātaḥ sākṣād api śatakratuḥ ।
dadur na cainaṃ samare hantuṃ śekur mahārathāḥ ।। kṛṣṇas tu samare rājañ śaktimān api māgadham । anyo mṛtyur iti jñātvā na ca hiṃsitavān prabhuḥ । jarāsaṃdhasya nṛpates tadarthaṃ yāḥ samāgatāḥ ।। bārhadrathena rājendra rājabhiḥ sahitena vai ।।
bhūyaḥ kṛtvodyamaṃ prāyād yādavān kṛṣṇapālitān । viharanti sma sukhino vṛṣṇisiṃhā mahārathāḥ ।। ojas tejo balaṃ dhīr dhṛtir iti mahimā śrīr yaśo rūpam ājñā ।vīryaṃ cetyevamādīn paramaguṇagaṇān ye smaranto labhante ।yad bhaktānāṃ yam ājñāpy akhilajanamanaḥkṣobhaṇī naiti pārśvaṃ ।cetas tvaṃ tasya śaśvac caraṇakamalayor bhṛṅgatāṃ yāhi viṣṇoḥ । jagāmaiko vrajaṃ rāmaḥ kṛṣṇasyānumate svayam ।।
bhuktapūrvāṇy araṇyāni sarāṃsi surabhīṇi ca ।। vanyena ramaṇīyena veṣeṇālaṃkṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ।। gopaṃs tenaiva vidhinā yathānyāyaṃ yathāvayaḥ ।। tathaiva saha gopībhī rocayan madhurāḥ kathāḥ ।।
rāmaṃ ramayatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pravāsāt punarāgatam ।। jīvitasya phalaṃ prāptam adya te darśanena ca । adya smo nirvṛtās tāta yat tvāṃ paśyāma nirvṛtam ।। vikhyātas triṣu lokeṣu rāmaḥ śatrubhayaṃkaraḥ ।।
yādavāś ca balodagrāḥ sarve saṃgrāmalālasāḥ । tiṣṭhanti nṛpaśārdūlā hy apramattā mahābalāḥ । atha vā prāṇinas tāta ramante janmabhūmiṣu ।। ye sma dṛṣṭās tvayā tāta kāṅkṣamāṇās tavāgamam ।। ugraseno abhiṣiktaś ca māhātmyenānujena vai ।।
vadhaḥ pañcajanasyaiva jarāsaṃdhena vigrahaḥ । gomante ca śruto asmābhiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ saha vigrahaḥ । daradasya vadhaś caiva jarāsaṃdhe ca yā matiḥ । tac cāyudhāvataraṇaṃ śrutaṃ naḥ paramāhave ।।
vadhaś caiva śṛgālasya karavīrapurottame । tatsutasyābhiṣekaś ca nāgarāṇāṃ ca sāntvanam । tatpatnīnāṃ pralāpaś ca śakradevābhiṣecanam । mathurāyāvarodhaś ca jarāsaṃdhena dhīmatā । yuddhaṃ sarvair narendraiś ca yādavānāṃ mahātmanām । pratiṣṭhitā ca vasudhā śaṅkitāḥ sarvapārthivāḥ ।। tena sma parituṣṭāś ca hṛṣitāś ca sabāndhavāḥ ।। yādaveṣv api sarveṣu bhavanto mama bāndhavāḥ ।।
bhavadbhir vardhitāś caiva kathaṃ yāsyāma vikriyām ।। asmākaṃ bāndhavāḥ sarve bhavanto baddhasauhṛdāḥ ।। evaṃ bahuvidhālāpaṃ kṛtvā gopais tu lāṅgalī । jagāma yamunātīraṃ paśyan vṛndāvanaṃ mudā ।
tato vanāntaragato reme rāmo mahābalaḥ ।। gopālair deśakālajñair upānīyata vāruṇī ।। vanāntaragato rāmaḥ pānaṃ madasamīraṇam ।। pratyagraramaṇīyāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca ।।
sadyoddhṛtāvamuktaṃ ca prabhūtaṃ kamalotpalam ।। śravaṇaikāvalambena kuṇḍalena virājatā ।। vibabhāv urasā rāmaḥ kailāseneva mandaraḥ ।। rarāja vapuṣā śubhraḥ śaśīva ghanamālayā ।।
tathā bhujāgraśliṣṭena musalena ca bhāsvatā ।। śaiśirīṣv iva rātrīṣu yathā khedālasaḥ śaśī ।। ihaiva mābhigacchasva rūpiṇī sāgaraṃgame ।। nābhyavartata taṃ deśaṃ strīsvabhāvena mohitā ।।
cakāra ca halaṃ haste karṣaṇādhomukhaṃ balī ।। mumucuḥ puṣpakośaiś ca svaṃ rajorañjitaṃ jalam ।। cakarṣa yamunāṃ rāmo vyutthitāṃ vanitām iva ।। vyāvartata nadī bhītā halamārgānusāriṇī ।।
saṃkarṣaṇabhayatrastā yoṣevākulatāṃ gatā ।। phenamekhalasūtraiś ca cihnais tīrānuhāsibhiḥ ।। vegagambhīravakrāṅgī trastamīnavahaṃgamā ।। tīrajoddhūtakeśāntā jalaskhalitagāminī ।।
śaivālamaladigdhāṅgī ghanabudbudaviklavā । matteva kuṭilā nārī rājamārgeṇa gacchatī ।। unmārgānītamārgā sā yena vṛndāvanaṃ vanam ।। rorūyamāṇaiḥ khagamair anvitā tīravāsibhiḥ ।।
tataḥ strīvigrahā bhūtvā yamunā rāmam abravīt ।। viparītam idaṃ rūpaṃ toyaṃ ca mama jāyate ।। rauhiṇeya hasiṣyati māṃ nandaḥ saṃgatā tvayā । karṣaṇena mahābāho svamārgavyabhicāriṇī ।।
phenahāsair hasiṣyanti toyavyāvṛttagāminīm ।। suprasannamanā nityaṃ bhavasva tvaṃ surottama । karṣaṇāyudhakṛṣṭāsmi roṣo ayaṃ vinivartyatām ।। mārgam ādiṣṭam icchāmi kva gacchāmi mahābhuja ।।
pratyuvācārṇavavadhūṃ madākrāntālaso balaḥ ।। deśam ambupradānena nikhilaṃ bhāvayasva naḥ ।। lokā hi yāvat sthāsyanti tāvat sthāsyati me yaśaḥ ।। ity uktā sā tathā cakre yamunā rāmaśāsanam । anujñātā tu rāmeṇa yathāmārgaṃ jagāma sā ।
sādhu sādhv iti rāmāya praṇāmaṃ cakrire tadā ।। namo astu te jagannātha balabhadra halāyudha । prasīda devadeveśa rāma rāmeti gopakāḥ । punaḥ pratijagāmāśu mathurāṃ rohiṇīsutaḥ ।। parivartamānaṃ dadṛśe pṛthivyāḥ sāram avyayam ।।
pratyagravanamālena vakṣasābhivirājatā ।। sahasotthāya govindo dadāv āsanam uttamam ।। abhivādya mahātmānaṃ balabhadraṃ janārdanaḥ । punaḥ praṇāmam akarot svāgataṃ te halāyudha । bāndhaveṣu ca sarveṣu goṣu caiva janārdanaḥ ।।
sarvatra kuśalaṃ kṛṣṇa yeṣāṃ kuśalam icchasi ।। vasudevāgrataḥ puṇyā rāmakeśavayos tadā ।। babhāṣe puṇḍarīkākṣo hetumad vākyam uttamam ।। śrūyatāṃ yādavā vākyaṃ sarve cāvahitā mama ।
vayaṃ caiveha saṃbhūtā vraje ca parivardhitāḥ ।। nṛpeṣu janitaṃ vairaṃ jarāsaṃdhe ca vigrahaḥ ।। ratnāni ca vicitrāṇi mitrāṇi bahulāni ca ।। vṛddhiś cāpi parāsmākaṃ balato mitratas tathā ।।
eṣām apīha vasatāṃ saṃmardam upalakṣaye ।। purīṃ niveśayiṣyāmi mama tat kṣantum arhatha ।। bhavāya bhavatāṃ kāle rocatāṃ yadusaṃsadi ।। sādhyatāṃ yad abhipretaṃ janasyāsya bhavāya ca ।।
avadhyo asaukṛto asmākaṃ sumahacca ripor balam ।। na śakṣyāmo hy atas teṣām apayāne abhavan matiḥ ।। sainyena tadvidhenaiva mathurām abhyupāgamat ।। te kālayavanaṃ caiva śrutvaivaṃ pratipedire ।।
etasminn antare caiva yadūnāṃ nandivardhanaḥ । adyaiva divasaḥ puṇyo niryāma sapadānugāḥ ।। oghā iva samudrasya balaughaprativāraṇāḥ ।। susaṃnaddhair gajair mattai rathair aśvaiś ca daṃśitaiḥ ।।
niryayur yādavāḥ sarve mathurām apahāya vai ।। sṛtaplutaiś ca turagaiḥ kaśāpārṣṇipracoditaiḥ ।। pratyaṅmukhā yayur hṛṣṭā vṛṣṇayo bharatarṣabha ।। anīkāgrāṇi karṣanto vāsudevapurogamāḥ ।।
kīrṇaṃ nāgavanaiḥ kāntaiḥ ketakīṣaṇḍamaṇḍitam ।। susaṃnaddhair balais tatra tadā nṛpavarottamāḥ । anūpaṃ sindhurājasya prapedur yadupuṃgavāḥ ।। mumudur yādavāḥ sarve devāḥ svargagatā iva ।।
dadarśa vipulaṃ deśaṃ sāgarānūpabhūṣitam ।। puralakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ kṛtāspadam iva śriyā ।। viṣayaṃ sindhurājasya śobhitaṃ puralakṣaṇaiḥ ।। mandarodāraśikharaḥ sarvato abhivirājate ।।
babhūva puruṣopetaḥ sarvaratnasamākulaḥ ।। nāmnā dvāravatī nāma svāyatāṣṭāpadopamā ।। niveśaṃ tatra sainyānāṃ rocayanti sma yādavāḥ ।। niveśāya matiṃ cakruḥ kṛṣṇasyānumate sthitāḥ ।
senāpālāś ca saṃcakruḥ skandhāvāraniveśanam ।। deśe puraniveśāya sa yadupravaro vibhuḥ ।। nirmame puruṣaśreṣṭho manasā yādavottamaḥ ।। sukhino nyavasan rājan svarge devagaṇā iva ।।
jarāsaṃdhabhayāc cāpi purīṃ dvāravatīṃ yayau ।। caritaṃ vāsudevasya yaduśreṣṭhasya dhīmataḥ ।। madhyadeśasya kakudaṃ dhāma lakṣmyāś ca kevalam ।। ayuddhenaiva dāśārhas tyaktavān dvijasattama ।।
sa kālayavanaś cāpi kṛṣṇe kiṃ pratyapadyata ।। kiṃ cakāra mahābāhur mahāyogī mahāmanāḥ ।। yam asahyaṃ samālakṣya vyapayāto janārdanaḥ ।। brahmacārī purā bhūtvā na sma dārān sa vindati ।।
gārgyaṃ goṣṭhe dvijaṃ syālaḥ ṣaṇḍham ity uktavān dvijaḥ । yadūnāṃ saṃnidhau sarve jahasur yādavās tataḥ ।। evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ me ṣaṭśataṃ bhūpasaṃmitam । vatsarā dvādaśāś caiva cūrṇaṃ loharajodbhavam ।
syālo abhiśaptavān gārgyam apumān iti bhūpate ।। lipsuḥ putraṃ tato gatvā tapas tepe sudāruṇam ।। ārādhayan mahādevam acintyaṃ śūlapāṇinam ।। vṛṣṇīnām andhakānāṃ ca sarvatejomayaṃ sutam ।।
putraprasavajaṃ devād aputraḥ putrakāmukaḥ ।। gopamadhye yavanarāḍ gopastriṣu samutsṛjat ।। dhārayām āsa gārgyasya garbhaṃ durdharam acyutam ।। aputrasyātha rājñas tu vavṛdhe antaḥpure śiśuḥ ।।
vṛṣṇyandhakakulaṃ tasya nārado vai nyavedayat ।। upapraikṣata tejasvī vardhantaṃ yavaneṣu tam ।। tata enaṃ nṛpā mlecchāḥ saṃśrityānuyayus tadā ।। pahlavāḥ śataśaś cānye mlecchā haimavatās tathā ।।
nānāveṣadharair bhīmair matrurām abhyavartata ।। pṛthivīṃ kampayām āsa sainyena mahatā tadā ।। mūtreṇa śakṛtā caiva sainyena sasṛje nadīm ।। tato aśvaśakṛd ityeva nāma nadyā babhūva ha ।।
vāsudevaḥ samānāyya jñātīn idam uvāca ha ।। avadhyaś cāpi naḥ śatrur varadānāt pinākinaḥ ।। etāvān iha vāsaś ca kathito nāradena me ।। etāvati ca vaktavyaṃ sāmaiva paramaṃ matam ।
tathānye pṛthivīpālā vṛṣṇicakrapratāpitāḥ ।। samāśritya jarāsaṃdham asmān icchanti bādhitum ।। tato vṛṣṇyandhakāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ puraskṛtya mahāmatim । sametya mantrayām āsur jarāsaṃdhabhayena ca ।
kṛtvā ca niścayaṃ sarve palāyanam arocayan ।। vihāya mathurāṃ ramyāṃ mānayantaḥ pinākinam । kuśasthalīṃ dvāravatīṃ niveśayitum īpsavaḥ । apayāne matiṃ kṛtvā dūtaṃ tasmai sasarja ha ।।
ghoram āśīviṣaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prākṣepayat tadā ।। sa dūtaḥ kālayavanaṃ darśayām āsa taṃ ghaṭam ।। idaṃ covāca rājānaṃ rājñāṃ samsadi dūtakaḥ । bho rājann āha kṛṣṇas tvāṃ kim ebhiḥ śalabhais tava । aham ekas tavaiteṣāṃ samartho vāraṇe prabhuḥ ।। tvāṃ ca hatvā nṛpaśreṣṭha sabalaṃ sasuhṛdgaṇam । idaṃ tava balaṃ rājan grahīṣyāmīti niścitam ।। anyathā gaccha rājaṃs tvaṃ balenānena saṃyutaḥ । ity uktvā darśayām āsa ghaṭaṃ kṛṣṇapracoditam । pipīlikānāṃ caṇḍānāṃ pūrayām āsa taṃ ghaṭam ।।
ślokam ekaṃ likhitvā tu ghaṭamadhye akṣipat tadā । bhakṣyamāṇaḥ kilāṅgeṣu bhasmībhūto abhavat tadā ।। preṣayām āsa kṛṣṇāya bāhulyam upavarṇayan ।। dūtānītaṃ harir dṛṣṭvā patraṃ tad vācayaṃs tadā । bahubhir na viroddhavyaṃ durjayo api mahājanaḥ । sphuran tam api nāgendraṃ bhakṣayiṣyanti kīṭikāḥ ।
utsṛjya mathurām āśu dvārakām abhijagmivān ।। niveśya dvārakāṃ rājan vṛṣṇīn āśvāsya caiva ha ।। ājagāma mahāyogī mathurāṃ madhusūdanaḥ ।। prekṣāpūrvaṃ ca kṛṣṇo api niścakrāma mahābalaḥ ।।
na cainam aśakad rājā grahītuṃ yogadharmiṇam ।। hastaprāptam ivātmānaṃ hariṇā sa pade pade । nīto darśayatā dūraṃ yavaneśo adrikandaram ।। palāyanaṃ yadukule jātasya tava nocitam । iti kṣipann anugato nainaṃ prāpāhatāśubhaḥ । evaṃ kṣipto api bhagavān prāviśad girikandaram । ko hi nāma jagannāthaṃ balād yātuṃ priyād ṛte । hastaprāpta ivābhāti tasya gacchañ janārdanaḥ । yatra tiṣṭhati rājendras tatra cāśu viveśa vai । purā devāsure yuddhe kṛtakarmā mahābalaḥ ।।
śrāntasya tasya vāg evaṃ tadā prādur abhūt kila ।। cakṣuṣā krodhadīptena evam āha punaḥ punaḥ ।। sa surair abhyanujñāto lokaṃ mānuṣam āgamat ।। suṣvāpa kālam etaṃ vai yāvat kṛṣṇasya darśanam ।।
varadānaṃ ca devebhyas tejas tasya ca bhūpateḥ ।। tāṃ guhāṃ mucukundasya praviveśa vinītavat ।। pītāmbareṇa svīyena tam ācchādya sa bhūpatim । saṃdarśanapathaṃ tyaktvā tasthau buddhimatāṃ varaḥ ।।
prasvapantaṃ kṛtāntābham āsasāda sudurmatiḥ ।। pādenātmavināśāya śalabhaḥ pāvakaṃ yathā ।। cukopa nicrācchedena pādasparśena tena ca ।। sa dṛṣṭamātraḥ kruddhena saṃprajajvāla sarvataḥ ।।
kṣaṇena kālayavanaṃ netratejovinirgataḥ ।। kṛtakāryo abravīd dhīmān idaṃ vacanam uttamam ।। kṛtaṃ me sumahat kāryaṃ svasti te astu vrajāmy aham ।। parivṛttaṃ yugaṃ mene kālena mahatā tataḥ ।।
tam ālokya ghanaśyāmaṃ pītakauśeyavāsasam । śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ bhrājat kaustubhena virājitam ।। caturbhujaṃ rocamānaṃ vaijayantyā ca mālayā । cāruprasannavadanaṃ sphuran makarakuṇḍalam ।। prekṣaṇīyaṃ trilokeśaṃ sānurāgasmitekṣaṇam । apīcyavayasaṃ matta mṛgendrodāravikramam ।। paryapṛcchan mahābuddhis tejasā tasya dharṣitaḥ । śaṅkitaḥ śanakaiḥ kṛṣṇaṃ durdharṣam iva tejasā । kaś ca kālaḥ prasuptasya yadi jānāsi kathyatām ।। niḥśaṅko gatabhīḥ prāpto vipine girigahvare । padbhyāṃ padmapalāśābhyāṃ vicarasy urukaṇṭake ।। kiṃ svit tejasvināṃ tejo bhagavāṃs tvaṃ vibhāvasuḥ । sūryaḥ somo mahendro vā lokapālo aparo api vā ।। manye tvāṃ devadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ puruṣarṣabham । yad bādhase guhādhvāntaṃ pradīpaḥ prabhayā yathā ।। śuśrūṣatām avyalīkam asmākaṃ narapuṃgava । svaṃ janma karma gotraṃ vā kathyatāṃ yadi rocate । tasya putro yadur jyeṣṭhaś catvāro anye yavīyasaḥ ।।
vāsudevaṃ vijānīhi nṛpate mām ihāgatam ।। idaṃ kaliyugaṃ viddhi kim anyat karavāṇi te ।। avadhyo yo mayā saṃkhye bhaved varṣaśatair api ।। yaduvaṃśodbhavaṃ devaṃ jānāmi śāśvataṃ vibhum । ādyaṃ puruṣam īśānam acyutaṃ madhusūdanam ।। purā gargeṇa kathitam aṣṭāviṃśatime yuge । dvāparādau harer janma yaduvaṃśe bhaviṣyati ।। namas tasmai bhagavate puruṣāya mahātmane । anantāya mahābāho viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave ।। evaṃ stutas tadā viṣṇur mucukundena dhīmatā । vareṇa cchandayām āsa bhagavān acyutas tadā ।। punar apy abravīt kṛṣṇo mucukundaṃ mahābhujam । tvadarthe apy āgato vīra nāradena prabodhitaḥ । uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha bhadraṃ te yathākāmaṃ caratv iha ।
anvīyamānaḥ kṛṣṇena kṛtakāryeṇa dhīmatā ।। pareṇādhiṣṭhitaṃ caiva rājyaṃ kevalam ātmanaḥ ।। yat syāt tvaddarśane puṇyaṃ tan me kṛṣṇa bhaved iti । himavantam agād rājā tapase dhṛtamānasaḥ ।।
āruroha divaṃ rājā karmabhiḥ svair jitaṃ śubhaiḥ ।। ghātayitvātmanaḥ śatruṃ tat sainyaṃ pratyapadyata ।। mucukundena mahātmanā ।mathurāṃ punarāgatya । ādāyopayayau dhīmāṃs tat sainyaṃ nihateśvaram ।।
janārdano dvāravatīṃ ca tāṃ purīm aśobhayat tena dhanena bhūriṇā ।। kṛṣṇāya ca namas tubhyaṃ rāmarāmāya te namaḥ । vāmanāya namas tubhyaṃ kapilāya namo astu te ।। nānārūpa namas tubhyaṃ namas te karmasākṣiṇe । viśvarūpa namas tubhyaṃ hṛṣīkeśāya te namaḥ ।। evaṃ saṃstūyamānaś ca mucukundena dhīmatā । uttarāṃ diśam āśritya tapam ācara sāttvikam । kṛtajapyo hṛṣīkeśo vanānte niṣasāda ha ।। upatasthuḥ kulaprāgryā yādavā yadunandanam ।।
puṇyāhaghoṣair vipulair durgasyārabdhavān kriyāṃ ।। provāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho devān vṛtraripur yathā ।। nāma cāsyāḥ kṛtaṃ puryāḥ khyātiṃ yad upayāsyati ।। bhaviṣyati purī ramyā śakrasyevāmarāvatī ।।
sthānāni vidadhuś cātra brahmādīnāṃ yathākramam । catvarān rājamārgāṃś ca samān antaḥpurāṇi ca ।। bādhamānā ripugaṇān ugrasenapurogamāḥ ।। mīyantāṃ rājamārgāś ca prākārasya ca yā gatiḥ ।।
niyujyantāṃ ca deśeṣu preṣyakarmakarā janāḥ ।। yathānideśaṃ saṃhṛṣṭāś cakrur vāstuparigrahān ।। puṇye ahani mahārāja dvijātīn abhipūjya ca ।। sthapatīn atha govindas tatrovāca mahāmatiḥ ।।
vibhaktacatvarapathaṃ suniviṣṭeṣṭadaivatam ।। durgakarmaṇi saṃbhārān upalabhya yathāvidhi ।। sthānāni vidadhuś cātra brahmādīnāṃ yathākramam ।। gṛhakṣetrendrabhallāṭaṃ puṣpadantaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
puryāḥ kṣipraṃ niveṣārthaṃ cintayām āsa mādhavaḥ ।। purī sā vai priyakarī yadūnām abhivardhanī ।। viśvakarmā svamatyā vai purīṃ saṃsthāpayiśyati ।। tridaṣābhimukhaḥ kṛṣṇo vivikte samapadyata ।।
viśvakarmā suraśreṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇasya pramukhe sthitaḥ ।। kiṃkaraḥ samanuprāptaḥ śādhi māṃ kiṃ karomi te ।। tathā tvaṃ deva mānyo asi viśeṣo nāsti me prabho ।। eṣo asmi paridṛṣṭārthaḥ kiṃ karomi praśādhi mām ।।
pratyuvāca yaduśreṣṭhaḥ kaṃsārir atulaṃ vacaḥ ।। avaśyaṃ tv iha kartavyaṃ sadanaṃ me surottama ।। matprabhāvānurūpaiś ca gṛhaiś ceyaṃ samantataḥ ।। tatheyaṃ hi tvayā kāryā śakto hy asi mahāmate ।।
martyāḥ paśyantu me lakṣmīṃ puryā yadukulasya ca ।। kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakarmāṇaṃ devāmitravināśanam ।। purī tv iyaṃ janasyāsya na paryāptā bhaviṣyati ।। catvāraḥ sāgarā hy asyāṃ vicariṣyanti rūpiṇaḥ ।।
tataḥ svāyatalakṣaṇyā purī syāt puruṣottama ।। sāgaraṃ saritāṃ nātham uvāca vadatāṃ varaḥ ।। pratisaṃhriyatām ātmā yady asti mayi mānyatā ।। paryāptaviṣayākārā samagrā visahiṣyati ।।
samārutena yogena utsasarja mahārṇavaḥ ।। govinde caiva saṃmānaṃ sāgaraḥ kṛtavāṃs tadā ।। adyaprabhṛti govinda sarve samadhirohata ।। acireṇaiva kālena gṛhasaṃbādhamālinī ।।
cayāṭṭālakakeyūrā pṛthivyāḥ kakudopamā ।। cakāra tasyāṃ puryāṃ vai deśe tridaśapūjite ।। mānasena prayatnena vaiṣṇavī viśvakarmaṇā ।। vidhānavihitadvārā prākāravaraśobhitā । parikhācayasaṃguptā sāṭṭaprākāratoraṇā ।
nānāpaṇyasamākīrṇā khecarīva ca gāṃ gatā ।। samantataḥ saṃvṛtāṅgī vanitevāyatekṣaṇā ।। rathyākoṭisahasrāḍhyā śubhrarājapathottarā । bhūṣayantī samudraṃ sā svargam indrapurī yathā ।।
pṛthivyāṃ sarvaratnānām ekā nicayaśālinī । surāṇām api sukṣetrā sāmantakṣobhakāriṇī । aprakāśaṃ tadākāśaṃ prāsādair upaśobhitā ।। oghaiś ca vārirājasya śiśirīkṛtamārutā ।।
satārakā dyaur iva sā dvārakā pratyarājata ।। hiraṇyapratipūrṇaiś ca gṛhair gambhīranisvanaiḥ ।। kvacit kvacid udagrāgrair upāvṛttamahāpathā ।। abhipretajanākīrṇāṃ somaḥ kham iva bhāsayan ।।
viśvakarmakṛtāṃ divyāṃ ratnajālasamākulām । jagāma tridivaṃ devo govindenābhipūjitaḥ ।। janān imān dhanaughais tu tarpayeyam ahaṃ yadi ।। śaṅkham āhvayatopendro niśi svabhavane vibhuḥ ।।
ājagāma samīpaṃ vai tasya dvāravatīpateḥ ।। kṛṣṇaṃ vijñāpayām āsa yathā vaiśravaṇaṃ tathā ।। niyojaya mahābāho yatkāryaṃ yadunandana ।। janā ye asmin kṛśadhanās tān dhanenābhipūraya ।।
dehīti cābhibhāṣantaṃ nagaryāṃ nirdhanaṃ naram ।। ghanaughair abhivarṣadhvaṃ cakruḥ sarve tathā ca te ।। dvāravatyāṃ puri purā keśavasya mahātmanaḥ । kṛśo vā malino vāpi dvāravatyāṃ gṛhe gṛhe ।।
tatrastha eva bhagavān yādavānāṃ priyaṃkaraḥ ।। ekamāsīnam ekānte devaguhyadharaṃ prabhum ।। śādhi māṃ puruṣottama । yad bravīṣi mahābāho ।
yathaiva dūto devānāṃ tathaivāsmi tavānagha ।। mārutaṃ jagataḥ prāṇaṃ rūpiṇaṃ samupasthitam ।। sabhāṃ sudharmām ādāya devebhyas tvam ihānaya ।। tasyāṃ viśeyur ete hi na tu yā kṛtrimā bhavet ।।
sā yadūn dhārayet sarvān yathaiva tridaśāṃs tathā ।। vāyur ātmopamagatir jagāma tridivālayam ।। sabhāṃ sudharmām ādāya punar āyān mahītalam ।। devo devasabhāṃ dattvā vāyur antaradhīyata ।।
na bhayaṃ vidyate yatra sabhā sā dharmavatsalā । sudharmā yadumukhyānāṃ devānāṃ tridive yathā ।। dravyairalaṃkaroti sma purīṃ svāṃ pramadām iva ।। śuśubhe sā purī ramyā ratnajālasamākulā । nānāpakṣisamākīrṇā prāsādair upaśobhitā ।
balādhyakṣāṃś ca yuktāṃś ca prakṛtīśāṃs tathaiva ca ।। senāpatim anādhṛṣṭiṃ vikadruṃ mantripuṃgavam ।। uddhavo vasudevaś ca kaṅko vipṛthur eva ca । śvaphalkaś citrakaś caiva gadaḥ satyaka eva ca ।
baladevaḥ pṛthuś caivaṃ matreśv abhyantarā daśa । sthāpayām āsa matimān sarvakāryeṣv anantarān ।। yodhamukhyaś ca yodhānāṃ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥ ।। ācāryo dhanuṣāṃ vede sākṣāddroṇa ivāparaḥ । sātyakiḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca śatruhā yuddhadurmadaḥ ।
mumude yadubhiḥ sārdhaṃ lokasraṣṭā mahītale ।। prāptavān baladevas tu kṛṣṇasyānumate tadā ।। yaḥ sargajaiḥ suragaṇapriyakṛdbhir uccair ।dravyaiḥ samudranihitaiś ca samudrajātaiḥ ।hṛdyām akārayad aśeṣajagal lalāmāṃ ।śrīdvārakāṃ puravarīṃ tam upaimi viṣṇum । nṛpān udyojayām āsa cedirājapriyepsayā ।।
yathārhaṃ ca yathāyogaṃ praśrayaṃ pradadau nṛpaḥ । vivāhaṃ ghoṣayām āsa śiśupālasya māgadhaḥ ।। sarvam antaḥpuraṃ caiva vivāhe utsukaṃ kila । śvobhūte tu vivāhasya caidyasyeti ca bhūmipāḥ । saṃnaddhāḥ samapadyantāṃ vibhavaiḥ svair yathākramam ।। śiśupālo api rājā tu varaveṣeṇa saṃyutaḥ । kumārair ātmatulyaiś ca niyamastho abhavat tadā । śiśupālasya nṛpater vivāho bhavitā kila ।। sahasrākṣasamaṃ yuddhe māyāsu ca viśāradam ।। sudevaṃ vīryasaṃpannaṃ pṛthag akṣauhiṇīpatim ।।
putraṃ ca pāṇḍyarājasya kaliṅgādhipatiṃ tathā ।। aṃśumantaṃ tathā krāthaṃ śrutarvāṇaṃ ca bhārata ।। paṭuśaṃ ca mahābāhuṃ kāśyādhipatim eva ca ।। sabhārhān sakalān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrān mahābalān । vindānuvindāv āvantyau bāhlikān saha bāhlikaiḥ ।। saṃśaptakās tu te sarve āsyandā yavanās tathā । yavanasya sutaś cāpi ārṣāyaṇas tathā śakāḥ ।। svabhāvaś candrahāsaś ca pārasīkās tathāpare । virāṭo drupadaś caiva jayadrathavidūrathau । bhagadatto mahāsenaḥ śalaḥ śālvo mahābalaḥ । bhūriśravā mahāsenaḥ kuntibhojaś ca vīryavān ।। akṣauhiṇīnāṃ ṣaṣṭiṃ ca saptādhikadaśānugāḥ । svayaṃvarārthaṃ saṃprāptā bhojarājaniveśane ।
kasyāṇvavāye dyutimān saṃbhūto dvijasattama ।। vindhyasya dakṣiṇe pārśve vidarbhān yo nyaveśayat ।। babhūvur vīryasaṃpannāḥ pṛthag vaṃśakarā nṛpāḥ ।। krathasya tv aṃśumāṇ vaṃśe kaiśikasya tu bhīṣmakaḥ ।।
rukmī tasyābhavat putro rukmiṇī ca viśāṃ pate ।। prāspardhat saha kṛṣṇena nityam adbhutakarmaṇā ।। cakame vāsudevas tāṃ śravād eva mahādyutiḥ ।। tejovīryabalopetaḥ sa me bhartā bhaved iti ।।
kaṃsasya vadhasaṃtāpāt kṛṣṇāyāmitatejase । yācamānāya kaṃsasya preṣyo asāv iti cintayan ।। varayām āsa tāṃ rājā bhīṣmakaṃ bhīmavikramam ।। magadheṣu purā yena nirmitaṃ tad girivrajam ।।
vasor eva tadā vaṃśe damaghoṣo api cedirāṭ ।। bhaginyāṃ vasudevasya śrutaśravasi jajñire ।। sarvāstrakuśalā vīrā vīryavanto mahābalāḥ ।। tasyānvavāye saṃbhūtā bahavo rājavaṃśajāḥ ।
jarāsaṃdhasya rājendra damaghoṣo mahābalaḥ । jarāsaṃdhaḥ svasutavad dadarśainaṃ jugopa ca ।। kṛtāny āgāṃsi caidyena vṛṣṇīnāṃ tatpriyaiṣiṇā ।। kṛṣṇārthaṃ vairamabhavaj jarāsaṃdhasya vṛṣṇibhiḥ ।।
tāṃ dadau bhīṣmakaś cāpi śiśupālāya vīryavān ।। yayau vidarbhān sahito dantavaktreṇa yāyinā ।। aṅgavaṅgakaliṅgānām īśvaraḥ sa mahābalaḥ ।। parayā pūjayopetān ānināya purīṃ prati ।।
prayayur vṛṣṇayaś cānye rathais tatra balānvitāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā tān āgatān sarvān vāsudevapurogamān । pūjayām āsa pūjārhān nyavasanta bahiś ca te ।। nyaveśayac ca tān sarvān bhīṣmako nagarād bahiḥ ।। sthite tasmiñ jarāsaṃdhe ripau teṣāṃ mahātmani । saṃbhārāś caiva sarvatra vivāhāya samāhṛtāḥ ।। śaṅkhāś ca paṭahāś caiva sasvanāḥ sarvatas tadā । brāhmaṇāś ca samāyātā nānādigbhyas tathaiva ca । utthitāś caiva sarvatra dhvajāś ca samalaṃkṛtāḥ ।
caturyujā rathenaindraṃ devatāyatanaṃ śubhā ।। dāsīśatasahasraughair veṣṭitā tu jagāma ha । ambikāpūjanārthāya pādacārī yathāsthiti । dīpyamānena vapuṣā balena mahatā vṛtā ।। keśavo me bhaved bhartā nānyaḥ kaścid bhaved iti । evaṃ manasi saṃsthāpya puṣpāñjalipuṭābhavat ।
rūpeṇāgryeṇa saṃpannāṃ devatāyatanāntike ।। pṛthivīm iva gambhīrām utthitāṃ pṛthivītalāt ।। kṛṣṇena manasā dṛṣṭāṃ durnirīkśyāṃ surair api ।। tāmrauṣṭhanayanāpāṅgī pīnorujaghanastanī ।।
atyarthaṃ rūpataḥ kāntā pīnaśroṇipayodharā । tīkṣṇaśuklaiḥ samair dantaiḥ prabhāsadbhir alaṃkṛtā ।। rukmiṇī rūpiṇī devī pāṇḍurakṣaumavāsinī ।। haviṣevānalasyārcir manas tasyāṃ samādadhat ।।
rukmiṇī ca tadā devī dadṛśe kṛṣṇam īśvaram ।। acintayac ca sā devī dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam avasthitam । so ayam viṣṇur jagannāthaḥ sākṣād rāmānujaḥ kṛtī ।। asya cakraṃ sadā śaṅkhaṃ bhujayor ubhayorapi । śobhayetāṃ sadā tau tu daityadānavadāriṇau ।। asya haste sthitaṃ śārṅgaṃ daityadānavabhīṣaṇam । sadā bhāti mahac cāpaṃ loke khyātataraṃ hareḥ ।। yamāśritya gadā devī sadā kaumodakīti sā । daityadānavahantrī ca tad bhujopari dāruṇā ।। yad anujñāṃ samāśritya khaḍgo nandakasaṃjñakaḥ । ripūn hanti mahāvīryān asahyān daivatair api ।। asya syād vāhanaṃ viṣṇor garutmān pakṣipuṃgavaḥ । śakrādīṃś ca surāñ jitvā jahārāmṛtam uttamam ।। so ayam viṣṇur guruḥ sākṣād gopaveṣeṇa bhūṣitaḥ । gopastrīstanabhāreṣu vijahāra yathāsukham ।। yo nanarta hrade tasyā yamunāyās tadā hariḥ । amathnāt kāliyaṃ tasmin viṣāgnijvālamālinam ।। ayaṃ govardhanaṃ śailaṃ dadhāv ekena bāhunā । līlayā sa jagannātho kolakaṃ bālako yathā ।। ayaṃ sa puṇḍarīkākṣo yo hayaṃ prajaghāna ha ।। yaś cāṇūraṃ mṛdhe hatvā kaṃsaṃ caiva mahābalam । nanarta raṅge govindo gopaiḥ sārdhaṃ sayādavaiḥ ।। ayaṃ sa yādavaśreṣṭhaḥ padmakañjalkalocanaḥ । śyāmāvadātaḥ saśrīkaḥ sākṣādindrānujaḥ kṛtī ।। yuvā kṛtī purāṇātmā padmākṣaḥ padmasaprabhaḥ । so ayam adya jagannāthaḥ prāpto mām iha yādavaḥ ।। amuṣya pādayoḥ padmam udvahāmi na saṃśayaḥ । śuśrūṣāṃ pratiyokṣyāmi pādayoḥ padmasaṃjñayoḥ ।। evaṃ vicintayitvā sā vavande tāṃ śacīṃ tadā । tatpramāthe akarod buddhiṃ vṛṣṇibhyaḥ praṇidhāya ca ।। unmathya sahasā kṛṣṇaḥ svaṃ nināya rathottamam ।। samanahyanta dāśārhās tadājñāya tu sarvaśaḥ ।।
vājibhir vāraṇaiś cāpi parivavrur halāyudham ।। rāme cāsajya taṃ bhāraṃ yuyudhāne ca vīryavān ।। cakradeve sunakṣatre sāraṇe ca mahābale ।। ugrasenātmaje kaṅke śatadyumne ca keśavaḥ ।।
atidānte bṛhaddurge śvaphalke citrake pṛthau ।। gurum āsajya taṃ bhāraṃ yayau dvāravatīṃ prati ।। tataś ca yādavāḥ sarve yuddhāya samupasthitāḥ । saṃnaddhā niryayuḥ kruddhā jighāṃsanto janārdanam ।।
niryayau cedirājaḥ sa bhrātṛbhiḥ sumahārathaiḥ ।। kva vāsudevaḥ kva ca gopakāste ।kuto nu rājā yaduvaṃśajanmanāṃ ।kuto nu rāmo madamattagarhitaḥ ।kuto nu vīro yudhi sātyakiḥ kila ।।iti bruvanto nṛpasattamās tadā ।raṇāya yuktāḥ sabalāḥ samāgadhāḥ ।śaraiś ca khaḍgair yudhi pātayanto ।mahārathā niryayur ugravīryāḥ ।।atha sainye mahārāja māgadhasya mahātmanaḥ । śaṅkhaduṃdubhayaś caiva sasvanur yuddhaśaṃsavaḥ । yādavāś ca mahārāja śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। bherīṇāṃ ca mṛdaṅgānāṃ jharjharīṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ । nādāḥ samabhavantaś ca yadūnāṃ sainyasaṃcaye ।। tato yuddhaṃ samabhavat senayor ubhayor api । jarāsaṃdhapramukhato vṛṣṇayaḥ prathitās tadā । saṃkarṣaṇaṃ puraskṛtya vāsavaṃ maruto yathā ।। ṣaḍbhir vivyādha nārācair yuyudhāno mahāmṛdhe ।।
taṃ pratyavidhyat kārūṣo bāṇair daśabhir āśugaiḥ ।। aṣṭabhiḥ pratyavidhyat taṃ śiśupālaḥ pratāpavāṇ ।। anirdāntas tathāṣṭābhir bṛhaddurgaś ca pañcabhiḥ ।। jaghāna cāśvāṃś caturaś caturbhir vipṛthoḥ śaraiḥ ।।
gaveṣaṇasya sūtaṃ ca prāhiṇodyamasādanam ।। āruroha rathaṃ kṣipraṃ bṛhaddurgasya vīryavān ।। āruhya javanān aśvān niyantum upacakrame ।। nṛtyantaṃ rathamārgeṣu cāpahastāḥ kalāpinaḥ ।।
paṭuśaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā vivyādha yudhi mārgaṇaiḥ ।। tato balī cakradevaṃ bibheda daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। vidūratho api taṃ ṣaḍbhir vivyādhājau śitaiḥ śaraiḥ ।। dantavaktro api vivyādha bhānumantaṃ vidūratham ।
kṛtavarmā bibhedājau rājaputraṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। prativivyādha taṃ kruddhaḥ pauṇḍraḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ ।। tomareṇāṃsadeśe taṃ nirbibheda kaliṅgarāṭ ।। tomareṇa bibhedāṅgaṃ bibhedāṅgaś ca taṃ śaraiḥ ।।
kaliṅgasya tathānīkaṃ nārācair bibhiduḥ śitaiḥ ।। jaghāna rāmaḥ samkruddho vaṅgarājaṃ ca saṃyuge ।। saṃkarṣaṇo jaghānograir nārācaiḥ kaiśikān bahūn ।। nihatya tān mahābāhur jarāsaṃdhaṃ tato abhyayāt ।।
ciccheda cāsya bhallena dhvajaṃ ratnavibhūṣitam ।। cāpaṃ ca mahad āyattaṃ śarair eva halāyudhaḥ । rathaṃ cāsya mahārāja tilaśaś ca samāhanat ।। sa cchinnadhanvā viratho gadāmādāya māgadhaḥ । bibheda balabhadraṃ tu jaghāna ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। rathaṃ ca cūrṇayām āsa gadayāsya sa māgadhaḥ ।। pātyamānād rathāt tasmād avaplutya halāyudhaḥ । sātyakes tu rathaṃ prāyāt sarvakṣatrasya paśyataḥ ।। sātyakis tu mahārāja śarair vivyādha māgadham ।। baladevo mahārāja gadāṃ saṃgṛhya satvaram । jaghāna māgadhaṃ saṃkhye vajreṇeva giriṃ hariḥ । anivāryaṃ śarair eva praharṣogho mahodadheḥ । sṛjatāṃ śaravarṣāṇi nighnatām itaretaram ।।
rathai rathāś ca saṃrabdhāḥ sādibhiś cāpi sādinaḥ ।। chindantaś cottamāṅgāni vicerur yudhi te pṛthak ।। śarāṇāṃ patatāṃ śabdaḥ pakṣiṇām iva śuśruve ।। jugūha ghoṣaḥ śastrāṇāṃ jyāghoṣaś ca mahātmanāṃ ।।
taṃ prāvidhyata saptatyā bāṇair gāḍhaṃ janārdanaḥ । yatamānaś ca ciccheda dhvajaṃ cāsya mahābalaḥ । jahāra ca śiraḥ kāyāt sārathes tasya vīryavān ।। taṃ kṛchragatam ājñāya parivavrur janārdanam । dākṣiṇātyā jighāṃsanto rājānaḥ sarva eva te ।। tam aṃśumān mahābāhur vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ । śrutarvā pañcabhiḥ kruddho veṇudāriś ca saptabhiḥ ।। tato aṃśumantaṃ govindo bibhedorasi vīryavān । niṣasāda rathopasthe vyathitaḥ sa narādhipaḥ ।। śrutarvaṇo jaghānāśvāṃś caturbhiś caturaḥ śaraiḥ । veṇudārir dhvajaṃ chittvā bhujaṃ vivyādha dakṣiṇam ।। tathaiva ca śrutarvāṇaṃ śarair vivyādha saptabhiḥ । śiśriye ca dhvajaṃ śrānto nyaṣīdac ca vyathānvitaḥ ।। muñcantaḥ śaravarṣāṇi vāsudevaṃ tato abhyayuḥ । krathakaiśikamukhyās te rathavaṃśena sarvaśaḥ ।। bāṇān bāṇaiś ca ciccheda teṣāṃ yudhi janārdanaḥ । jaghāna caiṣāṃ saṃrabdho yatamānān yatān bahūn ।। punar anyāṃś catuḥṣaṣṭyā nijaghāna śitaiḥ śaraiḥ । kruddhān āpatato vīro prādravat tadbalaṃ tataḥ । etasminn antare vīro balabhadro mahāyaśāḥ । jaghāna gadayā vīraṃ jarāsaṃdhaṃ mahāmṛdhe ।। mūrchāṃ jagāma rājā tu nipapāta ca bhūtale ।। sātyakir vaṅgarājaṃ tu jaghāna niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ । tat sainyaṃ vimukhaṃ cāsīj jarāsaṃdhe pataty api ।। sātyakir balabhadraś ca jitvā yodhān sahasraśaḥ । śaṅkhaṃ dadhmatū rājānau sarveṣām agrataḥ sthitau । tataś ca vidrute sainye jarāsaṃdhe parājite । tayoḥ śaṅkhadhvaniṃ śrutvā gacchann eva janārdanaḥ । jitaṃ magadharājasya sainyaṃ bahunṛpāśrayam ।। ity evaṃ cintayitvā tu vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān । pāñcajanyaṃ mahāśaṅkhaṃ dadhmau yadukulodvahaḥ । pratijñām akarot kruddhaḥ samakṣaṃ bhīṣmakasya ha ।। kuṇḍinaṃ na pravekṣyāmi satyam etad bravīmi te ।। javena prayayau kruddho balena mahatā vṛtaḥ ।।
krātho aṃśumāñ śrutarvā ca veṇudāriśca vīryavān ।। krathakaiśikamukhyāśca sarva eva mahārathāḥ ।। govindaṃ dadṛśuḥ kruddhāḥ sahaiva priyayā sthitam ।। ādāya niśitaṃ bāṇam idamāha janārdanam ।।
are gopakadāyāda paradārapradharṣaṇa । vimucyatām iyaṃ bālā sthātavyaṃ ca kṣaṇāntaram । śiraśchetsyāmi te bāṇaiḥ sthito asi yadi matpuraḥ । ityuktvā niśitaṃ bāṇaṃ saṃdadhe dhanuṣi prabho ।
cikīrṣur dvairathaṃ yuddham abhyayān madhusūdanam ।। taṃ pratyavidhyat saptatyā bāṇair yudhi janārdanaḥ ।। jahāra ca śiraḥ kāyāt sāratheś cāsya vīryavān ।। dākṣiṇātyā jighāṃsanto rājānaḥ sarva eva te ।।
śrutarvā pañcabhiḥ kruddho veṇudāriś ca saptabhiḥ ।। niṣasāda rathopasthe vyathitaḥ sa narādhipaḥ ।। veṇudārer dhvajaṃ chittvā bhujaṃ vivyādha dakṣiṇam ।। śiśriye sa dhvajaṃ klānto nyaṣīdacca vyathānvitaḥ ।।
krathakaiśikamukhyās te rathavaṃśena sarvaśaḥ ।। jaghāna caiṣāṃ saṃrabdho yatamānāṃś ca tāñ śarān ।। kruddhān ādravato vīrān ādravat sa mahābalaḥ ।। pañcabhir niśitair bāṇair vivyādhorasi keśavam ।।
ājaghāna dhvajaṃ cāsya śareṇa nataparvaṇā ।। dhanuś ciccheda cāpy asya yatamānasya rukmiṇaḥ ।। prāduś cakāra divyāni dīptāny astrāṇi vīryavān ।। vāyavyaṃ vāruṇaṃ caiva māhendram atha nairṛtam । paiśācaṃ rākṣasaṃ caiva raudraṃ māheśvaraṃ tathā ।। etānyastrāṇi davyāni vivyādra yudhi keśave । tair eva tāni govindo nijaghāna janārdanaḥ ।
punaś ciccheda taṃ cāpaṃ ratheṣāṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। utpapāta rathād vīro garutmān iva vīryavān ।। nārācaiś ca tribhiḥ kruddho bibhedainam athorasi ।। kruddho bibhedainam atho śarair urasi pañcabhiḥ ।
visaṃjño mūrchito rājā vajreṇeva hato giriḥ ।। sāśvadhvajarathāṃś caiva sasūtānsapadānugān । rukmiṇaṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā vyadravanta narādhipāḥ ।। kṛṣṇabāṇavibhinnāṅgā vīkṣamāṇāḥ parasparam ।
pādayor nyapatad bhartur bhrātur jīvitakāṅkṣiṇī ।। abhayaṃ rukmiṇe dattvā prayayau svāṃ purīṃ tataḥ ।। jitvā tu sātyakirvīraḥ śiśupālaṃ mahābalam । baladevo api vārṣṇeyo jitvā magadhapuṃgavam ।
te api vīrā yathāyogaṃ jitvā tān yādavottamāḥ । prayayur dvārakāṃ hṛṣṭāḥ puraskṛtya halāyudham ।। rukmiṇaṃ ratham āropya prayayau svapuraṃ tataḥ ।। hīnapratijño naicchat sa praveṣṭuṃ kuṇḍinaṃ puram ।।
tadbhojakaṭam ity eva babhūva bhuvi viśrutam ।। janmāspadaṃ bhagavato bhṛgusūnor mahātmanaḥ । tacchaśāsa mahāvīryo rukmī jīvati tatra vai । bhīṣmakaḥ kuṇḍine caiva rājovāsa mahāmanāḥ ।। jarāsaṃdho api saṃprāpya saṃjñāṃ prāpa svakaṃ puram । sarvair nṛpatibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sajjayāvanatānanaḥ ।। śiśupālo api mandātmā lajjāviṣṭaḥ sabāndhavaḥ । paurajānapadair dṛṣṭaḥ so ayaṃ bhojasutāpatiḥ । idānīm anyathā vṛttaḥ svāṃ purī niryayau bahiḥ ।। ko nu nāma samartho atra kṛṣṇe jīvati sāṃpratam । rukmiṇīm anyathākartuṃ sabale sahasātyakau ।। iti paurāś ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā sunīthaṃ mandavikramam । āhuḥ parasparaṃ sarve gacchantaṃ svapuraṃ nṛpam ।
rukmiṇyāḥ keśavaḥ pāṇiṃ jagrāha vidhivat prabhuḥ ।। sītayeva purā rāmaḥ paulomy eva puraṃdaraḥ ।। damayantyā yathā rājā puṇyaśloko nalastathā । pativratā guṇopetā rūpaśīlaguṇānvitā ।।
cārudeṣṇaṃ sudeṣṇaṃ ca pradyumnaṃ ca mahābalam ।। cāruvindaṃ sucāruṃ ca bhadracāruṃ tathaiva ca ।। dharmārthakuśalās te tu kṛtāstrā yuddhadurmadāḥ ।। upayeme mahābāhur guṇopetāḥ kulodbhavāḥ ।।
sutāṃ jāmbavataś cāpi rohiṇīṃ kāmarūpiṇīm ।। śaibyāṃ sudattāṃ rūpeṇa śriyā hy apsarasopamām ।। parārdhyavastrābharaṇāḥ kāmaih sarvaiḥ samedhitaḥ ।। aśītiṃ ca sahasrāṇi ṣoḍaśānyāni bhārata ।
yajvānaḥ puṇyakarmāṇo mahābhāgā mahābalāḥ ।। evaṃ vivāhaṃ yadupuṃgavastadā ।kṛtvā tu rāmeṇa ca yādavaiḥ saha ।pure tu tasminnyavasatsukhaṃ harir ।yathaiva śakraḥ svapure jagadguruḥ । duhituḥ kārayām āsa svayaṃvaram ariṃdamaḥ ।। samājagmur mahāvīryā nānādigbhyaḥ śriyānvitāḥ ।।
sā hi taṃ cakame kanyā sa ca tāṃ śubhalocanām ।। pṛthivyām abhavat khyātā rukmiṇas tanayā tadā ।। vaidarbhī varayām āsa pradyumnam arisūdanam ।। rūpeṇāpratimo loke keśavasyātmajo abhavat ।।
nārāyaṇī candrasenā jātakāmā ca taṃ prati ।। upādāya tu vaidarbhīṃ pradyumno dvārakāṃ yayau ।। reme saha tayā vīro damayantyā nalo yathā । dhanurvede ca vede ca nītiśāstre ca pāragam ।।
patnyarthaṃ varayām āsa nāmnā rukmavatīti sā ।। prītyā ca raukmiṇeyasya rukmiṇyāś cāpy upagrahāt ।। dadānīty abravīd rājā prītimāñ janamejaya ।। anyaiś ca vṛṣṇibhiḥ sārdhaṃ vidarbhān sabalo yayau ।।
āhūtā rukmiṇā te api tatrājagmur narādhipāḥ ।। vivāhāyāniruddhasya babhūva paramotsavaḥ ।। vaidarbhayādavānāṃ ca babhūva paramotsavaḥ । remire vṛṣṇayas tatra pūjyamānā yathāmarāḥ ।।
akṣaḥ śrutarvā cāṇūraḥ krāthaś caivāṃśumān api ।। pāṇḍyaś ca nṛpatiḥ śrīmān ṛṣīkādhipatis tathā ।। abhigamyābruvan sarve rukmiṇaṃ rahasi prabhum ।। priyadyūtaś ca rāmo asāv akṣeṣv anipuṇo api ca ।।
ity ukto rocayām āsa dyūtaṃ rukmī mahārathaḥ ।। sabhām āviviśur hṛṣṭāḥ siktāṃ candanavāriṇā ।। sauvarṇeṣv āsaneṣv āsāṃ cakrire vijigīṣavaḥ ।। bāḍham ity abravīdd hṛṣṭaḥ saha dīvyāma paṇyatām ।।
maṇimuktāḥ suvarṇaṃ ca tatrāninyuḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। kalahāyāspadaṃ ghoraṃ durmatīnāṃ kṣayāvaham ।। rukmiṇā saha saṃpāte baladevo glahaṃ dadau ।। tāvad evāparaṃ bhūyo baladevaṃ jigāya saḥ ।।
suvarṇakoṭiṃ jagrāha glahaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। ślāghamānaś ca cikṣepa prahasan musalāyudham ।। ajeyo baladevo ayam akṣadyūte parājitaḥ ।। dantān vidarśayan hṛṣṭas tatrākrudhyadd halāyudhaḥ ।।
roṣam āhārayām āsa jitaroṣo api dharmavit ।। dhairyān manaḥ saṃniyamya tato vacanam abravīt ।। kṛṣṇākṣāṃl lohitākṣāṃś ca deśe asmiṃs tvam apāṃsule ।। anuktvā vacanaṃ kiṃcid bāḍham ity abravīt punaḥ ।।
cāturakṣe nivṛtte tu nirjitaḥ sa narādhipaḥ ।। ete bruvantu rājāno ye tathyavacanā iha । baladevaṃ tato rukmī mayā jitam iti smayan ।। bhūyaḥ krodhasamāviṣṭo nottaraṃ vyājahāra ha ।।
satyam āha balaḥ śrīmān dharmeṇaiṣa parājitaḥ ।। manasā samanujñātaṃ tat syād ity avagamyatām ।। tām anādṛtya vaidarbho duṣṭarājanyanoditaḥ । saṃkarṣaṇaṃ parihasan babhāṣe kālanoditaḥ ।।
naivākṣakovidā yūyaṃ gopālā vanagocarāḥ । akṣaiḥ krīḍanti rājāno bāṇaiś ca na bhavādṛśāḥ ।। rukmiṇaivam adhikṣipto rājabhiś copahāsitaḥ । rukmiṇyā bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ niṣpipeṣa mahītale ।।
jaghānāṣṭāpadenaiva prasahya yadupuṃgavaḥ ।। khaḍgam udyamya tāṃś cāpi trāsayām āsa pārthivān ।। raṅgamadhye haladharaḥ paribabhrāma siṃhavat । tenaiva tu jaghānāśu tatrasthān krathakaiśikān ।
nirjagāma sabhādvārāt trāsayan krathakaiśikān ।। keśeṣu rukmiṇaṃ gṛhya cakarṣa ca punaḥ punaḥ । tam ādāya sabhādvārāc charapātaṃ sasarja ha । vitrāsya dviṣataḥ sarvān siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgān iva ।। nyavedayata kṛṣṇāya tac ca sarvaṃ yathābhavat ।।
rukmiṇī tu tataḥ śrutvā nihataṃ bhrātaraṃ priyam । nigṛhya ca tadātmānaṃ krodhād aśrūṇy avartayat ।। jyeṣṭho bhrātātha rukmiṇyā rukmiṇīsnehakāraṇāt । aṣṭāpadena balavān rājā vajradharopamaḥ ।।
drumabhārgavatulye vai drumabhārgavaśikṣite ।। vṛṣṇayaś cāndhakāś caiva sarve vimanaso abhavan ।। rukmiṇī ca mahābhāgā vilapanty ārtayā girā । vilapantīṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā sāntvayām āsa keśavaḥ । vairasya ca samutthānaṃ vṛṣṇibhir bharatarṣabha ।।
rāmakṛṣṇau samāśritya yayur dvāravatīṃ purīm ।। māhātmyaṃ śrotum icchāmi śeṣasya dharaṇībhṛtaḥ ।। kathayanti mahātmānaṃ ye purāṇavido janāḥ ।। anantaṃ yaṃ vidur nāgam ādidevaṃ mahaujasam ।।
śeṣas tejonidhiḥ śrīmān akampyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। jarāsaṃdhaṃ gadāyuddhe jitavān yo na cāvadhīt ।। anvayur māgadhaṃ saṃkhye te cāpi vijitā raṇe ।। asakṛd baladevena bāhuyuddhe parājitaḥ ।।
sāmbo jāmbavatīputro nagare nāgasāhvaye ।। rājabhiḥ sarvato ruddho haramāṇo balāt kila । tataś cukrodha balavān adbhutaṃ cākaron mahat ।। lāṅgalāstraṃ samudyamya brahmadaṇḍānumantritam ।।
prakṣeptum aicchad gaṅgāyāṃ nagaraṃ kauravasya tat ।। sāmbaṃ niryātayām āsa sabhāryaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ ।। gadāyuddhe kurupatiḥ pratijagrāha taṃ ca saḥ ।। āvarjitam ivābhāti gaṅgām abhimukhaṃ nṛpa ।।
bhāṇḍīre kathyate rājan yat kṛtaṃ śauriṇā purā ।। dhenukaṃ ca mahākāyaṃ cikṣepa nagamūrdhani ।। sa gatāsuḥ papātorvyāṃ daityo gardabharūpadhṛk । nagaram abhimukhā yad āhṛtā halavidhṛtā yamunā yamasvasā ।।
anantasyāprameyasya śeṣyasya sumahātmanaḥ ।। yad akathitam ihādya karma te tad upalabhasva purāṇavistarāt ।। ālolatulasīmālam ārūḍhavinatāsutam । jyotirindīvaraśyāmam āvir astu mamāgrataḥ । akarod yan mahābāhus tan me vada mahāmune ।।
dvārakāṃ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ pratyavaikṣata vīryavān ।। yathārhaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣo nairṛtān pratyapādayat ।। tāñ jaghāna mahābāhur varadattān mahāsurān ।। trāsanaḥ surasaṃghānāṃ devarājaripur mahān ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca pratīpam akarot tadā ।। gajarūpeṇa jagrāha rucirāṅgīṃ caturdaśīm ।। naṣṭaśokabhayo mohāt prāgjyotiṣapatis tadā ।। bibharti ca mahī kṛtsnā sāgareṣu ca yad vasu ।।
mamaivopahariṣyanti daityāś ca saha dānavaiḥ ।। saṃjahāra tadā bhaumas tac ca nādhicacāra saḥ ।। yāś ca devamanuṣyāṇāṃ sapta cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।। ekaveṇīdharāḥ sarvāḥ satāṃ mārgam anuvratāḥ ।।
alakāyām adīnātmā murasya viṣayaṃ prati ।। nairṛtāś ca yathāmukhyāḥ pālayanta upāsate ।। aditiṃ dharṣayām āsa kuṇḍalārthe mahāsuraḥ ।। ye hi devamanuṣyeṣu kuṇḍale te śubhe ubhe ।
kṛtapūrvaṃ tadā ghoraṃ yad akārṣīn mahāsuraḥ ।। tasyāntapālāś catvāras tasyāsan yuddhadurmadāḥ ।। muruḥ putrasahasraiś ca varadatto mahāsuraḥ ।। aditiṃ dharṣayām āsa so asuro madadarpitaḥ ।
vitrāsanaḥ sukṛtināṃ virūpai rākṣasaiḥ saha ।। jāto vṛṣṇiṣu devakyāṃ vasudevāj janārdanaḥ ।। nivāso dhārakā devair upāyād upapāditā ।। mahārṇavaparikṣiptā pañcaparvataśobhitā ।।
tasyaiva devadevasya nirmitā viśvakarmaṇā । sudāśārhīti vikhyātā yojanāyutavistṛtā ।। lokayātrām imāṃ kṛtsnāṃ parirakṣanta āsate ।। narakasya vadhaṃ sarve cintayantas tadāsate ।
divyagandho vavau vāyuḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ papāta ha ।। muhūrtam antarikṣe abhūt tato bhūmau pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। vṛto devagaṇaiḥ sarvair vāsavaḥ pratyadṛśyata ।। pīḍito narakeṇājau lokapālasamanvitaḥ । icchan rakṣāṃ jagannāthād yādavād nāmasaṃyutāt । hananaṃ ca tathā viṣṇor narakasya durātmanaḥ ।। āgataṃ taṃ vṛtrahaṇaṃ pīḍitaṃ dānavottamaiḥ ।
pratyudyayur mahātmānaṃ pūjayantaḥ sureśvaram ।। pradyumnam atha deveśas tatputraṃ ca mahādyutim । vṛṣṇīn anyān sasvaje ca yathā sthānaṃ yathā vayaḥ ।। arghyādisamudācāraṃ pratyagṛhṇād yathāvidhi ।।
arghyādibhis tathā rājan madhuparkeṇa vṛtrahā । āsanaṃ lambhayām āsa svātmatulyaṃ śacīpatiḥ । sāntvapūrvaṃ kareṇāsya saṃspṛṣan vadanaṃ śubham ।। yena tvābhigato asmy adya kāryeṇāmitrakarśana ।। bādhate no hṛṣīkeśa lokapālān samantataḥ ।
svargaśreṇiṃ vihāyāśu nirgatāḥ sma vayaṃ diśaḥ । adityāḥ kuṇḍale mohāj jahāra ditinandanaḥ ।। nāhaṃ śaknomi taṃ jetuṃ tasmāt tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । tava caivāntaraprekṣī jahi taṃ pāpapūruṣam ।।
kāmavīryo atitejasvī vainateyo antarikṣagaḥ ।। niṣūdayitvā taṃ pāpaṃ kṣipram āgantum arhasi ।। pratijajñe mahābāhur narakasya nibarhaṇam ।। idaṃ provāca śakraṃ taṃ keśavaḥ keśisūdanaḥ । etad artham ihāgamya munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।। badarīvāsinaḥ śakra mām uktvā nirgatā hare ।। abhayaṃ ca mayā deva dattaṃ tebhyaḥ śatakrato । tad artham udyato deva taṃ hantuṃ dānavaṃ raṇe ।। tad artham āgato deva garuḍaḥ pakṣipuṃgavaḥ । kāmarūpo atitejasvī vainateyo antarikṣagaḥ ।
narakasya vadhārthāya yayau vai sa hi keśavaḥ । pratasthe garuḍenātha satyabhāmāsahāyavān ।। paśyatāṃ yadusiṃhānām ūrdhvam ācakrame balī ।। vidūrasthau prakāśete sūryācandramasāv iva ।।
stūyamāno yathā śakraḥ krameṇāntaradhīyata ।। svam eva bhavanaṃ prāyāt kṛṣṇaḥ prāgjyotiṣaṃ yayau ।। pakṣānilahato vāyuḥ pratilomaṃ vavau tadā ।। tato bhīmaravair meghair babhramur gaganecarāḥ । kṣaṇena samanuprāpto divam ākāśagena vai ।। dūrād eva ca tān dṛṣṭvā prayayau yatra te sthitāḥ । apaśyat parvatadvāri hastyaśvarathavāhanam । ārakṣakān mahārāja narakasya durātmanaḥ । pradadhmau devadeveśaḥ pāñcajanyaṃ mahāsvanam ।
kṣurāntān mauravān pāśān ṣaṭsahasrān dadarśa ha ।। garuḍasyopari śrīmāñ chaṅkhacakragadāsibhṛt । bibhran nīlāmbudākāraṃ pītavāsāś caturbhujaḥ ।। vanamālākuloraskaḥ śrīvatsendunibhorasaḥ । kirīṭamūrdhā sūryābhaḥ savidyud iva candramāḥ । jyāṃ vikūjan mahāśabdaḥ śrūyate aśaninisvanaḥ ।। jñātvā ca dānavaḥ sarvaṃ svayaṃ viṣṇur ihāgataḥ । krodhād rudhiraraktākṣo muraḥ kālāntakaprabhaḥ ।। abhyadhāvata vegena śaktiṃ gṛhya mahāsuraḥ । cikṣepa ca mahāśaktiṃ vajrakāñcanabhūṣitām ।। tām āpatantīṃ śaktiṃ tu maholkāṃ jvālitām iva । samādhatta śaraṃ caiva rukmapuṅkhaṃ janārdanaḥ ।। dvidhācchinat kṣurapreṇa vāsudevaḥ sa vīryavān । śaktiṃ ciccheda tatrāsau vidyutpuñja iva jvalan ।। punas tu krodharaktākṣo murur gṛhya mahāgadām । indrāśanir ivendreṇa visṛṣṭa iva nisvanaḥ ।। ākarṇamuktaṃ cikṣepa ardhacandraṃ surottamaḥ । madhyadeśe tu ciccheda gadāṃ tāṃ rukmabhūṣitām । punaś ciccheda bhallena dānavasya śiro raṇe । sa piśācagaṇaṃ sarvaṃ jaghāna yudhi keśavaḥ । niyutaṃ cārbudaṃ caiva sa murasya durātmanaḥ ।। ācchidya pāśān sarvāṃs tān mureṇa saha saṃgataḥ । sa muro dānavo rājan dadarśa yadunandanam । siṃhanādaṃ tataś cakre gadayā taṃ jaghāna ha । garuḍaṃ ca samājaghne mūrdhni deśe mahāsuraḥ । keśavaṃ pothayām āsa prāsaśaktyṛṣṭitomaraiḥ । tataḥ kruddho hṛṣīkeśaḥ kṣurapreṇāharac chiraḥ । tasya dānavamukhyasya dadhmau śaṅkhaṃ tadā hariḥ ।। kṣubdhāś ca dānavāḥ sarve tena śabdena parvatāḥ । bhagavān devakīsutaḥ । apaśyad dānavaṃ sainyaṃ ।
hayagrīvaṃ ca ditijaṃ tathānyāṃś citrayodhinaḥ । rodhayām āsa tan mārgaṃ svasainyena mahābalaḥ ।। nisundo balināṃ śreṣṭho ratham āruhya satvaram । jagrāha kārmukaṃ divyaṃ hemapṛṣṭhaṃ durāsadam ।।
vivyādha daśabhir bāṇair nisundo madhusūdanam । keśavaś cāpi saptatyā vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ । aprāptāṃś cāntarikṣe tāñ śarāṃś ciccheda mādhavaḥ ।। te sarve sainikāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ samantāt paryavārayan ।
śarajālena mahatā chādyamānaḥ surottamaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā tān dānavān sarvān sakrodho madhusūdanaḥ । tato divyena cāstreṇa pārjanyena janārdanaḥ । mahatā śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa tad balam ।।
pañcapañcaśarais teṣu ekaikena ca tān bahūn । pārjanyasya prabhāveṇa sarvān marmasv atāḍayat । dudruvur bhayasaṃtrastā bhagnās te dānavā raṇe ।। svasainyaṃ vidrutaṃ dṛṣṭvā niścakrāma punar mṛdhe ।
visṛjañ śaravarṣāṇi chādayām āsa keśavam ।। na vibhāti raṇe sūryo nāpi vyoma diśo daśa । śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa nisundo garuḍadhvajam ।। sāvitraṃ nāma divyāstraṃ jagrāha puruṣottamaḥ ।
tena bāṇena tān bāṇāṃś ciccheda samare hariḥ ।। bāṇair bāṇāṃs tu saṃchidya tasya kṛṣṇo mahābalaḥ । chatram ekena bāṇena ratheṣāṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ । punaś ciccheda tān aśvāṃś caturbhiś caturaḥ śaraiḥ ।।
sārathiṃ pañcabhir bāṇair dhvajam ekena cicchide । śaraikena punaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sutīkṣṇena śitena vai । śiraś ciccheda bhallena nisundasya surottamaḥ ।। sa mamāra mahādaityaḥ papāta ca mahītale ।
nisundaṃ tu gadāpāṇim āpatantaṃ raṇājire ।। tataḥ śārṅgavinirmuktaiḥ śarair vivyādha keśavaḥ । nisundo api mahārāja gadayāpothayadd harim ।। satyabhāmā tataḥ kruddhā gadayā bāhumuktayā ।
prāharad dānavendraṃ taṃ keśavasyaiva paśyataḥ ।। tatas tuṣṭo hṛṣīkeśaḥ satyabhāmām udaikṣata । sa tayā gadayā viddha udvamañ śoṇitaṃ bahu । muhyan saṃjñām avāpyātha nisundas tv abhyadhāvata ।
tataḥ kruddho hṛṣīkeśas taṃ jaghāna śilīmukhaiḥ । yaḥ sahasrasamās tv ekaḥ sarvān devān apothayat ।। nisundaṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā hayagrīvaḥ pratāpavān । śilāṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ tolayām āsa dānavaḥ ।। āvidhya sahasā yuktaḥ śilāṃ śailasamaprabhaḥ । gṛhītvā divyapārjanyam astram astravidāṃ varaḥ ।। divyāstreṇa śilāṃ viṣṇuḥ saptadhākṛta tejasā । tad vidārya mahac cāśma pātayām āsa bhūtale । tataḥ kruddho hayagrīvaḥ saṃdadhe dhanuṣi kṣuram । tataḥ kruddho hayagrīvaś cāpam ādāya cāparam । keśavaṃ vividhaiś cāstrair ājaghāna tadā yudhi । tac cāpi ca dhanuś chitvā pātayām āsa keśavaḥ । nānāpraharaṇākīrṇaṃ tathā ghoram avartata ।।
garuḍastho mahābāhur nijaghāna mahāsurān ।। vineśur dānavās tatra samāsādya janārdanam ।। saṃnikarṣagatāḥ kecid gatāsuvikṛtānanāḥ ।। garuḍasya hatāḥ pakṣaiḥ kecin mathitamastakāḥ । kecid dhanuḥprahāraiś ca pātitā dharaṇītale । kecit talanipātaiś ca pakṣapātaiś ca pakṣiṇaḥ । asṛjañ śaravarṣāṇi vṛṣṭimanta ivāmbudāḥ । vikṛtāṅgāsurāḥ sarve kṛṣṇabāṇaprapīḍitāḥ ।। śoṇitāktāś ca dṛśyante puṣpitā iva kiṃśukāḥ । vyadravanta suvitrastā bhagnāstrāś citrayodhinaḥ ।। punaś ca krodharaktākṣo vāyuvegena dānavaḥ । daśavyāmocchritaṃ vṛkṣaṃ samāruhya vanaspatim । vṛkṣam utpāṭya vegena pratigṛhyābhyadhāvata ।। cikṣepa sumahāvṛkṣaṃ śikṣayā tu ghanākṛtiḥ । vṛkṣavegāniloddhūtaḥ śuśruve sumahāsvanaḥ ।। tataḥ śarasahasreṇa tvaramāṇo janārdanaḥ । naikadhā taṃ praciccheda citrabhaktinibhākṛtim ।। punaś caikena bāṇena hayagrīvasya corasi । vivyādha stanayor madhye sāyako jvalanaprabhaḥ । viveśa so ativegena hṛdaṃ bhittvā vinirgataḥ ।
apāratejā durdharṣaḥ sarvayādavanandanaḥ ।। alakāyāṃ virūpākṣaṃ pāpmānaṃ puruṣottamaḥ ।। bāhyaprākāramadhye tu jaghāna puruṣottamaḥ । bhagavañ śrotum icchāmi vistareṇa kathām imām ।
avadhīn narakaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kathaṃ vada tapodhana । taṃ ca pañcajanaṃ ghoraṃ narakasya mahāsuram ।। puram āsādayām āsa tatra yuddham abhūn mahat ।। tataḥ prādhmāyac chaṅkhaṃ pāñcajanyaṃ mahābalaḥ । śuśruve sumahāśabdaḥ saṃvartaninado yathā ।। śrūyate triṣu lokeṣu bhīmagambhīranisvanaḥ । taṃ śrutvā narakaś cāsīt krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ ।। lohacakrāṣṭasaṃyuktaṃ trinalvapratimaṃ ratham ।। ratnakāñcanacitrāḍhyaṃ vedikābhogavistaram ।। vajradhvajena mahatā kāñcanena virājitam । hemadaṇḍapatākāḍhyaṃ vaidūryamaṇikūbaram ।। yuktam aśvasahasreṇa rathaṃ pararathārujam । lohajālaiś ca saṃchannaṃ citrabhaktivirājitam ।। rathamadhyagato vīraḥ sasaṃdhya iva bhāskaraḥ । nānāpraharaṇākīrṇaṃ rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam ।। vajraṃ tathoraśchadam induvarṇaṃ ।vyānaddhamuktānalatulyatejāḥ ।kirīṭamūrdhārkahutāśanābhaḥ ।karṇau tathā kuṇḍalayor jvalantau ।।dhūmravarṇā mahākāyā raktākṣā vikṛtānanāḥ । nānākavacinaḥ sarve daityadānavarākṣasāḥ ।। khaṅgacarmadharāḥ kecit kecit tūṇīrasaṃvṛtāḥ । śaktihastās tathā kecic chūlahastās tathāpare ।। gajavājirathaughaiś ca cālayantaś ca medinīm । niryayur nagarāc chūrāḥ susaṃnaddhāḥ prahāriṇaḥ ।। vṛto daityagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ narakaḥ kālasaṃnibhaḥ ।। bherīśaṅkhamṛdaṅgānāṃ paṇavānāṃ sahasraśaḥ । vādyamānān sa śuśrāva jīmūtaninadopamam ।। yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato gatvā sarve te vikṛtānanāḥ । parivārya garutmantaṃ sarve ayudhyanta saṃgatāḥ । mahatā chādayām āsuḥ śaravarṣeṇa sainikāḥ ।। śaktiśūlagadāprāsāṃs tomarān sāyakān bahūn । ākāśaṃ chādayām āsur vimuñcantaḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇāmbudākāraḥ śārṅgaṃ gṛhya dhanus tataḥ । visphārya sumahaccāpaṃ dhanur jaladanisvanam ।। vyasṛjac charavarṣāṇi dānavānāṃ janārdanaḥ । śaravarṣeṇa tat sainyaṃ vyadravat tu mahāhavāt ।। tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ ghorarūpeṇa rakṣasā ।। bhagnavyūhāś ca te sarve kṛṣṇabāṇaprapīḍitāḥ । kecic chinnabhujāś caiva cchinnagrīvā śirānanāḥ । kecic cakradvidhācchinnāḥ kecid bāṇārditorasaḥ ।। kecid dvidhākṛtāḥ śaktyā gajāśvarathavāhanāḥ । kecit kaumodakībhinnāḥ kecic cakravidāritāḥ ।। evaṃ vipothitā sarvā gajāśvarathavāhinī ।
yat samāsena vakṣyāmi tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।। yodhayām āsa tejasvī madhuvanmadhusūdanam ।। krodharaktākṣavadano narakaḥ kālasaṃnibhaḥ । jagrāha kārmukaṃ vīraḥ śakracāpam ivocchritam ।। tathārkakiraṇaprakhyaṃ bāṇaṃ jagrāha keśavaḥ । divyenāstreṇa samare pūrayām āsa taṃ ratham ।। uttamāstraṃ mahāpātaṃ mumoca narako balī ।। vajravisphūrjitākāram āyāntaṃ vīkṣya keśavaḥ । cicchedāstraṃ mahābhāgaś cakreṇa puruṣottamaḥ ।। vyahanat sārathiṃ cāsya śaraikeṇa jarārdanaḥ । sarathaṃ sadhvajaṃ sāśvaṃ jaghāna daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। tanutraṃ caiva ciccheda śareṇa madhusūdanaḥ । tato vimuktakavacaḥ sarpasyeva tanur yathā ।। hatāśvo viratho vīro vitanutraś ca dānavaḥ । jagrāha vimalajvālaṃ lohabhārārpitaṃ dṛḍham । āvidhya sahasā muktaṃ śūlam indrāśaniprabham ।। tadāpatat tu saṃprekṣya śūlaṃ hemapariṣkṛtam । dvidhā chinnaṃ kṣurapreṇa kṛṣṇenādbhutakarmaṇā । tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ ghorarūpeṇa rakṣasā । śastrapātamahāghātaṃ narakeṇa mahātmanā । athogracakraś cakreṇa pradīptenākarod dvidhā ।।
vibhaktaṃ krakaceneva gireḥ śṛṅgaṃ dvidhā kṛtam ।। kṛṣṇam āsādya deveśaṃ jagāmāstam ivāṃśumān ।। cakrotkṣiptanikṛttāṅgam uttamaṃ patitaṃ raṇe । vajreṇeva vinirbhinnaṃ yathā gairikaparvatam । taṃ hatvā narakaṃ bhaumaṃ viṣṇur yādavanandanaḥ । mumude tripuraṃ hatvā pureva tripurāntakaḥ । upātiṣṭhata govindaṃ vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।। yathecchasi tathā krīḍa bālaḥ krīḍanakair iva ।
ime te kuṇḍale deva prajās tasyānupālaya ।। nirvighnam ṛṣayo devāś carantu vigatajvarāḥ । prajāś carantu sukhinas tava deva prapālanāt । nirvighnaṃ brāhmaṇā deva bhūyāsus tava śāsanāt । ityuktvā sā dadau tasmai kuṇḍale lokaviśrute । antardhānaṃ gatā devī tadā bhartṛsamīpataḥ । vāsavāvarajo viṣṇur dadarśa narakālayam ।। dadarśa dhanam akṣayyaṃ ratnāni vividhāni ca ।।
mahārajatakūṭāni tathā vajrasya saṃcayān ।। śayanāni mahārhāṇi tathā siṃhāsanāni ca ।। dadarśa ca mahac chatraṃ varṣamāṇam ivāmbudam ।। varuṇād āhṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ narakeṇeti naḥ śrutam ।।
ratnasaṃnicyas tādṛg dṛṣṭapūrvo na ca śrutaḥ ।। upaninyus tatas tāni ratnāny antaḥpurāṇi ca ।। keśavāya mahārhāṇi yāny arhati janārdanaḥ ।। bhīmarūpāś ca mātaṅgāḥ pravālavikṛtāṅkuśāḥ ।।
rucirābhiḥ patākābhir vasānā vividhāḥ kuthāḥ ।। aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi deśajāś cottamā hayāḥ ।। tāvatīḥ prāpayiṣyāmo vṛṣṇyandhakaniveśanam ।। kāmavyāhāriṇaś caiva pakṣiṇaḥ priyadarśanāḥ ।।
prāpayiṣyāma tat sarvaṃ vṛṣṇyandhakaniveśanam ।। tāni santīha sarvāṇi narakasya niveśane ।। iti vijñāpitas tais tu dānavaiś ca janārdanaḥ । sarvam āhārayāmāsa dānavair dvārakāṃ purīm ।।
hiraṇyavarṣaṃ varṣantam āruroha vihaṃgatam ।। tato abhyayād giriśreṣṭham abhito maṇiparvatam ।। maṇīnāṃ hemavarṇānām abhibhūya divākaram ।। satoraṇapatākāni dvārāṇi śayanāni ca ।।
hemacitravimānaiś ca prāsādair upaśobhitaḥ ।। gandharvāsuramukhyānāṃ priyā duhitaras tathā ।। narakeṇa samānītā rakṣyamāṇāḥ samantataḥ ।। nivasantyo yathā devyaḥ sukhinyaḥ kāmavarjitāḥ ।।
sarvāḥ kāṣāyavāsinyaḥ sarvāś ca niyatendriyāḥ ।। sametya yadusiṃhasya sarvāś cakruḥ striyo añjalīn ।। hayagrīvaṃ nisundaṃ ca tāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ paryavārayan ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve praṇipetur vayodhikāḥ ।।
sarvāsām eva saṃkalpaḥ patitvenābhavat tataḥ ।। saṃprahṛṣṭā mahābāhum idaṃ vacanam abruvan ।। sarvabhūtarutajñaś ca devarṣir api nāradaḥ ।। sa bhaumaṃ narakaṃ hatvā bhartā ca bhavitā hi saḥ ।।
darśanena kṛtārthā hi vayam adya mahātmanaḥ ।। sarvāḥ kamalapatrākṣīr dṛṣṭyā vācā ca mādhavaḥ ।। yānaiḥ kiṃkarasaṃyuktair uvāha madhusūdanaḥ ।। śibikāṃ vahatāṃ tatra nirghoṣaḥ sumahān abhūt ।।
vimalārkendusaṃkāśaṃ maṇikāñcanatoraṇam ।। śākhāmṛgagaṇair juṣṭaṃ suprastaraśilātalam ।। saprapātamahāsānuṃ vicitraśikharadrumam ।। jīvaṃjīvakasaṃghaiś ca barhibhiś ca nināditam ।।
āropayāmāsa tadā garuḍe pakṣiṇāṃ vare ।। uvāha līlayā pakṣī garuḍaḥ patatāṃ varaḥ ।। dikṣu sarvāsu saṃhrādaṃ janayāmāsa pakṣirāṭ ।। saṃjahāra mahābhrāṇi vijahāra ca kānicit ।।
yayau vātajavaḥ pakṣī janārdanavaśe sthitaḥ ।। devasadmāni sarvāṇi dadarśa madhusūdanaḥ ।। bhrājamānāny atikrāmad aśvinoś ca paraṃtapaḥ ।। śakrasadma samāsādya praviveśa janārdanaḥ ।।
prītaś caivābhyanandat taṃ devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ ।। sabhāryo vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ naraśreṣṭho janārdanaḥ ।। satyabhāmā ca paulomyā yathāvad abhinanditā ।। āśliṣyete mahārāja te devyau lokaviśrute ।। idaṃ provāca paulomī satyabhāmāṃ haripriyām । prītāsmi darśanād devi kiṃ bhūyaḥ karavāṇi te । diṣṭyā hato bhavatyā tu narako duṣṭacetanaḥ । ity uktā sā tadā devī kṛtam ity abravīc ca tām ।
adityā bhavanaṃ puṇyaṃ devamātur maharddhimat ।। dadṛśāte mahātmānau mahābhāgāṃ taponvitām ।। janārdanaṃ puraskṛtya kama caiva śaśaṃśa tat ।। pradāyāditinandanaḥ ।vavande tāṃ śacībhartā mātaraṃ svāṃ puraṃdaraḥ ।
āśirbhir anurūpābhir ubhāv abhyavadat tadā ।। agṛhṇītāṃ varārhāyā devyāś ca caraṇau śubhau ।। yathāvad abravīc caiva janārdanam idaṃ vacaḥ ।। yathaiva devarājo ayam ajito lokapūjitaḥ ।।
tava ceyaṃ varārohā nityaṃ ca priyadarśanā । sarvalokeṣu vikhyātā divyagandhā manoramā । tatpurogamadevānām adhipas tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi । jarāṃ na yāsyati vadhūr yāvat tvaṃ kṛṣṇa mānuṣaḥ ।। devarājābhyanujñāto ratnaiś ca pratipūjitaḥ ।। devākrīḍān parikrāman pūjyamānaḥ surarṣibhiḥ ।।
divyam abhyarcitaṃ caityaṃ pārijātaṃ mahādrumam ।। yam āsādya janaḥ sarvo jātiṃ smarati paurvikīm ।। utpāṭyāropayāmāsa viṣṇus taṃ vai mahādrumam ।। pṛṣṭhataḥ satyabhāmā ca divyā yoṣābhivīkṣitā ।
tataḥ prāyād dvāravatīṃ vāyujuṣṭena vai pathā ।। anumene mahābāhuḥ kṛtaṃ karmeti cābravīt ।। pratasthe dvārakāṃ kṛṣṇo devalokād ariṃdamaḥ ।। āsasāda mahābāhuḥ purīṃ dvāravatīṃ tadā ।
pūjito devarājena dadṛśe yādavīṃ purīm ।। hatvā tu narakaṃ bhaumaṃ dattvā kuṇḍalam uttamam । hṛtvā taṃ pārijātaṃ ca praṇamya suramātaram । upāyād dvārakāṃ viṣṇuḥ śrīmān garuḍavāhanaḥ ।। devasadmapratīkāśāṃ samantāt pratināditām ।।
tathā krīḍāgṛhāṇi ca । udyānavanamukhyāni valabhīcatvarāṇi ca । saṃprāpte tu tadā kṛṣṇe । viśvakarmāṇam āhūya devarājo abravīd idam ।।
kṛṣṇapriyārthaṃ bhūyas tvaṃ kariṣyasi manoharām ।। kuruṣva vibudhaśreṣṭha yathā mama purī tathā ।। tena saṃyujyatāṃ kṣipraṃ purī dvāravatī tvayā ।। saṃgrāmān ghorarūpāṃś ca vigāhati mahābalaḥ ।।
alaṃcakre samantād vai yathendrasyāmarāvatī ।। viśvakarmakṛtair divyair abhiprāyair alaṃkṛtām ।। hṛṣṭaḥ sarvārthasaṃpannaḥ praveṣṭum upacakrame ।। dvārakāṃ prati dāśārhaś citritāṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।।
gaṅgāsindhuprakāśābhiḥ parikhābhir vṛtāṃ purīm ।। cayamūrdhni niviṣṭena dyāṃ yathaivābhramālayā ।। babhau cāruparikṣiptā dvārakā dyaur ivāmbubhiḥ ।। pūrvasyāṃ diśi lakṣmīvān maṇikāñcanatoraṇaḥ ।।
indraketupratīkāśaḥ paścimasyāṃ tathākṣayaḥ ।। citrakānanaramyaś ca pañcānananiṣevitaḥ । mandarādripratīkāśaḥ pāṇḍuraḥ pārthivarṣabha ।। sarvartukavanaṃ caiva bhāti raivatakaṃ prati ।।
bhāti bhārgavanaṃ caiva puṣpakaṃ ca mahad vanam ।। śatāvartavanaṃ caiva karavīrakarambhi ca ।। ramaṇaṃ bhāvanaṃ caiva veṇumad vai samantataḥ ।। bhāti puṣkariṇī ramyā pūrvasyāṃ diśi bhārata ।।
bahubhir devagandharvaiś coditair viśvakarmaṇā ।। praviṣṭā puṇyasalilā bhāvayantī samantataḥ ।। prākāravarasaṃpannāṃ sudhāpāṇḍuralepanām ।। āyasaiś ca mahācakrair dadṛśe dvārakāṃ purīm ।।
samucchritapatākāni yathā devapure tathā ।। dviguṇopaniveśāṃ ca dadṛśe dvārakāṃ purīm ।। striyo api yasyāṃ yudhyeran kim u vṛṣṇimahārathāḥ ।। tasmin puravaraśreṣṭhe dāśārhāṇāṃ yaśasvinām ।।
kāñcanair maṇisopānair upetāni nṛharṣaṇaiḥ ।। samucchritapatākāni pāriplavanibhāni ca ।। ramyasānuguhāśṛṅgair vicitrair iva parvataiḥ ।। prāsādaśikharāṇi ca ।gṛhāṇi ramaṇīyāni ।
parjanyatulyanirghoṣair nānārūpair ivādribhiḥ ।। ālikhadbhir ivākāśam aticandrārkabhāsvaraiḥ ।। vāsudevendraparjanyair gṛhameghair alaṃkṛtā ।। sākṣād bhagavato veśma vihitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।।
tāvad eva ca vistīrṇam aprameyaṃ mahādhanaiḥ ।। yaś cakāra mahābhāgas tvaṣṭā vāsavacoditaḥ ।। rukmiṇyāḥ pravaraṃ vāsaṃ vihitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।। vimalādityavarṇābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtam ।।
prabhayābhyabhavat sarvāṃs tān anyān bhāskaro yathā ।। viśvakarmakṛto divyaḥ kailāsaśikharopamaḥ ।। sāgarapratimas tiṣṭhan merur ity abhiviśrutaḥ ।। gāndhārī bharataśreṣṭha keśavena niveśitā ।।
subhīmāyā mahākūṭaṃ vāsaṃ suparamārcitam ।। lakṣmaṇāyāḥ kuruśreṣṭha nirdiṣṭaḥ śārṅgadhanvanā ।। yaṃ viduḥ sarvabhūtāni param ity eva bhārata ।। mahiṣyā vāsudevasya bhūṣaṇaṃ teṣu veśmasu ।।
atīva saumyaḥ so apy āsīd viṣṭhitaḥ parvato yathā ।। mahiṣyā vāsudevasya ketumān iti viśrutaḥ ।। yojanāyataviṣkambhaḥ sarvaratnamayaḥ śubhaḥ ।। upasthānagṛhaṃ yatra keśavasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
ratnajālāni tatraiva tatra tatra niveśitāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭitālasamutsedham ardhayojanam āyatam ।। paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānām ānītaṃ lokaviśrutam ।। tad apy utpāṭya kṛṣṇārtham ānītaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।।
pārijātas tu tatraiva keśavenāhṛtaḥ svayam ।। puṇḍarīkaśatair juṣṭaṃ vimānaiś ca hiraṇmayaiḥ ।। maṇihemaplavākīrṇāḥ puṣkariṇyaḥ sarāṃsi ca ।। sālās tālāḥ kadambāś ca śataśākhāś ca rohiṇāḥ ।।
āhṛtya yadusiṃhārthaṃ vihitā viśvakarmaṇā ।। sarvartuphalasaṃpannās teṣu kānanasaṃdhiṣu ।। tasmin puravare nadyaḥ prasannasalilā hradāḥ ।। aparāś cābhavan nadyo hemaśarkaravālukāḥ ।।
nīlotpalavibhūṣitāḥ । nadyaḥ padmacayodbhāsaḥ । bahūvuḥ paramopetās tasyāṃ puryāṃ tu pādapāḥ ।। nivāsaś ca kṛtas tatra varāhamṛgapakṣiṇām ।। vyaktaṃ kiṣkuśatotsedho vihito viśvakarmaṇā ।।
parikṣiptāni bhaumena vanāny upavanāni ca ।। prāsādāś caiva saṃvītā lokālokaviśāradāḥ । tasyaiva yadusiṃ hasya bhavanāl lokaviśrutāt ।। tasmād abhyadhikaṃ sadma vihitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā । rāmasya yadusiṃhasya śobhate atimanoharam । apaśyat svagṛhaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prāsādaśataśobhitam ।। tatra tatra prabhāsadbhiś citrakāñcanavedikaiḥ ।।
sphāṭikastambhavidhṛto vistīrṇaḥ sarvakāñcanaḥ ।। maṇihemanibhāś citrā ratnasopānabhūṣitāḥ ।। babhūvuḥ paramopetā vāpyaś ca vikacotpalāḥ ।। vyaktakiṣkuśatotsedhaḥ parikhāyūthaveṣṭitaḥ ।।
mahendraveśmapratimaṃ samantād ardhayojanam ।। prītaḥ śaṅkham upādhmāsīd dviṣatāṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।। rarāsa ca nabhaḥ kṛtsnaṃ tac citram abhacat tadā ।। viśokāḥ samapadyanta garuḍasya ca darśanāt ।।
dṛṣṭvā jahṛṣire bhaumā bhāskaropamatejasam ।। siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe sarveṣāṃ puravāsinām ।। prīyamāṇāḥ samājagmur ālokya madhusūdanam ।। ugraseno yayau rājā vāsudevaniveśanam ।।
rohiṇī ca yathoddeśam āhukasya ca yāḥ striyaḥ ।। cacāra ca yathoddeśam īśvarānucaro hariḥ ।। yathārhaṃ pūjayām āsa yādavān yādavarṣabhaḥ ।। praviveśa gṛhaṃ śaurir ādāya maṇiparvatam ।।
praveśayām āsa gṛhaṃ pradyumno rukmiṇīsutaḥ ।। pārijātaprabhāvena tato mumudire janāḥ ।। praviveśa gṛhaṃ śrīmān vihitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।। nyaveśayad ameyātmā vṛṣṇibhiḥ sahito acyutaḥ ।।
arcyam arcitam avyagram iṣṭe deśe nyaveśayat ।। tāḥ striyaḥ pūjayām āsa saṃkṣiptā narakeṇa yāḥ ।। hāraiś candrāṃśusaṃkāśair maṇibhiś ca mahāprabhaiḥ ।। bhūṣaṇair vividhair api ।gandhaiś ca vividhair divyair ।
vedakyā saha rohiṇyā revatyā cāhukena ca ।। kuṭumbasyeśvarī tv āsīd rukmiṇī bhīṣmakātmajā ।। sarvakāryasamādhyakṣā keśavasyātivallabhā । ādideśa gṛhān kṛṣṇaḥ paribarhāṃś ca puṣkalān ।।
satyabhāmā sadā viṣṇoḥ pārśvasthā saṃsadi priyā । sakhivac copagṛhyainam anujajñe gṛhaṃ prati ।। ūrdhvam ācakrame pakṣī yatheṣṭaṃ gaganecaraḥ ।। kṛtvā vegena mahatā yayau pūrvaṃ mahodadhim ।।
kṛṣṇo dadarśa pitaraṃ vṛddham ānakaduṃdubhim ।। kāśyaṃ sāṃdīpaniṃ caiva brahmagārgyaṃ tathaiva ca ।। ratnapravekair dāśārho vīryalabdhais tadārcayat ।। raṇāt pratinivṛtto ayam akṣato madhusūdanaḥ ।।
prītāś ca munayaḥ sarve rakṣitā yadusattamāḥ । iti prītā yaduvṛṣā vardhayanti janārdanam । cākriko ghoṣayām āsa puruṣo mṛṣṭakuṇḍalaḥ ।। nirvighnaṃ munayo rājaṃś carantu vividhaṃ tapaḥ । nihato narako duṣṭaḥ sānugaḥ sabalānvitaḥ । vavande vṛṣṇinṛpatim āhukaṃ vinayānvitaḥ ।।
vavande saha rāmeṇa pitaraṃ vāsavānujaḥ ।। sarveṣāṃ nāma jagrāha dāśārhāṇām adhokṣajaḥ ।। āsanāgryāṇi viviśur upendrapramukhās tadā ।। sabhāṃ samānayām āsuḥ puruṣāḥ kṛṣṇaśāsanāt ।।
sarvān duṃdubhiśabdena pūjayiṣyañ janārdanaḥ ।। sudāśārhīṃ sudāśārhā viviśuḥ kṛṣṇaśāsanāt ।। sarvārthaguṇasaṃpannā sā sabhā bharatarṣabha । śuśubhe abhyadhikaṃ śubhrā siṃhair giriguhā yathā ।।
ugrasenaṃ puraskṛtya bheje vṛṣṇipuraskṛtaḥ ।। samābhāṣya yaduśreṣṭhān uvāca madhusūdanaḥ ।। apadhyānāc ca pāpātmā bhaumaḥ sa narako hataḥ ।। maṇiparvatam utpāṭya śikharaṃ caitad āhṛtam ।।
īśā bhavantas tasyeti tān uktvā virarāma ha ।। jahṛṣur hṛṣṭalomānaḥ pūjayanto janārdanam ।। naitac citraṃ mahābāho tvayi devakinandana ।। lālayeḥ svajanaṃ bhogai ratnaiś ca svayam arjitaiḥ ।।
prīyamāṇāḥ sabhāṃ jagmur vāsudevadidṛkṣayā ।। dadṛśuḥ kṛṣṇam āsīnaṃ rāmaṃ caiva mahābhujam ।। abhyavādayatāṃ devau devakīṃ rāmakeśavau ।। aditir devamāteva mitreṇa varuṇena ca ।।
ekānaṃśeti yām āhur narā vai kāmarūpiṇīm ।। yatkṛte sagaṇaṃ kaṃsaṃ jaghāna puruṣottamaḥ ।। putravat pālyamānā vai vāsudevājñayā tadā ।। ekānaṃśeti yām āhur utpannāṃ mānavā bhuvi ।
yogakanyāṃ durādharṣāṃ rakṣārthaṃ keśavasya ca ।। devavad divyavapuṣā krṣṇaḥ saṃrakṣito yayā ।। dakṣiṇena karāgreṇa parijagrāha mādhavaḥ ।। mūrdhny upāghrāya savyena parijagrāha pāṇinā ।।
rukmapadmakaravyagrāṃ śriyaṃ padmālayām iva ।। avakīrya ca lājais tāṃ striyo jagmur yathāgatam ।। upopaviviśuḥ prītāḥ praśaṃsanto adbhutaṃ kṛtam ।। vijahāra mahākīrtir devair iva sa taiḥ saha ।।
niyogāt tridaśendrasya nārado abhyāgamat sabhām ।। kare saṃspṛśya govindaṃ viveśa mahad āsanam ।। tataḥ prāha mahābāhur āhuko nṛpatir munim । mune vācaya kiṃ cid vai purāṇaṃ paramottamam ।। tatheti hariṇā bhūpa harivaṃśasya pustakam । nikṣiptam āsane puṇye nārado avācayat tadā ।। śrotavyo apy uddhavaś cāśu bhūtvā maunam upāśritaḥ । sukhopaviṣṭas tūṣṇīṃ tāṃ nārado avācayat kathāṃ । āgataṃ śakravacanāj jānīdhvaṃ māṃ nararṣabhāḥ ।।
yāni karmāṇi kṛtavān bālyāt prabhṛti keśavaḥ ।। rājyaṃ jagrāha durbuddhir badhvā pitaram āhukam ।। bhojavṛṣṇyandhakān sarvān avamanyata durmatiḥ ।। ugrasenasya rakṣārthaṃ svaputraṃ paryarakṣata ।।
nandagopasya bhavane govrajeṣu ca vardhitaḥ । atyadbhutāni karmāṇi kṛtavān madhusūdanaḥ ।। yathānena śayānena śakaṭāntaracāriṇā ।। viṣadigdhaṃ stanaṃ kṣudrā prayacchantī mahātmane ।।
baleḥ sutāṃ mahāghorāṃ bhīṣaṇāṃ vikṛtānanām । punarjāto ayam ity āhur uktas tasmād adhokṣajaḥ ।। pādāṅguṣṭhena śakaṭaṃ krīḍamāno vyaloḍayat ।। bhakṣayan dadhi govindaḥ payaḥpānaṃ ca sāgrajaḥ ।
ulūkhale parāmṛdgād vṛkṣau satyopacāyinau । dāmodara iti khyāto vasudevasutas tataḥ ।। babhañjārjunavṛkṣau dvau khyāto dāmodaras tataḥ । krīḍatā vāsudevena nirjito yamunāhrade ।।
pūjyamānas tadā nāgair divyaṃ vapur adhārayat ।। śiśunā vāsudevena gavāṃ trāṇārtham icchatā ।। gopatir vāsudevena nihato ariṣṭakaḥ kṣitau ।। nihato vāsudevena gavāṃ trāṇāya durmatiḥ ।।
vṛkair vidrāvayām āsa grahītuṃ samupāgatam ।। gopaveṣadhareṇaiva kaṃsasya bhayam āhṛtam ।। pragrahaṃ bhojarājasya jaghāna puruṣottamaḥ ।। dānavo muṣṭinaikena kaṃsāmātyo nipātitaḥ ।।
vavṛdhāte mahātmānau brahmagārgyeṇa saṃskṛtau ।। yāthātathyena vijñāya saṃskāraṃ pratipāditau ।। siṃhaśāvāv ivodīrṇau mattau haimavatau yathā ।। āstāṃ goṣṭhacarau vīrau devaputrasamadyutī ।।
nandagopasya gopālāḥ śekuḥ pratisamīkṣitum ।। śrutvemau vyathitaḥ kaṃso mantribhiḥ sahito abhavat ।। nijagrāha tataḥ krodhād vasudevaṃ sabāndhavam ।। kālaṃ mahāntam avasat kṛcchram ānakaduṃdubhiḥ ।।
jarāsaṃdhaṃ samāśritya tathaivāhvṛtibhīṣmakau ।। pinākinaṃ samuddiśya kaṃsaś cakre narādhipaḥ ।। nartakā gāyakāś caiva kuśalā nṛttasāmasu ।। kuśalaiḥ kārayām āsa śilpibhiḥ sādhuniṣṭhitaiḥ ।।
samākīrṇāny adṛśyanta jyotirbhir gaganaṃ yathā ।। aruroha tataḥ kaṃso vimānaṃ sukṛtī yathā ।। śūrair adhiṣṭhitaṃ kaṃsaḥ sthāpayām āsa vīryavān ।। śuśrāva puruṣavyāghrau sūryācandramasāv iva ।।
na ca śete sukhaṃ rātrau rāmakṛṣṇau vicintayan ।। ubhau viviśatur vīrau śārdūlau govrajaṃ yathā ।। avamṛdya durādharṣau raṅgaṃ viviśatus tadā ।। augraseniḥ sa duṣṭātmā sānujo vinipātitaḥ ।।
karma tat keśavād anyaḥ kartum arhati kaḥ pumān ।। tad idaṃ śauriṇā cittaṃ prāpitaṃ bhavatām iha ।। śailasaṃghān atikramya nisundaḥ sagaṇo hataḥ ।। prāptaṃ ca divi deveṣu keśavena mahad yaśaḥ ।।
yajantu bahubhir yajñair yādavā vītamatsarāḥ ।। kṣipram āvedaye cedaṃ bhavatāṃ bhadram astu vaḥ ।। bhavatām asmi yūyaṃ ca mama yuṣmāsv ahaṃ sthitaḥ ।। mām apraiṣīt suraśreṣṭhaḥ prītās tuṣṭās tathā vayam ।।
saṃnatir hrīs tathā śrīś ca nityaṃ kṛṣṇe mahātmani ।। hatā brahmadviṣaḥ sarve yajadhvaṃ brāhmaṇāḥ sadā । namaskurudhvaṃ haraye sadā namata mādhavam ।। yajadhvaṃ satataṃ yajñair enaṃ lokanamaskṛtam । āraṇyakāḥ sadā santu bhavatāṃ jñānahetavaḥ । kṛtaḥ kṣemaḥ punaḥ panthāḥ puraṃ prāgjyotiṣaṃ prati ।। bhūyaś ca khalu vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ yādavottamāḥ । yat kṛtaṃ śauriṇā samyag lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।
dhanuṣaś ca ninādena pāñcajanyasvanena ca ।। rukmiṇaṃ yudhi nirjitya mahābalaparākramam । rukmiṇīm ājahārāśu keśavo vṛṣṇipuṃgavaḥ ।। uvāha mahiṣīṃ bhojāṃ śaṅkhacakragadāsibhṛt ।।
vaktraś ca saha sainyena śatadhanvā ca durjayaḥ ।। hataḥ saubhapatiḥ sālvaḥ śaubhaś ca dṛḍhadhanvanā ।। vikīrya puṇḍarīkākṣo dyumatsenam apothayat ।। jaghāna yo naravyāghro rāvaṇasyābhitaś carau ।।
gopatis tālaketuś ca nihatau śārṅgadhanvanā ।। ubhau tāv api kṛṣṇena sarāṣṭrau vinipātitau ।। sānubandhaḥ sarāṣṭraś ca kāśīnām adhipo hataḥ ।। athaindrasenir ānītaḥ kṛṣṇenādbhutakarmaṇā ।।
prāpya lohitakūṭāni kṛṣṇena varuṇo jitaḥ ।। acintayitvā devendraṃ pārijātadrumo hṛtaḥ ।। jaghāna sahitān sarvān vaṅgarājaṃ tathaiva ca ।। gāndhārīm āvahad dhīmān mahiṣīṃ priyadarśanām ।।
jigāya bharata śreṣṭhaṃ kuntyāḥ pramukhato vibhuḥ ।। cakrānuyāte sahitāñ jigāya puruṣottamaḥ ।। sauvīrarājasya sutāṃ prasahya hṛtavān prabhuḥ ।। veṇudārikṛte yatnāj jigāya puruṣottamaḥ ।।
pūrvadehe jahārāyaṃ bales tribhuvanaṃ hariḥ ।। yasya nādhigato mṛtyuḥ puraṃ prāgjyotiṣaṃ prati ।। baleḥ putro mahāvīryo bāṇo draviṇavattaraḥ ।। jarāsaṃdhaṃ mahāvīryaṃ mahotsāhaṃ mahābalam । asakṛj jitavān kṛṣṇo līlayā puruṣottamaḥ ।
paiṭhikaṃ cāsilomānaṃ nijaghāna mahābalaḥ ।। jaghāna puruṣavyāghraḥ śambaraṃ cārimardanaḥ ।। nirjitya puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ preṣayām āsa sāgaram ।। nirjitya puruṣavyāghro yamaṃ vaivasvataṃ hariḥ ।।
evam eṣa mahābāhuḥ śāstā sarvadurātmanām ।। devāṃś ca brāhmaṇāṃś caiva ye dviṣanti sadā nṛpa । daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca rākṣasānāṃ janārdanaḥ । devamātur dadau cāpi prītyarthaṃ vajrapāṇinaḥ ।। prāptaṃ ca divi deveṣu keśavena mahad yaśaḥ ।
bhayābhayakaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sarvalokeśvaro vibhuḥ ।। kṛtvā devārtham amitaṃ svasthānaṃ pratipatsyate ।। dvārakām ātmasātkṛtvā samudraṃ gamayiṣyati ।। dvārakā varuṇāvāsaṃ pravekṣyati sakānanā ।।
visṛṣṭāṃ vāsudevena sāgaraḥ plāvayiṣyati ।। ya imām āvaset kaścid anyatra madhusūdanāt ।। viṣṇur nārāyaṇaḥ somaḥ sūryaś ca bhavitā svayam ।। modaty eṣa sadā bhūtair bālaḥ krīḍanakair iva ।।
pramāṇaṃ hy atra vicchinnaṃ pramāṇaṃ sarvavastuṣu । yato ayaṃ devadeveśo na pramāṇe pramā bhavet । paraṃ hy aparam etasmād viśvarūpān na vidyate ।। anto hi karmaṇām asya dṛṣṭapūrvo na kenacit ।।
kṛtavān puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ saṃkarṣaṇasahāyavān ।। mahāyogī mahābuddhiḥ sarvapratyakṣadarśivān ।। yadubhiḥ pūjitaḥ sarvair nāradas tridivaṃ gataḥ ।। yathārhaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣo vidhivan madhusūdanaḥ ।।
namaskṛtya jagannathaṃ śirasā suprasāriṇā । yajñair iṣṭvā mahātmāno dvārakām āvasan purīm ।। tāsām apatyān yaṣṭānāṃ bhagavān prabravītu me ।। sarvā vīraprajāyinyas tāsv apatyāni me śṛṇu ।।
sudattā ca tathā śaibyā lakṣmaṇā cāruhāsinī ।। subhīmā ca tathā mādrī raukmiṇeyān imāñ śṛṇu ।। dvitīyaś cārudeṣṇaś ca vṛṣṇisiṃho mahārathaḥ ।। cārubāhuḥ kaniṣṭhaś ca kanyā cārumatī tathā ।।
catasro jajñire teṣāṃ svasāro garuḍadhvajāt ।। bhānur bhīmarikā caiva tāmrapakṣā jalaṃdhamā । mitrabāhur mitradhāmā mitrasenas tathaiva ca । mitravān mitravindaś ca mitravaty api cāṅganā ।।
bhadrakāro bhadravindaḥ kanyā bhadravatī tathā ।। satyajit senajic caiva tathā śūraḥ sapatnajit ।। kumāro vṛkadīptiś ca lakṣmaṇāyāḥ prajāḥ śṛṇu ।। jajñire gātravanty ete bhaginyānujayā saha ।।
aśrutaṃ śrutasenāyai pradadau madhusūdanaḥ ।। eṣa vām ubhayor astu dāyādaḥ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ ।। utpannaṃ kumudaṃ caiva śvetaṃ śvetāṃ tathāṅganām ।। citrasenaḥ sute cāsya citrā citravatī tathā ।।
nivāsano vanastambaḥ kanyā stambavatī tathā । upāsaṅgasya tu sutau vajraḥ sukṣipra eva ca ।। kāpālī garuḍaś caiva jajñāte citrayodhinau ।। evamādīni putrāṇāṃ sahastrāṇi nibodhata । ayutaṃ tu samākhyātaṃ vāsudevasya te sutāḥ ।। ayutāni tathā cāṣṭau śūrā raṇaviśāradāḥ । janārdanasya prasavaḥ kīrtito ayaṃ yathā tathā ।
aniruddho raṇe yoddhā jajñe sa mṛgaketanaḥ ।। bhrātarau devasaṃkāśāv ubhau puruṣasattamau ।। pauṇḍraś ca kapilaś caiva vāsudevasya tau sutau ।। tayor nṛpo abhavat pauṇḍraḥ kapilaś ca vanaṃ yayau ।।
samādhisthaḥ sa bhūteṣu dayāṃ kurvan mahāmatiḥ । sa nṛpaḥ samacittātmā viṣṇusāyujyam āptavān । jarā nāma niṣādānāṃ prabhuḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām ।। aniruddhasya vaidarbhyā bhāryā rukmavatī śubhā । tasyāṃ vajro aniruddhasya vajrasya tanayaṃ śṛṇu ।
sānor vajro aniruddhasya vajras tv ādāv ajāyata ।। anamitrāc chinir jajñe kaniṣṭhād vṛṣṇinandanāt ।। satyakasyātmajaḥ śūro yuyudhānas tv ajāyata ।। bhūmer yugaṃdharaḥ putra iti vaṃśaḥ samāpyate ।।
pradyumnaḥ sa kathaṃ jaghne śambaraṃ tad bravīhi me ।। śambarāntakaro jajñe pradyumnaḥ kāmadarśanaḥ ।। sanatkumāra iti yaḥ purāṇe parigīyate । jahāra kṛṣṇasya sutaṃ śiśuṃ vai kālaśambaraḥ ।।
tato na nigṛhītaḥ sa dānavo yuddhadurmadaḥ ।। dorbhyām utkṣipya nagaraṃ svaṃ jagāma mahāsuraḥ ।। nāmnā māyāvatī nāma māyeva śubhadarśana ।। tasyā mahiṣyā nāthinyā dānavaḥ kālacoditaḥ ।।
māyāvatī tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃprahṛṣṭatanūruhā । harṣeṇa mahatā yuktā punaḥ punar udaikṣata ।। atha tasyā nirīkṣantyāḥ smṛtiḥ prādurbabhūva ha । ayaṃ sa mama kānto abhūt smṛtvaivaṃ cānvacintayat ।। ayaṃ sa nātho bhartā me yasyārthaṃ hi divāniśam । cintāśokahrade magnā na vindāmi ratiṃ kvacit ।। ayaṃ bhagavatā pūrvaṃ devadevena śūlinā । kheditena kṛto anaṅgo dṛṣṭo jātyantare mayā ।। katham asya stanaṃ dāsye mātṛbhāvena jānatī । bhartur bhāryā tv ahaṃ bhūtvā vakṣye vā putra ity uta ।। evaṃ saṃcintya manasā dhātryās taṃ sā samarpayat । rasāyanaprayogaiś ca śīghram evānvavardhayat ।। dhātryāḥ sakāśāt sa ca tāṃ śṛṇvan rukmiṇinandanaḥ । māyāvatīm avijñānān mene svām eva mātaram । māyāś cāsmai dadau sarvā dānavīḥ kāmamohitā ।। cikīrṣitajño nārīṇāṃ sarvāstravidhipāragaḥ ।। iṅgitaiś cāpi vīkṣantī prālobhayata sasmitā ।।
mātṛbhāvaṃ parityajya kim evaṃ vartase anyathā ।। yā putrabhāvam utsṛjya mayi kāmāt pravartase ।। tat tvam icchāmy ahaṃ devi kathitaṃ kas tv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।। yā nareṣu prasajjante nagāgreṣu ghanā iva ।।
kathitaṃ tat tvam icchāmi kim idaṃ te cikīrṣitam ।। priyaṃ provāca vacanaṃ vivikte keśavātmajam ।। putras tvaṃ vāsudevasya rukmiṇyā nandivardhanaḥ ।। sūtikāgāramadhyāt tvaṃ śiśur uttānaśāyitaḥ ।।
pākaśāsanakalpasya hṛtas tvaṃ śambareṇa ha ।। atyarthaṃ śrāmyate vīra vivatsā saurabhī yathā ।। iha tvāṃ nābhijānāti bālam evāpavāhitam ।। vīra naivaṃvidhān putrān dānavā janayanti hi ।।
rūpaṃ te saumya paśyantī sīdāmi hṛdi durbalā ।। tanme manasi vārṣṇeya pratisaṃdhātum arhasi ।। yathā na mama putras tvaṃ na putraḥ śambarasya ca ।। kāmadevaś ca vīra tvaṃ ratiṃ māṃ viddhi vai prabho । śaṃkarasya ca śāpena tvam anaṅgagatiḥ purā ।। tat kālamāyayā rūpaṃ kṛtvā daityasya veśmani । viśīrṇā sāham uṣitā daityasyāsya ca veśmani ।
cakrāyudhātmajaḥ kruddhaḥ śambaraṃ sa samāhvayat ।। aṣṭamyāṃ nihato yuddhe māyayā kālaśambaraḥ ।। gṛhya māyāvatīṃ devīṃ svām agacchat purīṃ pituḥ ।। ājagāma purīṃ ramyāṃ rakṣitāṃ tejasā pituḥ ।।
māyāvatyā saha tayā rūpavān iva manmathaḥ ।। vismitāś caiva hṛṣṭāś ca bhīrāś caivābhavaṃs tadā ।। prekṣantyo hṛṣṭavadanāḥ pibantyo nayanāsavam ।। abhavan snigdhasaṃkalpāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ kṛṣṇayoṣitaḥ ।।
sapatnīśatasaṃkīrṇā sabāṣpā vākyam abravīt ।। yādṛk svapno mayā dṛṣṭo niśāyā yauvane gate । kaṃsāriṇā samānīya dattaṃ sāhārapallavam ।। śaśiraśmipratīkāśaṃ muktādāma ca śobhanam । keśavenāṅkam āropya mama kaṇṭhe nyabadhyata ।। śyāmā sucārukeśā strī śuklāmbaravibhūṣitā । padmahastā nirīkṣantī praviṣṭā mama veśmani ।। tayā punar ahaṃ gṛhya snāpitā rucirāmbunā ।। kuśeśayamayīṃ mālāṃ strī saṃgṛhyātha pāṇinā । mama mūrdhany upāghrāya dattā srak sā tayā mama ।। evaṃ svapnaṃ kīrtayantī rukmiṇī hṛṣṭamānasā । sakhījanavṛtā devī kumāraṃ vīkṣya taṃ muhuḥ । ity ato anantaraṃ tatra abravīd vākyam eva tat । idṛśaḥ kāmasaṃkāśo yauvane prathame sthitaḥ ।। kim arthaṃ cāmbudaśyāma sabhāryas tvam ihāgataḥ ।।
bhaved yadi na nītaḥ syāt kṛtāntena balīyasā ।। vijñāto asi mayā cihnair vinā cakraṃ janārdanaḥ ।। mūrdhavakṣobhujais tulyo halinaḥ śvaśurasya me ।। aho janārdanasyāsya divyā tvam aparā tanuḥ ।।
nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā śambarasya vadhaṃ prati ।। snuṣāṃ māyāvatīṃ caiva hṛṣṭacetā janārdanaḥ ।। ayaṃ te devi saṃprāptaḥ putraś cāpadharaḥ prabhuḥ ।। hatā māyāś ca tāḥ sarvā yābhir devān abādhata ।।
mā ca te śambarasyeyaṃ patnīty evaṃ vyathā bhavet ।। netrāgninā tryambakasya śūlapāṇeḥ purā yuge । māyārūpeṇa taṃ daityaṃ mohayaty asakṛc chubhā ।। atmamāyāmayaṃ rūpaṃ kṛtvā śambaram āviśat ।।
lokakāntasya sāhāyyaṃ kariṣyati manomayam ।। cirapranaṣṭaṃ ca sutaṃ bhajasya punarāgatam ।। śrutvā tu vacanaṃ devī kṛṣṇenodāhṛtaṃ tadā । praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe rukmiṇī vākyam abravīt ।। aho dhanyatarāsmīti vīraputrasamāgamāt । adya me saphalaḥ kāmaḥ pūrṇaś cādya manorathaḥ । cirapranaṣṭaputrasya darśanaṃ priyayā saha ।। āgaccha putra bhavanaṃ viśasva saha bhāryayā ।। tato abhivādya caraṇau govindaṃ mātaraṃ ca saḥ । pradyumnaḥ pūjayām āsa halinaṃ ca mahābalam ।। utthāpya taṃ pariṣvajya mūrdhny upāghrāya vīryavān । pradyumnaṃ balināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ keśavaḥ paravīrahā ।। snuṣāṃ cotthāpya tāṃ devīṃ rukmiṇī rukmabhūṣaṇāṃ । pariṣvajyopasaṃgṛhya snehād gadgadabhāṣiṇī ।। sametaṃ bhavanaṃ patnyā śacyendram aditir yathā । praveśayām āsa tadā rukmiṇī sutam āgatam । evam uktā tu kṛṣṇena rukmiṇī yoṣitāṃ varā । putraṃ prītyā pariṣvajya mūrdhni cāghrāya tāṃ snuṣām । gṛhaṃ praveśayām āsa snuṣayā saha bhāminī । tam eva māsaṃ sāmbas tu jāmbavatyām ajāyata ।।
rāmād anantaraṃ caiva mānitaḥ sarvavṛṣṇibhiḥ ।। rāmasyaiva priyasutaḥ so abhavaj jyeṣṭha ity api । nihatāmitrasāmantaḥ śakrodyānaṃ yathāmaraḥ ।। janārdanabhayāc caiva na śāntiṃ lebhire nṛpāḥ ।।
duryodhanasya yajñe vai sameyuḥ sarvapārthivāḥ ।। purīṃ dvārāvatīṃ caiva niviṣṭāṃ sāgarāntare ।। śriyaṃ draṣṭuṃ hṛṣīkeśam ājagmuḥ kṛṣṇamandiram ।। pāṇḍavapramukhāś caiva dhṛṣṭadyumnādayo nṛpāḥ ।।
ājagmur yādavapurīṃ govindabhujapālitām ।। viviśur yojanāḍhyāsu svāsu svāsv avanīṣv atha ।। dūtair ājñāpito devo balabhadrapurogamaḥ । sātyakiṃ purataḥ kṛtvā sasainyaḥ sapadānugaḥ ।। śārṅgaṃ ca dhanur ādāya kiṃ syād iti vicintayan । samīpaṃ mānavendrāṇāṃ niryayau kamalekṣaṇaḥ ।।
vyarājata yaduśreṣṭhaḥ śaradīva nabhaḥśaśī ।। kṛtvā siṃhāsane kṛṣṇaḥ kāñcane niṣasāda ha ।। siṃhāsaneṣu citreṣu pīṭheṣu ca janādhipāḥ ।। surāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca sadane brahmaṇo yathā ।।
idaṃ provāca bhagavān kṣatriyān draṣṭum āgatān । sarvan etan nṛpatayo yuṣmākaṃ samudāhṛtam ।। yad asmākaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭhās tulyaṃ tad bhavatāṃ sadā । gṛhyatāṃ vasu yad divyaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ nṛpasattamāḥ ।। te tatheti jagannātham ūcur yādavasaṃsadi । yadūnāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca keśavasyopaśṛṇvataḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā devadeveśaṃ prahṛṣṭāḥ kṣatriyās tadā । tumulaṃ durdinaṃ cāsīt savidyut stanayitnumat ।।
saṃveṣṭitajaṭābhāro vīṇāsaktena bāhunā ।। gāyann eva harīṃ sāmnā vasantaṃ yadusaṃsadi । nārado agniśikhākāraḥ śrīmāñ śakrasakho muniḥ ।। tad uddhatamahāmeghaṃ durdinaṃ vyapakṛṣyata ।।
āsanasthaṃ yaduśreṣṭam uvāca munir avyayaḥ ।। dhanyaś cāsi mahābāho loke nānyo asti kaś cana ।। āścaryaś caiva dhanyaś ca dakṣiṇābhiḥ sahety aham ।। kṛṣṇa paryāptavākyo asmi gamiṣyāmi yathāgatam ।।
guhyaṃ mantram ajānanto vacanaṃ nāraderitam ।। dakṣiṇābhiḥ sahety evaṃ pratyukte api ca nārade ।। yadi śrāvyam idaṃ kṛṣṇa śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ ।। śrotavyaṃ nāradas tv eṣa dvijo vaḥ kathayiṣyati ।।
yat tvayābhihitaṃ vākyaṃ mayā ca pratibhāṣitam ।। prabhavaṃ tasya vākyasya pravaktum upacakrame ।। asya praśnasya mahato yathā pāram ahaṃ gataḥ ।। carāmy ekaḥ kṣapāpāye saṃdṛśyati divākare ।।
krośamaṇḍalavistāraṃ tāvadvṛttaṃ samantataḥ ।। mama vīṇākṛtiṃ kūrmaṃ gajacarmacayopamam ।। tvam āścaryaśarīro asi kūrma dhanyaś ca me mataḥ ।। toye carasi niḥśaṅkaḥ kiṃ cid apy avicintayan ।।
kim āścaryaṃ mayi mune dhanyaś cāhaṃ kathaṃ vibho ।। yatrāham iva sattvāni caranty ayutaśo jale ।। dhanyāsi tvaṃ nadīśreṣṭhe nityam āścaryadarśane ।। hradinī sāgaraṃ yāsi rakṣantī tāpasālayān ।।
nāradaṃ devagandharvaṃ śakrasya dayitaṃ dvijam ।। tava satye niviṣṭasya vākyaṃ māṃ pratibādhate ।। yatrāham iva vistīrṇāḥ śataśo yānti nimnagāḥ ।। tena khalv asi yonis tvam ambhasāṃ salileśvaraḥ ।।
imāḥ samabhigacchanti patnyo lokanamaskṛtāḥ ।। svaṃ jalaughatalaṃ bhittvā vyutthitaḥ pavaneritaḥ ।। ṛte tu pṛthivīṃ loke kim āścaryam ataḥ param ।। kautūhalasam āviṣṭo hy abruvaṃ jagato gatim ।।
āścaryā cāsi bhūteṣu mahatyā kṣamayā yute ।। kṣamā tvattaḥ prasūtā ca karma cāmbaragāminām ।। vihāya sahajaṃ dhairyam atha māṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। nāsmi dhanyā na cāścaryā pārakyeyaṃ dhṛtir mama ।।
eṣv āścaryāṇi dṛśyante ete lokasya setavaḥ ।। dhanyā bhanto dṛśyante bahvāścaryāś ca bhūdharāḥ ।। tena ratnākarāḥ sarve bhavanto bhuvi śāśvatāḥ ।। ūcur māṃ sāntvayuktāni vacāṃsi vanaśobhitāḥ ।।
asmākam īśvaraḥ śūlī giriśo vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ । nāś caryo vāpi dhanyo vā tasmāt parataro bhuvi ।। vihāya taṃ mahādevaṃ nāsmān stotum ihārhasi ।। iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā kailāsam aham āgataḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ pārvatīśānam abruvaṃ vacanaṃ tadā ।। devadeva mahādeva nīlakaṇṭha vṛṣadhvaja । āścaryo asi bhavān eko dhanyas tvaṃ jagatīpate । tvattaḥ parataro nāsti devo jagati kaś cana ।।
yad idaṃ dṛśyate deva bhuvanaṃ sacarācaram । tasyādhāras tvam evāsi sarvasya tripurāntaka ।। atha mām abravīd devo virūpākṣas trilocanaḥ । nāhaṃ dhanyo na cāścaryo naivaṃ māṃ vaktum arhasi ।
mattaḥ parataro jñeyo jagat sraṣṭā dvijottama । brahmā prajāpatir dhanyaḥ sa cāścaryaḥ sureṣv api ।। tasya vākyasya paryāyaṃ paryāptam iva lakṣaye ।। pāraṃparyād upagataḥ praṇāmāvanatānanaḥ ।।
āścaryo bhagavān eko dhanyaś ca jagato guruḥ ।। tvattaḥ sarvam idaṃ jātaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṃgamam ।। bhavanti sarvadeveśa dṛśyaṃ sarvam idaṃ vapuḥ ।। teṣāmevāsi yat sraṣṭā lokānām api saṃbhavaḥ ।।
dhanyāścaryāśritair vākyaiḥ kiṃ māṃ nārada bhāṣase ।। ye lokān dhārayanti sma devās tattvārthadarśinaḥ ।। tanmayaṃ viddhi māṃ vipra dhṛto ahaṃ tair mayā ca te ।। vedopasthānikāṃ cakre matiṃ saṃkrāntavistarām ।।
uvāca caināṃś caturo mantrapravacanārcitān ।। ādhārāś caiva viprāṇām evam āha prajāpatiḥ ।। yuṣmat parataraṃ nāsti śrutyā vā tapasāpi vā ।। āścaryāś caiva dhanyāś ca yajñāś cātmaparāyaṇāḥ ।।
svayaṃbhuvo apīha parā vedānāṃ ca parā gatiḥ ।। tato aham abruvaṃ yajñān gṛhasthāgnipuraskṛtān ।। brahmaṇābhihitaṃ vākyaṃ yan me vedair iheritam ।। dhanyāḥ khalu bhavanto ye dvijātīnāṃ svavaṃśinaḥ ।।
bhāgaiś ca tridaśāḥ sarve mantraiś caiva maharṣayaḥ ।। pratyūcur māṃ paraṃ vākyaṃ sarve yūpadhvajāḥ sthitāḥ ।। āścaryaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇuḥ sa hy asmākaṃ parā gatiḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣo lokamūrtiḥ prayacchati ।।
so api dhanyo mahābāhur dakṣiṇāsahitaḥ kratuḥ । yad rūpaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣo dakṣiṇāpriyayā saha । dṛṣṭaś cāyaṃ mayā viṣṇur bhavadbhir abhisaṃvṛtaḥ ।। dhanyaś cāsīti bhavatāṃ madhyastho hy atra pārthivāḥ ।। dakṣiṇābhiḥ sahety evaṃ paryāptaṃ vacanaṃ mama ।।
dakṣiṇābhiḥ sahety evaṃ praśno mama samāptavān ।। sadakṣiṇe asmin puruṣe tad vākyaṃ paryayāgatam ।। tad etat sarvam ākhyātaṃ sādhayāmi yathāgatam ।। nārāyaṇaparā vedā nārāyaṇaparā makhāḥ । nārāyaṇaparaṃ jñānaṃ nārāyaṇaparaṃ tapaḥ ।। na ca nārāyaṇād anyat triṣu lokeṣu vidyate । nārāyaṇātmakam idaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। iyaṃ hi vedārthagatiḥ sanātanī ।nṛpā yadi śroṣyatha madvacaḥ param ।idaṃ tu satyaṃ sakalaṃ nṛpottamā ।ity evam uktvā sa divaṃ jagāma ha ।
vismitāḥ svāni rāṣṭrāṇi jagmuḥ sabalavāhanāḥ ।। viṣṇuṃ jiṣṇuṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ govindaṃ garuḍadhvajam । parāt parataraṃ brahma nārāyaṇam anāmayam ।। sarvavedāntavedyaṃ ca namaskṛtya guruṃ harim । dhanyo ayaṃ nārado yasmād dṛṣṭaḥ sākṣād dhariḥ svayam ।। dhanyā vayaṃ jagannāthaṃ nāradena vibodhitāḥ । sarve prītā jagannāthaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ puruṣottamam ।। ko nāma viṣṇur ity evam anye mūḍhā narādhamāḥ । dhanyāḥ sarvaṃ vāsudeva iti tattvārthatatparam ।। iti tattvena vijñāya nṛpā nārāyaṇaṃ param । tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā namaskṛtya punaḥ punaḥ । svam eva bhavanaṃ vīro viveśa yadupuṃgavaḥ ।। kṛtārthāḥ sarvathā vipra nārāyaṇasamāśrayāt ।
jātā hi vayam adyaiva tatkathāśravaṇād dvija । ity uktaḥ sa smitaṃ kṛtvā praṇamya munipuṃgavam । māhātmyaṃ śrotum icchāmi paramaṃ dvijasattama ।। karmaṇām anusaṃdhānaṃ purāṇasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
govindasya mahārāja śrūyatām idam uttamam ।। gāṇḍīvadhanvā bībhatsur māhātmyaṃ keśavasya yat ।। yudhiṣṭhiraṃ jitāmitram iti tac chṛṇu kaurava ।। nyavasaṃ pūjitas tatra bhojavṛṣṇyandhakottamaiḥ ।।
ekāhena mahābāhuḥ śāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। kṛṣṇaṃ vijñāpayām āsa paritrāhīti cābravīt ।। caturthāṃśaṃ hi dharmasya rakṣitā labhate phalam ।। brūhi tattvena bhadraṃ te yady api syāt suduṣkaram ।।
trayo hṛtāś caturthaṃ tvaṃ kṛṣṇa rakṣitum arhasi ।। yathā dhriyed apatyaṃ me tathā kuru janārdana ।। rakṣā ca brāhmaṇe kāryā sarvāvasthāgatair api ।। māṃ niyojaya govinda rakṣiṣyāmi dvijaṃ bhayāt ।।
rakṣyasīty evam uktas tu vrīḍito asmi narādhipa ।। gamyatāṃ kauravaśreṣṭha śakyate yadi rakṣitum ।। ṛte rāmaṃ mahābāhuḥ pradyumnaṃ ca mahābalam ।। tam agrato dvijaṃ kṛtvā prayātaḥ saha senayā ।।
