viśrāntavāhanāḥ sarve vāsāyopagatās tadā ।। samantād vṛṣṇisainyena parikṣitya janavrajam ।। dīptāyāṃ diśi vāśanto bhayam āvedayanti me ।। papāta mahatī colkā pṛthivī cāpy akampata ।।
yogam ājñāpayaṃ tatra janasyotsukacetasaḥ ।। sarve yuktarathāḥ sajjāḥ svayaṃ cāhaṃ tathābhavam ।। upāgamya bhayād asmān idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। yattā bhavantas tiṣṭhantu na bhaved vañcanā yathā ।।
tasya viprasya bhavane hriyate hriyate iti ।। hāheti hriyamāṇasya na ca paśyāmi rākṣasam ।। viṣṭambhitā diśaḥ sarvā hṛta eva sa bālakaḥ ।। vācaḥ sa paruṣās tīvrāḥ śrāvayām āsa māṃ tadā ।।
mām eva hi viśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇaḥ paryabhāṣata ।। śṛṇu vākyam idaṃ śeṣaṃ yat tvam arhasi durmate ।। yadi syād iha govindo naitad atyāhitaṃ bhavet ।। pāpasyāpi tathā mūḍha bhāgaṃ prāpnoty arakṣitā ।।
moghaṃ gāṇḍīvam etat te moghaṃ vīryaṃ yaśaś ca te ।। arjuno asmīti yā buddhiḥ sā vṛthā satyam ity uta । saha vṛṣṇyandhakasutair yatra kṛṣṇo mahādyutiḥ ।। vrīḍitaḥ śokasaṃtapto govindenopalakṣitaḥ ।।
vinindan kṛṣṇasaṃnidhau । mauḍhyaṃ paśyata me yo ahaṃ śraddadhe klībakatthanam ।। na pradyumno nāniruddho na rāmo na ca keśavaḥ । yasya śaktāḥ paritrātuṃ ko anyas tadaviteśvaraḥ ।।
dhig arjunaṃ vṛthāvādaṃ dhig ātmaślāghino dhanuḥ ।। daivopasṛṣṭo yo maurkhyād āgacchati ca durmatiḥ ।। evaṃ śapati viprarṣau vidyām āsthāya vaiṣṇavīm । yayau saṃyaminīṃ vīro yatrāste bhagavān yamaḥ ।।
viprāpatyam acakṣāṇas tata aindrīm agāt purīm । āgneyīṃ nair ṛtīṃ saumyāṃ vāyavyāṃ vāruṇīṃ tathā ।। rasātalaṃ nākapṛṣṭhaṃ dhiṣṇyāny anyāny udāyudhaḥ ।। tato alabdhvā dvijasutam anistīrṇapratiśravaḥ ।
agniṃ vivikṣuḥ kṛṣṇena pradyumnena niṣedhitaḥ ।। darśaye dvijasūnuṃ te māvajñātmānam ātmanā । kīrtiṃ ta ete vipulāṃ sthāpayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। iti saṃbhāṣya māṃ snehāt ।
sāntvayitvā ca taṃ vipram idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। yojayāśvān iti tadā dārukaṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। mām uvāca tataḥ śauriḥ sārathyaṃ kriyatām iti ।। prayātāḥ sma diśaṃ saumyām udīcīṃ kauravarṣabha ।।
apaśyaṃ samatikramya sāgaraṃ makarālayam ।। prāñjaliḥ samupasthāya kiṃ karomīti cābravīt ।। rathapanthānam icchāmi dattaṃ nadanadīpate ।। prasīda bhagavan maivam anyo apy evaṃ gamiṣyati ।।
tvayā pravartite gādhe yāsyāmi gamanīyatām ।। evaṃ niścitya govinda yat kṣamaṃ tat samācara ।। mām ṛte na pumān kaścid anyas tvāṃ dharṣayiṣyati ।। abhiśāpabhayād bhīto bāḍham evaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
rathena sahasūtena sadhvajena ca keśava ।। mānuṣās te na jānīyur vividhān ratnasaṃcayān ।। na hi kaścit pramāṇaṃ te ratnānāṃ vetsyate naraḥ ।। stambhitena yathā bhūmau maṇivarṇena bhāsvatā ।।
kṣaṇena samatikrāntā gandhamādanam eva ca ।। jayanto vaijayantaś ca nīlo rajataparvataḥ ।। varṇarūpāṇi bibhranto vividhāny adbhutāni ca ।। tāṃś cāpi pratijagrāha vidhivan madhusūdanaḥ ।।
vivaraṃ gacchato me adya rathamārgaḥ pradīyatām ।। pradaduḥ kāmato mārgaṃ gacchato bharatarṣabha ।। asaktaṃ ca ratho yāti meghajāleṣv ivāṃśumān ।। sapta dvīpān sasindhūṃś ca sapta sapta girīn atha । lokālokaṃ tathātītya viveśa sumahat tamaḥ ।
paṅkabhūtaṃ hi timiraṃ sparśād vijñāyate anagha ।। aśvā nāśaknuvan gantuṃ tato'haṃ saṃbhramānvitaḥ । tad āsādya hayā rājan niṣprayatnās tataḥ sthitāḥ ।। ākāśaṃ darśayām āsa rathapanthānam ūttamam ।।
bhaviṣyāmīti saṃjñā me bhayaṃ ca vigataṃ mama ।। sarvalokaṃ samāviśya sthitaṃ puruṣavigraham ।। ratha eva sthitaś cāhaṃ sa ca brāhmaṇasattamaḥ ।। caturo bālakān gṛhya brāhmaṇasyātmajāṃs tadā ।।
trayaḥ pūrvaṃ hṛtā ye ca sadyojātaś ca bālakaḥ ।। ahaṃ ca paramaprīto vismitaś cābhavaṃ nṛpa ।। yathāgatā nivṛttāḥ sma tathaiva bharatarṣabha ।। asaṃprāpte ardhadivase vismito ahaṃ tataḥ punaḥ ।।
dhanena tarpayitvā ca gṛhaṃ prāsthāpayat tadā ।। viprāṇām ṛṣikalpānāṃ kṛtakṛtyo abhavat tadā ।। arcayitvā sahasrāṃśuṃ bhāskaraṃ bhuvaneśvaram । sātyakiṃ purataḥ kṛtvā bhojayām āsa vṛṣṇipān ।।
tataḥ sabhāṃ praviṣṭāḥ sma saha vṛṣṇipuraḥsaraiḥ । vicitrāś ca kathā divyāḥ kathayām āsa bhārata ।। apṛcchaṃ tad yathāvṛttaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ yad dṛṣṭvān aham ।। parvatānāṃ ca vivaraṃ kṛtaṃ te katham acyuta ।।
yac ca tat paramaṃ tejaḥ praviṣṭo asi kutaś ca tat ।। yac ca te dīrgham adhvānaṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ tat kathaṃ punaḥ ।। yo ayaṃ dīrgho mahāmārgaḥ saṃkṣiptaḥ kena hetunā । etat sarvaṃ yathāvṛttam ācakṣva mama keśava ।।
viprārtham eṣyate kṛṣṇo nāgacched anyatheti hi ।। ahaṃ sa bharataśreṣṭha mattejas tat sanātanam ।। tāṃ praviśya bhavantīha muktā bharatasattama ।। tat padaṃ paramaṃ brahma sarvaṃ vibhajate jagat ।।
ādityavarṇaṃ vimalaṃ tamaḥpāre pratiṣṭhitam । samudraḥ stabdhatoyo aham ahaṃ stambhayitā jalam ।। paṅkabhūtaṃ hi timiraṃ dṛṣṭavān asi yad dhi tat । ahaṃ tamo ghanībhūtam aham eva ca pāṭakaḥ ।।
yac ca taṃ dīrgham adhvānaṃ kṛtaṃ cāpi gatāgatam । yogaśaktyā gataś cāhaṃ kṣipram āgatavāṃs tataḥ । candrādityau mahāśailāḥ saritaś ca sarāṃsi ca । cāturvarṇyaṃ matprasūtaṃ cāturāśramyam eva ca ।। cāturvedyasya kartāham iti budhyasva bhārata ।।
priyo me asi jagatpate । punaś ca paramaṃ tattvaṃ । paraṃ tattvaṃ suraśreṣṭha tvāṃ prapanno asmi mādhava । pṛcchāmi tvāṃ prapanno ahaṃ namas te puruṣottama ।।
ukthyaṃ bṛhadrathaṃ caiva mattas tad viddhi pāṇḍava ।। tena te kathayiṣyāmi nānyathā vaktum utsahe । vetsyase māṃ yathātattvaṃ tad vyākhyāsyāmi te anagha ।। brahmā rudras tathendraś ca varuṇaś ca tathā yamaḥ ।
kuberaś ca tathā cānye dikpālāḥ sanakādayaḥ । ṛṣayo devatā yajñā mattejo bharatarṣabha ।। muhūrtāś ca kalāś caiva kṣaṇāḥ saṃvatsarās tathā ।। vidyāś ca veditavyaṃ ca mattaḥ prādurbhavanti vai ।।
sac cāsac ca mamaivātmā sad asac caiva yat param ।। idam apy aparaṃ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu guhyaṃ sanātanam ।। sarveṣv api ca vedeṣu purāṇesu ca kṛtsnaśaḥ । yad agryaṃ kathitaṃ pārthaṃ sarvair munivaraiḥ sadā ।। varṇatrayasamāyuktam ṛgyajuḥsāmalakṣitam । praṇavākhyaṃ mahābāho viddhi māṃ jagatīpate ।। idaṃ japan mahābāho māṃ namaskuru yatnataḥ । tato māṃ vetsyase samyak satyam etac chapāni te ।। anyat sarvaṃ mahābāho vihāyaitat paro bhava । idam eva paraṃ śreyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā । tathaiva ca mano nityam abhavan me janārdane ।। yan māṃ pṛcchasi rājendra bhūyaś cāto janārdane ।।
pūjayām āsa manasā govindaṃ puruṣottamam ।। rājabhiś ca tathāsannair ye tatrāsan samāgatāḥ ।। karmāṇy aparimeyāni śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ ।। asaṃkhyeyāni divyāni prākṛtāny api sarvaśaḥ ।।
prabrūyāḥ sarvaśas tāta tāni me vaktum arhasi ।। karmāṇy uktāni vai rājan bhūyaś caiva śrutāni te ।। gantuṃ bharataśārdūla vistarasya mahātmanaḥ ।। ānupūrvyā pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanā nṛpa ।।
rāṣṭrāṇi nṛpamukhyānāṃ kṣobhitāni mahīkṣitām ।। yadūnām antaraprepsur vicakro dānavo hataḥ ।। samudramadhye duṣṭātmā narako dānavo hataḥ ।। nirjitaś caiva bhagavān varuṇo lohitahrade ।।
śiśupālaś ca saṃpūrṇe kilbiṣaikaśate hataḥ ।। mahāmṛdhe mahārāja jitvā jīvan visarjitaḥ ।। sālvaś ca vijitaḥ saṃkhye saubhaś ca vinipātitaḥ ।। hayagrīvaś ca nihato nṛpāś cānye mahābalāḥ ।।
rathena jitvā nṛpatīn gāndhāratanayā hṛtā ।। dāhitaṃ ca vanaṃ ghoraṃ puruhūtasya khāṇḍavam ।। dautyaṃ ca tatkṛtaṃ ghoraṃ vigrahe janamejaya ।। nivṛtte bhārate yuddhe pratidāsyāmi te sutān ।।
api satyaṃ ca kṛtavān kuntyā niryātya pāṇḍavān । yavanaś ca hataḥ saṃkhye kāla ity abhiviśrutaḥ ।। vijitau yudhi durdharṣau jāmbavāṃś ca parājitaḥ ।। gatau vaivasvatavaśaṃ jīvitau tasya tejasā ।।
nirjitau haṃsaḍibhakau hiḍimbaś caiva rākṣasaḥ । janamejaya yuddheṣu yathā te kathitaṃ purā ।। bhūya eva mahābāhor yadusiṃhasya dhīmataḥ । tvattaḥ śrutavatāṃ śreṣṭha vāsudevasya dhīmataḥ ।।
tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi vistareṇa tapodhana ।। kathaṃ ca devadevasya putratvam asuro gataḥ । yo abhiguptaḥ svayaṃ brahmañ śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā । sahavāsaṃ gateneha sagaṇena guhena ca ।। baler balavataḥ putro jyeṣṭho bhrātṛśatasya yaḥ । vṛto bāhusahasreṇa divyāstraśatadhāriṇā । asaṃkhyaiś ca mahākāyair māyāśatasahair balaiḥ । māyāśatabalair daityair amarādibhir arcitaḥ । saṃrabdho dvaṃdvayuddhārthī jīvan muktaḥ kathaṃ ca saḥ ।। manuṣyaloke bāṇena yathābhūd vigraho mahān ।।
baliputro raṇaślāghī jitvā jīvan visarjitaḥ ।। nityaṃ sāṃnidhyatā caiva gāṇapatyaṃ tathākṣayam ।। yathā bāṇasya tad yuddhaṃ jīvan mukto yathā ca saḥ । yathā ca devadevasya putratvaṃ so asuro gataḥ । yadarthaṃ ca mahad yuddhaṃ tat sarvam akhilaṃ śṛṇu ।। dṛṣṭvā vapuḥ kumārasya krīḍato asya mahātmanaḥ । baliputro mahāvīryo vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ ।। tasya buddhiḥ samutpannā tapaś cartuṃ sudāruṇam । rudrasyārādhanārthāya yathāsya syām ahaṃ sutaḥ ।। tato aglapayad ātmānaṃ tapasā so asurottamaḥ । devaś ca paramaṃ toṣaṃ jagāma ca sahomayā ।। nīlakaṇṭhaḥ parāṃ prītiṃ gatvā cāsuram abravīt । varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te yat te manasi vartate ।। atha bāṇo abravīd vākyaṃ devadevaṃ sanātanam । devyāḥ putratvam icchāmi tvayā dattaṃ trilocana ।। śaṃkaraś ca tathety uktvā rudrāṇīm idam abravīt । kanīyān kārtikeyasya putro ayaṃ pratigṛhyatām ।। yatrotthito mahāsenaḥ so agnijo rudhire pure । tatroddeśe puraṃ cāsya bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। nāmnā tac choṇitapuraṃ bhaviṣyati purottamam । mayābhiguptaṃ śrīmantaṃ na kaścit prasahiṣyati ।। tataḥ sa nivasan bāṇaḥ pure śoṇitasāhvaye । rājyaṃ praśāsate divyaṃ kṣobhayan sarvadevatāḥ ।। atha vīryamadotsikto bāṇo bāhusahasravān । acintayan devagaṇān yuddham ākāṅkṣate sadā ।। dhvajaṃ cāsya dadau prītaḥ kumāro hy agnitejasam । vāhanaṃ caiva bāṇasya mayūraṃ dīptatejasam ।। na devā na ca gandharvā na yakṣā na ca pannagāḥ । tasya yuddhe vyatiṣṭhanta devadevasya tejasā ।। tryambakenābhiguptaś ca darpotsikto mahāsuraḥ । bhūyo mṛgayate yuddhaṃ śūlinaṃ so abhyagacchata । ārādhya ca jagannāthaṃ śaṃkaraṃ vṛṣavāhanam । śūlinaṃ bhasmadigdhāṅgaṃ girivāsarataṃ sadā ।। jaṭinaṃ muṇḍinaṃ nityaṃ tryakṣaṃ girisutāśrayam । tuṣṭāva devam īśānaṃ vareṣyaṃ varadaṃ śivam ।। namas te bhasmadigdhāṅga śūline te namo namaḥ । namo virūparūpāya śmaśānaniratāya ca ।। harāya harirūpāya śaṃkarāya namo namaḥ । namas tubhyaṃ virūpākṣa vyāghracarmanivāsine ।। namas tuṇḍāya devāya nagnāya vikaṭāya ca । jñānapradāyine tubhyaṃ yogine yatacetase ।। nama ādyāya bījāya vṛṣāya vṛṣarūpiṇe । namo ghorāya ghorāya ghoraghorāya te namaḥ ।। ghorapriyāya ghorāya rudrāya vṛṣaṇāya ca । vṛṣaskandhāya moghāya gadine khaṅgine namaḥ ।। muṇḍāyātha virūpāya vāmadevāya te namaḥ । namo dakṣamakhaghnāya bhaganetraharāya ca ।। namaḥ smaravināśāya guhapitre namo namaḥ । namas tubhyaṃ namas tubhyaṃ dvīpicarmanivāsine ।। namo namaḥ paśupate sarvātman sarvabhāvana । manoratho jagannātha pūryatāṃ tava bhāvanāt ।। evaṃ stuto jagannāthaḥ śūlī vṛṣabhaketanaḥ । dehi bāhusahasraṃ me devebhyaś cāpy avadhyatām । balisūnur idaṃ vākyaṃ papraccha vṛṣabhadhvajam ।।
mayā balamadotsekāt sasainyena tavāśrayāt ।। imaṃ deśaṃ samāgamya vasanti sma pure sukham । nākapṛṣṭham upāgamya nivasanti yathāsukham ।। ayudhyato vṛthā hy eṣāṃ bāhūnāṃ dhāraṇaṃ mama ।।
na me yuddhaṃ vinā deva ratir asti prasīda me ।। bhavitā bāṇa yuddhaṃ te tathā tac chṛṇu dānava ।। svasthāne sthāpitasyātha tadā yuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। prasannavadano bhūtvā pādayoḥ patito abravīt ।।
diṣṭā sahasrākṣam ahaṃ vijetā punar āhave ।। pañcāñjaliśatair devaṃ pūjayan patito bhuvi ।। sadṛśaṃ prātsyase vīre yuddham apratimaṃ raṇe ।। harṣeṇābhyutthitaḥ śīghraṃ natvā sa vṛṣabhadhvajam ।।
yayau svabhavanaṃ yena yatra dhvajagṛhaṃ mahat ।। priyam āvedayiṣyāmi bhavato manaso anugam ।। yenāham iha saṃprāptaḥ kumbhāṇḍa śṛṇu me vacaḥ । vismayot phullanayanaḥ praharṣād iva sattama ।।
tvattas tac chrotum icchāmi varaṃ kiṃ labdhavān asi । devadevaprasādāt tu skandasya ca mahātmanaḥ । īpsitaṃ kiṃ tvayā prāptaṃ tan me brūhi mahāsura । kaccin trailokyarājyaṃ te vyādiṣṭaṃ śṛlapāṇinā ।। kaccid viṣṇuparitrāsaṃ vimokṣyanti diteḥ sutāḥ ।। na viṣṇor bhayasaṃtrāsāt prayāsyanti diśo asurāḥ ।।
vibudhāvāsaniratā bhaviṣyanti mahāsurāḥ ।। salilaughād viniḥsṛtya kaccid rājyam avāpsyati ।। kaccid vairocaniṃ tāta drakṣyāmaḥ pitaraṃ tava ।। punaḥ pratyānayiṣyāmo jitvā sarvān divaukasaḥ ।।
kaccin nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ jeṣyāmaḥ samitiṃjayam ।। yathā te hṛdayotkampaḥ sāśrubinduḥ pravartate ।। prāptavān asi sarveṣām asmākaṃ pārthivaṃ padam ।। bāṇo vācam asaṃsaktāṃ provāca vadatāṃ varaḥ ।।
nītimantam athāmātyam anayo nītimat tadā । tadā mayā mudā pṛṣṭaḥ śitikaṇṭhaḥ pratāpavān ।। tato ahaṃ patito mūrdhnā devadevasya dhīmataḥ । api prāpsyāmy ahaṃ yuddhaṃ manasas tuṣṭikārakam ।।
vijñaptaḥ sa mayā deva prāha māṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ । prahasya suciraṃ kālam ukto adya vacanaṃ priyam ।। mayūradhvajabhaṅgas te bhaviṣyati yadāsura ।। tadā tvaṃ prāpsyase yuddhaṃ sumahad ditinandana ।
praṇamya śirasā devaṃ tavāntikam upāgataḥ ।। aho na śobhanaṃ rājan yad evaṃ bhāṣase vacaḥ ।। dhvajaḥ papāta vegena śakrāśanisamāhataḥ ।। praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe mene cāhavam āgatam ।।
nanādāntarhito bhūmau vṛṣadaṃśo jagarja ca ।। śoṇitaṃ śoṇitapure sarvataḥ puram antikāt ।। svapakṣe coditaḥ sūryo bharaṇīṃ samapīḍayat ।। śoṇitasyāsravan ghorā nipetus tārakā bhṛśam ।।
lokakṣayakare kāle nirghātaś cābhavan mahān ।। aniśaṃ cāpy avicchinnā vavur vātāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।। trivarṇaḥ parigho bhānoḥ saṃdhyārāgam athāvṛṇot ।। bāṇasya janmanakṣatraṃ bhartsayann iva sarvaśaḥ ।।
arcitaḥ sarvakanyābhir dānavānāṃ mahātmanām ।। bāṇo balamadonmatto niścayaṃ nādhigacchati ।। bāṇasya sacivas tatra kīrtayan bahu kilbiṣam ।। utpātā hy atra dṛśyante kathayanto naśobhanam । tava rājyavināśāya bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। vayaṃ cānye ca sacivā bhṛtyā ye ca tavānugāḥ । kṣayaṃ yāsyanti nacirāt sarve pārthiva durnayāt ।। yathā śakradhvajataroḥ svadarpāt patanaṃ bhavet । raṇam ākāṅkṣato mohāt tathā bāṇasya nardataḥ ।। devadevaprasādāt tu trailokyavijayaṃ gataḥ । utsekād dṛśyate nāśo yuddhākāṅkṣī nanarda ha ।
daityadānavanārībhiḥ sārdham uttamavikramaḥ ।। acintayac ca tattvārthaṃ tais tair utpātadarśanaiḥ ।। yuddham evābhilaṣate na doṣān paśyate madāt ।। apīdānīṃ bhaven mithyā sarvam utpātadarśanam ।।
tenotpanno api doṣo naḥ kaccid gacchet parābhavam ।। doṣāṇāṃ na bhaven nāśa iti me dhīyate matiḥ ।। daurātmyān nṛpater asya doṣabhūtā hi dānavāḥ ।। sa bhavaḥ kārttikeyaś ca kṛtavāso hi naḥ pure ।।
tad viśiṣṭaś ca bāṇo api bhavasya satataṃ priyaḥ ।। darpotsekāt tu nāśāya varaṃ yācitavān bhavam । yuddhahetoḥ sa lubdhas tu sarvathā na bhaviṣyati ।। yadi viṣṇupurogāṇām indrādīnāṃ divaukasām । bhavitā hy abhayat prāptir bhavahastāt kṛtā bhavet । śakto dātuṃ samāgamya bāṇasāhāyyakāṅkṣiṇoḥ ।। na ca devavaco mithyā bhaviṣyati kathaṃcana । bhaviṣyati mahad yuddhaṃ sarvadaityavināśanam ।
svastipraṇihitāṃ buddhiṃ cakāra sa mahāsuraḥ ।। yathā balir niyamitas tathā te yānti saṃkṣayam ।। devyā saha nadītīre ramye śrīmati sa prabhuḥ ।। sarvartukavane ramye gandharvapatayas tathā ।।
gandhoddāmam ivākāśaṃ nadītīraṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।। vādyamānaiḥ sa śuśrāva gītam apsarasāṃ tadā ।। devadevaṃ suvapuṣaṃ sragviṇaṃ raktavāsasam ।। haraṃ sahomaṃ varadaṃ ramayanti manoramāḥ ।
bhavaṃ prasādayām āsa devī ca prāhasat tadā ।। prasādayantīm īśānaṃ prahasanty apsaroganāḥ । bhavasya pārṣadā divyā nānārūpā mahaujasaḥ ।। devyā hy anujñayā sarve krīḍante tatra tatra ha ।। atha te pārṣadās tatra rahasye suvipaścitaḥ । mahādevasya rūpeṇa tac cihnaṃ rūpam āsthitāḥ । nanṛtur bhūtapatayo vicitrābhinayānvitāḥ । devī prahāsaṃ mumuce tāś caivāpsarasas tadā ।। praharṣam atulaṃ cāpi lebhe prītamanā bhavaḥ ।।
devaṃ prakrīḍitaṃ dṛṣṭvā devyā saha nadīgatam ।। dīpyamānaṃ mahādevaṃ dvādaśādityatejasam । nānārūpaṃ vapuḥ kṛtvā devyāḥ priyacikīrṣayā । dhanyā hi bhartṛsahitā ramyanty evaṃ samāgatāḥ ।। manasā tv atha saṃkalpam uṣayā bhāṣitaṃ tathā ।
prāha devī tato vākyam uṣāṃ harṣayatī śanaiḥ ।। yathā devo mayā sārdhaṃ śaṃkaraḥ śatrusūdanaḥ ।। uṣā bhāvaṃ hṛdā cakre bhartrā raṃsye kadā saha ।। uṣe śṛṇuṣva kalyāṇi yadā saṃyogam eṣyasi ।।
dharṣayiṣyati yaḥ svapne sa te bhartā bhaviṣyati ।। apākrāmata harṣeṇa ramamāṇā yathāsukham ।। tataḥ sakhībhir hāsyantī harṣeṇotphullalocanā । tālikāsaṃnipātaiś ca anyonyaṃ jaghnur ūrjitāḥ ।। kiṃnaryo yakṣakanyāś ca nāgadaityeśakanyakāḥ । apsarogaṇakanyāś ca uṣāyāḥ sakhitāṃ gataḥ ।। uktā ca tatra tābhiḥ sā bhartā tava varānane । bhaviṣyaty acireṇaiva devyā vacanakalpitaḥ ।। na hi devyā vaco mithyā bhaviṣyati kadācana । rūpābhijanasaṃpannaḥ patiḥ saṃkalpitas tayā ।। uṣā sakhīnāṃ tad vākyaṃ pratipūjya yathāvidhi । dattaṃ manorathaṃ devyā bhāvayantī vyatiṣṭhata । jagāma bhagavān devaḥ svapuraṃ tripurāntakṛt ।
devadevo jagannātha upāraṃsīt tato haraḥ । gate ahani punaḥ sarvās tā nāryo jagmur adbhutāḥ ।। yayuḥ svān ālayān sarvā devī cādarśaṇaṃ gatā । puraṃ praviviśur hṛṣṭāḥ kāścid ākāśam āsthitāḥ ।।
dvādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣasya sakhīgaṇavṛtāṃ tadā ।। viveṣṭamānāṃ rudatīṃ devyā vacanacoditaḥ ।। śoṇitāktā prarudatī sahasaivotthitā niśi ।। citralekhā vacaḥ snigdham uvāca param ādbhutam ।।
baleḥ sutasutā ca tvaṃ prakhyātā kiṃ bhayānvitā ।। bhayadas tava vāmoru pitā devāntako raṇe ।। naivaṃvidheṣu vāseṣu bhayam asti varānane ।। ayaṃ devasamūhasya bhayadas te pitā raṇe ।।
airāvataḥ sa mṛdito gadayā cāsya bhāmini । nirāśo jīvite so abhūd vajrapāṇiḥ sahāmaraiḥ । mahāsuravaraḥ śrīmān baleḥ putro mahābalaḥ ।। evaṃ sābhihitā sakhyā bāṇaputrī yaśasvinī । svapnarūpaṃ yathā dṛṣtvaṃ nyavedayad aninditā । pitaraṃ kiṃ nu vakṣyāmi devaśatrum ariṃdamam ।। śreyo hi maraṇaṃ manye na me śreyo adya jīvitam ।। īpsito vā yatha ko api puruṣo adhigato hi me । jāgratīva yathāhaṃ syām avastheyaṃ kṛtā mama । niśāyāṃ jāgratī vāhaṃ nītā kena daśām imām ।
jīvituṃ spṛhayen nārī sādhvīnām agrataḥ sthitā ।। vilalāpa ciraṃ kālam uṣā kamalalocanā ।। ūcur aśruparītākṣya uṣāṃ sarvāḥ samāgatāḥ ।। kriyate na ca te subhru kaccid duṣṭaṃ manas tava ।।
prasabhaṃ devi saṃyogād yadi bhuktāsi bhāmini । vyabhicāreṇa te devi nāsti kaścid vyatikramaḥ ।। na ca svapnakṛto doṣo martyaloke asti sundari । evaṃ viprarṣayo devi dharmajñāḥ kathayanti vai । duṣṭā yā tribhir etais tu pāpā sā procyate bhuvi ।।
kathaṃ tvaṃ doṣaduṣṭā vai niyatā brahmacāriṇī ।। imām avasthāṃ nītā tvaṃ naiva dharmo vilupyate ।। tām āhur asatīṃ nāma satī tvam asi bhāmini ।। imām avasthāṃ nītāsi kālo hi duratikramaḥ ।।
kumbhāṇḍaduhitā vākyaṃ paramaṃ tv idam abravīt ।। tyaja śokaṃ viśālākṣi apāpā tvaṃ varānane । smṛtaṃ me yad idaṃ vākyaṃ yāthātathyena tac chṛṇu । samīpe devadevasya smara bhāmini tad vacaḥ ।। harmye śayānāṃ rudatīṃ strībhāvam upaneṣyati ।।
ity uvāca tato hṛṣṭā devī tava manogatam ।। tattvaṃ kim idam atyarthaṃ rodiṣīndunibhānane ।। abhavan naṣṭaśokā sā bāṇaputrī śubhekṣaṇā ।। smṛtvā tu vacanaṃ devyāḥ pratyuvāca sakhīṃ tadā ।
yathoktaṃ sarvam akhilaṃ prāptaṃ harmyatale mayā ।। vyādiṣṭaḥ sa kathaṃ jñeyas tatra kāryaṃ vidhīyatām ।। vyājahāra yathānyāyam arthatattvaviśāradā ।। kaścij jānāti tattvena kim idaṃ tvaṃ vihanyase ।।
kathaṃ jñeyo bhaved bhīru so asmābhī ratitaskaraḥ ।। rudatī prasabhaṃ bhuktā praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ sakhi ।। nagaraṃ lokavikhyātam ekaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ ।। na śaktāḥ śoṇitapuraṃ praveṣṭuṃ bhīmavikramāḥ ।।
purīṃ śāsati bāṇe tu jitvā śakraṃ śacīpatim । praviṣṭaḥ śoṇitapuraṃ bāṇam ākramya mūrdhani ।। ko nu nāma jagaty asmin manaḥ kartuṃ mahāsure । śāsaty etat puraṃ devi manuṣyo jīvitaspṛhaḥ । praviśet tam avajñāya bāṇaṃ kiṃ vāpi dharṣaṇam । kas tasyā jīvitenārtho bhogair vā syāc chubhekṣaṇe ।।
prāpto devyāḥ prasādena pārvatyā mattakāśini ।। vijñeyo yasya putras tu yan nāmā yat kulaś ca saḥ ।। taccharaiś ca samāviddhā bhrāntalocanaviklavā । daśām antyāṃ samāsthāya nidrāsukhavimohitā ।
uvāca kumbhāṇḍasutāṃ kathaṃ jñāsyāmahe sakhi ।। tvam eva cintaya sakhi nottaraṃ pratibhāti me । svakārye muhyate loko yathā jīvaṃ labhāmy aham ।। uṣāyā vacanaṃ śrutvā rāmā vākyam idaṃ punaḥ । uvāca rudatīṃ caiva kubhāṇḍatanayā sakhīm ।। kuśalā te viśālākṣi sarvathā saṃdhivigrahe । apsarā citralekhā vai kṣipraṃ vijñāpyatāṃ sakhi ।। asyāḥ sarvam aśeṣeṇa trailokyaṃ viditaṃ sadā ।। evam uktā tadaivoṣā harṣeṇāgatavismayā । tām apsarasam ānāyya citralekhāṃ sakhīṃ priyām । kṛtāñjalipuṭā dīnā uṣā vacanam abravīt । sā tac chrutvā tu vacanam uṣāyāḥ parikīrtitam । āśvāsayām āsa sakhīṃ bāṇaputrīṃ yaśasvinīm । citralekhām apsarasaṃ praṇayāt tāṃ sakhīṃ sakhī ।। bhartāraṃ yadi me adya tvaṃ nānayiṣyasi matpriyam ।।
tyakṣyāmy ahaṃ priyān prāṇāṃs tataḥ kamalalocane ।। naiṣo arthaḥ śakyate asmābhir vettuṃ bhāmini suvrate ।। na kulena na varṇena na śīlena na rūpataḥ । na deśataś ca vijñātaḥ sa hi coro mayā sakhi । prāptuṃ tac chṛṇu me vākyaṃ yathā kāmam avāpsyasi ।।
uṣāṃ harṣayatī śanaiḥ ।yathā ca śakyate asmābhir । ye viśiṣṭāḥ prabhāvena rūpeṇābhijanena ca ।। manuṣyaloke ye cāpi pravarā lokaviśrutāḥ ।। tato vijñāya paṭṭasthaṃ bhartāraṃ pratilapsyase ।।
na darśaye yadi sakhi tarhi vahnim ahaṃ viśe । sā citralekhayā proktā uṣāhitacikīrṣayā । kriyatām evam ity āha citralekhāṃ sakhīṃ priyām ।। tataḥ kuśalahastatvād yathālekhyaṃ samantataḥ । citrapaṭṭagatān mukhyān ānayām āsa śobhanā ।। atyujjvalaṃ mahācitraṃ piṅgavarṇavibhūsitam । uṣāyā darśayām āsa sakhīnāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
kiṃ naroragayakṣāṇāṃ rākṣasānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।। gandharvāsuradaityānāṃ ye cānye bhoginaḥ smṛtāḥ । tad etān paśya sarvāṃs tvaṃ yathābhilikhitān mayā ।। taṃ tvaṃ pratyabhijānīhi svapne yaṃ dṛṣṭavaty asi ।।
devadānavagandharva vidyādharagaṇān atha । atītya ca yadūn sarvān dadarśa yadunandanam ।। balabhadram atho dṛṣṭvā pradyumnam atha sātyakim । dadarśa yadusiṃhaṃ taṃ pautraṃ viṣṇor mahātmanaḥ । aniruddhaṃ raṇe ruddhaṃ pañcabāṇam iva sthitam ।। paṭe sthitaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā vīraṃ citrātmanā yadum । abravīc citralekhāṃ tām ayaṃ coraḥ sa vai sakhi ।।
so ayaṃ vijñātarūpo me kutastyas taskaraḥ śubhe ।। guṇaśīlābhijanato nāma kiṃ cāsya bhāmini ।। tataḥ paścād vidhāsyāmi kāryasyāsya viniścayam । devadevo jagannāthaḥ sākṣāc cakragadādharaḥ ।
dānavānāṃ raṇe hantā viṣṇur jiṣṇur jagatpatiḥ ।। yo vikramaṃ jagannāthas trailokyaṃ sacarācaram । nijaikapadapadme yo nilīnam akarod vibhuḥ । tasyāyaṃ devadevasya śaṅkhacakragadābhṛtaḥ ।
pautraḥ kṛṣṇasya vikhyātaḥ sarvalokeṣu bhāmini । bhartā tava viśālākṣi prādyumnir bhīmavikramaḥ ।। utpāṭya parvatān eṣa parvatair eva śātayet ।। tryakṣapatnyā samādiṣṭaḥ sadṛśaḥ sajjanaḥ patiḥ ।।
tvam evātra viśālākṣi yogyā bhava varānane । aśakyā hi gatiś cānyā agatyā me gatir bhava ।। antarikṣacarā ca tvaṃ yoginī kāmarūpiṇī । upāyaśilpakuśalā kṣipram ānaya me priyam ।।
upāyaś cintyatāṃ bhīru apratarkyaṃ priye sukham । siddhārthā saṃnivartasva yenopāyena sundari ।। bhaved āpatsu yan mitraṃ tan mitraṃ śasyate budhaiḥ । kāmārtā cāsmi suśroṇi bhava me prāṇadhāriṇī ।
adya nānayasi kṣipraṃ prāṇāṃs tyakṣyāmy ahaṃ śubhe ।। śrotum arhasi kalyāṇi vacanaṃ me śucismite ।। dvārakāpi tathā bhīru durādharṣā viśeṣataḥ ।। ayasmayapraticchannā guptadvārā ca sā purī । guptāvṛṣṇikumāraiś ca tathā dvārakavāsibhiḥ ।। prānte salilasaṃyuktā vihitā viśvakarmaṇā । rakṣyate puruṣair ghoraiḥ padmanābhasya śāsanāt ।। śailaprākāraparikhā durgamārgapraveśinī । saptaprākāraracitā parvatair dhātumaṇḍitaiḥ ।
nānuyokṣyasi māṃ devi sāhase asmiṃs tu karmaṇi । tato virama buddhiṃ tvaṃ duḥprāpāt svapnavastunaḥ । ātmānaṃ māṃ ca rakṣasva pitaraṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।। tava yogaprabhāveṇa śakyaṃ tatra praveśanam ।
kiṃ me bahuvilāpena śrūyatāṃ sakhi kāraṇam । yady ahaṃ taṃ na paśyāmi yāsyāmi yamasādanam ।। dūtam āsādya kāryāṇāṃ siddhir bhavati bhāmini । tasmād dautyena me gaccha jīvantīṃ māṃ yadīcchasi । kṣipram ānaya me kāntaṃ prāṇāṃs tyakṣyāmi vā priyān ।।
jīvitasya hi saṃdehaṃ kṣayaṃ caiva kulasya ca । kāmārtā hi na paśyanti dūṣaṇaṃ vai kulasya ca ।। prayatno yujyate kārye ṣviti śāstranidarśanam ।। tvaṃ ca śaktā viśālākṣi dvārakāyāḥ praveśane । saṃstutāsi mayā bhīru kuru me priyadarśanam । sarvathā saṃstutā te ahaṃ vākyair amṛtakalpakaiḥ । kāritā ca samudyogaṃ priyaiḥ kāntaiś ca bhāṣitaiḥ । bhartāram ānayāmy adya tava vṛṣṇikulodvaham ।।
aniruddhaṃ mahābāhuṃ praviśya dvārakāṃ purīm । yādavānāṃ tathaivāhaṃ kulodbhūtasamudbhavam । uktvā cāntarhitā kṣipraṃ citralekhā manojavā ।। sakhībhiḥ sahitā hy ūṣā cintayantī sthitā tu sā ।
sakhīpriyaṃ cikīrṣantī pūjayantī tapodhanān । kṣaṇena samanuprāptā dvārakāṃ kṛṣṇapālitām ।। dadarśa dvārakāṃ caiva divi tāreva saṃsthitām ।। tato dvāravatīmadhye kāmasya bhavanaṃ śubham ।
tatsamīpe aniruddhasya bhavanaṃ sā sma paśyati ।। sauvarṇavedikāstambhaṃ rukmavaidūryatoraṇam । mālyadāmāvasaktaṃ ca pūrṇakumbhopaśobhitam ।। barhikaṇṭhānatagrīvaṃ prāsādair ekasaṃcayaiḥ ।
maṇipravālasaṃstīrṇaṃ divyagandharvanāditam । dadarśa bhavanaṃ yatra prādyumnir avasat sukham ।। tatrāniruddhaṃ sāpaśyac citralekhā varāpsarāḥ । dadarśa madhye nārīṇāṃ tārāpatim ivoditam ।।
varāsanagataṃ tatra yathaivailavilaṃ tathā ।। vādyate samatālaṃ ca gīyate madhuraṃ tathā । na ca tasya manas tatra tam evārtham acintayat ।। striyaḥ sarvaguṇopetā nṛtyante tatra tatra vai । na cāsya manasas tuṣṭiṃ citralekhā prapaśyati । na cābhiramate bhogair na cāpi madhu sevate । vyaktam asya hi tat svapnaṃ hṛdaye parivartate । iti tatraiva buddhyā ca niścitā gatasādhvasā । sā dṛṣṭvā paramastrīṇāṃ madhye śakradhvajopamam । priyāsu gīyamānāsu nṛtyamānāsu sarvaśaḥ । kathaṃ kāryam idaṃ kāryaṃ kathaṃ svasti bhaven mama ।। tāmasyā chādayām āsa vidyayā śubhalocanā ।।
utpapāta gṛhītvā sā prādyumniṃ yuddhadurmadam ।। sahasā śoṇitapuraṃ praviveśa manojavā ।। adarśanaṃ tam ānīya māyayā kāmarūpiṇī । aniruddhaṃ mahābhāgā yatroṣā tatra gacchati ।। uṣāyādarśayac cainaṃ citrābharaṇabhūṣitam ।। citrāmbaradharaṃ vīraṃ kandarpasamarūpiṇam । tṛtīye tu muhūrte sā prāptā bāṇapuraṃ tadā । uṣāṃ tāṃ darśayām āsa paśyainaṃ yady asau bhavet ।। evam uktā tadā kanyā bāṇasya duhitā tataḥ । praveśayām āsa tadā saṃprāptaṃ svagṛhaṃ tataḥ ।।
praveśite aniruddhe tu prahṛṣṭā sahitā tayā । sakhījanasamāyuktā lajjamānā śucismitā । sā harmyasthā tam arghyeṇa yādavaṃ samapūjayat । citralekhāṃ pariṣvajya priyākhyānair ayojayat । tvaritā kāminī prāha citralekhāṃ bhayāturā ।।
guhye kṛte bhavet svasti prakāśe jīvitakṣayaḥ ।। citralekhābravīd vākyaṃ śṛṇu tvaṃ niścayaṃ sakhi । kṛtaṃ puruṣakāraṃ hi daivaṃ nāśayate sakhi ।। na vai devyāḥ prasādas te anukūlo bhaviṣyati । apramādāt kṛtaṃ guhyaṃ na kaścij jñāsyate naraḥ ।। sakhyā vai evam uktā sā paryavasthitacetanā । evam etad iti prāha sāniruddham idaṃ vacaḥ ।। diṣṭyā svapnagataś coro dṛśyate subhago janaḥ । yatkṛte tu vayaṃ khinnā durlabhapriyakāṅkṣayā ।। kaccit tava mahābāho kuśalaṃ sarvatogatam । hṛdayaṃ hi mṛdu strīṇāṃ tena pṛcchāmy ahaṃ tava ।। tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā uṣāyāḥ ślakṣṇam arthavat । so apy āha yaduśārdūlaḥ śubhākṣarataraṃ vacaḥ ।। harṣaviplutanetrāyāḥ pāṇināśru pramṛjya ca । prahasya sasmitaṃ prāha hṛdayagrāhakaṃ vacaḥ ।। kuśalaṃ me varārohe sarvatra mitabhāṣiṇi । tvatprasādena me devi priyam āvedayāmi te ।। adṛṣṭapūrvaś ca mayā deśo ayaṃ śubhadarśane । niśi svapne mayā dṛṣṭaṃ sakṛt kanyāpuraṃ mahat ।। evam evam ahaṃ bhīru tvatprasādād ihāgataḥ । na ca tad rudrapatnyā vai mithyā vākyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। devyās tu prītim ājñāya tvatpriyārthaṃ ca bhāvini । anuprāpto asmi cādyaiva prasīda śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । ity uktvā ramayām āsa so aniruddho mahāyaśāḥ । tataś codvāhadharmeṇa gāndharveṇa samīyatuḥ । anyonyaṃ rematus tau tu cakravākau yathā divā ।।
patinā sāniruddhena mumude tu varāṅganā । kāntena saha saṃyuktā divyasraganulepanā । ekadeśe gṛhasyāsya pracchanno caiva bhāminī । kareṇur dviradeneva varayām āsa saṃgatā ।।
papau tasya mukhaṃ sādhvī samāliṅgya yathākramam । netre cucumba sā devī bāṇasya duhitā yadum ।। bhūyo bhūyaḥ samāśliṣya yatheṣṭaṃ madamohitā । na tṛptim āyayau sā tu samāliṅgya yadūttamam ।।
tāmasyā vidyayā yuktaḥ prādyumnir atha tatkṣaṇāt । cintayām āsa taṃ dṛṣṭvā gṛhe strījanam adbhutam ।। ko ayaṃ vidhir mama mahān na jāne tv asya kāraṇam । svapno ayaṃ kiṃ mayā dṛṣṭa utāho vibhramo mama ।।
jāgarmy ahaṃ na me svapno na ca ma vibhramo mahān । keyam agre sthitā subhrūr lateva ca supuṣpitā ।। udbhrāntahariṇāpaṅgī bhrūlatābhaṅgabhāṣiṇī । pīnastanorujaghanā tāmrapādakarādharā ।।
nīlakuñcitakeśāḍhyā madhurasmitabhāṣiṇī । mama netrapathākrāntā candralekheva śāradī । kim idaṃ nātra jānāmi kenedaṃ pratipāditam ।। dṛṣṭvāsya vavṛdhe kāmas tām uṣāṃ madamohitām ।
sā ca tatpurataḥ sākṣāt pānaṃ kartuṃ samudyatā ।। atha tām iṅgitair jñātvā śrutvā caiva yathārthataḥ । ramayām āsa ramaṇīṃ kāmatas tāṃ manoramām ।। sā cāpi taṃ samāsādya harṣabhītākulekṣaṇā ।
kāmato ramayām āsa romāñcodgatakarkaśā ।। līlāsaṃlāpalalitair lalanā taṃ samācarat । kareṇur iva mātaṅgaṃ vāśitā girigahvare । aniruddhaṃ mahābāhuṃ nidrāparavaśaṃ gataṃ ।
tato niruddhaḥ svapne tu svapurāc citralekhayā । nīto bāṇapuraṃ sadyaḥ saṃgataś coṣayā saha ।। dṛṣṭvaivaṃ svapnasaṃsargaṃ uṣayā svasya cādbhutam । vacanena vimohitām ।।
sa tataś citralekhāṃ tām avekṣyovāca yādavaḥ । dvārakānagarāc chīgram ānītaś citralekhayā ।। bāṇasya nagaraṃ prāpya saṃgato asmy uṣayā rahaḥ । evaṃ svapno mayā dṛṣṭo vicitro adṛṣṭapūrvakaḥ ।।
ko ayaṃ vidhir mamāyātaḥ kā tvaṃ kaiṣā ca bhāminī । keyaṃ purī gṛhaṃ kasya tat tvam ākhyātum arhasi ।। iti bruvantaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā citralekhā vaco abravīt । api te kuśalaṃ vīra sarvatra yadunandana ।
ramamāṇāniruddhena avijñātā tu sā tadā ।। papau cāsyā mukhaṃ kāmī samāliṅgya dṛḍhaṃ yaduḥ । parasparaṃ samāśliṣya parasparamukhaṃ papuḥ ।। tayodyatāṃ tato mādhvīṃ papau śiṣṭām apāyayat । tayor evaṃ tadā kāmo vavṛdhe janasaṃsadi ।। citralekhā tataḥ sādhvī bhūṣayām āsa bhūṣaṇaiḥ । vastrair ābharaṇaiś citrair mālyaiś ca bahugandhibhiḥ ।। rarāja yaduvīras tu rohiṇyā candramā yathā । saudhamārge tatas tau tu daṃpatī rematuś ciram । tāṃ tathā ramayām āsa yatheṣṭaṃ yadunandanaḥ । parasparasya vadanaṃ papatus tau parasparam । alaṃkṛtas tayā tatra saṃgataś coṣayā rahaḥ । papau tasya mukhaṃ sādhvī samāliṅgya yathākramam । netre ca cumbito devī bāṇasya duhitā sakhī । uṣayā saha saṃyukto vijñāto bāṇarakṣibhiḥ ।। damayantyā nalo yathā ।vijahāra yathākāmaṃ ramayaṃs tām uṣāṃ śubhām ।। atha tasyām avasthāyāṃ sthavirā vetrapāṇayaḥ । āmuktakañcukā rājan kañcukīyāḥ samantataḥ ।। aniruddhaṃ tato jñātvā sārdhaṃ kanyāpure sthitam । uṣayā bāṇasutayā ramayantaṃ yatheṣṭataḥ ।। rakṣiṇaḥ sahasā gatvā bhītā bāṇāntikaṃ tadā ।। atha dīptāyudhodagrā nityaṃ suparirakṣakāḥ । te bhītāḥ kathayām āsur aniruddhasya ceṣṭitam ।। eṣa kaścin mahārāja uṣayā saha saṃgataḥ । sthitaḥ kanyāpure rājan kaś cāsau kuta ity api ।। āyātaḥ sahasā rājan na vidmo asya gatiṃ vibho ।। śrutvaitad roṣayuktas tu balaṃ bāṇo nirīkṣya tat ।
yathādṛṣṭam aśeṣeṇa kanyāyās tadvyatikramam ।। baleḥ putreṇa bāṇena vīreṇāmitraghātinā ।। yena naḥ kulacāritraṃ dūṣitaṃ dūṣitātmanā ।। asaṃpradānādyo asmābhiḥ svayaṃgrāham adharṣayat ।।
yaḥ puraṃ bhavanaṃ cedaṃ praviṣṭo naḥ subāliśaḥ ।। evam uktvā punas tāṃs tu kiṃkarāṃś codayad bhṛśam ।। te tasyājñām atho gṛhya susaṃnaddhā viniryayuḥ । yatrāniruddho hy abhavat tatrāgacchan mahābalāḥ । dānavāḥ samabhikruddhāḥ prādyumnivadhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। rudate tadbalaṃ dṛṣṭvā bāṣpeṇāvṛtalocanā । prādyumnivadhabhītā sā bāṇaputrī yaśasvinī ।। tatas tu rudatīṃ dṛṣṭvā tām uṣāṃ mṛgalocanām । hā hā kānteti vepantīm aniruddho abhyabhāṣata ।। abhayaṃ te astu saśroṇi mā bhais tvaṃ hi mayi sthite । saṃprāpto harṣakālas te na te asti bhayakāraṇam ।। kṛtsno ayaṃ yadi bāṇasya bhṛṭyavargo yaśasvini । āgaccheta na me cintā bhīru paśyādya vikramam ।। tasya sainyasya ninadaṃ śrutvābhyāgacchatas tataḥ । sahasaivotthitaḥ śrīmān prādyumniḥ kim iti bruvan ।। athāsyāpaśyata balaṃ nānāpraharaṇodyatam । sthitaṃ samantatas tatra parivārya gṛhaṃ mahat ।। tato abhyagacchat tvarito yatra tad veṣṭitaṃ balam । kruddhaḥ svabalam āsthāya saṃdaśya daśanacchadam ।। tato yuddham apoḍhānāṃ bāṇeyānāṃ niśamya tu । sā citralekhā sasmāra nāradaṃ devadarśanam ।। tato nimeṣamātreṇa saṃprāpto munipuṃgavaḥ । smṛto atha citralekhāyāḥ puraṃ śoṇitasāhvayam ।। antarikṣe sthitas tatra so aniruddham athābravīt । mā bhayaṃ svasti te vīra prāpto asmy abhimatas tava ।। tataś ca nāradaṃ dṛṣṭvā so abhivādya mahābalaḥ । prahṛṣṭaḥ sumanā bhūtvā yuddhārtham abhyavartata । vadhyatāṃ vadhyatām eṣa gṛhyatāṃ gṛhyatām ayam । hanyatāṃ hanyatāṃ kṣipram ity ūcur dānavās tada ।
sahasaivotthitaḥ śūras totrārdita iva dvipaḥ ।। niruddho api tayā tatra bahuśo yuddhadurmadaḥ । bhītayā bhīta evāsau dhāvati sma tathāsurān । prāsādāc cāvarohantaṃ bhayārtā vipradudruvuḥ ।। nadantaṃ siṃhavat tadā ।tasya nādena vai rājan ।
vadhāya teṣāṃ cikṣepa nānāyudhaviśāradaḥ ।। asibhiḥ śaktibhiḥ śūlair nijaghnū raṇagocaram ।। dānavaiḥ samabhikruddhaiḥ prādyumniḥ śastrakovidaiḥ । nākṣubhyat sarvabhūtātmā nadan megha ivoṣṇage ।।
sūryo divicaranmadhye meghānām iva sarvataḥ ।। daṇḍakāṣṭhājinadharo nārado hraṣṭacetanaḥ । sādhu sādhv iti vai tatra so aniruddham abhāṣata । prādravanta bhayāt sarve megho vāteritā yathā ।। vidrāvya dānavān vīraḥ parigheṇāśuvikramaḥ ।
gharmānte toyado vyomni nadann iva mahāsvanaḥ ।। prādyumnir vyahanac cāpi sarvaśatrunibarhaṇaḥ ।। yato bāṇas tato bhītā yayur yuddhaparāṅmukhāḥ ।। na śarma lebhire daityā bhayaviklavalocanāḥ ।।
trāsaṃ visṛjya caikasthā yudhyadhvaṃ dānavarṣabhāḥ ।। tān uvāca punar bāṇo bhayavitrastalocanān । bhavanto yānti vaiklavyaṃ klībā iva vicetasaḥ ।। kulāpadeśinaḥ sarve nānāyuddhaviśāradāḥ ।।
abravīd dhvaṃsatety evaṃ matsamīpāc ca naśyata ।। vyādideśa raṇe śūrān sarvān ayutaśaḥ punaḥ ।। anīkaṃ sumahadrātrau nānāpraharaṇodyatam ।। bāṇānīkaiḥ samabhavad vyāptaṃ saṃdīptalocanaiḥ ।।
athāntarikṣe vyanadan gharmānteṣv iva toyadāḥ ।। tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti ca tadā vāco aśrūyanta sarvaśaḥ ।। aniruddho raṇe vīraḥ sa ca tān abhyavartata । ayudhyata mahāvīryair dānavaiḥ saha saṃyuge ।।
tair eva ca mahāyuddhe nijaghāna mahābalaḥ ।। parigṛhya ca tān eva cāyudhair ahanad raṇe । sa daityasaṃghān samare nijaghāna mahābalān ।। aṣṭau trīṇi sahasrāṇi kiṃkarāṇāṃ tarasvinām । jaghāna samare caikaḥ sākṣāt pautras tu śārṅgiṇaḥ । nanāda vividhaṃ nādaṃ rodasī ca sa kampayan ।
sa tena vyacaran mārgān ekaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ ।। iti prakārān dvātriṃśad vicarann abhyadṛśyata ।। krīḍantaṃ bahudhā yuddhe vyāditāsyam ivāntakam ।। punar bhagnāḥ prādravanta yatra bāṇaḥ sthito raṇe ।।
kṛtvā cārtasvaraṃ ghoraṃ diśo jagmur hataujasaḥ ।। evaṃ bhayam abhūt teṣāṃ dānavānāṃ mahāraṇe । vamantaḥ śoṇitaṃ jagmur viṣādād vimukhā raṇe ।। yādṛśaṃ yudhyamānānām aniruddhena saṃyuge ।।
yudhyatām aniruddhena yathāvartata dāruṇam । tādṛśaṃ na bhayaṃ teṣām abhavad devasaṃyuge । dānavā giriśṛṅgābhā gadāśūlāsipāṇayaḥ ।। kecin mathitamastiṣkāḥ kecid bhinnagalāntarāḥ । viśālam ākāśatalaṃ dānavā nirjitās tadā ।।
bāṇaḥ krodhāt prajajvāla samiddho agnir ivādhvare ।। antarikṣacaro bhūtvā sādhuvādī samantataḥ । nārado nṛtyati prīto hy aniruddhasya saṃyuge ।। etasminn antare caiva bāṇaḥ paramakopana । yayau yatrāniruddho vai so asim udyamya dāruṇam ।। babhau bāhusahasreṇa śakradhvajaśatair iva ।।
nānāpraharaṇopetaḥ śuśubhe dānavottamaḥ ।। visṛjañ śataśo bāṇān dānavo atha mahābalaḥ । abhyadravac ca vegena prādyumnir yatra saṃsthitaḥ । abravīt tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ ।।
bāṇasya vadataḥ saṃkhye udaikṣata tato ahasat ।। uṣā ca pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayavihvalalocanā । prāsādamadhye saṃlīnā bhartāraṃ samudaikṣata ।। kartavyamūḍhā saṃbhrāntā citralekhā varāpsarāḥ । babhūva vimanā bhūtvā mṛtāsmīti vyacintayat । ṛkṣacarmāvanaddhāṅgaṃ daśanalvaṃ mahāratham ।। āruhya syandanaṃ vīro babhau bāhusahasravān ।
purā devāsure yuddhe hiraṇyakaśipor iva ।। tam āpatantaṃ dadṛśe dānavaṃ yadupuṃgavaḥ । saṃprahṛṣṭas tato yuddhe tejasā cāpy apūryata ।। asicarmadharo vīraḥ svasthaḥ saṃgrāmalālasaḥ ।
narasiṃho yathā pūrvam ādidaityavadhodyataḥ । āpatantaṃ dadarśātha khaḍgacarmadharaṃ tadā ।। rāgiṇaṃ cihnitaṃ rājan priyānakhapadais tathā । praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe prādyumnivadhakāṅkṣayā ।।
ajeyaś ceti matvā taṃ yuddhāyābhimukhe sthitam ।। aniruddhaṃ raṇe bāṇo jitakāśī mahābalaḥ । vācaṃ covāca saṃkruddho gṛhyatāṃ hanyatām iti ।। vācaṃ ca bruvatas tasya śrutvā prādyumnir āhave । bāṇasya bruvataḥ krodhād dhasamāno abhyudaikṣata ।। uṣā bhayaparitrastā rudatī tatra bhāminī । aniruddhaḥ prahasyātha samāśvāsya ca tāṃ sthitām ।। atha bāṇaḥ śaraughāṇi kṣudrakāṇāṃ samantataḥ । cikṣepa samare kruddho hy aniruddhavadhepsayā ।। aniruddhas tu ciccheda kāṅkṣaṃs tasya parājayam । bāṇo'niruddhaśirasi kāṅkṣaṃs tasya raṇe vadham ।। babhau pramukhatas tasya sthitaḥ sūrya ivodaye ।।
siṃhaḥ pramukhato dṛṣṭvā gajam ekaṃ yathā vane ।। vivyādha niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ prādyumnim aparājitam ।। tato vivyādha niśitair bāṇaiḥ prādyumnim āsthitaḥ । samāhatas tato bāṇaiḥ khaḍgacarmadharo nṛpa । tam āpatantaṃ niśitair abhyaghnan sāyakais tadā । krodhenābhiprajajvāla cikīrṣuḥ karma duṣkaram ।।
abhibhūtaḥ susaṃkruddho yayau bāṇarathaṃ prati ।। so atividdhaḥ śaraughais tu prādyumnir nābhyakampata ।। jaghānāśvāṃś ca khaḍgena bāṇasya rathamūrdhani ।। cakārāntarhitaṃ bāṇo yuddhamārgaviśāradaḥ ।।
tato avaplutya sahasā rathapārśve vyavasthitaḥ ।। jagrāha jvalitāṃ dīptāṃ ghaṇṭāmālākulāṃ raṇe ।। vārayantīṃ durādharṣāṃ cāmīkaravibhūṣitām । gurvīṃ bhārasahasreṇa viśvakarmakṛtāṃ tadā ।
prāhiṇot tām asaṅgena maholkāṃ jvalitām iva ।। tām eva prāhiṇoc chaktiṃ sarvaśatrubhayaṃkarīm । so abhiplutya tadā śaktiṃ jagrāha puruṣottamaḥ ।। sā bhittvā tasya dehaṃ tu jagāma vasudhātalam ।।
tato mūrchāṃ samāpede baliputraḥ pratāpavān । rudhirāplutagātras tu svaśakyā pīḍito bhṛśam । sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samāśritaḥ । upekṣase dānavendra kim evaṃ śatrum udyatam ।। māyām āśritya yudhyasva nāyaṃ vadhyo anyathā bhavet ।। vadhyatām ayam adyaiva na naḥ sarvān vināśayet ।।
anyāṃś ca śataśo hatvā uṣāṃ nītvā vrajiṣyati । vācaṃ rūkṣām abhikruddhaḥ provāca vadatāṃ varaḥ ।। ādāsyāmy aham enaṃ vai garutmān iva pannagam ।। gandharvanagarākāras tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
pauruṣeṇa samāyuktaḥ sa praikṣata diśo daśa ।। mumoca viśikhāṃs tīkṣṇāṃś channo māyādharo balī ।। veṣṭito bahudhā tasya dehaḥ pannagarāśibhiḥ ।। dehaḥ saṃveṣṭitas tasya bahudhā śararāśibhiḥ ।
niṣprayatnaḥ sthitaḥ svastho maināka iva parvataḥ ।। abhītaḥ parvatākāraḥ prādyumnir abhavad raṇe ।। na vivyathe sa bhūtātmā sarvataḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ ।। bāṇo dhvajaṃ samāśritya provācāmarṣito vacaḥ ।।
cāritraṃ yena me loke dūṣitaṃ dūṣitātmanā ।। rājan vakṣyāmy ahaṃ kiṃcit tan me śṛṇu yadīcchasi ।। kena vāyam ihānītaḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ ।। krīḍann iva ca yuddheṣu dṛśyate devasūnuvat ।।
kulaśīlatapovīryaiḥ sarvair eva samanvitaḥ । sarvayuddhe apy asaṃhāryo bhaved vīryādhikas tava । vijñāya ca vadhaṃ vāsya pūjāṃ vāpi kariṣyasi ।। gāndharveṇa vivāhena kanyeyaṃ tava saṃgatā । adeyā hy apratigrāhyā ataś cintya vadhaṃ kuru । ayaṃ hi puruṣotkarṣaḥ sarvathā mānam arhati ।।
kulaśauṇḍīryavīryaiś ca sattvena ca samanvitaḥ । na no gaṇayate sarvān vadhaṃ prāpto apy ayaṃ balī ।। yadi māyāprabhāvena nātra baddho bhaved ayam । sarvāsuragaṇān saṃkhye yodhayen nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। sarvayuddheṣu mārgajño bhaved vīryādhikas tava । triśikhāṃ bhrukuṭīṃ kṛtvā na cintayati naḥ sthitān ।।
na cintayati rājaṃs tvāṃ vīryavān ko apy asau yuvā ।। rucitaṃ yadi te rājañ jñeyo vīryabalānvitaḥ ।। kanyā ceyaṃ na cānyasya niryātyānena saṃgatā ।। yadi ceṣṭatamaḥ kaścid ayaṃ vaṃśe mahātmanaḥ । tataḥ pūjām ayaṃ vīraḥ prāpsyaty evāsurottamaḥ ।। rakṣyatām iti coktvaiva tathāstv iti ca tasthivān । bāḍham ity abravīd bāṇo hantuṃ vyavasitaḥ kila । uṣāṃ babandha nigaḍair dṛḍhaiḥ pāśaiś ca saṃyataiḥ ।। vyādideśa tato bāṇo rakṣiṇaḥ kiṃkarān bahūn । rakṣyatām eṣa duṣṭātmā sā ca rakṣyā kulādhamā ।। iti sarvān samādiśya bāṇo madabalānvitaḥ । kumbhāṇḍena yayau sārdhaṃ svam eva bhavanaṃ balī । evam ukte tu vacane kumbhāṇḍena mahātmanā ।
tathety āha ca kumbhāṇḍaṃ bāṇaḥ śatruniṣūdanaḥ ।। saṃrakṣiṇas tato dattvā aniruddhasya dhīmataḥ । aniruddhaṃ yodhayitvā bāṇaḥ svagṛham āviśat ।। yayau svam eva bhavanaṃ baleḥ putro mahāsuraḥ । saṃyataṃ māyayā dṛṣṭvā aniruddhaṃ mahābalam । ṛṣīṇāṃ nāradaḥ śreṣṭho abrajad dvāravatīṃ prati ।। tato hy ākāśamārgeṇa munir dvāravatīṃ gataḥ ।। gate ṛṣīṇāṃ pravare so aniruddho vyacintayat । naṣṭo ayaṃ dānavaḥ krūro yuddhaṃ prāpya na saṃśayaḥ ।। sa gatvā nāradas tatra śaṅkhacakragadādharam । jñāpayiṣyati tattvena imam arthaṃ yathaiva tat ।। nāgair viveṣṭitaṃ dṛṣṭvā uṣā prādyumnim āturā । ruroda bāṣparaktākṣī tām āha rudatīṃ punaḥ ।। kim idaṃ rudyeta bhīru mā bhais tvaṃ śubhalocane । paśya suśroṇi saṃprāptaṃ matkṛte madhusūdanam ।। yasya śaṅkhadhvaniṃ śrutvā bāhuśabdaṃ balasya ca । dānavā nāśam eṣyanti garbhāś cāsurayoṣitām ।। evam uktā niruddhena uṣā viśrambham āgatā । nṛśaṃsaṃ cāpi pitaraṃ śocate sā sumadhyamā । baddhaṃ nivedayām āsa prādyumniṃ garuḍadhvaje ।
priyaṃ nātham apaśyantyaḥ kiṃnarya iva saṃghaśaḥ ।। anāthā iva saṃtrastā rudimo bhayamohitāḥ ।। bāhucchāyāṃ samāśritya vasanti divi devatāḥ ।। yasyāniruddhaḥ pautraḥ sa vīraḥ kenāpi no hṛtaḥ ।।
vāsudevasya yaḥ krodhaṃ prajvālayati duḥsaham ।। atikruddhasya siṃhasya ghnataś ca gajasattamān । śoṇitaṃ pātukāmasya daṃṣṭrān prodhṛtya daṃśataḥ । sa vāsudevaṃ samare mohāt pratyudiyād ripuḥ ।।
kathaṃ jīvan vimucyeta sākṣād api śatakratuḥ ।। viprayogena nāthasya kṛtāntavaśagāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। netrajaṃ vāri mumucur aśivaṃ paramāṅganāḥ ।। salilenāplutānīva paṅkajāni jalāgame ।।
rudhireṇāplutānīva nayanāni cakāśire ।। kurarīṇām ivākāśe rudatīnāṃ sahasraśaḥ ।। utpetuḥ sahasā khebhyo gṛhebhyaḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ ।। gṛhe kṛṣṇābhiguptānāṃ kuto no bhayam āgatam ।।
pradharṣitā yathā siṃhā guhābhya iva niḥsṛtāḥ ।। tasyāḥ śabdena te sarve sabhām āgamya viṣṭhitāḥ ।। anyonyasya hi te sarve yathānyāyam avedayan ।। niḥśvasanto vyatiṣṭhanta yādavā yuddhadurmadāḥ ।।
nītijño hitavaktā ca yādavānāṃ priyaṃkaraḥ । kṛṣṇaṃ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ muhur muhuḥ ।। bhavantam āśritāḥ kṛṣṇa saṃvibhaktāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। sukhaṃ svapiti niścintaḥ kathaṃ tvaṃ cintayānvitaḥ ।।
tān majjamānān ekas tvaṃ samuddhara mahābhuja ।। cintāṃ kartuṃ vṛthā deva na tvam arhasi mādhava ।। prāha vākyaṃ sa vākyajño bṛhaspatir iva svayam ।। vicintayaṃs tv ahaṃ cāsya kāryasya na labhe gatim ।
tathāhaṃ bhavatāpy ukto nottaraṃ vidadhe kvacit ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ yādavāḥ sarve yathā cintānvito hy aham ।। aśaktān iva manyante sarvān asmān sabāndhavān ।। pratyānītas tato asmābhir yuddhaṃ kṛtvā sudāruṇam ।।
sa taṃ nihatya samare prāpto rukmiṇinandanaḥ ।। naivaṃvidham ahaṃ doṣaṃ smarāmi manujarṣabhāḥ ।। mama netraṃ durāsrāvam andhatāṃ ko anayad balāt । ko vā jaḍamatiḥ satyaṃ ratnaṃ me makuṭād dharet ।।
ko vā balaṃ durādharṣam avamatyāgrataḥ sthitaḥ । ko nu vā śiniputrasya cāpaṃ na smarati prabho । sānubandhasya tasyāhaṃ hariṣye jīvitaṃ raṇe ।। carāḥ kṛṣṇa prayujyantām aniruddhasya mārgaṇe ।।
saparvatavanoddeśāṃ mārgantu vasudhām imām । atraiva prāyaśas tatra yadi syāt kenacid dhṛtaḥ । jñāte pratikariṣyāmi yat tu prāptam anantaram । ābhyantarāś ca bāhyāś ca vyādiśyantāṃ carā nṛpa ।। keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā āhukas tvarito abravīt । anveṣaṇe aniruddhasya carān vyādiṣṭavāṃs tadā । abhyantaraṃ ca mārgadhvaṃ bāhyataś ca samantataḥ ।।
hayā rathāś ca vyādiṣṭāḥ pārthivena mahātmanā । ṛkṣavantaṃ giriṃ caiva mārgadhvaṃ tvaritā hayaiḥ ।। gantavyaṃ cāpi niḥsaṅgam udyāneṣu samantataḥ ।। āruhya tvaritāḥ sarve mārgadhvaṃ yadunandanam ।।
kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakarmāṇam acyutaṃ bhītabhītavat ।। cirāt prabhṛti me vaktuṃ bhavantaṃ jāyate matiḥ ।। hayagrīvaś ca sumahān sānubandhas tvayā hataḥ ।। kaṃsaś ca nihataḥ kṛṣṇa narakaś ca nipātitaḥ । anye ca bahavas tatra sainyāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ।
kṛtavān asi govinda pārṣṇigrāhaś ca nāsti te ।। pārijātasya haraṇe yat kṛtaṃ karma duṣkaraṃ ।। nirjito bāhuvīryeṇa svayaṃ yuddhaviśāradaḥ ।। tatrānubandhaś ca mahāṃs tena kāryas tvayā saha ।।
na hy anyasya bhavec chaktir vairaniryātanaṃ prati ।। uvāca vacanaṃ dhīmān anādhṛṣṭiṃ mahābalam ।। nākṛtajñā na vā klībā nāvaliptā na bāliśāḥ ।। teṣāṃ priyārthaṃ ca raṇe hanmi dṛptān mahāsurān ।।
kathaṃ pāpaṃ kariṣyanti vijñāyaivaṃvidhaṃ hi mām ।। na teṣu pāpaṃ vijñeyaṃ bāliśa tvaṃ prabhāṣase ।। kadācid iha puṃścalyā aniruddho hṛto bhavet । deveṣu samahendreṣu naitatkarma vidhīyate ।। evaṃ cintayamānasya kṛṣṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ । na vaktavyam idaṃ pāpaṃ tvadvidhena yadūttama । madhuraṃ ślakṣṇayā vācā arthavākyaviśāradaḥ ।।
asmākaṃ cāpi yat kāryaṃ tac ca kāryaṃ śacīpateḥ ।। devatārthe vayaṃ cāpi mānuṣatvam upāgatāḥ ।। viṣṇur madhunihā vīro devadevaḥ sanātanaḥ । snigdhagambhīrayā vācā punaḥ kṛṣṇo abhyabhāṣata ।।
pradyumnaputro apahṛtaḥ puṃścalyā tu hṛtaḥ striyā ।। tābhir hṛto na saṃdeho nānyato vidyate bhayam ।। kṛṣṇena tu mahātmanā । athāvagamya tattvena yad bhūtaṃ yadumaṇḍale ।।
udatiṣṭhan mahānādas tadā kṛṣṇaṃ praśaṃsayan । harṣayan sa tu sarveṣāṃ । madhuraḥ śrūyate śabdo mādhavasya niveśane ।। śanair gadgadayā vācā idaṃ vacanam abruvan ।।
ekaikaṃ śataśo rājan mārgitaṃ na ca dṛśyeta ।। anye kṛṣṇaṃ carā rājann upāgamya tadābruvan । sarve no viditā deśāḥ prādyumnir na ca dṛśyate । te api śāntimanaskā hi gamayeyuḥ kathaṃ ca naḥ । tadājñāpaya naḥ kṣipram aniruddhasya mārgaṇe ।। anyonyam abhyabhāṣanta kim ataḥ kāryam uttaram ।।
kecic cācintañ śūrā āsthāya bhrukuṭiṃ narāḥ ।। evaṃ cintayatāṃ teṣāṃ bahvartham abhibhāṣatām । aniruddhaḥ kutaś ceti saṃbhramaḥ sumahān abhūt । anyonyam abhivīkṣante yādavā jātamanyavaḥ । tāṃ niśāṃ vimanaskās te gamayeyuḥ kathaṃcana ।। aniruddho hṛtaś ceti punaḥ punar ariṃdama । evaṃ ca bruvatāṃ teṣāṃ prabhātā rajanī tadā । prabodhanaṃ mahābāhoḥ kṛṣṇasyākriyatālaye ।। kṛṣṇo api devadeveśaḥ kartavye mūḍhavat sthitaḥ ।। kiṃ mayā kāryam ity eva kuto nu bhayam āgatam । sarvathā yatnam āsthāya yatiṣye kāryam uttaram ।। diśām antaṃ gamiṣyāmi sāgaraṃ varuṇālayam । yatrāsau sthitavān pautro gamiṣyāmy aham adya vai ।। prathamaṃ kāṃ diśaṃ yāsye kena syāc chrūyate akhilam । yadi kaścid vijānīyāt tadā tu sukṛtaṃ bhavet ।
praviveśa sabhām eko nāradaḥ prahasann iva ।। dṛṣṭvā tu yādavān sarvān kṛṣṇena saha saṃgatān । tataḥ sa jayaśabdena mādhavaṃ pratyapūjayat । ugrasenādayaste ca tam ṛṣiṃ pratyapūjayan । madhuparkaṃ ca gāṃ caiva nāradāya dadau prabhuḥ ।। ṛjvāsīno yathānyāyam uvācedaṃ vaco arthavat ।।
utsāhanāśāt sarve vai klībā iva vicetasaḥ ।। atīte divase vīre yādavā adbhutaṃ mahat । vāsudevo abravīd vākyaṃ śrūyatāṃ bhagavann idam ।। tasyārthe sarva evāsma cintayāviṣṭacetasaḥ ।।
eṣa te yadi vṛttāntaḥ śruto dṛṣṭo api vā mune ।। bhagavan kathyatāṃ sādhu priyam etan mamānagha । prahasya nāradaḥ prāha śrūyatāṃ madhusūdana ।। aniruddhasya caikasya bāṇasya ca mahāmṛdhe ।। tasyārthe citralekhā vai jahārāśu tam apsarāḥ ।।
prādyumnibāṇayoḥ saṃkhye balivāsavayor iva ।। asmābhiś cāpi tad yuddhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sumahad adbhutam । baṇena māyām āsthāya baddho nāgair mahābalaḥ ।। hatvā dānavasaṃghāṃś ca koṭiśaḥ śataśas tathā । dṛṣṭam etan mayā viṣṇo prādyumner yuddham īdṛśam । vyādiṣṭas tu vadhas tasya bāṇena garuḍadhvaja । taṃ nivāritavān mantrī kumbhāṇḍo nāma tasya ha । kumārasyāniruddhasya tenāśaktena saṃyuge । bāṇena māyām āsthāya sarpair niyamanaṃ kṛtam ।
nāyaṃ saṃrakṣituṃ kālaḥ prāṇāṃs tāta jayaiṣiṇām ।। prāṇaiḥ kiṃcid gatair vīro dhairyam ālambya tiṣṭhati । prāyātrikān vai saṃbhārān ājñāpayata vīryavān ।। puṇyāhaghoṣaś ca tadā śuśruve brāhmaṇeritaḥ ।
niryayau sa mahābāhuḥ kīryamāṇo janārdanaḥ ।। gantum aichaj jagannātho bāṇaṃ hantuṃ mahāsuram । na hy anyena tam adhvānaṃ gantuṃ śakyaṃ mahābhuja ।। śrūyatāṃ ca tad adhvānaṃ gantavyam atidurjayam ।
taditaḥ śoṇitapuraṃ prādyumnir yatra sāṃpratam ।। samāhvayasva govinda sa hi tvāṃ tatra neṣyati । ekena sa muhūrtena bāṇaṃ saṃdarśayiṣyati ।। sa kṛṣṇapārśvam āgamya harṣeṇāvasthito abhavat ।।
caturdaṃṣṭraś caturbāhuś caturvedaṣaḍaṅgavit ।। samāṅguliḥ samanakho raktāṅgulinakhāntaraḥ ।। sahasram iva sūryāṇāṃ dīpyamānaḥ prakāśate ।। yasyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryaṃ dadau prītaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
ṛṣibhiś ca mahābhāgair vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ ।। sātyakau saṃniveśyātha rakṣyatāṃ dvāraketi ca । gamanāya matiṃ cakre vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān ।। pṛṣṭhato anu balasyāpi pradyumnaḥ śatrukarśanaḥ ।।
śrūyante sma tadā vācaḥ sūtamāgadhabandinām । na hi te pramukhe sthātuṃ kaścic chakto mahāmṛdhe ।। vijeṣyasi raṇe śatruṃ daityendraṃ sahasainikam ।। śṛṇvan vāco antarikṣasthaḥ prayayau keśavo raṇe ।।
bandimāgadhasūtānāṃ sarvaiś cāpi sahasraśaḥ ।। jayājaya jagannātha jaya cakragadādhara । jaya lokatrayāvāsa jayāśeṣajaganmaya ।। jaya nābhisamutthābja niṣaṇṇacaturānana । jaya kaustubharatnāṃśu vibhāsitajagattraya ।। jaya śrīkarapadmastha caraṇāmbhoruhadvaya । jaya tridhāmansarveśa jaya lokapitāmaha ।। jaya yajñapate deva jaya viśvaguro hare । jaya cakragadāśaṅkha padmadīptakarāmbuja ।। jaya śārṅgādihetyudyat sahasrabhujamaṇḍala । jaya cakrāgninirdagdha nikhilāsuramaṇḍala ।। jaya yogimanaḥpadma bodhakṛccaraṇāmbuja । nijaikapādasaṃlīna jagattraya hare jaya ।। jaya sthitilayotpatti kāraṇāśeṣakāraṇa । jaya viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśa jaya bāṇaṃ mahāsura । babhāra rūpaṃ somārka śakrāṇāṃ sadṛśaṃ hariḥ ।। vainateyasya bhadraṃ te bṛṃhitaṃ haritejasā ।।
smṛtvā smṛtvā ca tadrūpaṃ śaṅkhacakragadābhṛtaḥ । tṛptiṃ nādyāpi govinda prāpnuyāmo hareḥ sadā । vibabhau puṇḍarīkākṣo vikāṅkṣan bāṇasaṃkṣayam ।। carma śārṅgaṃ tathā cāpaṃ śaṅkhaṃ caivāsya vāmataḥ ।। sahasraṃ caiva kāyānāṃ vahan saṃkarṣaṇas tadā ।।
āsthito garuḍaṃ rāma udyann iva niśākaraḥ ।। pradyumnasya mahābāhoḥ saṃgrāme vikramiṣyataḥ ।। jagāma mārgaṃ balavān vātasya pratiṣedhayan ।। siddhacāraṇasaṃghānāṃ śubhaṃ mārgam avātarat ।।
svābhiḥ prabhābhir hīnāḥ smaḥ kṛṣṇa kasmād apūrvavat ।। kim idaṃ brūhi nas tattvaṃ kiṃ meroḥ pārśvagā vayam ।। manye bāṇasya nagaram abhyāśastham ariṃdama । rakṣārthaṃ tasya niyato vahnir eṣa sthito jvalan । tena no varṇavairūpyam idaṃ jātaṃ halāyudha ।।
tad vidhatsva svayaṃ buddhyā yad atrānantaraṃ hitam ।। tvayā vidhāne vihite kariṣyāmy aham uttaram ।। etac chrutvā tu garuḍo vāsudevasya bhāṣitam । cakre mukhasahasraṃ hi kāmarūpī mahābalaḥ ।
gaṅgām upāgamat tūrṇaṃ vainateyas tato balī ।। āplutyākāśagaṅgāyām āpīya salilaṃ bahu । pravavarṣoparigato vaitaneyaḥ pratāpavān । tenāgniṃ śamayām āsa buddhimān vinatātmajaḥ । sa pakṣābhyām upādāya vavarṣa salilaṃ bahu । agnir āhavanīyas tu tataḥ śāntim upāgamat ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvāhavanīyaṃ tu śāntam ākāśagaṅgayā । paramaṃ vismayaṃ gatvā suparṇo vākyam abravīt ।। aho vīryam athāgnes tu yo dahed yugasaṃkṣaye । tad eva varṇavairūpyaṃ cakre kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ ।
kṛṣṇaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaś caiva pradyumnaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। svapakṣabalavikṣepaiḥ kurvan ghoraṃ mahāsvanam ।। niyuktāḥ śūlinā pūrvaṃ rakṣaṇe nagarasya hi । ūcuḥ paramasaṃkruddhā jvālayanto diso daśa ।
kim artham iha saṃprāptāḥ ke vāpīme janās trayaḥ ।। prāvartayaṃś ca saṃgrāmaṃ tais tribhiḥ saha yādavaiḥ ।। teṣāṃ yuddhe prasaktānāṃ saṃnādaḥ sumahān abhūt ।। taṃ ca śrutvā mahānādaṃ siṃhānām iva garjatām । athāṅgirāḥ svapuruṣaṃ preṣayām āsa buddhimān । yatra tad vartate yuddhaṃ tatra gacchasva māciram । dṛṣṭvā tat sarvam āgacche tyuktaḥ prahvas tatas tvaran ।।
agnīnāṃ vāsudevena saṃsaktānāṃ mahāmṛdhe ।। svadhākārasya viṣaye prakhyātāḥ pañca vahnayaḥ ।। agnayaḥ samadṛśyanta jvalamānā mahāhave । svāhākārāśrayā pañca ayudhyaṃs te api cāgnayaḥ ।।
tayor madhye aṅgirāś caiva maharṣir vibabhau prabhuḥ ।। āgneyaṃ ratham āsthāya śūlam udyamya bhāsvaram । kṛṣṇaḥ provāca vacanaṃ smayann iva punaḥ punaḥ ।। mamāstratejasā dadghā diśo yāsyatha vikṣatāḥ ।।
ādadāna iva krodhāt kṛṣṇaprāṇān madhāmṛdhe ।। ardhacandrais tathā tīkṣṇair yamāntakanibhair yudhi ।। vivyādhāntakatulyena vakṣasy enam atho anadat ।। viṣṭabdhagātraḥ sahasā papāta dharaṇītale ।।
āvāhayaṃs tadā śīghraṃ bāṇasya puram antikāt ।। avagāhat tataḥ kṛṣṇo yatra bāṇapuraṃ tataḥ । atha bāṇapuraṃ dṛṣṭvā dūrāt provāca nāradaḥ । etat tacchoṇitapuraṃ kṛṣṇa paśya mahābhuja ।। atra rudro mahātejā rudrāṇyā sahito avasat । guhaś ca bāṇaguptyarthaṃ satataṃ kṣemakāraṇāt ।। nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā kṛṣṇas tv idam athābravīt । kṣemaṃ cintayatām atra śrūyatāṃ ca mahāmune ।। yadi vāvatared rudro bāṇasaṃrakṣaṇaṃ prati । śaktito vayam apy atra saha yotsyāma tena vai ।। evaṃ vivadatos tatra kṛṣṇanāradayos tadā । prāptā nimeṣamātreṇa śīghratvād garuḍena te । pradadhmau samare kṛṣṇo nādenāpūrayan diśaḥ । vāyuvegena taṃ dadhmau meghaś candram ivodgiran ।।
agniṃ jitvā tadā viṣṇur bāṇasya purarakṣiṇaḥ । praviveśa puraṃ kṛṣṇo bāṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ ।। tato bāṇapuraṃ prāpya śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau janārdanaḥ । tato hi balabhadras tu dadhmau śaṅkham anuttamam ।। pradyumnaś cāpi saṃkruddho dadhmau śaṅkham anuttamam । garuḍaḥ pakṣavātena bāṇasainyaṃ vyadhūnayat ।। caturṇāṃ ca mahārāja sāgarāṇāṃ yathā svanaḥ । prādur babhūva tumulaḥ śabdo bāṇapuraṃ prati । bāṇānīkāni sahasā samanahyanta sarvaśaḥ ।।
koṭiśaś cāpi bahudhā dīptapraharaṇaṃ tadā ।। nīlāñjanacayaprakhyam aprameyaṃ tathākṣayam ।। pramāthagaṇamukhyāś ca te ayudhyan kṛṣṇasaṃgatāḥ ।। abhyupetya tadātyugrair yakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥ ।
āpīyata tadā raktaṃ caturṇām api saṃyuge ।। tadbalaṃ tu samāsādya balabhadro mahābalaḥ । provāca vacanaṃ tatra parasya balanāśanam । kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahābāho vidhatsvaiṣāṃ mahad bhayam ।।
astram astravidāṃ śreṣṭho yamāntakasamaprabham ।। prayayau tvarayā yukto yato adṛśyata tadbalam ।। pramāthagaṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ balaṃ tad abhavat kṣitau ।। vetāḷaiś ca piśācaiś ca bhakṣayadbhiś ca māṃsakam ।
vātoddhūtair iva ghanair viprakīrṇair ivācalaiḥ ।। śuśubhe tatra bahulair anīkair bahudhānvibhiḥ । musalair asibhiḥ śūlair gadābhiḥ parighais tathā ।। adhāvat tad asaṃkhyeyaṃ śuśubhe sarvato balam । tataḥ saṃkarṣaṇo devam uvāca madhusūdanam । etaiḥ saha raṇe yoddhum icchāmi puruṣottama ।। iti bruvāṇaṃ rāmaṃ taṃ kṛṣṇo vacanam abravīt ।
eṣo abhilaṣitaḥ kāmaḥ prāg eva hi mamābhavat । ebhiḥ saha samāgantum iccheyaṃ yuddhadurmadaiḥ ।। savye pārśve ca pradyumnas tathā me dakṣiṇe bhavān ।। evaṃ bruvantas te anyonyam adhirūḍhāḥ khagottamam ।।
tato yuddhaṃ mahac cakre lāṅgalenātha lāṅgalī । sahasram ayutaṃ rāmo jaghāna ditinandanān । yugānte sarvabhūtāni kālasyeva didhakṣataḥ ।। caraty atibalo yuddhe yuddhamārgaviśāradaḥ ।। dānavān puruṣavyāghro yudyamānān sahasraśaḥ ।।
pradhmāpya bahuśaḥ śaṅkham ayudhyata janārdanaḥ ।। akarot samare śatrūn vainateyaḥ pratāpavān ।। nītā vaivasvatamukhaṃ vainateyena dhīmatā । abhajyata tadā saṃkhye bāṇavarṣasamāhatam ।।
nirjitya kaiṃkaraṃ sainyaṃ harir lokanamaskṛtaḥ । pāñcajānyaṃ mahāśaṅkhaṃ dadhmau daityabhayaṃkaram । etasminn antare rājan nāradaḥ prayayau raṇāt । kailāsaṃ merusaṃkāśaṃ dṛṣṭo rudreṇa pūjitaḥ । pṛṣṭaḥ kim iha devarṣe saṃprāptas tad vadasva me ।।
tataḥ prahasya devarṣiḥ prāha rudraṃ mahīpate । bāṇaḥ saṃhanyate deva kṛṣṇena halinā kila । tasya sarvam anīkaṃ tu bhagnaṃ tan nāvatiṣṭhati ।। kiṃ vartase adya niścinto bhartas te pīḍyate kila ।
kuruṣva tasya sāhāyyaṃ bhaktādhīno bhavān iti ।। nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā haraḥ prasphuritādharaḥ । niśvāsaṃ mumuce rājann astaḥ kaś cid vinirgataḥ ।। taṃ kiṃ karomīti haraṃ pṛcchantaṃ prāha bhūtapaḥ ।
gaccha bāṇapuraṃ śīghraṃ jahi kṛṣṇahalāyudhau ।। tathety antardadhe so api yayau yatra harir halī । pramathān āha rudras tu sajjā bhavata sattamāḥ ।। sajjair gacchata mātsyārddho mayūrondaravāhanau ।
gaccha nārada tatra tvaṃ bāṇam āśvāsaya prabho ।। eṣa mām āgataṃ paśya tvatkṛte daityasattama । ghātayāmi yaduśreṣṭhau prāptau yāv iha mandadhīḥ ।। tatheti nāradaḥ prāpto bāṇāyāvedayat tadā ।
punar yayau kṛṣṇapārśvaṃ khecaro vā garutmani ।। kārayām āsa rudras tu prayānodyogam uttamam ।। jvaras tu raṇam āgatya dadarśa halinaṃ raṇe । ghnantaṃ dānavadaiteyāṃs taṃ hantuṃ sa samāgataḥ ।
jvaras tripādas triśirās tadā samaradurjayaḥ ।। nadan meghasahasrasya tulyanirghātanisvanaḥ ।। kiṃ māṃ yudhyasi durbuddhe balavantaṃ mahāsvanam । tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan mokṣyase raṇamūrdhani ।।
yugāntāgninibhair ghorair muṣṭibhir janayan bhayam ।। rauhiṇeyasya śaighryeṇa nāvasthānam adṛśyata ।। savyena bāhunā bhasma cikṣepa balavakṣasi । śaighryāl lakṣye nipatitaṃ śarīre parvatopame ।।
pradīptaṃ patitaṃ tat tu giriśṛṅgaṃ vyadārayat ।। niḥśvasañ jṛmbhamāṇaś ca nidrānvitatanur muhuḥ ।। saṃhṛṣṭalomā glānākṣaḥ kṣiptacitta iva śvasan ।। dahyāmi sarvatas tāta kathaṃ śāntir bhaven mama ।।
balenāmitatejasā । prahasya vacanaṃ prāha kṛṣṇaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ । na bhetavyam itītyuktvā । kṛṣṇena paramasnehāt tato dāhāt pramucyata ।।
kṛṣṇena sahasā yuddhe jvaraṃ bhasmapraśāntaye । mokṣayitvā balaṃ tatra dāhāt tu madhusūdanaḥ । balabhadro hṛṣīkeśāc chāntiṃ prāptas tadā raṇe ।। tayor antaram āsādya tasthau yuddhāya keśavaḥ । vyāvidhya sahasā bāhuṃ jvaram etad uvāca ha ।
tāṃ darśayasva samare mayi yuddhaviśārada ।। yac ca te pauruṣaṃ sarvaṃ tad darśayatu no bhavān । tataḥ kruddho jvaro rājan duḥkhānām agraṇīr harim । cikṣepa cainaṃ tad bhasma jvālāgarbhaṃ mahāgadaḥ ।। bhasmanā viddhadehas tu devadevo janārdanaḥ ।
kṛṣṇaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śamaṃ cāgnir gataḥ punaḥ ।। jaghāna kṛṣṇaṃ grīvāyāṃ muṣṭinaikena corasi ।। tataḥ kruddho hṛṣīkeśo muṣṭinā nijaghāna tam । vakṣaḥsthale sa bhūtātmā mūrdhni caiva punaḥ punaḥ ।। tato jvaraḥ samāvidhya bāhū dhamanisaṃtatau । tābhyāṃ vakṣaḥ samāhatya dadaṃśa ca yadūttamam ।। tato asahañ jagannāthaḥ ānane samapothayat । parvateṣu patantīnām aśanīnām iva svanaḥ ।।
aṣṭābhiś ca tribhiś caiva bāhubhiś ca tadā raṇam । prāvartata mahāghoraṃ devānāṃ tatra paśyatām । muhūrtam abhavad yuddham anyonyaṃ sumahātmanoḥ ।। hantum aicchat tadā viṣṇur jvaraṃ lokabhayaṃkaram । yam akṣayaṃ samupanayañ jagatpatiḥ śarīradhṛg gaganacaraṃ mahāmṛdhe ।।
kṛṣṇo bhujabalābhyāṃ taṃ cikṣepātha mahītale ।। amuktvā vigrahaṃ tasya kṛṣṇasyāpratimaujasaḥ ।। praviśya hṛdayaṃ tasya babādhe yadusattamam । kṛṣṇaḥ skhalann iva muhuḥ kṣitau samabhivartata ।।
romāñ cotthitagātras tu nidrayā cābhibhūyate ।। tasya sthairyaṃ samālambya kṛṣṇaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ । vikurvati mahāyogī jṛmbhamāṇaḥ punaḥ punaḥ । so asṛjaj jvaram anyaṃ tu pūrvajvaravināśanam ।। sa vaiṣṇavajvaro gṛhya taṃ ca vai jvaram ojasā । kṛṣṇāya na saṃprayacchaṃs taṃ jagrāha punar hariḥ । ghoraṃ vaiṣṇavam atyugraṃ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkaraṃ । sṛṣṭavān atha tejasvī balavān bhīmavikramaḥ । jvaraḥ kṛṣṇavisṛṣṭas tu gṛhītvā taṃ jvaraṃ balāt । kṛṣṇāya hṛṣṭaḥ prāyacchat taṃ jagrāha tato hariḥ ।। tatas taṃ paramakruddho vāsudevo mahābalaḥ । svagātrāt svajvareṇaiva niṣkrāmayata vīryavān ।। āvidhya bhūtale cainaṃ śatadhā kartum udyataḥ । vyāghoṣayaj jvaras tatra bhoḥ paritrātum arhasi । māheśvaro vaiṣṇavaś ca yuyudhāte jvarāv ubhau । māheśvaraḥ samākrandan vaiṣṇavena balārditaḥ । kṛṣṇajvaro jvaraṃ pūrvaṃ gṛhītvā svena tejasā । nanāda sumahānādaṃ vaiṣṇavaḥ sa mahābalaḥ । caturbhujaś caturvaktraḥ sarvapraharaṇodyataḥ ।। tayos tu tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ jvarayor bāhuśālinoḥ ।। tato devāḥ sagandharvā divisthā yuddhalālasāḥ । dadṛśuś ca mahad yuddhaṃ bhūtāni ca samantataḥ । tato māheśvaro yuddhe tāḍayām āsa vaiṣṇavam । bāhunā tāḍitas tena nanāda bahuvistaram ।। sa gato vaiṣṇavaṃ rājan raudraṃ bhasmāyudhaṃ raṇe । dvābhyām atha ca bāhubhyāṃ gṛhītvātāḍayad balī ।। itarābhyāṃ samāhatya bāhubhyāṃ vaiṣṇavo jvaraḥ । nanāda sumahānādaṃ sarvalokasya paśyataḥ ।। tato raudro jvaro rājan muṣṭinātha jaghāna tam । dadaṃśa dantair bahudhā jvaraṃ keśavam āhave ।। bāhubhyām eva tau rājan yuyudhāte mahāgadau । anyonyaṃ tāḍayantau ca muṣṭibhir jvarasattamau ।। cakratuś ca mahānādaṃ jvarau tau lokaviśrutau । vaiṣṇavo atha jvaro rājan grahītuṃ raudrasaṃjñitam ।। yatate bahudhā tatra muṣṭinātha jaghāna tam । āhatya bāhunā bhūyo niṣpipeṣa punaḥ punaḥ ।। niṣpiṣṭahṛdayas tūrṇaṃ śūlino jvarasattamaḥ । nanāda bahudhā nādaṃ bhūmau viparivartate ।। gṛhītvā tu balād raudram ākṛṣya ca punaḥ punaḥ । kṛṣnāya hṛṣtaḥ prāyacchat kiṃ kariṣyāmy ataḥ param ।। haniṣye devadeveśa bhakṣayiṣye atha vā punaḥ । ity uktvā sumahānādaṃ cakāra raṇamūrdhani ।। utthāya ca hṛṣīkeśo jvaraṃ māheśvaraṃ raṇe । hantum aicchat tadā loko nirjvaro astv iti keśavaḥ ।
aśarīrā tato vāṇī tam uvācāntarikṣagā ।। ity evam ukte vacane taṃ mumoca hariḥ svayam ।। bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyasya jagataḥ paramo guruḥ ।। evam ukto hṛṣīkeśaṃ jvaro vākyam athābravīt । kṛṣṇasya pādayor mūrdhnā śaraṇaṃ so agamaj jvaraḥ ।। śṛṇuṣva mama govinda vijñāpyaṃ yadunandana । yo me manorathā deva taṃ tvaṃ kuru mahābhuja । tam uvāca jvaro bhūyaḥ sākṣād viṣṇur iva svayam । praṇamya śirasā devaṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ sthitaḥ ।। namaḥ kṛṣṇāya haraye viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave । ādidevāya devāya purāṇāya gadābhṛte ।। namaḥ sahasraśirase sahasracaraṇāya ca । sahasrākṣa namo nityaṃ lokānām abhayaṃkara । udgīthāya namo deva yajñādhipataye namaḥ ।। namas te cakriṇe nityam asihastāya te namaḥ ।। anantāya virūpāya namas te madhusūdana । namas te devadeveśa tubhyaṃ deva kapardine ।। namas te rākṣasaghnāya namo rāghavarūpiṇe । jñānajñeyāya devāya nama ādyāya viṣṇave ।। namas te narasiṃhāya daityarājavihāriṇe । namas tubhyaṃ varāhāya daṃṣṭroddhṛtavasuṃdhara ।। trivikrama namas tubhyaṃ baliyajñavināśana । vāsudevāya devāya namaḥ kaṃsavināśana ।। namaḥ sarvātmane deva sarvakartre namo namaḥ ।। prasīda devadeveśa bhītānām abhayaṃkara ।। namāmi devadeveśaṃ vareṇyam abhayapradam । viṣṇo tvāṃ sakaleśeśa tvāṃ gadādharam avyayam ।। namas te devadeveśa bhīto ahaṃ bhavanāśana । iti stutvā jagannāthaṃ nṛtyann iva tadā jvaraḥ । papāta pādayor viṣṇor niḥśvasan bhītabhītavat ।। prasīda viṣṇo deveśa pīḍito asmi janārdana । aham eko jvaras tāta nānyo loke jvaro bhavet ।
tava prasādān nānyaḥ syāj jvaraḥ samitiśobhana ।। evaṃ bhavatu bhadraṃ te yathā tvaṃ jvara kāṅkṣase । varārthināṃ varo deyo bhavāṃś ca śaraṇaṃ gataḥ । tatas tuṣṭo hṛṣīkeśaḥ stotreṇānena keśavaḥ । prītimāṃś cābhavat kṛṣṇo raudrajvaram uvāca ha ।
antakāle manuṣyāṇāṃ bhūyād bhogāya māmakaḥ । yo ayaṃ mayā jvaro sṛṣṭo mayy evaiṣa pralīyatām ।। evam ukte tu vacane jvaraṃ prati mahāyaśāḥ । kṛṣṇaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ punar vākyam uvāca ha ।। śṛṇuṣva jvara saṃdeśaṃ yathā loke cariṣyasi । sarvajātiṣu vinyastas tathā sthāvarajaṅgame ।। tridhā vibhajya cātmānaṃ matpriyaṃ yadi kāṅkṣase । catuṣpādān bhajaikena dvitīyena ca sthāvarān ।। tṛtīyo yaś ca te bhāgo mānuṣeṣūpapatsyate । tridhābhūtaṃ vapuḥ kṛtvā pakṣiṣu tvaṃ bhava jvara ।। caturdhā yas tṛtīyasya bhaviṣyati ca te dhruvam । ekāntaraś caturbhāgaḥ khorakaś ca caturthakaḥ ।। mānuṣeṣv atha bhedane vasa tvaṃ pravibhajya vai । jātiṣv athāvaśeṣāsu nivasa tvaṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।। vṛkṣeṣu kīṭarūpeṇa tathā saṃkocapatrakaḥ । pāṇḍupatraś ca vikhyātaḥ phaleṣv āturyam eva ca ।। apāṃ tu nīlikāṃ vidyāc chikhodbhedaś ca barhiṇām । padminīṣu himo bhūtvā pṛthivyām api coṣaraḥ ।। gaurikaḥ parvateṣv eva matprasādād bhaviṣyasi । goṣv apasmārako bhūtvā khorakaś ca bhaviṣyasi ।। evaṃ vividharūpeṇa bhaviṣyasi mahītale ।। darśanāt sparśanāc cāpi prāṇināṃ vadham eṣyasi । ṛte devamanuṣyebhyo nānyas tvāṃ visahiṣyati ।। kṛṣṇasya vacanaṃ śrutvā jvaro hṛṣṭamanā hy abhūt । provāca vacanaṃ kiṃcit praṇamitvā kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। sarvajātiprabhutvena kṛto dhanyo asmi mādhava । bhūyaś ca te vacaḥ kartum icchāmi puruṣarṣabha । tad ājñāpaya govinda kiṃ karomi mahābhuja । evaṃ bhavatu bhadraṃ te yathā tvaṃ jvara kākṣase । aham asurakulapramāthinā ।tripurahareṇa hareṇa nirmitaḥ ।raṇaśirasi vinirjitas tvayā ।prabhur asi me adya tavāsmi kiṃkaraḥ ।।jvarasya vacanaṃ śrutvā vāsudevo abravīd vacaḥ । abhisaṃdhiṃ śṛṇuṣvādya yat tvā vakṣyāmi niścayāt । yuvāṃ jvarau ca bhavatāṃ pīḍāyāṃ maraṇe tathā । pīḍāyāṃ ca bhavān svāmī maraṇe māmakas tathā ।। ihaiva līyatāṃ tāvaj jvaro māmaka eva hi । ājñāpaya priaṃ kiṃ te cakrāyudha karomy aham ।।
stuvan māṃ bhaktiyuktena stotreṇānena mānavaḥ । jvaradevāvayoḥ samyak cintayan yuddham adbhutam । na tasya jvarasaṃjātā pīḍā bhuvi bhaviṣyati । praṇamya mām ekamanāḥ paṭhet tu yaḥ sa vai bhavej jvara vigatajvaro naraḥ ।। tripād bhasmapraharaṇas triśirā raktalocanaḥ । sa me prītaḥ sukhaṃ dadyāt sarvāmayapatir jvaraḥ ।। ādyantavantaḥ kavayaḥ purāṇāḥ ।sūkṣmā bṛhanto apy anuśāsitāraḥ ।sarvāñ jvarān ghnantu mamāniruddha । pradyumnasaṃkarṣaṇavāsudevāḥ । provāca yaduśārdūlam evam etad bhaviṣyati ।।
varaṃ labdhvā jvaro hṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇāc ca samayaṃ punaḥ । evam astv iti govindaṃ babhāṣe keśavaṃ tadā । praṇamya śirasā kṛṣṇam apakrāntas tato raṇāt ।। bhaktānām abhayaṃkaram ।vāsudevaṃ mahātmānaṃ ।
vainateyaṃ samāruhya yudhyamānā raṇe sthitāḥ ।। ardayan vainateyasthā nadanto atibalā raṇe ।। saṃcukopa mahānīkaṃ dānavānāṃ mahātmanām ।। kṛṣṇabāṇāgnir udbhūto vivṛddhim upagacchati ।।
yugāntāgnir ivārciṣmān dahamāno vyarājata ।। tatrāśītisahasrāṇi nāgānāṃ nihatāni ca । lakṣaṃ ca rathavṛndaṃ tu hataṃ keśavasāyakaiḥ ।। aśvānāṃ śatasāhasram ayutaṃ pattināṃ tathā । niḥśeṣitātha sā senā palāyanaparābhavat । senāṃ bāṇaḥ samāsādya vārayan vākyam abravīt ।। daityavaṃśasamutpannāḥ palāyadhyvaṃ mahāmṛdhe ।।
utsṛjyotsṛjya gacchanti kiṃ bhavanto antarikṣagāḥ ।। mānayadbhir na gantavyam eṣo hy aham avasthitaḥ ।। apakrāmanta te sarve dānavā bhayapīḍitāḥ ।। bhagnāvaśeṣaṃ yuddhāya manaś cakre punas tadā ।।
balaṃ bhagnaṃ samālokya vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।। kimarthaṃ yuddham utsṛjya bhavanto bhayamohitāḥ ।। prāṇāṃs tyaktvā ca yudhyadhvaṃ sarve dānavapuṃgavāḥ । evaṃ saṃstūyamānās te kumbhāṇḍena mahātmanā । naiva tastambhire daityāḥ palāyanta samantataḥ । evaṃ kumbhāṇḍavākyaṃ te śṛṇvanto bhayavihlavāḥ । cakrāgnibhayavitrastāḥ sarve yānti diśo daśa ।। bhagnaṃ balaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇenāmitatejasā । saṃraktanayanaḥ sthāṇur yuddhāya paryavartata ।। bāṇasaṃrakṣaṇaṃ kartuṃ ratham āsthāya suprabham । devaḥ kumāraś ca tathā rathenāgninibhena vai । tataḥ kruddho haraḥ sākṣād nadī khaṅgī paraśvadhī । śūlī niṣaṅgī kavacī bāṇī kārmukavāñ śivaḥ । saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭo rudraḥ pradhāvati yato hariḥ ।।
tasyānuyātā vetāḷāḥ piśācāś candramālinaḥ । pibantaḥ śoṇitaṃ bhūyaḥ karālā nirṇatodarāḥ । ratho bhāti ghanonmuktaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ yathā śaśī ।। tato gaṇasahasrais tu nānārūpair bhayāvahaiḥ । nadadbhir vividhān nādān ratho devasya so abhayāt ।। ke cit siṃhamukhās tatra tathā vyāghramukhāś ca ha । nāgāśvoṣṭramukhās tatra prāvepann abhipīḍitāḥ । vyālayajñopavītāś ca ke cit tatra mahābalāḥ ।। kharoṣṭragajavaktrāś ca aśvagrīvāś ca saṃsthitāḥ ।। chāgamārjāravaktrāś ca meṣavaktrās tathā pare । cīriṇaḥ śikhinaś cānye jaṭilordhvaśiroruhāḥ ।। bhagnāḥ paripatanti sma śaṅkhaduṃdubhinisvanaiḥ । ke cit saumyamukhās tatra divyaiḥ śastrair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। nānāpuṣpakṛtāpīḍā nānāpraharaṇāyudhāḥ । vāmanā vikaṭāś caiva siṃhavyāghraparicchadāḥ । rudhirārdramahādaṃṣṭrā mahāmāṃsabalipriyāḥ ।। devaṃ saṃparivāryātha mahāśatrupramardanam । līlāyamānās tiṣṭhanti saṃgrāmābhimukhonmukhāḥ ।। tato divyaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā rudrasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ । kṛṣṇo garuḍam āsthāya yayau rudrāya saṃyuge । tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti covāca kruddho ahaṃkāragarvitaḥ ।।
bhagavān api govindaḥ smayann iva ca saṃsthitaḥ । sthito asmi tava saṃgrāme yatheṣṭaṃ kriyatām iti । hariṃ vivyādha kupito nārācānāṃ śatena saḥ ।। harir jagrāha kupito hy āstraṃ pārjanyam uttamam ।।
pracacāla tato bhūmir viṣṇurudraprapīḍitā ।। nāgāś cordhvamukhās tatra vicelur abhipīḍitāḥ । parvatāḥ prastutās tatra jaladhārābhir āplutāḥ ।। ke cin mumucire tatra śikharāṇi samantataḥ । diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva bhūmir ākāśam eva ca ।। pradīptānīva dṛśyante sthāṇukṛṣṇasamāgame । samantataś ca nirghātāḥ patanti dharaṇītale ।। śivāś caivāśivān nādān nadante bhīmadarśanāḥ । vāsavaś cānadad ghoraṃ rudhiraṃ cāpy avarṣata ।। ulkā ca bāṇasainyasya mukhāny āvṛtya tiṣṭhati । na vavau mārutaś cāpi jyotīṃṣy ākulatām iyuḥ । prabhāhīnāś ca oṣadhyo na caranty antarikṣagāḥ ।। etasminn antare brahmā sarvair devagaṇair vṛtaḥ । tripurāntakam udyantaṃ jñātvā rudram upāgamat ।। gandharvāpsarasaś caiva yakṣā vidyādharās tathā । siddhacāraṇasaṃghāś ca paśyanto atha divi sthitāḥ ।। tataḥ pārjanyam astraṃ tat kṣiptaṃ rudrāya viṣṇunā । yayau jvalann atha tadā yato rudro rathe sthitaḥ । niṣpetuḥ sarvato digbhyo yato haratanus tataḥ ।। mumoca ruṣito rudras tad adbhutam ivābhavat ।। tato viśīrṇadehās te catvāro api samantataḥ ।
nādṛśyanta śaraiś channā dahyamānāś ca vahninā ।। tato bhūtāni vitresur devāś ca bhayaviklavāḥ । hato ayam iti vijñāya āgneyāntarhite harau ।। tataḥ kruddho hṛṣīkeśaḥ pratiṣidhyāgnisaṃcayaṃ ।
jagrāha vāruṇaṃ so astraṃ vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān ।। prayukte vāsudevena vāruṇāstre atitejasi । āgneyaṃ praśamaṃ yātam astraṃ vāruṇatejasā ।। tasmin pratihate hy astre vāsudevena saṃyuge ।
mumocāstrāṇi catvāri yugāntāgninibhāni saḥ ।। vāsudevo api cāstrāṇi dṛṣṭvā viprahitāni vai । atrāṇāṃ vāruṇārthāya vāsudevo mumoca ha ।। jagrāha vaiṣṇavaṃ so astraṃ vyāditāsyāntakopamam ।।
bhūtayakṣagaṇāś caiva bāṇānīkaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ । diśaḥ pradudruvuḥ sarve bhayamohitalocanāḥ ।। pramāthagaṇabhūyiṣṭhe sainye dīrṇe mahāsuraḥ । nirjagāma tato bāṇo yuddhāyabhimukhas tvaran ।। bhīmapraharaṇair ghorair daityendraiḥ sumahābalaiḥ । vṛto mahārathair vīrair vajrīva surasattamaiḥ ।। japyaiś ca mantraiś ca tathoṣadhībhir ।mahātmanaḥ svastyayanaṃ pracakruḥ ।sa tatra vastrāṇi śubhāś ca gāvaḥ ।phalāni puṣpāṇi tathaiva niṣkān ।।baleḥ suto brāhmaṇasattamebhyo ।dadau dhanāny āśu yathā dhaneśaḥ ।sahasrasūryo bahukiṃkiṇīkaḥ ।parārdhyajāmbunadahemcitraḥ ।।sahasracandrāyutatārakaś ca ।ratho mahān agnir ivāvabhāti ।tam āsthito dānavasaṃgṛhītaṃ ।mahādhvajaḥ kārmukadhṛk sa bāṇaḥ ।।udvartayiṣyan yadupuṃgavānām ।atīva raudraṃ sa bibharti rūpaṃ ।sa vegavān vīrarathaughasaṃkulo ।viniryayau tān prati daityasāgaraḥ ।।mahārṇavodbhūtataraṃgasaṃkulo ।yathārṇavo lokavināśanāya ।bhīmāni saṃtrāsakarair vapurbhis ।tāny agrato bhānti balāni tasya ।।mahārathāny ucchritakārmukāṇi ।saparvatānīva vanāni rājan ।viniḥsṛtaḥ sāgaratoyavāsād ।atyadbhutaṃ cāhavaṃ draṣṭukāmaḥ ।। na nandī nāpi ca ratho na rudraḥ pratyadṛśyata ।।
astraṃ nārāyaṇaṃ nāma nārāyaṇajighāṃsayā । jagrāha śūlī bhūtātmā devānām atha paśyatām ।। mumoca ca yathāśakti rudro brahmātmasaṃbhavaḥ । vimuktaṃ tena tac cāstraṃ jagāma ca samīpataḥ ।।
śaṃkarasya tad astraṃ tu prahasan keśavas tadā । jagrāha līlayā viṣṇus tūṇau tac ca vyanikṣipat ।। kupito rudrarūpeṇa rudraḥ saṃhāramūrtimān ।। tataḥ śūlaṃ samādāya sarvaśatruvidāraṇam ।
devadānavagandharva yakṣapannagarakṣasām । bhayaṃkaraṃ mumocātha kṛṣṇam uddiśya śaṃkaraḥ ।। tac ca śūlaṃ harir dṛṣṭvā nijaśaktyā nyavārayat ।। tatas trilocanaḥ kruddhaḥ kālāntakayamopamaḥ ।
astraṃ pāśupataṃ yat tu loke khyātaṃ svavīryavat । jagrāhātmasamaṃ sākṣād dhantuṃ keśavam ojasā ।। vijñāyātha tadā viṣṇus tad evāstraṃ samādade ।। dve hy astre praśamaṃ yāte dvābhyāṃ saṃdhārite tadā ।
tripurāntakaraṃ bāṇaṃ jagrāha ca caturmukhaḥ ।। agnimārutasomānāṃ viṣṇos tejaḥ samutthitam । anenāhaṃ haniṣyāmi sabandhuṃ sasutaṃ raṇe ।। iti matvā virūpākṣo dakṣayajñavināśanaḥ । vijñāto vāsudevena cittajñena mahātmanā ।। bāṇenānena bhūteśo māṃ hantuṃ kila niścitaḥ । iti matvā tadā kṛṣṇaḥ pratikāraṃ samārabhat ।
tenāstreṇa tadā kṛṣṇo mantrapūtena keśavaḥ । haraṃ saṃjṛmbhayām āsa kṣiprakārī mahābalaḥ ।। vijṛmbhaṇaṃ nāma tataḥ so astraṃ jagrāha keśavaḥ । vijṛmbhayām āsa haraṃ tenāstreṇa mahābalaḥ । saśaraḥ sadhanuś caiva haras tenāśu jṛmbhitaḥ । saṃjñāṃ na lebhe bhagavān vijetāsurarakṣasām ।। saśaraṃ sadhanuṣkaṃ ca dṛṣtvātmānaṃ vijṛmbhitam । balonmatto atha bāṇo asau śarvaṃ codayate asakṛt । sṛṣṭim anyāṃ sṛjasveti tadā darpavivṛddhaye ।। śaktim anyāṃ sṛjann eva tadā darpavivṛddhaye । tato nanāda bhūtātmā snigdhagambhīranisvanaḥ । pradhmāpayām āsa tadā kṛṣṇaḥ śaṅkhaṃ mahābalaḥ । jṛmbhite ca hare tasmiñ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau sa keśavaḥ । śārṅgaṃ ca kūjayām āsa siṃhanādaṃ vyanīnadat ।। pāravaśyaṃ samāyātaḥ śūlī jṛmbhaṇatejasā । devaṃ vijṛmbhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvabhūtāni tatrasuḥ ।।
dānavāś ca tathā yānti diśo atha vidiśo api ca । bāṇaś cāpi tadā rājan bhītabhītaḥ samāśvasat ।। tato hāhākṛtaṃ sainyaṃ paśyataḥ śūlinas tadā । kiṃ kurmaḥ kva gamiṣyāma iti dānavasattamāḥ । sthitāś ca vimukhā rājan kartavye mūḍhacetasaḥ ।। atha rudro api sahasā jṛmbhaṇāstreṇa mohitaḥ । kṛtyākṛtyavimūḍhātmā na kiṃ cid pratyapadyata ।। dhyāthātho manasā tātaṃ bhaktigrāhyam atīndriyam । parāt parataraṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvalokeśvareśvaram । nārāyaṇaṃ prabhuṃ kṛṣṇam anantaṃ puruṣottamam ।। yadi dharmo bhavej jyāyān yuktaṃ madapasarpaṇam । iti dhyātvā haraḥ śīghraṃ tasmād deśād apākramat । apayāte tato deve kṛṣṇe caiva mahātmani । punaś cāsīt kathaṃ yuddhaṃ pareṣāṃ lomaharṣaṇam । abhidudrāva kṛṣṇaṃ ca balaṃ pradyumnam eva ca ।। tataḥ śaraśatair ugrais tān vivyādha raṇe guhaḥ । amarṣaroṣasaṃkruddhaḥ kumārapravaro nadan । śarāṇāṃ śatasāhasrair vivyādha samare guhaḥ । vāsudevaṃ sahasreṇa śatena balam eva ca । pradyumnaṃ bāṇasāhasrair jaghāna samare guhaḥ । śoṇitaughaplutair gātraiḥ pratyayudhyan guhaṃ tadā ।।
vāyavyāgneyapārjanyair bibhidur dīptatejasaḥ ।। tān astrāṃs tribhir evāstrair vinivārya sa pāvakiḥ । śailavāruṇasāvitrais tān sa vivyādha sāyakaiḥ । śaraughān astramāyābhir grasanti sma mahātmanaḥ ।। bāṇaughe vivṛte tasmin paramakrodhadīpitaḥ । yadā tadā guhaḥ kruddhaḥ prajvalann iva tejasā ।
saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭaḥ saṃkhye jagrāha sa guhas tadā ।। ugre paramadurdharṣe lokakṣayakare tadā ।। pradhāvan sarvabhūtāni dahyamānāni sarvataḥ । astratejaḥpramūḍhe tu viṣaṇṇe jagati prabhuḥ ।
keśavaḥ keśimathanaś cakraṃ jagrāha vīryavān ।। cakram apraticakrasya loke khyātaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। meghair ivātapāpāye savitur maṇḍalaṃ mahat ।। tasmin brahmaśirasy astre śaktiṃ jagrāha kāñcanīm ।।
krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ ।guhaḥ prajajvāla raṇe haviṣevāgnir ulbaṇaḥ ।। śatrughīṃ jvalitāṃ divyāṃ ।amoghāṃ dayitāṃ ghorāṃ sarvalokabhayāvahām । ghaṇṭāmālākulāṃ śaktiṃ cikṣepa ruṣito guhaḥ ।। nanāda balavac cāpi nādaṃ śatrubhayaṃkaram ।। sā ca kṣiptā tadā tena brahmaṇyena mahātmanā । āghāvantī mahāśaktiḥ kṛṣṇasya vadhakāṅkṣiṇī ।।
tato vidyādharāḥ sarve gandharvā ṛṣayas tathā । śaktiṃ prajvalitāṃ dṛṣṭvā dagdhaḥ kṛṣṇa iti bruvan ।। huṃkāreṇaiva nirbhartsya pātayām āsa bhūtale ।। siṃhanādaṃ tataś cakruḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।।
punaś cakraṃ sa jagrāha bhūtāntakaraṇaṃ tadā ।। musalaṃ lāṅgalaṃ caiva jagrāha ruṣito balaḥ । tato bhīmo guho devaḥ kartavye vismṛto abhavat । kumārarakṣaṇārthāya vibhajya svatanuṃ tadā । digvāsā devavacanāt prātiṣṭhat tatra kauṭavī ।
lambā nāma mahābhāgā bhāgo devyās tathāṣṭamaḥ । citrā kanakaśaktis tu sā ca nagnā sthitāntare ।। athāntarā kumārasya devīṃ dṛṣṭvā mahābhujaḥ । parāṅmukhas tato vākyam uvāca madhusūdanaḥ ।
digvāsā vikaṭā dhūmrā karāḷā nirṇatodarī । bāhū prasārya sahasā grasantīvāmbaraṃ mahat । apagacchāpagaccha tvaṃ dhigdhig ity eva so abravīt ।। kim evaṃ kuruṣe vighnaṃ niścitasya vadhaṃ prati ।। śrutvaiva vacanaṃ tasya kauṭavī tu tadā vibho । naiva vāsaḥ samādhatte kumāraparirakṣaṇāt । apavāhya guhaṃ śīghram apayāhi raṇājirāt । svasti hy evaṃ bhaved adya mokṣyase yotsyatā mayā ।। tāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā sthitāṃ devo hariḥ saṃgrāmamūrdhani । saṃjahāra tataś cakraṃ bhagavān vāsavānujaḥ ।। evam ukte tu vacane devadevena dhīmatā । apavāhya guhaṃ devī harasāṃnidhyam āgatā ।। etasminn antare caiva vartamāne mahābhaye । kumāre rakṣite devyā bāṇas taṃ deśam āyayau ।। apayātaṃ guhaṃ dṛṣṭvā muktaṃ kṛṣṇena saṃyugāt । bāṇas cintayate tatra svayaṃ yotsyāmi mādhavam । tasmād vaktrākṣi gacha tvaṃ yataḥ skandopagachati । etad eva paraṃ tasya bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ । bhūtakṣayagaṇās tatra bāṇānīkaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ । diśaḥ pradudruvuḥ sarve bhayamohitalocanāḥ ।। pramāthagaṇabhūyiṣṭhe sainye dīrṇe mahāsuraḥ । nirjagāma tato bāṇo yuddhāyābhimukhas tvaran ।। bhīmapraharaṇair ghorair daityendraiḥ sumahārathaiḥ । mahābalair mahāvīrair vajrīva surasattamaiḥ ।। purohitāḥ śatruvadhaṃ vadantas ।tathaiva cānye śrutaśīlavṛddhāḥ ।japaiś ca mantraiś ca tathauṣadhībhir ।mahātmanaḥ svastyayanaṃ pracakruḥ ।śaśāpa caināṃ ruṣito yaś ca māṃ bhaktisaṃyutaḥ । dvādaśābdaṃ namas kuryāt tenābhūd yat phalaṃ mahat ।। tadā saṃdarśanāt tasya tat phalaṃ naśyatāṃ mahat । sadā digambarā bhūyas tiṣṭha vā tvaṃ yatheṣṭataḥ ।। ity uktvā devadevo api vihāya guham acyutaḥ । parāvṛtya sthitas tūrṇaṃ sabalaḥ sasutas tadā । tadāprabhṛti rājendra digvāsāḥ sābhavat tadā । apākrāmad guho yuddhād yuddhāyaiva ca keśavaḥ । rāmapradyumnasaṃyukto garuḍe garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। nirjite ca jvare tasmin hare caiva guhe tadā ।
siṃhanādaiś ca daityānāṃ bāṇaḥ kṛṣṇam abhidravat ।। śaktīś caiva gadāś caiva cāpāni vividhāni ca । parighāṃś ca mahāghorāṃś cakrāṇi ca bahūni ca । bāṇānāṃ dhārayām āsa sahasram amitaujasām । dṛṣṭvā bāṇaṃ tu niryātaṃ yuddhāyaiva vyavasthitam । āruhya garuḍaṃ kṛṣṇo bāṇāyābhimukho yayau । gatvātha kiṃ cid dṛṣṭvaiva svabalaṃ keśavaṃ tadā । vainateyasamārūḍhaṃ kṛṣṇam apratimaujasam ।।
atha nāṇas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā pramukhe pratyupasthitam । uvāca vacanaṃ kruddho vāsudevaṃ tarasvinam । dvārakāṃ dvārakāsthān vā suhṛdo drakṣyase na ca ।। tvam adyāṣṭabhujaḥ saṃkhye kathaṃ bāhusahasriṇā । mayābhibhūtaḥ samare muhūrṣuḥ kālacoditaḥ ।।
mayā saha samāgamya yotsyase garuḍadhvaja ।। dvārakāṃ śoṇitapure nihataḥ saṃsmariṣyasi ।। adya bāhusahasraṃ me koṭibhūtaṃ niśāmaya ।। nāhaṃ guho na ca haro na jvaro nāpi cāgnayaḥ । baliputraṃ tu māṃ viddhi bāṇam apratimaṃ raṇe ।
parākramarasopetā mattebhād iva śīkarāḥ । niścaranti mahāghorā vātoddhūtā ivormayaḥ ।। jagad didhakṣann iva khe mahāsūrya ivoditau ।। apiban mṛtyunāviṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇo bāṇam abhidravat ।। kṣobhavisphūrjite tasya raktanetre babhūvatuḥ । jagad didhakṣū yugapan mahāsūryāvivoditau ।
ehy ehi yudhyasva raṇe kiṃ mithyāgarjitena te ।। bhavān eva jayen nityaṃ bahvabaddhaṃ prabhāṣase ।। cirāyāvāṅmukho dīnaḥ patitaḥ śeṣyase asura ।। kākagṛdhrabaḷaiś caiva sarvataḥ pāṭito atha vā ।
nirbibheda raṇe kṛṣṇas tv amoghair dīptatejasaiḥ ।। vinirbhinnas tu kṛṣṇena mārgaṇairmarmabhedibhiḥ । jvaladbhir iva saṃsaktais tasmin yuddhe sudāruṇe ।। tataḥ parighanistriṃśair gadātomaraśaktibhiḥ ।
vinindamānau saṃyattau yuddhe ceratur ojasā ।। musalaiḥ paṭṭisaiś cāpi chādayām āsa keśavam ।। yodhayām āsa samare dvibāhum atha līlayā । tatas tu samare hantuṃ hiraṇyakaśipor yathā ।
sahasrabāhunā sārdham aṣṭabāhur ayudhyata । bāṇena saha saṃgamya śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।। lāghavaṃ vīkṣya kṛṣṇasya balisūnū ruṣānvitaḥ । mumocāstraṃ tadā yuddhe kṛṣṇo bāṇaḥ pratāpavān । brahmaṇā vihitaṃ pūrvaṃ tan mumoca baleḥ sutaḥ ।।
prādur āsaṃs tato raudrā na prājñāyata kiṃ cana ।। sughorāṇi ca sarvaśaḥ । tamasā saṃvṛte loke । aho dhig iti devānāṃ carate vāg udīritā ।। ghorarūpā mahāvegā niṣpetur bāṇavṛṣṭayaḥ ।।
astre vimukte bāṇena dahyamāne ca keśave ।। pārjanyaṃ nāma bhagavān yamāntakanibhaṃ raṇe ।। tato vitimire loke sa cāgniḥ praśamaṃ gataḥ । dānavā moghasaṃkalpāḥ sarve abhuvaṃs tadā bhṛśam । tato devagaṇāḥ sarve praṇedur jahṛṣus tadā ।।
musalaiḥ paṭṭisaiś caiva śūlam udgarakasmaraiḥ ।। punaḥ saṃvārayām āsa keśavaḥ śatrusūdanaḥ ।। keśavasya tu bāṇena vartamāne mahāhave ।। tasya śārṅgavinirmuktaiḥ śarair aśanisaṃnibhaiḥ । tilaśas tad rathaṃ cakre sāśvadhvajapatākinam ।। ciccheda kavacaṃ kāyān mukuṭaṃ ca mahāprabham । kārmukaṃ ca mahātejā hastāc cāpaṃ ca keśavaḥ ।। vivyādha cainam urasi nārācena smayann iva ।। sa marmābhihataḥ saṃkhye pramumohālpacetanaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā mūrchitaṃ bāṇaṃ prahāraparipīḍitam । prāsādavaraśṛṅgastho nārado munipuṃgavaḥ ।। utthāyāpaśyata tadā kakṣāsphoṭanatatparaḥ । vādayāno nakhāṃś caiva diṣṭyā diṣṭyeti cābravīt ।। aho me saphalaṃ janma jīvitaṃ ca sujīvitam । dṛṣṭaṃ me yad idaṃ citraṃ dāmodaraparākramam ।। jaya bāṇaṃ mahābāho daiteyaṃ devapūjita । yad artham avatīrṇo asi tat karma saphalaṃ kuru ।। evaṃ stutvā tadā devaṃ bāṇaiḥ khaṃ dyotayañ śitaiḥ । itas tataḥ saṃpatadbhir nārado vyacarad raṇe ।। prāyudhyetāṃ dhvajau tatra tāv anyonyam abhidrutau । garuḍasya ca saṃgrāme mayūrasya ca yudhyataḥ ।।
anyonyaṃ jaghnatuḥ krodhān mayūrgaruḍāv ubhau ।। jagrāha śirasi kruddhas tuṇḍenābhyahanat tadā ।। padbhyāṃ pārśvābhighātāṃś ca dattvā ghorān anekaśaḥ ।। niḥsaṃjñaṃ pātayām āsa gaganād iva parvatam ।।
papāta tasmāt sahasā vegena mahatā balī । bāṇaḥ paramasaṃvignaś cintayan kāryam ātmanaḥ ।। mayātibalamattena na kṛtaṃ suhṛdāṃ vacaḥ । paśyatāṃ devadaityānāṃ prāpto asmy āpadam uttamām । cintayad bhagavān rudro bāṇarakṣaṇam āturaḥ ।।
nandikeśvara saṃyāhi yato bāṇas tato ratham ।। rathenānena divyena siṃhayuktena bhāsvatā । bāṇaṃ saṃyojayāśu tvam alaṃ yuddhāya cānagha । yāhi prabhavase tāta bāṇaṃ saṃrakṣa gamyatām ।। yato bāṇas tato gatvā bāṇam āha śanair idam ।।
mayā sārathinā vīra ehi yudhyasva māciram । sa nandinā tathoktaḥ san bāṇaḥ parabalārdanaḥ । tato yudhyasva kṛṣṇaṃ vai dānavāntakaraṃ raṇe । ārūḍhaḥ sa tathety uktvā mahādevasya taṃ ratham ।।
tathety uktvā bhavaratham āruroha sa dānavaḥ । āruḍhasya tu bāṇasya taṃ rathaṃ brahmanirmitam । śuśubhe rūpam atyartham ādityasyeva cāmbare । rūpam āsīt purā yadvat tripuraṃ vai didhakṣataḥ । dīptaṃ brahmaśiro nāma bāṇaḥ kruddho ativīryavān ।। lokasaṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ hi tat sṛṣṭaṃ padmayoninā ।। loke prakhyātayaśasaṃ bāṇam apratimaṃ raṇe ।।
ayam asmi sthito yuddhe yudhyasva puruṣo bhava ।। sahasrabāhū rāmeṇa dvibāhuḥ samare kṛtaḥ ।। pūrvaṃ bāhusahasravān । mahābalaḥ sa rāmeṇa । cakraṃ te darpaśamanaṃ karoti raṇamūrdhani ।।
yāvat te darpaśamanaṃ karomy adya svabāhunā । tiṣṭhedānīṃ na me adya tvaṃ mokṣyase raṇamūrdhani ।। atha tad durlabhaṃ dṛṣṭvā yuddhaṃ paramadāruṇam । tathā devāsurasamaṃ harṣān nṛtyati nāradaḥ ।। nirjitāś ca gaṇāḥ sarve pradyumnena mahātmanā । nikṣiptavādā yudhyasva devadevaṃ gatāḥ punaḥ । jagrāha puruṣavyāghro bāṇabāhupraśāntaye ।।
tejo yaj jyotiṣāṃ caiva tejo vajrāśanes tathā । prājāpatyaṃ ca yat tejas tac cakre paryavasthitam ।। tretāgneś caiva yat tejo yac cāgner brahmacāriṇaḥ । ṛṣīṇāṃ ca tapo jñānaṃ tac cakre paryavasthitam ।। pativratānāṃ yat tejaḥ prāṇaṃ ca mṛgapakṣiṇām । yac ca cakradhareṣv asti tac cakre saṃniveśitam ।। nāgarākṣasayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvāpsarasām api । trailokyasya ca yat tejaḥ sarvaṃ cakre vyavasthitam । yac ca tejas tathā śaṃbhor yamasya varuṇasya ca । vapuṣā teja ādatte bāṇasya pramukhe sthitam ।।
jñātvātitejasaṃ cakraṃ kṛṣṇenābhyudyataṃ raṇe । aprameyaṃ hy avihitaṃ rudrāṇīm abravīc chivaḥ ।। ajeyam etat trailokye cakraṃ kṛṣṇena dhāryate । bāṇaṃ trāyasva devi tvaṃ yāvac cakraṃ na muñcati ।। tatas tryakṣavacaḥ śrutvā devī lambām athābravīt । gachaihi lambe tvaṃ śīghraṃ bāṇasaṃrakṣaṇaṃ prati ।। tato yogaṃ samādhāya adṛśyā himavatsutā । kṛṣṇasyaikasya tad rūpaṃ darśayanty āgatāntikam । pramukhe vāsudevasya digvāsāḥ koṭavī sthitā ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvātha punaḥ prāptāṃ devīṃ rudrasya saṃgatām । lambādvitīyāṃ tiṣṭhantīṃ kṛṣṇo vacanam abravīt । bhūyaḥ sāmarṣatāmrākṣī vivastrāvasthitā raṇe ।।
hanmi bāṇaṃ na saṃśayaḥ । evam uktā tu bāṇena । bāṇasaṃrakṣaṇārthinī । girā madhurayā devī ।
