jāne tvāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sraṣṭāraṃ puruṣottamam । mahābhāgaṃ mahādevam anantaṃ nīlam avyayam । padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśa lokānām ādisaṃbhavam । devadeva jagannātha viṣṇo jiṣṇo jagatpate ।
nārhase deva hantuṃ vai bāṇam apratimaṃ raṇe ।। prayaccha hy abhayaṃ bāṇe jīvaputrītvam eva ca ।। mayā dattavaro hy eṣa bhūyaś ca parirakṣyate । na me mithyā samudyogaṃ kartum arhasi mādhava ।। evam ukte tu vacane kṛṣṇaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ । kruddhaḥ prabhāṣate vākyaṃ śṛṇu satyaṃ tu bhāminī ।। bāṇo bāhusahasreṇa nardate darpam āśritaḥ । eteṣāṃ chedanaṃ tv adya kartavyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। dvibāhunā ca bāṇena jīvaputrī bhaviṣyasi । saṃtyajya cāsuraṃ darpaṃ na ca māṃ saṃśrayiṣyati ।। evam ukte tu vacane kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā । provāca devī bāṇo ayaṃ devadevo bhaved iti ।। atha tāṃ kārttikeyasya mātaraṃ so abhibhāṣya vai । dhig dhig ity abravīt tāṃ tu duṣṭe dhvaṃseti keśavaḥ । provāca bāṇaṃ samare bhrāmayaṃś cakram uttamam ।। tataḥ provāca vacanaṃ bāṇaṃ kaṃsārisūdanaḥ ।
aśaktānām iva raṇe dhigbāṇa tava pauruṣam ।। nimīlitākṣo vyasṛjad bāṇaṃ prati mahābalaḥ ।। kṣepaṇād yasya muhyanti lokāḥ sasthāṇujaṅgamāḥ । kravyādāni ca bhūtāni tṛptiṃ yānti mahāmṛdhe ।। tamapratimakarmāṇaṃ samānaṃ sūryavarcasā । cakram udyamya samare kopadīpto gadādharaḥ ।। sa muṣṇan dānavaṃ tejaḥ samare svena tejasā । ciccheda bāhūṃś cakreṇa śrīdharaḥ paramaujasā । kṣiptaṃ tu vāsudevena bāṇasya raṇamūrdhani ।
bāṇasya rathamārge ca dvitīya iva bhāskaraḥ । viṣṇor astraṃ sunābhaṃ vai śaighryayogān na dṛśyate ।। bāṇasya chedanaṃ cakre tac cakraṃ raṇamūrdhani ।। kṛtvā dvibāhuṃ taṃ bāṇaṃ chinnaśākham iva drumam । punaḥ karāgraṃ kṛṣṇasya cakraṃ prāptaṃ sudarśanam ।। kṛtakṛte tu saṃprāpte cakre daitye vipātite ।
abhavat parvatākāraś chinnabāhur mahāsuraḥ ।। chinnaśākho yathā vṛkṣaś chinnapakṣo yathā khagaḥ ।। chittvā bāhusahasraṃ tu bāṇasya ca sudarśanam । jagāma devadevasya pārśvaṃ ripunighātinaḥ ।। provāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ cakro medaḥsamākulaḥ । ājñāpaya jagannātha śiraś chettuṃ durātmanaḥ ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇo hṛṣīkeśas tad ādatte sudarśanam । asṛṅmattaś ca vividhān nādān muñcan yathā ghanaḥ ।। tasya nādena mahatā keśavo ripusūdanaḥ । vyāvidhya sahasā kṛṣṇaḥ śiraś chettuṃ samārabhat । cakraṃ bhūyaḥ kṣeptukāmo nāṇanāśārtham acyutaḥ । tam upetya mahādevaḥ kumārasahito abravīt ।।
sahomayā haro devo jvareṇa ca samanvitaḥ । na hy enaṃ vadhakāmas tvaṃ yad icchet pārvatīhitam ।। hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāś catvāro lokaviśrutāḥ । hrādaḥ prahrādaḥ saṃhrādaḥ anuhrādaś caturthakaḥ ।।
prahrādāya varo dattaś caiṣāṃ madhye varāthine । avyadhyas tava vaṃśo astu daityaughāḥ satataṃ mayā ।। iti pratiśrutaṃ pūrvam aparāghaparāya ca । madhukaiṭabhahantāraṃ devadevaṃ sanātanam ।।
ādidevam ajaṃ viṣṇuṃ surādhyakṣaṃ purātanam । ajeyas tvaṃ tribhir lokaiḥ sadevāsuramānuṣaiḥ ।। tava prasādajo brahmā tathāhaṃ krodhasaṃbhavaḥ । vande ahaṃ tvāṃ jagannāthaṃ jagatām īśvaraṃ harim ।। namāmi nirguṇaṃ viṣṇo tvām ādyam akhilaṃ raṇe । niṣkalaṃ tvāṃ hare devaṃ namāmi puruṣottamam ।। trayīmūrte purāṇātmann namāmi tvāṃ janārdanam । ajeyo asi sadā viṣṇo yāce tvāṃ nityam avyayam । anivāryam asaṃhāryaṃ raṇe śatrubhayaṃkaram ।।
ye tvā deva prapadyante na te suvyaktimānavāḥ । bhaye mahati magnānāṃ trātā nityaṃ janārdanaḥ ।। ye cāpy asmatkṛtaṃ stotram abhidhāsyanti bhaktitaḥ । te sarvabhayanirmuktā bhaviṣyanti nirāmayāḥ ।। nāthas tvaṃ sarvalokānāṃ viśeṣeṇa mama prabho । kṣamyatāṃ deva bāṇasya matkṛte puruṣottama । tan me na syān mṛṣā vākyam atas tvāṃ kṣamayāmy aham ।। na hy enaṃ vadhakāmasya yadīcchet pārvatīhitam । kṣantavyaṃ bhavatā bhūyo yat kṛtaṃ bhaktavatsala । mānyas tvaṃ deva devānām asurāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
anyathā chedanaṃ kuryāṃ bāṇasyāsya durātmanaḥ । yasmān mānyaḥ sadā deva tasmāj jīvatu bāṇakaḥ । na tāvat kriyate tasmān mām anujñātum arhasi ।। jagāma tatra yatrāste prādyumniḥ sāyakaiś citaḥ ।। gaccha bāṇa kṣatenaiva devadevasya cāgrataḥ ।।
tac chrutvā nandivākyaṃ tu bāṇo agacchata śīghragaḥ । chinnabāhuṃ tato bāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā nandī pratāpavān । apavāhya rathenaiva yato devas tato yayau ।। tato nandī punar bāṇaṃ prāg uvācottaraṃ vacaḥ ।
bāṇa bāṇa pranṛtyasva śreyas tava bhaviṣyati ।। kṛttabāṇa mahādaitya tataḥ śreyas tvam āpsyasi । eṣa devo mahādevaḥ prasādasumukhas tava । jīvitārthī tato bāṇaḥ pramukhe śaṃkarasya vai ।। etac chrutvā vaco nandeḥ śoṇitāṅgaḥ sa dānavaḥ । pravṛtto jīvitārthāya śaṃkaraṃ pramukhe sthitaḥ ।
jaya deva jagannātha jayājeya harāvyaya । jaya bhaktipriya sadā jaya bhūtagaṇārcitaḥ ।। jaya bhasmapradigdhāṅga jaya nagnavidāṃ mukha । umāpate viśvapate jayājeyāvyaya prabho ।।
evamādi tadā bāṇo vilapan bhavatuṣṭaye । avasthāṃ kṛpaṇāṃ prāpto bhayaviklavalocanaḥ ।। tataḥ pranṛttaṃ bāṇaṃ ca cakram apratimaṃ raṇe । bāṇaṃ dvibāhuṃ kṛtvā tu svām eva prakṛtiṃ gatam । taṃ dṛṣṭvā ca pranṛtyantaṃ bhayodvignaṃ punaḥ punaḥ । nandivākyaprajavitaṃ bhaktānugrahakṛd bhavaḥ । karuṇāvaśam āpanno mahādevo abravīd vacaḥ । prānṛtyad bahuśo rājan yathā prīto bhaved bhava । tataḥ prīto abhavad rājan bāṇasyāsya sa līlayā । prasādasumukho ahaṃ te varakālo ayam āgataḥ ।।
yat prārthyase varaṃ bāṇa cirāya manasepsitam । tat te ahaṃ tvāṃ pradāsyāmi tridaśair api durlabham । rudravākyaṃ tataḥ śrutvā bāṇo manasi harṣitaḥ । varān manasi saṃdhārya pravaktum upacakrame । eṣa me prathamo deva varo astu yadi manyase ।। anyaṃ varaṃ vṛṇīṣvādya anugrāhyo asi me sadā ।। bhaktānāṃ nṛtyatām evaṃ putrajanma bheved bhava ।।
madbhaktā ye hi nṛtyanti teṣām evaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। tṛtīyaṃ tvam atho bāṇa varaṃ vara manogatam । tad vidhāsyāmi te putra saphalo astu bhavān iha । vareṇa sā tṛtīyena śāntiṃ gacchatu me bhava ।। akṣataṃ tava gātraṃ ca svasthāvasthaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
cakrapāṭanajā ghorā rujā te surasattama । na bhaviṣyati gātreṣu balavāṃś ca bhaviṣyasi । na te ahaṃ vimukhas tāta prasādasumukho hy aham ।। mahākāla iti khyātaḥ khyātiṃ gaccheyam īśvara ।। evaṃ bhaviṣyatīty āha devo bāṇaṃ mahādyutiḥ । divyarūpo akṣato gātrair nīrujas tvaṃ mamāśrayāt ।। mamātisargād bāṇa tvaṃ bhava caivākutobyahaḥ ।
evaṃ bhaviṣyaty avaśyaṃ yaṃ varaṃ tvam ihecchasi । taṃ taṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te yad icchasi mahāsura ।। dvibāhutve api me deho na virūpo bhaved bhava ।। bhavitā sarvam etat te yathecchasi mahāsura । bhaktas tvaṃ me na cādeyaṃ bhaktānāṃ vidyate mama ।
evaṃ bhaviṣyate bāṇa yat tvayā samudāhṛtam ।। tyaja mūḍhāṃ matiṃ bāṇa mā mohavaśago bhava । paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tatraivāntar adhīyata ।। evaṃ varān bahūṃl labdhvā bāṇaḥ prītimān abhavat ।
jagāma saha rudreṇa mahākālatvam āgataḥ । vāsudevo api bahudhā nāradaṃ paryapṛcchata । kvāniruddhas tu bhagavān saṃyato nāgabandhanaiḥ । śrotum icchāmi tattvena snehaklinnaṃ hi me manaḥ ।।
aniruddhe hṛte vīre kṣubhitā dvārakā purī । śīghraṃ taṃ mokṣayiṣyāmi yad arthaṃ vayam āgatāḥ ।। adya taṃ naṣṭaśatruṃ vai draṣṭum icchāmahe vayam । sa pradeśas tu bhagavan viditas tava suvrata ।।
evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena nāradaḥ pratyabhāṣata । kanyāpure kumāro asau baddho nāgaiś ca mādhava ।। etasminn antare śīghraṃ citralekhā hy upasthitā । bāṇasyottamasattvasya daityendrasya mahātmanaḥ ।
idam antaḥpuraṃ deva praviśasva yathāsukham ।। tataḥ praviṣṭās te sarve aniruddhasya mokṣaṇe । balaḥ suparṇaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca pradyumno nāradas tathā । vāsudevo api sahasā viveśāntaḥpure ripoḥ ।
śararūpā mahāsarpā veṣṭayitvā tanuṃ sthitāḥ ।। kṣitiṃ sarve abhyadhāvanta prakṛtyāvasthitāḥ śarāḥ ।। sthitiḥ prītimanā bhūtvā prāñjalir vākyam abravīt ।। śakto vai pramukhe sthātuṃ sākṣād api śatakratuḥ ।।
ityuktaḥ so adhirūḍhas tu saha dānavakanyayā ।। gurubhiḥ samanujñātās tatas te prayayus tadā । citralekhāsamāyukto yā priyā tasya nityaśaḥ । cakrāyudho gṛhya tadāniruddhaṃ । nighnaṃ cakre bāṇam udīrṇacakram ।
chittvā tu bāṇasya sa bāhucakraṃ । cakrāyudho gṛhya tadāniruddham । puro mahābāṇam udīrṇacakra । nipātite bāhuviśīrṇagātre ।
āruhya garuḍaṃ sarve jitvā bāṇaṃ mahāsuram ।। apaśyanta mahātmāno gāvo divyapayaḥpradāḥ । velāvanavicāriṇyo nānāvarṇāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। abhijñāya tadā rūpaṃ kumbhāṇḍavacanaśravāt । kṛṣṇaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhas tattvato arthaviśāradaḥ ।
āsthito garuḍaṃ devaḥ sarvalokādir avyayaḥ ।। garuḍa prayāhi tatra tvaṃ yatra bāṇasya godhanam । yāsāṃ pītvā kila kṣīram amṛtatvam avāpnuyāt । yāsāṃ pītvā kila kṣīraṃ na jīryanti mahāsurāḥ ।। vijarāś ca jarāṃ tyaktvā bhavanti kila jantavaḥ ।
atha kāryanirodhaḥ syān naiva tāsu manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। iti mām abravīt satyā tāś caitā viditā mama । viśanti sahitāḥ sarvāḥ kāryam atra vidhīyatām ।। so avagāḍho hi sahasā varuṇālayam antikāt ।।
dṛṣṭvā javena garuḍaṃ prāptaṃ vai varuṇālayam । vāruṇāś ca gaṇāḥ sarve vibhrāntāḥ prācalaṃs tadā । pramukhe vāsudevasya nānāpraharaṇodyatam ।। tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ vāruṇaiḥ pannagāriṇā । tatas tu tasya pramukhe vāsudevasya dhīmataḥ । dehā vidyotayanti sma kṛtsnaṃ vai varuṇālayam ।
cakreṇa bhagavāñ śauriś cakāra kadanaṃ mahat । bhagnaṃ balam anādhṛṣyaṃ keśavena mahātmanā । te bhagnāḥ sahasā yānti tam eva varuṇālayam ।। varuṇena prayuktāni dīptaśastrāṇi saṃyuge ।।
tāny ayudhyanta kṛṣṇena pradyumnena balena ca । tāni sarvāṇi sahasā nijaghāna raṇe hariḥ । bhagnaṃ varuṇam āśritya naiva sthānam avindata ।। tad balaṃ balibhiḥ śūrair baladevajanārdanaiḥ । pradyumenāniruddhena garuḍena ca sarvaśaḥ । śaraughair vividhais tīkṣṇair vadhyamānaṃ samantataḥ ।। tato bhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā । varuṇas tv atha saṃkruddho niryayau yatra keśavaḥ । saṃstūyamāno bahudhā varuṇaḥ paryavasthitaḥ ।।
salilasrāviṇā śreṣṭhaṃ cāpam udyamya viṣṭhitaḥ ।। āhvayann iva yuddhe sa visphāritamahādhanuḥ ।। hariṃ hara iva krodhād bāṇajālaiḥ samāvṛṇot ।। bāṇavarṣākulāḥ sarvā diśaś cakre janārdanaḥ ।।
smayann iva tadā kṛṣṇaṃ varuṇaḥ pratyayudhyata ।। vāsudevo abravīd vākyaṃ pramukhe tasya saṃsthitaḥ ।। mayodyataṃ vadhārthaṃ te tiṣṭhedānīṃ sthiro bhava ।। vāruṇāstreṇa saṃyojya nanāda sa mahābalaḥ ।।
vaiṣṇavāstrasya śamane vartante samitiṃjaya ।। āpas tu vāruṇās tatra kṣiptāḥ kṣiptā jvalanti vai । tataś cakraṃ samādāya jvālāmālāsamākulam । moktukāmo jagannātho vāruṇe pratyadṛśyata ।। tataḥ prajvalitāḥ sarve vāruṇāś cakratejasā । vaiṣṇave tu mahāvīrye diśo bhītāḥ pradudruvuḥ ।। tamo jahi mahābhāga rajasā muhyase katham ।।
pañcabhūtāśrayān doṣān ahaṃkāraṃ ca saṃtyaja ।। jyeṣṭhabhāvena mānyas te kiṃ māṃ dagdhum icchasi ।। tvayi na prabhaviṣyanti jagataḥ prabhavo hy asi ।। dharmiṇī bījabhāvena pūrvadharmasamāśritā ।।
tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ jagad idaṃ sa kathaṃ manyase mayi ।। akṣayaś cāvyayaś caiva bhavān eva mahādyute ।। ādikartāsi lokasya tvayaiva bahulīkṛtam ।। na hy ahaṃ prakṛtidveṣī nāhaṃ prakṛtidūṣakaḥ ।।
tasyā vikāraśamane vartase tvaṃ yathāvidhi ।। tān adharmavido mandān bhavān vikurute sadā ।। rajasā vāpi saṃduṣṭā tato mohaḥ pravartate ।। kiṃ mohayasi naḥ sarvān prajāpatir iva svayam ।।
varuṇenaivam uktas tu kṛṣṇo lokaparāyaṇaḥ । bhāvajñaḥ sarvavidvīras tataḥ prītimanā hy abhūt । gāḥ saṃprayaccha me deva śāntyarthaṃ bhīmavikrama ।। ityevam uktaḥ kṛṣṇena vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ । varuṇo hy abravīd būyaḥ śṛṇu me madhusūdana । kathaṃ ca samayaṃ kṛtvā kuryāṃ viphalam anyathā ।।
tvam eva deva sarvasya yathā samayabhedakaḥ । cāritraṃ duṣyate tāta na ca sadbhiḥ praśasyate ।। dharmabhāg īśvaro nityaṃ varjate madhusūdana । na ca lokān avāpnoti pāpaḥ samayabhedakaḥ ।। prasīda dharmalopaś ca mā bhūn me madhusūdana । na māṃ samayabhedena yoktum arhasi mādhava । hatvā māṃ naya gāvas tvam eṣa me samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। etac ca me samākhyātaṃ samayaṃ madhusūdana । satyam eva mahābāho na mithyā tu sureśvara ।। yady evāham anugrāhyo rakṣa māṃ madhusūdana । atha vā goṣu nirbandho hatvā naya mahābhuja । saṃbhāvayāmi dharmajñaṃ matto abhīṣṭo bhavān asi । satyaṃ prabhāṣase yat tvaṃ tasmān madbhāvabhāvitaḥ ।। iti vijñāpitas tena kṛṣṇaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ । bāṇavṛttāntam akhilaṃ śrāvayitvā tu pāne ।। bāṇāsuraṃ puraskṛtya dattaṃ kṛṣnāya godhanam । varuṇena gṛhītvā tu yayau dvāravatīṃ hariḥ । upāyād dvārakāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ śrīmān garuḍavāhanaḥ । avasad vṛṣṇibhiḥ sārdhaṃ stūyamānaḥ samāgataiḥ ।। eṣa te bāṇaviṣayaḥ proktas te janamejaya । pṛcchato bhavato rājan kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi । evam ukto atha bāṇasya gāvo muktvā mahāyaśāḥ ।
abhedyaṃ samayaṃ matvā nyastavādo gavāṃ prati । saṃprahasya tato vākyaṃ vyājahārārthakovidaḥ । mānayan varuṇaṃ devo gā bāṇasya vyamuñcata । tasmān mukto asi yady evaṃ bāṇena samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।
prasṛtair madhurair vākyais tattvārtham anubhāṣitaiḥ ।। kathaṃ pāpaṃ kariṣyāmi varuṇa tvayy ahaṃ prabho । gaccha mukto asi varuṇa satyasaṃdho astu no bhavān । tvatpriyārthaṃ mayā muktā bāṇagāvo na saṃśayaḥ ।।
tatas tūryaninādaiś ca bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaiḥ । argham ādāya varuṇaḥ keśavaṃ pratyapūjayat ।। keśavo ardhaṃ tadā gṛhya varuṇādyadunandanaḥ । balaṃ pūjayate devaḥ kuśalī ca samāhitaḥ ।।
varuṇāyābhayaṃ dattvā vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān । tvadarthaṃ dhenavo muktā bāṇasya tu durātmanaḥ । ity uktvā varuṇaṃ devo gā bāṇasya vimuñcata । prayayau dvārakāṃ cāpi śakrādyair amarair vṛtaḥ ।।
dvārakāṃ prasthito devaḥ śacīpatisahāyavān । gandharvāpsarasaś caiva kiṃnarāś cāntarikṣagāḥ । ṛṣayo nāradamukhā vasiṣṭādyā tapodhanāḥ । anugacchanti viśveśaṃ sarvabhūtādim avyayam ।।
vidyādharagaṇāś caiva ye cānye siddhacāraṇāḥ । āyāntam anugacchanti yaśasā vijayena ca ।। nāradaś ca mahābhāgaḥ prasthito dvārakāṃ prati । tuṣṭo bāṇajayaṃ dṛṣṭvā varuṇaṃ ca kṛtapriyam ।। kailāsaśikharaprakhyair nīlagrīvadharaiś ca taiḥ । pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣaṃ cakre cakragadādharaḥ ।।
saṃjñāṃ prayacchate devo dvārakāpuravāsinām । tenādhmāto mahāśaṅkhaḥ pūrayām āsa rodasī । śrutvā dvāravatī sarvā praharṣam atulaṃ gatā ।। pūrṇakumbhaiś ca lājaiś ca bahuvinyastavistaraiḥ । dvāropaśobhitāṃ kṛtvā sarvāṃ dvāravatīṃ purīm । suśliṣṭarathyāṃ suśrīkāṃ kṛtaratnopaśobhitāṃ ।। viprāś cārghaṃ samādāya tathaiva kulanaigamāḥ । jayaśabdaiś ca vividhaiḥ pūjayanti sma mādhavam । avandanyādavāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śriyā paramayā yutam ।।
trayo anupūrvyā varṇāś ca pūjayanti mahābalam । anantaṃ keśihantāraṃ śreṣṭhipūrvāś ca śreṇayaḥ । saṃstūyamāno govindo dvārakopari viṣṭhitaḥ ।। praharṣam atulaṃ prāptā dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ mahābhujam । bāṇaṃ jitvā mahādevam āyāntaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
prāpte kṛṣṇe mahābhāge sātvatānāṃ mahārathe ।। gatvā ca dūram adhvānaṃ suparṇo drutam āgataḥ । rakṣitā cāpi goptā ca dīrghabāhur janārdanaḥ ।। prāpto ayaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣo manāṃsy āhlādayann iva ।।
vāsudevagṛhaṃ devā viviśus te mahārathāḥ ।। avatīrya suparṇāt tu vāsudevo balas tadā । pradyumnaś cāniruddhaś ca gṛhān praviviśus tadā । sthitāny eva pradṛśyante nānārūpāṇi sarvaśaḥ ।। bhāsvanti tāni dṛśyante vimānāni sahasraśaḥ ।।
atha kṛṣṇo abravīd vākyaṃ kumārāṃs tān sahasraśaḥ । pradyumnādīn samastāṃs tu ślakṣṇaṃ madhurayā girā । sādhyā devās tathānye cāpy avandaṃs tān yathākramam ।। sahasrākṣaṃ mahābhāgaṃ dānavānāṃ bhayaṃkaram । vandadhvaṃ sahitāḥ śakraṃ sagaṇaṃ nāgavāhanam ।। saptarṣayo mahābhāgā matpriyārtham ihāgatāḥ । ṛṣayaś ca mahātmāno vandadhvaṃ ca yathāsukham ।। ete cakradharāś caiva etān vadanta sarvaśaḥ । sāgarāś ca hradāś caiva matpriyārtham ihāgatāḥ । diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva vandadhvaṃ ca yathākramam ।। vāsukipramukhāś caiva nāgā vai sumahābalāḥ । gāvaś ca matpriyārthaṃ vai vandadhvaṃ ca yathākramam ।। jyotīṃṣi saha nakṣatrair yakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥ । āgatā matpriyārthaṃ vai vandadhvaṃ ca yathākramam ।। vāsudevavacaḥ śrutvā kumārāḥ praṇatāḥ sthitāḥ । yathākrameṇa sarveṣāṃ devatānāṃ mahātmanām ।। sarvān divaukaso dṛṣṭvā paurā vismayam āgatāḥ । pūjārtham atha saṃbhārān pragṛhya drutam āgatāḥ । prāpyate yad ihāsmābhir iti vācaś caranti hi ।।
kiranti paurāḥ sarvāṃs tān pūjayanto divaukasaḥ ।। dvārakāvāsinaḥ sarve pūjayanti divaukasaḥ ।। sātyakiṃ colmukaṃ caiva vipṛthuṃ ca mahābalam ।। akrūraṃ ca mahābhāgaṃ tathā niṣadham eva ca ।
atha śakro mahābhāgaḥ samakṣaṃ yadumaṇḍale । stuvantaṃ keśihantāraṃ tatrovācottaraṃ vacaḥ । andhakaṃ ca śubhākṣaṃ ca tato vacanam abravīt ।। yojayitvā raṇe caiva yaśasā pauruṣeṇa ca ।।
ramayaty atitejasvī divīva ca divaukasaḥ । eṣa bāṇaṃ raṇe jitvā dvārakāṃ punar āgatāḥ ।। sthāpayitvā dvibāhutve prāpto ayaṃ svapurīṃ hariḥ ।। tad apy avasitaṃ kṛtsnaṃ naṣṭaśokā vayaṃ kṛtāḥ ।।
kālo yāsyaty avirataṃ viṣayeṣv eva sajjatām ।। pranaṣṭaśokā raṃsyāmaḥ sarva evāmarāḥ sukham ।। evaṃ stutvā sahasrākṣaḥ keśavaṃ dānavāntakam । āpṛcchya taṃ mahābhāgaḥ sarvair devagaṇair vṛtaḥ ।।
tataḥ punaḥ pariṣvajya kṛṣṇaṃ lokanamaskṛtam । ity uktvā yādavān sarvān kṛṣṇaṃ saṃpūjya vāsavaḥ । ṛṣayaś ca mahātmāno jayāśīrbhir mahaujasam । yathāgataṃ punar yātā yakṣarākṣasakiṃnarāḥ ।।
puraṃdare divaṃ yāte padmanābho mahābalaḥ । apṛcchata mahābhāgaḥ sarvān kuśalam avyayam ।। tataḥ kilakilāśabdaṃ nirvamantaḥ sahasraśaḥ । gacchanti kaumudīṃ draṣṭuṃ so anaghaḥ priyayā saha ।
dvārakāṃ prāpya kṛṣṇas tu reme yadugaṇair vṛtaḥ ।। vividhān sarvakāmārthāñ śriyā paramayā yutaḥ । viṣṇur yadukulaśreṣṭho vāsudeveti viśrutaḥ ।। jāto vṛṣṇiṣu devakyāṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi ।।
uktās te vistarāḥ sarve pūrvaṃ ye janamejaya ।। vāsudevagatiś caiva sā mayā samudāhṛtā ।। sarveṣv āścaryakalpeṣu nāsty āścaryam avaiṣṇavam ।। deveṣv api sadaityeṣu nāsti dhanyataro acyutāt ।।
gaganaṃ bhūr diśaś caiva salilaṃ jyotir eva ca ।। sarvam etaj jagaddhātā viṣṇur eva na cāparaḥ । anantaś caiva nāgānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ śaṃkaraḥ smṛtaḥ । jaṅgamājaṅgamaṃ caiva jagannārāyaṇodbhavaṃ ।
etasmāc ca jagat sarvaṃ prasūyeta janārdanāt । jagac ca sarvaṃ deveśas taṃ namas kuru bhārata ।। pūjyaś ca satataṃ sarvair devair eṣa sanātanaḥ । pūjyo ayaṃ devadeveśaḥ pūjyair api savāsavaiḥ । ijyaś ca devadeveśas taṃ namaskuru bhārata ।। ādikartā ca bhoktā ca bhūtādir bhūtir eva ca । namaskuru jagannāthaṃ bhūyo bhūyaḥ prabho nṛpa ।। namaskuru sadā viṣṇuṃ yādavaṃ bhūtabhāvanam । namasyāmo jagannāthaṃ devakīṃ ca hariṃ sadā ।। dhyāhi nityaṃ jagannāthaṃ prayatnaparamo bhava । śreyas tava sadā viṣṇur vidhāsyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। namas tasmin samādhatsva mano anudhyāhi tat param । upāsyaś ca sadā viṣṇur manasā rājasattama । namaskuru jagannāthaṃ bhūyo bhūyo jagatpate । vāsudevaṃ sadā dhyāhi keśavaṃ keśisūdanam ।। nārāyaṇam aṇīyāṃsaṃ dhyāhi yatnena sattamam । dhyāto hi sarvapāpāni nāśayiṣyaty asaṃśayam । vaṃśapratiṣṭhāṃ atulāṃ śravaṇādeva lapsyase ।।
keśavasya ca māhātmyaṃ nādharmas tān bhajiṣyati ।। teṣāṃ dharmo bhaved rājan nātra kāryā vicāraṇā । pṛcchatas tāta yajñe asmin nivṛtte janamejaya ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।
kalpa utthāya yo nityaṃ kīrtayet susamāhitaḥ । na tasya durlabhaṃ kiṃ cid iha loke paratra ca ।। brāhmaṇaḥ sarvavedī syāt kṣatriyo vijayī bhavet । vaiśyo dhanasamṛddhaḥ syāc chūdro gacchec ca sadgatim ।
nāśubhaṃ prāpnuyāt kiṃcid dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt ।। harivaṃśam imaṃ puṇyaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti mahīpatiḥ । āyur ārogyam aiśvaryam atulām ṛddhim āpnuyāt । aputro labhate putram adhano api dhanaṃ vrajet । ariṣṭaśamanaṃ sarvaṃ prāpnoti śubhasaṃtatim ।। vāsudeve parāṃ bhaktiṃ bhogān apy atulān bhuvi । avyāhataṃ pratāpaṃ ca yaśo vindeta mānavaḥ ।। harivaṃśam imaṃ śṛṇvan maṇḍalādhipatir bhavet । ācandratārakaṃ bhūmā vaśeṣām ṛddhim āpnuyāt । ya idaṃ śṛṇuyān nityaṃ viṣṇubhaktād dvijarṣabhāt । sadā digvijayī bhūyāc caturaṅgabalānvitaḥ ।। vede rāmāyaṇe caiva harivaṃśe ca bhārata । ādau madhye tathaivānte hariḥ sarvatra gīyate ।। tasmād dhariḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ । ādikartā mahībhartā śriyā sārdhaṃ jagatpatiḥ ।। tasya vaṃśam imaṃ puṇyam itihāsaṃ purātanam । ye narāḥ kīrtayiṣyanti nāsti teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ । asakṛt paṭha rājendra harivaṃśaṃ maharddhimat । manas te niścalaṃ bhūyāt prasanno astu janārdanaḥ । śrutavān amalo bhūtvā harivaṃśaṃ dvijarṣabhāḥ ।। saṃkṣepād vistareṇāpi tatra sarve tapodhanāḥ ।
proktā vai sarvavaṃśās te kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi te ।। śaunakādyās tu munayaḥ prītās tuṣṭās tadābhavan । namaskurvanti deveśaṃ bhaktinamrā munīśvarāḥ । ādidevaṃ hariṃ viṣṇuṃ namasyanti sma mādhavam । taṃ vedaśāstrapariniṣṭhitaśuddhabuddhiṃ ।carmāmbaraṃ suramunīndranutaṃ kavīndram ।kṛṣṇatviṣaṃ kanakapiṅgajaṭākalāpaṃ ।vyāsaṃ namāmi śirasā tilakaṃ dvijānām ।।muniṃ snigdhāmbudābhāsaṃ vedavyāsam akalmaṣam । vedāvāsaṃ sarasvatyā vāsaṃ vyāsaṃ namāmy aham ।। vande sarasvatīṃ devīṃ bhuvanatrayamātaram । yat prasādād ṛte snigdhaṃ jihvā na parivartate । harivaṃśasya śeṣasya kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśanīm । kasmin pratiṣṭhito vaṃśaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām ।।
etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ mama । tvattaḥ kathayataḥ sarvaṃ vedmy ahaṃ taṃ parisphuṭam । candrāpīḍaś ca nṛpatiḥ sūryāpīḍaś ca mokṣavit ।। janamejaya ity eva kṣatraṃ bhuvi pariśrutam ।। satyakarṇo mahābāhur yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।।
aputraḥ sa tu dharmātmā praviveśa tapovanam ।। sucāror duhitā subhrūr mālinī bhrātṛmālini ।। anvagacchata taṃ pūrvair mahāprasthānam acyutam ।। pathi sā suṣuve subhrūr vane rājīvalocanam ।।
pativratā mahābhāgā draupadīva purā patīn ।। dayārthaṃ tasya meghās tu prādurāsan mahātmanaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā kṛpānvitau gṛhya taṃ prakṣālayatāṃ jale ।। ajaśyāmau ca pārśvau tāv ubhāv api samāhitau ।।
ājagamānayo pārśvaṃ pibann apy anayoḥ stanau । ājaśyāmasya te pārśve rūḍhe vai saṃabhūvatuḥ । taṃ tathaiva ca tiṣṭhantaṃ ajapārśve kumārakam । tato ajapārśva iti tau cakrāte tasya nāma ha ।।
sa tu vemakaśālāyāṃ ubhābhyām abhivardhitaḥ ।। sevakasya tu tāṃ bhāryām ūhatus tasya kāraṇāt । vemakyāḥ sa tu putro abhūd brāhmaṇau sucivau ca tau ।। sa eṣa pauravo vaṃśaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।
jarāsaṃkramaṇe pūrvaṃ tadā prītena dhīmatā ।। apauravā na tu mahī bhaviṣyati kadācana ।। tatas teṣūpaviṣṭeṣu sadasyaiḥ saha śaunakaḥ । yathā puroktāni tathā vyāsaśiṣyeṇa dhīmatā ।।
prīṇāty asmān amṛtavat sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।। sukhaśravyatayā dhīra mano hlādayatīva naḥ । saute kim akarot paścāt sarpasatrād anantaram ।। yad ārabhata pārikṣit tan me kathaya suvrata ।
yad ārabhat tad ākhyāsye sarpasatrād anantaram ।। yaṣṭuṃ sa vājimedhena saṃbhārān upacakrame ।। yakṣye ahaṃ vājimedhena haya utsṛjyatām iti ।। pārikṣitaṃ draṣṭum adīnasattvam dvaipāyanaḥ sarvaparāvarajñaḥ ।।
arghyapādyāsanaṃ dattvā pūjayāmāsa śāstrataḥ ।। tatas teṣūpaviṣṭeṣu sadasyaiḥ saha śaunaka । kathā bahuvidhāś citrāś cakrāte vedasaṃhitāḥ ।। pitāmahaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ātmanaḥ prapitāmaham ।।
nimeṣamātram iva me sukhaśravyatayā gatam ।। tvayā tv abhihitaṃ brahmañ śaṅkhe kṣīram ivāhitam ।। tathā tṛptiṃ na gacchāmi śrutvemāṃ bhāratīṃ kathām ।। hetuḥ kurūṇāṃ nāśasya rājasūyo mato mama ।।
rājasūyaṃ tathā manye yuddhārtham upakalpitam ।। tasyānte sumahadyuddham abhavat tārakāmayam ।। devāsuram abhūd yuddhaṃ sarvabhūtakṣayāvaham ।। tatrāpy āḍībakam abhūd yuddhaṃ kṣatravināśanam ।।
mahābhāratasaṃhāraḥ saṃbhṛto agnir iva kratuḥ ।। rājasūyo mahāyajñaḥ kimarthaṃ na nivāritaḥ ।। mithyāpraṇīte yajñāṅge prajānāṃ saṃkṣayo dhruvaḥ ।। atītānāgatajñaś ca nāthaś cādikaraś ca naḥ ।।
anāthā hy aparādhyante kunetāraś ca mānavāḥ ।। na māṃ bhaviṣyaṃ papracchur na cāpṛṣṭo bravīmy aham ।। parihartuṃ na śakṣyāmi kālaniṣṭhāṃ hi tāṃ gatim ।। ataś ca balavān kālaḥ śrutvāpi na kariṣyasi ।।
lekhā hi kālalikhitā veleva duratikramāḥ ।। tena bhāvena te yajñaṃ vāsavo dharṣayiṣyati ।। daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa mā yajethāś ca taṃ kratum ।। tava vā yajamānasya kālo atra parameśvaraḥ ।।
tat praṇeyaṃ nibodhasya trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। tathā yajñaphalānāṃ ca vikretāro dvijātayaḥ ।। śrutvā parihariṣyāmi bhagavan yadi śakyate ।। yatasva parihartuṃ tad ity etad bhadram astu te ।।
kṣatriyā nāhariṣyanti yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati ।। ahaṃ nimittaṃ iti ced bhayaṃ tīvraṃ ca jāyate ।। lokān utsahate gantuṃ khaṃ sapāśa iva dvijaḥ ।। yajñasya punarāvṛttir yady asty āśvāsayasva mām ।।
vihito yajña eṣo atra devaiś ca brāhmaṇair api । tejasābhyāhṛtaṃ tejas tejasyevāvatiṣṭhate ।। aśvamedhaṃ kaliyuge punaḥ pratyāhariṣyati ।। āhariṣyati rājendra śvetagraham ivāntakaḥ ।।
yugāntadvāram ṛṣibhiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ vicariṣyati ।। vinivartiṣyate loke vṛttānte vṛttimatsv api ।। cāturāśramyaśithilo dharmaḥ pravicaliṣyati ।। dhanyā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti yugāmte janamejaya ।।
tasmād dvāparavidhvaṃsād yugāntaṃ spṛhayāmy aham ।। prāptā vayaṃ ca dharmaṃ svaṃ sukham alpena karmaṇā ।। tasmāt samudvegakare yugānte pratyupasthite । pranaṣṭadharmaṃ dharmajña nimittair vaktum arhasi ।।
evaṃ bhaviṣye tu gatiṃ yogenaiva vicintayan । yugānte pūrvarūpāṇi bhagavān abravīt tadā ।। yugānte prabhaviṣyanti svarakṣaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।। śūdrāś ca brāhmaṇācārā bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।।
śūdrā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti yugānte janamejaya । ekapaṅktyām aśiṣyanti yugānte janamejaya ।। paraṃ dharmaṃ haniṣyanti manuṣyā mandabuddhayaḥ । bhāryāmitrā bhaviṣyanti yugānte janamejaya ।।
alpodakās tathā meghā alpasasyā ca medinī । bhṛtyā anirviṣṭabhujo bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। nāryaś cāpi kariṣyanti kṛṣim eva kalau yuge । akutsanā ca patite bhaviṣyati yugakṣaye ।।
aśāntās tāpasā nityaṃ bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge । unaṣoḍaśavarṣāś ca prajāsyanti narās tadā ।। pramadāḥ keśaśūlāś ca bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। aṭṭam annam iti proktaṃ śūlo vikraya ucyate । catuṣpathā brāhmaṇa iti śivo veda udāhṛtaḥ । keśo bhaga iti khyāto rājan naivātra saṃśayaḥ ।
śūdrā bhovādinaś caiva bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। ṛtavaś ca bhaviṣyanti viparītā yugakṣaye ।। śūdrā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti śākyabuddhopajīvinaḥ ।। svādūnāṃ vinivṛttiś ca vidyād antagate yuge ।।
yathānimnaṃ prajāḥ sarvā gamiṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। citravarṣī ca parjanyo yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati ।। sarve corakule jātāś corayānāḥ parasaram । svalpenāḍhyā bhaviṣyanti yat kiṃcit prāpya durgatāḥ । sarve vāṇijakāś caiva bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।।
haraṇāya prapatsyante lobhānṛtavirodhitāḥ ।। pitṛdattāni vittāni nighnantas tanayāḥ sadā । grahaṇāya pravartante lobhād anṛtavādinaḥ । bhaviṣyanti yugasyānte nāryaḥ keśair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। yugānte samanuprāpte nānyā bhāryāsamā ratiḥ ।।
puruṣālpaṃ bahustrīkaṃ tad yugāntasya lakṣaṇam ।। avicārya grahīṣyanti dānaṃ varṇāntarāt tathā । rājacorādidaṇḍārto janaḥ kṣayam upaiṣyati ।। īhayāsukhino lokā bhaviṣyanti gate yuge ।।
saṃdigdhaḥ paralokaś ca bhaviṣyati yugakṣaye ।। ātmanaś ca durācārā brahmadūṣaṇatatparāḥ । ātmānaṃ bahu manyante manyur evābhyayād dvijān । yugāpakramaṇe pūrvaṃ bhaviṣyanti dvijātayaḥ ।। ṛṇaṃ ca vinayabhraṃśo yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati ।।
ajāś caivopayokṣyante payaso arthe yugakṣaye ।। aśāstraviduṣāṃ puṃsām evam eva svabhāvataḥ । apramāṇaṃ kariṣyanti nītiṃ paṇḍitamāninaḥ । śāstroktasyāpravaktāro bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।।
na kaścid akavir nāma yugānte pratyupasthite ।। coraprāyāś ca rājāno yugānte pratyupasthite ।। aśvamedhena yakṣyanti yugānte janamejaya ।। brāhmaṇā dhanatṛṣṇārtā yugānte samupasthite ।।
ekaśaṅkhās tathā nāryo gavedhukapinaddhakāḥ ।। saṃdhyārāgo atha digdāho bhaviṣyaty apare yuge ।। vākśarais tarjayiṣyanti gurūñ śiṣyās tathaiva ca । mukheṣu ca prayokṣyanti pramattāś ca narās tadā ।
viyoniṣu cariṣyanti pramadāsu narās tadā ।। bhikṣāṃ balim adattvā ca bhokṣyanti puruṣāḥ svayam ।। puruṣāś ca prasuptāsu bhāryāsu ca parastriyam ।। na kṛtapratikartā ca kāle kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati ।।
nivatsyanti kimācārāḥ kimāhāravihāriṇaḥ ।। kāṃ ca kāṣṭhāṃ samāsādya prapatsyanti kṛtaṃ yugam ।। śīlavyasanam āsādya prāpsyante hrāsam āyuṣaḥ ।। vaivarṇyād vyādhisaṃpīḍā nirvedo vyādhipīḍanāt ।।
evaṃ gatvā parāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ prapatsyanti kṛtaṃ yugam ।। vimarśaśīlāḥ kecit tu hetuvādakutūhalāḥ ।। apramāṇaṃ kariṣyanti vedoktam apare janāḥ ।। tadā mukhabhagāś caiva bhaviṣyanti striyo aparāḥ ।
bhaviṣyanti narā mūḍhā mandāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ ।। dāmbhikās te bhaviṣyanti vādaśīlaparāyaṇāḥ ।। śubhāny evācariṣyanti dānasatyasamanvitāḥ ।। bhaviṣyati tadā lokas tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam ।।
abhipatsyati vṛttyarthaṃ tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam ।। siddhim alpena kālena yāsyanti nirupaskṛtāḥ ।। bhaviṣyati yuge kṣīṇe tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam ।। cariṣyanti vasuṃdharāṃ ।
pranaṣṭavarṇadharmāś ca । pṛthivīm upabhokṣyanti yugānte pratyupasthite ।। kravyādā brahmarūpeṇa sarvabhakṣā vṛthāvratāḥ ।। vyavāhāropavṛttāś ca cyutā dharmāc ca śāśvatāt ।।
kāmātmāno durātmānaḥ sopadhāḥ priyasāhasāḥ ।। abhāvino bhaviṣyanti munayo bahurūpiṇaḥ ।। kathāyogena tān sarvān pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। bhakṣyabhojyaharāś caiva bhāṇḍānāṃ caiva hāriṇaḥ ।।
corāś corakṣaye cāpi kṛte kṣemaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। narāḥ śrayiṣyanti vanaṃ karabhāraprapīḍitāḥ ।। pitṝn ājñāpayiṣyanti putrāḥ karmāṇi sarvaśaḥ । snuṣāḥ śvaśrūs tathā caiva yugānte paryupasthite । vākśarais tarjayiṣyanti gurūñ śiṣyāḥ samantataḥ । koṭimūṣakasarpāś ca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān ।।
uddeśena naraśreṣṭha bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। maṇḍalaiḥ prabhaviṣyanti deśe deśe pṛthak pṛthak ।। narās tadā bhaviṣyanti sarve kālapratīkṣiṇaḥ ।। kauśikīṃ saṃśrayiṣyanti narāḥ kṣudbhayapīḍitāḥ ।।
pracariṣyanti durbhikṣa vyādhibhiḥ paripīḍitāḥ । ṛṣikāntagiridroṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। araṇyāni ca vatsyanti narā mlecchagaṇaiḥ saha ।। goptāraś cāpy agoptāraḥ prabhaviṣyanti śāsinaḥ ।।
mṛgamatsyavihaṃgaiś ca kīṭaśvāpadavaṃgamaiḥ । madhuśākaphalair mūlair vartayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। svayaṃ kṛtvā nivatsyanti yathā munijanās tathā ।। ajaiḍakaṃ kharoṣṭraṃ ca pālayiṣyanti yatnataḥ ।।
pakvānnavyavahāreṇa vipaṇantaḥ parasparam ।। bahvapatyāḥ prajāhīnāḥ krūrā lakṣaṇavarjitāḥ ।। hīnādd hīnaṃ tadā dharmaṃ prajā samanuvartsyati ।। durbalā viṣayaglānā rajasā samabhiplutāḥ ।।
āyuḥprakṣayasaṃrodhādd hiṃsā coparamiṣyati ।। evaṃ viplāvite loke pīḍitāḥ saṃkṣaye kāle । jñāninas te bhaviṣyanti pīḍayā viphalodyamāḥ । satyaṃ cāpi prapatsyanti vyavahārāpaśaṅkayā ।। kariṣyanti ca saṃkocaṃ svapakṣakṣayapīḍitāḥ ।।
catuṣpādapravṛttaṃ ca dharmam āpsyanti mānavāḥ ।। svādu kiṃ nv iti vijñāya dharma eva svadiṣyati ।। yadā hānir bhaviṣyati kaleḥ sarvāṇi bhūpate । pragṛhīte tato dharme prapatsyanti kṛtaṃ punaḥ ।।
eka eva tu kālaḥ sa hīnavarṇo yathā śaśī ।। pūrṇaś ca tapasā hīno yathā kaliyuge tathā ।। anirṇiktam avijñātaṃ dāyādyam iva dhāryate ।। guṇaiḥ karmābhinirvṛttir guṇās tathyena karmaṇā ।।
yuge yuge yathākālam ṛṣibhiḥ samudāhṛtā ।। āśiṣaś ca śubhāḥ puṇyās tathaivāyur yuge yuge ।। bhaviṣyanti mahārāja narā bahvāyuṣas tadā । kṣaṇaṃ na saṃtiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivartamānaḥ ।।
atītānāgataṃ vākyam ṛṣeḥ pariṣadā śrutam ।। atarpayata tac chotraṃ maharṣer vāṅmayo rasaḥ ।। ramaṇīyaṃ tad ākhyānaṃ kṛtsnaṃ pariṣadā śrutam ।। itihāsaṃ tam ṛṣiṇā pārāśaryeṇa darśitam ।।
atītānāgataṃ yad vai muninoktaṃ dvijarṣabha । punar drakṣyāma ity uktvā jagāma bhagavān ṛṣiḥ ।। loke pravadatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śiṣṭāḥ sarve tapodhanāḥ ।। ṛtvijaḥ pārthivāś caiva pratijagmur yathāgatam ।।
jagāma roṣam utsṛtya rājā viṣam ivoragaḥ ।। āstīko apy āśramapadaṃ jagāma ca mahāmuniḥ ।। anvaśāsac ca muditas tadā pramuditāḥ prajāḥ ।। dīkṣito vājimedhāya vidhivad bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ।।
saṃviveśopagamyātha vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। saṃjñaptam aśvaṃ āviśya tayā miśrībabhūva saḥ ।। asaṃjñapto ayam aśvas te dhvaṃsety adhvaryum abravīt ।। kathayāmāsa rājarṣeḥ śaśāpa sa puraṃdaram ।।
phalena tena sarveṇa bravīmi śrūyatām idam ।। kṣatriyā vājimedhena na yakṣyantīti śaunaka ।। daurbalyaṃ bhavatām etad yad ayaṃ dharṣitaḥ kratuḥ ।। ity uktās tatyajur viprās taṃ nṛpaṃ jātamanyavaḥ ।।
rājā paramadharmajñas tadāsau janamejayaḥ । yayā me caraṇo mūrdhni bhasmareṇūṣitaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। naināṃ draṣṭum apīcchāmi parikliṣṭām iva srajam ।। anvāste yaḥ priyāṃ bhāryāṃ pareṇa mṛditām iha ।।
punar naivopabhuñjanti śvāvalīḍhaṃ havir yathā । gandharvarājaḥ provāca viśvāvasur idaṃ vācaḥ ।। na duṣyatīyaṃ patnī te vihiteyaṃ vapuṣṭamā ।। saiṣā yoṣidvarā rājan ratnabhūtānubhūyatām ।।
yajvā hy asi kuruśreṣṭha samṛddhyā vāsavopamaḥ ।। tasmād āvartitaś caiva kratur indreṇa te vibho ।। ratim indreṇa rambhāyāṃ manyase yāṃ vapuṣṭamām ।। tvattaś caiva sudurdharṣāt triyajñaśatayājinaḥ ।।
ekena vai tad ubhayaṃ tīrṇaṃ śakreṇa māyayā ।। katham anyair anācīrṇaṃ naptur dārān atikramet ।। tathaiva tava durdharṣa triyajñaśatayājinaḥ ।। gaccha doṣeṇa kālo hi sarvathā duratikramaḥ ।।
ānukūlyena devasya vartitavyaṃ sukhārthinā ।। strīratnam upabhuṅkṣvemām apāpāṃ vigatajvaraḥ ।। aduṣṭās tu striyo rājan divyās tu saviśeṣataḥ ।। parāmṛṣṭāpy asaṃraktā nopaduṣyanti yoṣitaḥ ।।
śīlavatyo namaskāryāḥ pūjyāḥ striya iva striyaḥ ।। cakāra mithyāvyatiśaṅkitātmā śāntiṃ parāṃ tatra sa dharmajuṣṭām ।। viṣayam anuśaśāsa dharmabuddhir muditamanā ramayan vapuṣṭamāṃ tām ।। na ca viṣayaparirakṣaṇāc cyuto asau na ca parigarhati vapuṣṭamāṃ ca ।।
na ca tad aśakyam anyathā hi kartum । iti narapatir ātmavāṃs tadāsau tad anuvicintya babhūva vītamanyuḥ ।। iti nṛpatir adīnavikramas tad anuvicintya babhūva nirvṛtaḥ । prakṛṣṭam āyuḥ samavāpya durlabhaṃ labheta sarvajñaphalaṃ ca kevalam ।।
tathaiva kāmān vividhān samaśnute samāptakāmaś ca cirāya nandati ।। tathā maharṣiprabhavā imā giraḥ pravardhayante tam ṛṣiṃ pravartitāḥ ।। vyādhiṃ na cāpnoti ciraṃ ca bandhanaṃ kriyāṃ ca puṇyāṃ labhate guṇānvitaḥ ।। janayati ca sutān guṇair upetān ripujanamardanavīryaśālinaś ca ।।
vipulam api dhanaṃ labhec ca vaiśyaḥ sugatim iyāc chravaṇāc ca śūdrajātiḥ ।। vihāya duḥkhāni vimuktasaṅgaḥ sa vītarāgo vicared vasuṃdharām ।। sthairyeṇa jātena punaḥ smarantaḥ sukhaṃ bhavanto vicarantu lokam ।। kathitam idaṃ hi samāsavistaraiḥ kim aparam icchasi kiṃ bravīmi te ।।
